ma mdzad pa'i gong / gtso bor slob dpon tshad ma'i skyes bu'i drung du phar phyin/ /mngon pa kun las btus/ /tshad ma rnam nges rnams so so'i gzhung 'grel rgyab chos dang
bcas pa/ mdo rtsa dag me tog 'phreng rgyud sogs 'dul ba'i skor dang / rtsa she la sogs pa dbu ma'i skor rnams gsan zhing / /khyad par phar phyin

la thugs gnyer mdzad pa'i skabs su lo ngo gnyis kyi bar la sa the btsugs nas nyin gyi dus su tsha dro yang gsol long med/ na bza' ral ba yang 'tshem long med/ mtshan gyi dus
su mnal yang log long med de/ srod la bzhun mar bteg nas gzigs/ tho rangs shar sbyangs la 'bad pas zhal ras kun grod pa med bsregs pa lta bur gyur/ phar phyin dang bsdus
sbragsbasbrags nas zur bshad mdzad pa'i tshe/ ma rmongs thams cad ha las shing bod na ka ba ling 'grems gcig la shes rab che bar grags/ de nas lo gcig gi bar la gtso bor
tshad ma rnam nges dang / phal ba'i tshul du sde mdun mdo dang bcas pa la mkhas par sbyangs/ 'chag pa dri gong gi shug pa ri ru mngon pa kun las btus kyi slob gnyer mdzad
de/ snga dro gzhung mda' tshad ma shog bu bdun tsam re dang / TIkka shog bu mda' tshad lnga re tsam thugs la bzungs/ phyi dro bshad pa rtsal bshad bu mdzad nas zla ba
gcig la mngon pa kun las btus kyi rtsa 'grel thams cad thugs su chud/ bod na mkhas pa'i grags pas ni sa steng khyab/ po ti che ba'i slob gnyer gyi bar rnams su tshad ma'i
skyes bu dang yang rtse ba sogs las/ 'khrid dang dbang bshad man ngag bsam gyis mi khyab pa gsan par mdzad do/ /dgung lo nyer gcig bzhes pa lcags pho khyi'i lo la dbus gtsang
gi grwa skor mdzad/ lta ba ngan pa thams cad sun phyungs te yang dag pa'i lta ba la sbyar ro/ /thos bsam

la dka' ba spyod pa'i mdzad pa ste lnga pa'o/ /drug pa mkhas btsun bzang gsum gyi bla ma bsten tshul/ spyir yon tan khur gyis lci ba'i bla ma bcu phraggnyis ni 'di ltar/ bla
chen tshul khrims dpal bzang /1 /yab rje brag ston rgyal mtshan dpal/2 /rnam snang ba yon tan rgya mtsho/3 /slob dpon don grub dpal/4 /rtogs ldan bsod rin pa/5 /mkhan chen
brang po lung pa dkon mchog gzhon nu/6/ 'jam skya nam mkha' dpal ldan/7 /ti shri kun dga' blo gros/8 /mkhan chen dka' bzhi pa grags pa gzhon nu/9 /byang sems bsod nams
grags pa/10 grub chen bibhu ti dA pa/11 mkhas btsun kumA ra siddhi/12 /dbu mdzad bkra shis bzang po/13 /grub chen ze dmar ba/14 /sems dpa' chen po bsod nams sengge/15 /ti
shri kun dga' rgyal mtshan/16 'jam dbyangs don yod rgyal mtshan/17 dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/18 mkhan po kun dga' rgyal mtshan/19 mnga' ris ba sangs
rgyas ye shes/20 dpon rgyab seng /21rnams so/ /khyad par bka' drin che ba'i bla ma drug ni/ mdo la bka' drin che ba tshad ma'i skyes bu bsod nams mgon po/1 dbang bka'
la bka' drin che ba gu ru dpal ldan sengge/2 bshad bka' la bka' drin che ba rong pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/3 man ngag la bka' drin che ba yang rtse ba rin chen sengge/4 nyamsnyam
myong la bka' drin che ba thar lo nyi ma rgyal mtshan/5 /zab chos sna tshogs la bka' drin che ba 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho ste drug go /de yang thar lo dang mjal
tshul ni/ sngar khro phur chos gsung ba'i tshe/ phan phyin

nyan pa'i grwa pa ye shes sengge zer ba cig yod pa nyi ma kha yar du kho ma byung / phyin nyin cig byung ba dang / chos rje'i thugs la yong sems can thams cad don bya snyam
na/ 'di gcig pu'i don yang byar mi nus 'dug /gzhan don de rang cung snga sa 'dug pas/ da dung rang gi 'dod chos 'dra bsgrub dgos pa 'dra dgongs nas/ dbu zhwa rtsa ring sna
leb ring po can cig gsol/ po ti phra mo cig khur nas/ stag pa 'og nas mar byon pas/ bla yon dang 'dang dkar gyi bar der byis pa rtsed mo rtse ba mang po 'dug pa kun dga'
nas/ a lu lu/ paNDi ta byung zer nas mdun du rgyugs nas byung ste/ paNDi ta paNDi ta/ no mo buddha ya gyis dang zer bas rten 'brel bzang dgongs thugs la dgyes pa mu med
pa 'khrungs nas thar pa gling du phebs so/ /der thar lo nyi ma rgyal mtshan lo bzhi lhag tsam gyi bar du bsten nas sgra ka tsan gnyis/ mngon brjod/ snyan dngags/ zlos gar
sogs dang / rgya gar shar nub kyi yi ge'i rigs dang / skad rigs mi 'dra ba mang po zhor la bslab/ /khyad par dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i sbyor drug zhus nas bsgoms pas nyams
rtogs khyad par can 'khrungs/ mngon shes dang rdzu 'phrul mtha' yas pa zhig la mnga' brnyes so/ /rje btsun rong po rdo rje rgyal mtshan la dus 'khor gsan pa'i tshe/ zla
ba dgu bar ma chad par bsten nas dbang bshad man ngag mtha' dag bum pa gang byo'i tshul du mnos shing rje btsun rong pa'i zhabs kyis kyang / /dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud
man ngag bcas pa'i bstan pa

mtha' dag gtad nas rgya bod gang du'ang 'gran zla med par bsngags so/ /gu ru dpal ldan seng ge la dus 'khor gyis dbang gsan dus bla ma rdo rje shugs su zhal gzigs so/ /yang
rtse ba dang tshad ma'i skyes bu gnyis khro phu sogs su snga phyir lo mang po'i bar dpon slob tu sbrel nas chos rnams gsan te bka' drin che ba'i bla mar 'dzin to/ /kun mkhyen
'phags 'od rin po che ni phyis ri phug tu gdan drangs te/ pha brgyud gsang pa 'dus pa sogs zab chos thams cad bum pa gang 'byor gsan pas/ bla ma'i zhal nas 'o chos
bdag po la 'phrod do gsung zhing / /chos rnams grub pa dang tshogs 'khor dang zang zing gi 'bul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa phul bas/ der 'phags 'od rin po che'i zhal nas/ 'bul
ba 'di rnams nged la mi dgos kyi/ /khyed rang sde gog 'dzin pa la dgos pa yin mod/ mi rgan nged la 'bul ba'i tshab mang yo ga dang gsang 'dus la yig cha gsal po re yang
'jog grub pa gyis/ de nas 'chad nyan kho na gtso bor mdzad dgos so/ /de ma mdzad na mi rgan pa'i bsam pa mi rdzogs so gsungs pas/ phyis chos rje'i zhal nas/ rang res kyang
bsgoms na man lung gu ru tsam zhig yod ste/ kun mkhyen 'phags pa'i bka' bzhin 'chad nyan kho na byed byed nas sgom long tsam rang ma byung zhes gsungs so/ /mkhas btsun
bzang gsum gyi bla ma bsten pa'i mdzad pa ste drug pa'o/ /bdun pa gdul bya'i tshogs pa bskyangs tshul ni/ sngar dgung lo sum cu yan la khro phur bzhugs pa'i tshe yang

slob ma mang po bskyangs shing / phar tshad bsdus gsum dang mngon pa sogs kyi 'chad nyan gtso bor mdzad/ phar phyin 'grel chung gi TIkka/ mthong lam stong mthun/ lta pa ngan
sel/ bu ston chos 'byung sogs kyang skabs 'di dag tu rtsom par mdzad do/ /de nas lha gen rtse rgyal po sogs kyi gdung brgyud dri ma med par 'khrungs nas/ gan rje jing gir
rgyal pos ri ri chen por mtshan gsol zhing / rgyal po chen po rnam thos sras kyi rnam 'phrul du grags pa sku zhang chen po grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos/ yab mes
kyi bzhengs pa'i zhwa lu'i gtsug lag khang nyams pa rnams gsos/ rab bzhi la mchod pa chen po bzhi gsar du btsugs/ dge 'dun gyi sde la bsnyen bkur gyi gzhis rten bzang po
btings/ dam pa'i chos kyi khrims chen po ni bcas/ thugs la chos dpon mkhan btsun bzang gsum 'dzoms pa cig spyan 'dren par bzhed nas/ de la 'di snyam du ngas btsal ba'i
chos dpon de la 'bring las mi yong / lha la gsol ba btab te lung bstan zhu dgos dgongs nas/ dkon mchog la mchod pa bshams/ dge 'dun la bsnyen bkur byas/ chos skyong la gtor
ma btang / nga'i gtsug lag khang 'di 'dzin skyong spel gsul nus pa'i mkhan po dge ba'i bshes gnyen 'di dang 'dis byas na bzang ngam/ zhes ming smos te/ rmi lam brtags
pas/ sbyin bdag chen po'i lhag bsam dag pa'i nus pa la brten te/ rmi lam du mgon po 'jam pa'i dbyangs yin zer ba'i khye'u ser po lo bcu drug lon pa'i lang tsho can/ phyag
g.yas kyis ral gri dang / g.yon gyi

mdzub brda byed pa gcig dang / yang rnam thos sras yin zer ba'i mi ser po rgyal mtshan thogs pa gcig ste/ de gnyis sengge chen po gcig la bzhon nas byung pa mgrin gcig tu/
khyod kyi bsam pa rnam par dag pa de lta bu khong du chud nas/ nged gnyis khyod kyi drung du 'ongs kyi/ khyed kyi sems can gyi don zhe thag pa nas sems pa legs so/ /chos
dpon ming smos pa de rnams kyi khrod na na tshod lo brgyad cu lon pa zhig 'dug ste/ des ni sems can gyi don lo ngo gsum las mi nus kyi/ yang dag pa'i chos dpon gcig dgos
na/ khro phu phyogs na yod pas spyan drongs shig zer te mi snang bar gyur to/ /de'i mod la mnal bsad de/ ngas de 'dra ba'i gnas nas btsal pas rnyed par dka' la/ gal te rnyed
kyang bdud kyis bar du gcod pa srid pas/ da dung brtag go snyam nas/ rgya nag tu gser yig pa btang ste/ rgya'i rtsis mkhan kiM ha shang zer ba'i mngon shes can gcig la/
ngas bod kyi yul du gong ma'i sku rim la/ banamdhe'i sde chen po 'dzugs par 'dod pas/ de'i chos dpon su 'thad/ 'dra 'bag gyis la bskur zhig zer ba bsrings bas/ lo phyed
dang gnyis la gser yig pa slebs te/ kiM ha shang gisgi 'dra 'bag shog khra la ri mor bris nas/ bdag nyid chen po'i sku'i gzugs dbyibs dang / cha byad dang / lo 'di lon
dang / spyod pa sdod gnas kyi bkod pa 'di 'dra ba zhig yin zhes ri mor bris pa byung ba/ 'dra gnyis su bkod nas gcig tshag byas/ gcig pho nya la bskur nas khro phu'i phyogs
na 'di 'dra e 'dug 'tshol shog ces mngags pas kiM hwa shang gi lung bstan ji lta ba bzhin chos rje nyid rnyed do/ /tshul de lta

bus mtshams sbyar te chos rje nyid kyi dgung lo sum cu so gcig pa lcags pho spre'u'i lo la/ dpal zhwa lu gser khang gi gtsug lag khang chen po 'di nyid du spyan 'dren zhus
nas/ 'gro ba lha dang bcas pa'i mchod gnas dam pa mdzad cing / chos sde chen por thugs phab nas bka' pod bzhi'i bshad grwa btsugs/ bstan 'gro'i don rlabs po che 'grub tu
nye ba na/ nag phyogs kyi lha klu rnams 'khrugs shing / mi 'ga' zhig gis bsam pa bsgyur nas/ chos rje nyid kyi thugs bkrugs pas/ sbyin bdag chen po la zhu yig chos kyi don
grub ces bya ba le'u gsum pa zhig mdzad nas/ bdag ni sngon tshe las ngan bsags pa'i mthus/ /chos nub chos min dar ba gangs ri'i khrod/ /chos bzhin byed pa rtsa ltar 'dor
ba'i yul/ /zas phyir chos srog gtong ba'i bod 'dir skyes/ /tshul khrims bsrungs na zog po tshul 'chos can/ /thos bsam byas na grags 'dod tshe 'di pa/ /rang tshugs bzung
na nga rgyal dregs pa can/ /kun dang bstun na col chung blo mang po/ /chos bzhin byas na kun gyis brnyasbsnyaspa'i yul/ /chos bzhin ma byas rnam smin rang la lci/ /thams
cad dga' ba'i spyod pa ma shes pas/ /bdag gi ci byas skyon du gyur la gzigs/ /rang la mi phan gzhan la gnod pa yi/ /bdag gi bshad nyan 'di 'dras ci bgyi lags/ /za 'dug 'gro
chag las sogs ci byas kyang / /gzhan gyi khong khro'i rgyu ru gyur la skyo/ /da ni tshe yang ring du mi gnas shing / /nang gi dbang po yongs su mi gsal la/ /skye 'chi'i
sdug bsngal shin

tu bzod par dka'/ /cung zad shes pa nyams len dus la babs/ /ces sogs gsungs pas/ sbyin bdag chen po dang dkar phyogs kyi grwa bu slob kun rtab rtab por gyur nas drung du lhags/
phyag kyang bsgyel ba bzhin du btsal nas/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa 'gro ba'i mig gcig khyed ji ltar bzhed pa bzhin du bdag cag rnams kyis bsgrub lags kyi/ chos
sde chen po 'dir thugs phab nas chos kyi 'khor lo rgya chen po bskor du gsol/ yang bdag cag kha cig gis ni cung zad log par bsgrub pa kun kyang gnong zhing 'gyod lags/ bdag
cag la sgrib par mi 'gyur ba zhig sku mkhyen no/ /zhes gsol ba btab pas/ chos rje nyid kyis kyang zhal gyis bzhes nas/ sngags dang mtshan nyid kyi bshad grwa rgya chen
po btsugs so/ /mdor na dus der zhwa lur dge 'dun tshogs pa rgyun bzhugs phyed lnga stong / /phyogs nas chos bar la byon pa dang kun bsgril na bdun stong sum brgya rtsa
bzhi tsam re yong / chos 'chad brgya kha bud pa/ sngags mtshan nyid kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen dbus gtsang du ston chen thon pa nyis brgya drug bcu lhag pa dang / gdan sa chen
po ri phug tu yang 'dagsbyar chu bug sgo la bzhugs mkhan lnga brgya tsam re tshogs zhes sngon gyi yi ge rnying ma dag las 'byung ngo / /dgung lo drug cu re bzhi ba chu
mo sbrul gyi lo la khro phu lo tstsha ba'i gdan sa mdzad/ der yang bshad grwa dang sgom grwa rgya chen po bskyangs so/ /gzhan yang snga phyi nges med du/ dpal ldan sa skya/
bo dong e sogs dbus gtsang gi chos grwa rnams su bstan pa'i bya ba mdzad pa'i

tshul re re bzhin smos kyi mi lang bas 'dir zur tsam mo/ /gdul bya'i tshogs pa bskyangs pa'i mdzad pa ste bdun pa'o/ brgyad pa 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyis dga' ston spel tshul
ni/ de yang snyim pa'i me tog las/ skyes bu dam pa 'dis dbyar dgun gyis dus chos la/ phar phyin mngon pa kun las btus/ tshad ma rnam nges/ spyod 'jug rnams la nyid kyi
TTIkka btab pa dang / 'dul ba mdo rtsa la bya 'dul 'dzin gyi TTIkka btab pa gtso bor rgyun du gsungs/ gzhan yang mdo rgyud kyi bshad pa/ lung bka'/ dbang bka'/ gdams ngag

sngar khro phur bzhugs dus bon po'i grwa skor sogs log par smra ba thams cad tshar bcad/ gzhan yang snga phyi thams cad du lta ba ngan pa thams cad bsun phyungs te yang dag
pa'i lta ba la sbyor ba sogs mdzad de/ mdor na rtsod ngag gnam lcags rdo rje'i char drag po phab nas log smra bdud sde'i mgo bo 'gems pa la dpa' ba'i tshul gyis bstan pa
rin po che gsal bar mdzad pa yin no/ /rtsom pa ji ltar mdzad pa'i skor tsam brjod na/ gnyis med dus 'khor gyi skor la chos tshan che chung 'dres pa lnga bcu nga bdun/ rnal
'byor pha rgyud kyi skor la chos tshan sum cu tham pa/ ma brgyud la chos mtshan sum du so bdun/ rnal 'byor rgyud la chos tshan lnga bcu tham pa/ spyod rgyud la chos tshan
gcig /bya rgyud la chos tshan bco brgyad/ sngags spyi'i gsal byed gsung rab nyer gcig ste kun la dril bas rdo rje theg pa'i skor la bstan bcos nyis brgya dang bcu bzhi'o/
/mtshan nyid theg pa mdo sde/ 'dul ba/ mngon pa rnams dang / gtan tshigs rig pa/ tshad ma'i bstan bcos/ sgra'i bstan bcos sogs la chos tshan nyer lnga/ rigs gnas spyi'i

gyi snying

pos gang ba/ rgyan rin po che sna tshogs pas brgyan pa/ mtshan dang dpe byad du 'bar ba/ 'od dang 'od zer 'phro ba de'i khri rgyab la thugs dkyil gyi lha tshogs rnams kyis
bskor ba/ gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku la rdo rje dbyings rtsa ba'i lha tshogs kyis bskor ba/ gsang 'dus mi bskyod rdo rje'i sku khri rgyab la lha

kyai rdor/ bde mchog dus 'khor rnams zhal dngos su gzigs te/ ji skad du/ sa skya paNDi ta gnyis pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan gyis/ byams mgon 'jam pa'i dbyangs dang sgrol ma
sogs

rgyal sras nag pa'i sa la gnas rnams kyis/ /byin gyis brlabs shig lhag par rjes su bzungs/ /zhes dang / kye rdor bde mchog dus kyi 'khor lo sogs/ /mchog gi dkyil 'khor du ma
mngon sum gzigs/ /zhes sogs kyis bstod pa mdzad pa ltar yin la/ der ma zad mnal lam du yang mdo sngags kyi glegs bam mang po gzigs rtog grub pa dang / bla ma rje btsun
chen po grags pa rgyal mtshan sogs grub pa'i dbang phyug rnams kyis kyang rjes su bsngags nas mdo sngags kyi gsung rab la zhu dag mdzad par bskul tshul dang / dus gsum mkhyen
pa'i mngon shes dang rdzu 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i tshul rnams kyang 'dir re zhig mdor bsdus pa'o/ /bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i mdzad pa ste bcu pa'o/ /bcu gcig 'gro
kun smin grol la bkod pa'i mdzad pa ni/ de yang sku tshe'i stod smad thams cad du gzhan don la dus skad cig kyang mi g.yel khyad par du dgung lo drug cu re gnyis pa lcags
mo yos bu'i lo la g.ya' bzang pa dang sde srid phag mo grub pa'i 'khrugs bsdums la nyi ma dbus kyi rgyal khams la byon/ de'i lam bar thams cad du skye bo khri phrag mang
po smin grol la bkod/ jag dpon cogs pa sngo thur dang / srin po mgo dgu pa zer ba la sogs pa rnams kyang ma rungs pa'i sems zhi ste chos rje nyid skyel ba dang / bsu
ba dang bsnyen bkur byed/ gam pa byang thang gi rab btsun gtsug lag khang / drang srong srin por grwa thang gi gtsug lag khang / khra 'brug gi gtsug lag khang / 'ol kha tshe
thang gi

gtsug lag khang / gzhan yang yer pa/ gung thang / 'phrul snang / ra mo che/ mtshur phu/ byang u ri/ gzhu kun dga' ra ba/ snye mo tshal mig /gyab mdo phug la sogs pa'i gtsug
lag khang che chung / bshad grwa sgom grwa thams cad du byon nas/ sngags dang mtshan nyid kyi bshad srol sngar med pa rnams su srol btsugs/ yod pa rnams dar rgyas su mdzad/
skal ldan gyi 'gro ba mang po smin grol la bkod/ yul mi gcig pa khag khag so so rnams su dge bshes nga mkhas sam nga mkhas sam snyam pa mang po kha rong rong por smra
ste/ la las sngags la las mtshan nyid sogs dri ba byas pa na/ de thams cad kyi lan gang la gang dgos shar shar btab pas/ kun kyang the tshom chod cing lhag par yang dad
pa 'phel bar gyur to/ drags po'i yul ljongs su phebs pa na rje btsun sgrol mas dngos su sprul pa bkye nas yul de'i mi rnams kyi bsnyen bkur byed pa bskul ste/ de yang bud
med mi tshad nyis 'gyur gyi che ba gos chen ne tso kha gyon pa/ gtsang mo'i rgyan cha khra chom me ba/ dpon g.yog gsum gang nas byung cha med par 'ongs te/ yul mi rnams
la kye grong mi rnams/ sang nang par snga dro'i cha la yul mang rong la/ bla ma dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po 'byon gyi/ khyed cag gis zam pa 'dzugs pa dang / phebs bsu dang
phebs skyel sogs byas na tshogs rdzogs sgrib pa dag bsod nams chen po thob bo zer nas mi snang ba gyur to/ nang par snga mor mi de dag yul mang rong du 'ongs te thang
shing gi zam pa 'dzugs pa dang lam 'phrang sel ba sogs byed do/ /de'i tshe zhabs 'bring ba

dag gis khyed cag ci byed dris pa na/ 'di ltar gyur gyi lo rgyus smras te/ chu che che rnams la ni thang shing gi zam pa'i steng nas gdan drangs/ chung chung rnams la ni rgyab
tu khur nas gdan drangs te/ zhal la yun ring po'i bar du bltas nas phyag 'tshal byin rlabs zhu/ zhabs spyi thog tu blangs nas/ tshogs rdzogs par gyur cig sgrib pa dag
par gyur cig ces smon lam btab nas song ngo / de lta bu'i tshul gyis mthong thos dran reg gi 'gro ba dpag tu med pa 'khor ba mtha' can du mdzad de/ mdor na bdag nyid chen
po 'di'i snyan grags kyi gdugs dkar po gcig gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad khyab pas/ rgya gar yul gyi rgyal po buNya ma la sogs pas kyang / shAkya mu ne'i rgyal tshab/
bstan pa'i srog shing chen po/ bla ma bu ston chen po'i sku la bsnyun mi mnga' 'am/ thugs zer ma mchis sam/ ldang ba yang ngam/ gshegs pa spyod dam/ zhes sogs kyi zhu
'phrin skyes dang bcas pa phul ba dang / khyad par rgya nag gi rgyal po tho gon the mur gan gyi rgya nag tu gdan 'dren pa'i gser yig brdzangs kyang phyogs de'i gdul bya
dus la ma babs par gzigs nas gdan ma 'drongs so/ /gzhan yang stobs kyis 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po jing gir gan gyi bu tsha brgyud drug pa/ rgyal bu bradznyA cing ze'u
cing dbang hor gyi mi dpon brgya phrag dmag 'bum tsho gsum dang khri phrag gnyis kyi 'khor dang bcas pa/ chos rje nyid kyi drung du lhags nas dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang
sogs chos zab la rgya che ba zhus/ chos kyi yon du sku 'bum mthong grol chen mo la dbyar gyi

na bza'i tshul du gos yug nyis brgya dang brgyad cu rtsa dgu/ dgun gyi na bza'i tshul du ka shi ka'I ras dang / wa ra Na si'i ras bal las grub pa'i 'phyangs pa yug nyis brgya
dang brgyad cu rtsa dgu/ mchod rten gzhan thams cad la gos yug bcu gnyis bcu gnyis re'i na bza'i rgyu phul zhing / rin po che dang mchod pa'i bye brag bsam gyis mi khyab
pas rdo'i phung po bzhin du spangs nas phul bas/ chos rje'i zhal nas/ 'di lta bu'i yon phul ba ngo mtshar che mod kyi/ mi rgan nga'i 'dod pa ni da dung ma tshims zhes
gsungs pas/ rgyal bu na re/ ngas 'di lta bu'i mchod sprin phul bas bla ma ma mnyes na/ da ni de las khyad par du 'phags pa'i mchod sprin dngos su sbyor rgyu gzhan ma mchis
pas/ nga rang gi mnga' ris su gtogs pa'i zhing khams ci tsam yod pa de'ang bla ma khyed la 'bul lo/ zhes gsol pas/ chos rje nyid kyi bka' stsal ba/ rgyal bu lags/ sngon
yang dag rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi smon lam rnam par dag pa'i mdo las/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gdan ba der/ rgyal po'i chad pa'i ming yang med cing / /btson ra dang
khrims btson la sogs pa'i nyes pa de dag cis kyang med cing mi 'byung bar gyur cig ces gsung na/ dkon mchog gsum po ni skyabs gnas dam pa yin la/ de'i ngos nas mdo las/
dge 'dun dkon mchog ni thar pa thob pa'o/ zhes gsungs pas/ da res nged la chos kyi yon tu btson ra dang / khrims btson du chud pa dang / mig dbyung ba dang / yan lag gcod
pa dang / srog la bab

pa'i chad pa gtong ba sogs kyi nyes pas mnar ba thams cad ci bder btang nas mi 'jigs pa byin cig bcas gsung pas/ rgyal bus kyang de bzhin du bgyi'o/ /zhes lo bcu gnyis kyi
bar du 'bangs la nyes pa'i ming yang mi grags pa khrims su bcas/ rgyal bu 'khor dang bcas pa slar rang gi yul du bzhud do/ /dgung lo drug cu rtsa bdun pa me pho spre'u'i
lo dgun ra'i tshes lnga zla ba gro bzhin gyi 'grub sbyor la/ zhwa lu'i gdan sa thugs sras lo tstsha bar gtad/ chos rje nyid gtso cher ri phug tu brtan chags/ gdan sa gtad
nas kyang lo dgu'i bar la chos kyi 'khor lo rgyun mi chad par bskor nas gdul bya bsam gyis mi khyab pa smin cing grol bar mdzad do/ /'gro kun smin grol la bkod pa'i mdzad
pa ste bcu gcig pa'o/ /|bcu gnyis pa gzugs sku chos dbyings su brtul te byams pa'i thugs kar thim tshul ni/ dus lan gcig thugs sras lo tstsha ba zhwa lu na bzhugs yod pa
la ri phug tu byon gsung / drung du phebs dus su nga dang na zla'i dbus gtsang gi dge bshes tsho yang thams cad gshegs tshar 'dug nga grwa bskor byed dus kyi lan 'debs
pa rnams kyang zhang bya dpe ma gtogs da gcig kyang ma las 'dug nga yang ring por mi sdod pas/ shi tsa na shul du dge rtsa tig tig e yong rang mi shes/ dge rtsa rang gi sngon
du 'gro ba'am/ dga' ldan du 'gro ba'i phyi phyag byed pas/ khyod la yang shog byas pa yin gsungs nas spong thag chen po zhig mdzad/ dus 'khor lha khang du nag nya'i
sgrub mchod kyis cho ga mdzad pa'i tshe/ sku

bsnyel so mdzad nas/ da res sgrub mchod rgyas po gcig byas la/ de nas byams mgon gyi drung du 'gro gsungs pas/ la stod pa blo rgyas phyag btsal nas de skad mi gsung bar zhu/
dga' ldan byams pa rang gis chos gsung ba lags/ drung nas 'di ru 'gro ba'i don la bzhugs 'tshal zhes zhus pas ci yang mi gsung / yang skabs shig mdangs gsum rmi lam shin
tu bzang ba 'dug ste/ dga' ldan nas skasskras pa ring po gsum byung dbus la ni byams pa 'byon gyi 'dug go ngos gcig la ngas 'dzegs phyin/ ngos gcig po de la sus phyin nam
zhes gsung / de nas chu mo yos kyi lo dgun bzhugs la bab pa'i tshe/ da ni grwa pa rnams la zhwa lur dgun chos la byon gyis/ mtshams pa rnams mtshams bsdoms/ nga yang mun
khang bsrubs nas dge sbyor byed do gsungs nas nyin mtshan khor yug tu thugs dam la bzhugs so/ de nas shing pho 'brug gi lo zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes gcig nas sku bsnyung
ba'i tshul bstan/ bco lnga la zla ba sgra gcan gyis zin pa dang nag pa zla ba la nyi ma dmar nag shar pa sogs ltas ngan te/ rgyal sras thogs med bzang po sogs bu slob rnams
'dus/ gser gyi maNDal phul gsol ba rtse gcig tu btab pa'i dgos pa dang dgag bya 'ga' zhig gzigs nas re zhig sku khams dwangs tshul bzhes mod/ slar gdul bya rtag 'dzin
can rnams 'dul ba'i phyir du zla ba lnga ba'i tshes bcu drug nas snyun log pa'i rnam pa bstan cing / de nas chos rje nyid kyis dgung lo bdun cu don lnga bzhes pa/ shing

pho 'brug gi lo/ hor zla drug pa nyi ma karTa'i khyim du gnas pa'i nyi shu gcig gi tshes kyi chu tshod ma zad pa'i sang tho rangs/ gza'i dang po nyi ma/ rgyu skar gyi dang
po tha skar/ sbyor ba las bzang / byed pa bhin po rnams 'dzoms pa/ glang gi dus sbyor 'char pa'i dus su rgyal ba byams pa'i thugs kar thim nas de'i tshe 'ja' 'od rol mo'i
sgra dang me tog gi char sogs ngo mtshar ba'i cho 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung ngo / sku gdung ring bsrel gyi snying po can gyis zhing 'dir gdul bya'i tshogs gnyis
spel tshul yang / ji skad du rgyal sras thogs med bzang pos/ gdul bya'i don du zhing gzhan gshegs pa na/ /sku gzugs ring bsrel mang pos zhing 'di yi/ /gdul bya'i tshogs
gnyis 'phel zhing rgyas mdzad pa'i/ /chos rje rin po che la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes so/ gzims mal sku 'dra sogs 'dra 'bag tu bzhengs pa rnams la yang grub chen man lung gu
ru sogs 'ja' lus rdo rje'i sku brnyes pa'i sar gnas kyi byang sems rnams dngos su byon nas mchod pa 'bul ba sogs byung ste/ ji skad du/ lhar bcas 'jig rten kun gyis khyad
dngos su/ /mchod la ngo mtshar ci 'dra 'bag tsam la'ang / /'ja' tshon sku can grub chen man lung pas/ /mchod sprin 'phreng ba spel ba de la 'dud/ /ces so/ de ltar re zhig
dga' ldan yid dga' chos 'dzin du thugs las chur ngur gzhol ba'i tshul bstan kyang / /slar yang dag dang ma dag pa'i zhing khams rnams su 'gro ba'i don la sku gsung thugs

kun dga' blo gros dang / rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug yar klungs ba sengge rgyal mtshan sogs mkhas grub mang po chos rje nyid kyi rnal 'phrul du ngos 'dzin pa byung ngo / /de
yang ji skad du/ rgyal dbang lnga bas/ mgon khyod phul byung mdzad pa'i mai na ka/ /dag pa'i zhing gi bkod pa rgya mtsho ru/ /bye ba phrag brgyar yongs su gar bsgyur yang

ltar gyis sangs

rgyas shAkya thub pa yan byon zin pa rnams yin la/ de nas ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas dang po ni byams pa/ /gnyis pa byang chub sems dpa' seng ge /gsum pa ni rab gsal ste/ de
nyid sA la'i dga' tshal gyi ljongs gangs ri'i khrod 'dir gnas lnga rig pa'i paNDi ta chen po 'jig rten gyi mig skad gnyis smra ba'i lo tsA ba'i tshul bzung ba/ mdor na shes
bya thams cad mkhyen cing gzigs pa don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos na bu ston rin chen grub ces bya ba'i rgyal ba gnyis pa de'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs/ zhes pa ste sngon
'jug gi don bstan zin to/ /da ni rab gsal du 'tshang rgya ba'i tshul dngos ni/ mdo sde bskal pa bzang po las/ de bzhin gshegs pa rab gsal skye ba'i yul ni rgyu skar can
zhes bya'o/ /rigs ni rgyal rigs so/ /'od ni dpag tshad lnga'o/ /yab ni legs pa'i blo gros so/ /yum ni me tog ces bya'o/ /sras ni dus rig go /rim gro ni dga' ba'i dbang
phyug go /shes rab can gyi mchog ni bkra shis so/ /rdzu 'phrul can gyi mchog ni 'brug sgra'o/ /'dus ba dang po la ni nyan thos bya ba phrag 'bum mo/ /gnyis pa la ni dung

/ dus der 'khor gyi 'og mar

skye ba'i rgyu tshogs la 'bad pa gal che ste/ de yang gang zhe na gzhi tshul khrims rnam par dag pa la gnas dgos te/ chos rje nyid kyi zhal nas/ bstan pa'i snying po tshul
khrims bslab pa rin po che/ /'phral dang yun du bde legs thams cad 'byung ba'i rgyu/ /zhes gsungs shing tshul khrims ma bsrungs na/ thos bsam ma byas kyang phan pa med de/

rgyal ba rab gsal

gyi 'khor du skyes nas bdud rtsi'i bgo skal la longs spyod pa'i rgyu tshogs kyi gtso bo yin pa shes par byas te/ de lta bu'i tshul la 'bad par bya'o/ /'dir smras pa/ bgrang

ci yang bsgyur/ /rnam 'dren bzhi pa'i thugs kyi bang mdzod rnams/ /yongs rdzogs bdag gir bzhes nas sA la'i ljongs/ /zab rgyas chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i tshe/ /thub dbang

la/ /rjes chags 'dren byed rnam brgyad g.yo 'di ci/ /rgyal dang rgyal sras de sprul thams cad kyis/ /'byor 'gyur rgyal ba gsum par nges so zhes/ /bsngags brjod me tog dkar

chen po las chu thigs

tsam brjod pa'i sarga ste dang po'o/ / //kun mkhyen bu ston rin chen grub kyi rnam thar rdzogs so/|rab dkar zla ba'i rang bzhin mtshan dpe'i sku/ /rab snyan drug cu'i dbyangs
ldan tshangs pa'i gsung / /rab 'byams shes bya'i chos kun mkhyen pa'i thugs/ /'jam dpal smra ba'i lha des shes rab stsol/ /zhes tshigs su bcad pa sngon du btang nas/ gnyis
pa bdag nyid chen po de'i gsung las 'khrungs pa'i thugs sras bu chen rnams kyi rtogs brjod bshad pa la/ rig pa'i gnas lnga la mkhas shing bka' babs kyi bu chen byon

lar 'khrungs shing / de rjes rnal 'byor gyi

dbang phyug rong pa rga lo rnam rgyal rdo rje'i sras mkhas grub dam pa rong pa shes rab sengge 'khrungs pa ste/ mdor na rgya bod gnyis su bstan 'gro'i dpal du gyur pa'i paNDi
ta dang grub thob kyi skye ba brgyud mang bzhes so/ sku tshe 'di nyid du 'khrungs tshul yang mtshan shin tu che ste rigs bskrun pa'i yab la ma ltos bar mkha' spyod kyi
ril bu la brten nas 'khrungs pa'i phyir ro/ /de yang 'di ltar paN grub dA na shI la'i dus ye shes kyi Ta kis stsal ba'i skye ba 'dzin pa'i ngo mtshar mkha' spyod kyi ril
bu dkar po zhes bya ba zhig yod pa de/ dngul gyi ga'u'i nang du bcug nas rong ngur smrig gi sgrol ma'i sku rgyab tu gter du sbas so/ /phyis su rong pa shes rab seng ge grong
khar smon lam 'phel bya ba'i dge slong mngon shes dang nyams rtogs thar thor yod pa gcig gter de 'don du bcug nas 'di nyid kyi yum dang ril bu ster lugs kyi zhal bkod
zhib po mdzad skad/ smon lam 'phel bas kyang bla ma'i bka' bzhin ril bu khyer te rong e dmar nas nyi shar tsam la 'ongs pas pa bsnams bsam sding gi ri khrod du nyi ma phyed

pa zhig 'dug pa/ bla mas lung bstan pa'i yum de yin par ngo mkhyen/ de dag la mkhas btsun gzhon nu grub kyi bde mchog bcu gsum ma'i dbang gnang bar bzhed pa dang / rong
du rje shes rab sengge sku gshegs nas ril bu la 'od dang

dri bzang po 'khor ba sogs byung skad/ de nas dbang mdzad pa'i tshe smon lam 'phel bas mchod g.yog byed par zhus nas bum dbang ma rdzogs kyi bar la ril bu slas/ rdzogs pa dang
gsang dbang gi rdzas byin po la phyogs gcig byas/ rilral bu btab pa gcig zur du phye nas sbas/ gsang dbang gi rdzas gzhan rnams la byin tshar ba dang / btsun ma gral
