su byung nang du ma gtod/ nged la gzhan ci yang mi dgos/ dro bar jag ram sun gsum re drongs gsungs/ thugs dam kho na la bzhugs so/ /zhag lnga song ba dang / dge bshes
rgyal grub slebs byung / nga sku mdun du yongs pa yin zer ba zhus shog zer/ su yang ma gtong gsung gin 'dug byas pas/ kha sang nas ma khom pas dbang med yin mod/ khyod kyi
zhabs tog de la yid brtan mi thub zer/ der shAkya dpal dang rgan gzhon gyi khyad chos pas sgo phye zer ma thub par nang du byung / rgyu mtshan rnams lab ma nus par/ da
gsol ba yang mi bzhes/ su dang yang mi 'phrad par thugs dam mdzad kyin yod byas pas/ khong gis

brang la gcig rgyab khyod 'dra ba'i zhags tog pa yong ba ang / lan cha yang mi gtong ba zer nas gzims chung du shor song / de 'phral phyir byung ste/ da len en spyod brtsings
pa yin 'dug /daci drag zer/ da khyod shes mod/ en cig nas gsol ja de zhu ran pas 'dren du phyin na zhal lta yong ngam byas pas/ de kha drag zer/ shAkya dpal bas ja zhu
bar byon pas/ sngar gsung mi 'byon pa la/ der khyod kyis kyang go ma chod/ kho yang mos gus dang zhen pa yod pa skyon du song / khong rnams zhag bdun bar la ma byung na/
bu hrang lo chung 'dra ba'i gsang sngags kyi lag rjes bzhag rgyu yod pa yin te gsungs/ thugs dam grol lo/ /dgung lo drug cu re bzhi bzhes pa'i dus/ sku khams cung zad snyel
ba la sku rim sgrub pa zhus pas/ bsod nams kyi tshogs bsags pa la 'gal ba med/ nged chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i dgung lo'i tshad tshun sdod bsam na'ang / de'i steng
du gnas pa'i rigs su mi gda'/ 'on kyang re zhig khams bzang po yong gsungs/ dgung lo bdun bcu pa bzhes pa'i tshe/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen nyis brgya lhag tsam la/ rdor dbyings
'grel lugs kyi dbang dang / zhi byed brgyud pa phyi ma'i skor tshang ba gnang nas/ 'o dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen pa rnams la chos bshad pa'i mjug de tsam gyis bsdus mchis/
zhes gsungs te/ de yan la ston dpyid zla ba gnyis tsam re thugs dam la bzhugs/ thun mtshams rnams su

bstan bcos rtsom pa sogs kyang mdzad/ gzhan chos 'chad pa kho na mdzad pa gsungs so/ /de nas dgung lo bdun cu don gcig pa sa pho 'brug gi lo/ /hor zla dgu pa'i nyi shu brgyad
la/ lha rje mkhar kha ba dge slong la shog gyis gsungs nas/ nges kyi tshe'i 'dun pa chos rje'i dgung lo'i bar tsam 'dug na'ang / chos thams cad rten 'brel du 'char ba'i
don gyis da rdzogs tshar/ na tsha ci yang med/ khyed la shog ma byas na/ 'khor rnams la mi mangs kyis brjod zlos byung dogs snyad zad zad la bos pa yin gsung / zla ba bcu
pa'i tshes gnyis kyi snga dro sku zhang du dben sha ba la/ nges kyi khakhar sang nas gdan sa pa gcig bskos na 'thad zer ba rang re yab sras la yang yang labs pa yin yang
/ g.yas med byed kyin 'dug /da phyi'i lha sde mi sde ni mi gda'/ sde chung 'di'i bzo shor nas gda'i/ zhwa lu'i gtod rnams rgyal grub kyikyis gtod rgyu yin/ ri phug gi
phyag dpe dbang rdzas rnams gal che shos yin pas dpal bzang gigis gtod rgyu yin/ zhwa lu'i phyag dpe rnams shAkya dpal gyigyis gtod rgyu yin pas/ zags pa byung na bstan rgyun
la gnod pas ma zags pa gal che'o gsung / du dben sha bas phyag phul nas/ thugs sna mi btud par 'gro ba'i don du bzhugs par zhu zhus pas/ gdan sa ba de nged rang yod
thog 'dir bskos na legs par yod kyang de ni ma byung / da dung de la

thugs rtsol gyis gsung / gdan sa pa'ang thugs rtse gang 'thad de zhal lta gnang ba zhu zhus pas/ gang ltar na'ang sdom rgyun 'di gal shin tu che pa yin pas/ rab nged kyi sdom
phrug yin pa la phyi mtshan nyid/ nang gsang sngags thams cad tshang pa gcig /'bring sdom phrug yin pa la bka' bzhi 'phags yo ga dus gsum yod pa'i yon tan yar 'phel zhig
tha ma'ang sdom phrug yin pa bka' bzhi yod pa la sngags mtshan nyid sgra dang bcas pa la slob pa'i blo gros yod pa gcig la bskos mdzod gsungs/ du dben sha bas de yi ger
bris nas thugs dam gyis mnon par zhus pas/ mjug tu 'di'ang bris gsungs/ khro phu lo tsA las/ gal te phyis nas blo ldan skye bo 'ga'/ /byung na khyed cag dka' spyad ma 'jigs
par/ /byams chen gnas bcas zhabs tog rgya chen dang / /bshad sgrub shes rab snying brtses brgyan par mdzod/ /gsung ba mdzad nas thugs dam gyis mnan nas bzhag go/ de
nas zhal kyal dang ku re'i tshul 'ga' mdzad cing gsol ja bzhes nyi ma rgas pa dang du dben sha ba zhwa lur thegs/ de nas nyid kyi zhal lta la btsun chung bsod nams grub kyis
nged kyi phung po 'di me lha la phul/ thal ba 'di gtsang po la 'khyol ba zhig cis kyang gyis gsung / gzims chung du byon nas nya gnas la sku 'dra'i drung na mchod bshams
e yod gsung / des kyang bshams yod zhus pas/ 'o de legs gsung / phyag thal mo sbyar nas chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston

rin po che la skyabs su mchi gsungs/ spyan nam mkha' la cher mdzad/ de nas phyag mnyam gzhan mdzad de/ mdor na snyung ba ci yang med par/ nyid kyi dgung lo don gcig sa pho
'brug lo/ zla ba bcu ba'i tshes gnyis kyi nyi ma nub mtshams su dbu'i gtsug nas 'od dkar dmar gnyis thon nas gzugs sku chos kyi dbyings su bsdus te dga' ldan du rgyal ba
rab gsal gyi spyan sngar gshegs so/ /sku gdung me lha la phul bas/ gshed dmar gyi sku dang ring bsrel bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ rtsa dbu ma ro rkyang dang bcas pa mnyams par
byon/ phyi rten nang rten rnams ri phug tu bzhengs/ lo dus kyi mchod pa da lta'i bar du yod/ brgyud 'dzin gyi slob ma/ grub dbang nam mkha'i mtshan can/ 'jam dbyangs grags
pa rgyal mtshan lha btsun rnam rgyal sogs zhwa lu nyid du byon pa'i mkhas grub du ma dang / gzhan yang lo tsA ba skyabs mchog dpal bzang / bo dong lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal
mtshan/ lo tsA ba don bzang / sa skya 'khon gyi gdung rgyud 'am dbyangs bzhi thog pa sogs dang / sa bzang 'phags pa/ dbus pa blo gsal/ nya dbon chen po/ g.yag phrug
pa sangs rgyas dpal/ re mda' ba gzhon nu blo gros/ karmma pa dkon mchog gzhon nu/ kun mkhyen shes rab dpal bzang / mkhan chen grub pa shes rab pa sogs re re nas smos kyis
mi lang ba lta bu byon/ rje btsun chos kyi rgyal po shar btsong kha pa blo bzang grags

pa'i dpal gyis kyang 'di nyid la bde mchog bcu gsum ma dang / khyad par gsang 'dus 'jam dpal rdo rje zhus nas bsgrubs pas zhal gzigs zhes grags so/ /mi che ba'i slob ma/ si
tu byang chub rgyal mtshan/ hor gyi rgyal rgyud rgyal bu phing chang / hor bi ma la gu shrI/ rgya'i dpon chen dbang rgyal gro hong tshe dbang che chung sogs mtha' yas so/
/sgra rig pa'i skabs so/ /gnyis pa ni/ bsod nams dpal gyis tshad ma lhun grub pa/ /zhes gtan tshigs rig pa'i bka' babs kyi bu chen kun mkhyen chen po bsod nams dpal grub
ni/ 'khrungs yul nyang stod kyi sa'i sman ljongs/ rtsis gnas gsar rgyal khang bya bar/ yab yum rnag rigs dang cho 'brang sogs mi dman pa'i sras sui gyur te/ gzhon nu nas
rgyal ba'i bstan pa la rab tu byung zhing tshul khrims mig gi 'bras bu bzhin du bsrung bar mdzad/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i drung du spyir rig pa'i gnas mtha' dag
la makas par sbyangs/ khyad par mngon sum dang rjes dpag gi sgo nas gzhan bya phyi nang gi chos rnams thams cad gtan la 'bebs pa'i gtan bcos kyi gnas la/ dgra bcom pa chos
skyob kyi tshad ma me wa gha/ dbyig gnen gyis tshad ma smra ba'i sgrom/ phyogs glang gis rab tu byed pa brgya rtsa brgyad/ tshad ma kun las btus/ chos kyi grags pas tshad
ma sde bdun mdzad pa las/ gtso bo lus lta bu'i bstan bcos gsum/ rgyas pa rnam 'grel/ 'bring po rnam nges/ bsdus pa rigs thigs/

'khor yan lag gi bstan bcos bzhi la/ rgyud gzhan sgrub pa/ 'brel ba brtag pa/ gtan tshigs thigs pa/ rtsod pa'i rigs pa ste bdun/ de'i 'grel pa slob dpon chos mchog gis mdzad
pa'i tshad ma chos mchog /bram ze lha dbang gi tshad ma gzhan sel/ slob dpon dpa' bo'i rtog ge 'bar ba/ de la sogs te mang du yod pa las/ bdag nyid chen po 'dis gtso bo
lus lta bu'i bstan bcos bar pa tshad ma rnam par nges pa/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i TIkkA dang bcas pa dang / phal pa'i tshul du sde bdun mdo dang bcas pa la sbyangs
bas mkhas pa chen por gyur nas tshad ma'i bka' bsas kyi bu chen du grags so/ /dus der pas kyi rgol ba 'joms pa la dpal ldan phyogs kyi glang po dang / chos kyi grags po
lta bur gyur pas/ ji skad du/ mdo dang sde bdun rigs pa'i gzhung kun la/ /smra ba'i dbang por gyur khyod phyogs glang dang / /chos kyis grags pas phas kyi rgol ba rnams/
/mi smra'i brtul zhugs dag la bkod pa bzhin/ /zhes so/ slob ma bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'dus kyang thugs kyi sras bzhir grags pa ni/ 'chad pa la mkhas pa rin chen don bzang
/ rtsod pa la mkhas pa rin chen gser 'od/ rtsom pa la mkhas pa bsod nams don grub/ 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum la mkhas pa mkhas grub nor bzang rin chen ste bzhi'o/ /de rnams
la yang slob rgyud mkhas btsun bzang gsum

dang ldan pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung ngo / /gtan tshigs rig pa'i skabs so/ /gsum pa ni/ shes rab spyan gyis bzo rig 'bum sde gzigs/ /zhes bzo rig pa'i bka' babs rgyal ba'i
sras po sher 'bum pa ni/ spyir gyi rig gnas/ sde snod/ rgyud sde mtha' dag la mkhas/ nang tshan gsang sngags la mkhas/ bye brag pha rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa la mkhas/ khyad
par bzo rig pa'i gnas de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gzugs kyi cha tshad/ rgyud sde bzhi'i dkyil 'khor gyi thig dang bkod pa/ bde gshegs mchod rten brgyad kyi thig dang bkod
pa/ mdo rgyu dang bstan bcos rnam dag las gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang 'jig rten lugs kyi bstan bcos brtag pa rnam pa brgyad la sogs pa rang gzhan gyi 'dod pa skong ba'i
thabs sna tshogs la mi mkhyen pa bya ba med pas bzo'i gnas la bka' babs pa'i bu chen du grags so/ /de skad du'ang / bzo dang zlos gar lugs kyi shes bya la/ srid 'dir khyod
dang mtshungs pa ma rnyed pas/ /'jig rten byed po rang gis ma byas par/ ya mtshan ci las byung zhes bsam pas brel/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar ro/ /phal cher ri phug tu thugs
dam 'ba' zhig mdzad ces grags/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa dgung lo drug cu re gsum bzhes pa'i tshe so phag las grub pa'i sku 'bum mthong grol chen mo dpangs la chos rje'i
phyag khru drug cu re dgu/ zhengs la phyag khru nyi shu rtsa gsum yod pa/ phyi'i zur rnams na bde gshegs mchod rten

brgyad dang / gzhan yang dus 'khor lugs kyi mchod rten/ rnam rgyal mchod rten/ bdud 'dul mchod rten rnams bkod nas bzhugs pa/ rdo'i gdugs la rdo'i tog gis spras pa shin tu
ngo mtshar ba lta bas chog mi shes pa cig gi bdud rtsir byed cing / lha mi kun gyi mchod sdong bla na ma mchis pa 'di nyid kyi bzo rig pa mdzad/ phyis thugs sras lo tsA ba'i
thugs dam bkra shis sgo mangs kyi zhal talta yang mdzad ces gsungs so/ /bzo rig pa'i bu chen gyi skabs so/ /bzhi pa ring 'tsho'i don yod gso rig 'dzin pa'i dpal/ /zhes
gso ba rig pa'i bka' babs chos rje skyo ra lung pa dge slong don yod dpal bzang po ni/ 'khrungs yul dbyal gyi skyo ra lung du skyo 'od 'byung sogs dam po mang po'i gdung
rgyud du sku bltams gzhon nu nas rab tu byung / rig gnas spyi dang khyad par nang rig pa gsang sngags gsar rnying gi chos phal che ba deng sang lung pa'i ming 'gyur nas
thar ba zer ba dgon pa ste sngon dbya la lung par grags somkhyen/ lhag par dus 'khor dang sman dpyad kyi rig pa la sngon sbyangs kyi bag chags shin tu che bas dus kyi 'khor
lo'i skar rtsis kyi ri mo dang sman dpyad kyis 'phrin las mdzad/ de yang gso ba rig pa'i gzhung don gang gi don du gso bar bya ba'i lus kyi mtshan nyid dang / gang gso
bar byed pa'i nad kyi rgyu rkyen 'jag sgo'i brtag tshul dang / gang gis gso ba'i

gnyen po zas dpyad sman dpyad kyi bye brag dang / ji ltar gso ba'i thabs lag tu blang ba'i rim pa rnams la makas pa chen por gyur te/ thams cad mkhyen pa sku mnyel ba'i dus
su gsol sman gyi zhabs tog pa mdzad de snyim pa'i me tog las kyang / bla ma skyor lung ba sogs mkhas par sbyangs pa'i lha rje kun gyis gsol sman drangs/ zhes byung ngo /
yan lag brgyad pa sogs la 'grel bas ma bkral ba'i dka' gnad mang po yod pa la mchan bu zhus pas/ 'o na las sla bar gda'i/ sengge'i 'o ma de ro kha ba yin/ phag gi 'o ma
de kha ba de ltar ma yin par mngar ba yinazer ba lags mod gsungs/ nges par thams cad mkhyen par rang du 'dug /gzhan su la dris kyang bshad rgyu mi gda'/ rang res kyang mi
go bas de phyin chad mchan bu ma thebs pa thams cad drung rang du zhus nas btab pa yin gsung skad/ nag pa zla ba nam shar ba'i tshe chos rje'i yig cha'i steng nas sbyangs
te dus 'khor sku gsung thugs yongs rdzogs kyi dkyil 'khor zhal phye nas phyag len shin tu rgyas pa'i sgrub mchod zla ba phyed tsam re mdzad/ bdag 'jug longs ngos shes pa'i
grwa pa brgya nyi shu tsam re tshogs so gsungs/ dus 'khor sogs la yig cha

'ga' zhig kyang gsung rtsom mdzad/ de dag kyang legs po yang dag pa 'dug ces kun mkhyen bsod nams 'phel ba gsung ngo / /gzhan yang skar rtsis dang / 'bras rtsis sogs chos rje'i
gsung la zin bris btab pa dang / bstan bcos thor bu ba mang du mdzad do/ /rgyud 'dzin slob ma yang mkhas ba'i dbang po chos rje bsod nams don grub sogs mang du byon
no/ /gso ba rig pa'i bu chen gyi skabs so/ /tha snyad rig pa'i bka' babs kyi bu chen byon tshul bshad zin to/ gnyis pa nang mdo rgyud kyi don la bka' babs kyi bu chen byon
tshul la gnyis/ rgyu mtshan nyid kyi theg pa'i dang / 'bras bu sngags kyi'o/ /dang po la mdo sde/ 'dul ba/ mngon pa dang gsum ste/ gong gi gsol 'debs kyi 'phror/ ye nas
mdo sde shes pa'i don kun grub/ /rang rgyud dam chos dpal gyis 'dul mkhas bzang / /dngos slob yang rtse gsum la mngon pa rin chen ma rig las sangs rgyas/ /zhes bya ba yan
chad kyi bstan to/ /dang po/ ye nas mdo sde shes pa'i don kun grub/ /ces mdo sde'i sde snod la bka' babs kun mkhyen lung mang po can ye shes don grub pa ni/ 'khrungs yul
dbus dang nye ba'i sman ljongs jo bo chen po dpal ldan a ti sha'i bsti gnas snye thang zhes bya bar sngags rnying ma'i grub thob rim par byon pa'i gdung rgyud las sku 'khrungs/
gzhon nu nas

chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i drung du rab tu byung ste chab dang phyi dro'i kha zas zhal du 'khyer ba lta ci smos/ sku ma gshegs kyi bar la bzhes pa gdan gcig ma sdor dkar
kho na mdzad pas bod kyi btsun ma gcig par grags/ spyir shes bya mtha' dag la sbyangs/ khyad par sde snod gsum dang rgyud sde bzhi'i tshig don la mkhas pa chen por gyur/
bye brag mdo sde'i sde snod la bka' bab tshul bstan/ nang tshan chos rje'i gsung rab phar phyin lung gi snye ma dang bcas pa la bshad pa'i 'phrin las dang 'gro don nan
tan che bar grags/ ji skad du/ mdo sde rgyal ba'i yum gyi mdo rnams kun/ /rang gi bstan bcos ji bzhin 'chad pa khyod/ /gzigs nas rgyal ba'i rgyal tshab ma pham pa/ /dga'
ldan gnas su bde bar ngal gso mdzad/ /ces pa ltar ro/ /sku ma gshegs kyi bar thams cad du chos ma chags par gsungs/ dus der dbus gtsang gi lung chos pa thams cad dam pa 'di'i
slob mar ma gyur pa med gsung / sku las tshul khrims kyi dri bsung rdo rgyangs gang tsam gyi sa nas tshor yong ba dang / na bza'/ bzhugs gdan/ tha na zhabs phyags tshun
la tshul khrims kyi dri bzang po ldang ba dang / drung na chos nyan par 'khod pa sogs la yang de lta bu'i dri bsung gis khams dwangs shing rig pa gsal sing nge ba yong
zhes mkhas grub bsod nams 'phel ba'i gsung sgros las 'byung ngo / /phyag na rdo rje 'khor lo chen po'i sgrub thabs dang dkyil chog sogs gsung rtsom

yang mang ba yod ces grags/ dgung lo dgu bcu go gsum la ngo mtshar ba'i cho 'phrul dang bcas te sku gshegs so/ /mdo sde'i skabs so/ /|gnyis pa ni/ rang rgyud dam chos dpal
gyis 'dul mkhas bzang / /zhes 'dul ba'i sde snod la bka' babs mkhan chen lo tsA ba dang dharma shrI bha dra ni/ thog ma jo gdan tshogs grwa rgyun mdzad/ /phyis chos rje thams
cad mkhyen pas rjes su bzang nas zhwa lu'i dge bshes su gyur/ sgra ka lA pa dang / tsantra ba sogs legs sbyar la mkhas par sbyangs/ gzhan yang phyi mtshan nyid/ nang
gsang sngags/ khyad par gsang ba 'dus pa/ yo ga/ dus 'khor gsum la sbyangs nas mkhas pa chen por gyur/ nang tshan 'dul ba'i sde snod kyi gzhung mtha' dag la gzigs pa tsam
gyis don khong du chud pa'i mkhyen rab mchog tu yangs pa'i bka' babs tshul bstan no/ /chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i 'dul ba la gces pa'i gzhung brgyad ces pa 'di ltar/
'dul ba spyi'i rnam gzhan 'dul ba rin po che'i mdzes rgyan/ 'dul ba mdo'i rnam 'byed 'dul ba rgya mtsho'i snying po rab tu gsal byed/ las brgya rtsa gcig gi rnam bshad cho
ga'i gsal byed/ las cho ga dri med 'phreng ba zhar byung dang bcas pa/ dge slong ma'i rnam 'byed kyi T'ikka snying po don gsal/ ston pa sangs rgyas kyi rnam thar dad cing
dga' byed/ dge slong pha'i gleng 'bum/ ma'i

gleng 'bum ste brgyad yod do/ /de lta bu'i don la bslabs te/ de yang 'phags pa'i yul gyi slob dpon chen po yon tan 'od dang / shAkya 'od lta bu ste ji skad du/ 'dul ba 'bum
sde'i gzhung dang dgongs 'grel la/ shin tu sbyangs pas 'phyugs med mkhyen gyur nas/ /rgyal ba dgyes pa'i tshul khrims la gnas pa/ /khyod dang yon tan shAkya 'od mi nus/
/zhes pa ltar ro/ /jo gdan tshogs pa'am/ chos lung spos khang pa'i mkhan por bskos pas mkhan chen du grags/ tshogs pa'i mkhan po ma mdzad bar ri phug tu bzhugs lho sgo'i
slob dpon mdzad/ skabs shig sde srid phag mo grub pa'i gdung brgyud/ 'jam dbyangs gu shrI chen pos dbus su gdan drangs te chos mang po zhus/ chos grwa chen po rtses dang
sogs su tshogs chos gsungs/ /spyan snga grags pa byang chub kyis kyang chos zhus/ de nyid kyi rnam thar rje btsun btsong kha pas mdzad pa las kyang thams cad mkhyen pa bu
ston zhabs kyi thugs sras mkhan chen dharma shrI bha dra zhes 'byung ngo / /gzhan yang dbus gtsang gi blo gsal mang po dang / skal ldan dam tshig dang ldan pa mang po smin
grol la bkod/ phar phyin gyi zin bris/ mngon pa kun las btus kyi zin bris/ spyod 'jug gi zin bris/ dus 'khor gyi rgyud 'grel bshad pa dang / man ngag gnyis kyi zin bris/
gsang 'dus kyi man ngag gi zin bris sogs chos rje'i gsung rgyun reg gzigs su

bkod pa mang po dang / yi dam gyi sgrub skor sna tshogs dang sku 'bum mthong grol chen po'i dkar chag sogs kyang mdzad/ sgra'i 'gyur yang 'ga' mdzad/ sku khams bzang ring la
ri phug tu phyi rten sku 'bum sogs bzhengs/ de yang ngo mtshar zhing byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar ba byung / dngos kyi gdul bya rdzogs nas dgung lo lnga bcu nga dgu bzhes
pa'i dus su/ gdan sa chen po zhwa lu ri phug tu da lta dharma shrer grags pa'i mchod rten yin/sku gshegs/ 'dul ba'i bu chen gyi skabs so/ /gsum pa ni/ mngon pa rin chen
ma rig las sangs rgyas/ /zhes mngon pa'i sde snod kyi bka' babs/ dka' bzhi pa rin chen sangs rgyas mgon dpal bzang po ni/ 'khrungs yul zhwa lu pa/ de yang lo chen ratna
bha dras/ zhwa lu gser bkang zhes bya'i grong khyer du/ /lung rtogs yon tanamadzod 'dzin 'gos kyi rigs/ /sku zhang blon po rin chen seng ge de'i/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ 'gos
lo tsA ba khug pa lhas btsas sogs dam pa mang po 'khrungs pa'i gdung brgyud dpon rin chen sengge'i sras su sku bltams/ gzhon nu nas chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i drung
du rab tu byung / phyis de nyid las bsnyen rdzogs kyang mdzad/ spyir mdo dang rgyud sde'i gzhung lugs mtha' dag la sbyangs/ khyad par mngon pa'i sde snod la sngon goms
kyi mthu brtasrtas/ mngon

pa kun las btus/ chos rje'i TTikka nyi ma'i 'od zer dang / rten 'brel gyi rnam gzhug lung kun las btus pa sogs rgyab chos dang bcas pa la bshad pa'i 'phrin las dang 'gro phan
nan tar che/ mdor na ji skad du/ rgya mtsho lta bu mngon pa'i chos sde rnams/ /tshig don thugs su byon nas ston mdzad khyod/ /thogs med zhabs dang dbyig gnyen gang yin
zhes/ /blo gsal phal cher the tshom gnas su gyur/ /ces pa ltar ro/ /chos gsung ba'i dus su dge bshes su la'ang dgag pa mi mdzad/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston chen
pos gsung sgros rang la gtso bor mdzad/ /drung du dka' gnad kyi dri ba ci zhus kyang rin po che'i zhal nas 'di gsung zer ba tsam ka yong ba cig yod ces mkhas grub rin po
che bsod nams 'phel gsung ngo / /lo tsA ba skyabs mchog dpal bzang sogs slob ma mkhas pa mang po yang byon 'dug cing / gzhan yang spyan snga blo gros rgyal mtshan gyis
mdzad pa'i thog ma'i blo sbyong du/ kun mkhyen bu'i gsung lung du drangs pa la mchan bu 'di snyan tshar chos 'khong sgang gi dgon pa btabbtab pa'i yig chung na/ slob ma dka'
bzhi 'dzin pa rkang gcig /gnas brtan sprul par grags pa dka' bzhi dgon btab/ bstan pa la phan pa mtha' yas zhes bya ba 'dug pa yang / dka' bzi pa 'di ba yin nam dpyad
par bya ba'i gnas so/ /mngon pa'i bu chen

gyi skabs so/ | gnyis pa 'bras bu gsang sngags kyi bu chen byon tshul la lnga/ gar dbyangs thig gsum la bka' babs kyi bu chen byon tshul/ bya spyod rnal 'byor rgyud gsum la
bka' bab kyi bu chen byon tshul/ gsang 'dus la bka' bab kyi bu chen byon tshul/ dus la bka' bab kyi bu chen byon tshul/ nyams rtogs la bka' bab kyi bu chen byon tshul/ /de
yang gong gi tshig rkang gnyis pa las blangs te/ dbang po rnam pos gar thig dbyangs la byang / /rgyud gsum gzhon nu nas mkhas bsod nams 'bar/ /dngos slob yang rtse gsum
la tshul ldan khrims kyi snying por 'dus pa mkhas/ /phyi nang gzhan gsum chos kyi dbang kun 'dzin/ /nam mkha'i mtha' mnyam man ngag mchog tu grub/ /dngos slob yang rtse
gsum la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes so/ /dang po ni/ dbang po rnon pos gar thig dbyangs la byang / /zhes rje dbang rnon rin po che rgyal ba mchog grub dpal bzang po ni/ spyir
mtshan nyid dang sngags chog phal cher mi mkhyen pa bya ba med/ /khyad par sngags la bag chags sku gzhon nu nas che bar grags/ nang tshan rnal 'byor rgyud la 'gran zla dben
pa'i mkhas pa'i phul du gyur/ gsung tshangs ba'i dbyangs dang 'dra ba yod/ byang sgo'i slob dpon du bskos/snying grwa tshang /rgyud sde bzhi'i phyag

len gyi gnad spyi dang bye brag dus 'khor/ yo ga gnyis kyi gar dbyangs thig gsum gyis mtshon pa ni tha na rdor dril 'dzin tshul tshun phyag len ma 'dres pa khungs dang 'brel
ba shin tu mkhas par mkhyen pas chos rje yang mnyes te/ 'o gsang sngags kyi rdo rje slob dpon byed pa la dang po nas gdan mthon pa la tsong nga bsdad pa'i mi che che la
bzos pa de la yong ba min/ tha na ras lde dang lha bshos bzheng ba nas bslabs pas/ bla ma mkhas pa'i mchod g.yog byas pa la lag len dang 'brel ba yong ba yin/ lar yang sngags
pa bshad pa lag len/ sgom don bskyed rdzogs rnams dang / 'phrin las rnam bzhi sgrub pa'i cha lag phra mo tshun chad yod pa/ dper na phyug po'i sman rkyal 'dra ba gcig
dgos/ gzhan du na a ka ru dang ga bur yod pas/ tig ta dang hong len gyi tshab mi yong / sna tshang ba gang la gang dgos ma thogs pa yod pa cig dgos pas byung gda'i/ da
grong chog dang tshe 'di'i lag char ma song ba cig cis kyang 'tshal lo gsung ngo / /dus de skabs yo ga ba rnams kyi gtsug gi nor bur bzhugs nas bstan 'gro'i don mdzad/ chos
rje'i pa'i 'khrid gnyer ba yang lo bdun gyi bar mdzad/ de yang nyid kyis gsung nas/ sa yi steng na 'gra zla ma mchis shing / /ngur smrig 'dzin pa'i nang nas mchog tu
gyur/ /dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rin chen grub/ /rdo rje 'chang dngos de yi zhabs

pad ni/ /rgyal ba mchog grub zhes bya'i dge slong gis/ /lo bdun 'phrin las 'khrid gnyer byas nas su/ /zhes sogs gsungs so/ /bla ma dang yi dam gyi lhas gsang mtshan mi bskyod
rdo rje zhes btags/ sku che ba'i yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab/ khyad par bde mchog 'khor lo'i grub thob tu grags so/ gar dbyangs thig gsum la mkhas pa'i skabs so/ /gnyis
pa ni/ rgyud gsum gzhon nu nas mkhas bsod nams 'bar/ /zhes mkhas grub khyung po las pa gzhon nu bsod nams ni/ 'khrungs sa tshong dus kyi khyung po lhas bya bar/ bla ma khyung
po pa'i gdung brgyud du 'khrungs pas mtshan yang de ltar grags zer ba snang mod/ gang ltar yang bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i mkhas grub cig byon 'dug /spyir rgyud sde mtha'
dag la mkhas/ mtshan nyid kyi bka' pod bzhi la yang sbyangs/ khyad par bya rgyud/ spyod rgyud/ rnal 'byor rgyud gsum la bka' babs che ba'i bu chen du grags/ nang tshan
rnal 'byor rgyud la mkhas pa'i tshad du phyin/ nub sgo'i slob dpon du yang bskos/ shar sgo'i slob dpon ni thugs sras lo tsA bas mdzad zer/ khyung lhas pas dang po zhwa
lu'i zur 'chad mdzad cing ban brag nag ces bya ba'i dgon pa'i bla ma yang thogs shig da lta grang chen pa/ mdzad/ sku tshe'i mjug la ri phug gi byang ngos su chos phug dgon
pa

gsar du btab/ phyi rten sku 'bum gcig bzhengs/ der bzhugs nas mkhas mang brgya phrag la chos 'khor bskor/ 'gro phan shin tu che bar grags/ slob ma'i gtso bo yang / sa skya
gdung brgyud chu mig bdag po bzhi thog pa kun dga' bkra shis / chos rje shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan sogs sa ngor phyogs su chos brgyud spel ba dang / mkhas grub nor bzang
rin chen dang sngags 'chang don 'grub legs pa sogs zha lu rang gi slob brgyud 'dzin pa du ma dang / rje btsun btsong kha pa chen po sogs byung ste/ spyir gyis grub mtha'
ris med la mkhas grub 'di nyid kyi bka' drin chen pos khyab pa byung ngo / /khyad par rje btsun btsong kha pa chen pos chos gsan tshul sogs de nyid kyi rnam thar na gsal
bas bla ma'i gtso bor gyur te/ mdor na mnyam med ri bo dga' ldan pa'i 'phrin las kyi rgya mtsho'i mtha' khyab pa'ang / rje 'di'i rnam thar gyi che ba bla na med pa'o/ /gsung
rtsom phyis su bzhugs pa mthong ba la 'jam dpal gsang ldan gyi dkyil chog dang rdo rje 'byung ba'i rnam bshad sogs yod 'dug chos rje'i rnam thar yon tan rin po che'i
lhun po yang mdzad 'dug/gzhan ji tsam yod ma nges so/ /chos phug dgon pa na phyi rten dang khyung lhas pa'i sgrub chu yin zer ba'i chu mig sogs da lta'ang yod do/ /bya
spyod rnal 'byor rgyud gsum la mkhas pa'i skabs so/ /gsum pa ni/ tshul ldan khrims kyis snying por 'dus pa mkhas/ /zhes grub chen tshul khrims snying po ni/ rnam thar yod
pa khungs chod kyang ma rnyed/

'khrungs yul ba ri ba yin/ spyir mdo sngags kyis bsdus pa'i chos dang / khyad par rgyud phyi ma las kyang gang zhig rab gsang 'dus pa'i rgyud 'di nyan pa dang / 'don par byed
pa dang ni sems par byed pa dang / mchod pa byed pa dang ni 'dri 'am 'drir 'jug pa/ byang chub rdo rje 'drar lta de la rtag phyag 'tshal/ zhes rgyud kyi phyogs gcig yan
chad 'dzin pa thams cad rdo rje 'chang dang 'dra ba'i phyag bya'i yul du gsungs shing / gzhan yang 'jam dpal zhal lung las/ 'di'i don rnam par 'pho byed pa/ /gang gi dus
su gnas pa der / /sangs rgyas bstan pa rin chen yang / /gnas par rab tu bshad pa yin/ zhes dang / sgron gsal las/ thub pa chen pos chos phung po/ /brgyad khri bzhi stong
gsungs pa ni/ /dpal ldan 'dus 'di snod yin te/ /de bas de ni rgyud kyi rtse/ /zhes sogs rgya cher bsngags pa rgyal ba'i gsung rab kyi snying po rgyud sde thams cad kyi
rtse mo dang / mdo sde kun gyi za ma tog tu gyur ba/ mtha' drug tshul bzhi'i rgyas btab nas mkhas grub phal gyis rtogs dka' ba las/ sangs rgyas gnyis pa nA ga dzu na'i zhabs
kyis legs par bkral ba/ kun mkhyen chos kyi rgyal po bu ston lo tsA ba'i bzhed srol gyi mthar thug dpal gsang ba 'dusad pa 'phags skor gyi dbang bshad man nang gi bka'
thams cad chos rje de nyid las bum pa gang byor thob pas mkhas pa chen por gyur/ zab lam

rim pa lnga'i don bsgoms pas zung 'jug gi rtogs pa mthar phyin nas grub pa kun gyi gtsug rgyan bla na med par gyur to/ /'dus pa la mkhas pa'i skabs so/ /bzhi pa ni/ phyi nang
gzhan gsum chos kyi dpal kun 'dzin/ /zhes gong gsum bde chen pa rigs ldan chen po 'jam dbyangs chos kyi dpal ba ni/ 'khrungs yul nyang stod skya la chad kar zhes bya ba/
yab jo btsun chos bzang dang / yum ma gcig dge bsnyen brtson 'grus dpal bya ba gnyis kyi sras su me pho 'brug gi lo la 'khrungs/ chung ngu'i dus nas dgyes rdor bslab ma
dgos par rtol shes su gyur/ lo dgu bzhes pa'i dus su lcog ro chos sder slob dpon dge 'byung zhes pa la klog slob par byon pas/ yul phyogs pa thams cad dar 'phyar byed pa
dang thug /rten 'brel legs dgongs pa byung / slob dpon gyis sbyor klog bslabs pa tsam gyis klog phul du phyin pa zla ba gcig la mkhyen cing / 'dul ba lung la klog dar mdzad
pas gleng 'bum phal cher thugs la chud nas srod tho rangs zla bo rnams la bshad pas thams cad mos par gyur to/ /slob dpon sher brtson pa la yi ge bslabs pas zla ba gcig
la mkhyen par gyur/ dgung lo bcu la mkhan po gzhon nu brtson 'grus dang / las kyi slob dpon byang chub bzang po gnyis las rab tu byung / sdom rgyun de yang zhwa lu mkhan
po btsun shes rab 'byung gnas kyis rgya gar du bhA ya la blangs pa'i brgyud pa shin tu

nye ba yin skad/ dgung lo bcu gcig nas bcu gsum gyi bar la slob dpon dge 'byung ba'i drung du 'dul ba'i sde snod bslabs/ dgung lo bcu bzhi nas bcu dgu'i bar bshad nyan mdzad/
nyi shu la dpal zhwa lu'i chos grwa chen por mtshan nyid kyi slob gnyer mdzad par phebs/ chos rje bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa de nyid sgrol sa dmar du mchod gzhi la byon
pa dang dus mtshungs te der phebs pa dang chos dung 'bud pa dus mnyam du byung bas rten 'brel 'grig /mkhas pa skyabs mchog dpal gyis slob chung mdzad nas tshad ma rnam
nges rtsa 'grel tshig don rab gsal dang bcas pa bslab/ de nas sa skyar byon nas sde snod 'dzin pa kun rgyal ba la rnam 'grel tshar gcig gsan/ skabs shig bla ma chos mgon
dpal la sbyor drug zhus nas bsgom pas rtags rgyud nas bshad pa bzhin rdzogs pa shar/ dus 'khor/ spyan ras gzigs sogs kyis zhal bstan/ re ma tis sros snying gi sngags phul/
tshe ring ba'i rten 'brel byas gsung / phyag rdor 'khor chen gyi bsnyen mtshams lo drug mdzad/ sngags mi 'dra ba gnyis yod pa de/ gong ma bye ba gcig dang / phyi ma 'bum
phrag nyi shu rtsa gcig bzlas pa yin gsungs/ bskyed rim la mnga' brnyes shing nus mthu bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung ngo / /de nas dus 'khor bslab par bzhed nas gdan sa
chen po ri phug chos kyi pho brang du phebs/ kun

mkhyen rin po che dus 'khor chos 'byung gi skabs kyi dam pa'i chos la bshad nyan byed tshul gsung ba dang mnyam du chos rar phebs pas rten 'brel legs dgongs/ de nas bzungs
te rgyud kyi bshad pa tshar bcu bdun gsan par mdzad/ de'i tshe da res chos 'go rang la slebs pa bya snyam nas byon kyang dpal gyi bla ma slob ma ste/ bshad pas don grub la
phyag 'tshal/ zhes gsung ba'i skabs rang la chos rar phebs kyin yod skad do/ /bshad pa sad 'dzugs pa'i nub mo mnal lam du ka pA la nang mchod kyis gang ba re gsol ba nges
pa can du yong gsungs/ de la sogs te ngo mtshar ba'i ltas kyang du ma byung / dus 'khor gyi dbang bka'/ bshad bka'ka/ man ngag gi bka' sogs mdor na dus 'khor gyi skor
ma lus pa bum pa gang byo'i tshul du gsan nas dus kyi 'khor lo'i phyi nang gzhan gsum la mkhas pa chen por gyur/ lugs 'di nyid la bka' babs kyi bu chen du grags so/ /gzhan
yang bla ma chos kyi brtson 'grus/ bla ma rin rdor ba/ 'jag chen byams pa dpal sogs la'ang chos gsan/ dus phyis chos rje 'jam rin pa'i drung du bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/ de
nas dben pa'i gnas khyad par can dpal 'og min bde chen du bzhugs nas dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa/ mdzub 'khrid/ dbang bka'/ man ngag gi bka' sogs chos 'khor
rgya chen po bskor/ rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa sngon

ma mdzad dus mnal lam du sham bha la'i rigs ldan gyi rgyal bo phebs nas phyag sbrel/ 'gro don rgya chen po yong ba yod pas bshad nyan la brtson par mdzod gsung ba dang / lho
phyogs dpal ldan 'bras spungs kyi mchod rten la 'dzegs nas thig tshad blangs pa dang / sum cu rtsa gsum du phebs nas lha'i rnga bo che brdungs pa sogs rmis so/ /dgung lo
don bzhir phebs dus dpal zhwa lu'i grwa pa 'ga' byung ba la rgyud kyi bka' chos tshugs pas zhabs la snyung gzhi drag po cig byung nas slob ma rnams kyis chos mtshams mdzad
na zhus pas chos ma chag par byed dgos gsungs te/ khyogs la btegs nas kyang chos gsung pa mdzad/ de'i tshe tho rangs dbu sngas su chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston
rin po che phebs nas nad 'dis mi skyon/ der ma zad lo 'ga' zung gi bar du chos 'phel ba yong zhing / khyod rang dus 'khor dngos yin par 'dug ces dbugs dbyung mdzad/ gzhan
yang mi ma yin gyi don mdzad cing chos gsungs pa'i lo rgyus 'di ltar/ mdol chung na srul rdo ra zer ba'i bud med cig yod pa des lcog rer phyin nas log yong pa'i lam durta
pa gcig dang 'phrad mos khyod ga nas byon pa lags byas pas de na re/ nga skyin mkhar 'jugs kyi dbu bdud bya ba yin/ bde chen na rin po che chos kyi dpal brgyud gsung ba
la nyan du 'gri gin yod pa yin/

khyod rang nga la phyi mig ma lta bar rgyug /ri sna ya gi na dngos grub cig yod zer nas song / mos phyi mig bltas pas rgyab stong par 'dug lo/ /ri snar slebs pa dang snum grod
pa gang rnyed do/ /de la sogs te lo rgyas mang ste 'dir ma spros so/ /skabs shig sangs rgyas 'od dpag med kyi sku chen po zhig nam mkha' nas byon nas/ rigs kyi bu khyod
'jig rten gyi khams 'di la skyo na bal po phyogs su skyes/ de nas sangs rgyas snang ba mtha' yas kyi drung du mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ro gsungs/ dngos
kyi gdul bya rdzogs nas me pho byi ba'i lo/ /rgyal gyi zla ba'i yar ngo nas sku snyung tshul cung zad bzhes te/ de nas zla ba phyi mdakar rtsis pa'i lo ma 'phos sing
/ cho 'phrul chen po rta'i zla ba 'jig rten grags pa'i dbang du byas na me mo glang gi lo/ /hor zla dang po'i tshes gsum gyi nub mo dben gnas dam pa 'og min bde chen du ngo
mtshar ba'i ltas dang bcas te sku gshegs/ rgyud 'dzin gyi gtso bo yang zhwa lu na mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs grags rgyal/ kun mkhyen bsod nams 'phel sogs du ma/ gzhan yang
lo chen skyabs mchog dpal bzang / shangs pa kun mkhyen sher dpal/ rje nyid kyi gdan sa pa nyang stod pa kun bzang rin chen sogs mang du byung ngo / /rje rin po che blo
bzang grags pa'i dpal gyis kyang dus 'khor gyi dbang bshad kyi bka' phal mo che gsan nas 'phrin las nam mkha'i ra ba las 'das so/ /dus 'khor la mkhas pa'i saskabs so/

lnga pa ni/ nam mkha'i mtha' mnyam man ngag mchog tu grub/ /ces nang don man ngag la bka' babs grub pa'i dbang phyug nam mkha'i mtshan can ni/ yab sku zhang chen po grags pa
rgyal mtshan gyi sku'i gcung po lce rdo rje'i dbang phyug gi sras su gyur te/ sku gzon nu'i dus nas snga ma'i skye ba rnams thugs kyis dran zhing tha lam gyi spyod pa gtan
mi mdzad/ klog dang yi ge sogs kyang brda bstan pa tsam gyis mkhyen cher skyes nas chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa las dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa bzhes/ byang chub mchog tu
thugs bskyed pa dang rig pa 'dzin pa sngags kyi sdom pa'ang nos/ bla ma dang yi dam gyi lhas gsang mtshan la lI ta badzra ste'o la ba'i rdo rje zhes btags so/ /rgyu 'bras
kyi theg pa'i chos la thos bsam mang du mdzad/ de nas rang gi mched zla sku zhang kun dga' don grub kyi rgyal srid 'dzin grogs gyis zer ba zhus kyang ma gnang zhing rab
tu 'byung ba la thugs shin tu rings yang yab yum gyi bka' ma grol bar brten re zhig khyim du bzhugs te btsun mo khab tu bzhes nas rigs kyi sras bskrun pa dang rgyal srid
chos bzhin du skyong ba sogs kyang sngon bdag gi ston pa'i mdzad pa dang rjes su mthun pa bskyangs te zhang bdun ni 'di dag gi dus na yang thos bsam sgom gsum gyis dus 'da'
bar kho na mdzad/ khyad par chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i drung du dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i sbyor ba

yan lag drug zhusanas bsgoms par 'akridazhu ba drug cu rtsa lnga tshogs pa'i khrod du rje nyid las nyams rtogs bzang ba sung yang ma byung bas chos rje yang shin tu thugs dgyes
so/ /gzhan yang snga phyir thugs sras lo tsA ba/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ chos rje rgyal sras dgu dngul chu pa sogs bla ma mang du bsten/ de ltar
sngags 'chang rdo rje 'dzin pa chen por gyur mod kyi bstan pa'i rtsa ba dge slong gi rten gyis 'dzin dgos par gzigs te slar dgung lo sum cu so gnyis pa la chos rje thams
cad mkhyen pa'i rgyal tshab thugs sras lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal gyis mkhan po mdzad nas rab tu byung zhing bsnyen par rdzogs/ mtshan slob dpon rin chen nam mkha'
mchog grub ces bya ba yang de nas grags/ thugs sras rje zhi bar gshegs nas gdan sa'i 'os la rje nyid dang mkhan chen mangga'i mtshan can/ chos rje grags pa rgyal mtshan
te gsum byung yang bum pa bkrugs pas thams cad mkhyen pa grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi mtshan thog mar thon nas gzhan gnyis ma 'thon/ rwa tsa nub kyi gnas gsar dudage 'phel chos
rdzong gi dgon pa btab nas yo ga rdo rje dbyings kyi sgrub mchod 'dzugs pa sogs bstan pa'i bya ba rgya cher mdzad/ skabs shig lha mo sha ma Na'i sgo nas sku tshe phyi
ma'i skye ba brtag pa mdzad pas mnal lam du rgyal ba byams pa mgon po byon nas phyag gnyis kyis bum pa bzung bas spyi bo nas dbang bskur/ ma 'ongs pa'i zhig khams

dang gdul bya lung bstan/ gzhan yang spyan ras gzigs/ 'jam dbyangs dkar po/ rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa/ thub pa'i dbang po/ tshe dpag med/ gshed dmar 'jigs byed sogs thugs dam gyi
lha tshogs mang po'i zhal gzigs/ 'gro ba nad gdon gyis gtses pa mang po la srung skud re tsam/ ljags chab re gnang ba'am/ gsang chab sogs nas 'thungs pas kyang nad gdon
thams cad lhag med du zhi zhing grol 'gro ba dang / rdo rje'i chos srung rnams bka' las mi 'da' ba bran du 'khol nus pa dang / gzhan yang lkog gyur gyi gnas mkhyen pa dang
/ sku lus las me 'bar ba dang / gzhan snang zil gyis non pa sogs/ mngon shes grub rtags bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan zhing zung 'jug gi rtogs pa sku tshe 'di nyid
la brnyes par mdzad pa de dag ni rnam par thar pa'i snying po tsam btus pa yin no/ rgyud 'dzin gyi gtso bo mkhas ba'i dbang po tsandra shrI ratna/ rdo rje 'dzin pa rin chan
dpal grub/ mkhas grub mgon po rgyal mtshan sogs mtha' yas so/ /man ngag la mkhas pa'i skabs so/ /de ltar phyi tha snyad rig pa la bka' babs kyi bu chen bzhin/ nang rig
pa mdo la gsum dang / sngags la lnga ste kun dril pas thugs sras bu chen bcu gnyis byon pa'o/ /gnyis pa 'khor dag pa rnam brgyud byon tshul la gsum ste/ mchod g.yog dge
bshes

gnyis byon tshul/ dge slong chen po bzhi byon tshul/ sku'i rim gro pa gnyis byon tshul lo/ /de yang gsol 'debs las/ nyer gnas bshes gnyen 'jam dbyangs tshe dbang zung / /skyabs
mchog bsod nams grub don grub dpal/ /bde rgyal mchod g.yog gtso bo gnas brtan bzhi/ /dam pa'i zhabs 'bring drug la gsol ba 'debs/ /gong gsal bzhi nas dge slong mig gcig
pu/ /dpe gnyer gzigams g.yog gtor bshom bsod nams grub/ /dam pa'i cos kyi dung 'bud rin chen skyabs/ /rim gror brtson mdzad gnyis la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes pas don bstan
pa'o/ /dang po ni/ nyer gnas bshes gnyen 'jam dbyangs tshe dbang zu / /zhes pa ste/ mchod g.yog pa dge ba'i bshes gnyen dus 'khor ba 'jam dbyangs dkar po ni/ 'phags pa'i
gnas brtan chen po nags na gnas kyi sprul pa yin par grags shing / skutshe 'dir mdo sngags yongs rdzogs kyi dge bshes chen por gyur/ sdor dkar gdan gcig ma'i brtul zhugs
'dzin/ skabs shig khong la bsam yas rgyal pos bar gcod brtsams te snar thang mkhan chen pa dang / sa skya'i gnas drug mkhan chen pa/ /slob dpon 'jam dkar ba khyed gsum
pa'i dgon pa byang 'jag thang gi mkhan slob la gdan 'dren zhu ru yong pa yin pas 'byon dgos zer nas rgyal po kho rang dngos su byung ba la/ der jo bo rdo rje ri phug mas
bar byas nas sngon la sa skya dang snar thang

bskor shog /mar lam nged kyis khong sprod pa'i khag khur byed zer nas brdzangs/ slob dpon 'jam dkar ba khyod rang 'gro 'dod na ni de ka yin mod/ mi 'dod na thugs sras lo tsA
ba la gzungs grwa lnga'i dbang bskur zhig zhus nas srung ba zhig thogs zer/ de dus thugs sras pa dbang bskur ba mi mdzad pas/ khong gis dbang gnang bar zhus pas zhal phyis
ma bzhes/ der dus nas nga la rgyu mtshan 'di 'dra 'di tshul byung zhus pas/ da 'o na los byed gsungs nas gzungs grwa lnga'i dbang bskur mdzad/ 'khor lo btags pas/ lha
'dre kho yongs kyang slob dpon 'jam dkar ba ma mthong / slob dpon pas lha 'dre kho mthong yang bar chad kyis ma tshugs so/ /snar thang mkhan chen dang / gnas drug mkhan
chen pa gnyis ni de nas zla ba gnyis tsam nas gshegs 'dug zer/ de chos rje thams cad mkhyen pas gsan te/ thugs sras lo tsA ba la nyid kyis dbang bskur ba yin nam gsungs/
rgyu mtshan rnams zhib par zhus pas/ a ka kha khong dge bshes khyad 'phags yin pas de 'dra byung na mi byed pa'i thabs yang mi 'dug /gzhan nged yod ring la dbang de ma byas
na legs pa yod te tshar gsung ngo / /chos rje nyid kyis kyang chos shes la nyams su myong ba rgyal sras thogs med 'di yin ces bsngags pa mdzad pas/ khong gis rjes su dngul
chu rgyal sras rin po che'i zhabs la'ang gtugs te/

phyis de nyid kyi slob ma'i gtso bo rgya 'jam dpal gsum gyi nang mtshan gcig tu yang gyur to/ /gnyis pa dge ba'i bshes gnyen yo ga ba rin chen tshe dbang ni/ spyir mdo rgyud
thams cad dang nang tshul rnal 'byor rgyud kyi skor la mkhas pa chen por grags/ chos rje'i phyag bzhes rnams la reg gzigs dang / khyad par bla ma bsod nams 'od zer dang
/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen nam mkha' dri med gnyis kyis bskul nas rdo rje 'byung ba'i lag len rin chen bsam 'phel gyi dka' 'grel legs bshad rmad byung ba sogs yo ga la yig cha
yang mang du mdzad ces grags so/ /mchod g.yog pa gnyis kyi skabs so/ /gnyis pa ni/ skyabs mchog bsod nams grub pa don grub dpal/ bde rgyal mchod g.yog gtso bo gnas brtan
bzhi/ /zhes byung bas dge slong chen po bzhi ni/ mkhas pa skyabs mchog dpal/ bla ma dge slong bsod nams grub/ slob dpon don grub dpal/ slob dpon bde rgyal lo/ /de rnams
chos rje'i drung du bsnyen rdzogs pa su byung yang dad dge mdzad/ de yang chos rje nyid kyi las chog dri ma med pa'i 'phreng ba mgo mchod brjod nas/ mjug rdzogs pa kun
tshang rgyas pa ser bzhag 'bring / ser chos gnyis bzhag bsdus pa ste/ blo nus dus skabs dang sbyar nas/ rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum nyams su blang / zhes bya ba'i don skabs su
gang 'brel sna tshogs mdzad pas de rnams blo la med na dge slong byas nas las chog re yang mi shes zhes bka' bkyon

par mdzad pas/ kha skong gi dge 'dun nyi shu rtsa grangs re tsam tshogs 'ong ste/ las chog blo la med pa la der 'du mkhan mi 'od gsung skad/ de ltar na gong gi dge slong bzhi
ni sbyangs pa'i yon tan bcu gnyis kyis mdzes shing / btsun pa brtan pa'i yon tan/ mkhas shing phan thogs pa'i yon tan te brtan mkhas kyi yon tan gnyis dang ldan pa'i dge
ba'i bshes gnyen kho na'o/ /gnas brtan bzhi'i skabs so/ gsum pa ni/ gong gsal bzhi las dge slong mig gcig pu/ /dpe gnyer gzims g.yog gtor bshoms bsod nams grub/ /ces 'byung
bas/ de yang gong gi dge slong bzhi'i nang tshan bla ma dge slong bsod nams grub 'di ni/ sku tshe mang po'i gong nas kun mkhyen yab sras gnyis kyis rjes su bzungs/
dus 'dir sku zhang pa'i nang blon dpon skya chen po'i sras su 'khrungs/ sku gzhon nu nas chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i nye gnas kyi tha chung gtor gsos 'bul ba/ tha na chab
sgron pa sogs nas phyis rim gyis phyag dpe'i do dam/ gzims g.yog /gtor bshom sogs tshad ma mdzad/ chos rje'i drung nas kyang rab tu byung ba dang bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i
bar thams cad mdzad/ rjes su thugs sras lo tsA ba la gdan sa gtad pa'i gong du ja gcig gsol ba'i grwar yab sras gnyis kyi 'phros la/ bsod nams grub khyed kyang gleng mo
'di rnams nyan gyin ja drangs pas rgyu mtshan chen po yod pa

yin / 'o da ni nged kyi na tshod kyang yol/ thos bsam sgom gsum gyis bstan pa dang / 'brel ba dngos su yod pa rnams kyi don yang byas zin/ 'ga' zhig gi don byed pa dang bsgom
par bya ba'i don mngon du byu zhing / brgyud nas gdul bya dang bstan pa 'dzin pa la nyid kyis gos 'dir sdod la 'gro ba'i don gyis shig /'di'i rgyu mtshan dge sdings su'ang
'di lta bu zhig byas nas/ sems can gyi don gcig nas gcig tu brgyud de bya rgyu yin na'ang / rten 'brel phra mo zhig 'phyugs par 'dug pa'i rgyu mtshan go mchis/ de'i
rgyu mtshan rnams bsod nams grub la rting du gleng mo yong pa yin no ang gsungs/ de ltar nang du yab sras gnyis bka' gros de bzhin mdzad/ gzhan snang du snyim pa'i me tog
las 'byung ba ltar/ gdan sa'i 'os 'thusthuspa sogs mdzad do/ /gdan sa gtad grub nas re zhig nas bla ma dge slong bsod nams grub kyis chos rje'i zhabs la byug pa zhu yin
yod tsa na/ 'o cag gi gdan sa bskos pa la mi rnams ci zer ba gda' gsung / khong dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po thams cad ni 'di kha rang yin shin tu lags gsung ba gda' lags/
nang so yon bdag pa rnams dang mi mang byings tsho/ chos rje dus gsum mkhyen pa yin pa la/ gdan sa'i cha 'di ma dgongs pa yin pa 'dra zer gyin gda' lags zhus pas/ dus ngan
snyigs ma'i sems can rang ngos nas gang zag gi ched 'dzin pa 'di kha'o rgyal bar gda'/ khyod rang la yang

skye ba snga ma'i dge sbyor la brten pa'i 'di pas drag pa gcig re ba yin na'ang gsal po mi 'dug /sngon gyi dus su bla ma'i dkor zhig la 'bags pa'i skyon byung tshod du gda'/
khong la khyod kyang zhabs tog che ba gcig yin/ khyod rang lo gcig gnyis khong gi nye gnas gyis shig /de nas mi nus na nged kyi zla la bsdang bas chog ces gsungs nas bla
ma dge slong bsod nams grub thugs sras lo tsA ba'i ne gnas mdzad dgos pa byung ngo / /de nas bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis chos rje yab sras 'bras yul skyed
mo'i tshal du gdan drangs nas/ dpon slob sum cu tsam byon pas/ kyi 'phrad na mar phebs pa'i tshe/ /khal ma dang dge 'dun byings la khyed rang rnams sngon la song / nged
gdan sa ba dang bsod nams grub rnams rting la yong ngo gsung nas rjes la byon pa'i dus su/ chos rje'i gsung nas/ khyed dpon slob gnyis kyis sa phyogs 'di'i yar mar rnams
la 'grim 'grul ji snyed cig byas pa yin te dran no gsung / thugs sras pas thar thor dran zhus/ bla ma dge slong bsod nams grub kyis ci yang ma zhus pas/ 'di la 'di bas drag
pa'i re ba yod pa yin te gsung yab sras gnyis kar bzhad mo mdzad kyin 'dug /dmu mda'i thang dkyil na pha bong gcig gi steng du sku mnyel gsos nas bzhugs/ thugs sras rjes
'khar bsil gyi yu bas pha bong de'i 'og grus nas/ dung phreng rul

'phro gnyis/ ma na hu ma rul ba gcig /zangs kyi lcug phran sor gnyis tsam pa zhig 'dug pa rnyed nas/ de rnams phyag tu bzung nas bla ma dge slong bar 'di dag ngo shes par gda'
ye gsungs pas mi shes/ nga'i yin nam snyam pa byed pa gcig byung zer/ thugs sras rje'i zhal nas/ 'di 'dra la brten nas sngar gyi nyams sad pa 'dra ba yong ba yin te zhus
pas/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pas de mi yong ba'i rten 'brel dum tsam phyugs tshod gda'/ de las rten sgam gyi ga'u de gnad che ba yin te/ da nyid kyi khong la de'i rgyu
mtshan shod cig gsungs te bzhengs nas byon/ de nas thugs sras rjes bla ma dge slong bsod nams grub la 'o skol gnyis kyis sham 'bar du stod phyogs nas yong ba'i dge bshes
rang rab la dus 'khor gyi bshad pa dang / rdo rje 'phreng ba'i dbang byed pa la zla ba 'ga' bsdad/ de nas e dmar du yong ba'i lam du dmu ba'i yon bdag mang pos la khar
bsgugs/ ma da na'i tshogs 'khor mang po byung bas nyid bzi/ khal ma dang grogs rnams sngon la thegs nas rkang thang gcig dang rang re gnyis rjes la yong pas/ nyid rta khar
ma chags par nged kyis pha bong 'di'i rtsar babs pas yun ring po zhig gnyid du song / de'i dus nyid kyi lag pa la thod 'phreng skor gcig gi dkyil na dung gcig btsud/
mdud 'dzin la man hu dang dung cig byas/ zangs kyi 'jur mig 'di phreng ba la brgyus nas grangs 'dzin byas pa gcig 'dug pa ngas 'dir sbas bzhag

pa yin/ gzhan thod 'phreng rnams ni rul nas shul yang mi gda' de dran ne gsungs pas ci yang ma dran ka zhus/ der chos rje'i zhal nas/ rgyu 'grub de tsam gyi bag chags bzhag
nas de kha ma legs pa yin no gsung / de nas 'bras yul du dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis dus 'khor zhor la gsan/ gsang 'dus rim lnga'i khrid la zla ba
gsum dzad nas zhus pas/ de dus dge slong bsod nams grub kyis kyang zhor la 'khrid zhus nas bsgoms pas/ skye ba snga ma'i dge sbyor gyi don mngon du gyur te/ tshe snga phyi'i
dpon slob rnams kyi 'brel tshul dang / kha kha sangkha sing thugs sras rjes gsungs ba'i rgyu mtshan thams cad dran gsos nas/ chos rje yab sras kyi drung du zhus pas/
thugs dgyes nas 'o de tsam re dgos/ de ma byung na chos la nges shes mi skye/ rgyu 'bras the tshom gyi gzhir song nas sangs rgyas kyi lam btsal yang mi rnyed pa yin gsung
ngo / mdor na dus de nyid nas brtsams te sngon sbyangs kyi 'phro sad/ nyams rtogs khyad par can thugs la 'khrungs/ bla ma'i zhabs tog kho na gal che bar dgongs nas chos
rje thams cad mkhyen pa yab sras gnyis dang skad cig kyang mi 'bral ba'i nye gnas kyi gtso bo mdzad do/ /de'i stobs kyis sa lam gyi yon tan thams cad gong nas gong du gyur
te phyis de nyid kyi skyab mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug yin par gsungs

so / gnyis pa ni/ dam pa'i chos kyi dung 'bud rin chen skyabs/ /zhes dge ba'i bshes gnyen rin chen skyabs ni/ chos dung sgrog pa sogs mdzad la/ gzhan yang chos rje nyid kyi
sku'i rim gro la brtson par gyur to/ /dus phyis mdo khams smad kyi bstan 'gro'i dpung gnyen kun mkhyen 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa dkon mchog 'jigs med dbang po zhwa lu ri phug
tu byon/ chos khri thang kha'i bu ston nga 'dra ma'i drung du gsol 'debs tshigs su bcad pa 'ga' brtsams/ der gsung gleng la nga nyid bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i 'khor
na dung 'bud pa zhig byas sam zhes gsungs zer te/ gzhan gyis sgro btags pa ma yin pa gsungs nges can yin na/ gong gi chos dung sgrog pa de yin par nges shing / de ltar na
sku che ba'i yon tan de tsam gyis shes so/ /rim gro ba gnyis kyi skabs so/ /'khor dag pa rnam brgyad la mchod g.yog pa gnyis/ dge slong bzhi/ rim gro ba gnyis zhes brgyad
bgrangs kyang bla ma dge slong bsod nams grub gnyis su gyur pas dag pa rnam bdun tshang ngo / /de ltar gong du bstan pa rnams ni/ bu lugs zhes grub mtha' 'bur du dod pa'i
bka' srol bzungs te chos rgyun spel bar mdzad pa'i brgyud 'dzin gyi gtso bor gyur ba'o/ /de las gzhan pa'i dngos slob rags rim gyi mtshan tsam smos na 'di ltar/ 'jam
pa'i dbyangs kyi sprul pa gnyis ni/ chos rje don yod rgyal mtshan dang / dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gnyis so/ /spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul pa gnyis ni/
byang

sems bsod nams grags pa dang rgyal sras thogs med bzang po gnyis so/ mtha' 'khob 'dul ba'i paN grub gnyis ni/ kha che paNDi ta su ma na shrI dang tI shrI chen po bsod nams
blo gros gnyis so/ gzhan yang sa skya paNDi ta gnyis pa drung chos bstod tshig me tog phreng ba mdzadkyi rgyal mtshan/ bla ma 'dis lta ba 'khrungs tshul gnyis byung ste phyi
ma de chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i bka' drin las dbu ma'i lta ba 'khrul med rnyed/ sngon ma de dol po bas bskyangs zhes grags rgyud sde spyi rnams rtsom pa'i bsgrub
pa mdzad/lo tsA ba blo gros dpal/ lo tsA ba 'dis chos rje'i gsung la zin bris sogs mang du mdzad ces gragschub rtse mo/ /stag lung lo tsA ba shAkya bzang po/ mtshungs med
g.yag sde paN chen/ sngags 'chang g.yung ston zhwa lu'i mnye mchod kyi 'chams srol btsugrdo rje dpal/ 'ba' rab rgyal mtshan pa'i rnam sprul du chos rje nyid kyis lung bstandpal
bzang / shangs pa dge bsnyen yongs 'jam dpal gsar ldan gyi dkyil chog sogs mdzad/grags rgyal po/ bla ma rdza pa rin zhwa lu khul du byung zhing mthu che bar grags/po
che/ dwags sgam po papochos kyi sengge/ gnas rnying pa rin chen tog /rtsis kyi mkhan po nam mkha' rin chen/ stag ston gzhon nu dpal/ rnal 'byor byang chub seng ge/ dge
bshes zur char ba/ mkhan po spyi bo lhas pa/ mkhan chen khro phu ba bsod nams seng ge /chu mig mkhan po dkon mchog dpal/ tshal pa thams cad mkhyen pa si tu dge ba'i blo
gros/ mkhan chen gros pa chen po/ lung rigs 'dzin pa bsam grub dpal

mkhan chen drang po lung pa/ ba ri ba grags pa rin chen/ dge bshes blo ldan bzang po/ yar klungs chos dpal mgon po/ mkhan chen nam mkha' blo gros/ bla ma sangs rgyas grags
pa/ slob dpon dar ma byang chub/ drung dngos grub rgyal mtshan/ yog pa 'jam dpal grub bzang mdzadrgyal mtshan/ / dus 'khor ba shAkya dpal/ bla ma rdo rje gzhon nu/ mus pa
bde legs bzang po/ gu shrI kun dga' rin chen rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs shAkya rgyal mtshan/ bla ma chos grags dpal bzang gu shrI/ si tu byang chub rgyal mtshan/ khyung
po tshul shar pa chos kyi bdag pokhrims mgon po/ shangs dkar pa chos rje'i drung du byams chos sogs bslabsrin chen rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ rtogs ldan zla
ba seng ge/ chos rje don grub rin chen/ bla ma mgon po dpal chos rje'i rnam thar rin chen 'grel mdzadba/ mkhan chen snye mo phu gdung du 'khrungs nas chos rje'i drung
du rgyud sde bzhi la sbyangs tshogs pa'i gdan sar bskos/gzhon nu mgon po/ /chos lung rje tsong kha pa'i bla ma yin/mkhan chen bsgom gyin bzhugs pa tshogs pa'i mkhan por gdan
drangs/gras pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen grags pa tshung dus su 'khrungs nas tshogs pa'i mkhan po mdzad/bshes gnyen/ de la sogs te mkhas grub kyi slob ma rgya gar/ rgya
nag/ kha che/ bal po/ hor/

yu gur/ sog po/ 'ga'/ bod kyi dbus gtsang / mnga' ris/ mdo stod smad la sogs mdor na 'dzam bu gling gi sa cha phal cher khyab pa byung ngo / /de ltar bdag nyid chen po de dag
gi rnam par thar pa'i rjes su zhugs te/ rig pa'i gnas lnga dag la bslab cing 'dun par bya'o/ de ltar yang rje btsun sa paN gyis/ rang blo shes bya kun la ma sbyangs na/
/thams cad mkhyen pa nam mkha'i mtha' ltar ring / /da ltar dgongs nas rgyal dang de sras kyis/ /shes bya'i gnas la sbyangs zhes legs par gsungs/ /zhes so/ gal te man ngag
gi don cung zad gcig la sgril te sgom pas chog gis/ de lta bu'i gnas la sbyangs mi dgos so snyam na sa paN gyis/ sgom na thos pa mi dgos zhes/ /blun po blo rgya chung
ngu smra/ /thos ba med pas sgom pa tsam/ /'bad kyang dud 'gro'i sgrub thabs yin/ /ces so/ /tshe 'dir yun tung la shes bya'i gnas de dag rgya che bas/ don khong du chud par
mi 'gyur zhing / cung zad tsam shes pas ni tshe phyi ma sogs la phan pa ci yang med do snyam na sa paN gyis/ rig pa nang par 'chi yang bslab/ /tshe 'dir mkhas par ma gyur
kyang / /phyi mar gzhan la bcol ba yin/ /nor la rang nyid len pa 'dra/ /zhes gsungs so/ /gzhan yang 'di lta bu'i lo rgyus dag mnyan cing bzung nas dam pa gong ma'i yon
tan brjod pa la yang sbyar bar bya'o/ /rim gro bskyed de dam pa'i chos nyan pa la yang sbyar bar bya'o/ /mdor na rang dang gzhan gyi dad

pa yongs su spel ba'i thabs su sbyar bar bya'o/ /de ltar yang dkon mchog ta la'i gzungs las/ dad pas sngon 'gro ma ltar bskyed pa ste/ /yon tan thams cad 'byung zhing 'phel
bar byed/ /dwogs pa sel zhing chu bo rnams las sgrol/ /dad pas bde ba'i grong khyer mtshon par byed/ /ces sogs dad pa'i phan yon rgya cher gsungs pa ltar shes bar bya'o/
/'dir smras pa/ rin chen mchog tu grub pa'i lhun po la/ /rgyal sras gser ri'i phreng bas yongs bskor ba'i/ /ngo mtshar bkod pa blta la nyi zla zung / /dal med 'od kyi sgron
me spor ba bzhin/ /rig gnas mdo rgyud gzhung lugs phyogs re la/ /bka' bab stobs kyi bu chen zhes brjod kyang / /gzhung lugs cha kun rdzogs pa'i mtshan mo'i mgon/ /thub
bstan chu gter bzhad pa kho na yin/ /mkhyen pas 'jam dpal gzhon nu'i khengs pa 'phrog/ brtse bas pad dkar 'chang ba'i rjes su 'gro/ /nus pas gsang ba'i bdag po'i dpal la
'khu/ /re re'ang de lta'i yon tan khur du lci/ /rtogs brjod lus kun tshang ba'i nor bu'i gter/ /dus kyis bskal pabs ma thon gang gi tshe/ /lo rgyus 'khrul ba'i g.ya' bral
btso ma'i gser/ /thos brtson sngon goms bag chags stobs kyis bskrun/ /e ma bdag gi kun mkhyen yab sras kyi/ /rnam thar baiD'ur dkar po'i them skas la/ /nye bar 'dzeg pa'i
skal ba mchog thob nas/ /thub bstan gsal ba'i sgron ma nyid gyur cig /ces dpal ldan zha lu pa'i bstan pa la bka' drin che ba'i

ba'i skyes bu dam pa rnams kyi rnam thar lo rgyus ngo mtshar dad pa'i 'jug ngogs zhes bya ba las/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i thugs sras rnams kyi rtogs pa brjod pa'i sarga
ste gnyis pa'o// //kha ba'i dus bu 'khrigs pa'i sa 'dzin dag /nyi gzhon 'char kha'i zer gyis 'khyud pa bzhin/ /'chi med grub pa'i lha mo dang sgrol ma/ /tshe sbyin yid
bzin 'khor los shes rab stsol/ /zhes tshigs su bcad pa sngon du btang nas/ gsum pa brgyud 'dzin mkhas grub rim byon gyi rnam thar lo rgyus rgyas bsdus sna tshogs su bshad
pa la gnyis te/ gsol 'debs kyi tshig zin ltar byas nas bshad pa dang / der ma 'dus pa kha 'gengs kyi tshul du bshad pa'o/ /dang po ni/ gsol 'debs shloo kare don tshanaganyis
dang gsum du phye nas rim bzhin 'byung ba 'di ltar/ / | //gzhan yang bu ston lugs 'dzin rim byon pa/ /snyan pa'i grags pa 'bar ba'i rgyal mtshan 'chang / /sku zhang
bkra shis g.yas 'khyil rgyal mtshan 'dzin/ /mtshungs med dam pa gnyis la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes so//dang po mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs grags pa rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po ni/ bu ston thabs cad mkhyen pa'i rnam sprul du yang grags shing / dus 'dir sgo mor bi zhes bya ba'i grub thob cig gi dbon rgyud du rab byung drug pa'i
shing mo sbrul gyi lo la sku 'khrungs/ sku gzhon nu nas thugs sras lo tsA ba'i drung du/ rab tu byung zhing

rjes su bsnyen rdzogs kyi mkhan po yang de nyid ka yin/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i thugs sras bu chen rnams bsten nas mdo rgyud kyi don la sbyangs pa rgya cher mdzad/ khyad
par thugs sras lo tsA ba'i drung du/ de nyid la mnga' ba'i chos phal cher bum pa gang byor gsan te thugs kyi sras gcig pur gyur bas/ rjes su thugs sras rje sku mya ngan
las 'da' khar yang sku zhang nam mkha'i mtshan can la zhal chems su/ snga mo nas chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa nas brgyud pa'i phyi mtshan nyid/ nang gsang sngags thams
cad kyi dbang / bshad pa/ gdams ngag sna re tsam ma gtogs bum pa gang byor 'phrod yod pas/ dbon po grags rgyal 'di la gdan sa bskos na yong bar bdogs pas de'i bka' gros
mdzad pa las tub la byon zer ba'i phar mi mgyogs par thongs gsung / de ltar thugs sras rje zhing gshegs nas bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i khri thog tu snga rting gnyis phebs
pas/ snga ma la dgung lo nyi shu rtsa lnga ba sa mo sbrul gyi lo khri thog tu phebs/ lo bcu drug bzhugs nas chos 'khor bskor te mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal ldan rin chen
la gdan sa gtad/ de rjes yang gdan sar bskyar ma phebs te lo sum cu so drug gi bar khri thog tu bzhugs nas zhwa lu ri mthil gyi sde dgon rnams lugs gnyis kyi sgo nas
skyong bar mdzad/sne'u gdong gong ma chen po dbang grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi ti shrI mdzad nas dbus phyogs su yong lan du mar phebs/ gong ma chen pos sbyin bdag mdzad de/
kun mkhyen

bu ston zhabs kyi gsung rab kyang 'ga' re par brkos mdzad/ zhwa lu'i gdan sa snga rting dril bas lo lnga bcu nga gnyis kyi bar bzung nas 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi sgo nas

lur ye li'i nadskyol/ dus 'khor rgyud dang 'grel ba de sngas 'go ru zhog /rten 'brel gcig 'dug gis gsungs nas bzhag go /de nas sku lus la shed tsam med pas/ thugs rig
dang po byung bas/ thugs dam 'phel bo byung gsung / bsnyung g.yog mthil ma dge bshes chos 'byor yin pas/ chos 'byor khyod phan thogs po rang gcig byung bas/ bsod nams thob/
'phags mdzod laspa min yang pha ma dang / /nad pa dang ni chos smra dang / /srid mtha'i byang chub sems dpa' la/ /yon ni gzhal du med par gsung / /zhes sogs kyis lung
drangs nas/ nga nang pa ni yin chos smra ba'i gang zag ni yin no/ /skyes mtha'i byang chub sems dpa' yang min pa'i tig pa yang med gsung ngo / /de nas zhag gsum song ba'i
snga dro bzhugs gdan la/ snam gdan chen po cig yod pas/ de'i phyogs bzhi nas

bteg nas nyi ma la gdan drangs/ dro bar dus su slebs pa dang ja skol gsung / slob dpon gnyis thugs brel bas/ cung zad gcig 'gor bas ja mgyogs po thong / nga la yang dkar yol
thongs gsungs/ ja bzhes pa'i tshul mdzad/ khyed rnams kyis gsol 'debs shig gyis shig gsungs/ thugs dam la spyan hrig gi bzhugs 'dug /gsol 'debs tshar ba dang mnyam du/
sa pho rta'i lo nag pa zla ba'i nyi gza' mig dmar dang skar ma khrum smad yin/shu drug /rje btsun de nyid kyi dgung lo bdun cu don brgyad bzhes pa'i tshe dben tsar sku gshegs
so/ /de'i tshe 'ja' 'od rol mo'i sgra sogs kun gyi mthun snang du grub pa byung zhing / sku gdung gshed dmar gyi steng nas zhugs kyis sbyangs pas ring bsrel dang lha
sku sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung nas phyi rten rnam rgyal mchod rten ri phug tu bzhengs so// 'di nyid kyi gsung 'bum snye mo ru mtshams dgon pa dkar po bya bar bzhengs
tshul gyi dkar chag gcig 'dug pa 'di ltar/ kabar rnam 'joms dkar po'i dkyil chog la 20 barNa sha wa ri'i rjes gnang khrus chog dang bcas pa la 10 dus 'khor gyi zin bris
la 18 thugs rje chen po'i dmar 'khrid dang gsol 'debs la 18 rta mgrin nag po'i sgrub thabs dang rjes gnang la 5 donazhags kyi de nyid bcu drug la 6 mngon brjod kyi rnam
bshad sde bdun gsal ba'i sgron me la 110 mdzod kyi sbyor TIka mkhas pa'i yid 'phrog la 137 mngon brjod kyi tshig le'ur byas

pa la 36 mdzod kyi dka' 'grel mkhas pa'i yid 'phrog la 175 kun bsgril bas shog grangs lnga brgya dang bzhi bcu bzhugs so/ /kha bar phar phyin gyi sbyor Tika mkhas pa dga' byed
la 67 don bdun cu'i sa mtshams la 6 sum cu pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa la 3 sum cu pa'i rnam bshad la 14 bskal bzang sangs rgyas stong rtsa'i mtshan 'bum la 8 bzhugs gnas
gsal bo'i me long la 37 mdzod kyi thal phreng gnam lcags 'bar la 73 phyag chen dmigs pa gegs sel dbyangs can ma'i bstod pa byin rlob ma/ rab dkar gangs rtse marnams la
2 phag dkar gyi bstod pa/ rjes gnang / 'jam dkar gyi bstod pa/ dbyangs can ma'i bstod pa blo gros rgyas byed rnams la 6 phar phyin gyi thal 'phreng la 23 phar phyinbyin gyi
thal 'phreng bsdus pa la 11 sbyor bsdus ltag 'then ma la 5 rig pa'i sgo la 14 legs bshad nor bu'i 'phreng ba la 10 thal 'phreng nor bu'i 'phreng ba blogasal gyi mgul rgyan
la 18 bsdus chos nor bu'i 'phreng ba la 10 rdo rje thog la 6 tshad ma rnam par nges pa'i sbyor TIka gzhan phan nor bu'i 'phreng ba'i le'u gnyis pa yon la 83 gzhan don
le'u dang sbyor pa la 130 tshad ma'i thal 'phreng mdor bsdus la 10 kun bsgril bas shog grangs lnga brgya dang sum du so dgu bzhugs so/ /gsung 'bum 'di dag de lta phyogs
'di na bzhugs pa mi snang zhing / phyis dpe rgyun rnyed sla ba'i phyir du dkar chag 'di yang

bdag gi mthong ba las 'dir bris pa'o// gnyis pa ni/ yid bzhin nor bu ltar bzang rin po che/ /zhes mkhas grub smra ba'i nyi ma nor bzang rin chen dpal bzang po ni/ thugs sras
lo tsA ba dang / khyung lhas pa sogs bsten nas mdo sngags mtha' dag la sbyangs/ khyad par kun mkhyen bsod nams dpal grub kyi thugs kyi sras dam par gyur te/ rigs pa'i bstan
bcos tshad ma sde bdun gyi bdag por gyur/ 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum la gzhan dring mi 'jog pa'i rnam dpyod mchog tu yangs shing 'gran zla med pa'i mkhas pa chen por gyur
pa yin te/ bstod pa las/ 'chad pa'i tshe na legs bshad char rgyun 'bebs/ /rtsod pa'i tshe na phal rgol spobs pa 'joms/ /rtsom pas mkhas pa kun gyi yid 'phrog pa'i/ /mkhas
grub nor bzang zhabs la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes 'byung ba ltar ro/ /gzhan yang dus der smra ba'i sengge rong ston shAkya rgyal mtshan dang / mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang
po gnyis dpal 'khor sde chen du rtsod pa mdzad ces zer nas rtsod pa dang nga la yang gdan drangs/ mdor na ji skad du/ thog mar shes bya kun la mkhas par sbyangs/ /bar du
mkhas pa'i tshogs su legs par bshad/ /phyis nas 'dris pa'i don la brtson pas bsgom/ /dus gsum rgyal ba yongs kyi bzhed gzhung yin/ /zhes gsungs pa'i don yang bdag nyid
chen po 'di la mnga' bar sems so/ /sngon gsung 'bum gyi rim pa'ang ci rigs pa byung tshod 'dug kyang / rjes 'jug ma rungs pa dag gis bdag

nyid chen po 'di dag gi 'chad rtsod rtsom gsung gyi mdzad pa ba gang che ba rnams khyi rgan gyi rnam bar gaNDi'i sgra bsgrags pa bzhin du rjes med du btang ba'i lag rjes snga
phyi kun tu bzhag nas mi mngon pa'i dbyings la gshegs so//gsum pa ni/ rnam dpyod phul phyin zla ba dpal rin te/ /zhes mkhas pa'i dbang po tsandra shrI ratna ni/grub pa'i
dbang phyug sku zhang nam mkha' mtshan can gyi thugs kyi sras gcig pur grags shing / spyir shes bya rig pa'i gnas mtha' dag la mkhasashing rgyud sde bzhi la dbang 'byor
ba'i rdo tsandra go mi zer ba'ang gsung rtsom gyi mdzad byang mang po la yod de bod skad du btsun pa zla ba zhes pa'orje 'dzin pa kun gyis nang nas mchog tu gyur cing /
de yang ji skad du/ rje nyid kyi zhal nas/ rgyud 'grel man ngag cha shas yongs rdzogs ngos/ /rnam dpyod bzin mdzes mgrin pa'i dbyangs snyan pa'i/ /ri dwags matsan ma rab
tu mdzes bkod nas/ /bstan pa'i ku mud skyong 'di skal ba bzang / /de phyir brtson pa'i bser bu cher g.yos te/ /snyoms las chu 'dzin dra ba kun bsal nas/ /legs bshad bsil
zer du ma rab spros te/ /mi shes mun tshogs deng bar gyis shig kye/ /zhes so/ /khyad par yo ga rnal 'byor rgyud kyi phyag len gyi gnad mtha' dag la shin tu mkhas pas/ ji
skad du/ bris thig gar dbyangs bzhi la tsandra shrI ngas/ /legs par sbyangs te da lta nga min gzhan pa su/ /zhes dang / gsung tshangs pa'i dbyangs ltar snyan 'jebs pa yod
pas/ bdag gis gsung

dbyangs bsgrags pa na/ /'jig rten mes po tshangs pa yang / /dbyangs snyan brjod pa'i snyems bral nas/ /rang gi gnas su yib pa snyam/ /zhes sogs gsungs so/ /gnas gsar dge 'phel
gyi ri ngos su sangs rgyas gling zhes bya ba'i dgon pa btab/ der phyi rten sku 'bum sogs kyang du ma bzhengs/ mkhas mang brgya phrag la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor zhing
gdul bya dpag tu med pa'i don mdzad do// | gsung 'bum gyi rim pa deng skabs ma tshang ba bzhugs pa bdag gis ma mthong yang / kha thor du snang ba la/ rgyud sde spyi rnams/
dus 'khor gyi cho ga'i lhan thabs/ gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa'i zin bris/ gsang 'dus 'jam rdor gyi bstod chen shin tu legs/ 'jigs byed dpa' bo gcig pa'i lhan thabs/ gdong
drug gi gnad 'grol yig gshed dmar lha lnga'i phyag len gyi rim pa/ rdor dbyings kyi lhan thabs/ khams gsum rnam rgyal gyi dka' gnad gsal byed/ bshad rgyud rdo rje rtse mo'i
rig ma bcu drug gi 'grel ba/ chig 'bum gyi 'grel pa/ dka' gnad gsal byed kyi lhan thabs/ dbang chog dpal mchog rigs bsdus kyi dka' gnad gsal byed/ gtsug dgu'i dka' gnad
gsal byed/ mi 'khrugs pa'i dka' gnad gsal byed/ phyag rdor 'gro bzang gi dbang chog grub dbang nam mkha'i mtshan can gyi rnam thar gsol 'debs sogs mang du bzhugs so//rgyud
'dzin mkhas btsun bzang gsum dang ldan pa'i slob ma mang du byung yang /gtso bor gyur pa thugs kyi sras dam pa

shar chen thams cad mkhyen pa ye shes rgya mtsho'o// gsol 'debs las/ so rig sngags 'chang mthu chen shAkya dpal/ /'khrul rtog kun zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan bsgreng / /dka'
bzhi rin chen thub bstan rgyal mtshan 'dzin/ /mtshungs med dam pa gsum la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes 'byung bas/dang po rje sngags 'chang rin po che bla chen shAkya dpal ni/
sngon mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags dang / 'phags pa'i yul gyi slob dpon mi thub zla ba dang / sa skya'i rje btsun bsod nams rtse mo rnams su
skye ba bzhes shing / de rjes shambha la'i rgyal phran tsandra sang ga ta zhes bya ba'i khyim du tshun mi'i sras su 'khrungs te/ rigs ldan rgyal ba sa skyong chos ston pa'i
'dun sar/ dus 'khor gyi rgyud dang rgyud 'grel rnams gsan nas sku na phra mo la gshegs pa'i tshul bstan/ de nas bod kyi sa cha g.yor por/ snye mdo kun mkhyen kun dga'
don grub tu 'khrungs nas 'gro ba'i don mdzad cing / de nyid kyi skye ba ni sngags 'chang rin po che 'di nyid yin no/ /'di'i yab ni sngags rnying ma'i gdung rgyud so zur snubs
gsum sngags pa'i rgyal por grags pa'i nang nas so zhes bya ba'i rigs rus dri ma med par 'khrungs shing / mthu dang rdzu 'phrul la mnga' brnyes pa so ston chos skyong
dpal dang / yum sngags mo btsun ma dpal gnyis kyi sras su/ snye mo ru matsams kyi dben gnas dbal 'ug tshang zhes bya bar shing mo lug gi lo/ /dpyid

zla ra ba'i nyer lnga'i tho rangs sku bltams/ shing lug 'di chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa dgung lo drug cu ra drug dang / g.yung ston rdo rje dpal gyi dgung lo bdun du con gnyis
kyi thog yin no/ /lhums su zhugs dus yum gyi rmi lam du lto bar phyag na rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs grub pa cig rmis/ yab la bshad pas/ mtshan ril por gnyid
log na rmi lam sna tshogs 'char yong ba de ma shes sam gsung / yang nub gcig lta bo nas nyi ma 'od zer rab tu 'bar ba gcig shar ba rmis nas/ yab la bshad pas/ 'dre ru rnam
rtog langs na mthong tshad 'dre ru 'gyur/ rtog pa ma rags gsung / yang nub gcig sa gzhi thams cad skye bos gang nas rang la phyag dang mchod pa snatshogs 'bul ba rmis nas
yab la zhus pas/ rang re gnyis la rang de tsamagyi re go med/ 'on kyang bla mas lung bstan yod pas/ lus kyi sems can de la nor nyan gcig yod pa gda' gsung ngo / lung bstan
tshul ni/ yab kyi sngar gru shes rab sengge'i drung du rab byung nod du phebs pas/ gru'i zhal nas rab tu 'byung ba 'di bstan pa'i gzhi rtsa yin pas khyad par du 'phags
mod kyi/ khyod la ma 'ongs par byang chub sems dpa' chen po zhig gzhan don la khyod kyi bur 'khrungs pa 'dug pas yul du log nas khyim thabs gyis shig ces gsungs so/ /sku
'khrungs nas byis pa smra shes tsam gyi dus na/ rtsed mo mi mdzad par/ sgom zhig byed gsungs nas/ mnyam gzhag mdzad cing spyan

gzim me'i bzhugs/ skabs shig phyir byon nas/ lu ma 'khyil ba sbal cong gis khengs pa gcig gi gdong na bzhugs te/ skyabs 'gro gcig mdzad kyin 'dug pa la/ yab kyis o lo ci byed
yod dris pas/ sems can shin tu mang po la chos bshad kyin yod gsungs skad/ snying rje shin tu che bas/ matsan yang byang sems chen po zhes btags so/ /yab de thugasal cung
zad mi 'tshams pa byung na/ pha rol po de'i zhing sar ser ba sgos 'bebs kyi mthu rang mdzad pa zhig yod kyang dam pa'i 'di'i mdzad spyod gzigs pa nas de 'dra mi mdzad
pa zhig byung gda'/ de nas nyid kyi sku zhang grags pas/ g.yung ston rdo rje dpal spyan drangs nas phug pa chen mor rdo rje gzhon nu'i khrom dbang gcig mdzad pa der phebs
pa'i gzigs snang la/ dkyil 'khor gyi dbus na lcags phur khru gang pa gcig yod pa yi dam gyi lha dngos su gzigs shing / de'i gnas gsum nas 'od zer dkar dmar mthing gsum
byung nas rang gi gnas gsum du thim pas zad med kyi ting nge 'dzin la yun ring po 'byams pa byung / des da nas shes bya thams cad la gzhan dring mi 'jog pa'i thugs rab skyes/
snye mdo kun mkhyen chen po de g.yung ston pa'i bla mar 'dug pa/ de dus khong pas ngo mkhyen pas/ dbang mdzad 'phro la nga'i bla ma 'dir phebs 'dug skyabs su mchi/ gson
gshin 'phrad pa'i dus kyang byung gsungs te dgyes nas dga' ba drug gi mgur gsungs so/ /de nas gsung rab rnams kyi

lung med na/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus bla ma 'dis gzhan rjes su 'dzin pa na/ bka' ma dag par 'gro bas/ nged kyis 'bul dgos gsungs te/ lo de'i 'phro zla ba brgyad tsam bzhugs nas/
gsang sngags rnying ma'i rgyud dbang bka'/ man ngag dang bcas pa khong rang la mnga' ba thams cad bum pa gang byor gnang / chab klog bod yig lanytsa/ wartu/ dha ri ka/ na
gur sogs kyi yi ge/ ri mo/ gzan yang rin chen sna bdun/ dug bcos pa'i man ngag/ gso ba rig pa'i skor rnams kyang g.yung ston nyid kyis rdzogs par phul lo/ /skabs su zhal
kyal la/ gzhan ma rnams bla mas slob ma rjes su 'din pa yin na'ang / nges ssalob mas bla ma rjes su 'dzin pa 'di rang mtshar che ang gsung / de rjes yum dang bcas zhwa lur
rim gro chen mo la phebs te/ ri phug tu byin rlabs zhu bar byon nas/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che/ chos khri thang kar theg pa chen po'i sems bskyed
chen mo gsung gin 'dug pa de rdzogs par gsan/ chos grol ba dang / chos rje bla brang du phebs nas nye gnas la da ci slob dpon rin chen dpal grub gyi rcer 'dug pa'i bu chung
zhwa mar po gyon pa gcig 'dug de ga na yod tshol la bos shog gsung / yo ga ba dbang rnon yod du byung ste/ chos rje'i sku mdun du khrid nas slebs dus/ thugs dam sAtstsha

gi bka' gnang bas/ btsar sham

ser po kyugs kyugs gong pa med pa'i 'tshem 'phro gcig khyer byung pas de gnang / nyid cag 'um bu'i gdan sa 'dir mi khugs pa gda' yi/ 'on kyang nyid cag sems can chen po gcig
yin gda' bas/ sde 'di thal khung du song skyor mdzod cig gzung / dus phyis rje rin po che'i zhal nas/ nged zhwa lu par lhag par zhen che zhing zhabs tog gang 'grub byed
pa 'di/ mkhyen rab dbang phyug bu ston chen po'i bka' yin/ gdan sa de yong rgyur 'dug na'ang / gos de la gong pa med pa'i lan 'dug gsung ngo / /de nas zhwa lu'i lha khang
rnams su byon te/ ri mo sogs lha ngos bzungs bas/ kun ngo mtshar ba gyur ring/ nyid kyi zhang po 'jam dbyangs ba zer ba'i chos sde'i slob dpon gcig yod pa des/ yum sras
gnyis mar 'byon khar/ bu chung 'di'i mgo 'don nged kyis byed/ cis kyang 'dir skyol gsung ba'i zhal ta nan can gnang zhing / yul du phebs dus yab mkhris pa 'pho lhung gi
bsnyung gzhi yin zer bsnyel nas zhag brgyad tsam song 'dug de'i bsnyung g.yog zhus te bzhugs pa la/ tho rangs shig mnal bsad nas yab kyi sku mdun du shog gsungs te byon pas/
gzims mal gyi rgyab na ke tshang cig yod pi nang na/ sdig sbal kha sbyor gyi thun dong du ki la ya 'bru bcu gnyis pa'i rdo thun/ rem nyi'i kha bzhi'i bsad thun/ gza'

gtad / khyod nyon cig mi ngas mi lo lnga bcu nga gcig bar du pha jo sras sngags pa'i rkang ma drangs/ 'dre thog tu lham dbub/ nor thog tu chos ma btsongs/ rang thog tu dgra

gcig mdzad/ spyi bo nas 'od dkar bo phug ron gyi sgong tsam zhig thon te byang phyogs su thal gyi song de/ da ltar yab 'das nas ser ba bsrung dgos gyi yul chung 'ga' re
yod pa rnams su yum gyis ser bsrung mdzad do/ sdigs mdzub kyis ser ba bar snang nas 'ded cing / rdzas rus sbal yod pa dag las me 'bar ba gzigs nas yum la rdzas

sngags yod na bdag la gnang pa zhu gsungs pas/ bu la cis kyang ster/ nga la yang pha jos gnang ba yin/ sngags la yi dam gyi snying po zer ba gcig bzla dgos/ rdzas la phreng
ba zer ba gcig 'brong ko ltar mnye dgos kyin gda'/ de las zab pa med gsung / de thugs la bcang nas spyod lam ci mdzad kyang / zhal nas bzlas brjod shub bur gnang ba rgyun
mi chad pa gcig byung ngo / de rjes lo gsum tsam yong ba dang zhwa lu las zhang po 'jam dbyangs pas gdan 'dren byung nas sras kyis yar phebs/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen

nas/ mngon rtogs rgyan gyi rtse 'grel/ kun mkhyen bu'i TIkka dang bcas pa la thugs sbyong mdzad skabs/ gdan sa chen po zhwa lu ri phug tu sbyin bdag gcig gis tshar 'gyed

/bzhag par bya ba cung zad med/ /yang dag nyid la yang dag blta/ /yang dag mthong na rnam par grol/ /zhes sogs kyi gzhung dris/ sgro gleng mdzad/ tshig brtsegs thor thor

chiDa phyi ma dge slong gi sdom pa yang mkhan chen lo tstsha ba de nyid la nod cing / lo chen de'i zhal nas/ gsang sngags pa la thog mar rdo rje slob dpon gyi rgyu bsnyen
