ba zhig yod pa de

mtshams har 'don mdzad/ bla brang shar ma'i sgo brdungs byung / der rje rin po ches ci yin gzigs pas sgo phye gsung / ngag bcad kyis brda mdzad nas mi dbye gsungs pas/ khyod
la phan pa byu rgyu yod/ cis kyang sgo phye zhig zer nas 'gas sgo gcig yod pa dbye dgos byung ste nang du phebs/ khong pa rta mgrin gyi grub thob tu byed pas/ spyi bor
rta mgo'i phyag rgya bcings/ i haM haM haM zer rta'i skad bton/ rje rin po che'i zhabs la thal lcag gcig brgyab/ steng shod thams cad du yar rgyug mar rgyu mdzad/ de nas
khyod la kha sang nas cho 'phrul de 'dra byung yang bar chad kyis ma tshugs pa ngo mtshar che/ da sgrub pa byed lugs 'di bzhin gyis gsung ba'i bslab byu mang du mdzad nas
phyir phebs song / de nub nas cho 'phrul zhi zhing / bskyed rim la brtan pa thob pa yin skad/ de nas phyag na rdo rje 'gro bzang gi zhal dngos su gzigs/ bsnyen mtshams grol
ba nas bzungs te/ chos kyi rje thugs sras lo tstsha ba chen po de nyid sku ma gshegs gyi bar la zhag gcig tu yang mi 'bral ba'i gzhis byes thams cad du nye gnas kyi mthil
mdzad/ rgyal ba'i gsung rab phal mo che/ de'i dgongs 'grel du gyur ba'i bstan bcos/ khyad par bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa nas brgyud pa'i mdo sngags kyi chos bka' ma
lus pa bum pa gang byo'i tshul du lo chen de nyid las thob pa'i sangs rgyas kun gyi ngo bor gzigs nas bka' bzhin sgrub pa'i mchod pas dus rtag tu mnyen par mdzad do/gzhan
yang bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal

mtshan / rgyal sras thogs med bzang po dpal/ lo chen byang rtse/ mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs grags la sogs la chos mang du gsan/ de rjes lcags kyi phur re zhig sgrub pa mdzad/
de nas sbyem chung du mon pa ke ti'i sgrub pa zhag bdun du mdzad pas/ gza' mon pa nag po'i gzugs su byung ba la/ khyod rang gi lus ston gsungs bas rA hu la dkar po zhi ba'i
nyams can cig byung / 'di min pa'i lus dngos ston gsungs pas/ kha rlang gi dug mi bzod zer/ nga bskyed rim las rgyal ches bas cang mi 'ong gsungs pas/ yug gcig nas khyab
'jug mgo dgu pa/ rtse mo bya rag gi mgo can/ nyi ma'i thad du slebs pa lus dmar po/ mig me dpung 'dra bas gang ba ltar mi bzod pa gcig la/ bskyed rim 'phangs bstod de
bka' bsgos/ dam bzhag mdzad de/ rkang dmar nag khrag gi rgya mtsho'i dbus/ zhes sogs kyi bstod bskul yang der gsungs/ yang gnas de nyid du skyems chung bkor bdag dam la btags
shing / dpal chen po zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i sku gcig yod pa yi dam gyi lha dngos su gzigs nas/ chos sku 'gyur med bde chen longs spyod sku/ zhes sogs kyi bstod pa
yang mdzad/ de rjes yangs su phyag rdor 'byung 'dul gyi bsnyen pa mdzad pas/ dngos su zhal gzigs shing shar phyogs su song la 'gro ba'i don gyis shig ces lung bstan/ gser
'gyur dang / ril bu la sogs pa'i med pa'i grub pa chen po brgyad brnyes/ skabs shig gnas gsar lung du bzhugs pa'i nub gcig mnal lam du bud med sngo sangs

ma / rta dang zhur la zhon pa gcig byung nas/ bdag la nad pa gcig yod pas phebs dgos zer/ rte de la chibs nas byon pas/ khang bzang shin tu che ba nor gyis phyug pa gcig gi
nang du gdan drangs te/ be phrug dkar po'i do ras che gcig gi steng na/ gha haM gi ber gyon pa'i mi gcig nyal 'dug nas/ 'di na zer/ ga na dris pas/ nyang stod pa snam du
mda' phog byung zer nas rkang ba nar gyis brkyangs byung la gzigs pas/ bol mtshams na yungs kar 'bru gnyis 'dug pa phyag sen gyis bton/ gzhan ci yang mi 'dug gsungs pas/
de kas 'tshal bdog lags zer te/ phyag rdor 'khor chen gyi bzlas lung zhus/ phyag 'tshal ba la gzigs pas/ sang dkar po'i la thod gcig 'dug pa mi 'bud pa'i be'i 'og na sbrul
mjug nyug ger 'dug gang yin nam dgongs pa la bud med das sngor bzhin gdan drangs/ phyir log 'gro khar phyag gcig phul nas/ ming po bubs lhag pa gcig bdog pa/ de'i srog
skyabs ming la klu chen thod dkar zer ba lags/ da phyin chad nged ming sring khyed kyi bka' 'bangs su mchi zhing / mjal rten me tog mtshon pa gcig 'bul zer te/ nas khyor
gang zhal ras la gtor byung bas mnal sad/ de nyin gnas sngon khog ser zho shin tu rgod pas/ mi rnams kyi pra phab ste gang bya dris pas/ jo mor mo babs nas/ 'di'i ser lam
slob dpon shAkya dpal min pa gzhan gyis mi chod/ khyed rang rnams dpya bsdus la khong la phul zer ba bzhin zhus

pas / rje rin po ches ser lam bcad/ de lo khong rnams kyis nas bsdus pa'i phung phul bas/ nas khal nyis brgya lhag tsam byung / rje rin po che'i zhal nas/ lha 'dre'i 'bul ba
'di yang thabs 'dra ba la re ba min pa khong rang gi nor des phan mi thogs pa 'dug gsungs/ de la sogs pa'i snang srid kyi lha 'dre kun gyi mchod gnas su gyur pa yin gda'/
de rjes sku zhang chen po si tu ye shes kun dga' nyid mi phyed pa'i dad pa dang ldan pas/ zha lur zhugs nas thugs dam mdzad dus zhwa lu chos sde'i bshad gsar ba rnams/
gong ma chen por gnang sbyin zhu ba'i cha la/ kham chu dang 'khrug long cher byung bas/ ram sel skyon gyis chos skyong gi mthu rang babs kyis dgra phyogs kyi lte bo rnams
gzer dang khrag skyugs shing shi nas mi rnams na re/ slob dpon shAkya dpal gyis mu stegs pa'i rang 'thag gcig bskor bas/ me lhab lhab 'bar chu thor thor 'byung zhing mi
thams cad gsod kyin 'dug zes rin po che la kha zer ro/ de dus rje nyid kyi slob ma phyogs glang khros te/ thog 'phang dgos bsam pa la zhal shes kyi man ngag med par/ thun
dong kha nas mkhar bstan te bton pas/ thog ma de la gnyis nam mkha' mthong ma khad shor nas gcig gar song cha mi 'dug gcig ri phug gi sku 'bum thang la drug cu ba gtang
ba'i khag dmar ba gcig yod pa la rgyugs nas/ de'i shugs kyis sku 'bum chen mo la rdo'i tog yod pa gas shing chos 'khor kyang thugs cung zad 'khyoms/ de nas la chung de lung
pa'i rgyab na zhing

rmo ba'i glang dmar gcig yod pa la skrog nas de dang mi gcig shi/ thog mdel gnyis thun khrod du song bas bsgribs nas ma shor/ shur sgra chen po byung bas khong rang yang rtsed
nas phyag rdor gyi thang ka har tshon ma byin rlabs can du byed pa gcig yod de mgo bgyon nas bsdad 'dug go/ der rje'i drung du rgyu mtshan zhus pas/ khyod nyams chung
pa la thug /kham mchu de tsam la thog spung bas gar lang / bstan pa'i dgra bo gnyis kyi tshe thar 'dug pa gsung skad/Teachings at sNe gdongde lta bu'i za zing sna tshogs
kyi thugs sun nas bya bral gyi rnam pa mdzad de dbus su phebs/ shar dwags la sgam por thugs dam mdzad bar 'byon dgos dgongs kyang sku tshe snga ma'i las 'brel gyi sne'u
gdong gong ma chen po dbang grags pa rgyal mtshan dang mchod yon du gyur/ dbus phyogs su gzhan don 'phrin las shin tu che/khyad par pho brang sne'u gdong du yo ga rnam 'byor
rgyud dang rdo rje 'phreng ba sogs phyi nang gi dkyil 'khor mang po zhal phye/ chos rgyal chen po zhal ngo gdung brgyud/ nang blon/ gdan sa che chung gi bla ma dge ba'i
bshes gnyen rnams dang gzhis kha gong 'og gi mi dbon sogs mdor na bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i gdul bya smin grol la bkod/Renovations at bSam yasdpal bsam yas mi 'gyur lhun
gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang la nyams gso mdzad/ mnal lam du rgyal po shing bya can 'ongs nas phyag byas te dngul bra tshan ba'um gcig la gan dar dkar po kha gang btags
nas phul/ zhig gsos chen po

'di'i cha rkyen gang dgos nges kyis kyang bgyi ba lags zer bas/ de nas sa rdo dang shing sogs dka' tshegs mi dgos bar 'bad med du byung gsung / lha 'dre mi gsum gyis las byas
bar snang ste/ yar klungs chu gling du mi zhig la rgyal gdon zhugs pa de na re/ dbus gtsang gi lha 'dre thams cad bla ma shAkya dpal gyis bsam yas kyi zhig gsos la bskul/
nga yar 'gro dgos byung pas/ bskom thang chad zer ro/ de'ang sger gyi gdung rab las/ grub chen kun dga' snying po dang / mkhas grub sangs rgyas gsang ba sogs/ /yo ga'i
grub chen mgrin gcig tu/ /bdud dpung 'dul ba'i lung bstan thob/ /mthu stobs can gyi spyod pa brnyes/ /bla ma shAkya dpal ba la/ /bcom ldan so sor 'bras ma sogs/ /lha mo
lnga yi srung 'khor dang / /gzhan yang dbang 'khrid mang po gsan/ /zhes bya ba 'dug pas/ grub pa'i slob dpon chen po de dang de dag gis kyang rjes su gnang ba thob nas bstan
'gro'i don mdzad pa zhig yin par mngon no/ /check passage!!!chos rgyal sne'u gdong bas dgon sde chen po mang du phul rung ma bzhes/ grwa'i phu na snye mdo zer ba'i dgon
hrul zhig yong ba bzhes nas der phebs/ nye gnas rgyan bkras kyis sde chen po de tsam phul ba ma bzhes par/ de kyang rul phug ron min pa sdod mkhan tsam med pa 'di 'dras
ci mdzod lags zhus pas/ rje'i zhal nas lam bu rang la che bdog gis gsung / gzims khang gong mar thegs pas/ po ti mang po 'thor zhing chud bzod pa gzigs te/ nga'i dpe cha

ma dpe btsal du dkon pa tshod 'di 'dra bar gyur pa ches 'phangs ang gsung skad/ de na 'dug pa'i slob dpon bsod nams rgyal mtshan bya bar/ kho rang gi spo pa rgan po zhig yod
pa sngang 'da' dus kha chems su 'dir dgon pa gud pa'i tshe na nged kyi bla ma kun mkhyen kun dga' don grub de nges par 'byon pa yod/ khyod rang dang mjal na 'di phul/ ma
'jal na bu tsha rabs la kha chems zhog zer nas bum pa gcig gtad 'dug pa/ de khyer nas rje nyid la phul pas/ dge bshes dge 'dun rgyal mtshan la mi go chod byung 'dug khyod
kyis nga ngo shes sam gsungs pas/ khong pa yang sbo po ba'i ming byung bas sngar las kyang ches dad par gyur/ dgon par nyams gso mdzad nas der gdul bya bskyangs/ phyag
rdzas gang byung rnams zhwa lu chos sder dus mchod chen po snga rting 'grangs pas lo bcu gsum gyi bar du bzungs/ bka' las/ nga la 'di tsam gyi tshe ring po yong ba med kyang
/ chos rje yab sras kyi dus mchod bzungs pa 'dis tshe bsrings 'dug gsung / gzhan yang dbus gtsang gi dgon sde mang por bsnyen bkur dang 'bul ba rgya cher mdzad/ de ltar
dngos kyi 'dul bya re zhig rdzogs nasdgung lo bdun cu don brgyad bzhes pa chu pho byi pa'i lo la snye thang du sde srid sgar chen phebs dus su dpon g.yog gis zhus ngor
byon/check passage!!!bzhed don thams cad grub pa dang snye mdor phebs nas/ gzims khang gi gdung rtsa nag por song la gzigs nas/ da nga yang 'gro ran gda'/ rje phag mo gru
pa yang gdan

sar lo bcu gsum las ma bzhugs/ nged kyis 'dir lo bco brgyad tsam song 'dug gsungs/ yar lung la sang thegs rgyu'i de ring / snye mdo ba rnams la shog gyis/ ban rgan dang da
e 'phrad mi shes pas phyi phyag gi chos shig ster ba yin gsungs nas/ de nyid las rgyu 'bras zhib rgyas 'dra dar/ gcod dbang nam mkha' sgo 'byed cig gnang /de nas pho brang
rgyal bzang smon mkhar du phebs/ gong ma chen po'i drung du bka' dbang 'ga' re 'bul ba tshe/ nam mkha' thams cad 'ja' tshon gyi dra bas khebs pa byung nas/ rje nyid kyi
zhal nas/ chos rje bu ston yab sras nam mkhar nged kyi bsu ba la phebs 'dug mchod pa rgya chen po gshoms gsungs/ de la sogs te dag pa'i snang ba dpag tu med pa gzigs shing
/ snyun tshul bzhad gad dang bsres pa gcig mdzad de/ lo de'i smin drug can gyi zla ba'i nyer lnga'i nub mo/ 'ja' 'od rol mo'i sgra dang / me tog gi char 'bebs bzhin pas
sku 'da' tshul bstan/ sku gdung ril bor bzhugs pas 'gro ba mtha' yas pa'i re ba bskong ba'i yid bzhin gyi nor bu lta bu'o/Major Disciples/slob ma'i gtso bo sde srid phag
mo grub pa'i gdung rgyud rnams dang / drung rin po che byang chub rdo rje/ chos rje bzang po dpal/ lha btsun bsod nams rin chen/ shar dwags po ba thams cad mkhyen pa'i
bshes gnyen sogs mang du byon cing / gso ba rin pa'i bstan bcos rin chen sna bdun dang / rgyud sde mang po'i sgrub dkyil sogs gsung rtsom gyi rim pa'ang ji snyed cig bzhugs
shing / rgyas bar rnam thar gyi yi

gega ma mo slob dpon hUM ka ras mdzad pa yod pa las shes so//gnyis pa ni/ 'khrul rtog kun zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan bsgrengs/ / zhes 'khrul zhig chen pa de ni/ sngon 'phags
pa'i yul du grub chen ku ku ri pa dang / ljongs 'dir dpyal kun mkhyen shes rab dpal bzang po sogs mdor na nam mkhas grub pa rgyud mar sku skyer bzhes pa'i mthar/ 'di
nyid du lhums su bzhugs pa'i tshe yang / yum gyi rmi lam du thar pa nas yong zer ba'i rnal 'byor pa he ru ka'i chas spras nas gar mdzad pa zhig gnas g.yar ba'i tshul du
byung zhing / de yang zhwa lu'i shar gyi dur khrod zung gsum ri'i phu na chos lung zhes bya ba'i sgrub gnas yod pa der yab rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug dka' bzhi ba gzhon
nu rgyal mtshan dang / yum sgrub chen ma tshul khrims 'bum gnyis kyi sras su rab byung bdun pa'i sa mo yos kyi lo la 'khrungs/ bltams nas cher ma lon par/ hrI ShDI'i sngags
thol byung du sgrog pa dang chos 'chad pa'i tshul mdzad pa zhig byung / res dga' nga thar pa nas 'ong / nga rang la dngul gyi rdo rje sems dpa' 'ang yod ces tshig lab
mdzad/ skabs shig yum gyi rgyab tu 'khyer te/ rdo rje gdan du phebs pas/ thar pa mthong ba'i la khar slebs pa dang / a lu lu/ nga rang gis dgon pa mthong byung a ma mgyogs
por byon gsung ba sogs sngon gnas rje dran mang du mdzad/ dgung lo bdun la yum sku gshegs/ yab kyi zhwa lu pa dge slong rin chen skyabs zer ba

gcig la klog slob tu bcug ste/ de nyid chos 'chad mdzad pa'i dge bshes chen po yin pas/ dbang dang lung 'khrid bshad pa sogs chos zhu mkhan byung tshad kyi gral du bcug pas/
de las rdo rje 'phreng ba dang / sbyor dkyil bcu gnyis/ mi tra brgya rtsa sogs dbang chos kyang mang du gsan/ dgung lo bcu la chos rje mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa grags
pa rgyal mtshan gyi drung du rab tu byung / mtshan tshul khrims rgyal mtshan zhes gsol/ zhwa lu pa'i dge bshes mkhas mchog rin chen tshul khrims kyi spyan sngar mdo phyogs
la sbyangs shing / dpe 'dzin gyi dbu tshugs pa dang me tog gi char babs/ rgyal po chen po rnam thos sras kyi zhal mngon sum du bstan/ pa rnam dga' ba gdong du phebs
te/ kun mkhyen dga' gdong ba las rnam 'grel sogs gsan/ skabs shig na bza' gcig dang lhung bzed rkun mas khyer bas/ dpal ldan lha mo la zhal bkyal gyi tshul du grwa kyang
chos byed kyi chas ka re tsam bsrung skyob mi byed pa zhes gsungs pas/ de ma thag bu mo gtsang ma gcig la lha mo babs nas rje'i phyag nas khrid de la gnam gshol bo'i grong
pa gcig gi 'ong khang sgo dang nge ba zhig gi nang du slebs/ der gdang la lhung bzed dang na bza' bkal nas gda' ba mod la rkun ma ngos zin nas byung skad/ de'i tshe 'jam
dbyangs chos dpal bzang po'i snyan pa gsan te 'jal bar phebs par brtsams pa na/ grogs dag gis mtshan nyid kyi slob gnyer smar ba'i skabs 'dir sgom chen pa'i bla ma bstan
pa mi rigs zhes gshol

btab kyang ma thebs par zhabs drung du phebs te mjal bas/ bla mas kyang rang re mi la dang skam po ba mjal ba lta bu yin zhes dgyes dgyes ci yang mdzad/ der ne gu dang sbyor
drug sogs snga phyir zab chos shin tu mang ba gsan/ sang zhu rgyu'i chos da do nub rmi lam bzungs te zhus pas kyang / dngos su gnang ba dang zhus dag thub pa 'ong gin 'dug
gsung / slar ri phug tu phebs te/ sngar gyi mkhan po 'jam dbyangs grags rgyal de nyid dang / las kyi slob dpon mkhas grub nor bzang rin chen sogs dad pa'i dge 'dun bcu
phrag gcig gi dbus su dge slong gi dngos bor bsgrubs/ de nas snar thang lo tsA ba sengge shri las sgra ka lA pa'i bshad pa yongs rdzogs/ tsandra pa'i dka' gnad dang / zhar
byung snyan ngag me long gi rtsom khrid/ sdeb sbyor rin chen 'byung gnas/ ming gi mngon brjod 'chi med mdzod sogs rig gnas la sbyangs pa phul du phyin pa mdzad/ dbus
su phebs nas 'bras spungs pa 'jam dbyangs bkra shis dpal ldan dang / se ra ba gung ru rgyal mtshan bzang po gnyis mkhas zer ba gsan nas thog mar 'bras spungs su phebs/ der
chos 'brel 'ga' re zhus pas thugs tshims rgyu rang ba byung / slar se rar thegs pa'i nyin gtsang nas chas skyel mi dge bshes kun grags bslebs/ 'bras spungs pa'i chos skyong
ma dga' bar chas skyel gyi bong bu 'chi la thug'thug/ rje nyid kyis sku chos kyi bla bas shing bden pa bdar bas ma shi tsam byung / mtshan mo kun

grags kyis rtsa chun gcig sngas su bcug ste nyal bas/ srod la khos ku co drag po gcig bton byung / ci byung gsungs pas/ bdag gi mdun 'dir bud med smug nag dre'u la zhon pa
'jigs su rung ba zhig 'ongs nas/ nga'i dre'u la rtswa ster dgos zer ba la/ rtswa nga rang gi bong bu la dgos/ mi ster byas pas/ mo na re/ khyed dpon slob la bar chad gcig
yong ba 'dug pas/ ngas gcad nas dre'u rmig pa 'di ltar song shad 'ongs pa yin zer/ rtswa chug 'phog tu byung bas skad shor zer skad de bsten srung ma chen mo rdo rje brtan
ma 'di shin tu 'go ba yod snang / gung ru rgyal mtshan bzang po la mdo phyogs kyi gzhung mang po gsan zhing / khyad par dbu ma'i lta ba la bden grub bkag tsamagyi stong
nyid med dgag la mi bzhed par mtha' bral chen po'i lta ba bkral nas chad kyin 'dug pas thugs kyang mos pa byung / rje tsong kha pa'i dngos slob gzhan dang khyed cung 'chad
tshul mi mthun par 'dug pa ci lags zhus pas/ ngas rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i zhabs rdul yun ring du bsten nas gsung gi bdud rtsi myangs pa yin te/ de'i bar la ni dbu ma'i
lta ba 'di kho na gsung gin 'dug dngos slob gzhan dang 'chad tshul mi mthun pa 'dug ci yin ma shes gsung skad/ se rar chos gsan ring la 'bras spungs chos skyong gi cho
'phrul mang bar byung ste nub gcig mnal lam bzung nas rta mgrin zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i sku shin tu che ba gcig tu sprul nas btul bas 'bras spungs chos skyong des kyang
sku de 'dra zhig tu sprul

byung / de nas rje nyid kyis rta mgrin gyi sku zhabs 'og gzhi gser gyi sa gzhi la bsgrad pa dbu gzugs khams su snyeng nge ba gcig tu sprul pas khong gis kyang de bzhin sprul
byung / slar nyid kyi sku chung la rnam pa gsal ba yung 'bru dum bu bcur byas pa'i cha tsam gcig tu sprul te 'bras spungs chos skyong gi snying dkyil du bzhugs nas gzir
bas de ma thag skad ngan drag po shor te phyin chad rje nyid kyi slob brgyud tshun la bar chad mi byed pa'i bro phul ba yin gda'/ lar bskyed rim sgom pa rnams kyis phra
mo'i rnal 'byor la slob pa gal che ba 'dug gsung / yang nub gcig 'od gsal du dbus kyi lha 'dre thams cad kyi lte mnachad bye mas non 'dug nas/ ci byung ba yin dris pas/ khyed
kyi 'khrul 'khor byas pa'i rdul gyi nged tsho 'di 'drar gyur kyin 'dug zer skad/ de nas lha sar jo bo'i drung du smon lam mdzad nas zhwa lur phebs te chos grwa 'di dang
dga' ba gdong gnyis ka'i zur 'chad pa gnang nas rgyu mtshan nyid kyi theg pa'i chos 'khor rgya cher bskor/ /thams cad mkhyen pa grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi drung du bu
lugs kyi dbang bshad man ngag mtha' dag rdzogs par gsan/ gzhan yang snga phyir mkhas grub zla pa dpal rin/ mkhas mchog nor bzung rin chen/ mkhas pa dpal bzang ba rnams kyi
drung du gtso cher bu lugs/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang bo las sa lugs/ byang sems gzhon nu rgyal mchog las bka' gdams lugs/ grub dbang rin chen 'phel

las stod 'brug gi skor/ 'jam dbyangs chos dpal bzang po las shangs chos skor/ lce rdo rje sengge las phyag rdor gtum po sogs kyi skor/ dpal ri ba chos rgyal dpal bzang las
ni gu'i skor dang dpyal lugs phag mo skor gsum sogs/ grub chen mgon po rgyal mtshan las 'bro sgom ras pa nas brgyud pa'i nA ro chos drug dang sems khrid yid bzhin nor bu
sogs/ gnyag ston dar ma bzang po dang / ri ba chos grags gnyis lam gcig gi gcod skor sogs/ bla ma rong po blo bzang la sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor sogs/ bla ma don legs pa la
'od zer dri med dang bde chen ral gcig gi chos skor sogs/ rtogs ldan rnam grol zla ba la rta mgrin gyi skor sogs/ bla ma skal ldan grags pa la seng gdong ma'i skor sogs/
rgya gar gyi dzo ki dngos grub bzang po la gtum mo'i man ngag sogs gsan te snga phyir yongs su 'dril ba'i bla ma sum cur nye ba tshul bzhin du bsnyen par mdzad de mdo rgyud
chos kyi bang mdzod chen por gyur pa yin no/ de ltar thos bsam gyi sgro 'dogs chod/ da ni 'dzam bu'i gling gi gnas chen rnams su phyin la/ tshe dang sgrub pa mnyam pa
zhig bya'o dgongs pa na bla ma rnams kyi re zhig 'chad nyan byas na legs tshul dgongs/ de nas thams cad mkhyen pa grags pa'i mtshan can gdan sa gshol bu'i thugs 'dun gnang
nas/ dbus phebs phyi res kyi dus zhwa lur sang nyin phebs rgya'i do nub rje'i mnal lam du sengge chen po rgyan sna tshogs kyis spras pa gcig gi steng du/ rgyal po

chen po rnam thos sras kyi sku nyi ma'i snying po ltar 'bar zhing 'ong zer 'phro ba gcig gi mdun na rje btsun grags pa'i zhabs 'khor rta ba mang pos bskor ba 'byon pa'i sna
la mi dkar po gcig gis gdugs dkar po nor bu'i tog can rin po che'i rgyan can zhig khyer nas nam mkha' la ye rer 'ong zhing 'dug zhwa lu ba'i dge 'dun rnams kyang bsu ba
la 'byon gyin 'dug pa phyag 'tshal gdong gi thad tsam du slebs dus mi dkar po de na re gdugs 'di sus 'dzin/ sus 'dzin zer ba la/ gzhan 'dzin zer mkhan ni mi 'dug rje nyid
kyi ngas bzung chog ces nam mkha' la 'phur nas gdugs de bzung bas phangs shin tu mtho bar slebs te thugs la/ mdo ngag las shing ta la bdun srid du 'phags te zhes pa'ang
'di 'dra la zer rgyur 'dug snyam pa 'khrungs/ de yang gdan sa 'di yod pa'i ltas su gda' gsung zhing mi dkar po de ni spyan ras gzigs su nges so/ /de dus zhwa lu ba kun gdan
sa su la yong ngam zhes gleng zhing / 'ga' zhig nas paNDi ta sangs rgyas bzang po zer ba'i rgya gar ba zhig pra 'bebs su bcug nas dge bshes chen po rnams kyi mtshan smos
te 'di dang 'di la yong ngam zhes dris pas/ phal cher la lus la skyon chags pas mi yong zer/ 'ga' zhig sems bzang po mi 'dug pas mi yong zer/ 'o na su la yong ba 'dug
dris pas/ ming smos pa 'di dag ma yin pas/ sa ma dhi pA la phA la can gcig la yong zer/ the tshom du gyur nas grwa pa

dbus su yang 'phros gleng byung dus rje nyid kyis bkyal ka'i tshul du gdan sa gzhan su la yong / khyed tsho'i mgo la nga'i lag pa 'jog pa yin mod gsung ste/ de skabs rtsed
mo mdzad par go yang rjes su thugs mkhyen gsungs par 'dug ces gleng / de nas rje nyid kyi dgung lo zhe gnyis pa lcags sprel lo/ /hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i tshes gcig la bra
brang nas gdan sa'i 'os kyi ming 'phel byed pas thams cad bla brang du 'dus shog ces pa'i brda byung bas phebs te/ der ston chen bzang po'i thog thams cad mkhyen pa grags
pa'i zhabs kyi bka' lung mang po stsal ba'i mthar/ rje nyid bzhugs gral gyi mtha' tsam na bzhugs pa spyan 'bru tshugs su gzigs te/ btsun gnas dpon po 'di la thams cad mkhyen
pa yab sras kyi byin rlabs 'jug gzhan phan 'phrin las che ba yong zer ba byung bas tshes drug gi nyin bsko bzhag byed pas 'di la sus 'gal rkyen byas pa de rang gi mgo
la rang gis chu drangs pa yin no gsung ba'i bka' bskyur byung / de 'phral rtab rtobs su bzhengs nas phyag phul te/ gdan sa mi pher ba'i rgyu mtshan gsol rtsis gnang bas/
mkhas grub nor bzang rin chen sogs gral mgor bzhugs pa'i dge bshes thams cad mgrin gcig tu gsung shed chen pos/ khyod kyis ci yang mi shes sdod sdod ces bkag nas ci yang
gsung rgyu ma byung bar zhal spobs lus/ da ni sde chen po 'di 'dra'i khur 'khyer ba mi yong bas gnas mchog dpal gyi rtsa ri tra la bros nas mi la ras pa 'dra

ba zhig bya dgos dgongs te de nub yab kyi sgrub gnas dga' ldan dgon par phebs/ sang tho rangs snga mor thegs rtsis kyis sku khres tshun chad khyer chog yod pa la/ chos skyong
gi cho 'phrul du mtshan mo de la kha ba chen po mi srid pa zhig babs nas tho rangs 'byon ma thub cing / nam langs pa dang kha ba chod mi chod spyil bu'i steng nas gzigs
su phebs pas/ rje rang gi slob dpon mkhas mchog rin chen tshul khrims zhu ba'i bgres po de nyid/ de na yar tshegs chen pos phebs te mjal ma thag spyan chab 'don pa tsam
gyi bka' nan chen pos thugs bcun nas zhwa lung 'khrid par mdzad do/ zla ba de kha'i tshes drug gi nyin yongs kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams dang bstan pa'i sbyin bdag sku
zhang rnam rgyal dpal bzang sogs kyi spos sna dang bcas te khri thog tu spyan drangs nas chos kyi rgyal thabs su dbang bsgyur ro/ /tshes brgyad kyi nyin ri phug tu thams
cad mkhyen pa grags pa'i zhags kyi sgos kyi gnang sbyin mdzad nas bka' las/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa chen po'i gdan sa 'di mkhas btsun bzang gsum du rlom pa mang po
zhig gis ma thob pa ma gtogs mi 'dod pa med pa gcig yin te/ khyed la bla ma rnams kyi byin rlabs 'jug par 'dug pas gtang ba yin no/ 'di 'dra mi pher snyam pa'i sdug bsngal
bya mi dgos/ chos sde 'di la yo 'khyoms chen po byung na ma gtogs gzhan 'jig rten gyi bya ba rnams bka' gros

la dbang ba'i mi bcu bzhi rkang yang ba gnyis dang bcas pa byed du bcug nas 'jig rten la kha mi 'jug par rang re dbyar dgun gyi chos ma chag par 'chad pa gal che/ gzhan gzhis
byes kyi 'dod chos zhu mkhan byung na yang rtsol pa bskyed nas byed pa gal che/ de ltar byas pas tshe sgrub tu'ang 'gro zhing khri thogs 'dir slebs phyin chad longs spyod
kyi 'phongs pa mi 'byung ba yin no/ /gsung ba sogs bka' slob dpag med mdzad cing de skabs dus 'khor lha khang du zhag gnyis gzims pa'i mnal 'od gsal du 'pho thub pa sogs
byung ngo / /de nas dbyar chos ma 'dzugs tsam gyi nyi shu gcig gi nub mo lho phyogs kyi nam mkha' la 'phur byon pa na ri bo gcig gi rtser khang pa mang po 'dug pa'i nang
nas bud med dmar mo zhig byung ste/ re zhig 'dir bzhugs mdzad nged la chos 'brel zhig kyang dgos zer/ rje nyid kyi nged dbyar chos 'chad dgos pas sdod pa'i long med gsung
nas 'phur byon pa na bud med na re/ da 'o na kun rdzob byang chub kyi sems ma nyams par cis kyang mdzod/ khyed la rnam pa thams cad du legs po 'ong gi zer ba dang /
yang zhag 'ga' nas bud med gcig gis rnam pa thams cad du gri thod dang ma bral ba gyis zer te/ gri gug shes rab dang / thod pa thabs mtshon pas thabs shes dang ma bral bar
gyis ze ba 'dug gsung / gzhan yang dbyar chos kyi dus thod dbyug dang ma bral ba gyis zer ba gcig kyang rmis te stong nyid snying rje ya ma bral bar bsgom dgos pa'i brdar
'dug gsung / nub gcig chos rje

thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston chen po bzhugs pa'i sku mdun du dkyil 'khor gcig bris pa'i khar khri bshams pa la rje nyid bzhugs su bcug /sku phang du phod kha/ rus rgyan/ gri
thod/ kha TaM ka sogs sngags chas sna tshogs shig gtad/ mdun du mchod pa sna lnga gcig kyang bshams/ sder kha'i tshul du zhib zan dkar mos bkang ba bcug gsum btang nas gsang
sngags dang / rigs sngags dang gzung sngagasakyi gzhi thams cad khyod la gtad do/ /zhes gsungs nas chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa khang pa'i steng du gshegs/ dge 'dun
mang pos rje nyid la me tog gtor zhing gong gi tshig de yang yang skyor nas ngo mtshar du mdzad pa zhig rmis gsung / de skabs zang zang ne rings pa'i gdan sa pa gcig thams
cad mkhyen pa grags pa'i zhabs la bsnyen rdzogs zhu bar byon nas/ rje nyid la las slob byed dgos par 'dug pas sang snga mor 'dir phebs mdzod gsung ba'i bka' shog gnang
/ der go sa'i stabs kyi mkhan po ma gtogs las slob sogs byed dgos yong bsam pa med pas sngar lasakyi cho ga thugs la bzung ba ni med/ mi yong zhus pas ni ma byung bar de
nub gzim mal sku 'dra rin po che'i drung du mchod pa bshams legs bshad rgya mtsho kun mkhyen bu sto nadrung / /zhes sogs bston pa shlau ka bco brgyad lhag tsam 'phral du
brtsams nas gsol pa phur tshugs su btab ste las chog dpe cha de tshar gcig bsgrags/ tho rangs mnal lam bzung ste

dpe de tshar gcig bklags shing de nas thugs bsam tsam yang ma btang bar nam lang ma thag las grul du phebs/ las slob kyi brjod pa mtha' dag sngar sbyangs sbyangs pa rnams las
kyang byang pa tshig zur gcig tsam yang ma 'khrul ma chad par thon byung ste da ni thams cad mkhyen pa chen po'i thugs kyi byin rlabs dngos su zhugs pa yin zhes gsung
ste/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa la gsol ba 'debs nus na byin rlabs 'phral du 'jug pa'i phan yon de tsam yod ces rang cag rnams la 'doms pa'i tshig go/ de dus khams mi nyag
gis zhwa lur bar byed 'phrin ngan la brten zhwa lu bas dmag byas te/ chos sdings bcoms pas sde gzar chen po g.yos te thabs gang gi sgo nas kyang ma 'dum ste/ rje nyid
kyi bka' las/ khams pa rnams la gtam ci tsam lab kyang go ba mi len 'dug/ rang re chos pa rnams kyi re ltos/ nus bla ma dkon mchog dang mkha' 'gro chos skyong min pa gzhan
med/ khyod grwa pa rnams kyis dam can chos rgyal la gtor ma phul te 'phrin las bcol mdzod gsung / zhwa lu chos sde pas drug cu pa'i gtor ma bsgrubs te gtor rdzong byed
pa na dgra phyogs kyi khams pa gcig chos skyong gi bkug pa bzhin ltad mo la yong pas dmar gtor chen po sha khrag gis brgyan pa de mthong ma thag tu sna khrag 'byams/ de
nas gom pa bdun bor ba'i sa de nyid du khrag skyugs te tshe'i dus byas/ gzhan yang dus phyis zhwa lur sku rim la dgongs re bzhin drag gtor re mdzad pas/ dar rgyas pa rnams
kyis zhwa lu ba'i btsun pa'i gtor

ma ka 'dra/ rnam pa zan pa ma gtogs dgos pa gang yang mi 'byung zer 'phyar kha btang ba rje'i snyan du thebs pas/ ngas spyir sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa sgos chos sde 'di snying
rje chen pos zhi ba'i sgo nas bskyangs dgos snyam pa ma gtogs 'jam dpal gshin rje gshed kyi las sbyor brtsams na tshangs pa brgya byin sogs kyang sgrol mi thub pa ma yin/
lar de tsam du ma song na kho pa rang la bzlog rim gyis zer ba'i lon thong / rtags en tsam zhig bstan gyis gsungs nas drug cu pa'i gtor ma gcig bsdebs par mdzad pas/
dar rgyas pa'i mi do gcig shi/ gzhan 'od dang thog 'tsheg khyi ngu ba sogs cho 'phrul sna tshogs byung ste slar gser gangul dang na bza' sogs 'bul ba rgya chen po byas te/
'gyod bshags mi 'bul ka med byung ngo / de rjes rin spungs chos rgyal nor bu bzang pos zangs dkar du spyan 'dren byung nas tho rangs rdo skas la phebs tshe sgro'i skad
lta bu shob shob chen po gcig byung pa sku 'khor rnams kyi thos/ ci yin nam zhu ba la jo mo ri phug mas nga bsgril gyi dogs skyor gyin 'dug pa'i rma bya'i sgro thul gyi skad
yin gda'/ khyed chos tshang ma gsung / zangs dkar du phebs te chos rgyal chen po de nyid la gshed dmar gyi dbang bka' sogs chos mang ba gnang pas mi phyed pa'i dad pa
brtan po thob/ de nas bzungs mchod yon thugs yid gcig 'dres su gyur pa yin te/ sde pa rin spungs pa'i gdung rabs mkhas pa dkar shag gi mdad pa las/ |'chad

pa tshangs dbyangs 'brug sgra nges/ /blo gsal char 'dod bye'u yi/ /yi rangs padmo rgyas par byed/ /rtsod pa lung rigs rdo rje yis/ /lta ngan brag ri gshig par nus/ /rtsom pa
snyan dngags nor bu yis/ /shes ldan mgul ba mdzes byed cing / /chos kyi 'byor pas phyug pa yi/ /mkhas btsun tshul khrims rgyal mtshan de/ /yun ring bar du yang yang bsten/
/bka' lung man ngag rgya chen po/ /ngoms pa med par gus pas gsan/ /zhes 'byung ba ltar ro/ /sde pas 'brong sgang du spyan drangs dus lkugs lung sgrub chen ma bya ba'i
grub pa brnyes pa'i rnal 'byor ma gcig yod pa de na re/ sang 'brog sgang du grub chen ku ku ri pa phebs par 'dug /nga ni mjal du 'gro khyed tsho e 'gro gsung / der rnying
ma'i gter ston ayon kun skyong gling pa yang mjal bar phebs nas rje nyid kyi sku skye snga phyi'i lung bstan slob dpon padma'i shog ser gyi nang nas byung ba'i lo rgyus
zhus shing shog dril phul/ ri phug tu gsung chos mang po gnang dus/ rtsa ri nas bla ma rtsa san pa dpon slob rnams 'bras mo ljongs su gnas sgo 'byed par 'gro rtsis kyi lam
zhor du rje'i sku gzhogs su 'byor nas 'bras mo ljongs su slebs mi slebs brtag pa zhus pas/ rje nyid kyi zhal nas/ 'bras mo ljongs kyi lung pa de mthong ba tsam yong /
gzhan nang du mi sleb pa 'dug ces bka' stsal/ khong rnams kyis phyin pas ri rtse zhig nas lung ba de'i dbyigs legs par mthong / da lung sa ni chod/ lam rgyus ni yod/ sngar
'phros yul du log nas 'gro mkhan gzhan 'dug na 'khrid do zer phyir log pas

gangs chen po babs te mthar ba yin 'dug lo/ /rin spungs pa dang nyang stod shar kha ba sogs sde pa yas phyin ma cham pa'i dmag dpung rnams snang gsal dang grong stod du tshogs
nas rdo sgyogs 'phen res byas pas/ mi dang dud 'gro mang po kha dag la gtong pa la rje nyid thugs brtse bar gyur te/ zhwa lu chos sde'i las sna khag la bka' gnang nas/
rang re dge 'dun rnams kyis byu rgyu'i gtso bo sems can gyi don yin pas/ sde pa yos phyin gyi 'khrug 'dum la 'gro ba'i stalta gon gyis gsung / zhwa lu tshogs chen gyi chos
dung tshogs khro sogs sgar chas su mdzad nas grwa chen btegs pa'i dge 'dun na bza' ngur smrig can gyi sa dang nam mkha'i mdangs 'phrogs pa lta bu byung zhing / rgyan
gong gi thad tsam nas dpal ldan lha mo'ang dre'u chen po 'jigs su rung ba zhig la zhon pa'i zhal gcig phyag bzhi ma rgyan cha lugs thams cad re ma tai ji lta ba bzhin byas
nas phebs pa rje rin po che nas dngos su gzigs/ grong stod kyi thad du dge 'dun rnams kyi bzhugs sgar btab/ chos dung btang nas nyi ma kha yar bar chibs mdzad kyang / rin
spungs nas da nga rang gri yul du sdod pa la de 'dra'i 'jug sgo med gsung shin tu 'grig dka' ba la/ snga dro gcig rje nyid kyi khra mde phyag tu bsnams nas/ da len khra
ma 'di la phyag dam gnang bzhud de/ sde pa rin spungs pa'i bstan pa yar 'phel yong rabs khas len pa'i lan gsungs pas/ de ma thag chos rgyal nor bu bzang po bzhengs nas
rje nyid la phyag 'tshal khra ma la

phyag dam mdzad/ yig mkhan gcig la rje'i zhal snga nas bka' lung gnang ba de yi ger bris gsung / de la thugs dam zhus pas phyis de kho na bzhin byung ngo / de dus dmag rnams
kyi dbus su khri chen po bshams te rje nyid nas las rgyu 'bras kyi gsung chos mang po gnang bas thams cad ma rungs pa'i sems zhi nas dad pa'i gnas la bkod/ dge 'dun rnams
kyang bzhugs sgar gyi mtha' la dre'u'i rmig rjes rkyang khru re yod pas bskor ba kun gyis mthong bas ya mtshan du gyur/ ri phug tu phebs pa'i skabs shig la slob dpon gzhon
nu ba bsnyungs nas mo rtsis la grong sgra 'debs dgos pa shar nas/ bla brang du bsngo zhus phul bas rje nyid nas kyang chog gnang ste bar do'i rnam shes 'gugs pa'i tshe/
slob dpon pa khag ste bzhengs nas nga la bla brang du da ltar shog gsung 'dug zer nas shor 'gro ba byung zhing / rje nyid nas nye gnas la slob dpon khong ma grongs 'dug
pa gsungs/ grongs yod mchis mod zhus pas/ rnam shes bkug dus gson po'i rnam par byung ma grongs 'dug gsung pa dang / yang slob dpon rin tshul ba sku gshegs dus nye gnas
la nga'i rus pa 'di bsreg sbyor bla brang du zhus la snam skar 'di'ang phul/ pur la rtags ma byung bar ma reg ces zhal chems'chams mdzad/ nye gnas kyi bla brang du de bzhin
snyan gsan phab ste snam sbyar pur la g.yogs nas zla ba gcig song song sgug kyang rtags ci yang ma byung / rje nyid la bsam rtse nas gdan 'dren byung bas/ nub gcig 'od
gsal du slob dpon rin tshul ba snam sbyar

sku la bzhes nas rje'i sku mdun du byon te/ bdag zhag zhe dgu'i bar du dge sbyor gcig la bsdang bsam kyang / rje rin po che phyogs phebs la thugs ring ba 'dug cing / rgyal
rdor kho yang 'u 'thug 'dug pas da bdag gis 'gro bzhu zer/ nye gnas la pur rtags byung yod ltos dang gsungs pas shangs nas byang sems dkar po zags 'dug zer ro/ dus phyis
bsam sdongs su bzhugs skabs lcog ro dan phug gi mchod rten gyi nang na tshe chu'i gter yod pa mkhan nas mnal lam bzung ste nam mkha' la 'phur nas gzigs su phebs pas/ dan
phug lha mo rta pa dpon g.yog lnga bud med gzhon nu ma rin po che sna tshogs pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i rtsam bar byas te dbus ma de'i lag tu tshe bum khyer nas tshe chu
'di yin lags te slob dpon padmas khyed la phul gsung ba ni med lags zer/ 'o na phar skyol gsungs pas mchod rten gyi bum pa la thims mo zhes gsungs/ de la sogs de ngo mtshar
ba'i lo rgyus mang ste 'dir de tsam las ma spros shing / mdor na chos gsung ba'i rnam thar ni phyis su sku khams shin tu bsnyel ba'i skabs re tsam ma gtogs sku mtshams
kyi dus na yang skal ba dang ldan pa rnams rjes su bzung ste/ sku tshe ringrings ltapo dbang bshad man ngag mtha' dag gi chos 'khor rgyun mi chad par bskor ba mdzad/ rtsod
pa mdzad pa'i tshe na lta ba ngan pa rnams sun byung ste yang dag pa'i lta ba la dkri ba mdzad/ rtsom pa mdzad pa'i tshe

mkhas pa rnams mgu ba bskyed pa'i legs bshad kho na 'byung ste/ de yang mngon pa mdzod kyi TIkka/ dbu ma rigs tshogs kyi TIkka/ byams chos phyi ma bzhi rnams la rnam bshad
re re mdad pa yod ces grags la/ rgyud sde rnams kyi sgrub dkyil bla ma yi dam gyi bstod tshigs/ nyams mgur sogs bka' 'bum mthar chags su bsgrigs thub na po ti du ma longs
pa yod tshul 'dug kyang / dus der bka' bsdu mkhan ma byung ba zhig gam/ phyis su ni dpe rgyun shin tu dkon no/ dgung lo drug cu re brgyad bzhes pa'i tshe zhwa lu ba'i che
'gres rnams la nged kyang na so rgas/ nam 'chi cha mi 'dug pas nged rang yod thog la gdan sa ba gcig bkod dgos pas de'i bka' gros mdzad gsungs/ der thams cad kyi phyag
kyang 'gyel ba ltar btsal nas de 'dra bka' mi stsol bar gsol ba btab kyang ma 'grub par gdan sa'i 'os 'thus shig ces pas bka' nan lci ba phebs te 'os bsdus shing grwa dmangs
kyi 'os rnams las mang shos gcig dang / shar chen ye shes rgya mtsho'i 'os gcig dang / rje nyid kyis 'os gcig te gsum po'i ming gser bum du bcug nas the'u tshe mnan/
nub gcig gsol ba btab pa'i sang nyin gser bum dkrogs pas kun mkhyen chos grub dpal bzang po'i mtshan thog mar 'thon te/ tshes bcu'i nyin bsko bzhag byed rgyal khong gar song
cha med du bros/ dge 'dun thams cad thugs khral du gyur kyang rje'i zhal nas/ khyed rnams sems khral mi 'tshal/ tshes bdun gyi nyin mo bstan bsrung

ma chen mo rang nas bkug yong ba yod gsung / de kho na bzhin khong la yang zhabs la sgrog bcug pa ltar gyur nas bros kyang mthar bar log 'byon dgos pa byung ste gdan sa gtad
do/ de nas yab bka' bzhi pa'i zhal gzigs kyi mgon po phyag drug pa'i bris thang gcig dang bcu gcig gzhal gyi gser sku gcig ma gtogs dngos po gzhan ci yang ma bsnams par
parnam bsam lding du mkhan btsun gzhon nu grub kyi gdan sa bskyangs shing der bshad sgrub gnyis ka mdzad/ dus res 'ga' nyams dbyangs kyi tshul du/ ye shes dwangs chos kyi
pho brang na/ /kun gzhi stong nyid mthong grol sangs rgyas bzhugs/ /thar mchog ya mtshan can gcig de na gda'/ /rnam dag phyag macod re ru phul na legs/ /zhes sogs legs
ma bdun ldan gyi mgur dang / spyir rgyan 'dogs la rnam pa mang por gda'o/ /'jig rten 'khrul pa'i rgyan cha phyi nas 'dogs/ /rnal 'byor gyis sems rgyan zhing chas 'dogs/ rgyan
'dogs kyi rnam pa 'di ltar lags/ /snang ba phyogs med shar pa phyi yi rgyan/ /rig pa 'dzin med grol ba nang gi rgyan/ /phyogs med mtha' dbus bral ba gsang ba'i rgyan/
/de gsum rnal 'byor nga'i lta ba'i rgyan/ /lta legs mkhan thar pa rnams ci dgyes mdzod/ /rang sems lta ba rtogs pas skyid par gda'/ /rang sems lta ba rtogs pas bde bar
gda'/ /zhes sogs lta bsgom spyod 'bras kyi nyams dbyangs sogs du ma mdzad do/ /lan gcig rin spungs nor

bzang sku khams ma bde bar skyabs 'jug dang brtag pa dgos zhu ba'i mi sna byung la bka' las/ sngar yin na rmi lam bzung nas yul snang la ji lta ba yong ba yin te/ da rmi lam
ma zin ma thag 'od gsal du shor 'gro ba gda'/ 'on kyang mnga' zhabs kyi phyed sbyin par btang na sku tshe bsring nus pa tsam 'dug ste/ de lta bu ni dka' pas gzhan thabs
mi 'dug phebs/ de sogs mngon mkhyen thogs pa mi mnga' yang / mnal lam la byung ba lta bu mdzad nas lung ston pa las byung rgyal du mi gsung / dgung lo bdun cu bzhes pa'i
tshe gshin gson gyi dad 'bul byung ba'i dngos po rnams la gzhi byas te zhwa lu ri phug tu dus mchod chen mo'i skabs dge 'dun stong phrag phyed gnyis la bsnyen bkur zhag
lnga dad 'bul 'gyed bcas gya nom pa gnang zhing / bu ston bka' 'bum rags bsdus par du brko ba bzhed nas dka' bcu don 'grub bkra shis ming bkra'i khyad lho ka bzhi'i yon bdag
rnams kyi sar 'bul sdud la mngags shing rje nyid kyi sde dpon la lar bka' shog phyag mdud sogs stsal/ po ti kha cig par du bzhengs grub mtshams su sku khams cung zad
mnyel bas/ de gsung par 'di dag par brkos ma tshar ring tshe'i rten 'brel bsgrigs dgos pa 'dug gsungs nas dbon bkra shis mgon pos tshe dpag med kyi bris thang bzhengs pa'i
bkod pa mdzad/ de dus zhwa lu nas gos chen gyi zhabs phyags hag se gcig 'bul mkhan btang bar slebs pas nga'i tshe'i rten 'brel bsgrig dus lham gog te 'khyer byung / kho
rang gi mgo la gcig rgyob la phyir bskyur

gsung yang de ltar byed nus pa ma byung / bka' las ngas thams cad mkhyen pa'i bka' 'bum rags rim par brkos ma grub par bsdad snyam yang sems can spyi mthun gyi las dang sgos
zhwa lu pa'i skal ba de tsam du zad do gsung / slar zhwa lu nas mkhan chen gdan sa pas mtshon dge 'dun bgres pa rags bsdus pebs nas brtan bzhugs rgyas par phul te gsol
ba btab pas/ khyed rang rnams zla ba 'di ma tshes bar sdod/ de nas thag chad cing yod pa yod ces bka' gnang yang bzhugs pa ma shar/ lan cig rje'i zhal nas mdangs nga'i rmi
lam na/ bka' bzhi ba mchog grub dpal 'bar gyi lha'i gdan yin zer ba gsang pa cig dang rnying pa gcig ste gnyis btings nas/ zhing khams gzhan na gdul bya che na gdan gsar
pa 'di la bzhugs pa zhu/ zhing 'di ka gdul bya che na rnying pa 'di la bzhugs pa zhu zer gyin 'dug pa la/ ngas gdan gsar pa de la bsdad pa rmis gsung / der khong rnams
kyis dus pas ad ta ku re byas pa yin gdan rnying pa de la bsdad gsung / yang skabs shig thugs mnyam bzhag la dum gcig bzhugs nas/ sangs rgyas kyi chos 'khor gsum po dus gcig
la bskor zer ba yang blor mi shong rgyu mi 'dug /ngas da ci bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje 'khor lo chen po dang / dus 'khor/ bde mchog /gshed dmar rnams kyi dkyil 'khor
dwangs gsal rnyogs med go

sa gcig na rnam pa tha dad du 'dug kyang phan tshun sgrib pa dang bral ba sa le ba rnams kyi nang du bzhugs te dbang bzhi rdzogs pa dkyil 'khor de rnams su gcig car du thob
gsung / yang lan gcig da lta rang mchod pa bzang po bshoms shig/ ngas zhi mtha' cung zad yid la byas pas rje btsun spyan ras gzigs sogs yi dam gyi lta thams cad byon nas/
bu khyod dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sras yin pas/ 'gro kun phan bde'i lam la 'god pa'i go cha che dgos pa la/ de lta bu'i blo ma bskyed cig gsung gin 'dug gsung
/ yang nub gcig da lta nga'i mdun 'di na rje btsun sgrol dkar bzhugs pa'i thugs ka na/ oM tA re tu ttA re ma ma shI la dhwa dza A yuHpuShTiM ku ru ye sAhA/ ces pa'i sngags
'phreng 'khor lo dang bcas pa skya bram me bdug gsung / der phyag phyi bdag gi 'o na da len sku tshe brtan par yong lags sam zhus pas/ de ma yin 'dug sngar bzlas sgom
'dra byas par/ rje btsun mas dbugs dbyung mdzad pa tsam yin 'dug gsung/ yang snga dro gcig mdangs mgon po tshe dpag med 'khor bcas nam mkhar lan gsum byon nas rigs kyi bu
zhing 'di'i bya rdzogs zin pas da bde ba can du 'gro gsung gin 'dug ste/ ngas ma phyin gsung / der gzims dbon byang chub chos ldan gyis/ 'o na 'di nas zhing khams gang du
phebs/ bdag cag rnams gsol ba gang du 'debs zhus pas/ nga 'di nas dga' ldan du rje btsun byams pa dang / rgyal ba rin chen grub kyi spyan sngar sher phyin gyi mdo dang
/ rgyud sde rnams kyi don la som nyi'i

dra ba yod pa rnams bsal te sangs rgyas kyi don gyi bstan pa 'dzin pa yin no gsung / gzims dpon gyi yid la rje nyid zhi bar gshegs na 'di dang 'di byed dgos snyam pa'i rnam
rtogs ngan pa 'ga' zhig 'gyus pa thugs kyis mkhyen nas/ en ma bzang ma bza de 'dra'i bsam blo ngan pa gtong pa min/ nga shi ba'i mjug tu 'di ltar gyis gsung ba'i zhal bkod
mang po mdzad/ zhwa lur mang ja gral 'gyed kyi thog mkhan slob dge 'dun spyi la zhal chems kyi rdo rje'i bka' shog stsal ba 'di ltar/ bla ma dang dkon mchog gsum la phyag
'tshal lo/ /mkhan chen gdan sa pas thog drangs/ zhwa lu sde dgon gyi dge 'dun drag zhan rnams kyi dgongs rgyu la/ rang re'i chos sde 'dir rtsod dus kyi thams cad mkhyen
pa bu ston rin po ches phyag phab/ mdo rgyud man ngag thams cad kyi bstan pa'i srol chen btsugs/ bod khams kyi gdul byar gyur pa thams cad phan bde'i lam bzang po la bkod
pa nas bzung ste/ sems dpa' chen po yab sras kyi bar/ sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa'i rnam thar lta bu bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung ba de lags/ de rjes nged kyis kyang gzhon
nu nas rab byung byas thos bsam gyi sgo nas rig pa'i gnas lnga la gang shes kyi slob 'dun dang / man ngag rnams la'ang nyams len rnal 'byor la gang brtson byas pas bla
ma rnams kyis rjes su 'dzin cing byin gyis brlabs pa dang / khyad par rdo rje btsun mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal

bzang pos thugs brtse bas bskyangs pa'i bka' lung khur che ba dang du blangs te phyogs lhung dang nye ring spangs/ 'jig rten gyi bya ba la kha ma bcug dge sbyor ci 'phel gyi
ngos nas sdug sran bskyed pas/ mi mthun phyogs kyis ma tshugs bar lo nyi shu rtsa drug gi bar du chos sde'ang mar 'grib med tsam byung ba de yin/ da mkhan chen gdan sa
bas kyang 'jig rten gyi bya las rnams/ khong rang las sne na yod pa rnams sngar lugs bzhin khur 'khyer du bcug rang re dbyar chos dgun chos ma chag par byas/ ri phug tu dge
sbyor gang 'phel byas na thams cad la mdzes khyabs che zhing / tshe gnas pa'i thabs su'ang 'gro ba lags nged kyang na so rgas/ nam 'chi mi shes par 'dug pas/ rang la sems
pa'i cha rkyen sen sen byung ba rnams sbyin bdag gi rdzas chud zos med tsam du byung rim gyis dge phyogs su btang bas 'gyod med kyi lugs lags da lta bem rig ma bral tsam
yod na'ang / der bsnyen bkur dang bcas pas mtshon 'di dge ba'i rtsa pa sngon 'gro dngos gzhi'i sku skal 'dus dgu chen mo lags so/ /de bstun bsam sdings su'ang nyin gang
tsam ma gtogs rgya chen gshoms pa'i cha rkyen med pas de lugs kyi dmigs bsal bslab bya'i bkod pa byas yod/ rjes su bu slob sbyin bdag rnams kyis phyi rten nang rten gyi
bkod gshoms byed pa'i srol 'dug na'ang ri phug bla brang 'du khang dang bcas pa 'di 'og min chos kyi pho brang dang 'dra bas/ bcos rnams legs par byas pa 'di lha khang
dang mchod rten re

tsam bzhengs pa las phan yon che zhing lhag bsam pa yod pas des tshang ba bdog go/ dus mchod sogs gzhi rten med pas gshoms pa'ang ma 'dug cing / yod na yang nam zhugs las byed
la la'i nor sogs snyoms chung la la rtsa phud la 'gro ba'i kha gsag gzhogs slong khrag pa tsir rnag tsir gyi rnam pas dge 'dun la'ang 'tsho ba rnam dag tu 'gro shas chung
ba 'dug med pa dang mi dgos pa mthun gda'/ spyir yang gsung gi rten bzhengs pa byin rlabs dang bsod nams che/ khyad par thams cad mkhyen pa chen po'i gsung 'bum rnams

yin mchis/ blo las su rung na/ mi res par shin bcu pa re'i khur bsnams na'ang las sla ba'i rigs su 'dug ste/ de bzhin 'grub shas chung ba 'dug pas phyag rgya chen po'i ngang
la zhog thongs/ gzhan rten bzhengs sogs kyi dge ba rgya che che las par po ti gnyis 'di yang bstan pa'i rgyun dang 'phrin las gzhan phan che zhing byin rlabs che bar

/ don la shar chen ye shes rgya mtsho'i bu chen gyi gtso bo yin pa dang / rnam 'byor rgyud kyi skor phal che ba zhwa lu ba'i phyag len ji lta ba bzhin mdzad pas/ sa zhal
