gu ru thod 'phreng rtsal dang / 'phags pa'i yul gyi rig 'dzin shri sidha zhes la sogs su sprul zhing / bod kyi sa char yab sna nam rdo rje bcud 'joms/ bla ma gnam kha'u
pa/ chos rje bla

ma dam pa sogs kyi skye brgyud bstan mthar/ dus 'dir thon mi saMbho Ta'i gdung rgyud yab rgyal ba shes rab dang / yum dpal ldan rdo rje bde ma zhes bya ba gnyis kyi sras su
gyur te/ lhums su bzhugs pa'i tshe yab yum la lta bu gzhon nu rin po che'i tog gis spras pa'i rgyal mtshan lag tu khyer ba drung du byung ste bdag la gnas g.yar zhes pa
dang / nyi ma shar ba dang gsung rab kyi khri la 'dug pa sogs rmis so/ /de nas chu pho byi ba'i lo smin drug zla ba'i tshes bco brgyad kyi tho rangs g.yo ru grwa'i rgyal
chen gling du bltams so/ /de dus rim gral gzungs grwa lnga sgrogs pas mtshan yang grwa lnga rgyal po zhes gsol/ rtsed mo'i rnam pa yang chos 'chad pa dang gtor sgrub/ bgegs
bskrod tshul dang lhag par dkon mchog gi rten mchod gshom tshul 'ba' zhig mdzad/ 'dri klog sogs tshegs chung ngus mkhyen cing / yum de'i thugs la 'jig rten gyi srid skyong
ba zhig yong ngam dgongs te/ skye bo gso thigs/ sa skya legs bshad/ mi chos gnad 'phreng sogs 'jig rten lugs kyi bstan bcos sna tshogs slob tu bcug pa na/ bka' mi bcag
pa'i phyir du gzigs shing lkog tu bde bar gshegs pa'i gsung rab dgongs 'grel dang bcas pa la gzigs/ dgung lo bcu gsum pa la yum gyi dgongs lhur mdzad de sne'u gdong du
phebs/ gong ma grags pa 'byung gnas kyi yar rgyab dpon chen gyi las kha gnang zhing / rim pas dgung lo bco lnga la gzhis ka gong dkar gyi rdzong

dpon mdzad/ rgyal srid chos bzhin du skyong ba dang / btsun mo khab tu bzhes te rigs kyi sras bskrun pa sogs phyi rol du bstan zhing / nang du 'di dag gi skabs su yang thos
bsam sgom gsum las mi g.yel ba kho na mdzad/ dgung lo nyi shu pa la brag thog ba bsod nams bzang po'i drung du yongs rdzogs dge bsnyen dang / rab tu 'byung ba la thugs shin
tu ring yang / yum gyi dgongs pa cung zad ma khrol bas bar ma rab byung tsam bsgrubs/ dgung lo nyer bdun pa la byams pa gling pa paN chen bsod nams rnam par rgyal ba'i
drung du dge tshul gyi sdom pa mnos/ mtshan kun dga' rnam rgyal zhes btags phyis rim gyis dgung lo bzhi bcu rtsa gsum pa la sngar gyi mkhan po byams gling pa de nyid dang
/ mkhan chen rab 'byor sengge bas las slob chos rje nam mkha' lhun bzung bas gsang ston sogs mdzad de/ dad pa'i dge 'dun grangs tshar ba'i dbus su dge slong gi dngos po
brnyes bar mdzad la/ snga phyir chos gsan pa'i bla ma ni gong du smos pa brag thogs pa sogs las sa lugs ci skor/ byams gling pa las dus 'khor dang rig gnas skor/ shar chen
ye shes rgya mtsho las bu lugs kyi skor gtso bor gsan cing / gzhan yang dus zhabs pa don grub kun dga'/ dpal nags kyi rin chen/ zhwa lu mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs grags
rgyal/ snye mdo sngags 'chang shAkya dpal sogs bla ma nyi shu rtsa bzhi gus pa chen pos mnyes par mdzad nas/ bstan pa yongs rdzogs kyi bdag por gyur to/ /khyad par shar chen
thams cad mkhyen pa

ye shes rgya mtsho'i drung du bde mchog lU mi ba'i dbang sogs bka' nyi shur nye ba gsan cing / shar chen nyid kyis mdzad pa'i de kho na nyid bcu'i snying po gsal bar byed pa
legs par bshad pa'i sgron me zhes bya ba'i steng nas bshad pa dpyis phyin par gsan te/ mdor na rnal 'byor rgyud kyi skor gyi phyag khrid/ gar dbyangs/ thig sogs ma tshang
ba med par bum pa gang byo'i tshul du nos/ chos bka' tshar ba dang slob dpon rin po ches/ da ni chos bdag po la 'phrod kho bo bsam pa tshims zhes gsungs nas/ bu ston rin
po che'i dbang bum dus 'khor nas bshad pa'i cha tshad dang ldan pa bum chu'i rgyun dang bcas pa/ bu ston rin po che'i phyag bzo ma byang chub kyi sing las grub pa'i dus
'khor gyi phur ba/ kha TAM ga/ gzhan yang rab gnas kyi bye brag tu mnga' 'bul/ bum sman sgam tshad ma/ hor dril/ hor chol sogs sngags chas kyi khyad nor bzang po stsal
cing sras kyi thumthu bor gyur to/ /der yo ga skor gyi gzigs rtag gnang dus rdor dbyings kyi phyag dpe thams cad rlung chen pos shar phyogs ngos su 'khyer ba/ tshol du phyin
pas da lta'i gong dkar rdo rje gdan gyi gling gi thad nas tshang ma rnyed de/ phyis sa gnas der dgon pa 'debs pa'i lung bstan du dgongs 'di la rten 'brel chen po 'dug
gsungs/ de yang mdo sngags bstan pa'i rtsa lag tu gyur ba'i chos sde zhig 'debs pa'i dgongs pa gtad na dgung lo so gsum pa sa pho spre'u'i lo la sa chog mdzad/ lo skor gcig

tsam gyi ring la dpal rdo rje gdan mi 'gyur bde ba chen po'i gtsug lag khang rten dang brten par bcas pa ma lus pa grub nas dge 'dun gyi sde khyad du 'phags pa dang / mdo sngags
kyi bshad nyan dang rgyud sde rnams kyi nyams len gyi rgyun mi nyams pa'i phyir du cho 'phrul zla ba la gur rigs bsdus sogs dkyil 'khor sum cu skor gyi sgrub mchod/
sa ga zla ba la dus 'khor gtso bor gyur pa'i sgrub mchod/ gro bzhin zla ba la dpal rtse dbyings gsum sogs rnal 'byor rgyud kyi sgrub mchod/ rgyal gyi zla ba la rdo rje phur
ba'i sgrub mchod sogs btsugs shing / 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi mdzad pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa bstan nas gdul bya grangs tshad las 'das pa yang dag pa'i lam la bkod/
rtse gcig tu thugs dam zab mo la bzhugs pas rtogs pa khyad par can brnyes te/ thun mong du snang ba la yang zhal gyi tshems 'ga' zhig lhung ba lha sku dang ring bsrel gyi
phur por gyur/ zhing 'di'i mdzad pa mthar phyin nas dgung lo drug cu rtsa lnga pa me pho 'brug gi lo/ nag pa zla ba'i tshes bcu drug tsaman nas sku snyun tshul cung zad
bstan/ de nas nyi shu lnga'i thun la slebs pa tsam na gzugs sku chos kyi dbyings su bsdus te dag pa'i zhing khams gzhan du gshegs so// | //gnyis pa ni/ mkhyen rab snyan grags
rin chen mchog tu grub/ /ces rdo rje 'chang sku zhang mkhyen rab chos rje ni/ sngon gyi 'khrungs rab ji ltar bstan tshul yang ji skad du/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs dang shA
ri'i bu/ /khri srong lde'u btsan 'brom ston dang / /nyang dang chos

dbang lha yi bu/ /sasnga ma'i skyes rabs zur tsam mo/ /zhes zhwa lu lo tsA ba rin chen chos skyong bzang pos gsungs pa ltar yin la/ de yang sku tshe 'di'i gong du ri rab kyi
byang phyogs lcang lo can gyi pho brang du dpal phyag na rdo rje'i sras kyi thu bo lha'i bu bzang po zhes bya ra gyur nas/ dga' ldan du byamasamagon dang rgyal ba rab gsal
la chos gsan pa na/ 'dzam bu gling du yul byang phyogs kha ba can gyi ljongs su sems can gyi don la bsams bzhin du srid bzungs shig ces lung bstan te gnang ba stsal ba'i
rkyen gyis 'di nyid du skye ba bzhes zhes grag go/ sku bltams pa'i yul ni zhwa lu phu nub kyi gnas gsar dge 'phel du yab sku zhang dpal 'byor bzang po dang / yum sa skya
mal mgon pa'i sras mo rin chen sangs rgyas 'dzoms pa gnyis kyi sras su rab byung bdun pa mi phe 'brug gi la sa ga zla ba'i tshes bco lnga la me tog gi char dang sa g.yo
ba sogs ltas ngo mtshar ba mang po bcas te 'khrungs so/ /lhums su bzhugs pa'i tshe yang nub gcig yum gyi rmi lam du mngal gyi nang nas nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor zhig phyir
'thon nas nam mkha'i mthongs su byung ste 'od zer rab tu 'phro ba dang bcas pa rmis so/ /sku bltams nas cher ma lon pa zhig la sku rdzi sogs kyis phyag phyi byas te/ sku
zhang chos rje phyogs las rnam rgyal pa'i drung du gshed dmar lha lnga dang 'chi med rnga sgra sogs kyi dbang gsan/ dgung lo gsum nas bdun gyi bar la gshed dmar gyi snying
po nyin

rer nyer gcig re chag med dang / de nas dgung lo bcu'i bar brgya re/ dgung lo bcu gcig gi thog tu glang chen brag tu gshed dmar gyis bsnyen pa yongs rdzogs dang bcas pa mdzad
pas zhal gzigs pa byung ngo / /dgung lo dgu bzhes pa'i skabs su tshe thar gyi zhon ra rgan mo zhig yod pa lug rdzi la khyod nga la ma nyan pas mthu byas nas sngon la bshan
pa gsod/ de nas khyod rang gsod gsungs te/ gsol zan la rnam sras drag gtor gyi gzugs bcos/ nyi ma phyed tsam gyi bar yun la thugs dam sgrub pa'i tshul mdzad de/ phyi
dro gtor ma 'phan pa mdzad pas de ma thag bshan pa chad thung sar tshig brtsegs la brten nas grir shi bas/ lug rdzi bred nas tshe thar byir ma'i tsal dang bcas te 'gyod
bshags phul lo/ /dgung lo bzhi tsam nas rab tu 'byung 'dod gting nas byung yang / yab yum gyis ma gnangs phyis dgung lo bcu bzhi bzhes dus thugs la 'di snyam du/ ngor pa
rdo rje 'chang de mkhas btsun bzang gsum 'dzoms shing / khams pa'i grwa pas bskor ba zhig yod zer bas/ der rab byung la bros na nyag kyang nya/ yab yum rnams kyi sa nas rjes
bsnyegs klang glags mi rnyad pa gcig 'ong ba 'dug dgongs ngor du 'bros par brtsams pas/ yum gyis rig nas yab yum bka' bgros mdzad da cis kyang rab tu 'byung dgos na zhwa
lu kho nar byas pas chog ces gsungs

pas / de nas dgung lo bco lnga bzhes pa sa pho rta'i lo rgyal gyi zla ba'i tshes gnyis la gdan sa chen po ri phug bla brang du mkhan chen 'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan
pa'i zhal snga nas dang / slob dpon dka' bzi pa rin chen rgyal mtshan sogs mkhan slob dge 'dun dang bcas pa bcu bdun gyi tshogs las dge tshul gyi sdom pa yang dag pa
bzhes bar mdzad/ mtshan rin chen mkhyen rab mchog grub ces bya bar gsol/ de'i tshe me tog gi char mang bo bab pas las gral pa kun na re/ dge bshes bzang po zhig yong ba'i
snga ltas su 'dug go zer skad/ de nas 'ga' zhig gis phar phyin la thog mar thugs gnyer gnang ba 'thad ces zhu ba la/ rje rin po che rin chen dpal grub pa'i gsung gis nged
kyang na sorgas/ dge 'phel gyi rdor dbyings sgrub mchod kyi gtso bo yang drung gis mdzad dgos pa yong shing / grub dbang nam mkha'i mtshan can gyis nged la gnang ba'i chos
rnams kyang bdag po la 'phrod pa byed dgos pas/ thog mar rdor dbyings la gzigs pa cis kyang 'gab gsungs pas/ rdor dbyings la thugs sbyongs mdzad/ phyag rgya dbyangs sogs
sin tu zhi bar zhus/ lag len 'di la shin tu nges pa dgos pas o song kyis ma yong gsungs nas/ dpon slob gnyis kyis dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs kyi bris thig sogs phyag len
phra zhib tshun chad thugs yul du nges pa dang / dbyangs kyi sa tshigs shin du nges pa'i bris sgrub tshar gsum mdzad/ de nas bka' bzhi pa

rin chen rgyal mtshan gyi drung du/ phar phyin gzhung 'grel dang bcas pa'i rgyugs 'bul gnang nas bshad pa tshar gcig gsan/ shar chen thams cad mkhyen pa ye shes rgya mtsho
la rdo rje 'byung ba'i bshad bka' shin tu zhib pa/ 'dus pa 'phags lugs kyi bskyed rdzogs kyi bsad pa sogs 'phags yo ga dus gsum gyis mtshon pa'i rgyud se bzhi la bu ston
thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsunggsang rab yod pa thams cad kyi steng nas lag len dgos pa phran tshegs tshun dang / bshad pa dgos pa rnams don tshoms su gsungs pas/ sngags skor
gang shes 'di'i shes rgya la sku drin shin tu che ba yin gsung / dgung lo bco brgyad bzhes pa'i skabs dpe mtshams mdzad de phar phyin 'grel chung / byams chos phyi ma bzhi/
tshad ma rnam nges/ mngon pa gong 'og/ 'dul pa mdo rtsa sum brgya ba dang / dbu ma rtsa 'jug rnams kyi gzhung thugs 'dzin gnang zhing mtshan nyid kyi grwa sa thugs mos
bzhin du'ang 'byon rtsis gnang bas/ mnal lam lam du gsang sngags rkyang pa gzhan phan che ba'i lung bstan dang / mtshan ma gzigs nas thugs 'dun gshol/ ngor e waM du rje
rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po la lam 'bras sogs gsan/ dgung lo nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa sa mo glang gi la sngar gyi mkhan po kun mkhyen tshul khrims rgyal mtshan dpal bzang
po de nyid dang las kyi slob dpon dka' bzhi pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ gsang ste ston pa shar chen ye shes rgya mtshos mdzad nas mkhan ssalob dag 'dun dang bcas pa bcu
gsum gyi dbus su/ dpal zhwa lu'i gtsug lag khang gi

cha mkhas pa tsandra'i gzims khang dkar por bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/ de'i tshe me tog gi char chen po babs/ mkhan po rin po che de nyid la theg pa chen po'i sems bskyed rgyal sras
dngul chu ba'i yig cha'i steng nas gsan te byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa yang dag par bzhes/ gzhan yang bde mchog lU i ba'i dbang bka' sogs bde skor/ dpal dus kyi 'khor
lo'i bshad bka'/ man ngag gi bka'/ de dag gi rgyab chos 'grel chen dri med 'od sogs dang / lnga bsdus/ gza' lnga/ rgyu mtshan rtsis sogs dus 'khor gyi skor/ gsang 'dus
kyi bshad bka' dang man ngag gi 'khrid/ gshed skor sogs rgyud sde bzhi la brten pa'i dbang bshad man ngag gi skor bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa
yang sras kyi bka' 'bum phal che ba'i lung gsan no/ dka' bzhi pa rin chen rgyal mtshan la gtso bor mdo phyogs kyi skor gsan/ rje rin po che rin chen dpal grub pa la dpal
rtse dbyings gsum gyis mtshon pa'i rnal 'byor rgyud kyi dbang bka'/ bshad bka' sogs gtso bor gsan te/ rdor dbyings kyi dbang gi skabs su snga sor thugs sras lo tsA bas
grub dbang nam mkha'i mtshan can la kun mkhyen bu'i dbang rdzas rnams gnang nas rnal 'byor rgyud kyi bstan pa'i bdag por bskos/ de bzhin du nam mkha'i mtshan can gyis rje
dpal grub pa la gnang nas bstan pa gtad/ rje de nyid kyis 'di nyid gnang nas rnal 'byor rgyud kyi bstan pa'i bdag por mnga' gsol lo/ /gzhan yang chos rje rong po

blo bzang pa/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ gu ru shes rab bzang po/ mkhar chen brag pa nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ ri khrod
dga' ldan pa chos rje nam mkha' tshul khrims/ mon rdzong ras pa zla ba rgyal mtshan te yongs su dril bas mkhas grub kyi bla ma bcu gnyis tshul bzhin du bsten nas/ dgung
lo bco lnga nas lnga bcu nga brgyad kyi bar chos gsan pa rnams dril bas/ dbang zur bka' mi 'dra ba brgya dang nyer drug/ khrid zur pa lam 'bras kyi skor/ ne gu'i skor sogs
khrid bka' mang po yod pa rnams kyang re rer bgrangs pas khrid chen sum cu tsam/ brgya rtsa rgya mtsho sogs re rer bgrangs pa'i rjes gnang drug cu/ lung bka' dang bshad
bka' gnyis stong dgu brgya bcu gnyis tsam gsan te chos kyi bang mdzod chen por gyur pa mdzad do/ /sgrub pa mdzad tshul yang sngar dgung lo bcu gcig la gshed dmar gyi bsnyen
pa dang / bcu drug pa la rdo rje 'jigs byed dang / yo ga rdo rje dbyings sogs kyi bsnyen sgrub mdzad/ dgung lo nyer gsum pa la thar lo nyi ma rgyal mtshan sogs kyi sgrub
gnas ra tsa shar gyi phu na smon mkhar rdzong zhes bya ba yod pa der lo gsum gyi bar la thugs dam sgrub pa kho na mdzad/ mnal phal cher 'od gsal du chud chos skyong rnams
bran bzhin du 'dus nas 'phrin las byed pa sogs byung ste/ lan gcig g.yal byung bas zhal gyi ma le bud de/ ci byas kyang ma tshud par nye gnas e ma 'chi 'bod par gtong
rtsis mdzad pa'i tho rangs mnal lam du mi nag

po dung long can cig gis ma le ngas 'jug pa yin zer nas bcug pa rmis/ gnyis sad nas ma le tshud 'dug gsungs skad/ gzhan yang gur zhal gnyis dang / dpal ldan rdo rje rab brtan
ma sogs dngos su byon nas/ gnod byed byung na nged rang rnams 'ong nas sgrol ba yin/ khyed rang gis gtor ma lag tu blangs nas brgyab nas sems bskyed la gnod pas ma byed
zer/ 'khrul zhig rje'i drung du sbyor drug gi 'khrid gsan te ri phug gi gzims khang gong du mun mtshams la bzhugs pa'i tshe 'od gsal gyi mdangs la zhwa lu pa rnam/ shangs
bsreg shing tshun/ rta nag mda'/ stag la tshun tsam gyi khang zhing / mi dang dud 'gro/ tha na chu nang gi srog chags sogs gang byed thams cad mngon sum ltar gzigs so/
/de nas bzungs 'dod na mun pa la yang dpe cha mthong ba byung pas/ kre'o rab 'byams pa sogs la mtshan mo mun nag la lung mang po byas pa'i rgyu matsan de yin gsung / dgung
lo so gcig pa la dbang ldan chos 'khor gyi gdan sar phebs/ der gtsug lag khang gsar bzhengs dang chos 'khor rgya cher bskor de na 'khod pa'i dge tshul slong rnams kyang
'dul ba'i kun spyod ma dag par gzigs te/ gong tshig gi dus mi phyugs pa'i phyir grib tshod lta ba dang / zas skom gyi 'og tu chab gtong ba sogs phyag len phra mo tshun
'dul ba'i gzhung dang sbyar nas bslab ste btsun pa rnams 'dul khrims la bkod/ skabs shig zhwa lu phu'i glang chen brag sogs kyi ri mtho

po rnams su byon nas sgrub pa mdzad/ nyin gcig po ta la'i lho phyogs chos 'byung grub ces bya ba'i rtse la bzhugs pa'i tshe/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ba zhig gis sku tshe'i tshad
dang phyi ma'i zhing khams lung bstan/ dgung lo so dgu pa la sku khams shin tu bsnyel ba byung nas/ sngar rgyal ba mus chen pa'i lung bstan la dgung lo so bdun khongs
su rtsa rir byon nam mkha' spyod du gshegs pa zhig yod gsungs yod pa de las ni thal 'dug na'ang / 'chi sa rtsa ring byung na phyi ma mkha' spyod du 'gro dgongs pas der
'byon rtsis mdzad/ lha sar phebs nas zhabs skor 'bum thar mdzad pa'i tshe skor lam du ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ba sngon mo zhig gis gser btul ma zho gang phul/ jo bo bcu gcig
zhal gyi drung du phyag mchod mdzad pa'i tshe sems can la dmigs pa'i snying rje drag pos smre sngags chen po shor bas/ jo bo'i zhal nas khyod mthong thos dran reg gi sems
can thams cad ngan song du mi 'gro ba'i sems rgya chen po bskyed zer ba zhig byung gsung / rtsa rir gshegs pa la zhwa lu'i dpal ldan rdo rje rab brtan ma shin tu 'phreng
bas dngos su na bza'i thu ba nas 'then pa dang / 'tshubs par byung bas slar yang gtsang la phebs dgos byung / ri phug gi gzims khang shar chen du bzhugs nas bu lugs kyi
dbang bka' rnams lo gsum gyi bar la dbang sbyin mdzad/ khyad par dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs te/ dbang bka' tshar brgyad gnang ba'i tshe
rdo rje rnal

'byor mas dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor du rje nyid la dngos su dbang bskur gnang bas/ nye brgyud thun mong ma yin pa bzhugs pa'ang da lta'i dbang rgyun 'di ka yin cing
/ lugs gzhan las khyad par du 'phags par shes bar bya'o/ /dgung lo zhe lnga pa la yo ga'i cho ga yod pa'i grwa sa dpal 'khor bde chen/ mkhar kha chos sde/ rtsis gnas gsang
/ zha lu/ bsam grub rtse rtse tshan/ lha bo sogs dgon sde thams cad la rdo rje rtse mo'i sgrub mchod 'pher ba thams cad dbang ldan chos 'khor du 'dus shog ces pa'i spring
yig stsal/ rtse mo sgrub mchod zla ba phyed kyi bar la tshar gnyis grub/ dkon mchog gi drung du mchod pa'i bye brag rigs so so re re la'ang mar me/ lha bshos/ spos
hreng sogs brgya rtsa brgyad re phul/ dge 'dun rnams la'ang bsnyen bkur 'phul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa mdzad de rdo rje rtse mo'i sgrub mchod bod gangs can gyi khrod du de
las legs tshogs che ba dus gsum du ma byung ba zhig mdzad/ dgung lo zhe bdun pa la ri phug tu nag nya la dus 'khor sgrub mchod tshugs pa gnang zhing dge sleng chos legs
pa sogs grwa pa lnga bcu tsam la dus 'khor rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa mdzad/ dgung lo lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa la thugs dam gyi nang rten gser sku rdo rje 'chang bzhengs/ nga
bzhi pa la rgyan mkhar zam kha brag khung du bdud rtsi ril bu'i sgrub pa mdzad nas ril bu zos ba'i gang zag 'das dus 'ja' zug pa dang me tog gi char bab pa sogs mthong

ba'i chos la ngo mtshar mang du byung ngo / /dgung lo nga drug pa la sku mtshams la bzhugs dus sa skya'i bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan pas nA lenDa'i gdan
sar phebs dgos pa'i zhu nan byung ba rje nyid kyis lugs gnyis thad nas mi 'pher tshul dang / khyad par na so rgas/ mig mi gsal ba'i stobs kyis sngar gdan sa yod na'ang sprod
ran gda' zhing cis kyang mi yong / de bas chos rje paN chen shAka mchog pa da lta glang thang na bzhugs pa de las 'os med ces zhu ba gnang yang / slar da dung rab lo
gsum/ tha ma lo gnyis cis kyang gnang dgos zhes bka' nan ches pa sogs kyis lo de'i zla ba drug pa'i tshes bcun la ri phug nas phyag bteg de dus zhwa lu/ tshong 'dus kyi skya
btsun thams cad ri nyil ba bzhin 'dus nas thams cad kyang sems 'phreng bas ngu chom byed pa rnams la thugs kyis ma bzod par phyag 'tshal gdong du chos khri brtsigs pa'i
steng nas der 'dus pa'i skye bo khri phrag rgal ba la theg pa chen po'i sems bskyed gnang / rim gyis zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bcu gsum la rong ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i
rgyal tshab tu mnga' gsol/ der btsun gsar sum brgya lhag tsam la rab byung dang bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa stsal/ mgon khang gsar bzhengs dang chos zhu ba stong phrag gcig
dang sum brgya tsam la gsung ngag lam 'bras kyi bka' chos gnang / de'i ston bo gtsang du phebs nas ri phug tu sgrub mchod mdzad pa dang zhwa lu gzhi grwa dang phyogs nas
mjal mkhan rab tu mang po la dbang

khrid lung sogs chos 'khor bskor nas dbyar chos lam 'bras gsung ba la nA lendrar phebs/ dgung lo drug cu pa la ri phug tu phebs nas sgrub mchod sogs sngar lugs bzhin dang /
sgrub thabs rgya mtsho'i rjes gnang sogs gsung chos shin tu mang ba gnang / bu ston yab sras kyi bka' 'bum yig mkhan bcu bdun tsam gyis yi ge 'bru ma zhe gcig tu bzhengs
pa legs par grub/ de nas nA lendrar phebs nas chos 'khor rgya chen po bskor te/ mdor na rje nyid kyi chos gsung tshul sogs gzhan mang du smos ci 'tshal/ tha na dbang bka'
gnang ba rang yang / dus 'khor sku gsung thugs yongs rdzogs kyi dbang bka' tshar sum du so lnga/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho tshar bcu/ rtse mo rigs bsdus kyi dbang bka' tshar
nyer lnga/ dpal mchog rigs bsdus tshar bcu dgu/ rdor dbyings tshar brgya dang nyer bdun/ chos dbyings gsung dbang tshar sum cu/ khams gsum rnam rgyal tshar bcu bdun sogs
gzhan gyis tshar re re tsam yang bskur thub pa dka' ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po de dag gi dbang tshar lan grangs de tsam zhig mdzad de gzhan rnams des rigs 'gre zhing rgyas
par rje zhwa lu lo tsA bas mdzad pa'i rnam thar mthong ba don ldan nyid la blta bar bya'o/ /de ltar dgung lo drug cu re gnyis pa me mo sbrul lo yan gyi mdzad pa rnams rje
zhwa lu lo tsA bas yi ger btus nas spyan lam du phab ste rjes gnang byin rlabs kyi bka' don gyi tshang pas/ da ni

zhal nas gsung pa'i bka'i slad du rje nyid nas lung thugs rje bzung tshal/ zhes sku dngos la lung gnas ba zhus pas tshegs pa mang po la lung stsal/ de nas lo de'i zla ba bdun
pa brgyad pa la sku mtshams mdzad pa'i dus/ mtshan lam du nam mkha' thams cad de bzhin gshegs pas gang ba'i khrod nas bud med dmar mo zhig gis mkha' spyod kyi gzhig gsos
grub yod pas shog zer ba cig byung gsung / de rjes yang slob ma rnams la chos bka' rgya cher gnang ste/ 'o de tsam yin/ de grub pas blo bde gsung ba sogs thugs sna bsdus
pa'i tshul mdzad pas nA lendra'i grwa rgan rnams kyis dwogs pa la gtsang du bzhud 'dod pa yin 'dra snyam sa skya bdag chen ngo chen la sbran nas nA lendra rang du bzhugs
dgos ba'i zhu ba phul/ rje nyid nas bcu bzhi mchod grol grol sdod/ de nas cha mi 'tshal gsung / zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes bcu bdun gyi nyin/ nga bu ston chos rjes yo
ga'i bstan pa spel du btang pa yin/ zhwa lu ba rnams kyi rten 'brel cung zad log pa'i stobs kyis mdzad pa tha ma 'dir ston dgos pa byung / 'on kyang sems can re re'i mdun
na nga'i sprul pas khyab yod pas gsol ba thob ces sogs gsung zhing / tshes bco brgyad kyi snga dro'i cha la thugs dam chag med kyi rim pa thams cad mdzad/ lhag par bhu
ri pa'i rgyun bshags tshar mang ba gsung ba dang srid pa gsum 'bar sogs nas/ he ru ka dpal bsngags pa lhan cig gar byed shog ces pa'ang brgya phrag mdzad/ de'i tshe yang
me tog gi char mang po bab/ de nas srod kyi cha la sku

gshegs pa'i tshul bstan/ gdung sbyangs pas ring bsrel bres gzhal nus pa dang / gshed dmar/ nA ro mkha' spyod ma/ phyag na rdo rje'i sku sogs byon/ gsung las 'khrungs pa'i bu
chen bsam gyis mi khyab mod/ brgyud 'dzin gyi gtso bo/ mkhan chen rigs 'dzin rgyal po/ dpon po rin chen rgyal po/ lo chen chos skyong bzang po/ rdo ring kun spang pa chen
po/ sbyang lung gzhon nu chos grub sogs yin cing / gzhan yang de skabs kyi mkhas grub phal cher dam pa 'di nyid kyi slob mar ma gyur pa med pas 'brug pa kun legs kyis
kyang thog mar rje 'di nyid la bsnyen rdzogs zhus pa'i lo rgyus snang / sku dngos kyi 'dul byar ma gyur pa'i slad ma'i rjes 'jug rnams la gsung gi bdud rtsi'i bgo skal stsol
phyir thub bstan rin po che'i btsas su 'gro ba'i bka' 'bum yid bzhin gyi nor bu dag kyang yod do/ /gzhan yang gzugs sku'i bkod pa bsdus rje btsun zhwa lu lo tsA ba la
zhal dngos su bstan nas bdud rtsi ril bu'i sgrub tshul gnang ba sogs ngo mtshar gyi bkod pa bsam gyis mi khyab cing gsang ba'i rnam thar brjod kyi mi lang ba gda' bas/ rjes
'jug thams cad kyang bskal pa bzang po'i tshul shes par byas te/ gsol ba 'debs pa la 'bad par bya'o/ /rje nyid me mo sbrul gyi lo/ rgyal gyi zla ba'i tshes bco brgyad
la zhi bar gshegs pas dpal na lendra'i chos grwar dus kyi tshes grangs la mchod pa 'bul ba'i las byed rnams la yang chos rje

bco brgyad pa zhes da lta'i bar du grags nas yod do/ / | //gsol 'debs las/ rigs 'dzin skyo ston sngags 'chang rgyal po'i zhabs/ /thams cad mkhyen nges lo chen chos skyong bzang
/ /rin chen grub bstan rgyal po'i srid 'dzin mkhas/ /mtshungs med dam pa gsul la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes 'byung bas/ dang po mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang skyo ston rigs 'dzin
rgyal po'i zhal snga nas de ni/ sngon gyi dus na lha'i bu bzang skyong dang / de nas jo bo chen po dpal ldan a ti sha dang / grub chen mi tra dzo ki dang / rgyal sras
thogs med bzang po dpal rnams su sku skye ba bzhes tshul gsungs pa'i phyir na/ dam pa 'di'i rnam par thar pa gzhan dag kyang so so skye bos tshad 'dzin par mi nus shing
mtha' rtogs dka' ba zhig go/ dus 'dir 'khrungs pa'i yul ni tshong 'dus kyi sa'i cha dgon pa dge lung par grags pa'i gnas de nyid du/ skyo 'od 'byung skyo ma gcig lab sgron
gyi bla ma/bsod nams bla ma/ mnyam med sangssnang thang mkhan po rgyas bsgom pa/ skyo ston snar thang mkhan posmon lam tshul khrims sogs mkhas shing grub pa brnyes pa'i
skyes bu dam pa mang po 'khrungs pa'i dbon brgyud du yab skyo ston padma rdo rje dang / yam bya mchu nang pa'i sras mo rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i rnam 'phrul du grags pa bsod
nams skyid ces bya ba de nyid kyi sras su skye ba bzhes te/ de'ang lhums su zhugs dus klu'i dbang po'i rnam pas yum la gnas g.yang ba'i tshul du byung zhing / slar rab
byung bdun pa'i me mo sbrul gyi lo la/ me tog gi

char dang / 'ja' 'od rol mo'i sgra sna tshogs bar snang las sgrog pa sogs ngo mtshar gyi cho 'phrul du ma dang bcas sku bltams/ dgung lo gsum bzhes dus su/ 'jam dpal mtshan
brjod/ bzang po spyod pa'i smon lam/ tshe gzungs rnams bslab ma dgos par rang rdol du byung / gzhan yang dus 'khor bsdus brgyud sogs kyi tshig thar thor zhal 'don gnang
ba dang / byis pa tshogs pa'i dus su yang de dag la gsung bshad gnang tshul sogs byung pas/ yab kyi zhal nas kyang nged kyi bu 'di ngo mtshar can gcig 'dug gsung ste mnyes
so/ dgung lo lnga bzhes pa lcags mo bya'i lo/ hor zla dang po'i tshes brgyad la/ yab kyi bu chung 'khrid nas ri phug tu 'khrul zhig rin po che tshul khrims rgyal mtshan
la 'jigs byed kyi dbang zhus/ dbang gi dus su me tog gi char chen po bab cing 'khrul zhig rje'i bka' las/ dge lung ba'i bu chung 'di btsun pa la chug cig /'di la bstan pa
'dzin nus pa'i dge bshes shig yong ba 'dug go gsung / yab kyi drung du thog mar phyag rdor 'khor chen gyi dbang zhus/ gzhan yang 'jigs byed kyi bskyed rim sogs kyi 'khrid/
rdzogs chen a ro'i 'khrid sogs gsan/ mthu gtad ser gsum gyi zhal bzhes man ngag chig brgyud bka' rgya ma 'ga' re yang zhus mod kyi phyis su de 'dra gzhan la spel mi dgos/
rang gis yang sems la ma zin par brjed du bcug gsung / dgung lo bcu gsum pa sa mo sbrul gyi lo/ hor zla bzhi pa'i dmar phyogs kyi rdzogs pa dang po'i nyin ri phug chos

kyi pho brang chen po'i dri gtsang khang gi gzims chung ka bzhi mar/ kun mkhyen tshul khrims rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos mkhan po dang / las slob byang sems tshul khrims/ gris
tshod pa mkhas grub chen po nor bzang rin chen gyis mdzad de dge 'dun bcu phrag gcig tshogs pa'i dbus su dge bsnyen bzung dge tshul gyi bar bsgrub par mdzad/ de'i tshe
yang ngo mtshar ba'i ltas mang po byung bas mkhan slob dge 'dun dang bcas pa zhal mthun par jo sras 'di la bstan pa'i bdag po zhig yong ba 'dra zhes gleng ba mdzad/ der
'dus tshogs su rab byung ston mo'i tshul du mang ja'i bsnyen bkur zab pa gcig btang / dus de nas bzung ste dgongs mo thug pa phor gang tshun chad zhal du mi 'khyer ba'i
kun spyod gtsang sing deb kho na dang / 'bral dge tshul gyi bslab bya phra rags thams cad la dag ther mdzad de rang bzhin gyi kha na ma mtho ba cung zad tsam gyis ma gos
par gnang / de nas hor zla lnga pa'i tshes brgyad kyi nyin slob dpon byang sems tshul khrims kyi spyan sngar bzhugs te/ 'grel ba don gsal dang / phar phyig kyi TIkka lung
gi snye ma sogs thugs 'dzin gnang zhing bshad sbyong zhib pa mdzad nas dgung lo bco lnga ba lcags mo lug gi lo sa ga zla ba'i nyi shu gcig la zhwa lu'i mthil gyi 'dus tshogs
dbus su phar phyin gyi bshad gsar gnang / dge 'dun rnams la bsnyen bkur gyi ston mo rgya cher bsgrub te zla ba phyi ma tshes 'phral la e waM chos ldan du phebs/ rje
btsun kun dga' bzang po la lam 'bras sogs

gsung chos rgya cher gsan pas/ rje dei' bka' las/ khyed bstan pa la phan pa'i dge bshes bzang po gcig yong pa 'dug pas re zhig mdo phyogs kyi slob gnyer ma dgos/ de'ang bla
ma mkhyen rab dbang phyug gi phyag phyir phyin na legs po 'ong gsung / mtshan mo ngor gyi lam 'bras lha khang du bzhugs nas sku gnyer gyi sang nyin spor rgyu'i mar me rnams
rje nyid kyi de nub spar nas mar me brtag pa mdzad pas thams cad rgyal mtshan 'dra ba byung pas thugs dgyesdges grags bro khrab pa'i lo rgyus gsung / dgung lo bcu drug
bzhes pa'i dus bzhad grwa tshang chen mor chos rje mkhyen rab dbang phyug grags pa bzang po'i spyan sngar phebs te phar phyin 'dul mngon sogs la mkhas par sbyangs/ de dag
gi rgyab chos mang po'i lung dang / gzhan yang spyod 'jug /bslab btus/ mdo kun las btus sogs gsan/ khyad par kun mkhyen nam mkha' bsod nams pa slob chung du bsten nas
mdo phyogs mtha' dag blo gros kyi bum par bskyil ba mdzad/ ston chos kyi thog zhig la bshad dpon tshang du dpon slob thams cad byon nas/ kun mkhyen nam mkha' bsod nams pas
brgyad stong 'grel chen gyi bshad pa gnang ba gsan pa'i tshe/ mtshan mo thugs yul du mi bde ba'i dogs pa 'ga' shar byung bas tho rangs kyi char kun mkhyen nam bsod pa de
nyid 'jam dbyangs smra ba'i sengge zhig tu gyur nas/ khyod kyi mi bde ba rnams kho bas sel ba yin pas kha bzed cig gsang / zhal du ljags brkyangs pa 'dra ba zhig la ro
mchog

dang ldan pa gsol rgyu yod pa'i nyams zhig byung ste/ de ka'i mod la the tshom gyi mdun pa thams cad rang grol du gyur/ gsung rab mtha' dag la thogs pa med pa'i rnam dpyod
kyi rig rtsal rdzogs pa byung ngo / /slar yang dgung lo nyi shu rtsa bdun pa la ri phug tu phebs nas/ dus mchod chen mo'i skabs bstan pa'i rnam gzhag rgyas par gnang ste
rab 'byams smra ba'i sengge chen po'i mtshan rtags bzhes/ dgung lo sum cu so bzhi pa lcags pho stag gi lo hor zla lnga ba'i tshes lnga la/ bkra shis kyi gtsug lag khang ri
phug chos kyi pho brang chen por mkhan po sngar gyi rje btsun 'khrul zhig chen po de nyid dang las kyi slob dpon sku zhang mkhyen rab chos rje/ gsang ste ston pa'i slob
dpon kun mkhyen chos grub dpal bzang / grib tshod pa gnas brtan rgyan dar bas mdzad cing / mdor na yongs su 'dril ba'i dge slong 'dul ba 'dzin pa nyi shu'i dbus su rje rang
gi sku'i gcung po bla ma nor bu'i drung dang lhan cig bsnyen rdzogs bzhes te dge slong gi dngos por gyur to/ de ltar sgom pa thob nas bsrung bya'i gnas phra zhing phra
ba'i bar thams cad spyan gyi 'bras bu ltar bsrung pa mdzad pa/ nged sdom pa blangs tshun chad ltung bas gos ma myong zhes rje rang gis dngos su zhal gyis bzhes kyin yon
'dug pas skyabs su mchi ba der gda' 'o/ /gzhan du na sdom pa bsrung rgyu'i gong du bsrung bya ngo shes pa yang shin tu dka' zhing / de yang 'dul ba'i dbang du byas nas so
thar rigs brgyad kyi nang tshad tshangs spyod dge bsnyen man chad bud med dang ma bral zhing / de yan chad bud med

dang bral bas rtsa bzhin sdom dgos pa zhig ni de dus nas 'byung / de'i steng du bar ma rab 'byung dang dge tshul gyi sdom pa blang zer yang bsrung bya de ka ma gtogs yan lag
gi bsrung bya so so'i ngos 'dzin tsam yang mi dgos pa zhig dang / de nas dge slong bsgrub pa yin zer yang bsrung bya gong gi de ka ma gtogs/ lhag ma bcu gsum/ spang ltung
sum cu/ 'ba' zhig pa dgu bcu/ so sor bshags pa bzhi/ nyes byas brgya dang bcu gnyis dag la rtog 'jug tsam yang byed mi dgos pa zhig da lta'i chos gzugs rang cag kho na
ma zad/ gnas dus kyi grags ldan mang po la yang zhib tu brtags tshe yong gin yod pa 'dra/ de 'dra ba ni sdom pa dge tshul slong yin par 'dod kyang / bsrung bya tshangs spyod
dge bsnyen las ma bsrung pas/ thugs sras lo tsA ba chen pos ston pa'i zhu yig las/ rtsa bzhi sdom kyang lhag ma la sogs bag yangs spyod cing blang dang dor ba bya ba
mi shes dge slong yin zhes bdag la bstod/ /ces dge slong du 'dod pa ha cang thal che ba yin tshul gsungs/ bod 'dir gleng dar mas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa bcom dus lha lung
dpal gyis rdo rjes thugs snying rje chen pos kho rang bsad/ de rjes khyim pa 'ga' zhig gis btsun pa bcos te sngon gyi lha khang rnying pa'i gyang ris su gnas brtan bcu
drug bris pa la dpe byas nas skra bregs shing sham thabs kyang sngo dmar ser gsum brtsegs ma gyon/ stog 'gag gi gong pa dag kyang dkar po byas lag tu spos phor bzung la
ming gnas

brtan dgra bcom pa btags pa yin skad/ de dag gis dbyar gnas phyed zer nas zla ba re tsam bud med dang lhan cig mi nyal bar byed/ de nas dgag dbye byed zer nas bud med dang
nyal ba byung ste/ de dang cha 'dra bar ma dgongs pa'i nyen yang mi 'dug /bstan pa phyi dar gyi thog ma la yang rA chen lo tsA ba dge slong rdo rje grags pa gsang sngags
la mkhas shing grub pa brnyes pa'i skyes bu dam par gyur pa ni rtsod pa dang bral ba zhig yin/ khong gi drag po mngon spyod kyi 'phrin las bcol nas mi mang po bsgral ba dang
/ chas yang bkag med du gsol zhing rigs kyi sras bskrun par mdzad pa grags che/ de tsam mdad nas 'dul 'dzin du zhal gyi ma bzhes na skyon ci yang ma mchis te/ mdo dag
las/ ji ltar grong khyer skye bo'i mi gtsang lud/ /de ni bu ram shing ba'i zhing la phan/ /de bzhin byang chub sems dpa'i nyon mongs lud/ /de ni sangs rgyas chos rnams bskyed
la phan/ /ces sngags bla med tsam du ma zad phar phyin theg pa'i skabs na yang / gang zag khyad par can la dmigs bsal yod par gsung / rA chen khong gis 'dul 'dzin du
zhal gyi bzhes nas bsnyen rdzogs kyi mkhan po gnang bas/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston chen pos/ kye ma gangs ri'i khrod 'di na/ /mkhan slob khyim pas byed pa dang
/ /ces sogs gsung nas thugs shin tu yang ba'i gnas su mdzad pa yin no/ /da ni dkyus la 'jug ste/ de yang rje nyid kyi dgung lo so lnga pa la dbus su phebs pa'i lam zhor
'bras yul skyed tshal du rong ston shes bya kun rig gi bu

chen kun mkhyen sangs rgyas 'phel ba'i drung du/ tshad ma rnam 'grel/ 'bum rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum rnams kyi bshad lung stabs gcig tu gsan/ rim gyi mkhas pa'i chos grwa gsang
phu ne'u thog tu phebs gling smad kyi paNDi ta chos rje yon tan rgya mtsho la brten nas slar yang skyar sbyang gi tshul du/ phar tshad kyi gzhung mtha' dag la thugs gnyer
mdzad/ de nas 'bras spungs su thegs nas slob dpon ldan ma pa la dbu ma rtsa ba shes rab/ dbu ma la 'jug pa rig pa drug cu pa/ stong nyid bdun cu pa/ zhib mo rnam dag
/rtsod bzlog rnams gsan/ de'i skabs shig bla ma byang sems de mo thang pa'i snyan pa gsan pas thugs 'phrog pa byung rung / 'phral ri bo dge ldan du phebs nas der ba so chos
rje khri la bzhugs pa dang dus mtshungs pas de nyid sogs mkhas pa 'ga' la gtugs te/ rje btsong kha ba'i dbu ma'i skor la rang bzhed kyi bshad srol byung ba rnams legs
par gzigs dgos dgongs kyang / tho rangs mnal lam du bud med gcig na re/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen pa myur du mngon par rdzogs pa sangs rgya bar 'dod na byang chub sems bsgom par
bya'o/ /de kho na la gces spras su bya'o/ /zhes bya ba kho na bshad gda' bas de dgongs sam/ zer ba dang mnal sad pas dge ldan du phebs 'grul gshol te de mo thang du shar
rgyag phebs/ de skabs nam zla dgun po yin pas chu 'khyag gi lam zhig la snga dro thogs thag rgal nas 'byon

dgos pa zhig byung ste/ zhabs la 'khyag pa rke 'khor lta bur chags zhing zhabs 'bring pa gcig yod pa des smre ngag drag po bton pas/ nyid kyi zhal nas/ spyod 'jug las/ nya
pa gdol pa zhing pa la sogs pa/ /rang gi 'tsho ba tsam gyi don du yang / /grang dang tsha la sogs pa'i gnod bzod na/ /'gro ba'i don du bdag ltas ci mi bzod/ /ces gsungs pa
ltar chos phyir grub thob gong ma rnams kyi dka' ba ci tsam spyad 'dug ltos dang gsung / zhal gdams mang po'i sgo nas lam bstungs te 'khrid pa gnang / de yang blam ma de
thang pa chen po sku mtshams dam po la bzhugs nas gzhan la mjal kha gnang gin mi 'dug na'ang / rje nyid phebs rgyu'i nub mo 'od gsal du rje btsun sgrol ma na bza' dar gyi
bun bun byas nas/ khyed kyi tshe rabs mang po'i gong nas rjes su bzung ba'i byang chub sems dpa' gcig sang nyin 'byon pa yod ces lung bstan byung ba'i rkyen gyis nang
par nye gnas la yang / de ring sar gnas kyi byang chub sems dpa' zhig 'dir 'byon kyin yod 'dug pas/ gsol ba zhabs tog bzang po'i grab kyis/ nged dang de 'phral mjal dgos
pa'i bsgug tu ma ster gsung / nye gnas des kyang grab zin pa dang rgyang nas blta zhing bsgug cing sdad de 'dug/ der rje dpon slob gnyis kyis kyang gung tshigs snga ba la
phebs te de 'phral mjal/ bla ma'i zhal nas/ lam bar la 'o rgyal chen po byung na'ang 'dir phebs bgo bcad bka' drin che gsung ba sogs dges pa mu med pas skyan gyi 'bras bu
ltar bcos

so / /der theg pa chen po blo sbyong dang 'brel ba'i zab chos rnams rdzogs par gsan te dus de nyid du bdag gzhan brje ba'i byang chub kyi sems rin po che thugs rgyud la spungs
pa bzhin du gyur pas chos rje de thang pa de nyid bka' din che ba'i bla ma zhig tu yang mdzad/ de thang dgon par bzhugs rtsis gnang yang yum gyi yi ge nan ches pa bskur
bas slar gtsang du phebs/ rje btsun dam pa 'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyi drung du theg pa chen po'i sems bskyed kyi cho ga chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa nas
brgyud pa rgyal sras dngul chu ba'i yi ge'i steng nas gsan/ phar phyin lung snye ma'i bshad pa/ spyod 'jug gi bshad pa de'i TIkka bus mdzad pa'i lung / 'dul ba la gces
pa'i gzhung brgyad kyi bshad lung sgrags ma/ bde gshegs snying po'i mdzes rgya dang / mdo phran mang po'i lung sogs rgyu mtshan nyid theg pa'i chos skor mang po dang / gshed
dmar lha lnga/ 'jigs byed zhe dgu ma/ gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa rnams kyi dbang bka'/ gzhan yang rjes gnang sgrub skor sna tshogs dang bcas pa gsan no/ /kun mkhyen chos
grub dpal bzang po'i drung du phar phyin/ 'grel pa don gsal/ tshad ma rnam nges/ 'dul ba mdo rtsa/ mngon pa kun las btus/ bka' gdams gzhung drug dang / gsang 'dus pa'i rgyud
le'u bcu bdun ma dang / nyer gcig pa dang / mtha' drug rab gsal/ 'grel pa sgron gsal/ lha mo bzhi zhus/ sgrub thabs mdor byas sogs rgya gzhung mang po dang / 'gos kyi
stong thun

sogs dang tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dbang gsan/ chos rje mkhan chen rin po che bshes gnyen bzang po rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i drung du phyag rdor 'gro bzang gi dbang dang
de'i rgya gzhung mang po'i lung / rnam sras kyi rjes gnang las tshogs man ngag sna tshogs dang bcas pa gsan/ shar chen ye shes rgya mtsho'i drung du/ don zhags/ rnam 'joms
dkar po sogs kyi dbang bka' de dag gi chos skor mang po'i lung gsan/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje'i drung du dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang bshad man ngag dang bcas
pa/ gsung 'dus 'phags lugs/ ye shes zhabs lugs/ 'jig rten dbang phyug dang bcas pa'i dbang dang rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa/ man ngag rim lnga dmar 'khrid/ gser sdings pa'i
nag 'khrid skor sogs gsang 'dus skor gyi chos bka' rje de nyid la mnga' ba phal cher dang / gzhan yang gshed skor yongs rdzogs/ lo nag gi dril gsum/ dbang rtse dbyings
gsum sogs kyis mtshon pas mdor na rgyud sde bzhi dang 'brel ba'i dbang bka'/ bshad bka' man ngag gi 'khrid/ de dag gi rgyab chos rgya bod kyi yig cha du ma dang khyad par
thams cad mkhyen pa yab sras rnams kyis mdzad pa'i gsung rab mtha' dag gi lung sogs zab chos shin tu mang ba gsan/ 'khrid rnams kyang myong 'khrid kho na mdzad cing / khyad
par sbyor drug u rgyan bsnyen bsgrub sogs dus 'khor gyi rdzogs rim rnams dang / gsang ba 'dus pa rim lnga sogs zab bzhes mdzad pas de dang de'i lam gyi drod rtags phag
cher dus der rdzogs nas zung 'jug bde ba chen po'i ye shes kyi rtogs

pa brnyes pa'i tshul ni/ rnam thar gsol 'debs las/ sbyor drug spros med rim pa lnga sogs kyis/ rdo rje'i lam la gnang du bsnun pa'i tshe/ /mtha' gnyis kun spangs bde stong
dbyer med pa'i/ /zung 'jug mngon du gyur la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes 'byung ba ltar ro/ /de nas bu slob yang mang du 'dus par brten/ slob gnyer ba grwa pa brgyad cu skor zhig
phyag phyir 'khrid nas bzhang grwa tshang chen mor phebs/ der chen blo gros rin chen gdan sar bzhugs 'dug pas/ rje nyid nas grwa tshang chen mo'i zur 'chad pa mdzad de/
thog mar phar phyin gyi spyi don/ gzhung don sogs mkhyen rab dbang phyug yab sras kyi dgongs don so sor bkral nas bshad pa gnang / de'i zhe bzhad po dang / shangs/ snar thang
/ rta nag nyang stod sogs nas 'ong ba'i blo gsal gyi grwa slob yang tshan cher 'dus te/ de dag so so'i blo rab 'bring thams cad dbye bas skabs su gang bab kyi/ kha dog
dkar dmar rtsi ba nas bzung / phar tshad dbu gsum/ 'dul mdzod rnam gnyis sogs gzhung chog bar zhal gyi bzhes nas phebs kyang / mtshan lam du bstan bsrung ma chen mo byon
nas khyed 'dir ma bzhugs shig /bzhugs na sa chas ka thams cad ngas khyer 'gro ba yin gsung dre'u la bskal nas theg pa sogs byung zhing / sku khams

kyang log pas rta nag tu bzhugs pa'i thugs 'dun gshol nas zhwa lur phebs/ mon rdzong ras pa zla ba rgyal mtshan gyi spyan sngar phebs nas mar mi yab sras kyi thugs bcud rje
'ba' ra ba chen po skyes mchog rgyal mtshan dpal bzang la bka' bab pa'i/ phyag chen/ nA ro chos drug sogs dang mkhas grub khyung po'i zab chos rtsa ba ni gu chos drug /sdong
po phyag rgya chen po/ yal gal lam khyer rnams rnam gsum/ me tog mkha' spyod dkar dmar/ 'bras bu 'chi med 'phyug med kyi skor rdzogs par gsan no/ /de yang rgyal ba'i
gsung rab kyi don rnams thos bsam gyi gtan nas phab kyang rtse gcig tu nyams su ma blangs na 'bras bu sangs rgyas zer ba'i sgra bo che de mi thob par dgongs/ dgung lo bzhe
bcu zhe dgu ba shing mo sbrul gyi lo nyid rang gi bu slob dka' bcu pa rin chen bsod nams rnam rgyal la 'chad nyan gyi 'khur phog /rje rang bya bral mdzad nas lcags kyi
phu nu bstod nu gyen lung bde ba can zhes bya ba'i ri khrod dben pa zhig yod pa der phebs nas bsgrub pa'i dam bca' mdzad pa 'di ltar/ rang bzhin nyams dga' gzhan gyi 'tshe
ba med/ /chu dang 'o ma 'bras khu'i 'byor ba yod/ /chags dang sdang ba'i gtam yang ma thos pa'i/ /dben pa'i gnas 'dir kho bo yid rab spro/ /dad dang 'dun pas bsgrub pa
gtso bor bgyid/ /chos dang chos min blang dor ma 'dzol bar/ /le lo rnam g.yeng dbang du mi btang zhing / /bla ma'i drin gyi 'tsho ba'i gdams ngag rnams/ /sbyor ba dpyid
las lam gyi gzhi bzung nas/ /dngos gzhi dbyar las lta bur nyams sa blangs/ /de yang

rgyu med 'bras bu ri bong rwa/ /snga ma snga ma'i nyams myong mthar phyin bya/ /zhes gsungs te sku mtshams dam par bcad nas lo bdun gyi bar nye gnas ma gtogs su la'ang mjal
kha med cing rtse gcig tu bsgrub pa la bzhugs so/ /de nas chu pho byi ba'i lo'i dbyar sos kyi dus la bab pa na rgyab ri'i rtse la nyin mo'i rnal 'byor skyong du res 'ga'
tsam pebs/ gnas de nyid du thugs dam 'phel zhing khyad par snod bcug kyi snang ba sna tshogs 'di dag pa rab 'byams 'ba' zhig ma gtogs 'akrul snang a 'thas su ye mi 'char
ba zhig byung gsung / de yang rnam thar gsol 'debs las/ dag pa'i ye shes snang ba las byung ba'i/ /rin chen du ma las grub gzhal yas khang / /chos kyi yi ges mtshan pa nam
mkha'i khams/ /gang bar gzigs pa'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs/ /de nas bzung ste 'od kyi snang ba las/ /legs par grub pa'i sangs rgyas byang chub sems/ /cha shas yongs rdzogs
shin tu mdzes pa'i sku/ /mngon sum gzigs pa'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs/ /dbang po'i gzhu ltar yid 'ong sprin dbus nas/ /rta bdag brgyad kyi bskor ba'i rnam thos sras/ /rings
bar tshur byon bka' sdod zhal bzhes pa'i/ /mthu stobs rmad du byung la gsol ba 'debs/ /mchog zung gcig dang gnas brtan bcu drug gis/ /yongs bskor thub pa'i dbang po
gsar mdog can/ /sprin bral mdun gyi nam mkha'i dbyings su byon/ /byin rlabs lung bstan brnyes la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes 'byung ba'i de dag gi don

ni / lan cig 'dzam bu'i gling gi zhing 'di'i khang khyim ri rab la sogs pa thams cad dbyings su dag pa'i nang na rgyu rin po che sna tshogs las grub pa'i gzhal yas khang chen
po phyi bltas nang gsal gyi dbus su rgyud sde bzhi'i lta tshogs thams cad gsal lam 'dres pa/ ngo bo gcig la rnam pa tha dad rgyud ssade gang dang lha gang du bltas pa
de dang der 'char ba/ lha de dag gi drung na rje rang gi sku yang de snyed du gyur nas byang chub tu sems bskyed pa dang / de'ang len pa sogs rgyud sde gong 'ong dang mthun
pa so so dus gcig la grub pa shin tu ya mtshan pa gcig byung ste/ de nas bzungs thugs yul du mi bde ba'i rnam pa nam byung ras kyi sangs rgyas byang sems kyi sku'i gzigs
snang re nges pa can du 'ong zhing des sel bar 'gyur gsung / yang skabs shig rgyab ri'i rtse na 'bum pa gog po gcig 'dug pa'i rtsar nyin mo'i rnal 'byor skyong gin bzhugs
pas byang ngos kyi nam mkha' nas tshur sprin chen po gcig lding yong pa 'dra zhig la sengge dkar mo'i steng na rnam thos sras sku nyi ma 'bum gyi gzi brjid dang ldan
pa rta bdag brgyad kyi bskor ba lcags nang gi lung par mi gshong ba tsam gzigs pa byung / yang lan gcig rnam thos sras sku sngar dang 'dra ba la chibs da 'khor med pa'i zhabs
thang gi rnam pa can phyag tu zhwa lu'i tshogs dung khyer nas khyed gdan 'dren la yong bas 'byon dgos zer brda byed pa zhig byung bas ci yin nam dgongs pa 'khrungs te/
de'i skabs zhwa lur mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs pa zhi bar gshegs nas gros pa thams cad kyi rje nyid gdan sar

spyan 'dren zhu bar thag bcad pa yin lo/ /de nas shing pho stag gi lo zla ba gsum pa'i tshes bco lnga'i nyin zhwa lu ba'i chen po khri lho ba slob dpon chos rab pa dang / chen
po khri byang ma drung rgyal pa gnyis kyis mtshon bla ma las sne khag sgrub gnas de nyid du 'ong nas gdan sar phebs dgos pa'i gsol 'debs dang sbrags zhu rten phul bas/
rje'i bka' las/ nged spyir na so rgas/ khyad par deng sang sde dgon chen po 'dzin pa la chos 'jig rten gnyis nas yod pa gcig dgos/ nged kyi chos phyogs rang nas mi pher
zer rgyu ma 'dug na'ang / 'jig rten phyogs nas blo ha cang 'khums drag pa dang / ri mi 'bab pa'i dam bca' zhig kyang yod pas/ da res nged la de skad mi gsung ba mdzod ces
zhu chas phyir sprod pa gnang / der khong rnams kyis/ bdag tsho yul rgya gar snyeg pa'i don sa la'i lbags pa'i ngang tshul yin/ zhal bzhes tig tig cig ma gnang bar 'dir
lo mang bsgug dgos pa byung yang bsgug cing bsdad do zer nas bsdad pa yin gda'/ de dus tho rangs shig rje'i mnal lam du/ ston pa gtso 'khor gsum gnas brtan bcu drug dang
bcas pa mdun gyi nam mkhar byon 'dug pa'i ston pa'i zhal nas/ zang zing mi 'jig chos dang byams/ /zhes sogs lung 'dren dang bcas te gsung pa'i mthar nyid la chos shod cig
pa'i brda mdzad pa zhig byung / nyid kyang spro shugs chen pos slar thugs bskyed gsal 'debs tshul gnang ba'i khrod mnal sad cing / thugs la da re gdan

sar phyin nas chos bshad na sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la phan thogs cung zad yong rigs su 'dug dgongs po byung ste/ slar khong rnams la khyed kun gyi u tshugs de 'dra pas/ nga
lo gcig gnyis khas len pa la thug go gsung ba gnang / de nas sa ga zla ba'i tshes bcu la zhwa lu pa'i chibs bsu slebs te tshes bco lnga la zhwa lu bla brang du phyag phebs
pa yin/ gza' skar 'phrod sbyor dge ba'i tshes pa bco brgyad kyi nyin 'dus pa rgya mtsho'i mgon du phebs shing sde pa lcags stod pa sogs yon bdag che phra mang pos khri
ston/ khri 'bul sogs legs tshogs kyi rten 'brel sgo du ma nas bsgrigs te zhus/ rje nyid kyi thugs dam zab mo las mi g.yel ba'i ngos chos 'chad kyi 'khur chen po bzhes/
dbyar chos tshugs skabs rig ra gtong ba gnas nas/ rig ra/ lung ra/ bsdus ra sogs sgrigs tshe so sor bkod nas mdzad/ thams cad bshad nyan la 'bad pa'i don dgos pa'i bka'
khyab yang yang gnang / gzhis byes kyi slob gnyer ba yang sngar bas mang du 'phel te mtshan nyid pa sil ma bu tig gcig mthil thong pa nas bka' rab 'byams mtha' dag khong
du chud pa'i dge bshes kyi bar bgrangs pas lnga brgya las ma nyung ba rgyun du byung / sngags la yang dus mchod chen mo'i dkyil 'khor che chung ma nges pa'i cho ga gtong
mkhan rnams/ rje rang gi spyan 'tshugs mdzad nas btsun pa ming 'di zhes bya ba khyod kyi dkyil 'khor 'di'i cho ga yong ba gyis/ ming 'di zhes bya ba khyod kyi dbyangs 'di
dang gar 'di shas pa gyis/ dpe 'di dang 'di la ltos shig gsung ba

sogs mdzad/ 'ga' zhig gis dbang ma thob ces zhu ba la/ dbang ngas sang nyin byed pas khyod rang do nub sta gon la shog gsungs te mi re tsam la'ang de 'phral gnang / gzhan yang
chos zhu mkhan phal cher la dgyes bzhin du gnang ba mdzad/ de yang sngar grwa tshang chen mo'i zur 'chad ma mdzad gong la dbus su lan gcig phebs nas lha sa'i chu rags
dkar po rab brtan gyi 'khris su byang chub kyi sems sgom gyin bzhugs pa'i tshe/ rje btsun byams mgon gyi phyag g.yas pa brkyangs te rje'i dbu thog tu bzhag nas rigs kyi
bu khyod shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i gzhung lugs rnams kyi bdag por 'gyur ro/ zhes lung bston pa'i tshul gsal bar byung ste/ 'di skabs 'chad nyan 'phel po byung bas
de'ang de la blta ba 'dra dgongs pa 'khrungs/ mdor na chos gsung tshul yang dbang gi dus sbyang gzhi sbyong byed sbyangs 'bras sogs ngo legs par 'phrod cing dbang dus kho
nar lhan skyes kyi rtogs pa 'char nus pa lta bu ma gtogs/ dkyil chog gi klog rgyugs la dril gsil btags pa'i bum chu'i skal 'gyed tsam la dbang bskur bar sgro btags nas
mi mdzad pa cig yod ces grags/ bshad pa mdzad pa'i tshe yang 'gal dang ma 'brel sogs 'chad tshul log pa'i skyon mtha' dang bral ba mdo la lung rig gtan tshigs dpe dang bcas
te gsung / sngags la'ang mtha' drug tshul bzhi sogs rgyud kyi bshad thabs dang 'brel chags pa ma gom shes nas skyon 'jug pa'i gnad la bshad pa dpyis phyin pa mdzad nas
gsungs/

shes nas mi chun pa'i skyon 'byung ba'i zab mo'i gnad 'ga' zhig cung zad sbas nas gsung ba sogs ma bshad log bshad ha cang bshad pa'i skyon dang bral ba mdzad ces grags/ khrid
gnang ba'i tshe na yang dmigs pa'i zab gnad rdzogs pa/ de la yon tan nad nas skye tshul/ nyams kyi brang gegs sel tshul/ lam gyi bogs 'don tshul sogs sman pa mkhas pas
nad bcos bzhin du mdzad pa ma gtogs de ka yin lo/ / zer lo/ 'dug lo/ bshad lo kho nas cho ga ba mi mdzad par grags/ tha na lung gnang ba'i tshe yang gsal dag snyan gsum
'dzoms pa gcig mdzad nas gsung bar grags/ rtsod pa mdzad pa'i tshe yang gzhung lugs rab 'byams thugs su chud pa'i gsung gi gdangs su/ byams pa thog med rjes 'brang dang
bcas klu sgrub yab sras rjes 'brang dang bcas/ phyogs glang chos grags rjes 'brang dang bcas/ yon shag rnam gnyis rjes 'brang dang bcas/ de kun gyi gdan sa pa nga yin shog
ces thugs ngar ba'i tshul mdzad pa dang / dngos snyobs kyi rig lan nas drangs pa'i tshig 'bru rnon po re re tsam gyi phyir thal mdzad pa'i mod la/ mkhas rlom dregs ldan
rnams kyi blo gros kyi byin nya rang sar 'dar nas de 'phral rnam dpyod kyi 'tsho mi thub par/ mi smra ba'i sa la 'gyel 'gro ba zhig 'byung gsung / rtsom pa mdzad pa'i tshul
yang / legs bshad gsar spel mang na/ dam pa gong ma'i gsung gi 'phrin las yal 'gro ces/ gsung rtsom gnang ba la thugs ha cang mi dgyesdges kyang / gzhan gyi zhus ngo
re bar phyin gyi rnam bshad nyi ma'i 'od zer/ 'dul

ba'i spyi don/ mngon pa mdzod kyi spyi don/ de dag gi zur sgol sna tshogs sogs mtshan nyid kyi yig cha 'ga' dang / sngags la'ang / bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ maNDal tshigs bcad ma/
rtog bdun gyi TIkka/ 'jigs byed bskyed rim gyi bshad pa/ rdzogs rim gyi dmigs pa/ de'i bshad pa sogs dang / ma gcig gi gcod skas don thug snying gi khrid yig /nam mkha'
sgo 'byed kyi lhan thabs/ ayon bsnyen bsgrub kyi 'khrid yig /rgyun 'khyer gyi man ngag sogs mdzad pa yod ces gsungs/ rgyun du 'phral 'bul mkhan byung ba tshun dge 'dun
la bsngos nas dpyad dngos spus gtsang ba zhig phyag tu thebs yang / 'di rang res bdag tu bzung mi nyan/ yar nas su bsgyur la dge 'dun gyi ja rdor dang thug thal yong pa gyis
gsung nas gnang / gsung gleng ci 'dra zhig mdzad kyang chos mthun gyi zhal lta kho na ma gtogs don med kyi smra brjod mi gsung / gzhan gyi mi'i skyon tshang bru ba'i
tshig gleng ba gsan na'ang 'o cag de 'dra byed pa ma yin/ dus kun tu rang skyon rang gi bzung ba khe che/ mi'i skyo tshang brus nas dgos pa gang 'dug /cis kyang mi nyam na
nga'i sgo 'di yan la chags sdang rmongs lab khyer ma yong zhes bka' bkyon mdzad/ lan gcig sku khams cung zad mnyel pas nye gnas sogs kyi rim gro bya bar zhus pas dus la
babs na rim gro byas kyang mi phan/ 'on kyang da res mi 'chi ba'i rmi ltas shig byung gsung / mtshan lam ji 'dra byung zhus pas/ nga g.yu lo bkod par 'gro dgos snyam te/

thang chen po me tog sna tshogs kyi gang ba zhig la kha shar du bltas nas 'gro gin gda' bas/ rdo'i khri gcig la khye'u zur phud can gcig bsdad 'dug /ngas 'phags pa 'jam dpal
yin las che/ dngos grub cig zhu byas pas/ de na re/ dngos grub 'dod na 'di na yar rgyug zer/ brag ri mthon po skas ring po btsugs pa gcig bstan byung / ngas g.yang za bzhin
du skas de la 'dzegs phyin pas/ rtse mor sleb tu nye ba na/ slob dpon byang sems tshul khrims pa brag tog tu phebs nas la'u la'u shog gsungs nas phyag gis 'then pa gnang
/ der slebs pa na/ me tog sna tshogs bkra ba'i ljongs chen po zhig la gur dkar po mang po phub nas/ de dag la skye bo'i tshogs du mas mchod pa 'bul zhing smon lam 'debs
kyin 'dug /ngas slob dpon byang sems pa la/ gur 'di dag na su bzhugs pa lags sam dris bas/ rje btsun byams mgon dang/ rang re'i mkhan brgyud kyi bla ma rnams bzhugs pa
gda'/ pha gi na chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bzhugs gsung / mjal bar 'dod de bdag gi mjal kha e thob zhus pas/ thob gsung te slob dpon pas 'khrid nas/ gur dkar po zhig
tu phyin pa na/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa lha'i 'khor mang pos bskor te theg pa chen po'i chos gsung gin 'dug pa'i drung du slebs/ chos rje nga la spyan cer ba zhig gzigs
nas shing tog 'dra mo re sna tshogs dro ba gcig gnang byung ba zos pas bde gsal gyi ting nge 'dzin la cham te 'gro ba dang / re zhig gdan sa 'dir sdod dgos pa'i brda
zhig mdzad

byung / de ngang yang lan gcig 'ja' tshon 'dra ba'i skas ring po zhig la 'dzegs nas phyin pas khang pa gcig gi nang na 'khrul zhig rin po che tshul khrims rgyal mtshan bzhugs
pa'i drung du slebs/ der en tsam song ba dang 'khrul zhig rje bzhengs nas skas ring po gcig la 'dzegs nas 'byon gyin 'dug /gar gshegs zhus pas nga dga' ldan du 'gro gsung
/ bdag kyang 'khrid par zhus te phyi bzhin du 'dzegs nas phyin pas skas 'gor rnam sras byon 'dug nas/ nga la khyed 'byon ma ran par ci la 'byon zer 'u thug thug mdzad
kyin 'dug /'khrul zhig rje la zhus pas/ 'o na lo 'ga' sdod de nas shog gsung pa zhig byung pas da res mi 'chi ba yod gsung / byang chub kyi sems kho na la nan tan du mdzad
pas/ sku tshe 'dir bya dang ri dwags dud 'gro'i rigs kyang bag phebs nas gnyen gshin gyi ma la bu bzhin du 'khor nas yong ba dang / sku mtshams kyi dus dang 'gol bzhugs
mdzad pa'i tshe na phun ron dang byi'u rnams sku pang du sdod pa la sus thob byed cing / ma thob pa rnams gsol lcogs kha sogs su gral bsgrigs nas sdod pa sogs yong gin
yod ces grags/ de bzhin du dmu rgod ma rung ba'i sems 'chang ba rnams kyang rje'i sku mdun du slebs pa dang gshisshisrgyud 'jam rting gi 'gro ba 'byung ste/ lan gcig mag

paN grub du ma'i gdan sa yin tshul/ chos rje yab sras kyi mdo dang sngags kyi bstan pa'i srol chen btsugs tshul/ de nas bzung rje nyid kyi yan la gdan sar phebs pa thams
cad mkhas shing grub pa brnyes pa sha stag yin tshul/ de dag gi bka' drin las da lta mdo sngags gnyis ka'i bshad nyan gyi rgyun ma chad pa yod tshul/ slad nas kyang mkhan

ma bsgrub pas zhal ngo phal cher dus gcig la grongs/ rje nyid kyi rjes sgrub gnang dgos dang bcas gzhan snang du 'o rgyal chen po byung 'dra pa la dkar po slob dpon bkra
shis rab gsal

gyis / da lo sku mnyel po byung lags sam/ zhus pas/ nged la rmi las sgyu ma'i go bar ri yod pa 'dis phan byung gsung / rje'i sku tshe ring thung sogs thugs dam kyi ltas ci
'dra lags/ zhus pas/ nga lo bdun cu don bzhi'i thog tu slebs na rgas dang nyen 'chi dang nye bya ba de yan na ang gsum/ gnas dar thugs dam kho nar bzhugs pa la gsung chos
sogs ni rgya cher ma gnang/ dgung lo bdun cu don bzhi pa lcags pho rta lo hor zla lnga ba'i mgo nas bsnyun pa'i tshul bstan/ bka' las/ da ste spo zos na zla ba bzhi e sdod
yin no/ /gzhan ji ltar byas kyas 'chi ba yin gsung / sman dpyad rim gro mi dgos tshul gsung kyang phyag phyi dag gis nan gyis zhus nas dpon tshang rnam rgyal ba bcar bzhugs
kyi gsol sman drangs/ zhwa gur mang 'gyed dang bcas te skur mi sgrub/ thar pa mkhan chen gyis brtan bzhugs phul bas/ bka' las/ drung pa 'dir ched du brtan bzhugs 'bul
bar byon pa la ngo dgos pas re zhig bsdad do gsung / zla ba gsum gyi bar bsnyun las bral ba'i tshul bstan cing slar hor zla dgu ba'i mjug'jug tsam nas bsnyun log/ de'i
tshe yang sde ba lcags stod pa dang / tshong 'dus pa so so nas em 'chi re gsol sman gyi 'phrod rten 'bul bar ched mngags btang / thar ba mkhan chen khong yang bskyar du
brtan bzhugs 'bul bar phebs pas/ rje'i bka' las da rang da tsam yin/ zhing 'di'i 'dul bya rdzogs/ tshe yang mthar son 'dug pas don du gyur na des chog /gzhan lo brgya bsdad
kyang tshim

pa mi yong gsungs/ hor zla bcu pa'i tshes lnga nas nam mkha' la 'ja' tshon gyi dra ba dang me tog gi char nyin re bzhin byung / nyer brgyad kyi nyin g.yab cheen du ja gral
la bzhugs skabs rdo rje bsdu ba'i phyag rgyas se gol gyi sgra chen po tog cing / badzras mAdzaHdzaHhUM baM hoH gsung zhing spyan nam mkha' la gzigs shing dbu gug gug mdzad/
thar pa mkhan chen gyi dri ba zhus pas/ rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi lha tshogs rnams byon pa la ngas spyan drangs te rang gi lus la bstim pa yin gsungs/ yang gnam stong gi
nyin mo sngar bzhin nam mkha' la 'ja' 'od me tog gi char 'khrigs pa la gzigs te phyag thal mo sbyar nas spyan chab bsil zhing / bsod nams rgyal mtshan da lta rang yongs rdzogs
gnas lnga ma brgya rtsa gcig skad chen pos thon cig gsungs/ dbon drung gis de bzhin bton tshar ba dang / 'o da ci chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa dga' ldan nas byon te/
nga la der shog gsung gin 'dug /ngas smon lam btab/ rten 'brel mang po bsgrigs pa yin/ rten 'brel gyi gnad cig khyod la 'ang 'dug pas gsol 'debs 'don du bcug pa yin gsung
/ da ni rjes su lo chen thams cad mkhyen pa rin chen chos skyong bzang po'i khri gshol ssakabs khong gdan sar phebs dgos byung ba de'i lung bstan du gsal lo/ tshes gcig
gi nyin de ring tshes ba du yin gsung / tshes pa gcig lags zhus pas/ de tsam thad kha sang zla ba snga ma'i nyer gcig la nga dga' ldan du 'gro

snyam yang / khyod tsho'i rim gro 'dra ba des 'gro ma thub/ lar rten 'brel gyi byed pa 'di ya mtshan 'dug /da ste tshes gsum gyi nyin 'byung 'dus kyi phung po 'di bskyur ba
yin gsung / nye gnas kyis rab lo gsum/ 'bring lo gcig/ ma mtha' zla ba 'di'i nyi shu gcig tshun bdag rnams kyi tshogs rdzogs phyir bzhugs dgos zhus kyang ma gnang / tshes
gnyis kyi nyin do nub dge 'dun drag pa thogs shig gdan drangs la chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsol 'debs/ mkhyen rab dbang phyug grags pa bzang po'i gsol 'debs/ 'khrul
zhig chen po'i gsol 'debs rnams mgyogs bul ran pa'i gdangs kyis snyan la tshig gsal ba zhig thon cig rje de rnams kyang dga' ldan na bzhugs yod/ nga yang dga' ldan du 'gro
gsung / de'i dgongs mo srod la rje btsun sgrol ma byon byung ngo mchod pa phul la khyed rang rnam pas smon lam thob cig gsung / de bzhin du yang yang mchod pa bshoms
shig gsung ba byung / de nas mgo zla'i tshes gsum la thugs dam chag med kyi rim pa rnams nyi ma phyed yan la grub par mdzad pa'i mthar nga la don dam par 'chi rgyu med/ kha
zhe med par gsol ba thob/ nga'i rnam thar blta 'dod pa rnams rgyal sras thog med kyi rnam thar la bltos shig ces gsungs nas phyag mnyam gzhag dang zhabs rdzogs skyil mdzad
de mod la sku gshegs so/ der bu slob phal cher yang 'dus nas dgung zhag zhe dgu'i bar rgyud sde bzhi dang 'brel ba'i cho ga mar ngo mdzad tsang sku gdung lo gcig

gi bar ril bor za ma tog tu bzhugs pa la mchod pa phul/ lcags lug mgo zla'i tshes gsum gyi tho rangs sku zhang bsod nams mchog grub sogs thugs sras rnams kyi gshed dmar lha
lnga'i steng nas gdung sbyangs pas dbu ril por byon/ ring bsrel dang lha sku'i bye brag bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang sku'i zhun kyang khal gcig lhag pa zags nas byung zhing
'dra sku che chung gnyis bzhengs pa las che ba zhwa lu ri phug gi gtsug lag khang du bzhugs su gsol/ gsung las 'khrungs pa'i bu chen re re nas smos kyi mi langs zhing /
'on kyang gtso bor gyur pa ni 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhan chen dkon mchog tshul khrims/ dpon chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ sku zhang bsod nams mchog grub/ rgyud sde 'dzin
pa chen po chos rig rgyal mtshan rnams so/ /de dag gi nang tshan rgyud sde 'dzin pa chos rig rgyal mtshan de nyid ri phug byang gling gi gdan sa mdzad/ zhwa lu ba'i bstan
pa la 'chad rtsom gyi 'phrin las dang bka' drin mchog tu che'o/ /de nyid kyi slob ma'i gtso bo srad dgon ston pa chos rje bsod nams dpal 'byor sogs yin la/ da lta khang
rnying grwa tshang pa'i phyag len du mdad pa'i gsang 'dus/ gdugs dkar sogs kyi sgrub dkyil sogs kyang chos rig rgyal mtshan gyi mdzad pa mang zhing mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs
dpal bzang po khri la byon pa'i mgo tsam na chos rig rgyal mtshan byang gling gi gdan sar bzhugs pa dang dus mtshungs so/ /

skyo ston rin po che chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan ni mkhan chen rigs 'dzin rgyal po'i sku mched skyo dpal ldan rdo rje sogs kyi sras su chu mo glang gi lo la tshong 'dus
dge lung pa'i khyim du 'khrungs shing / gzhon nu nas rang gi khu bo chos rje rigs 'dzin rgyal po'i drung du rab tu byung / mtshan nyid kyi phyogs su thugs gner phul du phyin
pa mdzad nas dka' bcu rab 'byams pa bzhengs/ dgung lo sum cu so gcig pa chu mo lug gi lo sku zhang rin po che bsod nams mchog grub dpal bzang pos mkhan po mdzad nas
gtsug lag khang chen po zhwa lur phug gi bla brang shar chen du bsnyen par rdzogs/ lo de'i hor zla drug pa'i tshes pa bcu bdun gyi nyin bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i gdan
sar lo chen chos skyong bzang po'i rgyal tshab dam par dbang bskur nas khri thog tu lo bcu bzhi bzhugs chos kyi 'khor lo rgya chen po bskor zhing mkhan chen rigs 'dzin rgyal
po'i rnam thar sogs bstan bcos kyang mang du mdzad snang ngo / /skyo ston yab sras kyi skabs so// | //gnyis pa ni/ thams cad mkhyen nges lo chen chos bzang / /zhes zhwa
lu lo chen thams cad mkhyen pa rin chen chos skyong bzang po de ni/ sngon gyi dus na yang 'phags pa'i yul kyi ma hA paNDi ta du mar sku'i skye ba bzhes pa'i tshul bstan
cing / dus 'dir 'khrungs pa'i gnas ni zhwa lu mthil gyi khang gsar gong ma zhes bya ba der/ 'gos lo tsA ba khug pa lhas btsas dang / bu ston thams cad mkhyen

pa'i mngon pa'i bka' babs kyi bu chen bka' bzhi pa sangs rgyas mgon sogs skyes chen dam pa mang po 'khrungs pa'i rigs rgyud sku zhang blon po rin chen sengge'i gdung las 'phel
ba'i yab dpon bsam 'grub dpal bzang dang / yum rin chen chos 'dzoms la sras lcam sring bzhi 'khrungs pa las/ rje 'di thog mar 'khrungs pa'i sras po gcig pu nyid de rab
byung bdun pa'i lcags mo bya la sku bltams nas btsas ston kyang rgya cher byas shing / mtshan chos skyong 'bum zhes gsol te/ de 'ang sngon bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa chen
pos ri phug gi sku 'bum mthong grol chen mo bzhengs pa'i tshe/ dpon rin chen sengges srog shing du dri ldan shug pa 'thud ma mi dgos pa'i sdong po gcig grub shin tu bzang
ba gcig phul bas/ chos rje nyid kyi bka' stsal pa/ ma 'ongs pa na khyod kyi rigs brgyud la nga'i bstan pa 'dzin pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen gcig 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes
lung bstan pa ni rje 'di nyid yin no/ /gzhon nu'i skabs sku rtsed kyi tshul mdzad pa na'ang chos 'chad nyan dang / dgon pa 'debs pa dang / dbang bskur ba dang / bsgom
mdzad pa'i tshul sogs gnang ba las byis pa tha mal gyi spyod pa ni gang yang mi mdzad do/ /cung zad mnal log pa'i tshe yang mar me dang du ba'i snang ba 'char ba sogs sngon
gyi thugs dam gyi 'phros dpa'i rtags mang du byung ngo / /dgung lo brgyad bzhes pa'i tshe nyang stod

shar kha ba dang / rong rin spungs pa dmag 'thab nas snar thang gi nye log pa lon du g.yun byas tshe/ rje'i yab bsam 'grub dpal bzang kyang shar kha ba'i dmag dpon la phebs
pas mtshon lam du 'das shing rje 'di nyid me me drung chos rgyal pas shar kha chos kyi rgyal po bdag chen bkra shis 'phags pa'i zhabs phyir bskyal/ der bzhugs ring la bod
yig 'bri klog sbyangs te bod skad la bag chags chung pas bslab pa dka' mo byung gsung / lanytsa dang / wartu sogs kyang bal po lha bzo ba zhig gis bslabs pas mkhas par
mkhyen/ rgya bod kyi 'bri klog thams cad thugs su chud de bdag po bkra shis 'phags kyi spyan sngar sangs rgyas byang sems mang po'i rtogs brjod klog pa dang / bla ma dge
ba'i bshes gnyen mang po la chos kyi dri ba mdzad pa'i 'phrin pa'ang mdzad de/ sku na phra yang thugs rdzogs pa dang / chos kyi snang ba 'ba' zhig dgongs par 'khrungs so/
/bdag chen gyis kyang zhwa lu khang gsar gong ma nga'i bu 'di gzhan dang ye mi 'dra ba chos snang can gcig 'dug /btsun pa 'os ba 'dra gsung ba phebs/ 'on kyang gzhan gyis
bkag pas re zhig skya bo la bzhugs dgongs pa byung zhing thugs la rab tu 'byung 'dod kho na las gzhan med pas dkon mchog gi rten drung du'ang smon lam mang po mdzad/ mo
ston mkhas pa zhig la mo cha mdzad pa/ kho na re/ sprin cog mo tsam zhig gnam khar byung / de je cher song bas nam mkha' khengs/ zer ba'i mo zhig bab ces zhus pas thugs
dgyes pa byung ngo / de nas dgung lo nyer gnyis pa

la chos mdzad par thag bcad/ yum gyis kyang pha gnyis 'dzin mkhan med kyang chos rang 'thad gsungs te chu pho rta lo dbyar zla tha chung gi nya la chos grwa chen po dpal 'khor
sde chen du 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog bzang pos mkhan po dang / chos rje kun dga' dpal bzang pas dge tshul gyi slob dpon mdzad/ mkhan slob dag gi spyan sngar rab tu byung

ltar bsrungs/ tha na zhal tshom tshun skra dang kha spu mnyam du 'breg par gsungs pa yin dgongs nas bzhag pas/ bal po 'dra zer nas chos mdzad bal po zhes btags skad do/
/chos grwa de nyid du khang gsar grwa tshang gi slob dpon ting 'dzin 'od zer ba la gtugs te thog mar rig pa la 'jug pa'i sgo bsdus gra mtha' yas pa nas brtsams te/ 'dul ba
dang / pha rol du phyin pa'i bstan bcos 'grel chung don gsal la thugs sbyong mdzad/ de'i tshe thugs rus chen pos nyin mtshan thog thag tu dpe cha 'dzin shar rig lud/ mno
bsam gtong ba sogs 'bad pa cher mdzad pas/ gzhan gyi lo zla bas rje'i zhag re'i thugs gnyer chod che ba byung bas kun the tshom du gyur nas/ chos mdzad bal po 'di 'dra
ci yin mi shes/ gsung rab rnams kyi tshig don ma lus pa shes nas smra ba zhig 'dug go/ zhes gleng zhing ha las pa byung zhes grags/ chu mo lug

gi ston ka slob dpon ting 'dzin pa sku gshegs nas chos rje bsod nams grags pa yongs 'dzin du bsten te/ 'grel ba don gsal dang mdo sde rgyan sogs kyi zhib bshad/ kun rig gi
dbang / phag dkar/ parna sha wa ri/ rnam 'joms rnams kyi rjes gnang / khyad par dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud 'grel gyi bshad bka' bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i phyag bzhes/
mkhan chen dharmA shrI pa sogs dngos slob kyi gsung sgros zin bris skor dang bcas pa la dpyis phyin par thugs sbyong mdzad/ dgung lo ner lnga pa shing mo bya'i lo gdan
sa chen po zhwa lu ri phug tu phebs nas sa ga zla ba'i dus mchod chen mo la phyogs ris kyi grwa bskor ba sogs gzhis byes kyi dge bshes mkhas pa mang po tshogs pa'i 'dus
pa rgya mtsho'i dbus su byams chos lnga la gtso bor bshad pa mdzad/ de'i tshe me tog gi char chen po babs pa skye bo kun gyis mthong ba sogs ngo mtshar gyi cho 'phrul grangs
las 'das pa byung / de dus zhwa lu na skad gnyis smra ba'i lo tsA ba gnas brtan legs rgyal ba bzhugs pa/ khong gi sar phebs te kho bo sgra shes bar byed 'dod pas thos
so ba tsam ma yin pa'i mthar phyin pa zhig bslab par zhus pas/ 'o khyed gzhan dang mi 'dra ba'i sgra'i slob gnyer gnang bzhed byung ba de legs/ mkhas pa zer ba de mdzad
'dod na sgra shes dgos/ da ni khyed rang dang por ka bA la'i gzhung / byings mdo/ uN sogs rnams khyis bangs kyang thon pa/ zhal

pa'i khar sran ma bkrams pa lta bu gang 'dod nas tog rtse blangs chog pa zhigzhag thugs 'dzin mdzod/ de nas ngas a rur lag mthil du bzhag pa ltar sgra rig pa gtsang sing nge
ba phyag tu 'bul lo ang gsung / de kha bzhin mdo gsum po thugs la byang bar bzung ste/ snar thang lo tsA ba'i rnam bshad las gsan te/ sa ris bskyar cag sogs la brtson pa
chen po mdzad pas/ zla ba gnyis na rdzogs par mkhyen/ zhar la sdebs sbyor dang snyan dngags sogs kyang gsan/ dus 'khor gyi brgyud pa la legs sbyar gyi skad du sdebs sbyor
dbang po rdo rje zhes bya bas bcings pa'i snyan dngags kyi bstod pa'ang mthud do/ da yang bod 'dir de snga yan la sgra ka bA la 'chad pa rnams phal cher grub pa'i yi ge
