gsungs/ khong gis snar thang lo tsA ba saMgha shri la gsungs/ des zhwa lu lo tsA ba gnas brtan legs rgyal ba la gsung / des rje 'di la gnang / de nas rgya cher 'di la skad
do/ /dgung lo nyer drug pa me pho khyi'i lo/ hor zla drug pa'i tshes nyi shu la dpal 'khor

sde chen gyi gtsug lag khang du chos rje don grub grags pa dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas kyi mkhan po dang / las kyi slob dpon chos rje bsod nams grags pa dang / gsang te ston
pa mkhar chen grags pa bsod nams blo gros/ dad pa'i dge 'dun kun dga' blo gros sogs 'dul ba 'dzin pa bcu tshogs kyi dbus su bsnyen par rdzogs pa dge slong gi sdom pa
mnos te dgra bcom pa chen po'i rnam par gyur pa yin no/ /de nas chos 'khor sgang du thugs te skad gnyis smra ba'i dbang po stag tshang lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen drung du
bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa nas brgyud pa'i rdo rje 'phreng ba'i dkyil 'khor rnams kyi dbang bka'/ dkyil mchog rdo rje 'phreng ba/ mngon rtogs rnal 'byor rdzogs 'phreng
/ sbyin bsreg 'od kyi snye ma ste phreng bskor gsum du grags pa'i lung / gzhan yang gsang 'dus ye shes zhabs lugs sogs kyi dbang bka'/ byu rgyud so so'i rgyud kyi nang mtshan
'dod lha du ma'i rjes gnang rig gtad/ mdo rtsa dang so thar gyi mdo/ mngon rtogs rgyan 'grel pa don gsal dang bcas pa'i bshad bka' sogs chos kyi rnam grangs bsam gyis
mi khyab pa gsan/ ka lA pa'i tshig don byang par mkhyen yang / legs bshad kyi cha 'dra 'ong ngam dgongs nas nyid kyi TIkka las kun bshad yan gsan te sngar las lhag pa'i
cha mi snang zhing / byings sgrub kha gcig gi rjes 'grel dbye ba'i mdo ma rnyed snang ba sogs la legs bshad pher phul chog pa byung ste stag lo chen po yang thugs shin
tu dgyes so/ /

skabs shig ngor brgyud nas khro phu'i gnasad mjal la phebs/ lo chen thugs rje dpal ba'i dngos slob dpal sdings lo tsA ba grags blo gros zhes bya ba sgra tsandra ba'i don la
mkhas pa'i pha rol du phyin pa zhig yod de tshur lam dpal sdings su phebs te mjal/ lo tsA ba la ja 'dren dang 'bul nod kyang mdzad de tsandra pa dpyis phyin pa bslab pa'i
snyan gsan phab/ dpal 'khor sde chen du phebs te slar yang bdag chen bkra shis rab brtan pas bdag po phag rgod khyung rgyal la phyag dam mdzad de seng ge rtse pas gsol
chas mthun rkyen gang dgos phul zhing dpal sdings su zla ba bzhi tsam bzhugs nas thog mar tsandra ba'i mdo/ byings kyi tshogs/ uN sogs dang bcas pa rgya gar gyi skad du thugs
'dzin gnang zhing 'grel pa dharma dA pa dang / lo chen thugs rje dpal ba'i rnam bshad chen mo'i steng nas 'khrid par mdzad cing / de dag gi gsal bar mi ston pa'i dka'
gnas su yod pa rnams ni 'grel bshad ratna ma ti las rgya dpe'i steng nas gsan pas/ rnam bshad la mi 'thad pa 'ga' snang ba rnams kyang dag papa 'chos nus pa byung ngo /
de ltar tsandra pa'i gzhung 'grel ca lag yi ge'i mdo/ ting mtha' dang / u Da sogs kyi 'grel ba dang / ner bskyur gyi TIkka sogs yongs su rdzogs pa zla ba bzhi la shin tu
mkhas pa mkhyen pa'o/ /de nas ni bod du bsgyur ba'i sgra mdo chen mo gnyis cha lag dang bcas pa dang / snyan dngags dang / mngon brjod/ sdebs sbyor dang / zlos gar dang
/ skar rtsis sogs tha

snyad rig pa'i gtsug lag mtha' dag thugs su chud nas lo tsA ba chen po'i go 'phang mngon du mdzad pa yin la/ nang rig pa'i mdo rgyud dgongs 'grel dang bcas pa la ni rje 'di'i
rtsa ba'i bla ma thams cad kyi nang nas sku zhang mkhyen rang chos rje de nyid bka' drin 'gran zla dang bral zhing / sku tshe snga ma nas kyi bla ma yin pa sogs nas rdo
rje 'chang dongs las tha lam pa'i 'du shes skad cig tsam yang thugs la 'khrungs ma myong ba zhin yin gda'/ de'ang sngar mtshan gsan pa tsam gyis sku lus 'tshug mi thug
pa'i thugs dad rang dbang med par tshud cing / dus phyis nas kyang mkhyen rab rje'i rnam thar dang 'phros gleng cung zad re byung na yang phyag thal mo sbyor/ spyan chab
dbang med du 'khrungs pa zhig yod skad/ de lta bu'i bla ma de nyid sngar zhwa lu lo tsA ba gnas brtan legs rgyal ba la sgra gsan dus nas bzungs dpon slob mthun mong ma yin
pa'i thugs rtse gcig pa pha dang bu'i rnam thar las kyang lhag 'byung zhing / gsung chos gsan pa'i rnam grangs yang gnyis med dus 'khor gyi skor/ pha rgyud gsang ba 'dus
pa dang gshed dmar gyi skor/ ma rgyud sgyu 'phrul chen mo dang mai tri mkha' spyod sogs kyi skor/ gzhan yang rdor dbyings sogs rnal 'byor rgyud/ rnam snang mngon byung
dang phyag rdor 'gro bzang gi skor sogs spyod rgyud/ 'chi med rnga sgra sogs bya rgyud de mdor na zab mo rdo rje theg pa dang 'brel ba'i dbang bka'/ bshad bka'/ khrid bka'/
lung bka' sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa gsan pa rnams ni rgyas par gsan yig las shes so/ /gzhan

yang snga phyir sku zhang chos rje dge slong ba/ zhwa lu mkhan chen chos grub dpal bzang dag/ mkhan chen dkon mchog tshul khrims/ zhwa lu ba dge bshes gsal ba grags/ rang 'byams
pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ snye mo sku zhang chos rje sogs las gtso bor bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa nas brgyud pa'i mdo sngags kyi chos phal mo che gsan par mdzad do/
/ngor pa rdo rje 'chang gi rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug/ kun mkhyen go bo rab 'byams pa/ paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ chag lo tsA ba
zhi pa/ dka' bzhi pa thugs rje dpal/ gong dkar rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/ rje dge 'dun grub sogs mdor na 'dir ma smos pa rnams yongs su dril ba'i bla ma lnga bcu
tham pa bsten nas thun mong ba sgra tshad bzo gso'i gzhung dang / thun mong ma yin pa mdo rgyud dgongs 'grel dang bcas pa la bslab te sa'i steng na 'gran zla thams cad
dang bral ba'i ma hA paNDi ta 'dzam bu gling gi mdzes rgyan gcig pur gyur to/ /nang du dngos por 'dzin pa'i 'chang ba mtha' dag las grol ba'i rtags su dus lan gcig zhwa
lur bzhugs skabs ri phug tu phebs nas mkhyen rab rjes gnang ba'i / ther ma bzang ba gcig la chos mdzad de/ bla yer skem du bzhag/ khang thog nas dpon slob rnams sgra'i sa
ris mdzad pa dang bstun te gzigs rtog mdzad pa'i lugs mdzad na'ang sa ris kyi thugs yangs nas re zhig gzigs pa ma byung / de'i bar

la ther ma mis khyor nas mi gda' skad/ de'i sang nyin sku zhang gi chos rje mthu stobs pas rtsad chod nas kha sang gi ther ma rku mi khongs shes byung / ther ma bslang nas
khrims la sbyor rgyu yin gsung na'ang rje nyid nas ther ma kho bos blos btang tshar bas mi dgos na khrims lta ci smos gsungs/ ther ma rkun ma de rang la stsal te bzhes par
mi mdzad do/ /yang dus phyis dbus su byon nas zhwa dbar sprul pa'i sku'i phyag phyi mdzad nas kong phyogs su phebs pas kong po zhig gis phor ba'i do po cig phul de khams
pa brtson 'grus zer ba la bskur bas khos phor ltang khyer nas bros pa nye gnas dang sgar pas zin/ khrims la btugs pa'i nyes pa byung ba la rje nyid kyi zhal nasas/ ngas
phor pa blos btang te dge ba'ang bsngos tshar/ de 'dra ma byed ces phor ltang kho rang la gnang nas nyes med mdzad/ de dus sne gdong zhol du sde ba yar mar gyi phul ba'i
na bza' bzang po kha cig gnas tshang la bcol yod pa/ yar phebs dus gnas tshang gi rje'i na bza' btsongs nas rin yang zos tshar 'dug/ zhabs 'bring pa dag tshig pa bzos te
sne gdong du zhus pa'i nyes dmigs la thugs na'ang / rje nyid kyis bdag la bskyin pa'ang mi dgos na khrims ga la 'chel zhes zhu ngo mdzad pas sne gdong gong ma chen po'ang
byang chub sems dpa'i spyod par gda' gsungs nas rje nyid pa shin tu dad pa byung skad do/ dgung lo nyer lnga pa shing mo bya'i lo rgyal mkhar rtse pa'i bdag po bkra shis
rab brtan pa'i phyag mdzad nas nged kyi khu bo bdag chen chos kyi rgyal po si'u rab brtan kun bzang 'phags pa de nyid nas srol gtad

pa'i dag pa'i mdzad pa rlabs po che'i nang nas mchog tu gyur ba rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur nas lo re bzhin du gser chos po ti bcu gsum re dang / skya chos po ti bcu gsum re bzhengs
srol yod pa nyams med je bzang du byung na'ang / zhus dag pa mkhas pa gsung rab kyi byi ngor nus pa dkon na da ni khyod kyis bstan pa la gces spras su 'gyur ba'i zhu
chen mdzod cig ces pa'i bka' lung nos pas bstan pa la dgongs te zhal gyi bzhes nas dpal 'khor chos sde'i gsar lcog khang chen du lo bco lnga'i ring tsam bka' 'gyur gyi zhus
dag mdzad/ de yang dpyid ka dang / dbyar gyi ring dpal 'khor chos sder bzhugs nas gsung rab rnams phyi mo la legs par gtugs te don zhus dang tshig zhus kyi cha dpyis phyin
du gnang zhing / bod kyi sgra mdo sum rtag dang bstun te ngag yig kyang thugs rtsom mdzad/ ston ka dang dgun po gung seng gi tshul du zhwa lu sogs su phebs nas bstan
pa bya ba rgya chen po mdzad cing / nyin zhag re'i khongs su yang yig 'bri mchod sbyin pa dang / nyan dang klog dang len bu dang / 'chad dang kha ton byed pa dang / de sames
pa dang bsgoms pa ste/ spyod pa 'di bcu'i bdag nyid ni/ bsod nams 'di bcu bla na med/ /ces pa ltar chos spyod bcu tshang dbus pa re gnang ngo / dgung lo so bdun tsam
gyi dus nyid kyi yum rang bzhin gyi mkha' 'gro ma de nyid sku gshegs te/ /gdung zhugs la sbyangs shing sA tshA btab/ zhwa lu grang chen pa dang / dkar po grwa tshang pa
gnyis la nag nye sgrub mchod kyi

thebs su zhing bzang po kha cig kyang phul/ de nas dgung lo bzhi bcu tsam gyi dus dpal 'khor chos sder zhus dag mdzad bzhin pa las lan cig mnal lam du/ zhu dag pa'i sku chas
do dam chos khrims chen mo bsod don pa zer pa gcig yod/ des rje nyid la sku 'ga' gcig phul ba sku la mnabs pas gong pa grwa lhan rnams gser chos las byas 'dug pas 'di 'dra
ci yin mi rung gsung pas de na re/ me gtong pa la mkho pa yin/ mdun de yang gser chos las byas pa yin zer ma rmis/ mnal sad pa na zhu dag ni sngar bstan pa la bsams nas
bgyis pa yin na'ang / rmi lam 'dis da ni dkar gyi rang bzhin du zad do dgongs nas/ rim phyir dgung lo zhe gnyis pa chu pho stag gi lo yul dbus kyi sa'i sman ljongs su
phebs/ gong dkar rdo rje gnad dang / stag lung sogs su chos bsgyur ba dang / phan tshun 'grel gtems dogs gcod sogs bstan pa'i bya ba rgya chen po mdzad cing / spyan ras gzigs
karma pa chos grags rgya mtshos gsang sku sogs gnang sbyin bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang bcas bod kyi skye bo rig gnas shes par 'dod na skad gnyis bsgyur pa'i zhu chen
gyi lo tsA ba mahA paNDi ta 'di nyid kyi zhabs la gtug par byos shig ces pa'i bka' shag mdzad nas bstan pa'i sgron mer bskos/ gzhan yang pho brang sne gdong dang / yar rgyab
chos kyi rgyal pos spyan drangs de dben gnas dam pa e waM dang / rgyal chen gling sogs su mi'i dbang po yab yum sras dang bcas pa mkhyen rab kyi dbang phyug de dag gi
thugs kyi re ba

yangs su bskangs sing / mi'i dbang po rnams kyis gsol ba btab nas dgung lo nga gsum pa chu mo glang gi lo rgya ston lcags ri pa'i gdan sar phebs te chos kyi 'khor lo bskor/
nga lnga pa shing mo yos bu'i lo grwa thang gi gtsug lag khang chen po dge 'dun gyi sde dang bcas pa phul nas/ der bzhugs te nags pa zla ba la dus kyi 'khor lo'i sgrub mchod
sogs dge rgyun mang po'ang gsar du btsugs shing / sa skya/ ngam ring / rta nag skyed tshal/ gsang phud rtse dang / se ra/ 'bras spungs/ nAlendra/ dwags keng / mdo khams
sogs mdor na dgon sde che phra mtha' yas pa nas chos zhu mkhan dge bshes mang po 'dus pa la sgra ka tsan/ tshad ma/ phar phyin/ 'dul ba/ mngon pa sogs dang / dus 'khor/
gshed dmar/ rdor 'phreng sogs kyi dbang bka'/ sbyor drug lam 'bras sogs gsung chos po 'khor yug tu gnang zhing / de nas dgung lo drug cu re gcig pa lcags mo bya'i lo phyag
na yod pa'i / rten rab sogs mchod cha/ gser dngul ja gos dar/ rta drel/ zangs chas sogs dngos po thams cad bsdoms te chos sde chen po zhwa lu nyid du 'gyed chen thog
mkhan slob rnams las zhu yig mdzad pa na'ang yab sras rtsa ba'i bla ma sku zhang mkhyen rab chos rje'i dgongs rdzogs la dmigs pa yin zhu bo'i phyag dam gnang zhing / mkhyen
rab chos rje thugs la dran pas spyan chab mang po mdzad/ de ltar 'gyed chen gnang ba la drung chen bkra shis dpal

ldan pa don g.yog rdzong bar gnang bas/ ri phug gi 'du khang la zhig gsobsosbyas pa'i dga' ston dang 'grig cing skabs su bab pa byung / zhwa lu ba'i rgan rabs kyi dran pa tshun
la 'gyed de las bzang pa lag tu len mi dgos rna bas kyang ma thos pa yin skad/ de'i tshe zhwa lu mkhan chen dkon mchog tshul khrims gdan sa bshol du nye pas/ zhwa lu
ba rnams nas rje nyid gdan sar spyan 'dren pa'i gros kyang bshams/ zhwa lu chos sde mo dben dang bcas pa'i zhu yig 'bul bar brag dkar rab 'byams pa sogs yang yang rje nyid
kyi drung du 'ongs kyang dbus phyogs su mi'i dbang po rnams kyi zhu nan ches pa'i mdzad dka' par gyur nas nged kyi rje bu ston gyi gdan sa pher ba'i yon tan med gsung
/ khengs skyung ya gis phyag dam mdzad/ de'i tshe zhwa lu'i rgyan gong du bu mo zhig gi khog tu bstan sru ma chen mo rdo rje rab brtan ma brloms nas nga rang gi paNDi ta
dbus nas 'byon pa yod pas spyan drongs shig bskul ba dang / zhwa lu ba'i mkhan slob dge 'dun thams cad kyang thag chod kyi spyan 'dren par drung chen gnyis/ dbu chos bzhi/
spyi pa gsum bcas grwa thang gi chos grwa chen por slebs/ grwa'i bla ma dge 'dun rnams ni rje nyid la dad zhen gyi gdung shugs ha cang ches pas gzhan du phebs 'jug pa ma
bzod cing / zhwa lu ba dang gnyis rgya 'dre shor nye ba lta bu'i zhal ma 'cham pa'i dbang gis phyag g.yog rnams la blo g.yeng chen po byung na'ang / rje nyid nas blo sbyong
bsgom la khyad che gsungs

su la'ang bka' bkyon mi gnang / de nas mi'i dbang po rnams dang / chos sde chen po gra'i gzhis byes kyi yon tan mkhan po rnams kyi thogs drangs/ dbus phyogs kyi grwa slob yon
bdag thams cad 'dus nas/ rje rin po che da cha sku na smin pas dbus bzhugs spro zhing / thugs dam 'phel ba sogs nas cis kyang gtsang du mi 'byon par bzhugs dgos zhes dbu
nan gyis zhus kyang rje'i zhal nas/ dbus skyid cing dge sbyor smar mod kyis/ de bas gzhan la tshig re tsam phan na de rang dga'/ gzhan la phan na dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal
kyang dang du len nus pa zhig dgos pa yin/ dge sbyor than thun dang / bde skyid don du mi gnyer/ na so rgas kyang re zhig a tho yod/ zhwa lu ba rnams mos zhen che bas bsam
pa mi bzlog/ dge 'dun gyi bka' yang mi bcogs pa yin/ da res rje bu ston gyi bstan pa la bsams nas 'gro ba lags so gsung / 'on kyang slar dbus phyogs su 'gro ba'i don
la phebs pa'i zhal bzhes bzang po ni mdzad do/ /de nas mi'i dbang po rnams kyi pho brang so sor gdan drangs nas 'bul ba bzang po byas zhing / rim pas gtsang du chibs kha
bsgyur/ yang rgyab sogs nas chos rgyal chen po dpon g.yog rnams kyang thugs phreng bzhin du chibs skyel du dol sna mo la'i bang byon/ skyid shod du lcags mal mdzad/ gam pa
phur smyug la ba sogs kyi thab 'dzin dang / slar dbus su phebs dgos zhu ba dang / zhabs brtan shis brjod

kyi zhu phrin bzang po'ang slebs/ de nas rim bzhin rong rin spungs mi dbang chen pos zhag lnga'i bar thab 'dzin bten nas bsnyen bkur 'bul ba mtha' yas pa mdzad/ stag gru khar
zhwa lu ba'i thab 'dzin bzang po sleb/ dga' ba gdong du nang so lhun grub rtse bas bsnyen bkur zab/ de ltar nyid kyi dgung lo don bzhi pa shing pho khyi'i lo smin drug
zla ba'i tshes pa bcu dgu'i nyin zhwa lur phyag phebs pa yin/ phebs pa'i nyin kyang nam mkha' la 'ja' kha dog sna tshogs pas gdugs dang rgyal mtshan dang / me tog dang /
ljon shing gi rnam pas khyab cing / dge 'dun brgya phrag shin tu mang pos rol mo dang / mchod rdzas sna tshogs thog pas ser sgreng / skye bo'i tshogs kyis glu gzhas sogs
rtsed sna mi 'dra ba du ma dang bcas tshong 'dus kyi bgam pa gong nas zhwa lu bar la khrom chen pos 'brel zhing lam la yang mi thar ba lta bur gyur te/ de 'dra ba ni sngar
zhwa lu mkhan po mi dgos gzhan su la yang byung ba'i sgros med zer dogs med pa yang 'dug rje 'di nyid 'brel tshad don ldan gyi skyes bu dam pas lam gyi yon tan mthar phyin
pa de'i rten 'brel gyi che ba yin par gda'/ tshes bcu dgu la phebs nas nyi shu la thugs ngal gsos/ nyi shu gcig la lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyi 'dren pa rgyal ba
rin chen grub kyi sengge'i khri la mnga' gsol/ 'di skabs zhwa lu ba'i chab srid sengge rtsa ba'i skyong skabs yin gshis khri ston 'bul ba dang bcas pa bzang po sgrub/ rje
nyid nas kyang ri mthil gnyis su mang 'gyed gya nom pa gnang

de nas ri phug tu thog mar bsnyen rdzogs zhu ba mang po byung ste de dag la dge slong gi sdom pa stsal/ nye skor chu lho byang gi yon bdag che phra mang po nas bsnyen bkur
dang khri ston gyi mang ja zhu mkhan rim pas slebs/ khyad par dbus nas gnang rtse sdings dang / bde chen yangs ba tsan nas spyan mnga' chos kyi rgyal po'i zhabs kyi legs
'bul dka' shog ched du mngags nas phebs pa'ang 'di ltar/ rgyal ba'i gsung rab mdo sngags mtha' dag dang / tha snyad gtsug lag khang rab 'byams thugs chud nas/ gangs can bstan
pa 'dzin pa'i gtsor gyur ba/ kun mkhyen bu ston ring lugs rgyas gyur cing / ces shis brjod pa sngon du 'gro bas thams cad mkhyen pa de nyid kyi sengge'i khri la mngon
par 'khod nas/ bstan pa mtha' dag 'dzin pa'i rgyal thabs la dbang bskur pa skad gnyis smra ba'i dbang po gang gi phyag tu bzhes pa nas/ sku khams bde bar gdan sa'i 'dren
pa dam par/ gtso bor gyur ba'i 'dus pa rgya mtshos bkra shis kyi mnga' gsol grub pa'i skabs su/ 'di nas kyang spro ba dang bcas pa'i ngag gis phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas byang
sems rnams la bden pa bskul ba'i gsol ba 'debs pa byas te/ dengdengs nas bzungs te bstan pa 'dzin pa'i 'phrin las yun ring du skyong ba'i bzhed pa yar ngo'i zla ba ltar
gong nas gong du 'phel bar gyur cig /ces sogs kyi bka' yig ja gos dar gyi gnang

sbyin blos mi 'khyud pa dang bcas pa'ang byung ngo / /de ltar zhwa lu nyid du gzhis byes kyi dge 'dun bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'dus pa la/ sgra snyan dngags sogs tha snyad kyi
gtsug lag gtso bor gsungs/ rab byung dang bsnyen rdzogs kyang mang bar sgrub/ chos sde chen po'i sgrigs rnams gzhag rnams dam par mdad/ dge rgyun chags pa rnams kyi thebs
su gzhis rten bzang po btsugs/ dge 'dun gyi tshogs su'ang bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i bka' chems kyi yi ge rnams lan mang du klog pa mdzad de/ tshogs kyang nyin re bzhin
kun spyod 'jam du song zhing khrims 'jags pa mdzad/ mkhan po'i bya ba yang bu ston chen pos mkhan po gdan sa pa la gdams pa'i zhal chems nas 'byung ba bzhin mdzad/ de
nas zhwa lu'i dgun chos gsungs te/ thog mar blo mtho ba'i don du bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i phar phyin lung gi snye ma gsungs/ de nas kun gyi go sla ba bu ston chos 'byung
chen mo'i bshad lung gsungs/ de nas skye bo'i tshogs shin tu mang po la/ bsnyen gnas dang / skyabs 'gro dang / bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang / ma Ni'i lung sogs nyin re
bzhin chos mi 'dra ba du ma gsungs/ gsung chos gnang ba de dag kyang tshig zur phyin pa dang / rna bar 'bab pa'i gsung gdangs snyan pos bsdu na shlauka gcig la chos thams
cad 'dus pa 'chad thub pa dang / rgyas pa na shlauka gcig gi don la yang nyi ma rtser gang 'gro ba dang / de dag kyang gsung rab kyi gnad ston pa/ sems

la phan pa 'ba' zhig ma gtogs don go rgyu ci yang med pa'i sgra cal col ni nam du'ang mi srid do/ /de dus chos ra rgya che bas bzhugs khri'i rtser bsdad kyang gsung ha cang
mi che ba dang / chos ri'i mtha' rgyang ring bor bsdad kyang gsung ha cang mi chung ba dang / me tog gi char pa lag pas 'dzin thub pa babs pa sogs ya mtshan gyi rtags mang
po' byung / de nas rgyun par ri phug chos kyi pho brang du bzhugs/ sku zhang bsod nams mchog grub dpal bzang pos bskul te/ rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang bu ston thams cad
mkhyen pa nas brgyud cing phyag len gyi rgyun ma nyams par dbang zhu mi grwa slob shin tu mang po la gnang / sbyor ba yan lag drug gi 'khrid kyang btsugs shing / ri phug
gi chos khri thad kar phebs te nyi ma mang po'i bar la dge 'dun shin tu mang ba la brgyad stong pa sogs kyi gsung chos gnang / bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i rnam thar snyim

gyi skabs su spyan chab mang po mdzad/ de lta bu'i tshul gyis gdan sa lo bcu gcig gi bar bskyangs te de dus zhwa lu ri mthil gyi chos grwar 'chad nyan 'phel tshul sogs

gsal chol leb re dang / sgra'i mtshams sbyor lnga ba gyo le ba re mi shes mkhan yod pa mi srid skad/ de yang lung las/ gang zhig gser gyi ri la gnas gyur na/ /de yi 'dab chags
rnams kyang gser du gyur/ /zhes pa ltar/ rje 'di'i byin rlabs kyi rnam 'phrul 'ba' zhig tu zad do/ /gzhan du na/ mkhan po slob bong bu lta bu res pas na/ grwa pa khyi
lod lug khyu las mang pa re 'ong zer ba de yang bden pa gda' 'o/ /phyis kyi gnas skabs gzigs pas gsal lo/ /de nas sa skya'i bdag chen 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams sku

gsungs/ de nas yar rgyab chob kyi rgyal pos spyan 'dren dod drag pas/ slar yang nyi ma dbus kyi cha la khams su slebs/ sna bo la nas chos rgyal chen pos chibs su mdzad/

gyi bsam pa'i re ba yongs su gang

pa'i tshe/ /kun mkhyen gnyis pa sa paN nyid dang mtshungs/ /gnyis med ting 'dzin ngang la 'jog pa'i tshe/ /nA ro'i zhabs dang dpal ldan birU pa/ /byams pa'i thugs kyis

sha dang mgon po khyod/ /nam yang dbye ba med par bdag gis khums/ /zhes so/ thugs sras skyogs ston lo chen gyi zhal nas kyang / bdag cag gi rje bla ma dam pa chos rje thams
cad mkhyen pa zhwa lu lo tsA ba zhes grags pa'i yid bzhin gyi nor bu 'di nyid rtsod dus kyi rgyal ba gnyis pa rang yin/ deng sang gi mkhas grub gzu bor gnas pa rnams

'bum phrag gsum pa rin chen chos

kyi dbang po dang / skyogs lo thams cad mkhyen pa rin chen bkra shis ngo mtshar bye ba'i blo gros sogs kyis mdzad pa'i rnam thar gyi yi ge ma mo ngag las shes so/ /gsung rtsom
kyang bla ma yi dam gyi bstod pa'i rab byed skor dang / zhi ba lha/ spang lo chen po/ kun mkhyen dol po pa/ mkhyen rab pa chos rje rnams kyi rnam thar/ dus 'khor dang
/ bde mchog dril bu lus dkyil sogs kyi cho ga'i skor/ mngon rtogs rgyan 'grel pa/ sgra ka lA pa'i 'grel pa tsandra pa'i 'grel pa/ ka lA pa'i mtshams sbyor lnga bye brag
tu bshad pa/ ming ye yan gyi spyi bshad/ ka lA pa'i sa bcad/ snyan dngags me long gi bsdus don/ sdebs sbyor gyi bsdus don/ tsandra pa'i yi ge'i bsdu ba/ sum rtags kyi 'grel
pa/ dag yig za ma tog bkod pa sogs de ltar mdzad pa'i bstan bcos rnams kyang bsregs bcad brdar ba'i gser bzhin du 'khrul pa'i g.ya' dang bral ba bstan pa'i su 'gro ba
sha stag go/ 'gyur rnam grangs mi 'dra ba che chung sdoms bzhi bcu zhe brgyad tsam nyid kyi rgya dpe las gzhi 'gyur mdzad pa dang / de las gzhan pa'i 'gyur bcos dang / hor

'da' ba mdzad nas dgung lo brgyad cu gya bzhi pa la zhwa lu ri phug tu nye gnas chos 'khor blo gros kyi gzim mal sku 'dra

bzhengs / de la rab tu gnas pa dang nyid kyis mdad nas zhwa lu'i gdan sar skyo ston bsod nams rgyal mtshan bskos/ de nas grwa thang du phebs te dgung lo brgyad cu gya bdun
pa me mo phag gi lo grwa'i gdan sar thugs sras pad dkar lo chen bskos nas nyid kyi me tog gtor/ der gdul bya phyi ma thams cad smin grol la bkod de/ brgyad cu rtsa brgyad
pa me pho byi ba'i lo ngo mtshar gyi cho 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang bcas rgyal ba byams pa mgon po'i thugs khar sprul pa'i sna ba bsdus so/ /nang rten rin po che
'ba' zhig las grub pa'i rje nyid kyi snang brnyan dang / gser 'bum thog tshad ma sogs grwa'i gtsug lag khang du bzhengs shing / lo dus kyi mchod pa rgya chen po'ang gnas
de nyid dang zhwa lu gnyis su sngar btsugs par grags mod/ da ni gtam tsam yang ri bong gi rwa bzhin du dkon pa'i chos te/ de yang rgya rol las/ srid gsum mi rtag ston ka'i
sprin dang 'dra/ 'gro ba skye 'chi gar la lta dang mtshungs skyes bu'i tshe srog nam mkha'i glog 'dra ste/ /ri zar 'bab chu bzhin du myur mgyogs 'gro/ zhes pa ltar yin
pa'i tsul de lta bu'i don la yang bsam par bya'o/ / / /gsum pa ni/ rin chen grub bstan rgyal po'i srid 'dzin mkhas/ /zhes 'byung bas/ rgyal ba byang gling pa dpon po rin
chen rgyal po de ni/ sku 'khrungs pa'i gnas sngar ri phug gi dgon smad mtshams na byang gling zer ba'i grong yod pas/ der mkhas grub chen po mgon pa rgyal

mtshan zhes bya ba sogs bshes gnyen dam pa 'ga' zhig gi rnag rigs kyi dbon brgyud du sku 'khrungs shing mtshan la dbon po zhes thogs pa'i rgyu mtshan yang de ltar yin/ gzhon
nu nyid nas ri phug dgon par rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje'i drung du rab tu byung / phyis bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa'ang de las bzhes par mngon/ kun mkhyen chos grub
dpal bzang dang / mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs bshes gnyen pa sogs bla ma dam pa mang du bsten/ khyad par rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje nyid bka' drin 'gran zla dang bral
ba'i rtsa ba'i bla mar mdzad/ rgyud sde bzhi la mkhas pa'i mchog tu gyur pa'i gsang sngags rab 'byams pa chen por gyur cing / dpal 'khor bde chen du phebs nas rin sdings
grwa tshang gi bla ma thogs shig mdad/ de nas ri phug dgon stod byang gling du bzhugs nas chos 'khor rgya chen po bskor cing / brgyud 'dzin slob ma'i gtso bo yang / gnas
brtan bstan pa bzang po/ 'brog khang pa don grub rgyal mtshan/ sku zhang chos rje bsod nams mchog grub/ byang gling pa rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan sogs mtha' yas/
mdzad pa rnam thar rgyas pa dang gsung 'bum gyi rim pa deng skabs ma rned kyang gsung rab thor bu tsam bdag gi mthong ba la rdor dbyings kyi dkyil mchog rin chen bsam 'phel
gyi lhan thabs/ de'i slob ma dbang bskur la mkho ba'i lhan thabs/ mi 'khrugs pa'i dkyil mchog gi dka' gnas bo dong pa'i chos brgyud 'dzin pa paN chen pad ma gar dbang
yang thog mar zhwa lu'i rtsi grwa mdzad cing rje 'di'i slob ma yin cing phyis bo dong pa'i bstan 'dzin gyi gtso bor gyur to/ /

gsal byed de'i ro bsregs kyi cho ga shin tu gsal ba/ kun rig gi cho ga'i zin bris/ 'jam dpal chos dbyings gsung dbang gi phyag rgya'i 'ching tshul/ gshed dmar lha lnga'i lhan
thabs sogs snang zhing / de dag kyang tshig sbyor legs legs 'dra ba mi 'dug na'ang / don gyi dka' gsan 'ba' zhig gsal bar ston pa'i legs bshad rmad du byung ba kho na
yod/ gzhan yang snye mo sku zhang chos rje rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan gyi zhal gdams las/ lta ba'i mthar thugs chos kun sgyu mar sbyangs/ bsgom pa'i mthar thug rig pa
brjen la bor/ /spyod pa'i mthar thug sdig spong dge ba bsgrub/ /chos 'di snying la bzungs shig gzhon nu rnams/ /zhes gsungs pa lta bu'i lta bsgom spyod 'bras phyin ci ma
log pa gzhir bzungs te/ 'jig rten chos brgyad kyis ma g.yos bar thugs dam nyams bzhes lhur mdzad cing / gsung rtsom rnams kyi sbyar byang phal cher la'ang phyogs med kyi
bya bral ba dge slong rin chen rgyal pos sbyar ba'o zhes gsung ba kho na yod/ zhal las kyang / 'jig rten gyi byang ngoms nas skye bo dam par rlom pa dang / chos nas bshad
pa bzhin mi byed par tshe 'di'i 'du long mang po bsags nas bstan pa 'dzin pa yin zer ba dang / de lta bu'i bla ma'i zhabs tog yong du re yang / ji skad du/ rjes paN gyi/
khyi rgan ya skan phug pa'i khrag /rus pa'i bcud du bsgos nas 'cha'/ /zhes pa ltar mkhas pa dag khrel ba'i rgyu kho na yin zhes gsungs skad de don la yang mang ba snang
ngo / /mdor na bdag nyid chen po 'dis ni/ rgyal bstan spyi dang bye

brag kun mkhyen bu ston zhabs kyi bstan pa la phyag bris che ba mdzad pa yin te/ kun gzigs lnga pa chen po'i zhal nas kyang / /zab don 'byor pa blo dang mtshams pa'i rin/ /'bad
pa chen pos nyer 'khug rgyal ba'i bstan/ /rgyas mdzad bzang po'i skal ba ldan pa'i rje/ /yongs 'dzin dam pa'i mgon la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes bsngags pa mdzad pa yin no/
/'di nyid kyi ri phug byang gling gi gdan sa mdzad pa'i ring la/ mkhan chen rigs 'dzin rgyal po dang / 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog tshul khrims khri thog tu bzhugs so/ gsol
'debs las/ sku zhang rigs las rin chen mchog tu grub/ /rnam bkra bskyed rim shis pa'i dpal la 'byor/ /rgyal ba kun 'dus tshar pa rdo rje 'chang / /mtshungs med dam pa gsum
la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes 'byung bas/ dang po sku zhang rigs las rin chen mchog tu grub/ /ces pa lce btsun rin po che bsod nams mchog grub dpal bzang po da ni 'khrungs yul
zhwa lu phu nub kyi gnas gsar dge 'phel du/ yab rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje'i sku'i gcung po sku zhang rgyal ba rnam sras pa dang / yum mkhar ba ba'i sras mo hor
btsun rgyal mo gnyis kyi sras su rab byung brgyad pa'i kun 'dzin zhes pa sa pho byi ba'i lo la sku bltams/ mtshan tshe brtan lhun grub rgya mtsho zhes gsol/ sku gzhon nu'i
dus nas thugs sgam zhing chos srid kyi gnad la mkhyen pa'i spyan bkra ba zhig byung pas rgyal mkhar

rtser bdag chen don grub 'phags kyi nang blon mdzad/ de skabs phyag g.yog rnams kyi sku rgyan dang na bza' sogs dang 'khor la 'os pa'i cha byad phul pa na/ lus bem po mi gtsang
ba'i snod 'di la rgyan btags pa dgos pa gang yod pa yin nam dgongs pa thugs la shar zhing 'jig rten chos brgyad kyi sbub nas grol ba zhig de dus nas ka yod ces grags/
phebs bzhud sogs kyi tshe ngan slongs rnams dang srang kha'i khyi sogs la gsol zan gyi sku sbyor re sgrig chug mdzad de gnang / mthong smon du phebs nas 'jig rten gyi bya
ba la snying po ci yang mi 'dug pas da ni sa skya'i gong ma rnams kyi mdzad pa ltar rten skya po yin yang dge sbyor byed dgos pa 'dug gsung nas gzim chung du thugs dam
kho na mdzad/ de'ang 'chi ba mi rta pa la thugs sbyong ba'i tshul dang sa lugs kyi bde mchog dril bu lus dkyil la nyams bzhes gnang / de skabs mkhyen rab rje rgyal rtser
bdag po'i drung du phebs nas rje nyid la rgya mtsho dge sbyor gang byed kyin yod ces gsungs pa la/ bdag sa skya'i dril bu lus dkyil la byed kyin yod zhus pas/ sku zhang
chos rje nam mkha'i mtshan can nas bzung nged rang rnams la byin rlabs kyi tshan ka tsha ba'i gnad cig yod pas gshed dmar lha lnga 'di la byas na legs gsungs/ de nas dbang
bka' sogs ni sngar sor mkhyen rab chos rje las thob zin pas de 'bral phyag dpe gzigs nas gshed dmar lha lnga'i bsnyen pa mdzad/ mkhyen rab chos rje

dpal 'khor chos sde'i brag tag tu bzhugs skabs bka' lung la/ byed la yab 'di gshegs dus grogs byed mkhan med pa'i 'o rgyal ba gcig yod pa 'dug ste/ 'on kyang bla ma mos gus
dga' tshad 'dug pas bya ba gang la yang bar chad med pa dang / khyad par ri phug shar chen gyi rdo rje 'chang bzhugs pa'i mchod kang du dkar me'i mchod pa dang / rdor dbyings
dus 'khor sogs kyi bsgrub mchod rnams ma chags par yongs pa 'dug ces sogs ma 'ongs lung bstan pa cig kyang zhal 'chems kyi tshul du gnang / de nas bdag chen dpon g.yog
'dul chung du phebs dus gsol rgyu'i bshas lug 'ga' re gsod pa'i zhal bkod mdzad dgos pa byung pas thugs la tshad med pa'i snying rje drag po 'khrungs shing / rgyal sras
thogs med pas/ thogs med dus nas drin gyis bskyangs pa'i ma/ /las kyi shina'ang 'chi ma dbyungs rig na/ /de dag sha yi ched du bsad pa'i sha/ za ba rig pa min no shas
rab grub/ /ces gsungs pa rjes su dran nas sha zhus kyi mi bzhes pa'i nges 'byung dang zhen log gi 'da' byung / skabs shig zang phu lung mjal bar ri phug nas zhabs thang mdzad
nas byon/ ayon padma la gsol ba tab pas mkhyen rab rje dang ngos su mjal nas gdams pa dang rjes su bstan pa yang thog gsungs/ de rjes rkyang 'dur bde ba can sogs kyi
bla ma grub pa'i dbang phyug rin chen dpal gyi drung du phebs nas

gshed dmar spros med dang / ma gcig gi zab don thugs snying la sogs gsan zhing der rgyal sras dngul cha pa'i zhal nas/ bag med sdig pa chen po bskyed pa'i rgyu/ /chang dang
gsad sha spong zhing zas gzhan yang / /ched du 'bad rtsol sgo nas mi bsgrub pa'i/ /dam bca' mtha' ru skyol zhig sangs rgyas dpal/ /zhes gsungs pa'i tshul la bslab dgos dgongs
nas rdor dkar mdzad par dam bca' phul bas/ bla mas de ltar gnang ba ngo mtshar che mod 'on kyang da dung chos mdzad na legs zhes gsung ba dang / gzhan 'ga' zhig nas
kyang mkhyen rab chos rje'i chos brgyud 'dzin pa la sku mdun drung rang gi rab byung bzhes na 'gro phan che tshul zhus shing / rje rang gi thugs la'ang rab tu byung 'dod
kho na 'khrungs te/ khyim thabs kyi bya ba mtha' dag de 'phral dug bzhin du skyur ba gnang / dgung lo sum cu so gsum pa drag po bzhes pa lcags sprel lo/ /hor zla brgyad
pa'i dmar phyogs kyi bzang po gnyis pa'i grib tshod skyes bu gcig gi dus/ 'og min gnyis pa ri phug chos kyi pho brang du/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang skyo ston rigs 'dzin rgyal
pos mkhan slob sbrags ma mdzad cing / gsang ston 'dul 'dzin shes rab legs pa dang / dus go ba gnas brtan bkra shis rab gsal/ dad pa'i dge 'dun rgyal ba byang gling pa
rin chen chos kyi rgyal po sogs mkhan slob dge 'dun dang bcas pa lnga phrag gnyis la gcig gi lhag pa'i dbus su dge bsnyen dang / tshigs snga ma dge tshul dang / bsnyen
par rdzogs pa

dge slong gi dngos po'i bar dus gcig la bsgrub te 'dul ba 'dzin pa yongs kyi mchog nye ba 'khor gnyis pa lta bur byas so/ /de nas bzung bslab bya phra mo tshun chad la spang
blang mdzad cing tshul khrims rnam par dga' gzhir bzung ste/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyi drung du dus 'khor bdag po chen po'i dbang / gshed dmar bcu gsum ma/
gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa/ phyag rdor 'gro bzang rnams kyi dbang bka'/ zhwa lu pa'i 'khrid chen bzhi sogs gsung chos mang ba gsan/ zhwa lu mkhan chen dkon mchog tshul khrims
kyi drung gur rigs bsdus kyi dbang / nA ro mkha' spyod kyi skor/ gser chos dmar po skor gsum sogs gsan/ chos rje byang gling dpon rgyal ba'i drung / rdor dbyings rtsa lugs
'grel pa lugs/ rtse mo rigs bsdus/ rdo rje mi 'khrug pa jo lugs/ phyag rdor 'chi bdag 'joms pa/ shAkya sengge gtsug gtor dgu pa/ 'chi med rnga sgra/ tshe dpag med/ grub
rgyal lugs sogs kyi dbang bka'/ bu ston bka' 'bum sogs lung rab tu mang po/ gsang ba'i dus nag 'khrid gser sdings pas mdzad pa'i skor dang / sems 'khrid yid bzhin nor
bu/ dmar 'khrid tshem bu lugs sogs 'khrid bka' mang ba gsan/ dus 'khor shar chen pa'i chos rje rgyal yam gsum pa'i drung rdo rje gdan bzhi'i yab bka' yum bka'i dbang rdzogs
par gsan/ mon rdzong ras pa zla ba rgyal mtshan gyi drung dmar po skor gsum/ gur zhal gnyis/ rta mgrin

skyer sgang lugs sogs kyi rjes gnang chos skor lung dang bcas pa/ gzhan yang ba ri brgya rtsa'i rjes gnang / rgya gzhung gi lung / ye shes kyi mgon po phyag drug pa nag po
bar chad kun sel/ gsang bsgrub/ grib sel/ gnad dbab/ mgon dkar yid bzhin nor bu/ lha bzhi dril sgrub/ mgon po mtshan kha sogs kyi rjes gnang / de dag gi sgrub skor las tshogs
dang bcas pa'i lung / phag mo gzhung drug skor/ rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi chos tshan du ma'i lung / shangs chos na gu'i skor/ dam pa sangs rgyas nas brgyud pa'i dam chos
sdug bsngal zhi byed skor/ lce sgoms pa'i mgur 'bum/ man ngag rin spungs sogs dang / gcod dbang nam mkha'i sgo 'byed/ grub rgyal lha mang gi dbang sogs zab chos shin tu
mang ba gsan zhing 'di skabs khrid gsan pa rnams kyang bla ma'i spyan sngar nyams myong ma skyes bar bsgom par mdzad pas/ sku zhang chos rjes khyed la nyams dga' rab skyes
'dug ste/ da dung des sa lam cung mi chod pas/ a pha'i glu 'di la nyon gsung / dwangs gsal rnyogs med kyi sems nyid 'di/ ngo bo rig pa rang bzhin stong / /mtshan nyid
gsal ba gsum ldan te/ /gdod nas lhan skyes lhun grub po/ /ces sogs mgur gnang / 'di skabs mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen la lam 'bras gsan rgyu'i zhu yig 'bul mkhan btang
bas/ re zhig 'then mdzod/ nged dbyar dga' ba gdong du lam 'bras 'chad pas de dus shog gsung ba 'byor nas re zhig sku mtshams mdzad/

de nas dga' ba gdong du phebs te rje mus pa'i drung du/ gsung ngag lam 'bras/ nA ro mkha' spyod/ bde mchog dkar po sogs kyi dbang khrid lung dang bcas pa mtha' dag bum pa gang
byor gsan/ de dus mus chen gyi mkhan po dang / rje nyid kyi las slob gnang ste chos rje 'ba' rab nam mkha' rgyal mtshan bsnyen rdzogs bsgrub/ dga' ba gdong gi grwa pa
mang pos kyang rje nyid la gsung chos zhus te gzhan don gyi sgo bye/ sngar rab tu ma byung ba'i gong du mkhyen rab rje'i drung / dus 'khor/ gshed dmar sogs dbang dang bshad
bka' mang po gsan pa yin la/ de dag dang 'og tu 'byung ba'i lo chen thams cad mkhyen pa dang bcas pa mgon bka' drin che ba'i bla ma rnams yin no/ /gzhan yang lo tsA ba
rin chen bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ dpal 'khor ches sde'i mkhan po jo gdan pa sogs chos 'brel gsan pa'i bla ma ni mang du yod snang ngo / /de nas ri phug gi gzim khang gong
du dpal rdo rje dbyings kyi bsnyen pa mdzad nas kha skong gi sbyin bsreg gi dus/ thab nang du me kha dog shel ltar dwangs pa'i dbus su dung dang rgyal mtshan/ dpal be'u
sogs kyi rnam pa shin tu gsal 'byung ba mchod g.yog rnams kyi mthong nas dad par gyur/ bla brang shar chen du gshed dmar gyi bsnyen sgrub mdzad pa'i tshe yang ngo mtshar
gyi rtags sna tshogs shar/ dgung lo zhe drug pa dpal gdong zhes pa chu mo bya'i lo snye mo ru dgon gsar smon 'grub chos

sdings kyi gdan sa spyan 'dren pa'i zhu ba slebs/ rje nyid nas dgon chung sdug bsngal gyi btson ra yin par dgongs/ nged kyi dgon pa'i bdag rkyen mi pher bas mi yongs zhes sna
len mdzad kyang bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i chos kyi rgyal srid 'dzin pa mkhan chen dkon mchog tshul khrims dang / chos rje byang gling dpon rgyal ba gnyis kyi zhal
nas/ ru dgon pa 'di nged rang rnams kyi chos brgyud kha gtsang du 'dzin pa dang / khyad par sku zhang gi gdung rus gcig pas lugs gnyis kyi 'brel pa mthun pa 'dug pas cis
kyang phebs dgos gsung zhing bla ma'i bka' gyen du ldog ma nus par lo gsum zhal bzhes mdzad nas pho nya rnams phyir brdzangs nges/ slar hor zla gnyis pa'i mjug la ri phug
nas btegs te shar gru khar gzhis ka rin spungs pa'i gnang sbyin gyi ja zhal khrab/ rnam rgyal gling pas gtso mdzad snye mo pa rnams kyi chibs bsu'ang 'byor te nags pa zla
ba'i tshes brgyad la rigs ldan chos kyi rgyal po rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhabs btegs sengge'i khri la mnga' gsol mdzad/ chos dung byin rlabs can
dung gshog gi nang la nor bu'i bye brag yod pas thog drangs sprod rnams rtsis pa zhes brkyangs te thog ma'i shis brjod kyang dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud tshig zab mos mdzad
pas nam mkha' la 'ja' kha dog sna lnga dang / bkra shis rtags brgyad/ ral gri/ padma sogs kyi dbyibs can mang pos 'brel/ me tog gi char chen po nyi ma gsum gyi bar du bab
pa sogs dus kyi 'khor

lo'i bshad pa'i 'phrin las 'phel ba'i rten 'brel mtha' dag rang 'grig tu byung / de yang rgyud las/ nags pa'i mthar ni dkar po'i tshig la gzhan la phan pa'i bla ma'i dkyil
'khor dag ni bzhengs byas nas/ sdig pa'i dri ma 'phrog pa'i dbang bdun rnams ni bsod nams/ don du bu rnams dag la sbyin par bya/ zhes gsungs pa dang rjes su mthun par dpal
dus kyi 'khor lo'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor chen po bzhengs te byis pa 'jug pa'i dbang bdun/ dbang gong ma che chung / rdo rje slob dpon bdag po chen po'i dbang dang
bcas pa dbang cha nyi shu rtsa lnga pa tshar drug la gnang de nas dbyar chos kyi dus sgrub dkyil phyag len gyi skor la gsung bshad dang skal bar ldan pa'i slob ma nyi shu
tsam la rdo rje rnal 'byor yan lag drug gi zab khrid zla ba gsum gyi ring la grub pa gnang / de yang rang re bu lugs la nges don gyi khrid skyong ba'i tshe sems 'tshol sogs
kyi tha snyad mi mdzad pa'o/ de skabs rje nyid nas gcer mthong ngo shes kyi lta ba'i skabs sems 'tshol zhes pa'i brda chos shig kyang mdzad/ 'on kyang sems 'tshol zhes
pa ni phyag rdzogs kyi khrid byed pa rnams la grags che mod kyi ngo sprod kyi bshad pa ci yang ma song bar sems 'tshol zhig ces brjod kyang da lta'i gang zag phal cher
la brda chad cig rnyed rgyu yong dka' zhing / ngo sprod kyi bshad pa thob phyin chad sems log nas 'tshol rgyu med pa'i don zhig shugs la go yong pas sems 'tshol zhes pa 'di

rang dgos nus chung zhing / rje btsong kha pa'i dbu ma lta 'khrid kyi skabs thog mar dgag bya nges pa'i gnad gcig tu mdzad nas bdag 'dzin lhan skyes kyi blo'i 'char tshul la
ngos 'dzin dgos par gsung ba ni las dang po pa'i gang zag rnams la nad thog tu 'gro nges pa'i sman thun gcig tu mthong ngo / /de dus dge slong sangs rgyas 'phel gyi nyin
mo bsgom ma byas par sham thabs la lhan pa 'debs kyin bsdad pas/ rje nyid kyi thugs mkhyen gyis gzigs nas gsung chos skabs mi mang tshogs sar/ sbyor ba yan lag drug bsgom
nas rtags bcu rdzogs pa la/ rnam rtog gzhan gyi spro bsdu spangs te rtse gcig tu mnyam par 'jog dgos pa yin/ 'o skol gyi sgom chen pa rnams ni de'i dod du sham thabs la
ras kyi lhan pa 'debs kyin 'dug ces bka' bkyon mdzad pas thams cad han brdal ba bzhin gyur nas sgom la blo bskyed che ba byung ngo / /slar hor zla dgu pa'i nang du ri phug
tu phebs nas sku mtshams mdzad/ shing khyi nag nya'i dus su bu dgon par phebs nas gsung chos kyi 'phro rnams gnang zhing / tshe dpag med kyi sku rgyab mtho nyi shu rtsa
bzhi yod pa bzhengs pa'i nang bzhugs su thugs sras sems dpa' chen po rin chen rnam rgyal gyi 'chi med rnga sgra'i dbang rdzas shing tog bil ba phyag dreg ma byin rlabs
can gcig rje nyid kyi sku bsrung khron na yod pa de rten gyi thugs kar bzhugs pa gnang zhing gzhan yang mdo rgyud dang mthun pa'i ring bsrel rnam bzhis

phyur bur gtams par mdzad/ rab gnas dngos gzhi yang dus 'khor thugs dkyil gyi steng nas phyag g.yog dge 'dun nyis brgya dang bcas pas nyi ma gnyis kyi bar la gnang / gzhan
yang der 'dus pa dag la gsung chos rgya che bar gnang zhing zhal gdams mgur 'di'ang gsungs so/ / //nam 'chi cha med kyi tshe zhabs la/ /dus yun ring sdod rtsis ma byed par/
/skyes chen 'degs pa'i dus tshod du/ /blo nyams nga med pa'i chos shig mdzod/ /gus ldan gyi gtsug tu bsten 'os pa'i/ /mtshan ldan gyi bla ma g.yang chen de/ /snod ldan
gyi slob mas ci dgar spyod/ /de skal ldan gyi khyad chos yin par sems/ /a ho rkyen snang thugs phrad lam du 'khyer ba dang / /sems la shar tshad dran pas zin pa dang / /thams
cad rmi lam sgyur mar shes pa gsum/ /'di dag rjes thob dus su nyams su longs/ /bkra shis pa'i mchod dbyangs de la mdzod/ /ces gsungs nas hor zla brgyad pa'i mjug la
ri phug tu phebs shing bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa gnyis pa ma hA lo tsA ba dharmA pA la bha dra'i zhal snga nas kyi drung du/ rdo rje 'phreng ba dkyil 'khor bzhi bcu zhe
bzhi'i dbang bka' dang / dkyil chog rdor phreng / mngon rtogs rnal 'byor rdzogs 'phreng / sbyin sreg 'od kyi snye ma/ rje de nyid kyi mdzad pa'i brgyud 'debs/ paN chen
nags rin nas brgyud pa'i sbyor drug /nyi zla bsgrub pa sha wa ri'i sbyor drug /ye shes spyan

bsgrub / ma hA ya' rdzogs rim/ spar bu bas mdzad pa'i do ha'i yig cha/ de'i sa bcad/ mtshan don/ bsdus don rnams kyi lung / su kha chos drug gi 'khrid/ ne gu chos drug gi bka'
bcu dang sgyu lus dbang mo che/ chos drug rdo rje tshig rkang sogs ne gu'i 'khrid skor rdzogs pa/ mkha' spyod dkar dmar gyi bka'/ gzhan yang zhal bzhi pa'i rjes gnang
/ 'dod rgyal dang tshogs bdag gi rjes gnang sogs zab chos dpag tu med pa gsan nas nyams su myong ba mdzad do/ /de nas dge 'khor gyi sa cha na btsan brag zer ba'i sgrub gnas
yod pas der sku mtshams shin tu dam pa mdzad/ de grol nas ri phug tu brag po che'i dge slong kun dga' rnam rgyal dpon slob bcu skor dang / ri phug gzhi grwa sogs la sgrub
thabs brgya rtsa'i rjes gnang skor stsal zhing de'i tshe lhas me tog gi char bab pa kun gyi mthong ba byung / rgyal rtse nas bdag po'i bka' gnang nas dbang ldan chos
'khor gyi gdan sar phebs te rtse mo sgrub mchod dang gsung chos zhu mkhan rnams kyi re ba bskangs/ slar yang btsan brag ri khrod du phebs te dpon po shAkya dang / rtogs
ldan chos 'phel sogs la ne gu chos drug gnang nas khrid lo legs pas mnyes pa byung yang tshogs 'khor gyi dus sku khams mnyes pas/ zhabs 'bring pa dag gis sman pa zhig bos
pa legs tshul zhus pas/ de 'dra mi dgos/ khams dga' rab yongs/ ni gu chos drug 'di mkhyen rab rjes gnang dus kyang 'tshub pa byung 'dug de len

kyang de kha'i 'tshub tu gda'/ slar rtogs ldan chos 'phel la yang chos mgo mi 'thon pa'i bar chad gcig yong ba 'dra/ nga yang zhwa lur 'gro dgos pa'i rmi ltas shig byung gsung
/ de kho na bzhin byung ste rje nyid kya zhwa lur chos rje ser thang pa gshegs pa'i yar 'dren la spyan 'dren zhus/ btsan brag tu phebs nas gnas brtan bsod legs pa sogs
la dam pa sangs rgyas kyi zhi byed skor gnang nas rje mon rdzong ras pa'i thugs dgongs rdzogs pa'i chad du yin gsung zhing bsngo ba'i yon bshad dang bsgrags mon rdzogs
pa'i rnam thar gyi lung yang gnang / bla ma dran pa'i gdung shugs kyi spyan chab mang po bsil zhing gdung dbyangs kyi gsol 'debs mdzad/ de rjes snye mor phebs nas/ dus 'khor/
gsung 'dus/ kun rigs/ gur rigs bsdus sogs kyi dbang bka' dang / bu lugs kyi 'khrid chen bzhi/ 'grel chen dri med 'od sogs kyi chos 'khor bskor zhing gdan sa bsko bzhag
mdzad nas ri phug tu phebs/ glang chen brag nas spyan 'dren zhus te su kha chos drug dang / dmar khrid tshims bu lugs sogs bka' chos mang du stsal/ lha'i zhing khar bzhugs
khri rtsigs nas grub rgyal tshe dbang khrom chen po la gnang dus rje nyid kyi dbral ba'i dkyil na 'od dmar por li ma tsam gcig yod pa der gnas ba kun gyi mthong zhing
gsol dpon rgyal mtshan gyi dri ba zhus pas/ 'od yong

don med/ rje btsun rdo rje rnam 'byor ma'i sku yod pa'i 'od yin nam/ lar yang rje btsun nA ro mkha' spyod 'di la bsnyen pa byas pas rjes su 'dzin pa'i rtags mang po byung gsung
/ btsan brag tu sku mtshams shin tu dam pa zla ba gnyis tsam gnang ste de grol ba dang 'brog pa rnams kyi spyan 'dren zhus nas tshe dbang dang 'brog pa rnams la sdig
pa che tshul gsung nas ma Ni'i lung mdzad/ mi 'khrugs pa'i gzungs bzlas nas gsol tsan dang mas dang phye ma sogs la ljags phus btab pa mi phyugs thams cad la bkye zhing
nas bye gtor ba gnang / de lo btsan brag tu sgrub pa mdzad dus me tog gi char chen po rgyun du bab pa dang ri phug tu rting sor sku mtshams gnang dus kyang me tog rnam pa
sna tshogs kyi char bab pas zhabs 'bring pa dag the tshom du gyur te/ kha sing btsan brag nas bzung 'di lo me tog gi char bab kyin 'dug pa 'di rje rin po che'i sku tshe
la bar chad zhig mi yong ngam zhus pas/ nga sems la rang dbang thob pa'i rnal 'byor ba gcig yin/ da dung lo 'ga' zhig mi'i cha/ me tog gi char bab pa 'di ngas rnal 'byor
ma'i bskyed rim bsgom pa la lha rnams kyi mchod pa 'bul ba yin 'dug gsung / de rjes kun mkhyen 'phags 'od kyi sgrub gnas dbang ldan jo mtshar gsang ba 'dus pa'i rim lnga
la sgrub pa gnang bas de phyin chad gzhan sems shes pa'i mngon mkhyen thogs med du byung / gzhan yang thar pa chos sde/ skyor lung / zam kha brag sogs dben gnas mang por
sku mtshams dang chos

'chad gzhan phan gyi rim pa slar 'phel du mdzad/ zam kha brag tu bzhugs dus dge slong dge 'dun dpal 'byor sogs la nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs gnang ba'i dam bzhag gi dus
thugs 'ur phyag dril phyir phangs pa sogs mdzad kyang grub rtags kyi skyon yom byung / dgung lo drug cu re lnga pa chu pho 'grug gi lo tshung 'dus khri khang du spyan
'dren zhus te tshe bka' dang / phyag rdor u tsa'i rjes gnang sogs stsal/ de nas bzung lo re bzhin tshar gnyis gsum re nyung mthar gdan drangs te bka' chos mang ba gnang zhing
tshong 'dus mgur chen rgyal po nas phyag chen gyi ngo sprod cig dgos zhus pa la ri phug nas gsung mgur bka' shog 'di gnang ngo / | bsod nams dpal gyi mngon par mtho
zhing / /shes rab snying rjes legs par kha brgyan/ /'gro drug sems can bde la 'god mdzad/ /mi dbang chen po'i bka' phebs bzhin du/ /tshig phreng cung zad 'di ltar 'bul lo/
/kho bo'i gtsug na bla ma chos rje/ /dad pa'i mchod phrin dbus na bzhugs te/ /bdag la dges pa'i 'dzum zhal mer re/ /rgyan chad med par byin rlabs gnang ba/ /kho bo'i snying
dbus 'bab par yod do/ /bla ma'i mos gus rtag tu bsgoms shing / /gdams ngag zab mo legs par bsgoms la/ /rigs pa gcig pu stong gsal dri med/ /ngo cer 'phrod pa dgos pa
la ni/ /cir yang 'char ba sems kyi rang rtsal/ /ngo la bltas pas kha dog dbyibs sogs/ /ma grub

pa gcig 'dug pa 'di yi/ /ngo bo stong par 'dug pa lags mod/ /stong pa ci med yin nam byas na/ /'gag med snang ba rig pa'i rtsal zhes/ /sems kyi rtsal las phyi rol yul snang
/ /'di kun grub par 'dug pa lags so/ /ma rtogs dus na 'og 'gyu 'ba' zhig /rtogs pa'i dus na kho ra'i ngo la/ /gcer te bltas pas nyon mongs thams cad/ /rtsad nas rang 'gag
nyid du song nas/ /nam mkha' dwangs pa'i dkyil bzhin lta bu/ /'dug pa 'di la phyag chen zer ro/ /lan cig byung bas mi chog pas na/ /nyams len bsgoms dang ma phral byas
pas/ /yar mchod bla ma dam pa rnams la/ /mos gus tshad med skye ba 'dug go /'khor bar gnas pa'i sems can rnams la/ /snying rje'i gdung shugs chen po skye zhing / /bar gyi
snang ba 'di dag la yang / /zhen chags chung du 'gro ba 'di ko/ /bdag gi rgyud la skyes pa yin snyam/ /spyir ni 'gro drug sems can rnams la/ /rang rang mthong snang 'char
sgo sna tshogs/ /yong ba'i las ngan bsog pa dag kyang / /phyag rgya chen po'i ngang du sres nas/ /de dag sangs rgyas thob pa gcig ni/ /cis kyang byed ni dgos rgyu lags
so/ /bsgoms dang ma bral byas pa kho nas/ /rnam rtogs phri ru 'gro ba 'dug cing / /rnam rtog ma zad bar du yang ni/ /las 'bras dag kyang zad par mi 'gyur/ /sdig pa phra mo
nas ni spongs mdzod/ /dge ba phra mo nas ni sgrubs shig /las dang rgyu 'bras rnam gzhag shes shing / /lag tu 'khel ba dgos rgyur gda' 'o/ /da lam tshig

phreng cung zad bskur gsung / /'di ltar tsam zhig phul ba lags pas/ /spyan lam phebs pa legs par gsan mdzod/ /dgongs khrel 'jug na bla ma mkha' 'gro/ /yi dam rnams la bzod
par gsol lo/ /dgongs pa'i yul du 'bab pa 'dug na/ /thugs kyi nyams bzhes brtse ba chen pos/ /'gro drug rnams ni bskyang du gsol lo/ /zhes pa'o/ /lan cig brag dkar chen du
lcog pu mdzad nas thugs dam la bzhugs par dbyar mjug nub cig brag nyil te brag dum lug ro tsam gcig dbul phog kyang skyon ci yang ma byung bar bzhugs/ gzhan yang slob ma
rnams kyi log bsgrub bskur 'debs sogs zhus kyang nga la khong khro med pas dam tshig la skyon mi yong mchis gsungs/ der ma zad dpal mgon zhal bzhi ba/ rnam sras mdung dmar
can/ dpal ldan lha mo rdo rje rab brtan ma rnams dang mi lab pa bzhin du 'grogs nas bka' las mi 'da' ba'i tshul sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rnam thar mnga' yang / yon
tan sbed pa kho na mdzad/ lo re bzhin du yang hor zla dang po'i nang la sku mtshams dam pa nges ba can du gnang / rgyun du rang phal cher sku mtshams kho nar bzhugs/ chos
don du gnyer ba mtha' dag la dbang 'khrid rjes gnang lung sogs dang rab byung bsnyen rdzogs zhu ba byung tshad la dgyes bzhin du gnang / mdor na bstan pa'i bya ba 'ga'
zhig gis nyin mtshan mtha' dag khor yug tu bsgrubs so/ /de ltar zhing 'di'i gdung bya'i

don phal cher mdzad zin nas dbang ldan chos 'khor gyi rtse mo sgrub mchod la phebs zhor chur la parnam 'bir lung ri khrod du sku mtshams thogs shig gnang / de grol ba dang
sku grib kyi rnam pas sku khams ma bde ba la sku rim dang gsol sman gyi zhabs tog zhus pa'i dwangs bskyed byung rung / gsol bzhes par mi mdad pas sku shed je chung du 'gro
zhing ting nge 'dzin zas su za ba yin gsungs nas gsol rgyun chad de zla ba phyed bar bzhugs/ de skabs phyag g.yog rnams kyis zhabs pad ma brtan pa bzhin byung nas sku skye
bzhes sam mi bzhes zhus pa la/ dge sgyor la nam bzhag dus yal 'gro yin 'dug pas skye ba mi len/ chos sku la chos sku thim 'gro ba yin gsung / de nas rje nyid kyi dgung
lo bdun cu don gcig bzhes pa rnam 'phyang du 'bod pa sa pho khyi'i lo/ /nags pa zla ba'i tshes bcu gsum la phyag g.yog rnams la rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i dam tshig
gis bris sku sogs bkram nas mchod pa bsham gsung / khongs rnams kyi mchod gshoms grub nas mchod pa bshams yod zhus pas/ 'o de kas khyab gsungs nas thugs dam ting nge
'dzin la mnyam bzhag cung zad gcig mdzad pa'i mthar chos sku bde pa chen po'i go 'phang mngon du mdzad nas zhi bar gshegs so/ /rje 'di'i rnam thar tshong 'dus khri khang
nas mgur chen rgyal po grwa lnga rdo rje'i mtshan can gyis mdzad pa 'dug kyang tshig ris ha cang go bde ba zhig mi snang bas 'dir cung zad gsal du btang ste snying por dril
nas bkod pa yin pas yid

ches ba'i gnas su yod do/ | //gnyis pa ni/ rnam bkra bskyed rim shis pa'i dpal la 'byor/ zhes chos rje gro bo lung pa bkra shis dpal 'byor ni/ 'khrungs yul lcags kyi sgog lung
ba bya ba'i grong zhig tu yab yum rigs rus cho 'brang ma smang pa'i sras su sku 'khrungs/ gzhon nu nas zhwa lur rab tu byung ba mdzad nas rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos
rjes gtso bor gyur pa'i mkhas grub kyi bla ma mang du bsten zhing mdo sngags rig gnas mtha' dag dang khyad par rgyud sde bzhi la mkhas pa'i tshad du phyin te smin grol
lam la gdul bya dkri ba'i rdo rje 'dzin pa'i ded dpon mchog tu gyur/ sku tshe'i smad la ri phug gi gzims khang gro bo lung du sku mtshams dang chos 'khor bskor ba zung 'brel
gyis bstan pa la phyag bris che bar mdzad pas chos rje gro bo lung pa zhes pa'i mtshan grags kyi ba dan phyogs brgyar 'phyar/ gshed dmar bcu gsum ma'i sgrub dkyil zin
bris sogs legs bshad yi ger bkod pa yang mang du yong snang zhing dgung lo yang shin tu smin pa zhig bzhugs te rjes su tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i lam glu dpyid kyi
rgyal mo las/ ku sA li yi bla ma lam du mjal/ /gang zhus kyi chos 'brel lhug par stsal/ /khong bka' drin mi chung che bar 'khums/ /lar da lta gangs ri'i khrod 'di na/ /dgon
spyi chos kyi rang tshugs 'dzin pa la/ /khong 'gran zla bral ba'i zhwa lu ba/ /bod chos sde tsho'i srog shing dam pa lags

zhes gsungs te/ ku sA li'i bla ma rje 'di nyid yin no/ /brgyud 'dzin gyi gtso bo byang gling pa bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ chos rje bsod nams dpal
'byor rnams so/ / 'dir zhwa lu pa'i bstan pa la brgyud nas bka' drin che ba rje btsun rdo ring pa kun spangs chos rje'i rnam par thar pi rim pa zur tsam zhig bstan par
bya ste/ de la rje nyid 'khrungs dpal snal thar gi chos grwa dang 'dab chags pa/ chu sgo'i sbug rdo ring bsam 'grub smon mkhar zhes bya ba de/ bod chos rgyal gyi gdung brgyud
las byung pa'i ya' nang so dpal mgon rin chen pa dang / yum bkra shis rgyal mo gnyis kyi sras su rje nyid rab byung brgyad pa'i sa mo sbrul gyi lo/ /nags pa zla ba'i
tshes bcu bzhi'i nyi ngos la sku bltams/ 'khrungs ma thag nyid kye mes po'i zhang po zhwa lu pa'i slob brgyud mkhas grub rgyal mtshan dpal bzang la gshed dmar gyi dbang
gsan/ dgung lo drug la ngor chen rdo rje 'chang dang mjal/ dbang rjes gnang 'ga' gsan/ bdag cis kyang btsun pa zhig byed zhus pas/ khyod deng sang rdo ring bu gcig po yin
pas btsun pa byed rgyu mi yong / rjes su spun zla 'dra byung ba dang btsun pa gyis/ sa skya ba'i lam 'bras pa chen po zhig 'ong gsung / de nas rim gyi rin spung chos rgyal
nor bu bzang po'i gsol dpon las 'khur bzhes te dgung lo sum cu so bdun bar sde dpon gyi tshul bzungs nas yar dkon mchog mchod pa dang / mar ngan sprang mgon med la sbyin
pa gtong ba sogs mdor na sngon gyi rgyal blon

byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mdad pa dang 'dra ba mdzad/ lan cig mjal lam du e waM chos ldan du phebs/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug pa dang mjal/ rje rdo rje 'chang
ga na bzhugs zhus pas g.yab chen na bzhugs gsung / der phebs nas byin rlabs zhus pas dbu skra nas bzungs te btsun pa byed ran gda' gsungs then then pa 'ga' mdzad byung
bas mnal sad/ de nas chos grwa chen 'o grwa thang du phebs/ mtshungs med mkhanya chen shes rab zla ba'i drung du dgung lo so bdun pa shing mo sbrul gyi lo la rab byung
mdzad/ matsan kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma blo ldan shes kun dga' rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba gsol nas ri khrod gcig tu sku mtshams mdzad cing bzhugs pa na/ nub mang po'i bar
la mnal lam mi nag po dang bya nag khyi nag sogs 'ong nas khyod rang sa skya la rgyug /mi 'gro na brdung ba yin/ gsod pa yin zer ba dang / res 'ga' khyod mi 'gro na 'di
ltar byed zer sku chas thams cad khyer nas sa skya phyogs su phar 'gro ba sogs cho 'phrul mang po byung bas bskul te sa skyar phebs/ bdag chen chos kyi rgyal po blo gros
rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhabs drung du mjal/ phyag rdzas kyi dngos po thams cad phul/ bdag chen de nyid kyi mkhan po dang / las kyi slob dpon lha btsun pa sogs dad pa'i
dge 'dun grangs tshangs pa'i dbus su bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa bzhes/ de rjes bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi zhabs 'bring du bzhugs te 'brom

gyi jo bo bsten pa ltar mdzad pas/ lam 'bras snyan brgyud thun mong ma yin pa'i skor dang / gser chos skor/ mgon po che chung sogs mdor na dpal ldan sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud
rim pa dang mus chen sems dpa' chen po nas brgyud pa'i snyan brgyud chos skor ma lus pa bum pa gang byor gnang / chos 'di rnams gdung brgyud rim par nged kyi bar chig
brgyud du bzhugs pa yin/ da dung yang gdung brgyud kho nar spel ba'i 'dun pa byas/ bdag po bsod nams rgyal mtshan sa skyar gdan drangs pa yin na'ang gnas tshul de bzhin byung
ba sogs khyod rang gi bsod nams su 'dug /da khyod las gzhan 'os mi 'dug gsung zhing bka' rgya dang bcas te gnang ngo / /de nas sku zhang rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos
rje'i zhabs la gtugs te/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa nas brgyud pa'i pha rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod rdo rje'i dbang rim lnga dmar 'khrid/ gshed dmar lha lnga dang
bcu gsum ma sogs gshed skor/ 'khor chen sogs phyag rdor gyi rigs/ ma rgyud 'khor lo bde mchog nag po ba'i skor sogs dbang dang bshad bka' lung bka' mang po gsan/ gzhan
yang zhwa lu pa'i phyogs nas/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i gdan sa pa mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs bshes gnyen dang / chos rje dka' bzhi pa/ dbang phyug don yod pa rnams bsten
nas chos gsan par mdzad la/ spyir snga phyir chos gsan pa'i bla ma ni yongs su 'dril pas bdun cu rtsa gnyis bsten nas bod du bzhugs pa'i mdo rgyud dgongs 'grel

dang bcas pa'i dbang lung man ngag phal cher gsan pas snyan brgyud rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag tu gyur pa yin no/ /de nas tsha rong byang chub rdzong / bya 'gyur rdo rje'i brag
sogs la sgrub pa yang rgyun ring pa mdzad/ de yang sngar rab tu ma byung gong la/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug la kye rdor gyi dbang gsan pa'i tshe thugs rgyud la bde
stong gi nyams skyes shing / de rjes dgung lo nyi shu tsam la bsam grub rtser phyag rgya mtshan ldan zhig gi nye rgyas mtshams sbyar rlang sems dbu mar chud pa'i rtags
rnams kyang chang ba shar pas rjes su thugs dam mdzad pa shin tu drod pa byung ngo / /lan ci rdo ring du bzhugs pa'i tshe spyan ras gzigs zhal gzigs pa dang / grwa nang gi
ri khrod du bzhugs dus sku chas cung zad bkren pa byung bas nye gnas la ku ru ku lle'i gtor ma zhig 'chos gsungs pas/ sang gi gung tshigs la ldang ba tsam las med zer/
de ka la 'chos gsungs nas gtor ma phul bas rje btsun mas zhal dngos su bstan nas sang gi mthun rkyen rnams kyang 'phrin las kyi sa nas 'ong ba yod/ tshe mjug la longs spyod
chen po yong gsung ba'i lung bstan stsal zhing / der sang nyin mkhas pa'i dbang po rje btsun karmma 'phrin las pas mthun dus mang po 'bul du btang bas nye gnas pa'ang
shin tu dga' ste rjes su yang ku ru ku lle'i gtor ma 'chos pa drag zer ba zhig byung ngo / /de las sogs te thugs dam gyi lha tshogs zhal gzigs tshul sogs dang /

grub pa'i mtshan ma du ma dang ldan zhing ngo mtshar ba'i lo rgyus mang ste 'dir rgyas par 'brir ma langs pas tshar chen gyis mdad pa'i rnam thar ngo mtshar dad pa'i spu long
g.yo ba zhes bya ba yod pas der ga zigs shig /sku tshe'i smad la grub stod kha'u brag rdzong gi gdan sa rgyun ring ba mdzad nas chos 'khor bskor/ sde srid sengge rtse
pas bsnyen bkur zhabs tog dpag med mdzad de mchod gnas kyi gtso bor mnga' gsol/ zang zing gi 'bul ba byung ba kun kyang sku gsung thugs rten bzhengs pa dang dge 'dun gyi
sde la bsnyen bkur sogs 'phral dag mdzad/ zhal nas kyang / nged rang gi btag tu bzung ba la dam tshig rdo rje dril bu/ lam 'bras glegs bam snam sbyar dang lhung bzed sogs
dge slor gi 'tsho ba'i yo byad tsam ma gtogs med gsung / de nas tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po la snyan brgyud kyi chos rnams yongs su rdzogs pa stsal nas dgung lo bdun cu
don drug pa shing pho spre'u'i lo/ /smin drug zla ba'i tshes bco lnga la dben gnas dam pa kha'u brag rdzong du zhi bar gshegs so/ 'di ni sangs rgyas 'khor ba 'jigs si sprul
pa yin par gsungs pas sku che ba'i yon tan de tsam gyis kyang shes so/ /gsum pa ni/ /rgyal ba kun 'dus tshar pa rdo rje 'chang / /zhes byung bas/ tshar chen chos kyi
rgyal po de ni/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che dang / de rjes yar klung pa sengge rgyal mtshan/ pha rgod bsod nams bzang po/ mkhas pa stag tshang lo tsA
ba'i slob

ma dge slong dbang mo rnams su sku skye ba bzhes pa'i mthar dus 'dir 'khrungs pa'i yul ni/ mang mkhar gyis cha rma gshod dge ba'i tshal du/ yang chos rgyal rin chen dpal bzang
dang / yum bkra shis a 'tsho ma gnyis kyi sras su rab 'byung brgyad pa'i chu bya lo rgyal gyi zla ba'i tshes bcu re gza' nyi ma/ rgyu skar smin drug la babs pa'i nyin
sku bltams/ smra mkhyen tsam gyi dus nas yab kyi rdo rje gcod pa'i phyag dpe yod pa gzigs pas klog rang rdol du byung / chung ngu'i dus nas chos skyong stag zhon dang phyag
drug pa zhal gzigs shing bran du 'khol/ khyi smyon zhig gis rmug tu byung ba la he ru ka zhal brgyad pa'i bskyed rim gyi nga rgyal dang gsal snang rang shar du byung
bas khyi de yang rmug ma nus par bros/ yang 'jim pa la gtor ma'i gzugs bcos nas khyi der dngos su gtor rgyag gi tshul mdzad pas de kha nas khrag skyugs te shi'o/ /dgung lo
bcu bzhi la 'dzim chos lung du chos rje blo gros rgyal mtshan las dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa bzhes/ bcu drug pa la chos grwa chen po bkra shis lhun por phebs/ rgyal ba dge
'dun rgya mtsho las rab tu byung / mtshan blo gsal rgya mtsho zhes gsol/ chos rje blo gros rgya mtsho slob dpon du bsten nas mdo phyogs la sbyangs/ thugs gner la 'bad pa
cher gnang mi dgos pa gzhung lugs thugs su chud pas gzhan dag na re/ chos rje tshar pa slob gnyer mi byed 'dug ces zer

ba la/ kho bo blo gsal rgya mtsho nyal nas bsdad pas shes/ da shog ces bgro gleng mdzad pas/ grwa pa gzhan kun srod par bskyal tho rangs tshur bsus nas slob gnyer rem rem skad
byas pa thams cad sdug gyong lta bur song bas rtsod pa byed pa'i tshe blo zhum nas khal tham du bcug pa bzhin gyur to/ /dgung lo bcu bdun pa la thon pa mkhas btsun yon
tan rgya mtsho'i zhabs drung du phebs te chos mang po gsan/ der 'brum nad kyi snyun thebs nas spyan 'byed 'dzum tsam yang mi mkhyen pa'i shin du thu bar gyur/ dngos bar
'chi ba 'dug pas 'pho dmigs shig mdzad dgos dgongs pa na brang la lag pa grang mo gcig sbyar nas da lam 'pho ba byed mi dgos zer ba zhig byung ba de nas snyun rim gyis dwangs
te gtsang du phebs/ dreg nad kyis zhabs bsnyun nas rje dge 'dun rgya mtsho la brtag pa zhu bar mdzad pas/ deng sang chos rje kun spangs pa 'di mthu stobs che ba yod
'dug pas khyed rang der byon gsungs nas sengge rtser rdo ring rin po che dang mjal bar phebs/ phyag rdor u tsA rya'i rjes gnang stsal zhing sku tshe snga ma'i las 'brel
gyis thugs yid gcig tu 'dres/ de nas bkra shis lhun por byon nas mdo phyogs kyi thugs gnyer phyi 'phro mthud/ tshad ma'i bshad pa dang zhal blangs kyi skabs rje btsun sa
skya bdag 'di ltar bzhad ces yang yang gsungs pas/ chos rje tshar ba rang re'i chos grwar bsdad pa tsam ma gtogs sa skya pa yin 'dug ces ma rangs pa

byas skad/ snga dro zhig bkra shis lhun po'i khron pa chen mo'i thad der/ bud med dmar mo zhig gis khyed la rje rdo ring bas kha'ur byon gsung gin gda'/ de'i lag rtags 'di
yin zhes glegs bam zhig phyag tu phul nas yal song / de lta bus bskul nas kha'u brag rdzong du phebs te rje btsun kun spangs chen po dang mjal zhing gsung gleng mdzad pas/
chos rje mkha' spyod mas gdan 'dren zhu ru phyin gda'/ dpe cha 'di yang de'i chos skong yin gsung zhing mnyes mnyes mdzad/ de nas gsung ngag slob bshad/ gser chos skor/
mgon po che chung sogs mdor na dpal ldan sa skya pa'i snyan brgyud slob bshad du grags pa thams cad dang / gzhan yang mkhas grub khyung po'i chos skor dang / bu ston thams
cad mkhyen pa nas brgyud pa'i zhwa lu pa'i 'khrid chen bzhi sogs rje btsun de nyid la mnga' ba'i gdams pa phal cher bu pa gang byo'i tshul du gsan/ khyad par zhwa lu ba'i
lugs kyi 'khrid bka' rnams zhus pa la ma ltos bar khyed ma 'ongs par zhwa lu'i gdan sa mdad dgos nyen che bas cis kyang 'di rnams nyon gsungs nas stsal/ dgung lo nyer
gsum pa la kun spangs chen po dag zhing du phebs nas sa skya'i bdag chen ngag dbang grags pa'i zhabs phyi mdzad de dbus phyogs su byon/ nAlendrar bdag chen gyi sku tshab
mdzad nas chos 'khor bskor zhing grwa pa rnams rje nyid la shin tu dad par gyur pas

sa skya'i drung 'khor 'ga' res mtho gnon gyi rnam pa'ang ci rigs byas/ 'phran yul bya bzang gi ri khrod du rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi bsnyen sgrub mdzad pas zhal dngos su gzigs/
dgung lo so gcig pa chu 'brug lo nyang stod spos khang du mkhan po grags pa rgyal mtshan dang / las kyi slob dpon bkra shis rnam rgyal sogs dge 'dun nyi shu rtsa lnga'i
dbus su bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/ sdom rgyun de yang kha che paN chen gyi sdom rgyun yin pas/ gsungs las/ bdag gi tshe 'di'i ngo bsrung rgyab tu bor/ /phyi ma'i don chen 'ba'
zhig snying nas bsam/ /yongs rdzogs kha che'i paN chen bsod snyoms pa/ /shAkya shrI'i grar ni 'bad pas zhugs/ /zhes so/ /bo dong du rje btsun sgo rum pa la dus 'khor bdag
po chen po'i dbang sogs dang / chos sgo 'khrul zhig byams pa shes rab la bde mchog skor/ 'bras spungs pa tshe dbang bkra shis la yang phur sogs dang mgon poche chung gi
'tsham dbyangs rnams sbyor brdar mdzad/ gzhan yang rgyud gsum smra ba shes rab rin chen/ dwags po paN chen phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rngog ston bsod nams bstan 'dzin/ mdo khams
pa yon tan rgya mtsho/ 'gos rdo rje sengge/ nyan po chos rje/ grub dbang sbyin pa rgya mtsho/ brag ram dka' bzhi ba dkon mchog bzang po/ ldong gi sngags 'chang chos
skyong bsod nams/ brag dkar sems dpa' chen po/ zang g.yu gong pa/ star lung sbas don pa/ bsam sdings ba sangs rgyas ye shes/ rwa sgreng mkhan po dpal 'byor

bsam 'grub/ rong shag pa bkra shis rin chen/ khams lcags mo bkra shis sengge/ shambhar chos rje/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje nyid kyi yab chos rgyal rin chen rgyal
mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA ba sogs bla ma drug cu rtsa lnga bsten nas thos bsam gyi sgro 'dog gcod par mdzad/ lan gcig da dus la phebs dus nya mgo gru khar mnyan
pa dus la ma 'gyor pas nga tshu la gding ba btings nas 'gro gsungs bas mdun gyi man mkhar phag mo gru ba byon nas snyigs ma'i sems can nyon mongs can la gsang ba'i spyod
pa ma byed gsung bas gru la pebs/ gdan sa thel gyi 'jag spyi la sku 'dra rin po che phag mo grub pa dngos su gzigs/ der ma zad kye rdor/ bde mchog sogs yi dam zhi khro
mang po'i bsnyen bsgrub mthar 'khyol zhing / rgyun du'ang sngags kyi bzlas brjod nyin zhag re'i khong su aShTa/ oM gsum ma/ ya ma rA dza/ shA sa na/ sa lud kyi snying po
rnams so sor stong phrag re chag med du mdzad/ shA sa na bzla ba'i skabs phyag 'phreng la dngos su me 'bar ba sogs byung / bar skabs shig chu ba ri'i brag phug tu sgrub
pa mdzad pas mkha' 'gro mas tshogs kyi 'khor los mchod cing / sku lus kyi rtsa 'khor so so'i lha tshogs gsal bar gzigs nas/ gnas spyi bo bde chen gyi ri bo'i spor/ /rje
sku yi rdo rje yab yum bzhugs/ /mkha' 'gro so gnyis kyi 'khor gyis bskor/ /sku zla shel gsar ba'i mdangs

'od can/ pha gsol ba 'debs so rdo ring sa/ /bu mi mngon dbyings nas thugs rjes skyobs/ /tshogs mchod par 'bul lo drin can rje/ /lus snang stong spru skur byin gyis rlobs/ /zhes
sogs mgur gsungs/ /mang mkhar tsha lung rdo rje'i brag tu sgrub pa mdzad skabs thogs pa med pa 'phur ba'i rdzu 'phrul bstan cing / brag gi khong seng nas lcags kyi rdo
rje rtse dgu pa zhig gter nas bzhes/ dgung lo so gnyis pa shing rta lo thub bstan dge 'phel gyi khri la phebs/ der lam 'bras lo 'khor ma'i bka' chos shin tu rgyas pa dang
/ mgon khang gsar bzhengs sogs mdzad/ dgon pa shar sbug tu dbyangs can ma'i ljags bsnyen gnang bas me tog dkar po'i char dang pi waM gyi sgra gsan pa sogs byung / dgung
lo so brgyad kyi dus dbus su phebs pa'i lam zhor khro phur rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i cho 'phrul gzigs shing / bde mchog srin po rir zhal dngos su bstan/ 'phan yul bya bzang
gi ri khrod du thugs dam mdzad cing bzhugs pa'i skabs shig nam mkha' baiDU rya mthing gi kha mdog ltar dwangs pa'i dbus na sprin dkar lang long du 'khrigs pa'i khrod
nas lha'i bu mdzes shing yid du 'ong ba gnyis byung nas dri ba 'di ltar zhus so/ /e ma hoH kha bas bskor ba'i sman ljongs kyi/ /yul dbus sa yi thig le'i ngos/ /dben pa'i
ri sul yang steng na/ /bla ma sgom pa'i ku su lu/ /khyod kyi thog ma'i skyes yul gang / /dam pa'i yongs 'dzin su yis bzung / /da lta nyams len gdams ngag gang / /

phyi ma'i gtad so ji ltar yod/ /ces zer ba la rje nyid kyis lan 'di ltar gsungs so/ /ston dus bdud rtsi'i 'byung gnas ltar/ /dkar zhing yid 'phrog chu 'dzin gseb/ /gnas pa'i
'chi med gzhon nu gnyis/ /rna ba'i bdun rtsi sgra dbyangs snyan/ /shAkya'i bstan pa rab byung zhing / /dam pa'i ded dpon gyis bzung yang / /snyom las dbang gis bcings pa
yis/ /ser gzugs bdag gi skyes pa'i yul/ /gangs ri'i khrod kyi gtsang stod cha/ /chu bo pakSha'i lho yi ngos/ /grub stod sa skya'i bya 'dab ljongs/ /'brog mi la tsA'i gnas
kyi mda'/ / /'phrang gsum nang nas srin 'phrang gdong / /rmu rje gtsang pos bzung ba'i sa/ /der ni sngon gyi las dbang gis/ /dal 'byor rin chen rnyed pa yin/ /thub bstan
rin chen sgor zhugs nas/ /dam chos bdud rtsi nos pa yin/ /spyir ni yongs 'dzin bcu phrag bzhi/ /zung gnyis dag gis lhag par bzhugs/ /khyad par tshe rabs dpag med nas/
/rjes su bzung ba'i 'drin pa mchog /tshe 'dir rang sems lhan skyes 'di/ /skye med chos skur ngo sprod cing / /zab mo dbang bzhi'i chu bo'i rgyun/ /bum pa gang byor gnang
ba yi/ /bka' drin mnyam med rdo rings pa/ /'gran zla kun dang bal ba yin/ /nyams len gdams pa'i gtso bo ni/ /rgyal yum bdag med mkha' 'gro la/ /paN grub dbang po birU pas/
/nos pa nas bzung da lta'i bar/ /rtsa ba'i bla ma yan chod du/ /dbang bzhi'i cu bo ma nub pa'i/ /bla ma'i gsung ngag

bdud rtsi'i rgyun/ /tshad ma bzhi ldan dbang bzhi'i lam/ /rdo rje theg pa'i snying po yin/ /yang snying zab mo'i bla ma'i lam/ /rang sems bla ma phyag rgya che/ /yengs pa med
par sgom pa yin/ /phyi ma'i gda' gro da lta med/ /sgyu ma'i skyes chen 'degs pa'i tshe/ /kho bo'i bla ma slu med de/ /mdun gyi nam mkhar 'byon snyam yod/ /bde chen thugs
kyi dkyil 'khor dang / /rang sems stong pa spros bral gnyis/ /dbyer med bsres nas lhug par 'jog /gang ltar song yang 'gyod pa med/ /ces gsungs pas rin po che'i bum pa
bdud rtsis gang ba zhig phyag tu phal lo/ /dgung lo zhe gnyis pa la 'dar grang mo che'i sengge'i khri la mnga' gsol/ yang lan cig za phu lung du sku brnyan bde gshegs 'dus
pa'i spyan sngar thugs dam mdzad cing bzhugs pas sku gnyer gyis blo la bla ma 'dis gter 'don zer nas sku 'dra'i gzungs gzhug mi blug pa'i nges pa med snyam/ sgo drung nas
nya mgo mnan pas skad gdangs snyan po zhig gis chos kyi gsung gleng mdzad pa thos nas mi 'ga' re yod pa yin nam bsam ste thal gyis yongs pas sku gcig pur bzhugs 'dug skad/
der slob dpon padma zhal gzigs shing chos gsung zhes grags so/ /dgung lo nga bzhi pa shing mo yos kyi lo dbal zhwa lu'i khri thog tu phyag phebs/ grwa pa nyis brgya
lhag pa la gshed dmar lha lnga'i smin byed/ dbang tshad dgu mdzad nas stsal/ ma ha'i mchod pa'i dus gtor yang bar skabs su chag tu nye ba byung bas

ched kyis snga srol nyams pa gsos te legs par bcugs/ de skabs/ rgyal ba khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid nas bzung bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa yab sras kyis gtso mdzad/
bdag gi bla ma rje btsun gnyis spangs zhabs kyi bar du byon pa'i rtsa ba dang bcas pa'i dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams kyi bka'/ khro bo'i dpa' bo dpal gshin rje gshed
kyi lung / dpal zhwa lu gser khang gi gdan sa bcu gsum pa shAkya'i dge slong rdo rje 'dzin pa dpal dus dgra nag po ma he'i zhal gyis brtul zhugs grub pa'i yi ge/ sring ba
gsum na gnas shing phyu ga'i 'byung pho mi dang mi ma yin pa rnams la zlo ba/ zhes sogs kyi sgo yig bka' shog mdzad nas dngos gzhi'i dus/ rje nyid kyis dam can chos rgyal
yab yum la bka' bsgo mdzad pa'i tshe zhal ras thams cad dmar sbug tu gyur/ zhal brnyal gyi dbu gtsug tu phyag gi rdo rje bzhag nas rtsa brgyud bla ma'i mtshan nas brjod/
bstan 'gro'i phan bde spel zhing dgra bshegs tshar gcod pa'i dam bsgrags gnang bas/ der 'khor ba'i khrom thams cad bred cing skyi g.ya' bar gyur/ zhwa lung la shin tu sdang
ba'i dgra zhig de ka'i mod la kha nas khrag skyugs te shi/ de lta bu'i cho 'phrul mthong bas lo rgyun mang po'i bar la zhwa lu pa'i chos gnyis 'phrog 'dod pa sogs kyi
sde pa yas phyin thams cad snying lkog mar bros nas gtser ba byed nus pa ma byung ngo / de nas ri phug

chos kyi pho brag du gsung ngag slob bshad dang / bu lugs kyi khrid chen bzhi dang khrid chung bzhi sogs chos 'khor rgya chen po bskor/ lan cig gzims mal sku 'dra rin po che'i
drung du gcig pur gsol 'debs mdzad cing bzhugs pas/ sku 'dra rin po che gzi mdangs je cher rgyas shing de'i sku'i cha shas thams cad las 'od zer sna lnga 'phros nas bar
snang khyab pa dang slar tshur 'dus/ la la nyid kyi sku la thim/ la la sku 'dra rang la thim pa zhig byung ste rjes su gzigs snang ji ltar byung ba ltar bkod pa'i bris
sku zhig kyang thugs dam rten du bzhengs so/ de nas bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i bstan pa nyams pa rnams bsos te zhwa lu'i gdan sa 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug
la gtad sa skyong 'dar bas spyan drangs pa ltar 'dar stod grang mo che phyogs su phal cher bzhugs nas der gdul bya bsam gyis mi khyab pa smin grol la bkod/ dgung lo drug
cu rtsa lnga pa me pho stag gi lo/ zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bco lnga'i nyin gzugs sku'i snang ba chos kyi dbyings su brtul lo/ /sku gdung ring bsrel gyi snying po can ril
por bzhugs pa'i gser gdung thog tshad phyed gnyis tsam sde srid 'dar ba rin chen dpal bzang dang / yum a mdzes rgyal mo gnyis kyis lo bco lnga'i ring la sku rgyu bsgrubs
nas bzhengs pa dus phyis 'dar grang mo che'i gtsug lag khang la me skyon shor nas/ gser gdung mes bzhes pa'i sku tshag tu dngul gdung zhig bzhengs te deng sang 'dar grang
mo che na bzhugs so/ /brgyud 'dzin gyi gtso bo

ka bzhi gdung drug gi tshul du byung ste/ ka ta bzhi ni/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug/ yol pa mkhan chen gzhon nu blo gros/ bod mkhar ba mai tri don grub rgyal mtshan/
mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho dang bzhi'o/ gdung drug ni/ gtsang stod rab brtan dpal 'bar/ mkhan chen byams pa blo gros rnam rgyal/ zhabs drung chos dbang rin chen
dpal gyi rgya mtsho/ 'dren mchog blo gros chos 'phags/ rje gzhon nu stobs ldan/ mkhan chen bsod nams dbang po dang drug go/| rje yol pa gzhon nu blo gros ni/ yol gser sdings
su/ yab nang so mtsho skyes rdo rje dang / yum a sras a rgyal gyi sras su me mo phag la sku 'khrungs/ dgung lo bcu gsum pa la rtse rang mkhan chen nam mkha' bkra shis
pa'i drung du rab tu byung zhing rje tshar chen dang thog mar mjal/ nyi shu pa la sngar gyi mkhan po de nyid kyi drung du bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/ dgung lo lnga bcu nga bzhi
pa lcags pho 'brug la yar klung bkra shis chos sde btab/ dgung lo bdun cu don gsum pa sa mo phag la gnas de nyid du sku gshegs/ /| bod mkhar ba mai tri don grub rgyal
mtshan ni/ lha btsan po'i gdung brgyud du yab bshes gnyer bzang po dang / yum bu 'dren rgyal mo'i sras su me pho khyi lo rong g.yag sde'i sa char sku 'khrungs/ dgung lo bco
lnga la 'bras yul skyed tshal du 'bum ram pa shes rab rgyal mtshan gyi drung du rab tu byung / dgung lo nyi shu rtsa lnga pa la rje tshar chen dang thog mar mjal/ dgung
lo so dgu pa la lo pa spyan snga ngag

dbang chos grags kyi mkhan po mdzad nas bsnyen par rdzogs/ dgung lo drug cu re gnyis ba me mo phag gi lo dbo zla ba'i nyi shu gcig la lo dgon par sku gshegs/ /mang thos klu
sgrub rgya mtsho ni/ 'khrungs sa zang zang 'brog gi shel lung du/ yab lha mo lnga dar dang / yum sams ma rgyal 'dzoms gyi sras su chu mo lug gi lo la 'khrungs/ dgung lo
bco lnga pa la kun mkhyen lcags theng pa byams pa bsod nams dpal bzang las rab tu byung / dgung lo nyi shu rtsa gsum pa la rje tshar chen dang mjal/ de rjes mang mkhar gyi
sa cha rang byung khrus kyi rdzi dbu'i 'gram du mkhan chen sangs rgyas 'od zer ba las bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/ mnyam yod bya rgod gshongs kyi mkhan po mdzad nas 'chad nyan
rgya cher gnang zhing gtsug lag khang bkra shis gser khang bzhengs/ de rtings sde srid 'dar nas kyi spyan 'dren zhus te thub bstan dge 'phel dang grang mo che sogs kyi khri
la rim gyi phebs/ dgung lo bdun du don bzhi pa me pho spre'u'i lo la 'dar gyi ri khrod slob bshad nor bu'i gling du sku gshegs/ tshar chen yab sras kyi skabs so/ / | //gsol
'debs las/ bstan pa'i me ro slong ba mkhyen brtse'i dbang / /chos dkon mchog gi lam bzang ston las mkhas/ /rang gzhan don kun lhun grub rgyal mtshan 'chang / /mtshungs
med dam pa gsum la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes so/ /dang po/ bstan pa'i me ro slong ba mkhyen brtse'i dbang / /zhes mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam dbyas mkhyen brtse'i

dbang phyug ni/ 'khrungs sa bo dong e'i rdzong phun tshogs rab brtan du yab 'a a rgyal bo'i gdung brgyud rigs sngags 'char ba'i grub thob nam mkha' rdo rje dang / yum rdo rje
rnal 'byor ma'i sprul pa tshe brtan bu 'dren zhes bya ba gnyis kyi sras su rab 'byung dgu pa'i sheng pho spre'u'i lo/ zla ba bzhi pa'i yar ngo nyi ma me bzhi'i 'grub sbyor
yod pa'i nyin zhal nas a A zhes pa'i sgra sgrog cing sku 'khrungs/ smra mkhyen tsam nas nyi ma re la thugs dam gyi thun re chag med kyi tshul mdzad nas phyag mnyam gzhag
dang lus gnad bcas nas bzhugs pa'i nyi tshod bzung ste gnang / rten gsum gyi drung du mchod pa chung chung mang po bshams nas/ yon chab 'di ni sngo la dwangs/ /sngo
la dwangs pa bzhes su gsol/ /zhal sras 'di ni rtse mo snyung / /rtse snyung chen po bzhes su gsol/ /zhes sogs mchod 'phreng mdzad pa dang / rje sgo rum pa la bir srung sogs
gsan pa'i tshe/ /bir wa ba'i rnam thar gsungs pa rnams thugs la zin nas/ nub mo gzims pa'i bsgang la/ sdigs mdzub bstan pas ganggA gyen la ldog/ phyag 'tshal mdzad pas
dbang phyug tshal par gas/ /thal mo brdabs pas rtse gsum thal par song / /sngo nag 'bar ba khyed la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes bya 'i bstod pa yang gsungs/ sku gzhon nu'i dus
nas snying rje shin tu che ba dang / na bza' lang dmar ser kho na las mi gsol zhing zhal du dmar skyur gyi rigs mi bzhes/ dgung lo brgyad la rje sgo

rum pa kun dga' legs pas mkhan po dang / ru thog bla chen nam mkha' gzi brjid sogs dge 'dun lnga'i dbus su rab tu byung / mtshan mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug tu gsol/ de nas
ru thog bla chen klog yig gi slob dpon du bsten nas rgya bod kyi yi ge'i rigs mi 'dra ba mang po dka' tsheg mi dgos bar mkhyen/ dgung lo brgyad la rje tshar chen dang yang
mjal/ dgung lo dgu la tshe dpag med lha dgu'i gzhi bsnyen dang sgrub mchod bdag 'jug dang bcas pa brgya tshar/ kyai rdor gyi sgrub mchod brgya tshar sogs mdzad/ dgung lo
bcu gnyis la sngar gyi mkhan slob kyi drung du dge tshul gyis sdom pa bzhes/ de nas bo dong gi dben gnas bde gsal rab brtan du sku mtshams mdzad nas mgon po gur gyi bsnyen
pa sngags 'bum phrag lnga bcu rtsa drug bzla ba mdzad/ lha mo 'od zer can ma'i sgrub mchod mdzad pa'i tshe mnal lam du 'od zer can ma'i sku nam mkha'i khams thams cad
khengs pa zhig gzigs/ dgung lo bco lnga la rje sgo rum pa la dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang dang sbyor drug zhus nas bsgoms pas nyams rtogs khyad par can 'khrungs/ de nas
rta nag thub bstan rnal rgyal du mdo phyogs kyi thugs gnyer mdzad pa la byon zhing dgung lo bcu dgu pa la rtsis gnas gsar rgyal khang gi mkhan po'ang mdzad/ de yan la gur
gyi mgon po'i yi ge bdun pa 'bum phrag brgya dang nyi shu tsam gyi bsnyen pa dang gzhan yang

lhag lha du ma'i bsnyen sgrub tshang du 'khyol ba gnang / dgung lo nyi shu pa la rje sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa'i zhabs kyi mkhan po dang / las kyi slob dpon tshar chen chos
kyi rgyal po/ gsang ston ru thog bla chen nam mkha' gzi brjid/ grib tshod pa dpon ngag dbang bstan pa'i rdo rje/ kha skong ba gnas brtan sangs rgyas bzang po sogs kyi
dbus su bsnyen par rdzogs pa dge slong gi sdom pa bzhes/ rta nag tu thugs gner gyi 'pho 'thud pa tsam gnang ste rjes su slob dpon 'bum rab pa zer ba sogs nas thub bstan rnam
rgyal gyi gdan sar phebs dgos zer ba'i yi ge'ang phul/ de'i lan du/ sngon gyi smon lam las 'phros mtshams sbyar ba'i/ /snod ldan slob ma nam byung rjes su 'dzin/ /snang
shas dbang gis ma dad mi 'dod bzhin/ /slob 'khor sdud pa'i shes 'dod me mdog lags/ /zer ba skur pas yig 'brel kyang bcad do/ /snga phyir chos gsan pa'i bla ma yang / rgyal
ba sgo rum pa chen po/ /tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ ru thog bla chen/ lce ston paN chen/ rgya gar nub phyogs pa ma Ni ka nA/ /sngags 'chang chos skyong bsod nams mnga'
ris rigs 'dzin chen po/ byang gling pa rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ 'brug pa gcung smyon/ rgyal yum tshul khrims bzang mo/ 'bro'i sngags 'chang 'jam dpal blo gros/
gnubs sgom sbas

pa'i rnal 'byor smon lam rgyal mtshan/ shar gling pa kun bzang mthu stobs/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' grol mchog sogs bla ma sum cu so gnyis bsten nas gangs ri'i khrod 'dir bka'
ma rub pa phal mo che gsan par mdzad cing zhal nas kyang ji skad du/ a ho sngon gyi dam pa de dag gi /dkar ba du mas bod 'dir bsgyur ba'i chos/ /snyan brgyud phal cher ston
gyi chu 'dzin bzhin/ /mtshan yang lhag ma med pa'i dbyings su yal/ /'ga' zhig grong khyer rnying pa'i khron pa bzhin/ /deng sang dus na mtshan tsam lhag mar lus/ /glegs
bam phal cher dbul po'i gter bzhin du/ /sa rdul khrod na mun pa'i mal du gzims/ /dam pa'i rgyal po phal cher 'das gyur cing / /gdul bya'i 'bangs rnams bka' bzhin mi byed
par/ /thos bsam sgom pa'i khrims la mthong chungs pas/ /gsung rab slob dpon khros nas gsung mi 'byon/ /rgyu des dbang lung man ngag bshad pa'i bka'/ /cung zad lus pa'ang
chu skam nya bzhin nam/ /nam gzhug chad pa'i me tog ji bzhin du/ /lkog mar srod phyin gyur pa ma bzod nas/ /gzhan rkyen bstan la dad pa ches nyung zhing / /rang rkyen
shes rab snying rjer mi ldan pas/ /bstan pa gsal ba'i nus pa ma mchis kyang / /bstan pa'i sems khral tsam du ngas 'dir 'bad/ /ding sang dpyod ldan makas pa ches dkon zhing
/ /mkhas rloms phal cher phyogs re'i grub mthas khengs/ /ris med chos la dad pa'ang ma mthong na/ /mtha' yas dam

chos 'tshol ba'i skal ba ni/ /'byor ldan phal cher blun po'i rkang pa 'dzin/ /'ga' zhig grags 'dod mig rgyu'i rjes su 'brang / /phal cher lto gos bsgrubs pas rnam par g.yengs/
/mkhas blun 'byed pa'i mig ldan nyin skar mtshungs/ /grogs dag dal 'byor 'di ni g.yo ba dang / /slu med skye bo dam pa 'phrad pa dka'/ /thub bstan nyin byed 'di yang
nub nye bas/ /myur du dam chos btsal na mi legs bsam/ /de phyir nyin btsan ngal yong spangs te/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa rab gus pas/ /de ltar dka' bas dam pa'i chos
btsal nas/ /de nyid rtogs pa'i thabs la 'bad 'tshal lo/ /zang zing bde skyid 'ching bus mi mgu bar/ /dad brtson gtong phod gru rdzings cher bskyod de/ /ris med dam pa'i
chos tshul rgya mtsho cher/ /thogs med 'jug par nus pa de su yin/ /zhes gsungs so/ /sgrub pa nyams su bzhes tshul yang dgung lo bcu gsum gyi thog nas lo re bzhin du sku
