mtshams tha na'ang zla ba gsum tsam re ma chag pa mdzad/ rgyun gyi thugs dam spros bcas kyi rim pa la pham bsdus sku dal dus thun bzhi dang / shin tu brel tshe thun gnyis
sam/ bla ma rin 'byung / tshar gsum khug pa/ bir srung thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi bskyen rdzogs rnams thun re/ bde mchog lo nag dril gsum
re mos/ gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa/ gshed dmar lha lnga/ bde tshan ral gcig/ phyag rdor gtus chen/ rta mgrin yang gsang / sa phur/ phyag rdor a tsa/ sgrol dkar/ 'od zer can/
tshe dpag med/ gzungs grwa lnga

rnams kyi mngon rtogs bzlas dang bcas pa/ mkha' 'gro chos skyong la gtor ba bsngo thun bzhi/ gur gyi brag rdzong ma'i nag khrid/ brul gtor/ gtor ma brgya rtsa/ cha gsum sogs
nyin re'i khongs su chag med mdzad/ dgung lo so brgyad yan la kyai rdor man ngag lugs kyi bdag 'jug tshar sum brgya/ dus 'khor sku gsung thugs yongs rdzogs kyi bdag 'jug
tshar brgya dang nyer bzhi/ bde mchog lU i pa brgya dang drug cu rtsa lnga/ dril bu lus dkyil brgya dang lnga bcu rtsa lnga/ 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma lnga brgya lhag pa/
ro langs brgyang skor brgya tshar gcig /phyag rdor 'khor chen brgya dang lnga bcu lnga/ phag mo zhal gnyis ma brgya dang drug cu/ tshe dpag med dze tA ri nyis brgya dang
bzhi bcu rtsa grangs/ 'od zer can lha lnga nyis brgya dang lnga bcu rtsa brgyad/ kun rig brgya dang bdun cu/ gzhan yang mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho/ bde mchog lwa ba bcu gsum la/
dril bu lha lnga/ bong zhal can/ mai tri bcu gsum pa/ gsang 'dus 'jam rdor/ gur rigs bsdus/ bdag med lha mo bco lnga/ gshed dmar lha lnga/ sgrol ma phyi dkyil dang / lus
dkyil/ bde chen ral gcig/ nA ro mkha' spyod/ phyag rdor gtum chen/ mi g.yo bla med/ sa phur/ padma dra ba/ tshe dpag med lha so bdun ma/ gzungs grwa lnga/ rdo rje mi 'khrugs
pa lha dgu rnams la yang bdag 'jug tshar mang po song na'ang brgya bcu ma longs pa 'dug gsungs/ gzhan yang skye bdun ril bu'i sgrub pa mdzad pas sems can 'bum phrag
gsum 'khor ba las sgrol thub pa'i lung bstan byung pa dang / sa khyi zla ba dang po'i zhes bcu'i nub mo rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor mas zhal

gzigs lung bstan byung tshul/ kyai rdor gyi gzhi bsnyen mdzad pa'i tshe dpal kyai rdo rje zhal brgyad phyag bcu drug pa yum dang bcas pas zhal gzigs tshul sogs rgyas par thun
mong dang thun mong ma yin pa rnam thar rje rang nyid kyis mdzad pa yod pa las shes bar bya'o/ dgung lo nyer drug pa la ram sdings ma pa 'byung gnas rdo rje'i gdan sar
pebs nas chos 'khor bskor zhing de'i tshe me tog gi char dang dgon pa'i ltag na 'brug bdun nyal 'dug zer ba yang byung / de rjes skreg shing rin chen sgang gi gdan sa yang
bskyangs dgon pa de dag dang myug chos sde sogs su 'chad nyan dang sgrub mchod 'dzugs pa sogs bstan pa'i bya ba rgya cher mdzad/ de nas rje tshar chen gyis bka' bkod gnang
ste zhwa lu'i shar gyi chos lung du rgyal yum dbang mo'i spyan sngar chos gsan par phebs/ der rgyal yum dbang mo'i zhal nas khyed 'byon pa'i dus yol/ da nga rgan mo
'di 'drar gyur pas chos rgya chen po 'chad mi thub pa 'dug khyed ma 'ongs bar zhwa lu'i gdan sar phebs rgyur 'dug pas nged kyi chos skyong ma 'di gtad dgos gsungs nas lha
mo'i bka' gtad stsal zhing gzhan bu lugs kyi dbang chos kha shas gnang / zhwa lu mthil ba dang po phebs dus g.yu thog gi steng nas bya rog gcig 'phur nas rje nyid la bsu
ba byas/ log phebs dus kyang rgyan go dbar bskyal ba sor byung ste chos skyong gis su skyel zhus par snang dgung lo so drug pa la dpal sbug dgon pa btab/ de lo ri phug tu
rje tshar chen mjal bar phebs nas

der gsang 'dus rim lnga'i khrid don gnyer can dbang ma thob pa mang po 'dug par/ rje tshar chen gyis da lam khyed kyi dbang bskur mdzod gsungs nas zhwa lu pa'i grwa pa mang
rabs la gsang 'dus dang bde chen ral gcig gi dbang yang gnang rje tshar chen gyis zhwa lu pa'i las sne rnams lam/ nged sngar dge sbyor zhig la sgril snyam pa yod kyang khyed
kun gyis nan ches pas 'dir gdan sa lo gsum gyi ring byed dgos pa byung / da yang nged rang gi bsam pa bzhin byed dgos pas gdan sa'i 'os 'thus shig ces bka' stsal pas/
der thams cad kyis phyag phul nas da dung lo 'ga' de skad mi gsung ba zhu zhes zhus kyang zhal gyis ma bzhes/ de 'o na gnas gsar rje drung rin po che la zhu ba ma gtogs
gzhan gdan sa'i 'os med zer/ zhwa lu pa'i dge bshes bgres po smin ma dung mdog can nas/ btsun chung sran rdog mgo yan chad mgrin gcig tu bsdebs nas rje nyid la tshar chen
chos kyi rgyal po'i rgyal tshab zhwa lu'i mkhan po gnang dgos so zhes zhu ba dar der du byed/ sde pa rin spungs pas kyang bka' shog gnang bas rgyal yum dbang mo'i sngar
lung bstan gnang ba'ang dus la bab pa bcas lo gcig zhal bzhes mdzad/ rje tshar chen rin po che'i zhal nas/ ngas lo gsum byas khyed kyis lo gcig las ma byas na zhwa lu pa
tshos phyag rten kyang mi 'byor ram/ tha na'ang lo gsum nges par mdzod/ de nas bong sha za mi za bong bu'i kha stabs kyi dpe/ skyid po byung na tshe dang mnyam pa byas na'ang
legs/ sdug po byung na nam byung dus zhor thongs/ spyir 'di na bstan pa bsam

nas bya ba byed na dgon chung gzhan dang ye mi 'dra/ byed rgyu gang yang yod cing / 'chad nyan byed nus na sngar phan khyed rang gi dgon chung tshor 'chad nyan byas nga skad
sgra nam mkha' la rang deng mi 'gro/ lag rjes 'jog thub/ 'jig rten nas khams na skya ser 'di tsam zhig nar me ril me gang byed kyang rang re dbang che/ bza' cher mi bdog
lta pho rab gtam bza' zer ba yin/ gnas gsar pa phor pa yin pas/ gtam dga' mod ces zhal bkur yang gsung / de nas rab gnas su phebs te/ slar zhwa lur dge slong rdo rje 'dzin
pa'i chas tsam gyis byon na/ zhwa lu ba'i gzi brjid la gnod pa 'dug gsung / chibs rags mchor la mang ba dang bcas byon pa'i tshe/ zhwa lu pa'i bla ma las sne kun yang
thob rgyal bar chibs bsu thab 'dzin la 'ongs te/ de nas rim gyi tshong 'dus sogs nas dung rgya gling dang / zhwa lu pa'i dge 'dun mang pos ser sbreng dang 'phyar gar 'chams/
skye bo rnams kyis gzhas rgyag sogs bsu ba'i bkod pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sgo nas gdan drangs/ de'i tshe zhwa lu phyogs nas 'ja' sprin dkar po dar yug brkyangs pa
'dra bas rje nyid la bsu ba'i tshul du sne zug yong ba dang gzhan yang ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma byung zhing / zla ba drug pa'i tshes gcig lha'i bla ma rgyal sar 'byor
ba'i 'grub sbyor dge ba la/ zhwa lu ri mthil gyi dge 'dun rgya mtsho lta bu'i dbus su sengge'i khri gnyis bshams pa la yab sras lhan gcig bzhugs te/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal
pos me tog gtor zhing chos kyi rgyal tshab tu dbang

bskur / gos chen gyi ber thul dang / sku chos khyad du 'phags pa sogs kyang gnang zhing de'i tshe me tog gi char chen po yang babs/ sde ba gnas gsar ba sogs kyi khri ston gyi
bsnyen bkur bzang po'ang zhus/ de nas bzungs nye gnas phyag mdzod blo bzang lags kyi chos sde chen po'i srid phyogs khur bzhes dang / rje nyid nas zhwa lu gnas dgon gnyis
su 'chad nyan gyi khur chen po bzhes te/ chos 'khor rgyun mi chad pa lta bu bskor/ dus mchod chen mo'i skabs khams gsum rnam rgyal gyi cho ga yang chag tu nye bas/ 'di
skabs khro bo 'jig rten gsum las rnam par rgyal ba'i steng nas sa chog mdzad pas/ de nas bzungs gar pa zab mchor dang bcas pa lo re bzhin yar 'phel du song / dus mchod
pa la sa gar ma gtogs mchod gar sogs sngar med kyang rje nyid kyis gsar du btsugs/ zhwa lu'i gtsug lag khang dang bla brang nyams pa rnams la zhig gsos rgya che ba dang /
khyad par tshe dpag med kyi lhag khang du saMgha bha dra'i thugs bzhugs pa'i rgyal ba tshe mtha' yas kyi sku byin rlabs can de nyid kyi mthar tshe dpag med kyi snang brnyan
stong rtsa gcig gis bskor pa rje tshar chen gyi zhabs brtan la dmigs te gsar bzhengs mdzad/ gzhan yang dpal sbug /sdings ma/ myug chos sde/ sreg shing rin chen sgang
/ bo dong sogs gnas nges med rnams su'ang chos kyi 'khor lo rgya chen po bskor te gdul bya grangs kyi rab las 'das pa yang dag pa'i lam la bkod/ zhwa lur ma he mchod pa'i
chos rgyal yab yum gyi zhal brnyan la bka' bsgo

mdzad pa'i tshe dam can chos kyi rgyal po mdog khams nag spre'u dkar po dang mnyam pa zhig dngos su gzigs nas de wa bka' bsgo mdzad/ de'ang rje nyid sngon bu ston thams cad
mkhyen pa'i nye gnas bla ma dge slong bsod nams grub tu sku skye ba bzhes pas sku tshe 'dir zhwa lu pa'i bstan pa'i bdag por gyur/ gu ru chos dbang gi sras padma dbang chen
dang / sprul sku ratna gling ba sogs su 'khrungs pas dus 'dir rnying ma'i chos la 'gro phan dang 'phrin las che/ jo nang 'jam sgog tu 'khrungs pas sku tshe 'dir jo nang
pa'i lugs la mkhyen pa rgyas/ dpal ldan sa skya ba'i chos la sku tshe 'dir sbyangs stobs che zhing bka' bab che ba yin no/ /de yang gsan rgya la bltas nas sku tshe rang
chos gsan pa 'dra ba/ bsnyen pa'i grangs song ba la bltas nas sku tshe rang mtshams bcad nas bsnyen pa btang ba 'dra ba/ sgrub mchod song ba la bltas na sku tshe rang cho
ga mdzad pa 'dra ba/ dbang skur dang 'khrid bskyangs pa la bltas na sku tshe rang de dang de mdzad pa 'dra ba/ rtsom pa dang glegs bam bzhengs pa la bltas na sku tshe
rang yi ge 'bri zhing bzhugs pa 'dra ba yod do/ /dgung lo bzhi bcu zhe lnga pa sa pho 'brug gi lo zhing 'di'i mdzad pa phal cher rdzogs nas bo dong du phebs/ der hor zla
lnga pa'i tshes bco lnga la mkha' 'gro ma kha dog sna lnga so so'i sku mdog dang mthun pa'i seng ge'i chibs pa dngos su 'khrid nas spyan 'dren par brtsams pa na bu slob kun
gyis gsol ba btab

pas mkha' 'gro ma rnams slog yod gsungs nas yid gso ba mdad kyang slar zla ba de'i nyi shu gcig la dU ki ma rnams kyi tshogs dpon la gdan drangs te padma 'od kyi pho brang
du gshegs so/ /sku gdung rin po che ri phug gi byang ngos rgyal ba chos rdzong du gdan drangs te byang gling 'jam pa'i dbyangs rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan gyi zhugs 'bul
rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi cho ga'i steng nas mdzad spur khang gi thab ro la mchod rten khang brtsegs bzhengs ba da lta bzhugs/ khang brtsegs 'di la zhig gsos zhabs tog byas
na zhwa lu'i 'ong stod la ser ba mi yong ba zhig yod/ gsung las 'khrungs pa'i slob ma thugs kyi sras gsum du grags pa mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang
bsod nams chos 'phel/ dbon rin po dbang phyug rab brtan dang gsum mo/ gzhan yang 'phags mchog byams pa bskal bzang / gnubs sgom sbas pa'i rnal 'byor/ rwa chen bsod nams
rgyal mtshan/ thub bstan mkhan chen byams pa rab brtan/ brag dmar mkhan chen/ dbal sgang lo tsA ba ngag dbang chos kyi rgya mtsho/ rin lding slob dpon lha mchog pa/ lce'i
sngags 'chang don yod rdo rje/ chos rje dgos lung ba yab sras/ chos rje 'ug pa lung ba sogs mkhas grub kyi skyes bu dam pa mang du byung ngo / /| // mkhan chen bslab gsum
rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ni/ 'u yug sdings ma dang khad nye ba'i sa char/ yab rgya lhag dang / yum sgrol ma zhes bya ba gnyis kyi sras su me pho khyi'i lo'i tshes bcu
bzhizhig la sku

'khrungs / mtshan mtsho rgyal zhes btags/ cher gyur pa na ram sdings ma ba'i mkhan po drung pa 'ga' tshe ba'i spyan sngar rab tu byung / mtshan bslam gsum rgyal mtshan zhes
gsol/ /de nas 'bras yul skyel tshad du mtshan nyid kyi thugs gnyer mdzad cing bzhugs pa'i tshe sku tshe snga ma'i sbyangs stobs kyis rlung dbu mar tshud pa'i rtags snang
byung ste/ de'ang nam mkha' la mi'i rgyu mar 'brel ba'i don snying 'phyang phrul byed pa dang / de dag la sbrang ba'i tshogs 'dub 'dra ba zhig la zhib tu brtag tshe sangs
rgyas byang sems kyi gzugs du mthim 'gro ba rgyun du gzigs/ de la thugs yengs nas chos spyod bskul 'phro chad pas grwa pa rnams na re/ dbu mdzad bslab gsum pa chos spyod
bskul 'phro la yengs 'gro ba 'di 'dra ci yin nam zer skad/ lan cig ston po bsod snyoms la 'u yug phyogs la byon pas rje mkhyen brtse'i drung sdings ma dgon pa na bzhugs
pa dang mjal nas mi phyed pa'i dad pa thob/ mdo phyogs kyi thugs gnyer gyi 'phro yang bshol te bla ma'i phyag phyier khrid pa zhus nas bka' bzhin sgrub pa'i mos gus chen
pos mchod de sras kyi thu bor gyur to/ /rje mkhyen brtse'i drung zhing gshegs pa'i lo rting ma sa mo sbrul gyi lo nyid kyi dgung lo bzhi bcu zhe bzhi pa la bo dong bya gshongs
su 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gyis mkhan po mdzad nas bsnyen par rdzogs/ yon bder bo dong e'i mkhan po'i gdan sar yang phebs/ dgung lo lnga bcu gnyis pa
me mo glang gi lo smin drug zla ba'i tshes

gsum gyi nam gung tsam la bo dong gi sgrub sder sku gshegs/ /mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel ni/ 'khrungs sa shangs kyi mdog langs yul skyid pa'i
ljongs su yab 'bru'i sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen dang / yum 'bar ra ba'i btsun ma chos 'dzoms rgyal mo bya ba gnyis kyi sras su me mo phag gi lo la sku 'khrungs/
dgung lo bcu gcig pa la myug tu 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dpal 'byor ba'i drung du dge bsnyen gyi brtul zhugs nos/ mtshan bsod nams chos 'phel zhes gsol/ bco brgyad pa la gser
mdog can du paN chen grags pa thogs med kyi spyan sngar tshigs sdam dge tshul bsgrub/ nyi shu rtsa brgyad pa la gser mdog can gyi mkhan po dge 'dun nyi ma dang / las slob
grags pa thogs med sogs dge 'dun bcu phrag gcig gi dbus su bsnyen par rdzogs/ dgung lo so gsum nas bzungs kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi zhabs 'bring du bzhagus
nas sras kyi thu bor gyur/ de nas bo dong rta ra'i gdan sa/ lha sa nor bu chos gling / 'dar grangs chen sogs kyi gdan sa bskyangs/ dgung lo bdun cu don bdun pa chu mo
yos kyi lo/ rgyal gyi zla ba'i tshes bcu gnyis kyi tho rengs dpal ldan grang mo che'i bla brang chos dbyings dkar por ngo mtshar ba'i ltas dang bcas te zhing brje ba'i
tshul bstan to/ /mkhyen brtse yab sras kyi skabs so/ /| gnyis pa ni/ chos dkon mchog gi lam bzang ston la mkhas/ / zhes byung bas chos rje chu mig kha pa dkon

mchog dpal bzang po ni/ 'khrungs sa grib 'dar smad pa yin/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje sogs yongs 'dzin dam pa mang po'i zhabs la gtugs nas mdo rgyud kyi chos la thos
bsam mthar phyin pa mdzad cing / ri phug ti byang gling chu mig gi nye logs su sku mtshams bcad nas sgrub pa yun ring po'i bar du mdzad pas thugs dam rtogs pa mthar 'khyol/
sku tshe'i mjug la 'chad spel sogs kyang rgyun ring ba mdzad gda' zhing ma hA ma ya'i sgrub dkyil gyi lhan thabs sogs gsung rab 'ga' re yang yod par grags so//gsum pa
ni/ rang gzhan don kun lhun grub rgyal mtshan 'chang / /zhes byung pas chos rje 'brog khang pa don grub rgyal mtshan ni/ mkhyen rab rje'i zhabs kyang zin cing / lhag tu
rje dbon rgyal ba sogs kyi dngos slob kyi gtso bo yin pa dang / gsang sngags rab 'byams pa chen po yin zhes grags/ rdo rje 'jigs byed dang gshed dmar sogs bsgrubs pas zhal
gzigs shing nus mthu shin tu che ba byung la/ ri phug gi gzims khang shar chen gyi g.yab tu bu ston bka' 'bum sogs dbang lung mang po nyin zhag du ma'i bar la gnang /
slob ma'i gtso bo byang gling rje rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan dang chos rje bsod nams dpal 'byor/ sku zhang bkra shis rgyal mtshan sogs yin zhing / 'jigs byed kyi yig
cha mdzad pa sogs gsung rtsom kha 'thor bzhugs pa dag kyang snang

zhing rje 'di nyid kyi zhwa lu grang chen pa dang de rjes dkar po grwa tshang ba'i bla ma yang mdzad pa yin zhes grag go/ //gsol 'debs/ 'dul ba'i bstan pas 'gro rnams bskal
bzang sbyor/ /byang gling bkra shis bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan bzung / /rigs kun khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan rje/ /mtshungs med dam pa gsum la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes so/
/dang po ni/ 'dul ba'i bstan pas 'gro rnams bskal bzang sbyor/ /zhes chos rje gnas brtan bstan pa bzang po'i zhal snga nas ni/ gzhi tshul khrims rnam par dag pa dang ldan
pa'i sgo nas/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje'i dngos slob 'dul 'dzin dge slong chos legs pa/ mkhan chen rig 'dzin rgyal po/ chos rje dbon rgyal ba sogs yongs 'dzin
du ma bsten nas mdo sngags mtha' dag la mkhas par mdzad/ khyad par rnal 'byor rgyud kyi de kho na nyid bcu'i gnas la pha rol du son pas rdo rje slob dpon chen po'i go 'phang
mchog la gzhol ba yin te/ bstod pa las kyang / sangs rgyas bstan pa'i gangs ri la/ /gnas bcas sdom gsum lus stobs rgyas/ /rgyu sde'i mche sder bzang po can/ /smra ba'i
seng ge de la 'dud/ /ces bsngags pa don dang ldan pa zhig go/ de yang gtso bor chos grwa chen po dpal 'khor sde chen du rin lding grwa tshang gi gdan sa bskyangs nas yo
ga'i 'chad nyan sogs 'phrin las rgya che la rgyun ring ba byung tshul yod do// | //gnyis pa ni/ byang gling bkra shis bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan bzur/ /

zhes 'byung bas/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs byang gling ba chen po rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i rnam thar mdzad pa zur tsam zhig /rje nyid kyi bka' 'bum rin po che'i
dkar chag mkhas pa'i mgul rgyan bsam 'phel nor bu'i 'phreng ba zhes bya ba na bkod 'dug pas 'dir de kho na bri bar bya'o/ /bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la gus pas phyag 'tshal
lo/ /rin chen grub pa'i bstan pa'i khang bzang mchog /bkra shis 'dod dgu'i nor bu'i yongs gang rtser/ /bshad sgrub rgyal mtshan 'dzin la zla bral ba/ /dpal ldan yongs
'dzin bzang po khyod phyag 'tshal/ /gang gi mkhyen pa'i 'od zer 'bum phrag gis/ /thub dbang gsung rab pad tshal bye ba las/ /grub gnyis ci 'dod stsol ba'i legs bshad bcud/
/glegs bam gcig tu gus pas bka' bsdu bgyi/ /de la 'phags pa'i gnas brtan chen po nags na gnyis nyid snyigs dus kyi bstan pa dang 'gro ba la brtse ba'i thugs kyis bsam pa
bzhin du/ mkhas grub chen po mgon po rgyal mtshan dang / de'i dpon po chos rje rin chen rgyal po sogs bstan pa'i bdag po rim par byon pa'i brgyud du dpal zhwa lu ri phyag
gi dgon smad byang gling zhes bya ba'i khyim du bya'i lo la sku'i bkod pa bstan/ gzhon nu nyid nas byis pa'i spyod pa ring du spangs te/ rgyal ba'i bstan pa'i snying po
kun mkhyen bu ston chen po'i ring lugs dri ma med pa rtsod dus kyi rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje'i brgyud srol

'dzin pa dpal ldan dkar po grwa tshang gi grwa pa mdzad/ de'i rgyu mtshan gyis dbu skra gtsug phud 'bul ba dang / so thar gyi tshigs snga ma sogs sku zhang bsod nams mchog
grub kyi drung du bzhes sam snyam/ nges gsal ni ma mthong / gang ltar gzhi tshul khrims rnams dag rgyan du bzhes te/ mtshan rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan dpal bzang por
gsol lo/ /bstan pa dang sems can gyi don du thugs kyi go cha chen po bskyed de nyin mtshan thos bsam sgom pa las cung zad kyang mi g.yel ba mdzad/ dus mchod chen mo dang
bco lnga tshes gnyis kyi zan tshul skam po la bzhes thugs mdzad nas kyang thugs gnyer la rtse gcig tu bzhagus so/ /drung chen grang kha dkar po ba dang mnyam du bzhugs pas/
khyed kyi nyal lugs dang nga'i slob gnyer la brtson lugs 'dis ma 'ongs pa na/ khyed kyi sngas mgor ngas dril bu sila'ang zer/ cho ga gtong dgos pa 'dra gsungs pas/ kho
khros skad do/ /bem po mang po bsgrigs nas de la slob ma'i tshab mdzad de sgrub pa'i lha 'god pa'i phyag rgya sbyong ba sogs mdzad/ sku zhang grub pa'i dbang phyug rin
chen bsod nams mchog grub dpal bzang po/ chos rje sgog lung pa bkra shis dpal 'byor/ chu mig kha pa'am/ grib 'dar smad pa chos rje dkon mchog dpal bzang / 'brog khang pa
don grub rgyal mtshan/ rin sdings pa bstan pa bzang po/ /lha bo slob dpon srad dgon stod pa bsod nams dpal 'byor sogs bsten nas bu lugs kyi dbang lung gsan

bsam mthar phyin pa mdzad/ bka' las/ khyed tshong gcig pu la dbang chos zhus chog pa 'di las sla ba e 'dug /ngas srad/ nyang stod kyi sa char rlung dang kha char sogs la ma
'dzem par/ rgyab la khrel po 'khur nas chos 'di tsho chad dogs rtsad bcad nas zhus pa yin gsung ngo / /gzhan yang zhwa lu mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang tshar chen chos kyi rgyal
po dang / thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /ngor e waM chos ldan gyi mkhan po 'jam pa'i dbyangs dkon mchog lhun grub rnams la chos gsan/ bsnyen rdzogs
kyang rje dkon mchog lhun grub pa la bzhes sam snyam/ der ma zad shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun sangs rgyas seng ge/ mkhan chen dkon mchog dpal ldan/ rtogs
pa'i mnga' bdag la phyi rtogs ldan pa rnams la'ang chos gsan no/ bka' las/ ngas ngor du rje dkon mchog lhun grub la lam 'bras zhus dus/ sems ngo shes pa tsam ni byung /
phra zhing phra ba ni la phyi rtogs ldan pa'i bka' drin yin gsung ngo / pa rnam 'phags rgyal dgon par la phyi rtogs ldan pa'i gdan sa yang mdzad/ de'i dus su yang sku mtshams
kho na mdzad/ gyeng 'og thams cad dkyil 'khor dang mchod rten gyi thig gis bskangs so/ rje btsun thams cad mkhyen pa dpal ldan kun dga' grol mchog las sbyor ba yan
lag drug la sogs pa gsan pa sogs mdor na snga phyir bla ma dam pa mang du bsten nas gsan pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol du

gsan pa mdzad do/ bla brang shar chen du nags nya sgrub mchod la phebs dus shig dbu mdzad kyang rje 'dis mdzad/ de'i skabs chog shes pa ni mang po med pas/ dbang go chen dang
bstod chen gyi dus mchog g.yog gis mgo bsdams pa dang / 'brog pa gcig la the tshom skyes nas nang du yibs bsdad nas cho ga nyan no/ /slar khong rang gi yul du sleb nas
bla brang shar chen na cho ga yag po e 'dug ces 'dri mkhan byung ba la/ kho na re/ gzhan ni mi shes/ bzhugs khri'i 'khris de na byang gling chos mdzad pa ni/ 'khor lo dkar
po'i lta ba la/ 'khor lo dmar po'i lte ba la/ zer gyi 'dug go/ nags nya'i dkyil 'khor gyi steng nas 'jim dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug la dus 'khor gyi dbang yang
gnang 'dug /dpal 'khor chos sde'i rin sdings grwa tshang gi slob dpon yang mdzad/ mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis ri phug dbu mdzad chen mor
mnga' gsol nas zhing gzhan la ma gshegs kyi bar du gdan sa mdzad/ dus phyis rgyal ba chos rdzong gi ri khrod la zhig bsos mdzad de/ der thugs dam dang 'chad nyan kho na mdzad
do/ /rgyal ba chos rdzong du mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i sgrub mchod nyin zhag mang po mdzad dus ni/ nyin re bzhin du yang mchod 'phreng dang bstun nas me tog gi char chen
po babs pa las/ 'di 'dra 'ong ba ngo mtshar che zhus pas/ dkyil 'khor 'di la mkha' 'gro ma mang grags pas khong rang tshos dkyil 'khor mchod pa'i phyir me tog gtor ba
yin nam gsung skad/ rgyal ba chos rdzong du 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi sku

gdung rin po che zhugs 'bul rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi cho ga'i steng nas gnang ste/ gdung rnams thab nas spyan 'dren dus me thag chod kyang dbu ja ril du byon pa'i spyan gnyis
nas me 'khyug 'khyug 'bar byung ba la ni/ bka' las nga'i zhong gis thugs rje'i spyan gyis gzigs gsung rgyu yin pa gda'o gsung / de skabs kyi phyag phyi thams cad dang /
lhag par sbyin sreg gi sgang la khri'u shing brten pa la sku zhabs rang dang ngar pa bsdad yod cing / thab sogs gra bsgrigs grub pa dang / da' 'bus bdag bskyed cig byasakyi
gsung / nyi phug la bdag bskyed bzhes ba gnang song zhes rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan las dngos su thos/ de dus gzhugs 'bul gnang sa rgyal ba chos rdzong gi mdun
zhol da skabs rlung ra yin pa der mdzad de/ thabs kyi sa phag sogs la rgyab kyi la nyag gi mchod rten khang bu brtsegs pa 'di bzhengs pa yin 'dug go /mchod rten 'di la
zhig gsos dang zhabs tog byas na zhwa lu'i 'ong stod la ser ba mi yong ba zhig kyang yod do/ /rgyal ba chos rdzong gi rtse nas gos brda gzan dmar re brkyangs pa dang ri
phug nas chos zhu ba rnams 'byon yod skad/ byang gling du'ang chos brda la gos brda rang mdzad pa zhig yod par gda'/ bu ston bka' 'bum gyi lung gnang res gcig gis skabs der/
rgyal ba chos rdzong gi byang gi chu mig gi 'khris na shing sdong po gcig yod pa'i rtsar chos gsungs so/ /bka' 'bum

gyi lung zhu mi snga ma ni mang po yod kyang / /rjes su ni drung kun bkras pa gcig pu las ni ma byung ngo / drung lags kyis/ da bdag gcig pu la bka' chos gnang ba ni sku 'o
rgyal ba 'dug zhus pas/ khyed rang nyan nus na nga 'bu mi mang po la byed pa dang khyed gcig pu la byed pa la khyad mi gda' gsung / phyis lung rgyun tshang ma ma chad pa
ni/ drung kun bkras lags nas 'phel ba yin/ de la sogs pa'i ma 'ongs pa mkhyen pa'i gsung rang bzhin gyis bsnyad pa yang mang du thos/ drung lags 'di la ni thugs rtsis che
ste/ gzhan rnams la'ang drung kun bkras lags zer dgos gsung zhing dbang nam gnang gi mchod g.yog mdzad/ de gong khams gsum rnam rgyal gyi chog bdag sus byas la gegs byung
bas rnam rtog chen po byed pa zhig yod par/ drung lags su rje nyid nas zan bris kyang thugs rtsom mdzad nas gnang / gegs dang bar chad mi yong bar zhal gyis bzhes so/
drung lags kyis kyang bsnyen pa 'ang mdzad cing cho ga'i bdag po rgyun ring mdzad de gegs ni med sku tshe ni mthar phyin to dgung lo brgyad cu gya gsum bzhugs pa sman bla'i
zhal 'don nyin mtshan khor yug tu 'gro ba zhig go/ rje bla ma 'di ni rdo rje 'phreng ba'i dkyil 'khor so sor bgrangs pa'i dkyil 'khor brgya dang brgyad cu gya gsum la
bsnyel gso mi dgos/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho la bsnyel gso'i tshul tsam mdzad do zhes bdag gi bla ma rdo rje 'chang dbang phyag rab brtan gsung ngo / de yang khri khang sde
ba

chos rjes mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dbang gi gsol btab zhus pas/ 'di rgan slob tu song bas brjed gso dgos pa yod gsung / khong dpon slob kyi sems la dkyil 'khor chen po de la
bsnyel gso zla gcig tsam nges par dgos snyam nas yangs pa can du bzhugs zhag mang po mdzad rtsis bca' bsgrigs mdzad nas bzhugs pas zhag gnyis gsum song ba la/ byang gling
nas sta gon la byon zhes brda gnang ba byung skad/ bdag gi bla ma mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub pa'i gsung las/ dus phyis bod yul du dbang gnang mkhan gyi rdo rje 'dzin
pa rje byang gling pa lta bu ma byung / dbang gang gnang kyang sta gon da lta byed gsungs thogs pa med pa cig yod par gda' gsungs ngo / dpal kye rdo rje la sogs pa'i bsnyen
pa mthar phyin/ lam dus sogs chag med du mdzad cing dus rgyun du spros med kyi don la mnyam gzhag las nam yang mi g.yel phyag mnyam bzhag dang zhabs rdor skyil la nyin
mtshan phal cher bzhugs mdzad/ mtshan mo'ang sku'i phyogs bzhi ka la sku mnye bzhag pa thams cad na bzas bsdams/ lus gnad ma zhig par bzhugs pa dang sku cung zad seng ba
mthong pas dzA ti'i dud pa yang yang gtad dgos pa zhig yod ces thos/ sku gzugs phral ring ba/ zil che ba/ gsung rling pa/ thugs shin tu sgam pa/ drung du lo rgyus kyis
snyan 'bul mang po zhus na/ de su zer gyin gda'

gsung / khung btsun pa 'di 'drazhig zer gyin gda' lags zhus na/ de bden shas che gsung / gzhan 'dra zer gyin gda' zhus na/ de 'dra'i rigs la bden zer bcas na bslus yong gsung
/ skabs shig rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan sku chos ma gnang gong / paN khung gu lung du bzhugs dus/ ched gtad mjal bar phebs thugs sam la da res sgrol dkar gyi
rjes gnang zhig zhu dgos dgongs pa thugs la 'khrungs pa thugs kyis mkhyen nas rgyal ba chos rdzong du phebs 'phral sgrol dkar gyi thugs dam grub 'dug pa ltar rjes gnang
dang gsol ja zhal dkar khengs pa'i gsol ras gnang / bkra shis rgyas pa dang 'das ma 'ong gi bslab ston mthil phyin mang po gnang byung pas re ba khengs pa byung gsung / de
gong zhig byang gling du mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dbang gsan dus/ zhwa lu'i chen slob 'dra yang dbang la yongs pa sgug dgos byung / rje nyid khri'u shing gi khang khyel
bzhugs kho na'i ngang la sgug gin yun ring bzhugs/ slebs pa dang khyed tshos ka 'di ga kyang byas gsungs/ bka' bskyon drag po gnang song gsung / rje 'di bo dong sogs su spyan
drangs nas phebs dus/ phebs ma thag gi bzhugs gral de la/ byang gling nas phebs pa nas bzung / bzhugs stan der ma phebs bar gyi bzhugs 'tsher sogs kyi lo rgyus rgyas
par gsung pa dang / gsol ba'i rjes su bshos chang re phyag tu 'chir ba mdzad pa zhig yod gsung / bo dong du 'brug

lo gnas gsar nas mchod yon gshegs dus/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan sras gsum/ bo dong bkra shis sgang du phebs pa'i bsrung 'khor la rje 'dis phebs/ nyin re bzhin gzungs
grwa lnga'i dbang tshar re gnang gsung ngo / /mdor na gsung skyes kyi slob ma yang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug/ ngor chen paN chen nam mkha' dpal
bzang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs mus pa chen po ga ga na shrI bha dra/ bo dong mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ mdar grang mo cha'i mkhan chen bsod nams chos 'phel/ rog tsho
byang pa mkhas pa'i dbang po/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ ri phUg dbu mdzad lha mchog sengge/ chen po byang pa dpal ldan chos bzang / rin lding slob dpon yo ga
ba chen po rin chen sangs rgyas tshe dpal/ ri phug dbu mdzad ku sA li ba rgyal mtshan bzang po/ phreng chen slob dpon rdo rje 'dzin pa shAkya sengge/ ri phug dbu mdzad rdo
rje slob dpon lha bo pa rin chen ri phug dbu mdzad khro khang chos rje kun dga' mchog ldan sogs/ de dus kyi zhwa lu/ ngor/ dpal 'khor bde chen gyis zhal kya bstan 'dzin
phal cher dang / rgyud chen sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ gangs ri'i bla ma rje lhun grub don ldan

sogs mkhas grub kyi skyes sku gzhon dus phebs dus yang yang zhal mjal mod/ sku na phra bas chos gsan rgyu ma byung pas/ rjes su rnam thar du'ang / snga sor zhwa lu pa'i bka'
srol skyong ba rdo rje 'dzin pa'i dbang phyug rje byang gling pa la chos gang gang zhu zhu yod kyang / 'dug pa med pas zhu ma thub/ 'di skabs sku gshegs pas phyis 'gyod
pa byung / zhes gsungs te rje nyid sku gshegs pa'i dus rje btsun dgung lo bcu gcig 'gro ba tshal ka yin 'dug go/ dus skabs der yang slob ma rnying hral can khag cig gi bya
spyod la thugs gting nas khrel ba'i rtags su/ gsung rab kyi mdzad byang 'ga' zhig las kyang / bstan par zhugs kyang snying rjes dpon/ /dbang bskur kyang rim gnyis lam
mi sgom/ /nam tshig ji bzhin du'ang / bsrung bar dka' ba'i slob dpon tshul 'dzin pa/ /skyon ldan yon tan med pa gang de yi/ /bstan la phan par byang sems bskyed kyang / /rang
la yon tan med pa'i rgyu mtshan gyi/ /gzhan gyi rgyud la ban gyur te/ /slob mar gyur pa'i gang zag 'ga' zhig la/ /nad pa sman sbyar dus du song ba ltar/ /zla mo lha
dang chos dang dam tshig la/ /nyin par khA tas 'ug pa mthong ba bzhin/ /gnyis ka'i sems brgyud dkrugs nas phyin chad slad/ /skyes bu shi bas ro bzhin nas/ /mi byed  mthong
bar bdag yid skyod/ /zhes 'byung ngo /chen mang du bskrun no/ /de nas rgyal rtse rtse chen du spyan drangs pa'i dus zhig sku khams cung ma bde bar tshur lam zhwa lur bsam
yas su zhag shas bzhugs/ de nas byang gling du phebs nas sku grib la brten pa'i shin tu nyog pa zhig gi zhabs phyir dge slong bsam gtan pa bzhugs yod dus/ byang gling
gi tshom gyi steng du

bzhugs / mnal 'thibs pa dang shar gling nas star kha'i yal ga long shog gsungs/ blangs nas phul ba dang de ka To rar chu'i nang du bcug pa'i zil pa dang bcas pa de'i dbu la
bsil yab mdzad nas/ 'o nged tsho 'di 'dra'i bsil yab la sdod pa yin zhes lo ma bdun pa'i ri phur na bzhur pa'i 'phags pa'i gnas brtan chen po nags na gsan kyi sprul par
don gyis zhal gyis bzhes so zhes dge slong bsam gtan pa gsung ngo / rje nyid kyi dgung lo re bdun bzhes pa yos lo hor zla dgu pa'i tshes bzhi'i nyi ma gros chen la ri phug
byang gling bla brang gi tshom gyi zur bzhugs nas dga' ldan du gshegs/ sku gdung rin thang med pa'i yid bzhin nor bu de nyid 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i mchod dpon drung
dkon mchog legs pas phyag len mdzad de/ sprod rtse mchod rten gyi bum ldir 'dra ba zhig gi nang du sman dang dri bzang na bza' dang bcas pa bzhugs su gsol/ sa 'ja' li'i
phyogs bzhir steng khebs g.yogs pa'i steng du sprod rtse bzhag/ shing gi bre gcig legs par bkrus pa'i phyogs bzhir spyan bris/ smyug pa'i chos 'khor bcu gsum gyi tshul la
dar dkris pa'i mkhan maNDal gyi gdugs tog dang bcas te/ mchod rten gyi tshul byas pa mchod sprin rgya mtsho'i dbus su bzhugs so gsol zhing gsol 'debs rgyas par bsgrubs
shing / khyad par dgongs rdzogs dngos gzhi zhwa lu chos sder/ gnas

dgon gnyis kyi dge 'dun tsho chen du zhabs brtan bsgrubs pa'i nyin/ nam mkha' sngo sangs pa ser bu spu 'gul ba tsam yang med pa byung / ngor nas mkhan rin po che brang ti paN
chen nam mkha' dpal bzang spyan drangs nas/ sku gdung rin po che byang gling bla brag gi tshom du zhugs la phul/ pur ras thog khar nyi ma la skam dus me tog gi char sna
tshogs bab/ sku tshab gzims mal sku 'dra gser zangs las sku dngos su byon pa lta bu bsgrubs te/ de'i lo rgyus rgyas par dkar chag tu gsal lo/ zhal slob rnams kyis gsung
gi chu rgyun mi nyams par spel te/ mdor na ding sang kun mkhyen bu ston rin po che'i gsang sngags kyi bstan pa'i rgyun yod pa 'di ni rje 'di gcig pu'i bka' drin yin no/
/de skabs bka' 'bum phyogs gcig tu bzhugs pa'i ma byung 'dug/ de nas lo sum cu skor song ba'i dus/ /bdag gi lo bcu bzhi bco lnga tsam 'gro ba'i dus su pha ma la dge bskul
bgyis te/ glegs bam phyogs gcig tu bzhugs pa la/ thogs mar gsol 'debs bstod tshogs kyi skor la/ rje rang nyid la bstod pa dkon mchog gsum lam/ rin chen rgyud sde ma mkhan
chen thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i mtshan can gyi zhal snga nas la gsol pa 'debs pa'i rab byed/ sbyor drug brgyud 'debs stong nyid ma'i bskong mkhyen rang rje'i yan
chod/ bde mchog dril bu pa'i dbang khrid brgyud 'debs/ na' no mkha' spyod kyi rgyud 'debs/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i

dbang bka'i rgyud 'debs yon tan rjes dran ma'i kha skong chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa chen po man chod/ tshe dpag med grub rgyal lugs kyi rgyud 'debs/ thugs rje chen po'i dmar
khrid tshom bu lugs kyi rgyud 'debs mkhyen rab rjes mdzad pa'i kha skong / 'chi med rnga sgra'i rgyud 'debs rnams so/ | /ma rgyud skor la dpal 'khor lo sdoms pa nag po
pa'i sgrub dkyil gyi lhan thabs phun tshogs rab rgyas/ bde mchog lU nag gi man ngag gi thig rtsa/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa rdul tshon lha lnga'i sgrub dkyil gyi lhan thabs
phyag len gsal bar byed pa'i sgron me/ dpal mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i sgrub dkyil gyi lhan thabs gsang ba'i mdzod rnams kyi sgo 'byed pa'i lde mig /mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i
thig rtsa dang mchon gyi rim pa/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi zhi ba'i sbyin sreg ye shes me lce/ phag dkar shes rab gsal byed kyi sgrub thabs dang / mgon dkar yid bzhin nor bu'i
gtor chog /rje btsun sgrol ma lha bcu bdun gyi dkyil mchog dbang bzhi rab gsal slob ma sta gon yan/ sgron ma lus dkyil gyi sgrub dkyil gyi lhan thabs 'phrin las dpal 'bar
rnams so/ /pha rgyud skor la/ gsang 'dus rim lnga'i rgyun gyi nyams len rin po che dbang gi rgyal po/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i sgrub dkyil gyi lhan thabs
'jam dbyangs thugs rje'i chu rgyun/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa spyan ras gzigs

kyi dkyil 'khor las rim gyi cho ga'i ngag 'don thugs rje'i 'od zer/ gshed dmar spros med rgyun gyi nyams len/ bcom ldan 'das gshin rje gshed dmar po'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg ngag
'don don dang ldan zhing 'jug pa bde ba/ bcom ldan 'das gshin rje gshed dus dgra nag po'i mngon dkyil gyi lhan thabs dngos grub rab rgyas/ bcom ldan 'das gshin rje gshed
zhal drug pa'i mngon dkyil gyi lhan thabs phan bde kun gyi 'byung gnas/ dpal phyag na rdo rje gtum po lce lugs kyi dkyil 'khor las rim gyi cho ga'i ngag 'don phyogs bsgrigs
thar chags su bkod pa ngag 'don 'jug bde gsal ba/ dpal phyag na rdo rje gtum po chen po'i dbang gong ma'i cho ga /bla med spyi'i nyams len/ dmar 'khrid nyams len tshigs
bcad ma ngo sprod dang bcas pa rnams so/ /rnal 'byor rgyud pa/ cha gsum 'bring po'i lhan thabs gtor ma'i cho ga gsal byed/ rdor dbyings 'grel pa lugs kyi dbang chog
gi lhan thabs dbang gi rim pa gsal byed/ bcom ldan 'das 'jig rten gsum las rgya ma bar rgyal ba'i dkyil mchog gi lhan thabs ma rig mun sel sgron me/ dpal mo ka rdo rje sems
dpa'i dkyil chog gi lhan thabs phyag len gsal byed nyi ma'i 'od zer/ bcom ldan 'das shAkya sengge gtsug tor dgu pa'i dkyil mchog gi lhan thabs dgos 'dod 'byung ba'i nor
bu/ mi 'khrugs pa'i dkyil

'khor gyi cho ga'i lhan thabs gzhan phan thugs rje'i chu rgyun/ bcom ldan 'das nam mkha' ltar dri ma med pa chos kyi dbyings gsung gi dbang phyug gi dkyil chog gi lhan thabs
mkhas pa'i dga' ston gsal par byed pa'i sgron me/ chos dbyings gsung dbang gi thig rtsa/ de'i lha 'god tshul dang phyag rgya'i 'ching tshul gsung rgyun mu tig gi 'phreng
ba rnams so/ | /bya spyod kyi skor la/ bya spyod kyi rigs su gtogs pa'i rjes gnang spyi 'gro/ bkru bya ba srungs gsum gyi cho ga lag len gsal ba/ mchod rten gyi cha dbye
ba'i bstan bcos byin brlabs dpal 'bar gsal byed ces pa/ bde gshegs mchod rten brgyad kyi thig rtsa tshigs bcad ma dang / bde gshegs mchod rten brgyad kyi thig rtsa tshigs
lhug ma shin tu gsal ba/ grwa rdo rje sengge nas brgyud pa'i gtsug tor 'bar ba'i sgrub thabs gtor bzlog dang bcas pa/ sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs brgyud
'debs dang bcas pa 'chi med tshe stsol/ rnam sras zhi drag gi chog bsgrigs rgyal po'i thugs dam skong ba/ rnam sras kyi bskang gso rin chen dbang gi rgyal po rnams so/
/zhal gdams 'phrin yig gi skor la/ lam rim ngo sprod dge legs rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i zhabs drung du phul ba'i zhu 'phrin gnyis/ bla ma'i
gdan bzhugs kyi phyag

len rnams bzhugs so/ thog ma bar dang mthar dge ba/ drang srong chen po'i gsung ji lta'i/ gang gsung rin chen lde mig 'dis/ bu ston gsung mdzod kun la dbang / /dge tshogs dri
med chu rgyun des/ /yid can sgrib gnyis dri ma dang / 'dir nongs nyes pa'i dri bkrus nas/ /kun mkhyen rgya mtsho ro gcig gyur/ /bdag kyang kun mkhyen bu ston gyis/ /gsung
rab tshig don ma lus pa/ /'bad med myur du khong chud nas/ /'jam mgon bla ma khyed bzhin shog /bka' 'bum rin po che'i dkar chags mkhas pa'i mgul rgyan bsam 'phel nor
bu'i 'phreng ba zhes bya ba 'dis/ /zha lu pa bhi ratna pu par ma siddhi shAs dhA dza shri bha dras mdzes byed kyi lo/ mchu zla ba'i tshes bcu la dpal zhwa lu'i bla brang
du sbyar ba dge legs/ zhes pa ltar ro/ rje btsun byang gling pa chen po de nyid kyi bu chen zha lu nyid du grags che ba bla ma dam pa dpal ldan chos bzang / chos rje kun
dga' bkra shis/ ku sA li ba rgyal mtshan bzang po/ rin po che dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan dang lnga'o/ /de dag las bla ma dam pa dpal ldan
chos bzang pa'i lo rgyus zhib tu ma 'tshal mod/ 'on kyang rje nyid rang gi gsan yig phyag bris ngo ma yin nam snyam pa'i shog ril tshal bu chung ngu zhig bdag gis rnyed
de mthong ba na 'di ltar bris snang / thog mar shing mo sbrul gyi lo/ hor zla lnga pa'i tshes drug la/ 'og min stug po bkod pa dang tshul mtshungs pa'i ri

phug chos kyi pho brang chen por gzims lam sku 'dra'i drung / mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas dang / /las slob/ bskong dang bcas ba de dge slong lnga'i
dbus su rab byung gi sdom pa nos shing / me pho rta'i lo hor zla brgyad pa'i tshes bcu'i nyin/ las tshan rnams kyi spyan sngar sngags kyis grwa bskor kyang phul/ mkhan
chen de nyid las brgyad stong pa/ chos 'byung chen mo/ mtshan brjod dang bzang spyod sher snying rnams kyi lung / /rnam rgyal dang rnam 'joms gnyis kyi rjes gnang thob/ ces
bya ba 'dug pas mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs dpal bzang po'i zhabs zin lugs kyis de 'og tshar chen yab sras la'ang chos gsan pa zhig yin par shugs la go/ gtso bor ni rje byang
gling ba nyid kyis thugs sras yin te/ dus 'khor gyi bla brgyud gsol 'debs las/ dpal ldan bla ma'i thugs sras mchog /zab yangs chos kyi spyan dang ldan/ /bskal bzang 'gro
ba'i 'dren mchog gi /zhabs la phyag 'tshal skyabs su mchi/ /zhes 'byung ba ltar ro/ gzhan yang 'di nyid kyi zhwa lu grang chen pa dang / /phyis khri byang ma chen po'i
gdan sa mdzad de chos 'khor bskor/ mchog gi sprul ba'i sku tA ra nA tha dang / ngor mkhan chen/ sgrub khang ba dpal ldan don grub sogs gzhan phyogs kyi bstan 'dzin chen
po du mas kyang rje 'di'i zhabs la rab tu gus pas phyag mdzad nas chos mang du gsan tshul 'dug go /chos

rje kun dga' bkra shis dpal bzang po de ni/ 'khrungs yul mag dge sding gi phu ngos nas yin/ gzhon nu nyid nas zhwa lu ri phug gi btsun pa mdzad nas rje byang gling pa sogs
las gsan pa rgya cher gnang / rjes su bu ston bka' 'bum gyi steng nas chos gsungs pa'i gzhan phan 'phrin las bzang bo byung / ri phug gi gzims khang gro bo lung du sku mtshams
dang thugs dam kho na gnang ba ma gtogs grong chog sogs ye mi mdzad/ dgung lo brgyad cu gya gsum pa la thugs dam 'phel po byung gsung ba sogs mnyes mnyes mdzad nas
sku gshegs/ lo rgyus 'di ni mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub kyi gsung ngo / /ku sA li ba rgyal mtshan bzang po de ni mtshan yongs grags rtse chen dbon po bzhes 'byung
bas 'khrungs rtse chen phyogs nas yin nam snyam/ khong rang gi chos gsan tho phyag brig ma zhig bdag gi mthong ba na/ rang lo so gsum pa me mo bya'i lo/ bla ma dam
pa dpal ldan chos bzang gi drung du/ dus 'khor gyi dbang zhus bya ba 'dug pas bdag gis de nas yar ldog ste rtsis pas shing mo glang la 'khrungs par shes/ rdo rje 'chang dbang
phyug rab brtan las kyas lo brgyad kyi gzhon pa gcig yin pa 'dug /byang gling rje gtso bor gyur pas/ bla ma dpal ldan chos bza'/ sku zhang nam mkha' chos ldan/ sku zhang
chos rje dge slong pa/ 'brug pa padma dkar po/ bstan 'dzin nyi zla bzang po sogs la chos mang ba gsan tshul yod pa mthong / gzhan

yang ri phug dang zab mo brag tu'ang phebs nas bla ma ka bzhi ka bzhi pa zer ba'i grong yar klungs na yod pas 'i mi mi ngor 'khrungs pa'i bla ma ka bzhi par gragsnas sde pa
tshul khrims 'gyur med la chos gsan tshul ka bzhi nas rang gi rnam thar na 'khod 'dug /de 'ang nyid kyi mdzad pa'i rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa'i lam rim smon lam las/ la lar
dri med chu ni phun tshogs shing / /ljon shing sna tshogs me tog 'bras bus brgyan/ /dben zhing nyams dga'i dgon gnas ri phug tu/ /mtshan bcas mtshan med ting 'dzin sgom par
shog /ces gsungs pa ltar ri phug gi dung dkar spre'u'i bsam gtan khang bur sku mtshams bcad nas thugs dam kho na mdzad par grags/ rjes su ri phug byang gling gi gdan sa
yang mdzad cing / rdor dbyings mi 'khrugs pa/ bde mchog lI hi pa sogs kyi bla brgyud gsol 'debs lam rim smon lam dang bcas pa re/ chos rje bsod nams dpal 'byor/ mkhan chen
nam mkha' chos ldan sku zhang chos rje dge slong ba sogs la bstod pa legs pa le tshan re/ dus 'khor gyi zhi ba'i sbyin bsregs/ rgyas pa'i sbyin bsregs/ dbang gong ma'i
lhan thabs dang bcas pa'i gsung rtsom bdag gi mthong ba ni de tsam zhig te gzhan yang yod 'gro snyam/ slob ma'i gtso bo bla chen dge 'dun dpal bzang dang / bla ma bsam
'grub rgyal mtshan gnyis kyis yo ga'i dbyangs yig sogs mdzad/ rje btsun dam pa jo nang sprul pa'i sku tA ra na thas kyang

rje 'di la gsang 'dus 'phags skor gyi dbang chos gsan rgyu'i gsol 'debs dang rje su rim pas yongs 'dzin du bsten rtsis mdzad rung / nyid kyi dwang len ma mdzad pas thugs ma
rangs te rang gi rnam thar las/ rten 'brel 'grig na khong pa rang la sku tshe dang 'gro don legs po yong ba yod na'ang / ye mi mdzad gsungs nas rten 'brel ma 'grig /phyis
khong pa sgom mdzad pa'i rjes kyang med/ chos bshad pa'i rjes kyang med pa la dus 'das so/ zhes gshags gtong ba 'dug /lar rje btsun dam pa bar dor sangs rgyas kyi sku thob
zin pa zhig la dgongs dag zhu ba las ni 'os ci yod/ gzhan du na/ chos zhu zer nas gsol ba 'debs su 'gro dgos pa zhig dang / mjug tu ngan smras kyis kha gtong ba gnyis
chos min mtshungs pas gcig bzhag na mdzes so/ /rin po che dkon mchog rgyal mtshan ni/ /'khrungs yal dge 'khor ba yin/ ri phug gi grwa pa mdzad nas rje byang gling pa sogs
bla ma mang du bsten/ rjes su rgyal rtse rin sdings pa'i bla ma thogs shig mdzad/ de nas zhwa lu grang chen pa'i gdan sar bzhugs/ de rting dkar po grwa tshang pa'i bla
ma yang mdzad gsung / 'chad nyan rgya cher gnang nas bstan pa la phan pa chen po mdzad pa zhig te/ bstod pa las/ rin chen bye bar spungs kyang gzhal du dka'i/ /ches dgon
smin grol mchog gi bsam 'phel dbang / /bshad dang bsgrub pa'i rgyal mtshan rtse mo ru/ /bkod mdzes 'dren pa mchog der gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes 'byur ba ltar

ro / rje byang gling pa yab sras kyi skabs so/ | /gsum pa ni/ rigs kun khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan rje/ /zhes 'byung bas rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan bstan pa'i
rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ni/ yab 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi sku mched 'a zha'i gdung brgyud zhabs drung brtan pa'i drung dang / yum bsod nams 'bo le gnyis
kyi sras su rab byung dgu pa'i sa pho rta'i lo/ rgyal gyi zla ba'i tshes gsum la nyug bkra shis rgyal gyi pho brang du sku bltams/ de dus tshar chen dang mkhyen brtse
gnyis zhwa lu'i gdan sar bzhugs skabs yin gshis/ zhag bdun nas tshar chen phebs te/ mtshan nam mkha' don grub dbang po zhes gsol/ der tshar chen gyi 'od gsal la khye'u
'di ni 'khrul zhig rin po che'i skye ba yin no zer ba'i lung bstan tshar gsum byung / 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du smin byed kyi thog ma'ang stsal/
gsang mtshan dri ba mdzad pas/ gos dkar mo zhes zhal nor te gsungs pas/ tshar chen rin po ches/ he he zhang po drung pa rlung log pa 'dra gsung / thams cad bzhad mo shin
tu bro ba zhig byung zhing mnyes mnyes mdzad/ dgung lo gnyis tsam na mgon lag mang po la nad byung bar gzhan gyis thabs ni byas kyang ma phan/ gzhon nu bu rdzi'i rgyab
tu 'khur nas phyag nas gtor bas lug nad chad/ dpal sbug ri khrod 'debs pa'i che brag bshags pas rmo rmos bros

bros gsung yang brag la sdigs mdzub gtad de phaT gsungs pas rba gyen la ldog pa sogs byung / dgung lo bdun brgyad tsam la tshe sgrub bu ston gong khug ma'i sgrab pa zhag bdun
pa zhig kyang mdzad/ rje mkhyen brtse'i drung du dus 'khor sku gsung thugs yongs su rdzogs pa'i dbang gson pa'i thugs rgyud la ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo du ma 'khrungs/ sku
gzhon nu nas rab tu 'byung bar bzhed kyang yab yum gyis gsung nan ches pas dgung lo so gcig tshun dge bsnyen rdo rje 'dzin pa'i brtul zhugs kyis sde ba rin spungs pa'i
drung 'khor mdzad/ phag ri rdzong dpon gyi las khur bzhes pa'i dus gtsang rong gnyis 'khrugs nas sde pa gtsang pa'i dmag gis phag ri rdzong 'phrog tu byung ba la/ rin spungs
dpon g.yog gi dam tshig bsrung te rje nyid nas sna len tsam yang ma gnang mod/ phyag sbrel gyi rdzong dpon pa rnam rdzong shar bas sde pa gtsang pa dang nang cha rul
rkyen gyis rdzong gtsang la rtsis sprad nas kho rang yang mgo btad zhus/ rje nyid la 'dzin bzung sprad nas btson dong du bzhugs dgos pa'i 'o rgyal chen pos zos shing / de
dag gi tshe yang gsol ba'i phud la brten nas chos skyong rnams kyi gtor bsngo sogs thugs dam chags med mdzad/ de nas sger gzhis nas gser dngul sogs nor mang po sde pa gtsang
la phul te dgongs pa 'khrol cha zhus nas rang gnas su phyir phebs chog pa byung pas/ dgung lo so gcig pa sa pho byi ba'i lo la thub bstan man chen byams pa rab

brtan gyi drung du tshigs snga ma dge tshul gyi sdom pa bzhes/ mtshan dbang phyug rab brtan zhes gsol/ de nas yun mi ring bar mkhan po de nyid dang bskong dge slong grangs
tshang ba'i dbus su bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/ ri phug tu thugs gnyer gyi 'phro 'ga' zhig gnang nas rtse gdong che na kun dga' bsod nams gyi phyag phyi mdzad de dbus su phebs/
nA lendrar mkhan tshab mdzad nas chos 'khor bskor zhing gnas de nyid du rje btsun nA ro mkha' spyod ma zhal gzigs pa sogs byung / lha sar zhabs skor mdzad pas rdo rje sems
dpa'i sku shail ltar dwangs pa khru gang tsam zhig dbu gtsug tu yod pa'i snang ba shar zhing gzhan yang gnas rten khyad par can rnams mjal ba'i tshe ngo mtshar ba'i gzigs
snang dang byin gyi brlabs pa'i rtags snang bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung / snga phyir tshar chen yab sras/ mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang bsod nams chos
'phel/ 'phags mchog byams pa skal bzang / byang gling rje rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan rnams bka' drin che ba'i bla mar mdzad la gzhan yang dge ba'i bshes gnyen shin
tu mang ba bsten nas dbang khrid man ngag gi bka' mang po gsan te thugs su chud par mdzad do/ khyad par sngar rab tu ma byung ba'i gong du mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal
mtshan la gsung ngag slob bshad gsan dus kyi rdor gyi rgyu dbang gi tshe tshar chen yab sras gnyis kyang dkyil 'khor gyi thad

ka'i nam mkha' la bzhugs nas dbang gnang ba byung ste mkhan chen bslab gsum pa chen po'i zhal nas khong yab sras gnyis kyang dbang gnang gin 'dug /de 'dra'i dga' ba la ang
gsung de'i skabs shig rje bslab gsum rgyal mtshan la/ glang phu nas kyi sde pa mchen tshe don gyi gur zhal gnyis kyi chos skor zhus pas/ ngas chos 'chad mi thub pa rnams
dbon rin po che la zhus shig ces bka' gnang bas/ sde pa'i blo la dbon rin po che sku rten skya bo 'di 'dras gsung chos gnang ba ga la 'ong snyam pa byung / rjes sku chos
gang 'dod zhus chog pa byung ngas mngon mkhyen yin 'dug ces dad pa byung skad/ de nas nub chos lung du kyai rdor gyi bsnyen chen mdzad pas zhal dngos su gzigs shing ri phug
tu bzhugs dus mnal lam du A tsa rya gzi brjid can rgya dang sma ra dkar po gos chen gser ma dkar ser dmar ljang gi ber gyon pa/ mgo la rgya nag gi thag zhwa nag po can/
lag na man hu dang g.yang Ti'u'i spos phor bzungs te gdan 'dren zhu ba'i tshul du gyur pas/ ci yin nam dgongs pa na/ yar klungs bkra shis chos sde'i gdan sar phebs dgos
pa'i snyan zhu 'bul mkhan slebs te de la blta ba 'dug gsung / dgung lo zhe gsum pa lcags pho byi ba'i lo la dbus su phebs nas lag zla ba'i tshes bcu bdun gyi nyin bkra shis
chos sde'i khri la mnga' gsol/ der 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma dang tshe chog sogs kyi sgrub mchod gsar 'dzugs dang gsung ngag bla brgyud kyi 'phros lus sogs rten bzhengs
'ga' yang mdzad de ri phug tu phebs pas phebs nas dgung lo zhe lnga pa chu mo yos kyi lo ri phug byang gling gi gdan sa phebs te chos 'khor bskor/ 'di dang bkra shis chos
rje nyis 'dzin mdzad/ ri phug lo gsum tsam song ba dang bkra shis chos sder

zhwa lu pa'i ban smyon 'gar zhig gis mi bsrun pa'i rgyu 'grul sna tshogs byas te bla ma ka bzhi pa tshul khrims 'gyur med ngo chen la sbran nas ri phug gi gdan sar dpon chen
rgyal mtshan bzang po bskos chog pa sde pa gtsang la zhus nas byung gda' bas rje nyid kyi thugs la ni/ ji skad du spyod 'jug las/ nags na ri dwags bya rnams dang / /shing
rnams mi snyan brjod mi byed/ /'grogs na bde ba de dag dang / /nam zhig lhan cig bdag gnas 'gyur/ /ces pa'i don dus la bab po snyam pa 'khrungs to/ dbus phyogs su rgyun
ring ba bzhugs/ de'ang yar klungs shel brag sogs su sgrub pa mdzad pas thugs dam gyi lha tshogs dpag tu med pa zhal gzigs/ thugs rgyud la nyams rtogs khyad par can 'khrungs
shing slar bkra shis chos sder gsung ngag slob bshad zab mo'i chos 'khor yang bskor/ dgung lo lnga bcu nga dgu pa la bkra shis chos sde'i gdan sa rje btsun dpon mgon
po bsod nams mchog ldan la btad de slar yang dpal zhwa lu ri phug tu phebs nas thugs dam sgrub pa gtso bor mdzad cing mchog dman gyi gdul bya mang por gang la gang mtshams
kyi chos bstan nas smin grol la bkod/ dgung lo drug cu re gsum pa la ri phug byang gling gi khri la bskyar ma phebs nas bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i bstan pa dar bar
mdzad/ drug cu re lnga pa la 'dar stod bla ma'i gdan sa grang mo che'i seng khri la phebs nas gsang chen slob bshad kyi chos 'khor

bskor / rgyun gyi thugs dam spros bcas rim pa la tho rangs mnal sad 'phral ngag byin rlabs/ sengge sgra'i mngon rtogs bzlas pa sum brgya/ thugs rje chen po mig 'byed/ rnam
'joms gsang sgrub kyi bzlas pa nyer gcig tsam/ 'jam nag bzlas pa/ de nas rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi dra ma'i rnal 'byor sngon du btang ba'i bskyed rdzogs kyi rnal 'byor/ rdor
bzlas brgya re/ sngags gsum pa brgya rtsa la nyung mtha' byas pa'i gang 'gro/ bir srung gnyis sbrel/ dpal kyai rdo rje'i lam dus 'bring pa/ tshe sgrub lcags sdong ma'i bzlas
ba brgya rtsa/ dkar cha bzhi'i gtor za sogs/ khro bo rme brtsegs/ khro mo rme brtsegs/ snying ma'i khro bo rme brtsegs/ ni gu'i sgom thun/ rnam 'joms ljang sngon/ gu
ru zhi ba/ gu ru dmar chen/ mthong kha drag dmar/ padma tshe dbang rtsal/ rta mgrin tshe sgrub nye brgyud/ ye shes 'od mchog rdzong chen ma/ 'khor ba dong sgrug /bka' brgyad
dril sgrub/ 'joms byed phur pa spu gri/ thab thig gi rta mgrin tshe sgrub/ phyag rdor/ stobs po che/ de nas bzang spyod sngon du 'gro ba'i sems bskyed rgyas bsdus gang
rung re len/ a ra pa tsa na/ 'byung 'dul/ u tsa ra gos sngon can/ gtum po/ rta mgrin gsang sgrub/ 'gro ba kun sgrol gyi gzugangs gang mang dang bcas pa/ bla ma yab sras
kyi sku bstod rnams sngon du 'gro ba'i rab yangs ma brgya rtsa la nyung mtha' byas pa'i gang 'gro sogs sam zab sngon du 'gro ba'i lam dus rgyas pa bzlas pa dang bcas pa/
'jigs byed bcu gsum ma'i bzlas pa yud tsam re/ rdo rje

rnal 'byor ma'i 'khrid bzlas dang bcas pa/ rta mgrin yang gsang dpa' gcig /mkha' 'gro chos skyong rnams la gtor bsngo thun gnyis re/ brag rdzong mgur gyi gsang khrid/ zhal
gyi srung 'khor tshe sgrub/ zhal gyi gsang 'khrid/ pir srung sogs rgyas par mdzad nas nyal ba'i rnal 'byor gyi rim pa sngon du mdzad do/ /de yang rje 'di nyid sngon grub
chen ku ku ri pa sogs mkhas grub du mar sku skye ba bAzhes nas lam gyi rtogs pa mthar phyin pa zhig yin mod kyi/ dus 'dir ma dag pa'i gdul bya'i blo ngor tha mal pa'i tshul
bzung ba'i rnam thar yang bsam gyis mi khyab ste gsar rnying gi chos bka' thams cad la ma rtogs pa dang log par rtog pa'i dri mas dben zhing 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi
mdzad pa gang la yang thugs zab cing brling ba dang / sku rten skye bo'i dus nas tshangs par spyod pa dge sbyong gi brtul zhugs 'ba' zhig lhur len na phyis rab tu byung
nas tshul khrims rnam par dag pa sogs lta ci smos/ bdag gzhan brje ba'i byang chub kyi sems thegs rgyud la ji lta ba bzhin du 'khrungs pas gnod byed dag la yang gnod lan
phan pas sgrub pa 'ba' zhig mdzad de/ dper bgyis/ 'dar du bzhugs skabs/ kong po dung mtsho ba'i gnyer pa dang / nyid kyi phyag g.yog rta rdzi zhig yod pa 'khrug pa shor/
rta rdzis dung mtsho ba'i lag rdo zhig la gnyes la btang nas bsad par/ ston la spu nag thams cad sprod pa sogs nyid kyi

thugs bsun chen pos nyes pa bsgrubs pa gnang mod na'ang dung ma tshobs gri mdung khyer te gzims chung du 'tshangs pa sogs mi 'tshams pa mang du byas kyang thugs khro ba sogs
mi mdzad/ khong rang tshos mi 'tshams pa'i byad byas par brten chos srung thugs khros nas mar lam rta drel la shi go da mi shis ba sna tshogs byung / der mo ma 'dre mthong
byed pa gcig la mo btab par/ 'dar grang mo chen nas yin zer/ lcags kyi a tsa ra gnyis gnod pa byed cing 'dug go byas pas/ kho gnong la phog nas shin tu bred/ g.yo thabs
kyis 'dar dang bkra shis chos sder mang ja btang/ ma smin pa'i khog nas bshags pa byas rung / skor theng de ga rang la nga 'dar grang mo che nas 'bod mkhan byung zer lam
chal chol byed bzhin du smyo nas shi de'i gnas tshul gsan ma thag kho snying re rje gsung thugs khrel chen po mdzad cing kho'i sgrib sbyong 'ba' zhig mdzad pa lta bu'o/
/phyis kyi bla rul khag cig ni/ mi 'dod pa'i rkyen phran bu re la chos skyong gi bskul dang drag gtor 'phen pa sogs byed/ de la rtags dang nus pa gang yang ma mchis bzhin
du pha rol po der/ sngon las dang 'phral rkyen ci rigs pas rkyen ngan byung pa la/ nged kyi chos skyong gi mthu yin zer nas dga' ba sgom pa sogs don du rang gi sdom gsum
yun las 'bud pa dag la bltas nam bcol bzhin du chos skyong rang gis las byas pa de 'drar yang mi dgyes pa'i rnam pa mdzad pa ni ngo mtshar pa'i rnam thar zhig go /dgung

lo bdun cu don gnyis pa sa sbrul lo/ rje btsun dpon mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan dang / rje zhwa lu ba sogs la dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i bdag po chen po'i bar gyi dbang rdzogs
par sku mnyel bzhin pa zhig gi ngang nas gnang pas/ de nub gzigs snang du byang gling 'jam pa'i dbyangs rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan shin tu dgyes pa'i nyams dang bcas
zhal bstan/ skye bdun ril bu sgrub pa gnang ba'i tshe nub phyogs nas 'ja' kha dog sna lnga ba zhig sgrub khang gi steng du zug yong ba dang / gzims khang gi nang thams
cad du shin tu zhim pa'i dri bzang pos khyab pa dang me tog gi char lag pas 'dzin nus pa bab cing bum pa'i steng na spyan ras gzigs kyi sku bzhugs pa thun gyi sgang la bum
pa'i nang du thim song ba bu mo rtsa sgo yangs pa zhig gis dngos su mthong ba byung ste de'ang las dag pa zhig yin gda'/ lan cig thugs la da ni na so rgas pas dkyil 'khor
chen po'i rim gnyis kyi rnal 'byor sogs spros bcas rnams dor te lam zab mo ayon sgrub pa zhig la chig sgril bya'o dgongs pa na/ mnal lam du thugs dam gyi lha dpal kyai
rdo rje'i thugs kar ayon rin po che bzhugs pa zhig byung pas sngar gyi thugs 'dun de mi legs par mkhyen nas lha'i rnal 'byor sogs sku gshegs ka tshun chad la chag med mdzad/
de nas sku gcong gi rnam pa dang spyan gyis mi gzigs pa'i tshul bstan par lan cig yar klungs bkra shis chos sde nas 'ongs pa'i grwa gzhon

'phrin las rgya mtsho zer ba zhig yod pa des/ dpon slob chen mo sku sing dwangs byung na ni lags mod/ ma byung tshe dgrongs na 'ongs mchis/ rdo'i dos dang 'dra pa 'dug ces
skur ba btab pa gsan nas/ kho bden/ gzhan don mi nus pa'i lus 'di rdo'i dos rang yin 'dug gsung / dgung lo don drug bzhes pa chu bya lo tshes bcu zhig gi skabs gsung cho
ga rgyas pa dang gsol ja yang bzang zhing mang ba gnang / mjal mkhan byung tshad la bka' bsgo byin rlabs sogs zhus pa lam ltos bar gnang zhing byams pa bstan 'dzin la de
ring tshe bcu'i cho ga blo kha rdzogs pa rang byung / srod thun gyi gong du go bo ni rgyab 'gro ba yin no gsung / sa ma srib tsam la sku gshegs grab byung bas rtab rtab por
rje btsun dpon rin po che phebs nas gsol ba btab pas/ snga ma zhal gyis ma bzhes/ de nas yang gsol pa phur tshugs su btab pas/ da 'o na de 'dra rang gnang ci dgos thugs
dang bstun nas sdod pa lags gsung / de nas lo ril po gsum tsam gyi bar bzhugs nas bstan 'gro'i don rgya cher mdzad de mthar dgung lo bdun cu don dgu pa me pho byi ba'i
lo/ smin drug zla ba'i tshes bcu gnyis kyi nyi ma nub mtshams su zhing gshegs so/ /de'i tshe yang dpon rin po ches gsung shed drag pos bzhugs par gsol ba btab pas/ sngar
phyed la bsam nas lo de tsam zhig bsdad pa yin/ da cha de 'dra gnang gzhan drag ces bka' stsal/ gdung sbyangs pas tshems la dung dkar g.yas 'khyil kha sprod dang ring bsrel
tshan che ba byon zhing gzims mal sku

'dra sogs yar klungs bkra shis chos sder bzhengs so/ /gsung las 'khrungs pa'i dngos slob mtha' yas kyang bka' babs kyi bu chen gsum ni/ slob bshad bka' babs che ba dpon rin
po che mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ bu lugs la bka' babs che ba khyab bdag zhwa lu pa rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ rnying ma la bka' babs che ba glang bu nas 'jam dbyangs
chos skyong dbang phyug go /rje 'di'i rnam thar rgyal mchog lnga pas mdzad pa dang / de nyid gang las byung ba'i rtsa ba dpon rin po che mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan
gyi zin tho'i yi ge sogs bdag gi mthong la/ de dag na mi gsal ba'i ri phug tu 'jigs byed zhal gzigs byung tshul sogs gsang rnam gyi zin bris thor bu yod 'dug pa ma rnyed
do/ / | gsol 'debs las/ 'khrul sangs yo gar blo rgyas tshe yi dpal/ /shAkya'i bstan 'dzin zla med seng ge bzhin/ /rin chen chos kyi rgya mtsho rlabs 'phreng g.yo/ /mtshungs
med dam pa gsum la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes so/ / | dang po ni/ 'khrul sangs yo gar byo rgyas tshe yi dpal/ /zhes byung bas/ mkhas grub rin chen sangs rgyas cha dpal ni/
/byang gling rje rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan gyi slob ma'i gtso bor gyur/ rgyud sde spyi dang khyad par yo ga rnal 'byor rgyud la gzhan dring mi 'jog pa'i rnam dpyod
kyi mkhyen rab mchog tu yangs/ 'brog gi mi brgyud ku sA li pa rgyal mtshan bzang po'i dpon yin pas 'brog khang par yang gragsri phug gi 'brog khang du sgrub pa rgyun ring
mdzad/ de rjes dpal 'khor chos sder

rin sding grwa tshang gi gdan sa bskyangs shing gzhan phan 'phrin las shin tu che/ sku che ba'i yon tan slob dpon kun dga' snying po'i rnam 'phrul du grags so/ /slob ma'i gtso
bo mkhan po sku zhang nam mkha' chos ldan/ dbang ldan chos 'khor ba mkhas mchog bstan pa'i sgron me sogs mang du byung ngo / gnyis pa ni/ shAkya'i bstan 'dzin zla med
sengge bzhin/ /zhes grub dbang shAkya sengge ni/ 'khrungs zhwa lu ba yin/ tshar chen yab sras/ sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel sogs bla ma mang du bsten/ zhwa lu grang
chen grwa tshang gi rdo rje slob dpon mdzad/ sku tshe'i mjug la ri phug kho nar bzhugs shing / nags rin lugs kyi dus 'khor sbyor drug la thugs dam nyams len mdzad pas myong
rtags bsam gyis mi khyab pa thugs rgyud la 'khrungs/ dgung lo shin tu smin pa bzhugs so/ /slob ma'i gtso bo lha bo pa bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen rin chen bsod
nams mchog grub sogs byung ngo / / | gsum pa ni/ rin chen chos kyi rgya mtsho rlabs phreng g.yo/ /zhes rje btsun lha bo pa rin chen rgya mtsho dpal bzang po ni/ 'khrungs
yul rgyal mkhar spel bzhir 'khrungs pa yin gda'/ rgyal rtse lha bo grwa tshang gi rtsa grwa yin/ rjes su ri phug byangagling gi gdan sa mdzad nas chos 'khor bskor/ byang
gling pa rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan chos bzang / grong gsar lo tsA ba blo gros dpal bzang / chos rje rdo rje bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug
rab brtan/ sku zhang nam mkha'

chos ldan sogs bla ma mang du bsten nas rgyud sde bzhi la mkhas par sbyangs/ brgyud 'dzin slob ma mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ lha bo pa bkra shis rgya mtsho/
chen po chos dbang rgyal mtshan sogs mang du byung la/ sa pho 'brug gi lo rgyal mkhar spel bzhir sku gshegs/ gsol 'debs las/ 'jam mgon bsod nams mchog ldan rdo rjes mas/
/khyab bdag rin chen bsod nams mchog tu grub/ /phyogs 'dir lhag bsam ches dkar dam chos kyi/ /bka' drin stsol mdzad gnyis la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes 'byung bas/ dang po rje
btsun bka' 'gyur ba mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan de ni/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i sprul par yang grags la/ 'di nyid kyi yab ni gnas gsar pa'i gdung brgyud rdo rje 'chang
dbang phyug rab brtan gyi sku'i gcung po 'a zhe nam mkha' mgon pa dang / yam tshe dbang bsod nams dpal mo bya ba gnyis kyi sras su gyur te/ de yang lhums su bzhugs pa'i
tshe yum la rdol 'joms zer ba'i zhing steng nas dung dkar g.yas 'khyil rnyed pa dang / brag ri mthon po'i rtser 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug phyag na bum pa
bsnams te bzhugs pa'i brag rtsa na yum nyid 'khor bar spyi gtsug tu bum chu skye nor gyis blug pa sogs rmi ltas ngo mtshar ba mang du byung ngo / /lhag par sngar dang mi
'dra ba yum nyid la nges 'byung dang / byams snying rje'i thugs dam khyad par can thugs rgyud

la rang shar du byung ste/ de lta bu'i tshul ka mad sum cur spel nas yum gyis rtsom pa yang bgyis so/ /mngal gyi zla grangs thim nas rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i chu mo yos bu'i
lo/ hor zla bcu gcig pa stag gi zla ba'i dmar tshes dge bar gnubs khu lu pa gzhis kar mtshan ltas bzang po da bcas te sku 'khrungs/ gsung ma bye gong yum gyi bang bar khyer
te sku ngos gzhan gyi gral 'gor 'dug pa na gsung mi tser la/ gral 'gab tu 'phos pa na gsung tsa ra ba sogs mi dgyes pa'i tshul mdzad pas/ rmo mos 'di gral mjug tu bzhugs
'dod pa mi gda'/ gral 'go rang du bzhugs chug gcig zer ro/ dgung lo gnyis tsam la rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan phebs nas tshe dbang gnang ba rjes su 'ung thugs
dran bsod kyin yod 'dug /gsung sgo dbye tsa ma nas nga'i ming la btsun chung tshul khrims zer ba yin no gsung pa dang / sku rtse da kyang dgon pa 'debs pa dang chos 'chad
pa sogs kyi lad mo kho na mdzad/ dgung lo bdun la mchod gnas chen po zhwa lu ri phug 'di nyid du phebs/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan gyi drung du dbu phud phul/
mtshan mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan zhes gsol te lo 'phros 'khrungs yul du thegs/ dgung lo brgyad la slar yang ri phug tu phebs nas rdo rje 'chang dbang rab pa nyid kyis
mkhan po mdzad nas dge tshul gyi sdom pa yang dag pa bzhes/ de gong rje dbang rab pa'i mtshan lam du chos skyong yid bzhin nor bu'i pha nya des rgya spos dri

zhim po'i chun po zhig khyer te byung pas nyin par nyid rab byung sgrub par byon pas tshul khrims gtsang ba zhig 'ong ba 'dug gsungs nas mnyes mnyes mdzad/ de nas rje rdo rje
'chang dbang rab pa'i phyag phyir bzhugs te rim gyis thugs gnyer gsan sbyong rnams la 'grus par mdzad/ dgung lo bco lnga pa la yar klungs bkra shis chos sde'i gdan sar
rje dbang rab pa nyid kyis rgyal tshab tu bkod/ der bla ma'i mdzad sgo mtha' dge tshul bzhin du bsgrubs pas sku na phra mo la 'di 'dra 'ong ba zhes kun yid 'phrog cing dad
par gyur/ dgung lo nyi shu pa la rje sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub gyis mkhan po mdzad/ brang ti nam mkha' sangs rgyas kyis las slob dang / shar pa shes rab 'byung
gnas kyis gsang ste ston pa mdzad cing / dad pa'i dge 'dun grangs tshang ba'i dbus su bkra shis kyi gtsug lag khang dpal e waM chos ldan du bsnyen par rdzogs/ mkhan slob
de gsum las snga phyir chos bka' shin tu mang ba gsan/ rje dbang rab pa'i drung du/ lam 'bras slob bshad kyis mtshon pa'i dpal ldan sa skya ba'i chos skor/ dpal dus kyi
'khor lo sogs bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i chos skor/ gzhan yang gsang sngags gsar rnying gi chos bka' rje nyid la mnga' ba phal mo che bum pa gang byo'i tshul du gsan/
dgung lo nyi shu rtsa bdun pa la 2dar grang mo che'i gdan sa yang gtad de der bla ma'i zhabs tog dang chos gsan pa sogs la 'brom ston rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas kyi

rnam thar dang 'dra ba mdzad/ rje dbang rab pa yang lo snga ma dag la sku gshegs grabs char kha yar byung yang rje nyid nas gdung shugs drag pos gsol ba btab pas sku na shin
tu smin pa'i par bzhugs/ paN chen ngag dbang chos grags la yang rdo rje 'phreng ba sogs chos bka' du ma gsan/ dgung lo so bzhi pa la rje dbang rab pa zhing brjes nas kha'u
brag rdzong dang sa ngor zhwa lu sogs su dgongs rdzogs rgya chen po bskubs te yar klungs su byon/ bkra shis chos sder lam zab bla ma lha khang gsar bzhengs dang / dpal
dus kyi 'khor lo sogs dkyil 'khor mang po zhal phye nas sgrub mchod mdzad pa'i srol rgyud da lta'ang yod par grags/ gong dkar rdo rje gdan du sku mtshams mdzad nas dam
bca'i yi ge mdzad pa'i snying po 'di ltar/ da cha rang lo so brgyad pa 'brug lo zla ba dang po nas bzung ji srid 'tsho'i bar tshe 'di'i bde skyid snyan grags ched du mi bsgrub
pa dang / zas ster mi byung na 'phyol nyog tu ma song bar longs spyod/ ma byung na bcud len la sogs pa'i ngan ngon sa brten/ gos ster mi byung na gyon/ ma byung na'ang
chos gos rnam gsum ngan snyigs dang gtum mo la brten par byed/ chos bka' gter mdo sngags rnam dag zhu sa gang na yod kyang zhu/ khyad par khe dang rgyal kha gzhan la
bskur zhing gyong rang nyid kyis len pa gang yong yong byed/ lhag par lha'i bsnyen pa rigs mi gcig pa brgya phrag byed/ rtags dang mtshan ma yong re med kyang grangs bsnyen/
dus bsnyen/ gtso 'bum/ 'khor khrir logs pa brgya phrag gcig

co zhe dgu tshun la grub par bgyi/ de nas kyang ma shi na ci 'grub byed/ de dag gi khas len dang dam bca' la rta ri ba dang mnyams len lag thog yod pa la khyi mi ri ba byung
gi dogs 'dug pas yang yang zhus dag byed/ grub na khengs rloms spangs te chos chos su song ba byed/ de dag 'grub ma 'grub blta phyir yi ge bris pa yin zhes bya ba mdzad
nas rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur rin po che'i lung rgyun phyogs gang dang gang na yod ces 'tshol ba gnang pas/ kong po phyogs na gter ston 'ja' tshon snying po la yod 'dra zer
ba gsan nas kong por phebs/ dwags la sgam po'i phu gnyal lam rgyab tsan na chu chen pos lam bcad nas mi thar ba 'dug pa la bya rogs gcig gis sna drangs nas 'khyags zam zhig
rnyed/ der byon nas pha rir slebs pa dang 'khyags zam bsdibs/ jag pa 'ga' res rjes bsnyegs kyang chu lam thar ba mig hur re lus skad/ gter ston pas kyang mngon shes kyis
rig nas mi zhig phebs bsur brdzangs/ khos yongs nas phyag btsal mjal dar phul/ spos sna byas te gdan drangs/ khyed slob dpon la nga yong ba sus zhus gsungs pas/ skad cha
mi dgos khong rang gis shos yongs zer skad/ gter ston dang mjal nas khong la bka' 'gyur gyi lung tshad thub ni bzhugs yod tshad kyang min pa 'dug/ gter ston khong rang
gi phyag mdzub g.yas g.yon rtsa sprod mdzad nas ngu cag gnyis 'di ga byung ba ka bka'

'gyur gyi lung yin mod gsung / gter gsar dkon mchog spyi 'dus sogs chos bka' ci rigs pa gnang / phar yang sa lugs kyi chos 'ga' zhig phul te rim gyis dgung lo zhe gnyis pa
shing pho spre'u'i lo gtsang ljongs su chibs bskyod/ gdan sa chen po zhwa lu ri phug gi gzims khang rnam grol yang rtser lo gsum gyi sku mtshams bcad rgyar shin tu dam pa
la bzhugs/ sngar gnang ba'i dam bca'i lha grangs kyi ljags bsnyen rnams legs par grub pa mdzad/ de grol ba dang mnyam du sde pa bkra shis rtse bas gdan drangs pa bzhin dbus
su phebs nas bya dka' ba du mas bka' 'gyur yongs rdzogs kyi lung rgyun khungs ma chol mdzad cing de yang mdo mang gi lung rgyun shin tu dkon zhing lho brag ngos su bla
ma tshogs gnyis dpal grub la yod par gsan te sman lung khra tshangs pa'i zhabs drung blo mchog rdo rje zhu bar rdzong brda mdzad nas phyis lung tshang ma gsan thub pa dang
gong dkar chos sder slob ma mang por ljags lung gnas bas deng sang bod dang bod chen po'i rgyal khams thams cad du rgyal ba'i bka' dngos kyi lung rgyun mnyams pa yod
pa ni 'di nyid kho na'i bka' drin yin/ de nas zur chos dbyings rang grol la thog mar tshar lugs kyi chos bka' 'bul ba dang / de rjes 'bras spungs su phebs te/ rgyal ba lnga
pa chen po dang mjal zhing rim gyis dbu slar bzhes nas pho brang chen po po ta lar gsung ngag slob bshad dang rdo rje 'phreng ba sogs dbang chos bsam gyis mi khyab pa
'bul ba

mdzad / rgyal dbang rin po ches rje 'di nyid nas brgyud pa'i 'phreng ba'i dbang rnams chos grwa chen po 'bras spungs tshogs chen la gnang bas chos kyi 'phrin las je rgyas su
gyur/ snga phyir chos gsan pa'i bla ma mtha' yas kyang bka' rin che ba'i bla ma rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ rje sgrub khang pa chen po/ paN chen ngag dbang chos
grags/ rngog ston 'jam dbyangs 'od zer sogs yin no/ da ltar sku tshe'i ston smad thams cad du thos bsam sgom gsum dang gzhan don chos 'chad pa kho nas dus 'da' ba mdzad
la/ yar klungs bkra shis chos sde sogs su bka' 'gyur gyis mtshon pa'i gsung rab glegs bam cha tshang ba mang po dang gzhan yang sku gsung thugs rten gyi bye brag du ma
gsar du bzhengs/ bskyed rdzogs kyi ting nge 'dzin bzang po thugs rgyud la rgyun chad med par gnas shing / thugs dam gyi lha tshogs rab tu mang pos dngos dang nyams ci rigs
par zhal bstan nas byin gyis brlabs/ chos skyong rnams bran du 'khol ba'i rtags su rgyun gyis thugs dam bskang gso sogs mdzad pa'i tshe yang sha bsregs pa'i bsur dud kyis
gzims chung nang / khengs yod pa dang / drung du 'khod pa rnams kyi snang yul du gzugs mthong rgyu med pa'i nya ba sha dang / sha be sho be'i skad cha dir dir byed pa/
rten thugs rnams las me 'bar/ de'i nang nas sgra sgrog pa dang khrag 'dzag pa sogs cho 'phrul

du ma kun gyi mthun snang du grub pa la yang byung ngo / /dgung lo lnga bcu nga bdun pa sa mo phag gi hor zla dang po'i nang 'bras spungs su phebs nas rgyal dbang rin po cher
bka' chos mang po 'bul bar bzhed kyang gnas chung chos skyong gi da lam 'then pa lags tshul zhus par brten bka' chos shol te rgyal dbang rin po cher yang zhal chems lta
bu'i gsung bgros kyis zhu ba mang du mdzad cing lhag par sman sgom 'brang rgyas pas bstan 'gro'i dpal du thugs sna ma sdud par yun ring por zhabs pad brtan dgos pa'i gsol
ba btab pa na/ da cha rgyun ring sdod pa mi 'char/ zangs mdog dpal ayon chen po'i g.yas g.yon du bzhugs khri rim par bshams 'dug pa la rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po nas
rdo rje 'chang dbang rab pa'i bar gyi kha'u brag rdzong pa'i bla brgyud rnams bzhugs pa'i mthar khri stong pa zhig gda' bas de nged kyi yin pa 'dug /khyed rang lan cig
gong dkar du 'bod par shog gsung / de nas gong dkar chos sder sku mtshams kyi mus nas gsan yig bsgrig pa gnang zhing re zhig nas sku cung zad mi bde ba'i rnam pa la sman
sgom 'brang rgyas pa bos nas gsol sman gyi 'phrod bsten gnang bas dwangs tshul bzhes te/ sman sgom 'brang rgyas pa la bka' chos kha shas kyang gnang ba mdzad/ de nas lo de'i
tha skar zla ba'i tshes bcu bzhi'i nub mo nye gnas byams pa la/ sang zhogs snga ja mi dgos pas da dung ja zhim po skol gsung / byams pas sku bsnyun pa sogs med lags

sam / chab skol e dgos zhus pas/ na tsha med par chab skol ga la dgos zhes bzhad mo mdzad/ de nas srod thun gyi mjug la thugs dam 'da' ka ma gsal btab nas hig drag po gcig
gsung pa'i mod la sku gshegs/ de dus bkra shis lhun po'i sngags pa grwa tshang gi sgrigs rgyug pa zhig kyang chos zhu ba'i phyir du 'ong ba kho ba'i rmi lam du/ stan dkar
po kha gdam zhig gi steng du bla ma bzhugs pa'i zur bzhi nas bud med brgyad kyis bzung ste nam mkha' la ye re re bteg nas thag ring bor 'gro gin 'dug pa rmis/ tho rangs
snga mo nas mdangs nga la rmi lam 'di 'dra byung ci yin zhes blo ma bde ba'i rnam pa byed cing 'dug lo/ dgung zhag grol nas gdung yid bzhin gyi nor bu me mchod 'bul bar zhwa
lu mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang rin chen bsod nams mchog grub sde pa gzhung nas spyan 'dren mdzad pa bzhin/ gshed dmar lha lnga'i cho ga'i steng nas bzhugs 'bul mdzad/ gdung
khang zhal phye nas ring bsrel shel ltar 'tsher ba kha yar 'phel zhing nang rten dngul gdung thog tshad ma dang / gzims mal sku 'dra mthong grol yid bzhin nor bu sogs
yar klungs bkra shis chos sder bzhengs so/ / | /gnyis pa ni/ khyab bdag rin chen bsod nams mchog tu grub/ /ces mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub bstan pa'i rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po ni byang gling 'jam pa'i dbyangs rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshanmdzan gyi yang srid

mchog gi sprul pa'i sku yin la/ 'di nyid kyi 'khrungs yul zhwa lu mthil gyi sman khang zhes bar yab 'tsho byed dpon tshang sangs rgyas grags pa dang / yum sprul pa'i DA ki
ma ye shes 'tsho mo zhes bya ba gnyis kyi sras su rab byung bcu pa'i chu pho stag gi lo hor zla bcu gcig pa'i nyi shu gcig rgyu skar rgyal la babs pa'i nyin sku bltams/ de
yang byang gling rje zhi bar gshegs pa'i lo nas rje nyid 'khrungs pa'i bar 'dir lo bcu drug tsam 'gro mod kyi bsam yas chos skyong chen pos rjes su de nyid kyi sprul skur
ngos 'dzin gnang ba yin no/ /de skabs yum sras gnyis ka gshegs su nye ba'i bsnyun gzhi drag pos thebs nas dgon pa nub kyi sngags 'chang gru rig pa 'dzin pa dge bsnyen
gyis bgegs bskrod la sogs pa mang du byas kyang cher ma phan/ nye skor du rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan phebs te rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi byin rlabs gtor dbang dang
/ rje rang nyid kyi dbu skra bubs gcig byin rten sku srung du stsal bas bar chad las grol zhing shin tu bde bar gyur/ dgung lo gnyis tsam gyi dus ri khug tu yum gyi sku
rgyab la bsnams te rje dbang rab pa mjal bar phebs pas/ gzims chung gi thang kha'i lha mgron la phyag mdzub gtad de gang yin zhes bka' 'dri stsal bar/ lha rnams 'khrul
med ngo mkhyen nas 'di dang 'di'o zhes gsungs pas/ rje dbang rang pa'ang shin tu mnyes nas/ bu chung gis 'di 'dra ngo shes pa bgod re bro ya mtshan che ang gsung / sku gzhon
nu

nas chang dang sha mi bzhes shing dmar skyur shor na bsnyun pa zhig kyang byung / byis pa rtsed mo rtse ba'i gnas skabs su'ang rdza brdungs pa'i phye ma dang rtsam pa sogs
kyis dkyil 'khor 'bri ba'i tshul mdzad/ re 'ga' ni rtsel po kha phub pa'i steng du khyel stegs mdzad nas dbyings 'then pa'i lad mo dang dbang bskur ba'i rnam pa'ang mdzad
do/ /dgung lo dgu la ri phug chos kyi pho brang chen por rje dbang rab pa'i drung du gtsug phud phul/ mtshan bsod nams dbang por gsol/ yab de rong byams chen gyi gnyer pa
yin pas rong phyogs su khrid nas 'bras yul skyed tshal du thugs gnyer la brdzangs/ 'bum ram pa chen po thar pa rgyal mtshan gyi drung du kyai rdor gyi dbang bka' sogs chos
mang ba gsan zhing mtshan nyid kyi phyogs su slob sbyong gnang bar bzhed mod/ 'bum ram pa de nyid mtshan mo thugs rig dwangs khyad kyi thog kha'i gyang steng du bzhugs
nas thugs dam gnang ba sku rbab shor ba'i rkyen gyi sku gshegs/ de'i stabs kyis mtshan nyid kyi gsan sbyong ma grub par ri phug tu phebs nas dge slong rin chen 'phel la
slob dpon zhus te bu lugs kyi sngags cho ga skor gzigs rtog mdzad/ dgung lo bcu gsum pa shing pho stag gi lo sa skya bdag chen rin po che 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po
gdan sa ri phug nyid du phebs pa'i tshe/ byang gling bla brang du chigs sdam dge tshul sdom pa bzhes/ mtshan rin chen

bsod nams mchog grub ces bya ba'ang bdag chen nyid kyi btags/ bdag chen nas phyag mdud/ bdud rtsi ril bu/ bu ston rin po che'i bum chu sogs dang / | oM sA sti/ 'jam dbyangs
ngo bo bla ma'i mchog /bsod nams ye shes mthar phyin pa'i/ /chos kyi dbang po dam pa la/ /gsol ba 'debs so byin gyis rlobs// // sarba mangga lam //zhes bya ba phyag bris
su mdzad nas stsal/ 'di ngag tu 'don pa dang / da bya 'gyur du gsung ngag la ma 'bras shig 'chad pas de dus slebs pa gyis/ khyod la sa paN gyi sdom rgyun zhig kyang dgos
pa 'dug pas lo nyi shu lon pa na nga'i rtsar shog gsung / de'i lo snga ma'i zla ba brgyad pa'i nang du dge slong rin chen 'phel bsnyun nas sku gshegs khar lha bo pa chos
rje rin chen rgya mtsho gdan drangs te bdag gi dge gzhon 'di la bu lugs kyi dbang chos rnams gnang thub pa zhig sku mkhyen no zhes kha chems su bzhag cing / rje nyid la'ang
/ ngor du sgra'i slob gnyer zhig kyang byed e thub ltos/ rje dbang rab pa'i drung du chos zhu gang thub pa dang / rgyun du sgo gsum chos dang mthun pa gal che'o zhes
gsung rus pa can mang po gnang ba'i mthar grongs pa yin skad/ de nas chos sde lha bo pas kyang bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i bzhed srol gyi dbang tshan rnams rim gyis stsal/
dbang rnams grub pa dang phyag gi rdo rje dril bu rje nyid la gtad nas rdor dril bla ma'i phyag tu 'phrod pa yin pas blo bde'o gsung skad/ gzhan yang gang che na dpon

slob grub dbang shAkya sengge la mnyam sbyor rigs bsdus dang / 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma'i dbang bka'/ nags rin lugs kyi sbyor drug sogs gsan/ rin po che dkon mchog rgyal mtshan
la bu ston yab sras kyi bka' 'bum skor gsan/ de nas 'jam dkar ma ti lugs kyi bsnyen sgrub ma sha'i las sbyor dang bcas pa gnang pas thugs rab phul du phyin par gyur/ rje
dbang rab pa la 'jigs byed dpa' bo gcig pa dang brag rdzong ma'i phyi nang gsang gsum gyi 'khrid sogs chos bka' mang ba gsan zhing skye bdun ril bu sgrub pa gnang ba'i
phyag g.yog sogs kyang mdzad nas bdag 'khrul zhig rin po che'i dus zhabs phyir e yod lags zhus pas/ yod gsung / rgyal yum tshul khrims bzang mo'i skabs yang dam zhus pas/
med pa 'dra gsung / brag rdzong ma'i bsnyen mtshams mdzad skabs rje dbang rab pa'i drung du/ zhal 'don gnang rgyu'i sku bstod cing bka' rtsom zhus pa phyag bris su gnang
ba'i kha byang la/ ri phug dbu mdzad chen mo'i thugs dam zhes gnang 'dug pa gang yin nam dgongs kyang phyis ri phug gi gdan sa yong ba'i lung bstan yin 'dug gsungs/ dgung
lo nyi shu rtsa gcig pa la dpal 'khor chos sde'i rin sding grwa tshang gi bla mar gdan drangs/ ri phug nas phebs gdong du rje dbang rab pa'i spyan sngar phyag dbang zhu
bar byon pas bka' bsgo byin rbalas bkra shis smon lam gyi

tshigs bcad mang du gsungs pa'i mthar/ bltas pa tsam gyis khams gsum dbang du sdud/ /ces sogs gsungs nas bzhugs/ de ru snying ma zhig kyang byung song ngo ang gsung / dpal
'khor chos sder phebs nas sngar rin sdings pa'i bla mar phyag mi btsal ba'i rgyal rtse'i drung 'khor kun rje 'di'i sku gsung thugs kyi mdzad pas yid 'phrog te gang du mjal
yang phyag kyang 'gyel ba ltar btsal lo/ /rin sdings grwa tshang gi 'du khang nyams pa gsos te shing rtse ldebs ris sogs phun sum tshogs pa bsgrubs nas rab gnas la dpal
zhwa lu'i gdan sa bco brgyad pa mkhan chen sku zhang chos rje nam mkha' chos ldan dpal bzang po gdan drangs/ dgung lo nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa la bkra shis kyi gtsug lag khang
dpal e waM chos ldan dumakhan po sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub dang / las kyi slob dpon brang ti nam mkha' sangs rgyas kyi mdzad de bsnyen rdzogs bzhes mod/ sdom
rgyun de la dpyad gzhir mdzad nas phyis lha khang mkhan chen byams pa bsod nams bkra shis dpal bzang po las sa paN gyi sdom rgyun rnam dag de bskyar nas zhu bar mdzad do/
/rin spungs bla ma dgongs pa zhus nas ri phug tu phebs te nyin mtshan ngo mi mkhyen pa lta bu'i brtson 'grus kyis rgyud sde rab tu mang po'i dpe 'dzin dang gar dbyangs thig
gsum la sbyor brdar mdzad/ dgung lo nyi shu rtsa bdun pa la ri phug gi gdan sar phebs nas chos 'khor bskor/ skabs

shig rje sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub kyi drung du thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid sogs gsan pas/ mnal lam du lung pa thams cad chus mer ba khengs pa gzigs nas 'di 'khor
ba sdug bsngal gyi rgya mtsho chen po yin 'dug /sems can thams cad 'don thub na ni rab yin/ ma thub na tshe 'di'i pha ma gnyis 'don dgos dgongs te phyag tshul yul yul mdzad
pas sbal lcong 'dra mo phyag mthil du byung / da shar phyogs mngon par dga' ba thegs dgos dgongs te nam mkha' la 'phur bas mngon dga'i zhing yin snyam par phebs/ der
mi 'khrugs pa'i stong thang 'dra ba zhig sngo cham gyi gzigs pa dang mnyam du mnal sad/ yang nub gcig bde ba can la 'byon dgos dgongs te nam mkha' la 'phur ba na sgrub khang
gi gsol thab su phebs/ de na 'dug pa'i mi zhig la nga bde ba can du 'gro rgyu yin pa la gsungs pas/ de na re 'od dpag med ni 'di ga yin zer rje dpal ldan don grub phyogs
la mdzub brda byed kyin 'dug gsung / ri phug tu kyai rdor gyi bsnyen chen gnang skabs sku khams log ste shin tu ma bde ba byung ba'i mnal lam du rje btsun dbang phyug
rab brtan phebs nas de wa bitsu'i sngags 'phreng zhal nas 'khor bzhin pa de phyag gis bzungs te khyod la mi dgos na bton gtong gsungs pa dang / yang nub gcig rna bar brgyud
ldan gyi bla ma dam pa la bcud ldan gyi gdams ngag zhus nas dben pa'i gnas su nyams su

len par khyod gang la sdug zer ba dang / nub gcig phyag g.yon pa'i sku rus ma gtogs sha lpags bcad pa las sku mtshal gyi rgyun 'bab kyin 'dug pa/ mi zhi na re/ sdug bsran chung
rang drags pas khrag gi lhag dum pa lus song / gzhan lhag ma lus na yong ba 'dug ste zer skad/ snga phyi chos gsan pa'i bla ma ni yongs su dril bas drug cu re bdun tsam
bsten/ de yang sa zhwa gnyis kyi phyogs nas bka' drin che ba'i bla ma dbang phyug rab brtan/ lha bo pa rin chen rgya mtsho/ nyi ma gling pa tshul khrims bkra shis/ sgrub
khang pa dpal ldan don grub/ bka' 'gyur mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ /paN chen dpal ldan tshul khrims/ sa skya pa 'jam mgon bsod nams dbang phyug rnams yin la/ gzhan
yang rje btsun tA ra nA tha sogs las jo nang lugs/ paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan dang / drung pa brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan sogs las dge lugs/
gter bdag gling pa sogs las rnying ma'i skor/ rgyal ba dpag bsam dbang po sogs las dwags po bka' brgyud pa'i chos skor rnams kyang gsan te mdor na rgya gar nas brgyud
pa'i mdo dang sngags kyi bka' bstan bcos tshad ma rnams dang / bod kyi yang dpal ldan sa skya pa gong ma lnga dang / rjes 'brang ngor rdzong gong gsum/ bye brag kha'u brag
rdzong pa'i bzhad srol/ gsung ngag lam 'bras tshogs slob gnyis/ gser chos skor chos skyong rnams kyi man ngag gtso b.ro gyur pa'i dbang khrid zab mo ji
