snyed pa dang / de dag gi rgyab chos rje sa skya pa yab sras kyi bka' 'bum skor/ ngor pa rdo rje 'chang yab sras/ rong ston smra ba'i sengge/ kun mkhyen go bo rab 'byams pa/
mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen sogs sa lugs kyi mkhas grub grags che ba rnams kyi gsung 'bum gyi lung rgyun yod pa phal cher dang / bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i bzhed srol
rgyud sde bzhi dang 'brel ba'i dkyil 'khor so so'i dbang / rgyud rgya gzhung sgrub dkyil lag dang bcas pa thugs su chud par mdzad cing / de dag dang 'brel ba kun mkhyen
yab sras kyi bka' 'bum/ mkhyen rab bka' 'bum sogs dang / rje btsun btsong kha pa yab sras kyi gsung rab skor/ paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan/
rgyal dbang lnga pa chen po sogs kyi bka' rtsom phal che ba'i lung rnams kyang de dag de la gsan par mdzad/ gzhan yang phyag chen chos drug sogs 'brug lugs/ ne gu chos
drug sogs shangs chos/ man ngag brgya rtsa sogs khra phu lugs/ nges don rgya mtsho dang khrid brgya sogs jo nang lugs/ zhi khro bka' brgyad dang rdzogs pa chen po sogs
rnying ma lugs rnams gsan te chos kyi bang mdzod chen por gyur to/ /de yang zhwa lu ri mthil/ dpal 'khor chos sde rin sngings pa/ dus 'khor shar byang gnyis/ dbang ldan
chos 'khor rnams su bu lugs kyi dbang bka'/ bshad bka'/ khrid bka'/ gar dbyangs bris thig bzhi

sogs kyi phyag len gyi rgyun mi nyams pa'i ched du chos kyi 'khor lo bskor/ skyid shod lho mos gzhis kha/ gong dkar rdo rje gdan/ rgyal rtse gur pa grwa tshang / shab dge sdings
sogs su dpal ldan sa skya pa nas brgyud pa'i gsung ngag lam 'bras kyis mtshon pa'i smin grol zab mo'i chos 'khor bskor nas gdul bya grangs kyi ra ba las 'das ba rgyud
yongs su smin pa dang grol bar mdzad do/ /skabs 'di dag tu zhwa lu ri mthil gyi grwa rgyun tha dad du yong ba dang / mthil pa rnams grong dang khad nye'i stabs kyi 'dul
ba'i kun tu spyod pa las phyi rol du gyur cing gzhi gsum gyi tshig byed pa'i srol yang rim gyis nub pasra nyid kyi thabs mkhas kyis paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa blo bzang
chos kyi rgyal mtshan sku bgres tshul shin tu che yang nan gyis zhus nas zhwa lu'i mkhan sar gdan drangs/ sku zhabs paN chen rin po che'i bka' bkod gnang ba zhus te zhwa
lu mthil gtsang dgon la bsgyur nas zla ba ngo re bzhin gyi gso sbyong gnyis dang / dbyar gnas dgag dbye dang bcas pa gzhi gsum gyi cho ga'i srol rgyun rma med par btsugs/
bca' yig kyang bu ston rin po che'i dus kyi rnying pa sor bzhags la yul dus kyi bcos dogs sogs zin bris su phab nas sku zhabs paN chen rin po che'i spyan lam du gzigs
rtog phul bas thugs rab tu dgyes nas/ sku mdun du 'khod pa dag la chos rje 'dis mdzad pa ltar zhwa lu pa gzhan kun gyis byas na bstan pa nyams

pa gso ba las sla ba 'dug gsung / ri khrod byams pa gling yang sngar paN chen rang gis zhal 'dzin gnang ba rje nyid la dgon gnas kyi skal ba mdzod gsungs nas gsol ras su stsal/
dgung lo drug cu bzhes pa'i tshe dbus su phebs nas gong dkar chos sder dpal gyi rdo rje'i bsnyen chen gyi bcad rgya shin tu dam pa la bzhugs yod pa'i dus sku zhabs paN
chen rin po che sku na ches smin pas bkra shis lhun po dang gdan sa gnyis 'dzin gyi phebs bskyod gnang ma thub par gzhungs chen par mkhan po gdan sa pa zhig bsko dgos
tshul gyi snyan 'bul gnang bas/ sde srid 'phrin las rgya mtsho'i zhal nas/ kun mkhyen bu'i gdan sar mkhan po chos rgyun mi gcig pa zhig bskos tshe 'dre shar sgo dang glud
nub sgo'i dper 'gro'go/ da re ri phug dbu mdzad sman khang nas 'di spyod pa zhi dul che zhing mkhan po'i 'os che ba 'dug gsung rje nyid la mkhan po'i bsko 'ja' mdzad par
thugs 'dod la ma byung mod/ slar rgyal dbang rin po ches da lam sku mtshams kyi mur thams cad mkhyen pa'i rgyal tshab tu phebs dgos zhu ba ni dngos grub kyi sgo bye ba lta
bur 'gro bas ci kyang zhal bzhes mdzod ces pa'i phyag dam stsal/ de nas gtsang du phebs nas dgung lo drug cu re gcig pa dge byed ces pa cu pho stag gi lo cho 'phrul zla
ba'i tshes drug gi nyin zhwa lu ri mthil gyis sengge'i khri la zhabs kyi padma bkod/ gzhungs chen pos khri ston gyi bsnyen bkur dang

gzhan yang phyogs 'dus kyi bu slob yon bdag kun gyi mang ja 'gyed sogs dga' ston dpag med mdzad/ khri thogs tu lo ngo bcu bzhugs nas 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi sgo nas bstan
pa rgya cher spel ba dang / bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i zhal chems kyi yi ge dbu sngas kyi mgor bzhag nas de nang bzhin zhwa lu lha sde mi sde thams cad lugs gnyis kyi
sgo nas legs par skyong bar mdzad de mdor na mkhan chen 'di nyid kyi bka' drin ni zhwa lu pa rnams kyis gzhal bar mi nus shing dus thams cad du phyag 'ba' zhig bya ba rig
pa yin no/ /dgung lo bdun cu bzhes pa lcags mo phag gi lo sku zhang mkhyen brtse mchog grub la gdan sa gtad/ de rjes yang dbus gtsang gi ljongs su 'chad nyan mang du mdzad/
'dzam gling skye dgu'i gtsug rgyan rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho dang / dpal ldan sa skya'i bdag po sku mched sogs gangs ri'i khrod
kyi chen po grags pa thams cad zhal slob tu gyur na gzhan smros ma dgos zhing ma 'ongs pa'i rjes 'jug rnams la dgongs te legs bshad bka' 'bum gyi phreng ba yang 'jog pa
mdzad/ de yang dam chos 'chad pa'i tshe na 'dul bya dbang po brtul po ji 'dra zhig yin yang go ba khyad par can skye ba/ mi shes pa'i mun pa'i cha dang the tshom gyi ra
ri mata' dag lung rigs nyi 'od kyis bsal nas/ zab don gyi pad tshal 'byed nus pa kho na 'byung ngo / /rtsod pa'i tshul yang mtshan nyid kyi rtog ge'i phyogs bzung bas thal
skad kyi nga ro sgrog

pa sogs mi mdzad mod dngos shugs kyi rigs lam nas drangs pa'i dgag sgrub sogs kyi tshe na log rtog gi brag ri bsnyel nus pa'i gsung ngag gnam lcags kyi thog dang 'dra ba kho
na 'bab so/ /rtsom pa mdzad pa'i tshe na tshig rna bar snyan zhing don 'brel chags pa mkhas pa dag gis mthong na yid rang dbang med par 'phrog nus pa zhig te rje nyid kyi
bka' 'bum la bltas pas shes so/ /de lta bu'i 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi sgo nas bstan 'gro'i don rgya cher mdzad pa'i mthar nyid kyi dgung lo brgyad cu bzhes pa lcags
mo bya'i lo/ /gro bzhin zla ba'i yar ngo'i tshes bzhi'i nyin par gzugs sku'i bkod pa bsdus nas dga' ldan chos kyi pho brang chen por gshegs so/ /de ltar yang rgyal mchog
lnga pas/ rnam gsum mkhas pa'i bya bas gangs can ljongs/ /bstan dang 'gro ba'i phan bde rab spel nas/ /dga' ldan chos kyi mdun sar byams mgon gyi/ /sras kyi thu bor gshegs
la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar ro/ /sku gdung ring bsrel gyi snying po can bzhugs pa'i dngul gyi mchod rten thob tshad ma dang gser zangs las grub pa'i snang brnyan
sku tshad dang mnyam pa mthong grol yid bzhin gyi nor bu sogs zhwa lu'i dngul gdung lha khang du bzhugs pa lags so/ /tshul de ltar gsan rjes 'jug rnams kyang skyes bu
dam pa de dag gi rnam par thar pa nyams len gyi mthil du bzung nas rang dang gzhan gyi don bsgrub pa la mkhas par

bya'o / /de ltar yang / chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston chen pos mnga' ris zhang zhung gi dge 'dun rnams la springs pa las/ ston pa'i bstan pa lung dang rtogs pa'i chos/
/de 'dzin byed pa bshad sgrub rnam pa gnyis/ /yin gyi dka' spyad sdug bsngal khyad bsad nas/ /bshad sgrub shes rab snying brtses brgyan pa mdzod/ /bde bar gshegs pa'i
nag po bstan pa dang / /chen po bstan pa'i rnam dbye gsungs pa ltar/ /brtag pa gsum dang rton pa rnam bzhi yis/ /chos dang chos min legs par brtag par mdzod/ /chos ni gting
zab rang blos dbye dka' mod/ /'on kyang sprul sku lo tsA rin chen bzang pochen po yis/ /bshad cing gtan la phab pa'i gsung rab kun/ /dri med yin phyir de rnams gces par
blangs/ /bka' lung 'chad byed slob dpon gyismkhyen par ldan pas legs par bshad/ /blo gros slob ma snod kyi skyon bral ba desdon gnyer ldan pas gnyan cing bzung / /nges
'byung brtson 'grus ldan sbyor ba 'di dag tshang paspas nyams su blangs/ 'di gsum ldan na bstan pa 'dzin pa yin/ /de ltar blang dor blo yis legs rtogs nas/ /tshig la mi zhen
sgrub pa gtsor byas te/ /rnyed dka' 'jigs sla'i dal 'byor don yang phyir/ /bstan pa'i snying po sgrub pa lhur blang bya/ /sgrub pa'i chos de bslab pa rnam gsum ste/ /tshul
khris dag pas de las ting 'dzin skye/ /de las de nyid rtogs pa'i shes rab 'byung / /de yis nyon mongs spong ste

myang 'das thob/ /de phyir dang por nges 'byung bsam pa yis/ /rab byung spong ba bdun gyi sdom pa blangs/ /yan lag drug dang ldan pa'i tshul khrims ni/ /lhag pa tshul khrims
bslab par thub pas gsung / /de ni yon tan kun gyi rten yin pas/ /lus dang srog gi phyir yang mi btang ste/ /nyes pa phra mo'ang myur du phyir bcos te/ /mig gi 'bras bu
bzhin du bsrung bar bya/ /'dod pa'i nyon mongs me sogs zhi gyur pa'i/ /bsam gtan bzhi yi ting 'dzin skyon med la/ /bde bar gnas pa sems kyi ting 'dzin yin/ /de bas de phyir
ting 'dzin brtson par bya/ /mnyam par bzhag pa'i chos ni de kho na/ /legs par rtogs nas gang gis sgrib pa spong/ /de ni lhag pa shes rab bslab pa ste/ /de yi gnas lugs
rtogs pa'i shes rab skye/ /'di gsum sangs rgyas bstan pa sgrub pa'i chos/ /yin phyir gzhan gyi dbang du ma byung par/ /bag yod brtson pas de gsum nyams len pa/ /de ni sangs
rgyas bstan pa 'dzin pa yin/ /yang smras pa/ nges 'byung bsam pa brtan po dang / /spong bdun tshul khrims dag pa dang / /bya dang bya min shes pa dang / /nyes gnas chung
la 'dzoms pa dang / /bzhi po 'di dag ldan gyur na/ /don gyi dge slong bzang po yin/ /byang chub sems gnyis ma nyams dang / /bdag bde gzhan sdug brje ba dang / /chung
ngu'i phyir ni che mi gtong / /gtso cher gzhan gyi sems bsrung ba/ /bzhi po de

dag ldan gyur na/ /byang chub sems dpa' chen po yin/ /dbang gi chu bo ma nub cing / /lha yi rnal 'byor gsal ba dang / /dam tshig sdom pa brtan pa dang / /tha mal 'dzin pa shig
pa dang / /bzhi po 'di dag ldan gyur na/ /rig pa 'dzin pa chen po yin/ /zhes sogs gsungs pa ltar bsgrub dgos kyi/ de las gzhan du rang rgyud lam sbyar ba gzhan la chos
bshad kyang don du mi 'gyur zhing / de yang chos rje nyid kyi zhal nas/ deng sang kha ba can gyi yul ljongs 'dir/ /bdag kyang las kyi dbang gi 'dir skyes mod/ /'od stong
ldan pa'i dkyil 'khor nub la nye/ /rkang drung ldan pa'i dga' ba gang gis spel/ /bsti gnas phal cher gcan gzan gdug pas gang / /mgron po'i tshogs rnams gang du ngal gso
bya/ /rgyu skar rgyal po gnam stong mun par bzhugs/ /kun da'i tshal gyi gnyid gyur gang zhig yin/ /don mthun phal cher nor bur 'ching bu len/ /rin chen nor gyis phyug par
su zhig 'gyur/ /bung ba'i tshogs rnams dug gi me tog gzhib/ /sman mchog sbrang rtsi phul byung gang la 'gyur/ /de phyir thub pa'i gsung rab cha shas tsam/ /bshad kyang
gang gi rna ba'i snod du lhung / /de bas rang gi yid la nyer bzhag te/ /dben par bag yod bya ba'i dus la babs/ /ces gsungs pa ltar bstan pa'i snying po bsdus nas rang rgyud
la sbyar te dal 'byor thob pa don ldan du mdzod cig ces rang gzhan kun la thal mo sbyar nas gsol ba 'debs so/ /'dir smras pa/ snyigs ma'i lang tsho bdo

ba'i mun klong du/ /gsang chen kun da'i phreng ba bzhad pa'i gnyen/ /skal bzang yid kyi rdzing bur 'char mkhas pa'i/ /ngo mtshar 'phrul gyi zla ba ci yang shar/ /mkhyen pa
phun tshogs 'chi med lam gyi gzhir/ /thub gsung dbyar gyi dpal mo chags pa las/ /legs bshad chu 'dzin bu mo bzhad pa'i grus/ /mkhas mang mdongs mtha'i snying la bdud rtsi
ster/ /de dus cher rlom tsu ta'i 'khri shing phal/ /mkhas tshul gsum gyi ge sar mi ldan yang / /'khor dang zang zing yal ga mthor bteg nas/ /'bras med sprin char zol gyi
lha lam sgrib/ /grags 'byor 'dab phreng gos su ma klubs kyang / /bshad sgrub zung gis snye mas sgeg pa yi/ /srid lam dub pa'i yid can dga' ba'i tshal/ /bka' srol 'di yi
gong ma'i lam las brnyes/ /de phyir brgyud pa mchog gi rnam thar bzhin/ /bdag kyang deng nas tshe rabs thams cad du/ /theg mchog nor bu'i mdzod la dbang bsgyur nas/ /'gro
kun chos kyi phongs pa sel gyur cig /ces dpal ldan zhwa lu ba'i bstan pa la bka' drin chen ba'i skyes bu dam pa rnams kyi rnam thar lo rgyus ngo mtshar dad pa'i 'jug ngogs
zhes bya ba las gsol 'debs kyi dmigs su phye ba'i brgyud 'dzin mkhas grub rim byon gyi rtogs pa brjod pa'i sarga de gsum pa'o/ / / /yid 'ongs mtshan dpe'i 'dab stong g.yo
ba'i dbus/ /dbyangs snyan zil dngar chags pa'i me tog dkar/ /

rab bzhad pad dkar gzhon nu mtsho ldan mas/ /bdag blo'i bung ba tshim pa'i shes rab stsol/ /zhes tshigs su bcad pa sngon du btang nas/ gnyis pa gong gi gsol ba 'debs pa'i tshigs
bcad kyi gsal kha ma phye ba'i brgyud 'dzin rnams kyi 'phros don kha 'gengs kyi tshul du bshad pa la gnyis/ tshigs bcad kyis don mdor bstan pa dang / de nyid rgyas
par 'grel tshul lo/ /dang po ni/ gsol 'debs las/ kun mkhyen bu ston ma dros mtsho chen las/ /slob brgyud bgrang yas chu bo mtha' yas pa/ /ma dag rnyog ma yongs bral byon
zin dang / /slad mar 'byon 'gyur rnams la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes bya ba ste don ni go sla bar zad do/ /gnyis pa de nyid rgyas par 'grel tshul la gsum/ mkhan rabs byon tshul
bshad pa/ ri phug byang gling gi gdan rabs zur tsam bshad pa/ der ma 'dus pa'i dam pa 'ga' zhig gi mdzad tshul bshad pa'o/ /dang po la gnyis/ mkhan brgyud rnying ma byon
tshul dang / gsar ma ji ltar byon pa'i tshul lo/ /dang po ni/ rgyal po srong btsan sgam po'i bka' 'bum las/ /de nas byang sems sprul pa byung nas su/ /chos kyi me ro mdo
khams smad nas slong / /dge 'dun sde ba mang du 'phel bar byed/ /de yang byang chub sems dpa' mang po yis/ /nga yi ra sa'i sku gzugs 'di dag la/ /mchod pa zhabs tog mang
po byed par gyur/ /phyogs rnams kun tu gtsug lag khang skyong zhing / /dam pa'i spyod pa tshul bzhin byed par 'gyur/ /zhes lung bstan pa ltar/ bstan pa phyi dar gyi dus

su chos sde 'di nyid btab pa'i lo rgyus ni/ me mkha' rgya mtsho'i 'das lo'i 403nang gi lo grangs sum brgya don dgu sngar song zin pa'i rjes thog cu mo bya'i lo de la bstan
pa phyi dar gyi 'go zug nas lo ston rdo rje dbang phyug gi rgyan gong 'debs pa'i sa chog mdzad par bzhed/ de'i skabs su lce btsun shes rab 'byung gnas kyang 'khrungs te/
zho cu khar mo cher lce lim shis pa bdun dus gcig tu byung pa la/ dbyal ratna shris rim gro byas te lo bdun bzlog pas/ jo ba ratna byon pas 'tsheng / phyag rgya dril bu
dkrol bas 'tsheng / raksha'i phreng ba brdab pas 'tsheng / /hUM phaT 'brug sgra bsgrags pas 'tsheng / zer ba'i kha dpe byung / re zhig nas lce la 'bangs rnams kyis ngo log
byas te lce phal cher bsad/ lce btsun shes rab 'byung gnas kyi lo ston gyi spyan sngar bros shing lce 'bum gyi glegs bam rnams phyag rten du phul/ rab tu byung ste dka'
spyad drag pos nye gnas mdzad do/ /der rgyan gong brtsigs pa'i 'gan 'khur gnang bas yongs su rdzogs par grub te/ de nas chu mo yos kyi lo lce btsun rang gi chos sde 'debs
par dgongs te dpal zhwa lu gser khang gi gtsug lag khang bzhengs so/ /chos sde btab tshar ba dang 'go ba ye shes g.yung drung la re zhig gdan sa gtad nas lce btsun khong
rang rgya gar du phebs/ rdo rje gdan gyi slob dpon a bha ya ka ra la sdom pa bskyar ma zhus/ kha sar pA Ni spyan drangs bod du phebs

nas zhwa lu'i mkhan po mdzad pas mkhan brgyud kyi thog ma ni lce btsun shes rab 'byung gnas yin no/ /de la che ba'i yon tan bzhi yod de/ /rus lce yin pas che ba dang gcig /sdom
pa rgya gar paN chen la dngos su thob pa'i che ba dang gnyis/ yon bdag bal po'i rgyal po sogs rtsad po rnams yin pas che ba dang gsum/ las mnga' 'og gi yul sde chen
po ka ba bzhir grags pa rnams kyi byas pas che ba dang bzhi'o/ /nges pa'i don du 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs nyid yin no/ / | //de nas lce bsun sku 'das pa'i rjes su nyid kyi
gcung po shes rab ye shes kyi mkhan po mdzad do/ / | de'i su rtse g.yu thog sgra gser bzang zhes bya bas mkhan po mdzad cing / 'di skabs thob rgyal gyi bye ma g.yu zur
nas rang byon thugs rje chen po rnyed nas gtsang 'grams kyi lha khang du bzhugs pa de zhwa lu nyid du spyan drangs/ gnas la lcag sir btang zhing chos sde'i nang du khron
pa brko ba sogs mdzad/ 'on kyang khong rang sngar mkhas btsun che yang rjes su 'dod lha'i chad pas nyen nas bslab pa 'chal ste dpon brgyud du song ngo / /'di yan la lce'i
brgyud rang nas byung ba'i chos dpon sbrags pa'i mkhan po gsum mo/ / | de nas mkhan rab bzhi pa ni khyung po grags seng ste/ 'di ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen po to ba dang dus
mtshungs shing dwags po byang chub dbang rgyal dang gnyis pos po ta ri dang dmar po ti la tshad ma'i bstan bcos kyi 'gran

bshad byas/ grwa pa rnams kyang gnyis ka'i chos grwa 'grim pa zhig byung zhes mkhas pa'i dbang po rje btsun 'gos lo tsA ba gzhon nu dpal gyis deb sngon chos 'byung du yang
bshad gda'/ de'i rgyu mtshan ni/ gong du smos pa ltar g.yu thog sgra bslab pa 'chal bas dge bshes khyung po mkhan por bskos nas khong rang gi chab srid bskyangs/ re zhig
nas g.yu thog sgras rgyan gong la dmag byas te/ rten dang chos cha 'phrog go byas pas/ /khyung po na re/ rgyan gong bstan pa smad nas dar ba'i dus kyi gtsug lag khang thams
cad kyi ma mo yin/ chos sde 'di'ang rgyan gong las gyes pa'i yal ga yin pas dmag byed du mi rung gsung nan gyis bzlog kyang nyan du ma 'dod/ de la khyung po ma dgyes te
bros thabs kyis tshong dus kyi bag ma la gong du lam khyod la da phyi nas mi ldog go ces gabu bsnyung bzhes/ dbus su dmar po ri la byon nas der bshad grwa btsugs so/ /bar
der g.yu thog sgras rgyan gong dmag gis bcom te rten dang yo byad mang po zhwa lur drangs/ de rjes dbus su dge bshes khyung po'i sar pho nya bsrings te bzod gsol gyi 'bul
ba chen po'ang byas/ slar nan gyi gdan drangs pas byon te tshong 'dus kyi lam la mna' bskyal bas mi 'gro gsung lam bskor phyogs mdzad nas phebs shing sngar bzhin mkhan
po mdzad de chos gsungs so/ /rje su 'dis dga' ba gdong

chos kyi ka ba yang btab cing mkhan brgyud kyi thog mar yang khong rang bzhugs pa'i lo rgyus gnang ngo / /gzhan yang sngags rnying ma ba'i grub thob lha rje zur bu che'i slob
ma zur chung shes rab grags bya ba dang khong gnyis yon bdag gcig gis myad ror gdan drangs nas chos gsungs pa'i dus/ khyung po grags seng ge zhal nas/ zur chung shes rab
grags bya ba chos log mkhan 'di sun phyung la shog gsungs nas/ gla nar shAkya bzang po sogs khong rang gi slob ma dge bshes mkhas pa bzhi btang bas/ de dag gi lha rje
zur chung ba sun 'byin ma thub par tshur log pas khyung po na re/ khyed tshos zur chung pa sun phyin nam gsung / sun phyin par mi gda' zhus pas/ ma dgyes te zur chung pa
'dra ba'i lta ba ngan pa can/ skye bo thams cad log pa'i lam la 'khrid pa 'di bsad na/ sangs rgyas te the tshom med par thag chod/ de ci'i phyir na don du 'gyur na bkag pa
rnams kyang gnang ba'i phyir ro/ /zhes gsungs pa zur chung pas gsan te nangs par chos khri'i khar byon nas chos gsung khar bzhad mo mdzad/ chos bya ba 'di nga'i theg pa
chen po gsang sngags 'di yin par 'dug /sgrol ba la brten nas gsang rgya ba gsang sngags kyi lugs yin mtshan nyid pa la med snyam tsa na/ zur chung pa bsad na sangs rgya
gsungs nas khyung po grags seng lta bu'i mtshan nyid pa'i dge bshes chen po yang blo phug nga'i chos la gtod par 'dug pas dga' ba gcig byung

gsung ba sogs mdor na dus der mkhas grags che ba'i lo rgyus yod do/ / / /mkhan rabs lnga pa ni mkhan po mngonmdon pa ste 'di'i gong tsam du paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa mtshan
dngos bstan skyong dang rngog lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab gnyis kyi zhwa lur mngon pa kun las btus sogs kyi bshad grwa btsugs/ rngog lo chen po de ni zhwa lu'i chos sde
'di chu mo yos la btab pa'i lo nas lnga bcu nga bdun song ba rab byung thams cad kyi dang po'i nang gi sa mo phag la sku 'khrungs/ khong gis dgung lo bco brgyad pa mnga'
bdag rtse lde'i me pho 'brug gi chos 'khor gyi dus zhwa lu mkhan po khyung po grags seng kyang bzhugs yod/ rngog los dgung lo sum cu so bzhi pa cu pho spre'u'i lo rgya
gar kha che'i yul nas bod du phebs te chos 'khor bskor nas lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa sa mo glang la gshegs pa'i bar dar paN chen 'bum phrag gsum pa bstan skyong dpal bzang po
yang bod du phebs shing la paN de gnyis sdebs nas zhwa lur bstan pa'i bya ba mdzad cing da lta zhwa lu'i tshogs dung 'di nyid kyang 'bum phrag gsum pa'i chos dung zhes byin
rlabs che ba'i lo rgyus yod do/ / | /mkhan rabs drug pa ni zhwa lu pa gzhon nu brtson 'grus te 'di dang dus mtshungs bar gnyis pa zhig po'i slob ma gtsang pa gru gus
zhwa lur dbu tshad sogs kyi bshad pa btsugs shing / de nas bzungs te zhwa lu ba rnams gnyal ba'i TIkka sogs la

'chad nyan byed pa'i srol byung pas/ rjes su chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston chen po gdan sar phebs nas kyang lugs snga ma dang bstun pa'i phyir du dbu mdzad bkra shis
bzang po la gnyal TIkka gi lung gsan nas bshad pa gnang ba'i tshul yod do/ / | //mkhan rabs bdun pa ni wa chos byang / / | //brgyad pa ni bu ston seng ge 'od yin la 'dis
gnyal ba'i TIkka chud sogs logs su mdzad do/ / | / /mkhan rabs dgu pa ni mkhan po 'bul ba 'dzin pa mtshan dngos grags pa brtson 'grus te 'di yan la rab byung bsnyen rdzogs
kyi sdom rgyun yang slob dpon abha yA ka ra la lce btsun shes rab 'byung gnas kyis zhus pa'i sdom rgyun de yin pas/ mkhan po bsko ba'i tshe yang mkhan po gsar pa la sdom
rgyun de mi zhugs na mkhan po rnying pa'am/ de las gzhan yang rung ste sdom pa bskyar bsgrub dgos pa'i khrims yod par snang zhing / der ma zad 'dul ba'i bshad rgyun yang
bla chen po dgongs pa rab gsal gyi drung du lo ston gyi gsan/ de la 'go ba ye shes g.yung drug gis zhus/ de nyid la lce btsun shes rab 'byung gnas kyis kyang zhus mod
kyi gtso bor gyur pa ni 'go ba ye shes g.yung drung kho nas 'dul ba'i bshad grwa bskyangs te slob brgyud dar ro/ / | mkhan rabs bcu pa ni bka' bzi pa grags pa gzhon nu ste/
'di man chod kyi zhwa lu'i mkhan po

thams cad kyi sdom rgyun kha che paN chen las brgyud pa sha stag yin la/ 'dul ba'i bshad rgyun yang klums chen po shes rab tshul khrims las brgyud pa bla chen po'i bshad srol
bka' bzhi pas zul phu'i mkhan po chos grags rin chen la gsan nas dar/ yang kha che paN chen gyi snar klus mo cher dbyar gnas mdzad skabs 'dul ba me tog phreng rgyud gsungs
pa la 'dul 'dzin sengge zil gnon gyi TIkka mdzad de tshad ma'i skyes bu bsod nams mgon po la gnang / de la chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston chen pos gsan nas rjes
su zhwa lur dar ba'i tshul yang yod do/ /de yang mkhan po phyi marnams paN chen gyi sdom rgyun 'dzin pa'i rgyu mtshan ni/ kha che paNDi ta shAkya shribha dra bod la phebs
dus rgyan gong byang chub dge gnas kyi gtsug lag khang 'di nyid du rje btsun sa paN dang / mkhan chen rdo rje dpal ba sogs rab tu byung zhing bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i dngos
por bsgrub/ dus phyis sa skya pa bod khams yongs kyi bdag po mdad pa'i mjug tsam du bla ma bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal dang / ti shrir kun dga' blo gros gnyis bsnyen
rdzogs bzhes dus skyer sde snod 'dzin pa dpal ldan rgyal mtshan sogs dge ba'i bshes gnyen lnga bcu lhag tsam zhig 'dus nas so thar gyi sdom brgyud la khung dag mi dag
gis rtsad gcod dang dri ba zhib po byas pa'i tshe/ kha che paN chen gyi sdom brgyud 'di rtsod pa dang bral zhing /

de'i mkhan brgyud 'dzin pa'ang bka' bzhi pa grags pa gzhon nu yid chos khungs thubs kyi gnas yin 'dug pas de'i sdom rgyun long zhig zer ba yi ger bris pa la/ bla ma bdag nyid
chen pos thogs drangs/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen mang pos the'u tshe rgyab pa'i bka' shog byung skad do// | de lo mkhan chen bka' bzhi pa grags pa gzhon nu dpal bzang po de
ni 'khrungs yul dbu ru stod kyi lha lung ri mo can zhes bya ba'i grong khyer gsar du yab gyer gsar rgod ces pa de'i sras su rab byung bzhi pa'i dmar ser bzhes pa me mo sbrul
gyi lo la sku 'khrungs/ gzhon nur gyur pa tsam nas bya yul pa'i spyan snga bshes gnyen kham lung pa'i gnas su byon te/ mkhan po grags pa 'bum la rab tu byung zhing mtshan
grags pa gzhon nu zhes bya ba gsol/ re zhig nas jo gdan mkhan chen bde ba dpal dang mjal zhing de nyid nas skyes bu dam pa 'di jo gdan pa'i sde la phan pa'i dge bshes
zhig yong ba 'dug gsung te phyag phyir 'khrid/ de'i tshe mkhan po grags pa 'bum gyis po to ba rin chen gsal gyi lhung bzed dang dge ba'i bshes gnyen kham lung pa'i 'bral
spang jo bo rje'i sku 'dra byin rlabs can gcig yod pa'ang gnang / dgung lo bcu dgu pa shing mo phag gi lo/ dbyar zla 'bring po'i dus chos bzang po la g.yag sde ba'i dbang
mo zhes bya ba'i gnas su mkhan po bde ba dpal dang / las kyi slob dpon thugs rje dpal bzang / gsang ston chos ldan dpal bzang / dad pa'i dge

'dun gnas brtan byang chub sengge sogs 'dul ba 'dzin pa bcu drug gi dbus su bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/ mkhan chen bde ba dpal la gtsang 'bre'i TIkka dang sbyar ba'i phar phyin gyi
bshad pa dang spyod 'jug sogs gsan zhing / gzhan yang dbang dang rjes gnang du ma zhus/ khyad par 'jam dkar ma ti lugs kyi rig gtad zhus nas/ zla ba gza' 'dzin dang bstun
te ma sha'i las sbyor gnang bas myu gu me tog dang bcas pa byung / mnal lam du rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi zhal bstan nas/ ci 'dod gsungs pa la/ phyag gi ral gri de
gnang ba zhu 'tshal zhes zhus pas/ rig pa'i ral gri la byin yod/ khyod rang rdo rje 'di khyer gsungs nas gser gyi rdo rje sor bzhi tsam yod pa gcig gnang ba rmis/ de sad
nas shes bya thams cad la gzhan dring mi 'jog pa'i thugs rab phul du byung pa brnyes/ zul phur mkhan po chos grags rin chen la bya 'dul ba 'dzin pa'i TIkka dang sbyar ba'i
mdo rtsa'i bshad pa sogs gsan/ khro phu'i slob dpon gzhon mdzes la mngon pa kun las btus dang / tshad ma rnam nges rigs bsdus rnams gsan/ mkhan po yon tan 'bum la mdo
rtsa dang mngon pa gsan/ g.yag sde lo tsA ba bsod nams seng ge la bde mchog dang gshed dmar sogs gsan/ rong pa shes rab sengge la dus 'khor dang 'jigs byed kyi skor mang
po gsan/ ston pa kun rgyal la sbyor

drug gi skor mang po gsan/ grub mchog mda' cha pa la gsang sngags kyi skor mang po gsan nas don nyams su bzhes shing / de ltar chos gsan pa mtha' dal the tshom gyi dri ma dang
bral bar mdzad do/ /de nas dgung lo sum cu so brgyad bzhes pa shing pho stag gi lo tshogs kyi mkhan po mdzad cing / de'i rjes su zhwa lu'i mkhan po mdzad nas 'gro don
dang 'phrin las dar rgyas su gyur/ nyid kyi dgung lo lnga bcu nga drug pa chu pho byi ba'i lo tshong 'dus mgur mo'i bla brang shar du chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston
rin chen grub la bsnyen rdzogs gnang ste/ de dus ngo gdan bsod nams bzang po dge slong gsar bu pa'i gral na 'dug pa la gsang ston bskos pas gzhan dag gi dge bshes bgres
pa zhig la bskos nas bya ba rigs bsam zhes zhus pas/ zhal snga nas gsung gis/ nged 'di la gang zag khyad par can du re ba yin/ da len 'di la 'tshol dgos gsung / der the
tshom du gyur kyang rjes su khong gi tshogs pa'i mkhan po mdzad nas bstan pa dang sems can gyi don mdzad pa'i tshul la nges shes rnyed do/ /dbyar dgun gyi chos thog la mngon
pa kun las btus dang / 'dul ba mdo rtsa/ tshad ma bsdus pa rnams gsung / phar phyin gyi nyams 'khrid chag med lta bu mdzad/ gzhan yang chos kyi rnam grangs mi 'du ba
mang pos 'dul bya so so'i re ba bskangs shing nang du yang dag 'jog pa'i tshul la 'bad pa mi dgos par ting nge 'dzin gyi rtogs

pa khor yug tu shar/ lan cig stag gru khar tshogs pa dbyar gnas mdad dus sku khams cung zad bsnyel ba la brten sku mtshams dam po gnang zhing phyag rdzas kyi dngos po thams
cad spong dag mdzad/ de nas nyang smad kyi sngags rnying ma'i dgon po 'bir lung du phebs pa'i tshe/ nyid kyi dgung lo lnga bcu nga dgu pa/ /srin po zhes pa shing mo yos
kyi lo/ /tha skar zla ba'i tshes bco lnga'i mtshan mo'i dgung thun la/ /zla ba gza' las grol ba dang mnyam du sku gshegs/ de'i tshe tshong 'dus mgur mo'i yon bdag rnams kyi
sku gdung ril por tshong 'dus kyi sa char gdan 'dren dgos zer ba dang / chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston chen pos thog drangs snam sbyar byon pa'i dge slong gi dge
'dun nyis brgya lhag tsam gyi tshogs dang bcas pas bsu ba ser sbreng gi tshong 'dus kyi grong khyer dang khad nye bar gdan drangs/ der gdung zhugs kyi sbyangs pas me tog
gi char chen po babs pa dang nam mkha' las 'ja' 'od rol mo'i sgra sogs ltas sna tshogs byung / pur khang zhal phye ba'i ring bsrel bsam gyis mi khyab pa byon te dus phyis
gdung tshwa dang gdung thal bzhugs pa'i khang bu brtsegs pa'i ngos la yang ril bsrel 'jog pa byung zhes zer/ zhwa lur nang rten thub pa'i sku sogs bzhengs pa dag kyang
yod la/ gzhan pa phal cher sngar mgur mo'i mchod rten gyi nang du bzhugs zhes grags/ bka' bzhi pa gshegs pa shing mo yos de chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i dgung

lo nyi shu rtsa drug pa yin/ tshong 'dus mgur mor gdung gi bya ba la phebs pa ni slob ma'i gtso bor gyur pas yin gyi/ zhwa lu'i mkhan po mdzad pa'i dbang las phebs pa ni ma
yin te/ 'di nas dgung lo lnga tsam gyi ring khri phu dga' ldan gyi gtsug lag khang chen po'i sde snod 'dzin pa mtha' dag gi dbus su mkhas pa'i bya ba gsum gyis dus 'da'
ba mdzad nas bzhugs pa yin no/ /bar 'dir zhwa lu nyid du gdan sa stong nas med la/ 'on kyang sku zhang grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi sngar khong rang bzhed pa'i mkhan po'i 'os
su che ba mang po'i ming smos nas rmi lam brtags pas/ de kun gyi nang nas na tshod lo brgyad cu'i khongs gtogs pa'i rgan po zhig gi ming bsgrags te des sems can gyi don
lo ngo gsum bzhi tsam nus pa yin tshul byung yang tshe ring po mi thub par bsam ste/ mkhan por ma bskos zhing / chas 'chad du bcug nas mtshan dge ba'i bshes gnyen 'jam dbyangs
pa zhes bya ba zhig byung mod/ de nyid khri la mnga' gsol ma bgyis pas mkhan rab tu mi rtsi'o gsung ngo / /de ltar gong du smos pa'i mkhan brgyud rnying ma 'di rnams
ni/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos/ mkhan brgyud mgon po khyod kyi rnam 'phrul ston/ /zhes 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs nyid kyi sprul pa kho nar gsungs pa'i tshul yod do/
/mkhan brgyud snga ma bshad pa'i skabs so/ / | / /gnyis pa mkhan brgyud gsang ma ji ltar 'phel ba'i tshul

brjod par bya ste/ de yang dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ngo bo bu ston rin chen grub ces bya ba'i thams cad mkhyen pa chen po de nyid/ rnam thos sras kyi sprul pa'i zlos
gar nor 'dzin skyong ba'i dbang po sku zhang grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis smon lam dang mos dge phun tshogs kyi sgo nas dpal zhwa lu'i chos grwa chen po 'di nyid kyi khri
thog tu spyan drangs/ bdag nyid chen po gang gi 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi 'phrin las mu med pas rgyal ba'i bstan pa rin po che nam langs pa la nyi ma shar ba lta bu mdzad
de grub mtha' bu lugs zhes bya ba'i srol rmad du byung ba dar zhing rgyas nas/ gang gi gdan sar byon pa rnams la mkhan brgyud gsar ma zhes bya ba'i grags snyan dbyar
gyi rnga gsang srid rtse'i bar du ldir ba yin pa shes par bya'o/ /de la thams cad mkhyen pa'i mdzad tshul rag pa tsam ni gong du bstan zin mod/ 'dir rin chen bsod nams sengges
ngo mtshar gtam gyi rol mo nyi shu gcig tu sgrog pa yang 'di ltar ro/ / | rin chen byang chub sems kyi mdzad mnga' zhing / /'chad rtsod rtsom dang thos bsam bsgom
pa kun/ /ma lus lhan cig grub pa khyod min pa/ /gangs can ljongs 'dir sngon chad gzhan ma byung / /lo lnga lon tshe rang gi lhag pa'i lha/ /'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi dngos su
rjes bzung nas/ /'chad rtsod rtsom pa'i spobs pa mchog brnyes pa/ /gangs can ljongs 'dir sngon chad gzhan ma byung / /

bstan pa'i rtsa ba legs bzung 'dul ba yi/ /lung gi zhu chen gzhung brgya'i bshad srol dang / /lag len tshogs su bstan pa'i skye mched ni/ /ji snyed mdzad khyod dang mtshungs
sngon ma byung / /mtshan mo 'od gsal nyid las ma g.yos bzhin/ /ji ltar bzhed pa'i glegs bam la gzigs nas/ /nyin par de nyid gzhan la legs 'doms pa/ /gangs can ljongs 'dir
sngon chad gzhan ma byung / /ci 'dod dngos grub ma lus 'byung ba'i sar/ /sa bcu'i dbang phyug rgyal ba'i bstan bsrung mchog /rnam thos bu yi mda' lnga stsol ba 'di/ /gangs
can ljongs 'dir sngon chad gzhan ma byung / /sngon chad rang gi slob 'bangs dAn shi/ mngal gnas lha mig dag pas gsal bar gzigs/ /bar chad bdud las rgyal bar zhal bzhes
pa/ /gangs can ljongs 'dir sngon chad gzhan ma byung / /dus gsum rgyal ba ma lus bskyed pa'i yum/ /shes rab pha rol phyin pa'i lta ba'i gnad/ /'khrul med yum gyi lhums
su ngo sprod pa/ /gangs can ljongs 'dir sngon chad gzhan ma byung / /phyis 'byung rten cing 'brel ba 'byung la dgongs/ /dam rdzas snod kyi rin chen za ma tog /'khrul med
len dang yab sras mjal ba'i mdo/ /bsam bzhin 'chad pa sngon chad gzhan ma byung / /snga ma'i 'khrungs rabs gzigs nas sras rnams la/ /sngon chad phyogs 'dir yang yang son
pa rnams/ /ji snyed dran zhes dris dang dris pa'i lan/ /ngo mtshar 'di 'dra sngon chad gzhan ma byung / /mkhas mchog

mang po bod du byon na yang / /bser bus bskyod pa'i dar las byung ba'i sgras/ /ma 'ongs lung bstan phyi bzhin mthong ba ni/ /gangs can ljongs 'dir sngon chad gzhan ma byung
/ /yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i mnga' bdag gang de la/ /brgya phrag tsam gyi ring nas thos pa yis/ /sems med dung gi rang skad 'byin pa ni/ /gangs can ljongs 'dir sngon chad
gzhan ma byung / /phyi rgol dregs pas bstan pa'i gtso bo la/ /lta grub gsung ngag nan gyi dkrol ba'i tshe/ /gnyis ka 'khrul ba mi mnga' bka' stsol pa/ /gangs can ljongs 'dir
sngon chad gzhan ma byung / /chu bo'i 'jigs las skyobs phyir bcom ldan 'das/ /skyes mchog dam pa'i lam dang zab pa rnams/ /myur bar gyis zhes dngos su bskul byed pa/
/gangs can ljongs 'dir sngon chad gzhan ma byung / /stobs ldan gang gis bsgul bskyod mi nus pa'i/ /rdo ba las grub gdugs mdzes rdzu 'phrul gyi/ /nga la bdun srid 'phags pa'i
mchod rten gyi/ /rtse mor 'gel mdzad sngon chad gzhan ma byung / /mi phyed dad pa'i shugs 'char gtong ba pos/ /srog shing phul ba'i rten cing 'brel 'byung las/ /skyes
mchog dam pa lung bstan dbur dbyung ba/ /gangs can ljongs 'dir sngon chad gzhan ma byung / /'brom rje'i gdung 'dzin shAkya'i mtshan 'chang ba/ /dbon ras bdun gyi bar du
rnam thos bus/ /rjes 'dzin lung bstan skad cig mi g.yo bar/ /gangs can

ljongs 'dir sngon chad gzhan ma byung / /mdo khams phyogs nas skom nad chu 'dod pa/ /de nyid dpal ldan 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor du/ /rjes bzung dad pa'i rten bcas legs 'doms pa/
/gangs can ljongs 'dir sngon chad gzhan ma byung / /nyi ma'i zer dang mkha' lding dbang po las/ /brten nas rgyal ba'i zhing khams rab 'byams khams/ /smon pa'i gnas rnams
ji bzhin bgrod pa ni/ /gangs can ljongs 'dir sngon chad gzhan ma byung / /lta grub snying po mi pham mgon po la/ /zhus shing dag par 'khrul med rgyas btab nas/ /phyis
'byung 'dul bya'i log rtogs sel ba ni/ /gangs can ljongs 'dir sngon chad gzhan ma byung / /rgyud sde rgya mtsho'i dkyil 'khor ma lus pa/ /bsgrub pa'i chu rgyun bdud rtsi'i
byin rlabs nas/ /bskal brgya'i bar du snyigs mar mi 'gyur pa/ /gangs can ljongs 'dir sngon chad gzhan ma byung / /zhing gzhan gshegs tshe mi pham mgon po sogs/ /rgyal dang
rgyal sras mang po'i sku brnyan dang / /dbu nang ring bsrel phyur bur gtams gyur pa/ /gangs can ljongs 'dir sngon chad gzhan ma byung / /mgon po gang des rgyal ba'i bstan
pa la/ /mdzad pa'i tshul rnams mthong zhing thos pa yis/ /bcos min dad pas spu long rab tu g.yos/ /yang yang dran pas gsol 'debs 'di byas so/ /rgyal ba'i sras kyi rlabs
chen spyod pa rnams/ /su zhi gis kyang ma lus brjod mi nus/ /ji ltar rgya mtsho

che las chu thigs bzhin/ /bdag blos dpags la nyes gang bzod par gsol/ /gangs ri'i khrod byon mkhas pa gzhan dag las/ /ngo mtshar gtam gyi rol mo nyi shu gcig /ma sbas gsal
bar bsgrags pa stong gsum gyis/ /khor yug ri bo'i khongs las rgal gyur cig /grags pa'i rnga chen thos pa'i skye 'gro kun/ /mi shes ma rigs thib po'i gnyid sangs te/ /ji snyed
shes bya'i gnas rnams ji lta bar/ /mkhyen pa'i ye shes snang ba rgyas par shog /bdag kyang bu ram shing pa'i bstan pa la/ /mi nub rgyal mtshan srid mthar 'dzin pa dang
/ /thogs med dus nas brtse bas bskyangs pa yi/ /ma rnams phan bde'i lam la 'god par shog /ces pa 'di'ang chos rje nyid kyi rnam thar thun mongs ma yin pa'i bsdus don du
mthong nas 'dir bkod pa yin no/ de yang mkhas pa stag tshang lo tsA pa'i bzhed pa ltar na/ sangs rgyas chu mo phag la lhums su bzhugs/ shing pho byi ba'i lo la sku bltams/
dgung lo so drug pa sa mo phag la sangs rgyas/ bdun cu don brgyad pa lcags mo sbrul la dus 'khor gsung / brgyad cu pa chu mo lug la mya ngan las 'das te/ de nas lo nyis
stong chig brgya drug cu re bzhi 'das pa rab byung lnga pa'i rnam 'gyur zhes pa lcags pho stag gi lo chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa sku 'khrungs/ dgung lo sum cu so gcig
pa drag pa zhes pa lcags pho spre'u'i lo khri thog tu

phebs / drug cu re bdun pa gdong ngan zhes pa me pho spre'u'i lo gdan sa thugs sras lo tsA bar gtad/ bdun cu don lnga pa khro mo zhes pa shing pho 'brug la mya ngan las 'das
so/ /de yan la dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud gsung nas lo nyis stong nyis brgya zhe gcig song bar rje stag lo chen pos bzhed pa'i bstan rtsis su shes par bya'o// //de nyid
kyi gdanas dang po rgyal tshab thubs sras lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal rab byung lnga pa'i sa pho rta la sku 'khrungs/ dgung lo sum cu so dgu pa me spre dgun zla ra
ba'i tshes lnga la khri thog tu phebs/ gdan sa lo sum cu so gnyis bskyangs nas bdun cu don gcig pa sa pho 'brug lo zla ba bcu pa'i tshes gnyis kyi nyi ma nub mtshams la sku
gshegs/ / //gdan sa gnyis pa thams cad mkhyen pa grags pa rgyal mtshan rab byung drug pa'i shing mo sbrul la sku 'khrungs/ dgung lo nyi shu rtsa lnga pa sa mo sbrul lo
zla ba dang po'i gza' tshes dge bar khri thog tu phebs/ dgung lo bzhi bcu pa shing pho spre'u'i lo la mkhas grub sangs rgyas dpal rin la gdan sa gtad/ des lo brgyad mdzad
nas chu pho 'brug gi lo bya bral la thegs/ de nas yang rje nyid kyis dgung lo zhe dgu pa chu mo sbrul gyi lo khri thog tu bskyar ma phebs/ dgung lo bdun cu don drug pa
lcags pho spre'u'i lo la 'khrul zhig rje gdan sar bskos te brgyad cu gya bzhi pa sa pho 'brug lo smin drug zla ba'i tshes bco lnga la mya ngan las 'das so// //gdan sa

gsum pa rje mi la bzhad pa rdo rje'i rnam sprul du grags pa mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal rin gyi rnam thar sogs kyi yi ge zhib mo ni ma rnyed la/ 'on kyang mgur 'bum khrod kyi
kha 'thor tshan pa 'ga' mthong ba las brjod par bya ba 'di yin te/ de yang du ba mthong pa las/ me'i mtshan nyid rtogs nus pa bzhin no/ /de la rje 'di nyid gang du sku
'khrungs pa'i gnas yul dang / rigs rus yab yum sogs kyi khyad par 'chad rgyu mi snang yang rab byung drug pa'i me pho 'brug gi lo la sku 'khrungs par grags/ dgung lo nyi
shu rtsa dgu pa shing pho spre'u'i lo bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i khri thog tu phebs nas chos 'khor bskor/ de'i tshe nye gnas bsod nams grags pa la gsungs pa/ / / /gsan
dang nye gnas bsod nams grags/ /tshul 'chal ngan 'gror skye bar gsungs/ /bka' log bka' las 'das pa'i phyir/ /ngan song gsum du lhung gyur na/ /dal 'byor 'di ni rnyed par
dka'/ /da lta dal 'byor 'dzoms dus 'dir/ /tshul khrims gtsang ma bsrungs byas nas/ /phyi ma'i gtan sa bzungs shig ang / /chang ni phung khrol kun gyi gzhi/ /'di phyi'i
mdun ma stor bar byed/ /shes ldan nye gnas bsod nams grags/ /chang ni rnam par spongs shig ang / /zhes sogs dang / yang chos nyan pa'i slob ma rnams gnyid dang bred mo byad
pa gzigs nas gsungs pa/ / | //pha gsan gcig bla ma

rin po che/ /dgongs shig chos rje rin po che/ /spyir mgo nag mi la thugs rjes gzigs/ /sgos dus ngan gyi mi la byin gyis rlobs/ /chos dran bskul bgyis pa dgra ru ltas te/ /sems
dran 'dzin gyi thag pa rgyang du 'phen/ /rang dran tshad kyi spyod pa lag tu 'gal/ /rje dran mchog gi bla ma rin po che/ /spyir mgo nag mi la thugs rjes gzigs/ /zhes
sogs kyi mgur mdzad/ dgung lo sum cu so bdun pa chu pho 'brug gi lo la zhwa lu'i khri bshol nas la stod rgyal gyi rtsibs ril bya bral mdzad nas gshegs pas khra bo la'i rtser
rtogs ldan gnyis dang mjal nas skye 'chi'i 'jigs pa la 'tsher mi 'tsher gyi chos gtam byas nas dri ba dang bcas chos rje gar gshegs zhus pa la mgur gsungs pa/ / | //na
mo gu ru/ nga yar la 'gro yang la 'gro la stod phyogs la rang 'gro/ /spyi bo 'di ru bu ston chos rje snying ga ru mkhyen rab kyi dbang phyug /nga gzhas sam dga' mo zhig
byed pa'i dga' rogs su bu ston yab sras/ /nga gu yangs bde mo zhig byed pa'i rogs su bu ston yab sras/ /khyed phung po 'di la gces 'dzin gtsig ches na/ /skye 'chi la 'tsher
ba yang bden yong / /phung po 'di la ngan skyur zhig byas na/ /skye 'chi la 'tsher rgyu yang med do/ /zhes sogs mgur mdzad/ de nas 'om chung du slob dpon sangs rgyas
don grub sogs la phyag chen gyi 'khrid phog dus 'khrid la legs po byung bas thugs dgyes nas/ / //sems ye stong

nam mkha' yangs pa la/ /blo rnam rtog gi sprin dkar lang ma ling / /sprin byung pa de yang nam mkha'i dbyings nas byung / /sprin thim pa de yang nam mkha'i dbyings su thim/
/sprin nam mkha' las logs na med pa 'di/ /pha rgyal ba'i dgongs pa mthar thug yin/ /bu nyams su longs shig sgom chen kun/ /zhes sogs kyi mgur gsungs/ yang brag dmar spo
mthor sgrub pa mdzad skabs sgom chen pho mo 'ga' la gshed dmar spros med kyi 'khrid gnang / de nas la phyi gangs la 'byon gsung gin yod pa'i tshe dge bshes rnam pa gnyis
nyin mo thun gyi sgang la gnyid du song ba la bskul tshig 'di gsungs so/ / | / /rin chen 'dod dgu 'byung ba'i gter/ /mgon po mgon med kun gyis skyabs/ /dpal ldan bla ma bu
ston rje/ /rtag tu spyi bo'i gtsug gis mchod/ /brtag na snying rje chen po'i gnas/ /gzhig na 'gyur med dad pa can/ /mthong na kha khyer rkyang las mtho/ /bsgom na mtshar
po 'ga' zhig la/ /bsam na nges shes 'dren pa'i tshig /blangs na glu chung snyan pa'i tshig /'bral snang snying la phog pa'i tshig /bskul tshig rin chen 'phreng 'di smra/
/khyed gsan dang skal ldan dge bshes gnyis/ /bag med kyis ro nyal ma mdzad par/ /bag yod kyi rje la gsol ba thob/ /bag chags kyi sgrib pa sbyangs 'tshal lo/ /zhes sogs
mgur gsungs/ de nas la phyi gangs kyi ra bar gshegs nas gangs ches pas nye

gnas rnams kyis ldog par zhus pa la gsungs ngag / / /na mo gu ru/ pha drin can bla ma rin po che/ /rje 'gro ba'i mgon po thugs rje can/ /yid gdung ba'i sgo nas gsol ba 'debs/
/dus rgyun chad med par byin gyis rlobs/ /gangs chen gyi bgrod par dka' dang gcig /blo stobs kyi mdo phrug zhan dang gnyis/ /ra dwogs kyi 'khyag rom che dang gsum/ /bdag
'dzin gyi lcags sgrog dam dang bzhi/ /rnal 'byor pa ldog pa'i rtags bzhi yin/ /zhes sogs kyi mgur mdzad/ yang brag dmar spo mthor dgun bzhugs mdzad/ brin gyi yon bdag
pho mo rnams kyis bsnyen bkur bshams/ dge slong sangs rgyas na tsha dam pos zin pa la na tsha lam khyer gyi mgur gsungs pa/ rin chen gter gyur mgon po'i mchog /dpal ldan
bla ma bu ston mchod/ /dge slong nyon dang sangs rgyas la/ /brtse bas gdams pa tsig gsum smra/ /rting na na tsha kha na rlung / /dkar mo'i sa na 'khun zhing gda'/ /bla ma
dkon mchog mkhyen snyam pas/ /'bral med spyi bor sgom mdzad la/ /na dga' shi skyid thog 'gel gyis/ /gang byung legs la gtad par bya/ /gnod byed 'dre dang gdon bgegs tshogs/
/bla ma yi dam nyid du sgom/ /mos gus bskyed la gsol ba thob/ /byin rlabs dngos grub 'byur bar 'gyur/ /zhes sogs dang / yang la stod lho phyogs bdag po chen pos shel
dkar gyi chos dpon mdzad par phebs dgos pa'i gser yig pa byung dus chos dpon mi

mdzad par thugs thag bcad nas mgur gsungs pa// | /na mo gu ru/ dpal dam chos rin chen 'byung ba'i gnas/ /don bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa'i gtso/ /rje mkhas grub bu ston
zhabs la 'dud/ /bu rang la gros 'debs tshig gsum smra/ /blo thag chod kyi bya rgyal rgod po nga / /sems phyogs med kyi nam 'phangs spyod re ran/ /blo 'khris med kyi gshog
rtsal ngoms re ran/ /rgod po phyogs lhung gi rgyal 'dzin nye na gda'o/ /zhes sogs gsungs/ yang brgyad bskor du bzhugs dus bla ma chos rgyal gyis bdag la zhal gdams shig
dgos zhus pa la/ / | / /na mo gu ru/ dus gsum sangs rgyas ngo bo/ dgos 'dod 'byung pa'i nor bu/ /dpal ldan bla ma'i zhabs la/ /sgo gsum gus pas 'dod do/ /gsan dang bla
ma chos rgyal/ /thob dka'i dal 'byor thob cing / /mjal dka'i bstan dang mjal dus/ /chos la brtson par rig go /skyes phyin 'chi bar nges so/ /nam 'chi'i dus btab med do/ /'chi
tshe nges par phan pa/ /chos la 'bad 'bung thon cig /ces sogs gsungs/ yang gnas de nyid du dpon mo nyi zla bzang mos bdag sems med ma chen po lags pas chos dran pa'i
mgur zhig gnang bar zhu zhes zer ba la/ / | / /na mo gu ru/ 'gyur med bde chen bla ma'i zhabs la/ /dmigs med ngang nas phyag 'tshal mchod do/ /sems med la brtse ba'i snying
gtam/ /brjod

med ngang nas tshig gsum smra'o/ /bla ma'i dpon mi nyi zla bzang mo/ /thob dka'i dal 'byor mi lus thob cing / /mjal dka'i chos dang mjal dus dpon mo/ /sems med ma khyod sems
la ltos shig /brgya byin lta bu'i mig stong ldan pa/ /sems nyid ma mthong long ba yin no/ /tshangs pa lta bu'i dpung nged ldan yang / /rang rgyud ma thul dbang med yin
no/ /rnam thos bu 'dra'i nor dang ldan yang / /rang ngo ma shes dbul po yin no/ /zhes sogs dang yang dag bsnyen ma bkra shis chos 'dzoms dang dge bsnyen ma rdo rje dpal gnyis
kyis tshom bu dmar 'khrid zhus pas/ de 'phral dmigs pa phog nas tshar pa mdzad pa la/ lags sam bdag cag yun ring du thogs rtsis byas pa lags zhus pa la mgur 'di gsungs
so/ / //na mo khyed dang ldan sgom ma spun gnyis kyis/ chos zab mo dmar khrid zhu ba la/ /mi rgan dar drung du 'ong pa yin/ /'khrid zhus ma thag tu grol ba yin/ /ngo sprad
ma thag tu 'phrod pa yin/ /da 'gro snying 'dod na phyin pa drag /phyis yul du dran 'dzin 'khor mar thongs/ /rang thugs rje chen po'i spyi gtsug tu/ /pha drin can rtsa
ba'i bla ma la/ /yid gdung shugs drag po'i mos gus kyis/ /dus rgyun chad med par gsol ba thob/ /gnas gang du bsdad kyang gzhal yas khang / /grogs su dang 'grogs kyang yi
dam lha/ /las ci byed gzhan don 'gyur ba na/ /phyi bskyed rim sgom pa'i khyad chos yin/ /

blo rnam rtog byung na rang zhal ltos/ /sgra gang grags yi ge drug pa'i sgra/ /de kun gyis bgrang ba'i mos pa gyis/ /sngags yi ge 'bru gsum gsang ba yis/ /zas gang bza' bdud
rtsir bsgyur ba dang / /gos gang byon lha yi li/ /yul gang snang lha yi gzhal yas khang / /de kun la tshogs su 'dul bar gyis/ /gnyid 'od gsal 'char ba'i dran 'dzin dang
/ /sems gong du 'pho ba'i gdams ngag dang / /rjes bar do'i gdams pa legs par skyod/ /don tshangs la 'grig pa'i gdams ngag yin/ /lar 'chi ba 'ong ngo 'a dzi dzi/ /de byung
dus ci byed bsam mno thong / /khyed dad ldan sgom ma spun gnyis la/ /sems brtse ba'i sgo nas gdams pa yin/ /de sems la zhog la nyams len 'bungs/ /zhes gsungs/ /yang yon
bdag mkha' 'gro skyong gis gshed dmar spros med kyi 'khrid zhus nas dmigs rim gyi mgur gsungs pa dang / btsun chung shAkya gzhon nu yul du phyin nas 'khor ba la/ / | dran
mchog bla ma rnams dang / /yang dgos bu ston chen po/ /sgo gsum gus pas mchod do/ /spyi gtsug rgyan du bzhugs shig /ma phod bu la brtse bas/ /snying gtam tshig gsum smra'o/
/zhes sogs mgur gsungs/ yang brag dmar spo mthor sgom chen pa rnams la/ / | mtshan ldan bla ma rin po che/ /mi nub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin/ /'gro ba'i ma rig mun
pa sel/ /mkhas grub bu

ston zhabs la 'dud/ /spyi gtsug rgyan du bzhugs su gsol/ /dad ldan sgom chen pho mo kun/ /phyag rgya chen po'i skyong lugs 'di/ /blo 'das brjod par dka' lags na/ /ma sbas lhag
par bshad lags kyi/ /yengs med rna ba gtod par mdzod/ /ces sogs phyag rgya chen po'i 'khrid mdzad nas ngo sprod kyi mgur gsungs/ yang la phyi gangs kyi ra bar gshags
nas de na 'dug pa'i rtogs ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa rang yul la 'gro ba la/ / / /mkha' 'gros lung bstan dben pa'i gnas/ /grub thob kyi bzhugs gnas byin rlabs can/ /gnas la phyi
gangs la bsgom pa de/ /khyed bla ma chos rgyal ma lags sam/ /gnas do med gangs kyi ra ba ru/ /snying po'i don la rtse gcig gis/ /bsgrub pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzugs lugs kyis/
/de bla ma chos rgyal los kyang lags/ /pho dka' spyad pa'i snying rus can/ /rje btsun gyis rjes bzung skal ldan khyed/ /dgra 'phro rgod kyi dbang du ma shor bar/ /da
dung la phyi'i gnas la bzhugs/ /da dung bka' brgyud kyi gdan sa bzung / /da dung sgrub pa'i rgyal mtshan tshugs/ /thabs shes zung 'brel gyi rang rtsal ngoms gyin bzhugs/
/'tha' rgyas kyi bu slob skyong gin bzhugs/ /zhes sogs gdan mnan gyi mgur gsungs/ yang mtsho chen po kha dog shin tu nag pa zhig lam du gzigs nas/ / / /mtsho mo khyod kha
dog nag pa ci/ /sngar las ngan bsags pa'i gnong yod dam/ /zhes sogs mgur gsungs

yang pa bong gcig gi 'gram du gsang chab tshag gin bzhugs pa la/ dge bshes kun dga' dpal gyis/ btsun ma skal bzang slebs byung zhus pas/ / | bu nyon cig dge bshes kun dga'
dpal/ /rgyu song gi 'bras bu 'byung pa de/ /tshangs pas kyang bzlog par ma nus so/ /bu cal col ma mang sems la bltos/ /nga lus ni lha sku ngag gi sngags/ /yid ni phyag rgya
chen po'i ngang / /pag tsha bya yod dam yin/ /btsun ma skal bzang yong na'ang yong du chug /ces sogs mgur gsungs/ yang rgyal ba yang dgon pa chen po'i sgrub gnas shrI
gnam sding gi gdan sa shin tu gnyan pas gdan sar phebs tshad de 'phral sku gshegs nas gdan sa stong pas rje nyid kyi gdan sa mdzad pa zhal gyis bzhes nas shrI gnam sding
gi sgrub gnas bzung pas/ bdag po chen po'i zhal nas kyang / /spyang ki'i tshang du lu gu 'khyol lo/ /ci 'dra 'ong lta'o zhes dang / lho khri skor gyi mi thams cad kha mthun
par gnam sding bla ma'i dur sa bya ba yin/ zhwa lu chos rje khong sku tshe rings nas dur sar phebs pa yin yod zer ba gsan nas/ / / /kun mkhyen chos kyi rje la/ mos gus
gdung shugs drag pos rtag tu skyabs su mchi'o/ /rgyun du thugs rjes bzungs shig /nga'i blo phugs 'di chos rje la btod do/ /'gyod med kyi bde mo zhig byung pa/ /gang byung
legs pa la btod do/ /khris med kyi bde mo zhig byung pa/ /zhes sogs bde

mo bcu gcig gi mgur gsungs/ de lta bu'i tshul gyis bstan 'gro'i don rlabs po che mdzad pa zhig ste/ mgur tshom las gleng bar 'os pa ni/ re zhig de tsam mo/ gzhan yang shrI
gnam sding du 'dra sku ngo mtshar ba dang / zhwa lu ri phug tu gzigs mal sku 'dra dngos su byon pa 'dra ba bzhengs/ phyi rten pad spungs mchod rten yang gtsigs/ /nang rten
la thub pa'i dbang po'i gser sku lo brgyad pa'i tshad tsam yod pa zhwa lu'i gtsug lag khang gi sgo gsum lha khang na bzhugs so/ /zhes bya ba yang lo rgyus kyi yi ge kha
cig las 'byung ngo / /gdan sa bzhi pa 'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan rab byung bdun pa'i sa mo yos la sku 'khrungs/ dgung lo bzhi bcu zhe gnyis pa lcags spre rgyal
zla'i tshes drug la khri thog tu phebs/ lo nyi shu rtsa bdun khri thog tu bzhugs/ dgung lo drug cu re brgyad pa me khyi lo gdan sa chos grub dpal bzang la gtad/ bdun cu
don lnga pa chu khyi hor zla bcu gcig pa'i nyi shu bdun gyi tho rangs bsam sdings ri khrod du sku gshegs/ / | gdan sa lnga pa kun mkhyen chos grub dpal bzang po rab byung
bdun pa'i shing pho rta la sku 'khrungs/ dgung lo lnga bcu nga gsum pa me khyi rgyal zla'i tshes bcu la khri thog tu phebs/ gdan sar lo bcu bdun bzhugs nas dgung lo drug
cu re dgu pa/ chu pho stag gi lo tha skar zla ba'i nyer gcig gi nyi ma nub mtshams su sku gshegs/ gzims mal sku 'dra yang bzhengs

so / / | gdan sa drug pa 'jam dbyangs bshes gnyen bzang po rgyal mtshan pa/ rab byung bdun pa'i shing pho rta la sku 'khrungs/ kun mkhyen chos grub dpal bzang dang dgung lo
cig yin dgung lo bdun cu bzhes pa/ chu mo yos lo rgyal gyi zla ba'i tshes bco lnga'i nyin khri thog tu phebs nas lo bcu gcig bshags/ dgung lo brgyad cu pa chu mo glang gi
lo/ /hor zla drug pa chu stod kyi nya ba'i tshes bcu la sku gshegs so/ / | / /gdan sa bdun pa skyo ston rig 'dzin rgyal po rab byung bdun pa'i me mo sbrul la sku 'khrungs/
dgung lo lnga bcu nga brgyad pa shing pho stag gi lo/ sa ga zla ba'i tshes bco brgyad la khri thog tu phebs/ gdan sar lo bcu bzhi bzhugs nas dgung lo bdun cu don gcig
pa me mo yos la mkhan chen dkon mchog tshul khrims la gdan sa gtad/ don bzhi pa lcags pho rta'i lo hor zla bcu gcig pa'i tshes gsum la sku gshegs so/ /gdan sa brgyad pa
mkhan chen dkon mchog tshul khrims pa rab byung bdun pa'i shing mo glang lo sku 'khrungs/ dgung lo drug cu re gsum pa me yos mgo zla'i tshes bco lnga la khri thog tu phebs/
gdan sar lo ngo brgyad bzhugs nas dgung lo bdun cu pa shing khyi lo khri bshol nas bdun cu don gsum pa la sku gshegs/ mkhan chen 'di dpal 'khor chos sde'i mkhan po sogs
kyang mdzad/ grub mtha' sa lugs shas che/ rgyal ba sgo ru pa

kun dga' legs pa sogs slob ma mkhas btsun bzang gsum dang ldan pa mang du byung ngo / / | /gdan sa dgu pa lo chen thams cad mkhyen pa rin chen chos skyong bzang po rab byung
bdun pa'i lcags mo bya'i lo la sku 'khrungs/ dgung lo bdun cu don bzhi pa/ shing pho khyi lo smin drug zla ba'i nyi shu gcig la khri thog tu phebs/ gdan sar lo bcu gcig
bzhugs nas brgyad cu gya bzhi pa shing pho spre'u'i lo skyo ston bsod nams rgyal mtshan la gdan sa gtad/ dgung lo brgyad cu rgya brgyad pa sa pho byi ba'i lo grwa tshang
du sku gshegs so/ / | /gdan sa bcu pa skyo ston rin po che bsod nams rgyal mtshan rab byung brgyad pa'i chu mo glang gi lo la sku 'khrungs/ dgung lo sum cu so gnyis pa shing
spre chu stod zla ba'i tshes bcu bdun la khri thog tu phebs/ gdan sar lo bcu bzhi bzhugs nas dgung lo bzhi bcu zhe lnga pa me mo bya'i lo lha btsun rin po che la gdan
sa gtad do/ | /gdan sa bcu gcig pa lha'i btsun pa blo bzang bstan pa dpal bzang po ni/ mnga' ris su lha btsad po'i gdung brgyud du rab byung brgyad pa'i lcags mo yos la
sku 'khrungs/ dgung lo drug cu re bdun pa me mo bya'i lo/ /hor zla lnga pa'i tshes bcu bdun la khri thog tu phebs/ 'di mtshan gcig la paN chen nub ra ba yang zer/zhwa lu'i
mkhan po ma mdzad pa'i gong la rje dge 'dun rgya mtshos bkra shis lhun po'i gdan sa gshol nas 'di la bskos pas paN chen zhes gragsla mdzad pa rnam thar rgyas pa'ang mnga'
ris phyogs na yod pa'i ngag bgros tsam zhig thos mod skabs 'dir dpe lag tu ma 'byor ro/ / / /

gdan sa bcu gnyis pa mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs dpal bzang po dgung lo gang yin ma shes rung rab byung dgu pa'i chu mo yos kyi thog tu phebs/ gdan sar lo bcu gcig bzhugs nas shing
pho stag gi lo ri phug tu sku gshegs/ / gdan sa bcu gsum pa tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po ni rab byung brgyad pa'i chu pho khyi'i lo sku 'khrungs/ dgung lo lnga bcu nga
bzhi pa shing mo yos la khri thog tu phebs/ drug cu re lnga pa me pho stag gi lo/ gro zhun zla ba'i tshes bco lnga'i nyin 'dar stod grang mo cher sku gshegs/ / gdan sa
bcu bzhi pa 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ni/ rab byung dgu pa'i shing pho spre'u'i lo la sku 'khrungs/ dgung lo sum cu so
drug pa sa mo lug gi lo hor zla drug pa'i tshes gcig rgyal phur gyi 'grub sbyor yod pa'i nyin khri thog tu phebs/ gdan sar lo dgu bzhugs nas dgung lo bzhi bcu nye lnga
pa sa pho 'brug gi lo/ /hor zla lnga pa'i nyer gcig la bo dong phun tshogs rab brtan gyi gzim chung du sku gshegs/ / | gdan sa bco lnga pa mkhan chen jo gdan bsod nams dbang
po ni/ sku gzhon nu nas sde snod dang rgyud sde du ma la thos bsam mthil phyin pa ma zad/ tshar chen yab sras sogs bla ma mang du bsten/ jo gdan mkhan po rgyun ring mdzad
pa'i mthar rab byung bcu pa'i sa mo sbrul gyi lo rgyal gyi zla ba'i nang dpal zhwa lu'i khri

thog tu phebs/ 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum sogs kyis bstan pa la phyag bris che ba gnang / mdzad pa mtha' ma ri phug bla brang du bstan pa'i sku gdung rdo'i 'bum pa chung ngu da
lta 'ja' 'od 'bum pa'i 'khris na yod/ / /gdan sa bcu drug pa chos rje dkon mchog dpal ldan ni/ yab 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog lhun grub gyi gcung po lha mo dar dang / yum ngor
chen rdo rje 'chang gi dbon rigs dpal ldan bu dga'i sras su mi zad pa zhes pa me pho khyi'i lo sa skya'i gnyan kang gsar du sku 'khrungs/ mtshan la tshe brtan don grub
ces gsol/ dgung lo bcu gsum pa la e waM du phebs nas rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mkhan po dang / chos rje dge legs bshes gnyen pas las slob mdzad de rab tu byung / bcu
drug pa la 'bras yul skyed tshal du phebs/ dgung lo nyer bzhi'i bar bzhugs nas kun mkhyen shes rab 'od zer las mtshan nyid kyi bslab sbyang mthar phyin mdzad/ de nas sa
skyar rnam gzhag rgya chen yang mdzad de slar dgung lo nyer dgu la mkhan po sngar gyi dkon mchog lhun grub dang / las slob 'jam dbyangs sher 'od sogs dge 'dun grangs tshang
ba'i dbus su bsnyen par rdzogs/ gong du smos pa'i mkhan slob de rnams dang / rje sangs rgyas sengge/ sngags 'chang bstan pa'i nyi ma/ byang sems dkon rgyal/ spyan snga
dkon mchog rgya mtsho sogs las thos pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol du son par mdzad nas e waM gzims khang phrug gur bzhugs nas sgrub pa la

brtson / dgung lo sum cu so grangs nas 'chad nyan smar ba gnang / sa mo sbrul lo snon zla pa'i tshes gsum la e waM chos ldan gyi mkhan thog tu mnga' gsol/ de skabs dgung lo
bzhi bcu zhe bzhir phebs shing lo de'i dbyar chos sogs gnang nas mdo mkhar du chos rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho la gsung ngag sogs gsan/ de nas e waM gtso gyur gyis/ 'bring
mtshams stod smad/ skyed tshal gong / sa skya/ thub bstan yangs can/ thub bstan rnam rgyal/ rtsed gdong sogs su byon nas skye bo mang po smin grol la bkod/ dgung lo drug
cu re gnyis pa me mo phag gi lo dpal zhwa lu gser khang gi khri thog tu phebs/ ri mthil gnyis su bka' chos sogs bstan pa'i bya ba rgya cher mdzad/ 'chad pa dang rtsod pa'i
sgo nas gzhan phan mngon gsal du gyur/ rtsom pa'i phreng ba bka' 'bum dkar chag na gsal ba ltar ro/ /dgung lo drug cu re lnga pa lcags pho stag gi lo 'khrum gyi zla ba'i
tshes gnyis kyi srod char sku gshegs/ /gdan sa bcu bdun pa byams pa bsod nams dpa' bo ni/ 'jam dbyangs 'khon gyi gdung brgyud dri ma med par yab sngags 'chang chos kyi
rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen dang / yum rje btsun thugs rje'i bdag mo'i sras su rab byung dgu ba'i sa mo yug gi la la sku 'khrungs/ sku gzhon nu nas rab byung dang
phyis rim gyis bsnyen rdzogs sogs mdzad/ yab rje sngags

'chang chen po dang rtsed gdong gdung brgyud zhal ngo / shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ lo pa spyan snga sogs bla ma mang du bsten nas gsan bsam mthar phyin pa gnang /
rje dkon mchog dpal ldan la rdo rje 'phreng ba sogs bka' chos mang ba gsan/ kha'u bskyed lhas dang / bya 'gyur sogs su thugs dam bsgrub pa rgyun ring ba mdzad/ che ba'i
yon tan slob dpon chen po padma 'byung gnas kyi sprul par grags/ 'das ma 'ong gi bka' lung phal cher thog tu 'khel ba sogs mngon shes thogs med mnga'/ sa skya/ rtsed gdong
/ shab dge sdings gtso gyur gyi gnas mang por 'chad spel dang gzhan phan kho na mdzad/ dbus gnas la phebs nas yar klung bkra shis chos sde'i mkhan chen gzhon nu blo gros
la tshar lugs kyi chos bka' mang ba gsan lcags stod du phebs skabs mkhan chen 'jam mgon lhun grub pa la ne gu chos drug mdor bsdus pa zhig gsan/ dgung lo sum cu so gsum
pa lcags mo yos bu'i lo zhawa lu ri mthil gyi khri la mnga' gsol/ ri phug byang gling bla brang du rab byung bsnyen rdzogs ci rigs sogs 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyis bstan
pa'i sgron me mdzad/ de skabs zhwa khri bzlos mtshams su gyur pas khri khang gnas kyis rje nyid la khri 'bul ma phul bar sde srid gtsang gis bka' nan byon pa'i lo rgyus
kyang snang / bstan pa ris med nas dar dgos pa yin zhes sa zhal gnyis kyi grub mtha'i phyogs

zhen kho na yang mi mdzad/ shugs rgyud byang sems zhi dul chen ni chos lugs ris med nas skyong ba mdzad pas lho 'brug pa sogs kyang bka' 'bangs su dam bca' zhing gzhan yang
karma dge lugs sogs dad mos che/ nag rtsis pa'i lam 'phos cher ba'i dbang du byas nas dgung lo drug cu re gsum pa lcags mo bya'i lo/ /hor zla bcu gnyis ba'i dmar phyogs
kyi tshes bcu bzhi la sku gshegs/ / gdan sa bco brgyad par 'dir 'jam dbyangs dbon chen dbang phyug rab brtan la sde srid nas bka' phebs te gza' tshes bzang ba'i nyin btsun
gsar rnams la rab byung gi sdom pa mkhan po'i khri thog nas stsal rung / tshong 'dus sde rgyas pa sogs drung 'khor 'gas sde srid gtsang la chos rje gnas gsar pa khongs
la stobs 'byor tsam med lags pas/ sa skya bdag chen zhwa lu mkhan po la bskos pa'i shul du 'bum chung de 'dra bskos nas sde srid rin po che'i mtshan don la bzhad gad kyi
rgyu byed ces gleng mo btang pas/ sde pa gtsang pa thugs 'gyur nas ri phug dbu mdzad chen mo'i gdan sar bskyar ma phebs tu bcug go zhes grag la/ de'i phyir mkhan rab tu bgrang
ngam dpyad do/ / / /gdan sa bcu dgu pa sku zhang rin po chen mkha' chos ldan ni/ lce gdung dri ma med pa'i brgyud du 'khrungs/ brang ti paN chen gyi rab byung slob
bu yin nam sems/

nges gsal ma mthong / ri phug gi rtsa grwa mdzad nas mkhas grub rin chen sangs rgyas tshe dpal/ sku zhang chos rje dge slong rin po che/ sku drung chen po dpal ldan chos bzang
/ rtse chen dpon po ba ku sA li pa/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ byams pa bsod nams dbang po sogs bla ma mang ba bsten/ rab byung bcu pa'i blo ngan zhes pa lcags
mo byi lo/ /dpal zhwa lu'i khri thog tu phebs/ gdan sar lo ngo dgu bzhugs nas dpal rtse dbyings gsum sogs sogs rgyud sde rab tu mang po'i dbang lung man ngag gi chos
'khor bskor/ rin sding grwa tshang gi 'du khang rab gnas la phebs nas nyang stod yul gyi skye bo mang po'i don mdzad/ 'dar du phebs nas rnam rgyal stag rtse'i zhal ngo rnams
dang mjal 'phrad gnang / slob bshad nor bu'i gling du rje klu sgrub rgya mtsho la gshed dmar spros med kyi 'khrid sogs gsan/ stod phyogs su snga phyir gzhan don rgya
che ba mdzad nas sa mo sbrul gyi lo nags pa zla ba la la stod du sku gshegs so/ / gdan sa nyi shu pa shar chen byams pa shes rab 'byung gnas ni/ rigs phun sum tshogs pa
bdag chen shar pa'i gdung brgyud byang chub sems dpa' kun dga' dpal ldan dang / yam nang so shar phyogs nas kyi sras mo padma tshe ring gnyis la sras lcam sring bzhi 'khrungs
pa'i che ba rje 'di nyid yin te/ de yang rab byung bcu pa'i me pho spre'u'i lo/ /bzhad kyi khyel zhes par sku 'khrungs

dgung lo brgyad la khu bo bdag chen byams pa kun ga' bkra shis kyi mkhan po dang / rgya mtsho bla ma dkon mchog rgya mtshos las slob mdzad nas rab tu byung / khu bo rin po
che'i drung du thugs gnyer gsan sbyong smar ba gnang ste dgung lo nyer gcig pa la rtsed gdong phyogs las rnam rgyal gyi pho brang du phebs/ khri chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun
grub las bsnyen par rdzogs/ mkhan slob de rnams dang gzhan yang mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ lo pa spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ a mes zhabs kun dga' bsod nams sogs
bsten nas rim pas chos kyi gsan pa rgya cher mdzad/ mkhas btsun bzang gsum gyi dbang phyug tu gyur/ bdag nyid chen po jo bo dpal ldan a ti sha'i rnam 'phrul du grags/ dgung
lo sum cur phebs pa sing mo glang gi lo hor zla gsum pa'i rgyal ba ga sum pa'i tshes la e waM chos ldan gyi chos khrir 'khod/ gdan sa lo nyer brgyad mdzad/ dgung lo so
lnga pa rab byung bcu gcig pa'i rab myos zhes pa lcags pho rta'i lo/ dpal zhwa lu'i khri thog tu phebs/ gdan sa gnyis su 'chad nyan la brtson pa'i ngos/ dgung lo lnga bcu
nga brgyad du phebs pa rnam rgyal zhes pa chu mo sbrul gyi lo/ /cho 'phrul zla ba'i nyer gcig la sku gshegs/ phyis sku gshegs nas nang rten dang gzims mal sku 'dra sogs
ngor gyi lam zab lha khang sogs su bzhengs so/ gdan

pa nyer gcig pa paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i sku gsung thugs kyi mdad pa rgya mtsho lta bu las chu thigs ces zhig 'dir blangs
nas brjod par bya'o/ /de yang rje 'di nyid sngon bdag cag gi ston pa'i spyan sngar gnas brtan rab 'byor dang / sham bha la'i rigs ldan nyer lnga'i thog ma rigs ldan 'jam
dpal grags pa sogs su sku'i skye ba bzhes tshul gyi 'khrungs rab thub mong dang thun mong ma yin pa slob dpon padma 'byung gnas/ mnyam med dIbaM ka ra/ chos rgyal dwags
po lha rje sogs dang thugs rgyud gcig tshul gyi rim pa dag gzhan du shes par bya la/ 'di nyid du 'khrungs pa'i yul ni lhan drug brgya zhes bya bar/ sba ye shes dbang po
dang / g.yag sde paN chen/ dben sa bla ma sangs rgyas ye shes sogs dam pa du ma 'khrungs pa'i brgyud du yab dpon tshang tsha ring dpal 'byorar dang / yam mtsho rgyal gnyis
kyi sras su rab byung bcu pa'i rab myos zhes pa lcags pho rta'i lo la sku bltams/ mtshan chos rgyal dpal ldan bzang po zhes btags/ dgung lo gsum pa'i skabs nyid kyi mes
po 'tshe byed cig yod pa des mtshan brjod zhal 'don gnang ba sogs gsan nas bslab ma dgos par mkhyen gshis dgang lo lnga nas nyin re bzhin du mtshan brjod tshar lnga re 'don
pa mdzad/ gzhan yang sman bla dang rdo rje gcod pa sogs gzigs pa tsam gyis thugs su chud nas zhal 'don du spobs/

dben dgon pa'i dge slong dag lhan drug brgyar byon pa na gzhan gyi bkag kyang ma thub par de dag gi gam du phebs nas tshogs 'don rnams gnang pas rje sangs rgyas ye shes kyi
dben sa chen po blo bzang don grub kyi sku skyer thag bcad de spyan gyi 'bras bu ltar bskyangs/ dgung lo bdun lon pa'i dus tshems gsar pa brjes pa'i rkyen gyis thugs rgyud
la mi rtag pa rang 'khrungs su byung zhing gsol ba bzhes 'phro tshun chad ngan sprang dang / khyi dang byi'u sogs la ster ba mdzad/ dgung lo bcu gsum pa chu pho rta'i
lo la dben dgon du phebs/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas ye shes kyi drung du rab tu byung zhing dge tshul gyi sdom pa bzhes/ mtshan blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po
zhes gsol/ dpal ri bo dge ldan pa'i zab chos dben sa snyan brgyud du grags pa rnams rje sangs rgyas ye shes la rim gyis gsan/ de dag gi tshe rang gzhan gyi 'byung 'gyur
mang po lung ston pa dang mdo sngags kyi chos gang la yang thogs pa med par sngon gyi dam pa so so'i bzhed srol dang bcas pa gsungs pa kun yid ches te rje dben sa pa chen
po'i sprul sku yin dag go zhes sgrog cing dge 'dun 'dus pa rgya mtsho'i dbus su sengge'i khri la bkod/ rje sangs rgyas ye shes kyis me tog gtor/ de'i tshe nam mkha' las
kyang me tog gi char babs/ dgung lo bcu bzhi'i dus lha mo dbyangs can ma la bstod pa lha'i glu dbyangs

zhes bya ba dang / bcu drug pa la slob dpon zhi ba lha'i rtogs brjod padma dkar po'i 'phreng ba sogs snyan tshig gi sbyor ba phun sum tshogs pa'i rtsom pa'ang mang du mdzad/
'dul ba'i gleng 'bum chen mo dang lam rim che chung sogs thugs 'dzin gnang ste so thar dang byang sems kyi bcas pa phra zhing phra ba'i bar thams cad la spang blang tshul
bzhin du mdzad/ dgung lo bco brgyad pa me mo phag gi lo bkra shis lhun por phebs nas dka' chen bzhi la sbyangs pa mthar phyin pa gnang ste rnam 'grel la spyi bskyur bzhes/
dgung lo nyer gnyis pa lcags mo yos kyi lo paN chen dam chos yar 'phel las bsnyen par rdzogs nas rim gyis yul dbus kyi ljongs su phebs/ jo shaka rnam gnyis kyi drung
du smon lam rgya cher mdzad pas dag pa'i gzigs snang bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung ri bo dge ldan sogs su phebs nas dga' chen bzhi la dam bca' mdzad cing rgol ba ngan pa thams
cad sun phyung / slar yang gtsang du phebs nas skal ldan gyi slob ma mang por chos kyi dga' ston 'gyed pa dang rje sangs rgyas ye shes kyi sku gdung gi bya ba rnams
grub par mdzad nas da ni skye ba 'di la bltos pa'i za zir dang 'dres pa'i kun tu spyod pa'i mjug de tsam gyis bsdus/ rtse gcig tu dben pa'i ri sul bsten nas sgrub pa la nan
tan du bya'o dgongs pa na/ tho rangs mnal lam du rje rin po che btsong kha ba mdun gyi nam mkhar byon nas/ rang dang gzhan la phan pa'i phyir/ /thos pas ngoms par

mi bya ste/ /sa gsum brnyes pa'i sems dpa' yang / /thos pas ngoms pa med la ltos/ /zhes thos bsam la ched du bskul ba gzigs nas re zhig sngar ma gsan pa'i dbang lung man ngag
sogs thugs rtsol bskyed de gsan sbyang gnang / skabs shig brag skya'o rdo rje'i pho brang du phebs nas rlung dang 'khrul 'khor bcud len sogs la sbyongs mdzad pas sku la
na bza' cher gsol mi dgos pa dang bcud len la gdengs thob/ de nas sde srid lhun po rtse pa sogs nas nan gyi zhus te gangs can chos 'phel gyi gdan sar phebs/ der gtsug lag
khag nyams pa gso ba dang chos dang zang zing gi sgo nas phyogs de'i gdul bya rnams bde ba la bkod cing yid mchog tu rang ba mdzad/ de rjes sngon gyi thugs bskyed dang
smon lam dus la babs pas bkra shis lhun po'i gdan sar phebs dgos pa'i zhu ba byung nas rim gyis rgyal ba dge 'dun grub kyis dge'i khri la mnga' gsol/ /zhwa ser sogs thams
cad kyi bstan pa'i bdag por gyur nas paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa zhes pa'i snyan grags kyi rgya gar rgya nag thams cad du khyab par gyur to/ /dbus su phebs nas chos grwa
chen po dpal ldan 'bras spungs dge ldan rnam par rgyal ba'i gling dang / gzhan yang shangs ri bo dge 'phel sogs dgon khag du ma'i zhal 'dzin mdzad nas gnas de dang de
dag tu chos kyi 'khor lo rgya chen po bskor/ dga' ldan gser gdung gi steng du

gser zangs kyi rgya phibs dang lha sa'i jo bo rang byon lnga ldan gyi bzhugs gnas la gser thogs gsar bskrun mdzad cing / gangs ri chen po ti se sogs gnas chen khyad par can
du ma'ang zhabs kyis bcags nas mthong thos dran reg gi sems can mang po 'khor ba mtha' can du mdzad/ khyad par lho mon gyi yul grur phebs nas rtogs ldan gyi dmag bshams
nas mi sha len pa'i gdug rtsub can gyi spyod pa byed pa'i kla klo thams cad la dngos pa'i sbyin pa sngon du 'gro bas rje nyid kyi phyag phreng mgo thog tu 'jog pa gnang zhing
mi sha mi len pa'i mna' skyol gsungs pa tsam gyis thams cad rang dbang med par bka' bzhin spyi bos bsgrubs te skye bo khri khrag mang po'i srog skyob mdzad pa sogs rnam
par dkar pa'i mdzad 'phrin ni re re bzhin bgrang bar mi 'byod pa yin no/ dgung lo sum cu so bzhi ba mdzes byed ces pa chu mo yos kyi lo bkra shis lhun po'i cho 'phrul
smon lam 'dzugs pa mdzad/ dgung lo bzhi bcu zhe bzhi pa bzhes pa sa mo bya'i lo ngo mtshar ba'i matsan ltas bzang pos bskul nas bkra shis lhun po'i gsang sngags rgyud pa
grwa tsang 'debs pa mdzad cing 'grel pa bzhi bsgrags sogs rje rin po che'i sngags chog rnams dar bar mdzad/ gzhan yang dbus gtsang gi ljongs su 'chad nyan sogs bstan pa'i
bya ba rgya chen po mdzad cing rgyal dbang mchog gi sprul pa'i sku yon rgya mtsho la

bka' chos 'bul ba dang / de nyid sku gshegs nas gong sa kun gzigs rin po che ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho la sprul sku ngos 'dzin gnang nas rab byung bsnyen rdzogs kyi
bar thams cad mdzad/ dgung lo bdun cu don gsum pa sna tshogs zhes pa chu pho rta'i lo chu stod zla ba'i tshes gsum la dpal zhwa lu gser khang gi chos grwa chen po 'di nyid
kyi seng ge'i khri la phebs/ tshogs su khri ston 'gyed sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang chos sde'i mnga' zhabs pa rnams la'ang ston mo 'bru 'gyed sogs gnang bas/ zhwa lu
pa kun dzambha la'i khyim du bcug gda' zer glu byed pa byung skad/ zhwa lu ri mthil gyi dge 'dun tshogs yongs la rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i bla
ma'i rnal 'byor dang 'khrungs rabs gsol 'debs thub dbang zhal pang ma bcas kyi lung thog ma'i chos 'bral du stsal/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i yum gyi phyi rten ri phug
gi sku 'bum mthong grol chen mo la sngon rdo'i gdugs la rdo'i ganyji ras spras pa yod pa la/ snye mdo sngags 'chang chen po shAkya dpal gyi slob ma phyogs glang gi dgra
phyogs su thob phab pa lam du ma song ba'i skyon gyis thog nam mkhar shor ba rdo'i tog la phog nas ganyji rags shing 'khyoms pas grum chagchog tu gyur te/ 'di skabs lhung
du nye ba yod pas rje nyid kyi mnal lam du paNDi ta bgres po gzi brjid can zhig byon nas nged kyi mchod rten la khyod kyis rim gro gyis shig ces bskul

ba gzigs pa yang chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston nyid kyis bka'i gnang ba stsal bar dgongs te dgung lo don lnga pa shing pho spre'u'i lo hor zla bcu gcig pa'i tshes bcu
skor du gser zangs las grub pa'i gdugs gsar bzhengs kyis bzo grwa btsugs/ grub tu nye ba na sku 'bum la 'ja' sgor mor zug pa dang me tog gi char dang nam mkha' las sgra
snyan po sgrog pa sogs byung / hor zla bcu gnyis pa rgyal gyi zla ba'i tshes bcu bdun la rje nyid tshogs kyi mgon por phebs/ rdo rje slob dpon gyi phyag len rnams thugs
rgyus khog nas rdo rje 'chang rin chen bsod nams mchog grub kyis gnang zhing dpal zhwa lu'i grwa pa rags bsdus kyis gsung ram btegs nas rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor zhal
phye ste rab gnas bkra shis rgyas byed/ kha skong gi sbyin bsreg dang bcas pa'i gsung chog legs par bstar/ mchod rten gyi dbu gdugs la rje nyid kyis rgyun du dkrol bar
mdzad pa'i phyag dril zhig btags pa'ang dril bu gzhan dag sgra mi sgrob pa'i tshe de gcig pur rlung gis bskyod pa ma yin par sgra sgrog cing de yang zhwa lu ri mthil dang
khyad par bkra shis lhun pa'i chos grwar 'phel 'grib kyi ltas ston pa zhig yin par mngon te dus phyis go rSha'i dmag gis bkra shis lhun po ba tsam du nye ba na yang dril
ba de lo sprel bar sgra gcig kyang ma bsgrags pa byung zer ro/ /de nas re zhig bkra shis lhun por chibs kha bskyod nas stan chags shing zha lu ri mthil

gnyis su gzhi gsum gyi cho ga nyams pa gso ba sogs kyi phyag len spyan 'khrid la snye mo rgyal byed tshal gyi slob dpon don grub dpal ba rdzong bar mdzad/ dgung lo brgyad cu
gya gnyis pa lcags mo yos kyi lo ma he'i mchod pa'i dus gtor chen mo la chibs kha bsgyur nas ri mthil gyi sngags grwa kun gyi tshogs dbur phebs/ gshed dmar lha lnga'i steng
nas drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog dang khyad par dam can chos kyi rgyal po la bka' bsgo gnang mkhan rje tshar chen yab sras tsam ma gtogs mkhan po sngon ma 'ga' zhig la yang
phyag mdzub rengs pa dang shangs mtshal sher ba sogs cho 'phrul du ma byung 'dug mod/ rje 'di ni nges par dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po dang dbyer mi mnga' ba ma zad/
sngon g.yung ston rdo rje dpal du sku skye ba bzhes dus su phung po ri bo che nas zhal brnyan gter nas spyan drangs te/ dus gtor chen mo 'di btsugs pa yin pa'i phyir/ de
lta bu'i 'tshub cha yong ba lta mi smos/ khrom thams cad zil gyis mnan te bka' bsgo dam bsgrags rgyas par mdzad do/ /da skabs dam can chos rgyal yab yum gnyis la phod ko
re dang yum la ba glang gi ko rlon gyi gzugs sder bzhi dang bcas pa bzang gos las tshems grub tu gnang ba'ang 'dul ba mdzad cing / gzhan yang ri phug ti gtsug lag khang
la gnam yol khyad du 'phags pa dang rnam sras mchod pa la 'grems rgyu'i rgyal po chen po

rnam thos sras kyi zab sku sogs bzhengs nas sbyor 'jags gnang / de ltar rje 'di nyid dpal ri bo dge ldan pa'i bstan pa la ni/ ji skad du/ rje blo bzang grags pa'i bsten pa
la/ /mgon de dang dbyer med thams cad mkhyen/ /rje btsun blo bzang chos rgyan la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes dge lugs pa thams cad kyis mgrin gcig tu byas te da lta'i bar du gsol
ba 'debs kyin yod snang ba'i phyir/ ji ltar gsol ba 'debs pa'i tshig de yang sgro btags pa tsam ma yin par don dang ldan pa zhig yin pas phyogs der bka' drin che ba'i tshul
de tsam gyis shes par nus shing / de las gzhan pa'i bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i bstan pa la yang dngos dang brgyud nas bka' drin mchog tu che'o/ /de yang zhwa lu'i
mkhan rabs snga phyi kun tu sdom rgyun kho na gal che bar gsungs pa bzhin/ rje 'di'i so thar byang sems gsang sngags kyi sdom pa thams cad du bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa
las brgyud tshul rnam dag yod par bzhed do/ /rje 'di nyid chu pho rta'i lo la bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i rgyal tshab tu byon nas lcags mo glang gi lo yan bkra shis lhun
po dang gdan sa nyis 'dzin gyi tshul du skyong bar mdzad pas zhwa lu'i khri thog tu rang lo nyi shu bzhugs pa yin no/ /de nas dge byed ces pa chu pho stag gi lo/ /rje
nyid kyi dgung lo brgya phrag brgal bar bzhugs pa'i tshul yang yod med kyi de dag dgongs pa can du nges shing / lo

rtsis dngos bstan la dgung lo dgu bcu go gsum bzhes pa/ lo de'i nag pa zla pa'i tshes bcu gsum gyi tho rangs gzims khang rgyal mtshan mthon por gzugs sku'i nyin byed gzhon
nu nub phyogs bde ldan zhing gi mgon po'i thugs kar bsdus nas slar yang mchog gi sprul pa'i zlos gar rje btsun blo bzang ye shes kyi mtshan dpe'i zla ba gzhon nu yum gyi
shar ri'i phrag par 'dzegs so/ / / /gdan sa nyer gnyis pa rdo rje 'chang rin chen bsod nams mchog grub kyi rnam thar lo rgyus gong du song / rab byung bcu gcig pa'i dge byed
ces pa chu pho stag gi lo rje nyid kyi dgung lo drug cu re gcig pa hor zla dang po'i tshes drug la khri thog tu phebs/ gdan sar lo lnganga bcu bzhugs nas dgung lo bdun
cu bzhes pa 'gal byed ces pa lcags mo phag gi lo la sku zhang mkhyen brtse mchog grub la gdan sa gtad/ dgung lo brgyad cu pa blo ngan zhes pa lcags mo bya'i lo hor zla
bdun pa'i tshes bzhi la sku me tog 'thor ba'i tshul bstan to/ / | / /gdan sa nyer gsum pa sku zhang rin po che mkhyen brtse'i mchog grub dpal bzang po ni/ rnam thar sogs
'khrungs lo'i nges tshig yod pa ma mthong yang / lce'i gdung dri ma med pa las sku 'khrungs/ gzhon nu nyid nas mkhan chen bsod nams mchog grub kyi spyan sngar rab byung dang
/ phyis bsnyen rdzogs kyang de nyid la mdad/ tshul khrims

rnam par dag pa dang thugs zhi zhing dul ba sogs smin pa gsum shas che/ sde snod dang rgyud sde'i don la mkhyen rab kyi sgo shin tu yangs/ rab byung bcu gcig pa'i lcags mo
phag gi lo la dpal zhwa lu'i khri thog tu phebs nas chos 'khor rgyun ring ba bskor ro/ / | / /gdan sa nyer bzhi pa paN chen rin chen 'jam dpal bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal
bzang po ni/ 'khrungs sa zhwa lu mo dben gyi khang chub ba bya bar sku 'khrungs pa yin zer/ dgung lo dgu la mkhan chen bsod nams mchog grub kyi spyan sngar dge tshul mdzad/
nyid kyi sku'i gcung po 'jam dbyangs phun tshogs dang gnyis ka'i mkhan chen gyi nye gnas zhus te rje nyid nas mchod dpon dang gzim dpon sbrag ma rgyun ring ba gnang
/ dgung lo nyi su rtsa lnga la dpal ri bo gru 'dzin gyi pho brang dmar po'i bya 'dabs lha ldan ra mo che'i sa'i cha/ dga' ldan khang gsar du mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa
rin chen bsod nams mchog grub kyis mkhan slob sbrags ma mdzad cing / gsang ston gser mdog can mkhan po shAkya don grub/ dus go brjod pa'i slob dpon gong dkar ba bla ma
dge ba'i dbang po/ zhu ba po nA lendra pa gnyis khang gong gi bla ma kun dga' blo gros/ grogs ldan pa dge slong kun dga' nor bu ste/ mkhan slob dge 'dun gyi dbus su dgun
zla dang po'i yar ngo'i tshes drug gi phyi dro nyi ma bzhi cha lus pa grib tshod skyes bu gnyis kyi dus su bsnyen

rdzogs kyi sdom pa bzhes mkhan chen de nyid kyi drung du mdo sngags kyi chol tshul bsam gyis mi khyab pa gsan zhing rgyal dbang lnga pa rin po ches bsnyen rdzogs bskyar bzhes
skabs dang dge yang mdzad/ gzhan yang bco brgyad chos rje mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ pha bong kha pa 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ rigs 'dzin gter bdag gling pa/
dge slong 'phrin las rnam rgyal/ gong dkar pa rin chen rgya mtsho/ sger pa chos rje ngag dbang bstan 'dzin phun tshogs/ ngor sgrub khang ba dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ ngor
pa mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ sa skya zhabs drung a mes kun dga' bsod nams yab sras/ gdong khri chen bsod nams bstan 'dzin/ rin sding bla ma kun dga' byams pa/
byang gling pa smon lam lhun grub/ khang rnying slob dpon mkhyen rab brtan pa/ chen po rin chen bzang po/ lo phu mkhan chen ngag dbang byams pa dpal bzang / shel dkar mkhan
po bkra shis rgya mtsho/ gnas gsar ba 'jam dbyangs bstan 'dzin sogs bla mar bsten nas gsan bsam mthar phyin pa mdzad/ mkhan chen sku gshegs nas 'dar stod grang mo che'i
gdan sar phebs te slob bshad kyi chos 'khor bskor/ de rjes chos grwa chen po dpal zhwa lu gser kang gi khri thog tu phebs nas sde dang gtong gzhi sogs ne gnas phyag mdzod
rin chen chos

'phel la 'khur phog /rje nyid nas dbyar bzhugs 'dar dang dgun po zhwa lur bzhugs te chos ldan bshad sgrub 'ba' zhig mdzad de lug gnyis kyi sgo nas chos sde gnyis po yar 'phel
du gyur pas nges par 'di ni bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i rnam 'phrul kho na'o zer nas thams cad dad cing mos par gyur/ thugs dam gyi gtso bo rdo rje 'jigs byed la mthu
stobs dang nus pa rwa lo chen po dang tshul mtshungs pa byung zhing brgyud 'dzin slob ma yang mkhan chen byis pa mkhas btsun/ 'brog khang pa grub dbang 'jam dpal mkhyen
brtse/ chos rje smon lam lhun grub/ chen po bsod nams rgya mtsho sogs mang du byung ngo / /gsung rtsom gyi ris phyis su mthong ba la/ mkhan chen bsod nams mchog grub la
brten pa'i bla ma mchod pa'i cho ga shin tu rgyas pa/ de nyid kyi bka' 'bum dkar chag /gsan yig glegs lam gyi thog mtha' tshigs bcad/ gsang 'dus rim lnga'i rgyan gyi nyams
len/ sems nyid ngal bso'i khrid kyi rnal 'byor/ 'jigs byed kyi rA khrid 'chang thabs/ 'jigs byed dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs/ rje btsun sengge sgra la brten pa'i gdon
grol gyi cho ga bu ston gyi phyag bzhes gtsang ma/ ma he skad gtong ba'i lha 'dre la skad gtong lugs dang dam can chos kyi rgyal po la bzhes sgra 'bul tshul sogs 'dug go/
de ltar bstan 'gro'i don rgya cher mdzad nas rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i rgyal ba zhes pa shing po rta'i lo/ /hor zla bzhi ba'i tshes bco brgyad la sku gshegs/ gdung yid bzhin

gyi nor bu bzhugs pa'i dngul gyi mchod rten thog tshad ma dang / gser zangs las grub pa'i gzims lam sku 'dra sku tshad dang mnyam pa ngo mtshar ba rnams 'phrin las pa chen
po phyag mdzod rin po che chos 'phel gyi sgo gsum 'bad pa du mas rgyu yon spyan/ shing lug hor zla gsum pa'i tshes bco lnga nas ma spre zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes bco lnga'i
bar bal po'i bzo bo bha ri raM/ kiM se raM/ dha na mu pa ri dang bcas pa bzhes bzhengs te de dag la yon rjod dang / rab gnas dga' ston phun sum tshogs pa bsgrub nas zhwa
lu'i dngul gdung lha khang du bzhugs su gsol/ de dang 'dra ba'i gdung rten rnams dang / 'bum rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum gyi gsung rab glegs bam dang bcas pa 'dar stod grang
mo cher bzhengs so/ / / /gdan sa nyer drug pa mkhan chen rin chen byams pa mkhas btsun ni/ nyang stod 'breng rtse'i sa char sog lhun grub gling pa zhes bya'i sde dpon zhig
gi sras su sku 'khrungs/ dpal 'khor chos sde rin sdings grwa tshang gi grwa pa mdzad nas chos sde rin sdings pa rin chen byams pa kun dga' dpal bzang po'i spyan sngar
rab byung dang dge tshul gyi sdom pa bzhes/ phyis mkhan chen rin chen 'jam dpal gyi drung du bsnyen par rdzogs/ mkhan chen de nyid dang gzhan yang bla chen bsod nams rgya
mtsho sogs las bu lugs kyi chos bka' rnams rim gyis gnas/ rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i myos

byed ces pa shing mo lug gi lo dpal zhwa lu'i khri thog tu phebs nas 'chad nyan rgya cher mdzad pa'i matar/ sa mo phag gi sku gshegs/ gdung bzhugs pa'i tsandan gyi mchod rten
bre yan chad dngul las grub pa dang gzims mal sku 'dra bcas phyag mdzod dpon po rin chen bstan pa dar rgyas kyis ri phug tu bzhes so/ / | / /gdan sa nyer bdun pa paN chen
mchog gi sprul pa'i sku rje btsun blo bzang ye shes dpal bzang po'i mtshan gyis skyong bar mdzad pas/ rje 'di nyid thob rgyal brul tshang du yab zhabs drung bsod nams
dbang grags dang / yum tshe brtan bu khrid gnyis kyi sras su rab byung bcu gcig pa'i chu mo yos kyi la/ /gro zhun zla ba'i tshes bco lnga la ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang
chabs cig tu sku bltams/ 'khrungs nas ring por ma lon par gsung ngag gnang ba dang mdzad spyod kyangatha mal pa'i spyod yul las 'das pa zhig byung zhing bkra shis lhun
