po nas rje blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan gyi sku skye 'khrul med du ngos 'dzin gnang / dgung lo lnga la bla brang chen por gdan drangs shing sku gong ma'i chos kyi rgyal
thabs su dbang bskur/ dgung lo brgyad la dbus phyogasasu phebs nas rgyal dbang lnga pa chen po'i zhabs drung du dge tshul gyi sdom pa bzhes/ yongs 'dzin bsod nams grags
pa dang / blo bzang don grub sogs bsten nas rim gyis thugs gnyer gsan sbyong la 'grus par mdzad/ dgung lo nyer gnyis pa la rdo rje 'dzin pa

dkon mchog rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos mkhan slob zung 'brel mdzad de bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa bzhes/ 'dul ba'i gzhung mang po thugs la bzungs nas yongs 'dzin rnams kyi spyan
sngar dka' gnad la dri gtugs zhib po mdzad cing 'dul ba'i bcas mtshams mtha' dag phyag len la thebs par mdzad pas 'phags pa nye bar 'khor slar byon pa lta bur gyur/ mkhas
btsun bzang po'i yon ta na gyi thugs rgyud phyug kyang mkhas pa'i snyems dang bral zhing rtag tu dman cha 'dzin pa gtso bor mdzad de/ shar phyogs gong ma chen pos rgya
nag gi yul du spyan 'dren par brtsams shing gzhung sa mchod yon nas kyang phebs dgos pa'i zhu nan phul rung nged la rgyal po'i dgongs pa khengs pa'i lung rtogs kyi yon
tan med gsung 'byon du ma bzhed/ de bzhin du bod 'dir rgyal po 'ga' zhig gis rje nyid la bkur bzos che ba byas kyang rlom zhen mi mdzad/ 'ga' zhig gis log par 'khu yang
'khon 'dzin mi mdzad par ri btsugs pa bzhin du bzhugs pas slar 'phrin las je rgyas su gyur/ bka' gdams pa'i sku mched gsum gyi rnam thar 'ba' zhig lhur mdzad de/ rten gsum
bzhengs pa/ dge 'dun la bsnyen bkur ba/ chos 'chad pa kho na ma gtogs gzhan gyi ngo srung dang / sku rtsed 'phyar g.yeng gi rnam pa gtan mi mdzad par grags/ sku gong ma
paN chen blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan de nyid zhwa lu'i khri thog tu phebs nas

dngos brgyud du mas bka' drin che ba ltar/ rje 'di nyid kyang kun mkhyen bu'i gdan sar gdan 'dren zhu thub pa zhig byung na mchog dang / de min dgon pa'i zhal 'dzin gnang ba
zhig ma byung ba'i thabs med tshul zhwa lu pa'i bla ma'i sa sne kun blo mthun bsam rtse gcig bsgril gyis gsol ba 'debs par chen slob rnams byan las mi yong gsungs nas zhal
bzhes ma mdzad/ slar yar zhwa lu ri mthil gyi dge 'dun tshogs chen yongs rdzogs bkra shis lhun por zhabs bteg nas gsol 'debs su byon pas/ rje nyid kyi mjal phyag thog
bka' lung la/ khyed zhwa lu pa rnams chos sde gzhan dang mi 'dra pas/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i bzhed srol rgyud sde'i phyag len rnams zhib rgyas che zhing sngon dus
nas bstan pa'i 'byung khungs yin par ma zad dus deng sang yang mkhan chen rgyal ba'i dbang po de nyid kyi rtsa ba'i bla ma khyab bdag zhwa lu pa rin chen bsod nams mchog
grub sogs kyi bka' drin la brten/ chos rgyun nyams chag tu ma gyur pa gdan sa 'gangs chen po yod 'dug na'ang / nged da cha lang tsho yol/ khams kyi bde dog ches pas/ nged
rang ngo bos gdan sa der 'chad nyan gyi rgyun skyong ba sogs byed mi thub par ming tsam gyis skyong khul byas pa la dge mtshan mi 'dug ste/ 'on kyang da res dge 'dun rnams
kyi gsung gcog ma phod pas re zhig da ka byed do gsung nas dgyes bzhin du zhal gyi bzhes so/ /rje nyid kyi dgung lo lnga bcu nga brgyad pa rab byung gnyis pa'i kun

ldan zhes pa lcags pho byi ba'i lo/ chu stod zla ba'i nyi su gcig la zhwa lu ri mthil gyi sengge'i khri la zhabs kyi padma bkod rgyu'i dgongs bzhed grub kyang 'phral sku'i
'tsho skyong dang sbrags pa'i bcad rgya gnang dgos byung pas/ bla brang rtsis bzhes su bka' chen dar rgyas chos 'phel gtong ba mdzad cing slar gdan sar phebs rgyu'i zhal
bzhes dang bcas ri mthil gyi dge 'dun rnams la mang 'gyed sogs stsal/ de skabs zhwa lu sogs su rje nyid chibs bsgyur yong res grwa bsgrigs kyi 'ur langs nas phyogs nas mi
mang po 'dus pa rnams la ri phug tu bum chu zhal 'byed btang pas de nyin bkra shis lhun po nas ri phug bar la 'ja' tal gyi zug pa sogs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas byung zhes grags/
de ltar gdan sa'i zhal 'dzin gnang nas zhwa lu pa'i bstan pa la dngos brgyud du ma nas phan pa'i dgongs pa mdzad pa zhig ste/ las byed rnams la'ang dgon pa'i sgrigs
bkod sogs yang dag byed dgos pa'i bka' lung khur lci ba'i phyag dam gnang / de lta bu'i tshul gyis bstan 'gro'i don du gyur pa'i rnam par thar pa re re nas brjod kyis mi
lang zhing dgung lo don lnga la phebs pa me mo sbrul gyi lo/ gdung bya rtag 'dzin can rnams chos la bskul ba'i phyir re zhig gzugs sku'i bkod pa chos kyi dbyings su brtul
lo/ / / /gdan sa nyer brgyad pa mkhan chen ngag dbang yon tan 'byung gnas

dpal bzang po la rnam thar sogs yod pa ma mthong yang / sgra snyan dngags sogs rig gnas la mkhyen pa rgyas shing / rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtsho'i zhabs 'bring du bzhugs
nas/ de nyid la dbyangs can sgra mdo sogs kyi sgri'i ri mo rnams kyang zhib par phul/ gzhan yang blo gsal don gnyer can du ma la tha snyad gtsug lag gi gzhung lugs 'chad
cing spel ba sogs mkhas pa mgu ba bskyed pa'i mdzad pa 'ba' zhig bstan/ zhwa lu'i khri thog tu phebs nas gsung chos gnang ba sogs ma byung na yang zhwa lu pa'i bstan don
la rgyar dgongs dgon ma lag mchod gzhis dang bcas pa'i gtan tshigs she bam chen mor grags pa sogs brtsams nas rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtsho mchod yon la phyag dam
gyis gnon par zhus/ gtan tshigs de nyid btsan cha che ba'i zhwa lu pa'i lha sde mi sde thams cad da lta'i bar bzos bde ba sogs byung zhing phyis kyi mkhan po la bltos te
'di nyid bka' drin che ba'i gnas dmapa'o/ / | / /gdan sa nyer dgu pa mkhan chen thu'u bkan pa blo bzang chos kyi nyi ma de nyid ni/ 'khrungs yul mdo smad kyi sa cha a mdo
pho rod kyi phun tshogs lung par grags pa'i nang tshan nor du thang zhes pa'i yul khyim du yab bra sti dpang skyabs rgyal dang / yum chos 'tsho skyid ces bya ba gnyis kyi
sras su rab byung nyi ma'i me sbrul hor zla bcu gcig pa'i tshes bdun la sku bltams/

zhag 'ga' zhig nas bra sti dgon pa'i chos skyong sku phebs kyi sar yum gyi lha mjal du khyer bas chos skyong gi dar mtshon sna lnga zhig phyag tu thogs nas yum gyi mjal skabs
bcu chung pang?dpang du bzung yod pa la dar tshon sna lnga de nyid kyis dkris nas bu chung 'di la gtsang sbra gal che tshul nan tan gnang / byis pa'i dus der khyim du
mi bzhugs pa dgon pa'i phyogs su yang yang bros pas/ skabs 'gar yab kyis rta bzhon pa'i pang du thogs te dgon par khyer nas zhab shas re sdod dgos pa byung / lan gcig dgon
par phyin pa'i lam du glu mang po zhig len gyin 'dun pa yab kyi ci zer nyan pas/ dgon pa khra khrar 'gro rgyu yin/ de na grwa pa mang po yod/ rgya gling bus pa sing sing
byed/ dung dkar bus pa 'ur 'ur byed/ rnga sbub brdungs ba chem chem byed/ nga rang khril skyil krung byas/ dge 'dun mang po la me tog gtor/ da yis am ring ba bshad rgyu
yin/ zhes zer gyin 'dug ci yin snyam the tshom du gyur te a khu zhabs drung pa bshad pas/ lam rim bshad rgyu yin zer 'dod pa 'dug kyang tshig dag po ma thon par am ring
byas pa red zer skad/ der grwa pa zhig gis 'o na khyod rang gis am ring shod dang nged tsho da nyan gyi byas pas/ nam mkha' la mdzub mo kyer nas lha mi zer/ sa la mdzub mo
btsugs nas khyi phag zer/ bar snang la lag pa yug yug byed cing nag po dkar po zer/

lag pa mnyam gzhag byas nas/ bla ma skyabs su mchi'o/ /sangs rgyas la skyabs su mchi'o/ chos la skyabs su mchi'o/ dge 'dun la skyabs su mchi'o zer nas mgo hril gyis btums nas
sdod kyin gda' skad/ der dge bshes shig 'dug pa de na re/ bde 'gro dang ngan 'gro gang du skye ba dkar nag gi las la rag pas/ dkon mchog la skyabs 'gro dgos zer rgyur
'dug byis pa 'di rang dga' ba gal yin zer nas phyag btsal pas gzhan dag kyang de ltar byed do/ /de lta bu'i brda chos gsung ba sogs mdzad pas/ thu'u bkan ngag dbang chos
kyi rgya mtsho'i sku skye yin par shes te dgung lo drug la a mdo dgon lung nas gdan drangs/ zhal snga nas ngag dbang dge legs rgya mtsho la dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa zhus/ yi
ge 'bri klog sogs kyang brda bstan pa tsam gyis mkhyen tshul bsten/ bla brang du sku gong ma'i sku chas nyag je phrar gyur pas/ gsol ba na bza' sogs kyang ngan ngon tsam
las med pa'i khar zhabs 'bring pa dag nas sku skye'i rigs chung dus gces la nga la btang na nor nyan mi yong zer tsha jun che ba byas kyang drin bzo kho na mdzad/ dgung
lo bcu gcig pa la sum pa mkhan po ye shes dpal 'byor ba'i drung du rab byung mdzad nas dgong lung byams pa gling du mtshan nyid kyi slob gnyer la zhugs/ de rjes lcang skya
rol pa'i rdo rje dang mjal zhing dgyes tshor chen po dang bcas dge tshul gyi sdom pa rang stsal/ lo phyi ma cho 'phrul zla ba'i smon lam gyi

dus dgon lung tshogs chen la skyes rabs so bzhi pa'i bshad pa mdzad nas chos 'khor bskor pas der 'khod pa rnams mi phyed pa'i dad pa thob/ dgung lo bcu dgu pa la dbus gtsang
gi yul grur phyag phebs nas thog mar rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtsho dang mjal zhing 'bras spungs sgo mang grwa tshang du mdo phyogs kyi slob gnyer rnams rim gyis mdzad/
de'i tshe 'jam dbyangs bzhad sprul dkon mchog 'jigs med dbang pos dge rgan mdzad/ sgo mang gi chos grwar sprul sku tsha gra'i gras la yang mi bzhugs par grwa rkyang
snyoms chung gi 'dzin tshul sha stag gnang / phur bu lcog tu rje ngag dbang byams pa'i drung nas lam rim sogs gsan pas thugs rgyud la khul che ba byung ste snga phyir rje
'di la mdo sngags kyi chos bka' mang ba gsan/ dgung lo nyer gcig pa sa mo glang gi lo/ sa ga zla ba'i tshes bco lnga'i nyin thub dbang gnyis pa ngag dbang byams pa las bsnyen
rdzogs kyi sdom pa yang dag pa bzhes/ de lo lcang skya rdo rje 'chang yang rgya nag nas bod du phebs pas/ de dang stag phu rin po che sogs las zab chos mang ba gsan
zhing / lhag par stag phu rje'i drung du nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i chos skor zhu bar brtsams pa na be bum dang bris sku sogs kyang rang bsgrigs su 'bul mkhan byung / 'bras
spungs su bzhugs skabs sa skya nas 'ong zer ba'i mi nag po zhig gis sa skya nas khams pa bla mas khyed la bskur byung zer nas po ti zhig sprad

byung ba zhal phye nas bltas pas/ mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i gsung ngag slob bshad kyi dpe yin par 'dug /mi de yang gar song cha med pa zhig byung ste sa skya'i
chos skyong gi sprul par gleng / tshul de ni rje 'di nyid tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i thugs sras kun mkhyen klu sgrub rgya mtsho'i sku 'phreng yin pas de'i brda chos
shig tu nges so/ /de nas gzhung sa chen pos dpal zhwa lu gsar khang gi khri thog tu phebs dgos pa'i bka' rgya gnang bas/ mi nus pa'i rgyu mtshan gnang rtsis la/ rje lcang
skya rin po ches/ snyigs dus kyi rgyal ba gnyis pa kun mkhyen bu ston rin po che'i gdan sa bskyang rgyu byung ba skal ba bzang zhing / rten 'brel gyi gnad kyang che
bas phyin pa 'gab gsung pas gtsang du de'ang rje nyid kyi dgung lo nyer gsum pa rab byung bcu gsum pa'i lcags mo yos kyi lo/ /gza' tshes phun sum tshogs pa'i nyin khams gsum
chos kyi rgyal po bu ston rin chen grub kyi sengge'i khri 'phang mthon por zhabs sen nye bar bkod/ de'i tshe gzhung sa chen po nas khri ston rgya che ba dang / bkra shis
lhun po nas kyang tshong 'dus sde pa ched mngags kyis 'dus tshogs su mang 'gyed/ rje nyid la khri 'bul sogs mdzad/ 'di lo ma he'i mchod pa'i lo yin pas/ bka'

las / ma he'i mchod pa'i skabs sngon gyi dus su g.yung ston rdo rje dpal dang / de rjes tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po dang / paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa blo bzang chos rgyan
rnams kyi ma he la bka' bsgo mdzad 'dug pa las gzhan pa'i gebs lnga pa'i yongs 'dzin mkhan chen bsod mchog pa dang / mkhan chen 'jam dpal ba sogs kyis kyang bka' bsgo ma
gnang 'dug des na bdag lta bus dam pa gong ma de rnams dang 'gran par rlom pa ni byis pa gri khar rtse ba dang mtshungs pas/ paN chen thams cad mkhyen pas nged la 'di lo
zhwa lur ma he mchod pa'i skabs yin 'dug pas/ khyed rang zhwa lur bsdad nas ma he'i bka' bsgo sogs byas na legs pa 'dug ces nan chags gsung kyang mi nus pa'i rgyu mtshan
zhus pa yin zhes gsung ngo / /zhwa lu bla brang du rig byed ma'i sgrub bsnyen kha skong gi sbyin bsreg dang bcas pa gnang pas bcad rgya grol nyin grub pa zhig gis ras yug
me tog dmar po'i ri mo can zhig phul/ de nas gdan sa chen po ri phug chos kyi pho brang du phebs rje btsun sgrol ma'i bsnyen mtshams gnang bas der gnas kyi khyad par thugs
dam shin tu 'phel ba byung nas gsungs pa/ / / /thugs spros bral bde chen mkha' dbyings su/ /sku cir yang 'char bas sprin dkrigs te/ /gsung mdo sngags legs bshad char
'bebs pa/ /pha rdo rje 'chang dngos bla mar 'dud/ /

dpal a hi sha dang bu ston sogs/ /rje mkhas sgrub du mas byin brlabs pa/ /gnas khyad 'phags zhwa lu ri phug tu/ /bdag skyid pa'i rgyang glung 'di ltar 'then/ /bya ne tso'i
gshog pa ltar ljang pa'i/ /spang rtsi sman me tog bkra ba'i ljongs/ /rang ci dkar 'dug cing chags pa yis/ /bdag rang dbang med par skyid du bcug /dbyibs mdangs mdzes mtshar
sdug me tog la/ /rkang drug ldan bung ba'i tshogs 'dus nas/ /skad dar dir glu dbyangs len pa yis/ /bdag rang dbang med par skyid du bcug /shing ljon pa g.yu yi lo 'dabs
can/ /'bras legs smin phang phung chags pa'i tshogs/ /lus tsha gdung sel ba'i grib bsil gyis/ /bdag rang dbang med par skyid du bcug /shing gzhon nu gnyen lcug ldem pa'i
steng / /bya byi'i spu rigs sna tshogs can/ /skad snyan pa'i rol mo khrol ba yis/ /bdag rang dbang med par skyid du bcug /mgon a ti sha dang bu ston rje'i/ /dpal byin rlabs
las byung grub chu'i rgyun/ /nad zug rngu 'joms pa'i sman mchog des/ /bdag rang dbang med par skyid du bcug /rang gtsang zhing gzhan gyi dri ma 'khrud/ /skad lhung lhung
'bab pa'i nyal 'gro'i tshogs/ /thag nye ring mtshams par 'bab pa des/ /bdag rang dbang med par skyid du bcug /rin bun 'khrigs pa'i sked 'ching can/ /gangs shel gyi mchod
rten lta bu dang / /brag rin chen spungs 'dras brgyan pa yis/ /bdag rang dbang med par skyid du bcug /grong 'du 'dzi'i gnas las thag ring zhing / /khong dbu rgod skye
bos dben pa'i mthus/ /sgra 'a 'ur med cing 'gol ba des/ /bdag rang dbang med par skyid du bcug /rgyus las su mi rung rgod pa'i tshe/ /ri'i rtse nas phyogs su bltas

pa na/ /sems skyo shas lam lam 'byung pa yis/ /bdag rang dbang med par skyid du bcug /lo zla ba dus bzhi'i 'gyur ldog dang / /shing me tog chu klung 'phel 'grib sogs/ /kun
'dus byas mi rtag chos ston pas/ /bdag rang dbang med pa skyid du bcug /lar mi med lung pa stong pa na/ /skyid dga' bde ster ba 'di 'dra snang / /mi kho bos ci dkar longs
su spyad/ /khyed 'du 'dzi can la ci cha yod/ /bka' mdo rgyud bstan bcos mtha' dag las/ /gnas dben pa'i che brjod mtha' yas gsungs/ /mi kho bas de dag tshad mar bzungs/ /khyod
rtog ge mkhan la ci cha yod/ /rje mkhas grub gong ma thams cad kyang / /gnas dben pa kho na bstan par mdzad/ /mi kho bos de la yar bltas byas/ /khyed bla chen rnams
la ci cha yod/ /ces sogs gsung mgur yang mang du gnang ngo / /grub dbang blo gsal bstan rgyan dang yang mjal zhing sku tshe snga ma'i las 'brel gyis thugs yid gcig 'dres
su gyur/ de nyid la zhal gdams gsung shog snang ba'i mthar yang / gnas 'og min chos kyi pho brang der/ /dus myur du zhal 'dzoms 'gyur ba smon/ /zhes gsung ba mdzad do/ don
la yang dpon slob gnyis mthar zhing brje ba'i lo zla gcig tu ma zad par na zhag khyad bcu gcig las med cing / de'i tshul thu'u bkan rin po che nyid kyi rnam thar na yang
'khod 'dug mod/ 'on kyang rje phur bu lcog pa'i slob ma blo bzang bstan rgyal zer

ba'i khams pa zhig ces khams pa yin rgyu gnang ba sogs ni rnam thar mdzad pa po rnams sa gnas kyis bskal pa'i dbang gis thugs rgyud med pa'i skyon phran bu byung ngam snyam
mo/ /snga phyir sum pa mkhan chen ye shes dpal 'byor/ lcang skya rol pa'i rdo rje/ 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa rin po che/ rje ngag dbang byams pa/ rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya
mtsho/ paN chen dpal ldan ye shes/ /sa skya'i bdag chen ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros sogs yongs 'dzin dam pa mang po las thos pa rgya mtsho'i pha mthar phyin pa mdzad cing
/ de ltar thos don rnams thugs rgyud la spungs nas nyams su bzhes pas nyes spyod mtha' dag 'gags shing yon tan yar 'phel du gyur pas mthar rtogs pa'i ye shes mngon du
byas te mdor na mkhas grub chen por nges pa yin no/ /phyis mdo khams smad kyi sa'i sman ljongs su phebs nas dgon lung byams pa gling dang / sku 'bum byams pa gling sa gos
dgon sde che phra du ma'i khri 'dzin mdzad nas chos 'khor bskor/ zang zing gi longs spyod rnams kyang lhag lus med par sku gsung thugs rten dang dge 'dun gyi sde la bsngo
ba mdzad/ zhwa lu ri mthil gyi gtsug lag khang la zhig gsos kyi mthun rkyen du dngul srang brgya phrag mang po'ang lan gnyis su bskur gnang zhing / mdor na shar phyogs
rgya mtsho chen po la thug gi bar du 'phrin las kyis khyab nas mthong thos

dran reg gi sems can grangs kyis mi chod pa 'khor ba mtha' can du mdzad pa dang / nang don du rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma dang / rta mchog rol ba sogs thugs dam gyi lha
mchog du mas zhal gzigs lung bstan dngos grub kyi mtshan ma brnyes tshul sogs ngo mtshar pa'i rnam thar mtha' yas kyang 'dir de tsam las ma spros shing / dgung lo drug cu
re drug pa chu khyi hor zla drug pa'i yar ngo'i tshes bcu'i nyin zhing 'di'i mdzad pa mthar phyin nas mkha' spyod rdo rje btsan mo'i pho brang du gshegs so/ rnam thar rgyas
pa gung thang rin po ches mdzad pa pu ti gnyis 'dug pas don du gnyer ba yod na der gzigs shig / / /gdan sa sum cu pa mkhan chen skal bzang tshe dbang ni/ skye ba snga
ma zhwa lu'i gtsug lag khang la phyag dang skor ba 'ba' zhig byed pa'i sprang po mgon med pa zhig tu gyur pa las tshe 'phos nas/ mo yan gyi grong bkra shis dkyil khang
pa zhes bya bar khyim bdag g.yung drung tshe brtan gyi bur skyes/ smra shes tsam gyi dus snga ma'i skye ba dran te gzhan dag la skor ba byas pa'i phan yon gyis mi lus thob
tshul sogs bshad pa na thams cad ya mtshan du byung / gtsug lag khang la bskor ba byas pa'i phan yon mthu che bar shes shing 'ga' zhig nas sprang po'i skye ba yin 'dug
pas ming la sprang phrug thogs zer/ chung ngu'i dus blo shin tu rno ba dang chos snang che zhing khyad par

skor ba byed pa la 'dun pa zhig byung / pha ma dag gis zhwa lu'i btsun pa byed bcug nas chos rje rin chen don grub pa'i dge phrug tu bskyal/ der zhwa lu'i sgrub mchod rnams
kyi cho ga phyag len rnams bslab/ khyad par dus 'khor gyi cho ga gzhung / 'phreng gar sogs mkhas par shes/ re zhig nas bla ma rin chen don grub de thugs gtum po zhig yod
'dug pas rkyen byas te dus 'khor gyi dpe cha khyer nas lha sa bar bros phyin/ de nas rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtsho la dus 'khor gyi cho ga 'phreng gar dang bcas pa
rgyugs 'bul byas pas rnam rgyal grwa tshang du 'jug pa'i bdag rkyen gnang / skabs shig rgya nag tu lcang skya rdo rje 'chang gi gdan sar dus 'khor gyi phyag len 'dzugs par
phyin pas dgongs bzhed 'grub ste/ phyir yong khar rje lcang skya rin po che nas khyod nged la phan thogs chen po byung / khyod rang bod kyi mi drag cig 'dod na yang nged
kyis yi ge bskur pas chog gsung / slar bod du slebs pa na sde pa gzhung gi rtse'i mgron gnyer mkhan po'i bsko 'ja' mdzad/ rang gi mos zhen gyi zhwa lu'i mkhan po byas chog
pa zhus pas kyang dgyes bzhin du gnang / zhwa lu'i gtsug lag khang gi g.yu thog shar phyogs ma gsar du spos/ dus 'khor gyi gar pa rnams la gar chas cha 'grig sogs dngos
'byor gyi zhabs tog rgya che bar bsgrub/ rgyal dbang mchog sku gong 'og gnyis kyi zhabs 'gyur dang gzhung sa chen po'i bstan srid kyi bya ba gang

la yang lhag bsam rnam dag gis kun nas bslangs te 'di phyi gnyis yod kyi legs tshogs kho na spel/ snga rting bsgril bas rgya nag tu lan gsum byon pas phyi ma paN chen dpal
ldan ye shes kyi sne shan la phebs dus gong ma chen pos kyang / bdag rkyen cho lo sogs stsal/ de yang mkhan po 'di nyid la lung dang rtogs pa'i yon tan gyi cha nas bsngags
su rung ba'i rnam thar ha cang gsal ba mi snang yang / gtsug lag khang dang dge 'dun gyi sde la rnam par dkar bas mdzad pa rgya che zhing bsod nams kyi dpal chen po dang
ldan pa zhig byung ngo / /de ltar sku zhang chen po grags pa rgyal mtshan yab sras rnams kyis gtsos/ tA'i su tu chen po byang chub rgyal mtshan sogs lha gzigs rlangs kyi
gdung brgyud rnams nas rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtsho mchod yon gyi bar du bstan pa stobs kyis 'dzin pa'i chos rgyal gong ma de dag gis thub bstan spyi dang bye brag
zhwa lu'i bstan pa la yang gces spras su mdzad de/ mkhan po bsko ba'i tshe yang mkhas pa dang grub pa'i cha nas gzigs te bsko bar mdzad pas na/ zhwa lu ri mthil gyi dge
'dun rnams kyang de dang de'i gnas skabs su gyur pa/ de phyin chad nas ni bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i ring lugs 'di nyid kyang gzungs zad kyi nad pa sman pas bor ba ltar
gyur pas da lta yan la mkhan po'i mtshan gsol ba ji

snyed cig byon 'dug mod/ de dag 'jig rten gyi ngos nas zhwa lu pa'i dbon po'i go ni mi chod ka med yin 'dug /khri thog nas 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyis bstan pa la bya ba byas
tshul gyi rnam thar ni ci yang 'gyir med pa kho na'o/ mkhan rabs bshad pa'i skabs so/ / | gnyis pa rgyud sde bzhi'i cho ga phyag len rnams kyi rdo rje slob dpon ri phug
dbu mdzad chen mo zhes rgyal ba byang gling pa'i gdan rabs byon tshul zur tsam smos na/ de yang gdan sa 'di nyid bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i sku dus nas bar ma chad pa
zhig byang pa yin nges kyang thog snga ma rnams rtsad mchod pas 'bri bar ma spobs/ chos rje dpon po rin chen rgyal po la rgyal ba byang gling pa zer bas de nas da lta'i
bar byon tshul 'di ltar yin te/ / | / /rgyal pa byang gling pa dpon po rin chen rgyal po'i mtshan gsol ba de ni/ mkhyen rab rin po che'i thugs kyi sras dam pa bu lugs kyi
bstan pa la phyag rjes dang bka' drin shin tu che bar brtsi ba yin te lo rgyus kyi khyad par rgyas pa ni gong du spros zin to/ / | / /de nas mgo byas pa'i gdan rabs gnyis
pa ni rgyud sde 'dzin pa chen po bla chen chos rig rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad/ / / /gsum pa ni byang gling 'jam pa'i dbyangs rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos
mdzad/ / | / /bzhi pa ni chos kyi rje rin po che kun dga' mchog ldan pas mdzad/ / | / /lnga pa ni rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan dpal

bzang pos mdzad/ / / /drug pa ni rje btsun ku sa li ba rgyal mtshan bzang pos mdzad/ / | / /bdun pa ni lha ba pa chen po yongs 'dzin rin chen rgya mtsho'i zhal snga nas kyis
mdzad/ / | / /brgyad pa ni rdo rje 'chang rin chen bsod nams mchog grub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos mdzad de 'di yan gyi mdzad tshul bshad du yod pa dag ni gong
gi skabs su brjod zin pa nyid do/ / | / /byang gling gi gdan rabs dgu pa chos rje sangs rgyas 'od zer de ni/ thugs rgyud byams sems dang zhe dul che zhing rgyud sde rgya
mtshor gzhan dring mi 'jog pa'i mkhyen rab kyi snang ba rgyas la/ brtan mkhas kyi yon tan gnyis dang ldan pas gdul bya rjes su 'dzin pa la mchog tu dpa' ba zhig go/ /
/ /gdan rabs bcu pa ni rdo rje 'chang smon lam lhun grub kyis mdzad de/ de nyid ni sku gzhon nu nas kun mkhyen bsod nams mchog grub las rab tu byung zhing / dam pa de dang
mtshungs med chos rje klu sgrub rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen rin chen 'jam dpal/ gnas gsar dpon rin po che ngag dbang blo gsal mchog ldan sogs yongs 'dzin dam pa mang du bsten
nas rgyud sde rab tu mang po'i tshig don la mkhas par bslabs/ phyis bsnyen rdzogs kyi mkhan po yang kun mkhyen bsod nams mchog grub nyid la zhus/ sde snod dang rgyud
sde'i don la dge bshes chen por byung pas

rgyal dbang lnga pa chen pos kyang ri phug gi gdan sar bsko 'ja'i phyag dam dang khri ston sogs stsal/ gdan sar phebs nas thos bsam sgom sgrub stabs gcig tu mdzad pas brgyud
pa gong ma'i byi rlabs zhugs te 'chad nyan shin tu 'phel zhing slob ma'i gtso bo yang / sku zhang blo bzang mkhas btsun/ grub dbang rin chen brtson 'grus/ rin sdings bla
ma rin chen bstan pa dar rgyas sogs brgyud pa zin pa mang du byung ngo / / / /gdan rabs bcu gcig pa pa chen grub dbang rin chen brtson 'grus de nyid ni/ byis pa'i dus nas
skyes stobs kyi shes rab shin tu che bas/ bu ston chos 'byung / dus 'khor chos 'byung / dus 'khor bsdus rgyud/ rgyud sde spyi rnam chen mo sogs blo 'dzin byas nas tshogs
rgyugs phul/ mkhan chen ratna manydzu shri/ mtshungs med smon lam lhun grub/ bla chen bsod nams rgya mtsho sogs la bu lugs kyi chos bka' phal che ba gsan/ chu pho 'brug
gi lo cho 'phrul zla ba'i tshes bco lnga la byang gling gi gdan sar phebs/ 'jig rten chos brgyad hrul bor zhig pas mkhas 'dod dang gzhan ngor mdzes chos lta bu mi mdzad
cing kyal ka dang ku re'i tshul du chos gsung pas/ grub pa'i dbang phyug ces pa'i mtshan yang de nas grags/ gsung gi brgyud pa zin pa'i slob ma yang / gnas gsar pa ngag
dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos mchog /

grub chen byams pa rgyal po/ dus 'khor ba yon tan dar rgyas/ bsam gtan sgang pa ye shes rgyal mtshan sogs dge ba'i bshes gnyen mang du byon no/ / | / /gdan rabs bcu gnyis pa
chos rje rin po che 'jam dpal blo gsal ni/ zhwa lu sa stod rtse tho ba'i mi brgyud sku 'khrungs/ mkhan chen rin chen 'jam dpal pas rab tu byung zhing grub dbang rin chen
brtson 'grus sogs bla ma mang du bsten/ phyis slob gnyer dang bsnyen rdzogs grub nas ri phug byang gling gi gdan sa rgyun ring ba mdzad/ dge 'dun gyi spyi rdzas la thugs
lhag par dkar zhing drang tshugs che ba ma zad grwa rkyang snyom chung ri phug tu slob gnyer byed pa dag la dar chu phor gang re las med kyang 'gyed par gnang / ri phug
tu rgyun ja ma chad par gsanang bas grwa ba yang slob gnyer byed pa'ang mang du 'phel/ zhwa lu pa'i skya ser kun kyang dad mos che zhing 'chad nyan yang rgya cher mdzad/
grub dbang blo gsal bstan rgyan gyi rab byung mkhan po yang 'di nyid yin no/ / | / /gdan rabs bcu gsum pa chos rje 'jam dpal tshul khrims ni/ zhwa lu nub pa zhes bya ba'i
mi brgyud du 'khrungs/ byis pa'i dus nas 'jam dpal mtshan brjod la kha ton byas pas don blo la 'jags shing shes rab che bar gyur/ zhwa lur slob gnyer rnams thebs nas rgyal
rtse lha bo grwa tshang gi gdan sar phebs/ snga phyi nges med du sku zhang blo bzang mkhas btsun/ grub dbang nor bu chos 'phel/ la

stod chu bzang sprul sku/ 'brog khang pa 'jam dpal mkhyen brtse sogs bsten nas chos gsan/ rjes su ri phug gi gdan sar phebs nas 'chad spel mang du gnang bas brgyud 'dzin slob
ma bla chen byams pa smon lam bsam gtan/ lce btsun bstan 'dzin 'phrin las sogs yin la/ dgung lo brgyad cu gya lnga tsam bzhugs so/ / gdan rabs bcu bzhi pa bla ma byams
pa smon lam bsam gtan ni/ zhwa lu gnas gsar lung grong byang ma'i mi brgyud du sku 'khrungs/ chos rje smon lam lhun grub kyi sku skye yin par gleng / sku na phra mo nas
skyes stobs kyi shes rab che zhing byang gling 'jam dpal tshul khrims pa'i dge phrug mdzad nas dus 'khor bsdus brgyud yongs su rdzogs pa blo ba bzung / sa skya'i lha khang
mkhan chen byams pa chos bkra shis kyi drung du rab byung dang bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/ nyin ltar gyis mtshan brjod tshar nyi shu rtsa ga cig re ma chag par kha ton mdzad/
chos rje 'jam dpal tshul khrims pa dang bla chen dus 'khor ba 'jam dpal bzang po/ dkar po slob dpon 'jam dpal mkhyen rab sogs bsten nas dus 'khor gyi rgyud 'grel phyag len
sogs la mkhas bar bslabs/ gzhan yang sa skya'i bdag chen ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros/ lha khang chen mo'i zur 'chad pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ rin sdings slob dpon rin
chen bstan pa dar rgyas/ srod rgyud mkhan chen bsam gtan rgya mtsho/ zhi ba lha'i sprul sku 'phags pa

dge legs rgyal mtshan sogs bla ma mang du bsten nas gsan bsam rgya cher mdzad/ phyis de dag las chos thob pa'i gsan yig kyang rtsam pa gnang / khang rnying grwa tshang dang
de rjes byang gling gi gdan sar phebs nas chos 'khor bskor/ dpal 'khor chos sde rin sdings pa/ dus 'khor ba/ chos 'khor ba rnams kying kyang gdan drangs nas chos mang du
zhus/ 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa dkon mchog 'jigs med dbang pos kyang rdor dbyings kyi dbang dang / dus 'khor gyi rgyud 'grel sogs gsan/ dgung lo drug cu re gsum pa la ri phug
tu sku gshegs/ / / /gdan rabs bco lnga pa chos rje rin chen byams pa chos 'phel ni/ zhwa lu bsam yas pa'i zhal ngo'i brgyud du me pho stag gi lo sku 'khrungs/ paN chen
dpal ldan ye shes kyi drung du rab tu byung zhing bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/ bla chen byams pa smon lam bsam gtan/ grub dbang blo gsal bstan rgyan/ lce btsun bstan 'dzin 'phrin
las sogs yongs 'dzin du bsten nas thos bsam rgya che ba gnang zhing thugs rgyud 'byongs pa'i tshad du phyin/ bu lugs kyi rgyud sde rnams la mkhas par gyur nas thog mar khang
rnying grwa tshang gi gdan sa mdzad/ der 'chad nyan rgyun ring pa gnang zhing gdugs dkar lha mang gi sgrub dkyil sogs kyang nag 'gros su sdeb/ de nas bla ma byams

pa smon lam bsam gtan sku gshegs nas byang gling gi gdan sar phebs te chos 'khor bskor/ slar thugs dam la sgril bar bzhed nas gdan sa yang bshol te ri phug shar gling gi char
sku mtshams thogs shig mdzad/ de nas dgun po zhwa lu mthil du phebs nas dgung lo lnga bcu nga bdun pa chu mo phag gi lo bzhi sde'i brang khang du sku gshegs/ / / /gdan
rabs bcu drug pa chos rje rin chen sbyin pa chos 'phel ni/ zhwa lu g.yu khang pa'i khyim du yab zhal ngo don ldan dang / yum bres snang bu khrid gnyis kyi sras su sku 'khrungs/
yab yum dag gis mtshan legs pa don grub ces btags/ de rjes rab tu byung zhal zhwa lu pa'i lugs kyi slob gnyer dang bsnyen rdzogs tshar nas dkar po grwa tshang pa'i
gdan sar phebs/ snga phyi nges med du bla ma rin chen don grub/ lce btsun bstan 'dzin 'phrin las/ mtshungs med byams pa chos 'phel/ grub dbang blo gsal bstan rgyan sogs
bshes gnyen dam pa mang du bsten nas chos gsan/ sa skyar phebs nas bdag chen dbang 'dus snying po la dbang chos du ma phul/ tshur yang kyai rdor dang phur ba'i dbang sogs
zhus/ bdag chen nas kyang / 'gyur med gzhom zhig bral ba'i brag ri'i rtser/ /mi 'jigs gdong lngas bteg pa'i khri steng du/ /khyab bdag gdod ma'i mgon po zhwa lu pa/ /rin
chen gtsug gi nor bu zhabs brtan shog /ces bya ba sogs

zhabs brtan bden chog dang bcas yongs 'dzin gyi gtso bor mnga' gsol mdzad/ de nas bla ma byams pa chos 'phel zur bzhugs gnang bas byang gling gi gdan sar phebs/ chos don du
gnyer pa dag la dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang sogs chos 'khor bskor/ de ltar gzhan don gyi skal ba rdzogs nas pho 'brug gi lo sman drug zla ba'i nyi shu lnga la byang gling
bla brang du sku gshegs/ / | / /gdan rabs bcu bdun pa chos rje rin chen lhun grub pa ni/ zhwa lu mo dben du sa mo phag la sku 'khrungs/ bla ma dam pa sbyin pa chos 'phel
ba'i dge phrug mdzad nas slob gnyer gnang ste dgung lo sum cu la byang gling gi gdan sar phebs/ der 'chad nyan gyi rgyun yang skyong bar mdzad/ gdan sar lo ngo bdun song
pa shing mo phag gi lo zur du bzhugs pa yin no/ /de nas bshad sgrub kyi bya ba 'phel rgyas su mdzad pa'i mthar nyid kyi dgung lo drug cu re gsum pa glang lo smin drug
can gyi zla ba'i yar ngo'i tshes bcu la sku gshegs/ / | / /gdan rabs bco brgyad pa bdag gi bla ma khyab bdag ye shes dpal 'byor de nyid/ zhwa lu dga' lung spag ra ba'i khyim
yab rje po thog rgod dang / yum ngag dbang chos 'dzoms gnyis kyi sras su me pho khyi'i lo la sku 'khrungs/ gzhon nu'i dus nas rang gi khu bo khang rnying dpon slob

gtsug rgyan pa'i dge phrug mdzad de kha bton chos spyod rnams bslabs/ chos rje gsung rabs rgya mtsho la rab byung dang dge tshul bsgrubs/ dgung lo bcu gsum tsam la ri phug
tu dge rgan sku gnyer rin chen bstan 'dzin gyi drung du bzhugs nas rgyud sde bzhi'i cho ga'i dpe 'dzin la 'grus par mdzad/ bla ma dam pa byams pa smon lam bsam gtan la rtse
mo rigs bsdus kyi dbang sogs dang / chos rje byams pa chos 'phel pa la dus 'khor gtso bor smos pa'i dbang bka' mang ba gsan te dkyil 'khor so so'i phyag len gar dbyangs
bris thig sogs la dpyis phyin par sbyangs nas ring por mi thog par mkhas pa'i go 'phang brnyes/ dgung lo nyi shu lon nas rje btsun bla ma blo bzang dge legs dpal bzang
po'i drung du bsnyen rdzogs bzhes/ mkhan po de nyid dang / lce btsun bstan 'dzin 'phrin las/ grab mchog blo gsal bstan rgyan/ gong gi bla ma gnyis pa bcas la rtsa ba'i bla
ma bka' drin can du 'dzin cing / gzhan yang chos gsan pa'i bla ma ni/ chos rje sbyin pa chos 'phel/ chen po ye shes bkra shis/ dpon slob rin chen legs grub/ chos rje khang
rnying pa rin chen skal bzang / sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros/ bdag chen dbang 'dus snying po/ bco brgyad khri chen ngag dbang kun dga' mkhyen rab sogs yongs
su dril bas bla ma nyi shu tsam dad cing gus pa'i sgo nas mnyes par mdzad cing de

dag las chos kyi gsan pa mtha' yas par mdzad pa yin no/ /de nas thog mar rab rgyas grwa tshang gi gdan sar phebs nas 'chad nyan gyi rgyun skyong ba mdzad/ dgung lo lnga bcu
nga gcig pa 'dzin byed ces pa me pho byi ba'i lo smin drug can gyi zla ba'i tshes bco lnga la ri phug gi khri thog tu phebs/ der lo gcig lhag tsam las ma bzhugs par khri
bshol nas bsam gtan khang bur thugs dam la bsgril nas bzhugs shing don du gnyer ba dag la gsung chos kyang ci rigs pa gnang/ rtse chen dus 'khor pa dang / dbang ldan chos
'khor bdag gis kyang dgon par spyan drangs te rtse mo rigs bsdus kyi dbang sogs zhus/ rgyun par ri phug tu thugs dam kho na mdzad/ zla ba ngo re bzhin gyi yar ngo mar ngo'i
tshes bcu dag la rje btsun na ro mkha' spyod ma'i sgrub mchod rgyas pa re yang gnang / da rgan po 'chi khar oM gsum ma kha re bgrangs nas sdod pa min pa gzhan nyams
len gyi chos tsam mi yong ba 'dug gsung pa zhig yod kyang de 'dra khengs skyung ba rang yin/ don la thugs dam zab mo kha chu bo'i rgyun bzhin du bzhugs nas dgung lo drug
cu bzhes pa shing mo bya'i lo/ /dbo zla ba'i tshes bcu gnyis la zhi bar gshegs so/ / / /gdan rabs bcu dgu pa chos rje ye shes bsam grub ni/ lcags mo yos la 'khrungs/ chos
rje byams pa smon lam bsam gtan la

rab byung dang / grub dbang blo gsal bstan rgyan la bsnyen rdzogs zhus nas khang rnying slob dpon mdzad/ dgung lo zhe brgyad pa sa pho stag gi lo byang gling gi gdan sar phebs/
der lo ngo bcu khri bzang nas me mo phag la zur bzhugs mdzad nas/ dgung lo drug cu re drug pa me pho spre'u'i lo zhwa lu'i gzim khang byang du sku gshegs/ / | / /gdan
rabs nyi shu pa chos rje skal bzang don grub ni/ 'khrungs sa zhwa lu phu shar gyir sgang pa yin/ bla ma dam pa ye shes dpal 'byor gyi rjes su bzungs nas rab rgyas bla ma
dang de rjes byang gling gi gdan sar phebs te der sku gshegs/ / / /gdan rabs nyer gcig pa chos rje rin chen dpal ldan da lta khri thog na bzhugs bzhin pa'o/ /ri phug byang
gling gi gdan rabs zur tsam smos pa'i skabs so/ / / /gsum pa gong smos kyi gdan rabs sogs su ma byung pa'i bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i gdung 'tshob kyi bla ma dge ba'i
bshes gnyen phyi rabs kyi gdul bya rnams la bka' drin che ba 'di rnams yin te/ de yang rdo rje 'chang rin chen bsod nams mchog grub yab sras dag gi gsung las 'khrungs
pa'i mkhas grub rin chen chos legs/ bla chen bsod nams rgya mtsho/ 'brog khang pa 'jam dpal mkhyen brtse/ 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos mchog ste bzhi yin na/ mkhas dbang rin
chen chos legs ni/ 'khrungs yul zhwa lu'i chu bskor rje sde ba yin/ rigs

pa'i gnas mtha' dag la mkhas shing byang sems zhi dul che la dbang lung man ngag mang po'i gter mdzod du gyur pa zhig go / / /bla chen bsod nams rgya mtsho ni gzhis ka rtse
sgo ri pa'i zhal ngo'i brgyud du sku 'khrungs shing gzhon nu'i dus nas tshul khrims rnam par dag la dus 'khor bsdus rgyud la sogs pa'i gzhung mang dag thugs su chud cing
gsang 'dus rim lnga dang gshed dmar sa spros med kyi rnal 'byor rnams nyams su bzhes pa'i thugs dam rtogs pa bzang ba dang / zhwa lu mthil gyi chen po'i gdan sar phebs nas
bu ston bka' 'bum la sogs pa'i chos 'khor rgyun ring ba bskor nas zhwa lu pa'i bstan pa la bka' drin che ba mdzad pa yin no/ / / /'brog khang pa grub dbang 'jam dpal mkhyen
brtse de ni ri phug tu tshe blos btang gis sgrub pa 'ba' zhig mdzad nas nyams rtogs bzang po thugs la 'khrungs pa'i rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen por grags shing
'chad nyan kyang rgya cher gnang ba'i 'phrin las kyi rgyun ma chad par yod do/ / / /'jam mgon dpal ldan chos mchog de ni zhwa lu tshe dben gyi nor rgyas khang gsar zhes pa'i
khyim du 'khrungs nas phyis rim gyis dge bshes chen por gyur ba'i mthar mthil gyi tshogs chen dbu mdzad dang rjes khang rnying grwa tshang gi gdan sa yang re zhig gi
bar du bzung / de nas ri

phug tu bya bral kun spang gi brtul zhugs lhur bzhes nas thugs dam sgrub pa gtso bor mdzad/ don gnyer can gyi gdul bya bsam gyis mi khyab pa smin grol la bkod cing / ka thog
rig 'dzin tshe dbang nor bu/ lcang skya rol pa'i rdo rje/ klong rdol blam ngag dbang blo bzang sogs kyis kyang dam pa 'di nyid kyi zhabs la gtugs nas chos mang du zhus
so/ /bla ma de dag gi gsung las 'khrungs pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen 'chad nyan gyi rgyun 'phel ba la grags che ba 'di rnams yin te/ sku zhang blo bzang mkhas btsun/ dus 'khor
bla chen 'jam dpal bzang po/ grub chen byams pa chos rgyal/ chos rje rin chen don grub dang bzhi'o/ / | / /sku zhang blo bzang mkhas btsun ni 'khrungs sa zhwa lu mo dben
pa yin kyang gnas gsar dge 'phel gyi gdung rgyud pa zhig gi zur sras su grags pas sku zhang pa'i mtshan thogs/ phyis rim gyis khang rnying grwa tshang gi gdan sa bskyangs
te 'chad nyan rgyun ring ba gnang / gsang 'dus sogs la yig cha 'ga' zhig kyang gsung rtsom dzad pa dang lung rtogs kyi yon tan rgya che la gzhan phan 'phrin las kyi
rgyun bzang ba byung ngo / / | / /dus 'khor ba bla chen 'jam dpal bzang po ni/ zhwa lur sku 'khrungs shing chos sgor zhugs nas rgyud sde spyi dang khyad par dus 'khor mkhas
pa rang mkhyen/ rjes su nyang stod mkhar kha dus 'khor ba'i gdan sar phebs nas

chos 'khor bskor/ sku tshe'i mjug la ri phug tu bzhugs nas dus 'khor/ gsang 'dus sogs rgyud ssade mang po'i dbang bka'/ bshad bka'/ khrad bka' sogs kyi 'chad spel gnang zhing
dgung lo dgu bcu la nye ba bzhugs par grag go / / /bla ma byas pa chos kyi rgyal po ni/ 'khrungs rA tsa shar nub kyi mda' rtse tho zhes pa yin/ chung ngu'i dus nas zhwa
lur btsun pa mdzad nas e waM mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims lhun grub pa'i drung du rab byung dang dge tshul bsgrub/ mtshan byams pa rin chen lhun grub chos
kyi rgyal po zhes btags/ mkhan chen de nyid kyi drung du/ mi g.yo ba dkar po/ 'jam dkar ma ti lugs/ sman bla/ rnam 'joms ljang sngon sogs kyi rjes gnang gsan/ 'jam mgon
dpal ldan chos mchog pa'i drung du/ gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa/ 'jam rdor/ gshed skor/ mnyam sbyor/ rigs bsdus/ ma hA ma ya/ padma dra pa sogs dbang bka' shin tu mang ba gsan/
grub dbang rin chen brtson 'grus la dus 'khor dang kyai rdor sogs gsan/ bla chen bsod nams rgya mtsho dpal mchog rigs bsdus sogs kyi dbang bka'/ chos skyong gi rjes gnang
sgrub skor sogs dang / 'brog khang pa grub dbang 'jam dpal mkhyen brtse la 'od zer can ma'i rjes

gnad las tshogs/ phyag rdor 'byung 'dul/ tshe dbang mda' 'phel ma/ sgrol ma nyi su rtsa gcig gi rjes gnang sogs chos bka' mang ba gsan/ gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang
kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas kyi drung du/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i skor/ rdo rje 'jigs byed sogs kyis mtshon dbang chos mang ba gsan/ /thog rig 'dzin chen po tshe dbang
nor bu la dus 'khor sbyor drug sogs gsan/ brag g.yab sku skye phun tshogs rgya mtsho'i ma chos rdo rje la 'jam dpal gsang ldan/ phyag rdor 'khor chen/ rdo rje gdan bzhi
sogs kyi dbang bka'/ gshed dmar spros med sogs khrid bka' mang ba gsan/ rin chen 'jam dpal chos dbang la bde mchog lcu i pa'i dbang bka' sogs gsan/ slob dpon 'jam dpal chos
dar la gsung 'dus rim lnga sogs gsan/ gzhan yang chos 'brel thor bu gsan pa'i bla ma ni/ grub dbang sangs rgyas bstan pa/ thar rtse nam mkha' bsam grub/ ngor pa dge slong
chos 'phel rgya mtsho/ rje btsun blo bzang ye shes/ rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtsho/ byang gling pa 'jam dpal tshul khrims/ rin chen 'jam dpal bstan 'phel/ yongs 'dzin
rin chen 'jam dpal don grub sogs mang du bsten nas thos pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol du phyin par mdzad do/ /dgung lo nyi shu lon nas bkra shis lhun po'i shar rtse zhal snga
nas yol dkar ba blo bzang mgon pos mkhan po

mdzad de bsnyen rdzogs bzhes/ de nas slob gnyer rnams tshar ba dang chen po byang ma'i gdan sar phebs nas 'chad nyan gnang pas/ re zhig gi tshe zhwa lu bla brang pa'i las byed
rnams dang thugs ma mthun par/ khong tshos bla ma nyid kyi phyag zhabs kyang bkyigs nas bla brang du btson la bzungs/ zhwa lu mthil gyi grwa pa rnams ni ri phug tu sgrub
mchod la bzhugs skabs yin gshis/ der lha mo'i cho 'phrul yin nam zer/ bud med gcig gis ma Ni chen mo nas rgyang skad chen pos ri phug ti btsun pa kun bos nas lo rgyus
bshad pas/ grwa pa rnams ha las ste zhwa lur rgyug nas bla brang gi sgo rtsar bsdad kyang sgo bsdams nas brda lan tsam yang ma byung / / / /dgon bla brang la me rgyag pa
yin no byas pas/ nang gi lte bo kun yang gtsug lag khang dang bla brang la bar khyad kyi chos nas 'brel med par brten/ mes bsregs kyang dog pas bred nas de ma thag bla ma
phyag zhabs bkyigs bzhag pa de ga la rab gsal ring mo'i sgo mang nas mar zhul thag la bsrings dgos pa byung / de lta bus rkyen byas te kha mchu cher langs pas thugs skyo
ba skyes nas ri phug gi rin chen skyed tshal du tshe blos btang gi sgrub pa 'ba' zhig mdzad/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i sbyor ba yan lag drug dang gsang 'dus rim lnga'i rnal
'byor sgom pa lhur bzhes pas

nyams rtogs khyad par can 'khrungs/ yul gyi gzhi bdag a sho'i brag btsan pa sogs mi ma yin mthu bo che rnams kyang dad nas dngos su 'ongs te zhabs tog byed pa byung / de'i
tshe sngar zhwa lu bla brang du sku la bdo ba'i lte bo thog rgod zer pa la yang kho rang gi mthong yul du rje nyid nam mkha' la 'phur byon pa'i chos gos kyi grwa zur kho'i
mig la rdeg cing 'dug zer/ nyin mtshan kun tu smre dngags drag po 'don dgos pa'i mig la zug zer bzod glags med pa byung ste rje nyid kyi drung du 'ongs nas bshags pa phul
bas/ zhabs skyong ba mdzad nas zhabs mthil lces bldags gyis gsung / khos kyang de ltar byas pas mod la sngar gyi sdug bsngal las grol ba sogs tshar gcod rjes 'dzin gyi
nus pa che bar bstan/ de nas don gnyer can mang po la/ dpal mchog rigs bsdus/ dpal mchog rdo rje sems dpa'/ 'jam dpal gsang ldan/ sangs rgyas mnyam sabyor sogs dus der dbang
rgyun chad du nye ba mang po'i dbang bka' dang / sbyor drug / rim lnga/ spros med sogs kyi chos 'khor rgyun ring ba bskor/ mthar zhing khams 'phos nas bur zhu ba'i tshe
yang / ljags spyan/ thugs sogs ma tshig par byon zhes grags/ brgyud 'dzin thugs kyi sras grub dbang blo gsal bstan rgyan/ lce btsun bstan 'dzin 'phrin las/ byang gling
pa byams pa chos 'phel/ chen po ye shes bkra shis

rnams so/ / | / /chos rje rin chen don grub de ni/ 'khrungs sa zhwa lu mo dben pa yin/ bla chen bsod nams rgya mtsho/ 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos mchog /grub dbang rin chen brtson
'grus/ chos rje 'jam dpal tshul khrims/ ka thog rig 'dzin tshe dbang nor bu/ sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros sogs bsten nas rgyud sde spyi dang khyad par dus
kyi 'khor lo la sbyangs/ rab rgyas grwa tshang gi slob dpon re zhig gi bar mdzad/ de rjes ri phug tu kun spang mdzad nas bzhugs/ dus 'khor nas bshad pa'i go la/ skyes bu'i
lus tshad/ sham bha la'i zhing bkod/ dpal ldan 'bras spungs kyi mchod rten sogs kyi dpe ris kyang mang du bkod/ khyad par gar dbyangs bris thig gi phyag len spel ba la
spro ba cher mdzad nas de dang de la mkhas grags thon pa'i slob bu yang mang du byung / gzhan yang dbang rjes gnang mi 'dra ba mang po'i rgyun 'chad spel gnang ba sogs bu
lugs kyi bstan pa la phyag rjes che ba mdzad nas sku tshe'i mjug la lhan sngon gyi ri khrod du phebs nas der zhing brje ba'i tshul bstan slob ma'i gtso bo/ chos rje gsung
rab rgya mtsho/ lce btsun bstan 'dzin 'phrin las/ rab rgyas slob dpon rin chen legs grub/ khang rnying slob dpon rin chen skal bzang

dkar po slob dpon spyi nang chos 'phel sogs 'chad nyan 'pher ba mang du byung ngo / / | / /grub dbang blo gsal bstan rgyan de nyid ni/ 'khrungs sa zhwa lu mo dben du yab jo
btsun sangs rgyas tshe dpal dang / yum sras mo dpal gyi sras spre'u zhes pa me mo lug gi lo sku bltams/ dgung lo lnga tsam gyi dus nas mi rtag pa dang 'khor ba la zhen pa
ldon pa'i nges 'byung dang skyo shas drag po lan mang du 'khrungs/ yab kyi klog sogs bslabs pas 'bad rtsol cher mi dgos par mkhyen tsang dgung lo bdun bzhes pa chu mo glang
gi lo/ /ri phug chos kyi pho brang chen por phebs nas rje bla ma byang gling pa rin chen 'jam dpal blo gsal dpal bzang po las rab byung dang dge tshul gyi sdom pa bzhes/
mtshan rin chen blo gsal bstan rgyan zhes pa'ang de nyid kyis btags/ rjes su thu'u bkwan rin po che blo bzang chos kyi nyi mas blo gsal bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan du bsgyur
ba mdzad/ zhwa lu pa'i don zhags/ rdor dbyings/ rtse mo/ dus 'khor sogs kyi slob gnyer gnang nas ri khrod byams pa gling du bi lung bla ma yon tan rgya mtshos bka' 'gyur
gyi lung gnang gi 'dug pa der yongs su rdzogs pa gsan/ de nas smon grub khyung rtser ma bab tha'i ji tshe ring bkra shis kyi mchod gnas mdzad dgos pa'i zhu ba phul ba
ltar der phebs nas bka' 'gyur klog 'don gnang

bas sngar thugs la nges 'byung drag po yod pa'i khar mdo sde rnams gzigs pas rkyen byas te 'khor ba'i phun tshogs gang la yang mi smon zhing de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam thar
la rjes su slob 'dod kyi dad pa tshad med pa 'khrungs/ snga phyi dril bas bka' 'gyur yongs su rdzogs pa tshar gsum rje rang nyid nas klog par mdzad/ bla ma dam pa byams pa
chos kyi rgyal po/ byang gling pa 'jam dpal tshul khrims/ dkar po chos rje ye shes grags pa sogs las bu lugs kyi dbang chos rnams gsan zhing de rjes 'ba' ra ba'i kun mkhyen
chos rje ngag dbang ye shes de nyid sngar ngo mkhyen cing thugs la 'dogs par yod pas 'ba' ra'i yang dgon bla brang du phebs/ rje de nyid la skyes mchog chen po'i gdams
pa rnams rdzogs pa zhig gnang dgos tshul zhus pas/ bla mas kyang dgyes bzhin du zhal gyis bzhes nas/ thar par 'jug pa'i gru bo skor gsum/ 'ba' ra ba'i khrid chen brgyad/
rje yang dgon pa'i ri chos chen mo sogs chos bka' shin tu mang ba gnang / smon lam lhun grub zer ba'i ras gzhig dang gnyis pos/ lus sbyong lnga bcu pa dang nyi shu pa
sogs 'khrul 'khor gyi lag len rnams kyang legs par bslabs/ de nas dbus phyogs su rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtsho la

bsnyen rdzogs zhu ba'i phyir du phebs kyang stabs 'grig min gyis phur lcog ngag dbang byams pa'i drung du bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i sdom pa bzhes te dge slong gi khrims nyis brgya
lnga bcu rtsa gsum gyi bcas mtshams phra zhing phra ba'i bar thams cad legs par srung bar mdzad/ bla ma de nyid sogs la sems bskyed kyang gsan nas byang sa'i gzhung
la thos bsam mthar phyin pa bskyangs te byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims yang dag pa la gnas bar mdzad/ slar yang 'ba' ra ba'i kun mkhyen chos rje'i drung du gsung chos
kyi lhag ma rnams gsan pa dang sgrub pa mdzod dgos pa'i snyan gsan 'bebs par phebs pas/ khyod sgrub pa byed rgyur 'dug gsungs nas thugs shin du dgyes par mdzad/ de yang
rje nyid kyi sgrub pa'i zhal bkod bsdus pa las/ bla ma rin po che la sgrub pa yun ring gi dam bca' zhig phul nas/ dge sbyor byed lugs kyi zhal bkod gcig zhus pa la/ 'di skad
gsungs/ sgrub pa gnyugs su bsring ba'i dam bca' len pa nan tar bzang / sgrub pa byed lugs la 'di ltar dgos pa yin/ dge sbyor gyi mgo legs par 'don pa'i ming kho/ tshe
stod tshe smad thams cad du gnas ri khrod kyi dgon pa bsten pa zhig dgos/ tshe 'di'i sgrub blo skad cig kyang med pa zhig dgos/ nye 'brel gyi 'khri ba legs par chod pa cig
dgos/ nor longs spyod kyi gsog rum nam yang

spong ba cig dgos/ pha yul gyi sred pa rtsa ba nas chod pa cig dgos pa yin/ zhes sogs zhal gdams mang du gsung tshul phyi yi ge zur na gsal ba ltar ro/ /kun mkhyen chos rje
'di ni gnyag dznya na ku ma ra'i skye ba yin par ayon rin po che'i lung gis zin cing nyid kyi mnal lam du'ang rgyal dbang lnga pa chen po la gsung chos 'ga' zhig 'bul dgos
pa'i grabs byas pa rmis tshul gsung ba la dpags na zur chos dbyings rang grol dang yang thugs rgyud gcig par zhal gyis bzhes par mngon zhing / rje nyid kyi rtsa ba'i bla
ma bka' drin can du 'dzin no/ /zab mo brag pa rje 'phrin las chos 'phel gyi thugs sras dam pa bsam gtan sgang gi bla ma ye shes rgyal mtshan la dpal ri bo dga' ldan pa'i
lugs kyi phyag chen rtsa ba rgyal pa'i gzhung lam gyi khrid dang / gcod dbang nam mkha' sgo 'byed/ gcod gzhung thar 'dod ded dpon ma'i khrid/ gzhan yang lam rim blo sbyong
gi skor dang / rgyal sras bka' 'bum/ bcu gcig zhal gyi dbang sogs dge lugs kyi chos bka' mang ba gsan/ bla ma 'di nyid 'phags pa'i gnas brtan pa ku la'i rnam 'phrul
yin gsung / shin tu mos pa mdzad/ de ltar thos bsam gyi sgro 'dogs chod nas dgung lo bzhi bcu bzhes pa me pho khyi lo nas brtsams te mthar sku ma gshegs kyi bar ri

phug gi sgrub khang rnam grol yang rtser gzims sgo'i them pa mi 'da' pa'i sku mtshams kho na la bzhugs so/ /de yang phal cher bug sgo 'dag sbyar mdzad de chab sogs kyang phyi
nas wa yur btsugs nas 'dren par mdzad/ lo re'i khongs su dbu skra lan re bsil ba mdzad pas de 'brag mkhan re skas btsugs nas nang du 'gro/ de tsam las gzhan pa'i rgyu
'grul bcad nas sgrub pa shin tu dam pa mdzad/ skabs shig sa skya'i bdag chen ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros dbus phebs gnang ba'i la zhor du zhwa lu'i ri mthil gyi gnas gzigs
mdzad nas phyi nang su la yang dogs gnas med par rje nyid kyi bug sgo'i 'gag tu byon yun ring po'i bar bka' mchid mdzad cing bzhugs pas/ de nas 'dag sbyar yang bshig ste
sku mtshams cung zad slod de mjal mkhan byung tshad gtong ba dang gsung chos kyang ci rigs pa gnang zhes grag go/ rje thu'u bkwan pa blo bzang chos kyi nyi ma yang zhwa
lu'i gdan sar phebs nas mjal zhing chos 'brel zhu ba gnang pas dpon slob thugs yid gcig tu 'dres/ thu'u bkwan rin po ches rje nyid la zhal gdams gnang ba 'di ltar ro/ /gnas
'khor ba'i phun tshogs thams cad la/ /yid gting nas log pa'i skyo shas kyis/ /chos sgrub pa snying por mdzad pa yin/ /khyod blo gsal bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan gyis/ /'dir
bsnyen bkur lha rdzas bcas bsrings shig /tshe

'di phyi'i mdun ma sgrub tshul gyis/ /gtam tshigs su spel ba dgos so zhes/ /gzugs yi ger bris nas bskur ba 'byor/ /dus deng sang rab byung thams cad kyi/ /chos thos pas bsgom
pa yal bor nas/ /tshong zhing las bun bskyed la sogs pa/ /dman khyim pa'i bya ba nyams len dus/ /tshe 'di snang 'khri ba kun bcang nas/ /mchog thar pa sgrub la rtse gcig
tu/ /thugs brtson pas gzhol ba khyed rnams la/ /bdag snying gi khong nas yi rangs so/ /lar da dung ji srid 'tsho yi bar/ /gyong lto gos gnyis la legs bkur nas/ /rten dal
'byor snying po len pa la/ /khyod snying rus skyed cig bstan rgyan pa/ /gzhi dam sdom rtsa ltar yal bor nas/ /lam bskyed rdzogs bsgoms kyang don med yin/ /don de phyir
srung sdom dag pa la/ /gnad dam par zungs shig bstan brgyan pa/ /lam mthun mong rim par ma sbyangs par/ /dpal gsang sngags 'jug pa'i gnas med pas/ /chos byang chub lam gyi
rim pa la/ /rgyud sngon du sbyongs shig bstan rgyan pa/ /rgyud kun slong ngan pa'i dbang gyur na/ /chos gang byas ngan 'gro'i rgyu yin pas/ /khyod nyams len gang byed
byang sems kyi/ /rtsis zin par mdzod cig bstan rgyan pa/ /dus nyin bzhin dag pa gang byas kun/ /dpal rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rgyur bsngo zhing/ /

de dmigs med lta bas rgyas btab na/ /dge 'dzad med 'phel lo bstan rgyan pa/ /lo zla ba re re tsam bsgoms pas/ /rgyud gang yang phyin par mi 'gyur pas/ /yun tshe dang sgrub
pa snyoms pa 'di/ /don gtso bo yin no bstan rgyan pa/ /'dir cung zad bsags pa'i dge ba yis/ /khyod sgrub pa gegs med mthar phyin cing / /gnas 'og min chos kyi pho brang der/
/dus myur du zhal 'dzoms 'gyur bar smon/ / zhes so/ /gzhan yang rje nyid sku mtshams dam po la bzhugs dus/ /byang chub sems dpa' dri med grags pa'i rnam 'phrul ma hA
paNDi ta dkon mchog 'jigs med dbang po zhwa lu'i phug tu phebs/ /de'i tshe rje nyid nas nged kyi bug sgor spyan zur g.yas nas zhal mjal dang phyag dbang gnang dgos zhes yi
ge phul bas/ kun mkhyen 'jigs med dbang po bug sgor mjal nas zhal mjal dang byin rlabs stsal ba'i lo rgyus de nyid kyi rnam thar nang na'ang yod ces zer/ da ltar sgrub
pa nyams su bzhes nas thugs rgyud la myong rtags 'khrungs tshul yang rje nyid kyi zhal nas/ bsre pa skor gsum la sogs chos drug gi /nyams len mi zhan nyams 'og tshud lags
kyang / chos log yin snyam ngag la bstan pa na/ /phan thogs mi 'gyur rang sar bsgom nus shog /gnyid ni phal cher 'od gsal ngang du 'gro/ lta log mi rung tshar gcod sla mod
kyang / /rang 'dod

las sbyor nyes pa che bsrung zhing / /bstan 'gro'i don 'gyur las la sbyor nus shog /ces dang / bdag gis rtse gcig bsgoms pa'i nus pa dang / /nang gi rtsa rlung khams kyis byed
pa yis/ /phyi ru lha sogs mthong snang mang yod kyi/ /mchog tu mi 'dzin gsang ba mi sgrog shog /de bzhin rig pa dwangs pa'i ngang nyid la/ /rang dang gzhan la bzang ngan
du ma zhig /byung dang 'byung 'gyur shes kyang zag bcas la/ /yid brtan mi rung kha rog sdod nus shog /ces gsungs pa ltar yon tan thams cad bum nang gi mar me bzhin du
mngon par mi mdzad kyang cung zad tsam ni tshig zur de dag las shes so/ gsung las 'khrungs pa'i slob ma'i gtso bo yang khyab bdag byang gling pa rin chen byams pa chos 'phel/
chos rje sbyin pa chos 'phel/ rje bla ma ye shes dpal 'byor/ /bya bral bla ma blo bzang rgyal mtshan/ spong ba pa chen po rje drung 'jam dbyangs bshes gnyen/ chos rje
ma Ni ba rin chen don grub sogs mang du byon no/ /bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i rnam thar snyim pa'i me tog dang / zhwa lu'i chos rab gsal sogs par pod longs tsam yang
bzhed par mdzad cing / gzhan yang gzhis ka rtse'i bshas ra 'bum pa nyams gsol gnang bas mtshon sku gsung thugs rten bskrun pa

dang / dge 'dun gyi sde la bsnyen bkur sogs rnam par dkar ba'i mdzad 'phrin re re nas smos mi lang zhing / dgung lo bdun cu don drug bzhes pa chu pho khyi'i lo chu stod zla
ba'i nyi shu gcig /kun mkhyen bu ston chen po dga' ldan gyi gnas su gshegs pa'i dus tshod kyi steng du thugs dam zab mo'i ngang nas gshegs pa'i tshul bstan/ sku gdung ril
por bzhugs pa'i mchod rten dang / gzims lam sku 'dra sku tshad dang mnyam pa sogs ri phug tu bzhengs so/ lce btsun chen po bstan 'dzin 'phrin las de ni/ zhwa lu phu nub
kyi gnas gsar dge 'phel du/ yab sku zhang pa'i gdung brgyud zhabs dang dpal chen don grub dang / yam kun dga' dpal mo gnyis la sras sku mched bzhi tsam 'khrungs pa las/
rje 'di nyid gsum pa yin cing / de'ang lhums su bzhugs pa'i tshe yum gyi rmi lam du mchod rten gcig gi nang nas gcig skye ba sogs rmi ltas ngo mtshar ba de 'dra kha yar byung
ngo / /da nas shing pho byi ba'i lo dpyid zla ra ba'i gza' tshes bzang po'i nyin sku 'khrungs/ de'i tshe 'brug gi skad lta bu sgra shin tu che ba zhig kyang brgyab pas/
nye logs kyi yul mi dag de ring sku zhang pa tsho thugs spro mdzad pa e yin/ me mda' gcig kyang bus song zer skad/ chung ngu'i dus nub gcig yab kyi chibs pa chos nyid
smug 'dzin zer ba

zhig yod pas/ de'i ming thugs la yang yang shar bas mtshan phyed tsam gyi ring mnal ma byung / ji zhig nas yul snang thams cad stong par 'dug dgongs pa'i lta ba rang 'khrungs
su byung pa dang / yang nub gcig mnal lam du bu mo 'ga' re nas nam mkha' la sus kyang mi reg /reg na dga' ba la zer/ ngas reg 'ong / nga pang du long las the gcig gsungs
pas/ bu mo gcig gis btegs nas nyid kyi phyag tu 'khyug pa lta bu zhig bsnams te nam mkha' la yug yug mdzad pas/ gnam rgyan 'dra mo zhig la thug nas nam mkha' thams cad
ling ling byas pa 'dra zhig byung pas/ bu mo rnams dga' nas ngo mtshar de 'dra zer ba'i mod la mnal sad/ phyis de skabs kyi rmi lam de yang chos nyid kyi don phran bu go
ba 'di la lta ba 'dug gsung / dgung lo bcu gsum tsam la ri phug byang gling bla brang du chos rje 'jam dpal tshul khrims pa'i drung du rab byung mdzad/ der bzhugs nas 'jam
dpal mtshan brjod dang / sku stod rnam gsum sogs nyer mkho'i chos spyod rnams 'dzin skyor 'grus pa gnang zhing rje 'jam dpal tshul khrims pa'i gsung gis/ zhabs drung bgres

pa dag la dpyad na khyed shes rab che rgyu rang mi 'dug /'on kyang sku zhang pa'i chos rje gong ma rnams yo ga rnal 'byor rgyud kyi bstan pa spel mkhan yin pas/ khyed kyang
rtse mo rigs bsdus kyi slob gnyer byas pa drag gsung / rtse mo'i dpe 'dzin mdzad cing yod pa na/ dpal 'khor chos sde'i nang tshan dus 'khor shar chen pas gdan sar phebs
dgos pa'i snyan zhu 'bul mkhan slebs te/ yab yum dag gis sku na phra ba sogs kyi mi yong shes thag bcad 'dug kyang / a khu bsod nams lags kyi zhal bzhes gnang grub pas/ dar
rtse mo'i dpe 'dzin gyi 'phrog shol te rgyal rtse'i dge rtsar dgas pa'i bde mchog mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i slob gnyer mdzad/ de nas nyid kyi dgung lo bcu drug bzhes pa
sa mo yos kyi lo/ chos grwa chen po dpal 'khor bde chen du phebs nas dus 'khor shar chen pa'i bla ma mdzad cing / snga phyir rje 'jam dpal tshul khrims pa'i drung nas/ 'chi
med rnga sgra dang / rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa sogs kyi dbang bka'/ sems nyid ngal gso sogs khrid 'ga' zhig kyang gsan/ dus 'khor ba bla chen 'jam dpal bzang po la dus 'khor
sku gsung thugs yongs rdzogs/ gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa/ gshed dmar lha lnga sogs kyi dbang

zur bka' mang ba gsan/ bla ma byams pa chos kyi rgyal po la/ sbyor drug /gsang 'dus rim snga/ gshed dmar spros med sogs khrid bka' chen po rnams dang / dpal mchog rigs bsdus
sogs kyi dbang bka' mang ba gsan/ bla ma rin chen don grub la/ bde mchog lo nag phyag rdor 'gro bzang / rnam sras kyi rjes gnang skor rnams gsan/ rje nyid kyi gcen bco
brgyad khri chen ngag dbang kun dga' mkhyen rab la rdor 'phreng sogs spyi bka' mang po dang / sgrub thabs rin 'byung sogs byin rlabs dang rjes gnang skor mang po gsan/ rtse
gdong khri chen bstan 'dzin lhun grub la gsung ngag slob bshad skor gsan/ mkha' reg chos rje blo gsal phun tshogs la zab lam nA ro mkha' spyod kyi skor dang rnam sras
be 'bum sogs gsan/ bka' 'gyur pa yon tan rgya mtsho la bka' 'gyur gyi lung gsan/ dge slong rin chen bstan dar la/ bu ston bka' 'bum/ thugs sras bka' 'bum/ mkhan rabs bka'
'bum sogs gsan/ de nas lho mon gyi ljongs su phebs nas ras chen sangs rgyas rin chen dang mjal/ bde mchog nA ro bcu

gsum ma'i dbang sogs mi pham padma dkar po nas brgyud pa'i 'brug pa'i chos skor rnams kyang rdzogs par gsan/ bla mas kyang lho phyogs kyi bka' brgyud pa'i grub thob gcig gi
sku skye yin tshul sogs rje nyid la gzengs bstod lung bstan dpe med mdzad nas thugs yid gcig tu 'dres/ gzhan yang snga phyir bsam gtan sgang pa ya' shes rgyal mtshan/ lha
ri gzims phug pa padma bshes gnyen/ chos rje gsung rab rgya mtsho/ grub dbang blo gsal bstan rgyan/ dbu mdzad bstan pa phun tsogs/ byang stag lung sprul sku sogs bla ma
shin tu mang ba gus pas bsnyen par mdad nas gsan bsam rgya cher gnang ste rgyas par gsan yig sogs yod pa las shes so/ /de nas ri phug tu sku mtshams mdzad skabs lta sgom
spyod 'bras kyi mgur gsungs pa 'di ltar/ rigs rnam kun gyi khyab bdag mchog /rgyal ba rin chen grub pa rje/ /bdag gi spyi bo'i rgyun du ni/ /rtsa ba'i bla ma rnams la 'dud/
/lta ba zhes bya gang la gsan/ /lta ba rang gi sems nyid lags/ /sgom pa zhes bya gang lags na/ /sgom pa rgyun chad med pa lags/ /spyod pa zhes bya gang lags na/ /spyod
pa blang dor med pa'i Da/ /'bras bu zhes bya gang lags na/ /'bras bu re dogs med pa lags/ /lta ba rang gi sems nyid de/ /

ma bcos so ma'i ngo bo lags/ /sgom pa rgyun chad med pa de/ /mnyam bzhag rjes thob med palags/ /spyod pa blang dor med pa de/ /spyod bya spyod byed dbyer med lags/ /'bras bu
re dogs med pa de/ /ngo bo gdod nas rnam dag lags/ /lta ba ma bcos so ma de/ /gsal stong rig pa dbyed med lags/ /sgom pa mnyam rjes med pa de/ /rdo rje lta bu'i ting 'dzin
lags/ /spyod pa blang dor med pa de/ /rig pa ye shes brtul zhugs lags/ /'bras bu gdod nas rnam dag de/ /chos sku skye ba med lags/ /zhes so/ de nas nor bu bde ldan pas
sbyin bdag byas te/ zhwa lu pa'i grwa pa rags bsdus la bu ston bka' 'bum gyi chos 'khor skor/ /gzhan yang dpang zur bka' mang po dang / byin rlabs/ rjes gnang / khrid bka'
sogs nyi ma re re bzhin du yang rgyun mi chad pa lta bu mdzad/ mdo ga gsang sngags mkhar gyi rje bka' 'gyur ba dga' ldan bstan 'dzin yang chos gsan par phebs/ khong la
na ro mkha' spyod kyi chos 'khor rnams gnang pa phyis de las brgyud nas bdag gi bla ma rje dngul chu pa chen pos kyang gsan nas zab lam nA ro mkha' spyod kyi smin grol
rnams shin tu rgyas par mdzad do/ /rje nyid kyi sngar bka' 'gyur gyi lung tshang ma gsan grub pa yin yang

gzhan la gnang ba ma byung pas/ 'di skabs rje nyid nas bkas bskul te bka' 'gyur bla mas zhwa lu pa'i grwa pa rags bsdus la bka' 'gyur gyi lung gnang bar bzhed pa la/ byang
gling nas chos rje byams pa smon lam pa'i zhabs 'bring ba 'ga' res grub mtha'i phyogs lhung dang chags sdang gi rnam pas/ bka' 'gyur bla ma'i chib pa ri phug gi gling mob
tu shor ba la bsnyad nas 'phrogs pas rkyen byas lung gnang ba'i bar gcod du gyur pas thugs skyo nas mgur gsungs pa 'di ltar ro/ skyabs kun 'dus kyi ngo bo thams cad mkhyen/
/mtshan brjod na bu ston rin chen grub/ /mgon khyod ni 'gro ba lhag par brtse/ /dus da lta rtsa ba'i bla mar 'dud/ /des mtshan ldan bla ma mang du bsten/ /chos zab dgu'i
gdams pa ma 'du zhus/ /don gcig las med do bla ma gsung / /de nyams su e long rang nyid soms/ /gzhi bdag tu bzung pa'i dgon pa ru/ /tshig kha zin gyi slob gnyer chags
sdang mkhan/ /ra tshil gyis phung dang 'dra'o gsung / /de go'am sprang btsun rang nyid soms/ /las mi dge 'dul ba'i dam chos de/ /tshig kha khyer rkyang dkar ltar mtho zhing
/ /bya ne tso'i kha sbyang cis mi mtshungs/ /da go'am rang rgyud 'dul ba mdzod/ /rang sbyangs pa'i grub mthar mkhas zer zhing / /gzhan khyad du gsod pa'i chos spong 'di/
/las 'jigs rung ngo bo bu ston gsung / /de go 'am rang rgyud 'dul bar mdzod/ /rang thos chung grub mtha'i rang

mthong gis/ /chos nga mkhas nga btsun zer zhing 'bar/ /las gang byas chags sdang skye ba'i rgyu/ /tsul bsam bzhin rgyal khams bskor na snyam/ /rgyud lung rigs kyi rang gzhung
mi 'khyongs pas/ /gzhan phyogs snga mi shes rtsod par gleng/ /dus lnga brgya'i spyod tshul sems la gzan/ /rang sems nyid ngo la kha rog ltos/ /lar lta ba 'di la'ang dgag
sgrub mang / /dgra bdag 'dzin 'dul ba'i snying rus la/ /don gshis kyi lta ba dbyings nas 'char/ /dbyings rnam dag la dgag sgrub su yi spobs/ /de go 'am sprang btsun rang
nyid soms/ /zhes pa'o/ /bkra shis lhun por phebs nas lo chen sprul pa'i sku blo bzang bstan 'dzin rgyal mtshan la sgrub thabs rin 'byung sogs chos bka' mang ba 'bul ba
mdzad/ lo chen gyi drung nas dbu ma'i lta khrid sogs gsan/ lho mtshams su byon nas 'gos yul g.ya' lung dgon par bzhugs skabs/ de'i phu ra gsum gyi gnas nang snying ri zhes
pa de nas rjes sangs rgyas rin chen pa'i bzhugs gnas dang khad nye bas bla ma dran pa'i mgur gsungs pa 'di ltar/ / / /rten mos pa'i gnas chen bskor ba la phyin pas/ /phu
gangs ri'i mdun sa spangs gshongs su slebs byung / /yid bla ma dran pa'i mig chu ru 'khor 'khor/ /de las ngan sbyong ba'i phyags shing zhig los yin/ /shar

ri bo la sems pa'i gangs ri yi dkar po/ /khong dar seng dkar mo'i 'khor sa ru bzang ngo / /nged nags ma'i ri dwags sems yid cig skyo dus/ /tshur phyi mig gzigs la sems gso
zhig mdzod dang / /lho ri bo la sems pa'i brag dmar gyi spo mtho/ /khong bya rgyal rgod po'i 'khor sa ru bzang ngo / /nged spang stod lha bya sems yid cig skyo dus/ /tshur
phyi mig gzigs la sems gso zhig mdzod dang / /nub grol gzhung la sems pa'i ne'u yi gsing ma/ /khong cang shes rta pho'i 'khor sa ru bzang ngo / /nged bdag med rkyang dkar
sems yid cig skyo dus/ /tshur phyi mig gzigs la sems gso zhig mdzod dang / /byang sta ma mtsho la sems pa'i g.yu mtsho yi sngon mo/ /khong nya chen gser mig 'khyil sa
ru bzang ngo / /nged mtsho stod ngang pa sems yid cig skyo dus/ /tshur phyi mig gzigs la sems gso zhig mdzod dang / /gnas lho phyogs la sems pa'i tsandan gyi nags tshal/
/khong rtsa ba'i bla ma'i bzhugs sa ru bzang ngo / /nged dad ldan bu slob sems yid cig skyo dus/ /tshur phyi mig gzigs la byin rlabs shig stsol dang / /zhes pa'o/ /de ltar
sku tshe'i stod smad phal cher thos bsam sgom sgrub dang 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum sogs kyis bstan 'gro'i don rgya cher mdzad nas/ dgung lo lnga bcu nga lnga zhes pa sa pho
rta'i lo/ hor zla bcu gcig pa'i tshes bcu gsum la sku gshegs/ gdung mes sbyangs pas dbu thod kyi cha nas

bdud rtsi ril bu 'dra ba'i 'phel gdung 'od zer 'phro ba gsum byon/ brgyud 'dzin slob ma'i gtso bo yang rje nyid kyi sku'i dbon po bco brgyad khri chen dge 'dun bkra shis dpal
'byor/ gnas gsar khri chen mkhyen rab dbang po/ /byang gling pa byas pa chos 'phel/ byang gling pa sbyin pa chos 'phel/ byang gling pa ye shes dpal 'byor/ byang gling
pa rin chen lhun grub/ chen po ye shes bkra shis/ rab rgyas slob dpon rin chen legs grub/ khang rnying slob dpon rin chen skal bzang / dkar po slob dpon legs bshad chos 'phel
sogs zhwa lu pa'i phyogs su 'chad nyan gyi rgyun 'pher ba rnams dang / gzhan yang paN chen rin po che'i yongs 'dzin 'brong rtse ba blo bzang tshul khrims/ gong smos
lo chen sprul sku blo bzang bstan 'dzin rgyal mtshan/ bka' 'gyur bla ma dga' ldan bstan 'dzin sogs mang du byung ngo / / / /de ltar lce btsun chen po bstan 'dzin 'phrin las/
grub mchog blo gsal bstan rgyan/ bla chen byams pa smon lam/ mtshungs med byams pa chos 'phel sogs yongs 'dzin dam pa mang po las bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i bzhed
srol gyi chos bka' phal mo che gsan zhing legs par sbyangs nas thugs su chud pa ni khyab bdag byang gling pa ye shes dpal 'byor dpal bzang po nyid yin la/ rje bla ma de la
ji ltar mnga' ba'i chos rnams yongs su

rdzogs par bdag nyid la dgyes pa chen pos gnang bar bzhed pa yod na'ang / rdor 'phreng sogs spyi bka' rnams dang dbang zur bka' kha shas re ma thob cing / gzhan ma phal cher
bum pa gang byo'i tshul du gnang ba yin no/ gzhan yang bdag gi bla ma byang gling pa ratna nI ra bho ga'i zhal snga nas dang / lce btsun ratna pra dznye ndra se na de nyid
las kyang bu lugs kyi dbang chos du ma'i bka' drin zhus so/ /gong du smos pa'i lo rgyus kyi tshogs 'di dag ni rang nyid kyi gong ma'i rnam thar gyi yi ge rnyed pa las
btus pa dang / gzhan 'ga' zhig las brgyud nas thos pa'i tshul rnams phyogs gcig tu bkod pa yin gyi/ da dung slad nas blo gros gzu bor gnas pa'i dpyod ldan 'ga' zhig srid
na de dag gis gsar du rnyed pa'i lo rgyus kyis zur rgyan bya bar spro na yang bkag pa med la/ mi bcos su mi rung ba dag mchis nas yang bco bar byos shig /de las gzhan pa'i
shes rloms gya tshom du zhugs pa dag gis sgro skur gyis bslad par ma byed cig /tshul de dag gis ni gsol 'debs kyi gzhung gi don rnams kyang legs par bkral zin pa'o/ /'dir
smas pa dpal stug zas gtsang sras kyi dgongs pa'i tshab/ /rlabs chen 'khyil ba'i snying po'i gzhal dka'i gter/ /ma lus 'dren pa'i dran dbang shing rta che/ /rtsod pa
yongs dang bral ba bu ston rje/ /gang gi bka' srol bzang po'i lus brtas shing / /bshad dang sgrub pa'i gom stabs lhod po ru/ /gangs

can 'dzin ma'i thig ler sgyur mdzad pa'i/ mkhas mang glang po'i yon tan bsam kyin dad/ /'dabs chags sgro yis sras brtan rdo rje'i brag /zad 'dod ji bzhin dam pa'i mdzad tshul
ni/ /dpag yas gangga'i chu rgyun byis pa'i blos/ /'bad pas hub kyis drangs kyang 'dren nus ci/ /'on te rtogs brjod tsandan rgyas pa'i tshal/ /ngo mtshar ga bur 'thul ba'i
nags klung nas/ /ngang tshul cha tsam phye pa'i dri gzhon mchog /bsod nams byed ba'i dpal las bskyod pa yin/ /a ho rnam dkar yongs 'du'i 'khri shing rtser/ /dus gsum
dge ba'i me tog brgya bye nas/ /yab rje thams cad mkhyen gzigs rin chen grub/ /dgyes pa'i mchod sprin bzang por smin gyur cig /ces dpal ldan zhwa lu pa'i bstan pa la bka'
drin chen ba'i skyes bu dam pa rnams kyi rnam thar lo rgyus ngo mtshar dad pa'i 'jug ngogs zhes bya ba las/ gdan rabs sogs bshad pa'i sarga te bzhi pa'o/ // /gsum pa gsol
'debs kyi mjug gi don la gsum/ /zhing mchog dam pa rnams la yan lag bdun pa 'bul ba/ 'dod don la smon lam gdab pa/ mdzad byang bshad pa'o/ /dang po ni/ | mchog gsum kun
gyi ngo bo dngos brgyud kyi/ /dpal ldan bla ma gdan gsum tshang ba'i mgon/ /dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i lha yi tshogs bcas la/ /ganggA'i klung rdul lus sprul gus phyag 'tshal/
/nam mkha' mdzod kyi sgo phye mchod par 'bul/

phra rags sdig ltung nes so cog kun bshags/ /dge tshogs gang gis bsgrubs kyang snying nas rang / /ston pa yongs la dam chos gsung bar bskul/ /zhi mthar mi gnas g.yung drung
rtag brtan gsol/ /bsod nams byas rnams mkha' mnyam sems can gyi/ /byang chen thob pa'i rgyu ru legs bsngos pa/ /bsam pa ji bzhin lhun gyis grub par shog /ces pa ste tshig
de dag go sla bas 'bru snon ma dgos so/ /gnyis pa 'dod bya'i don la smon lam gdab pa la bzhi ste/ bstan pa rgyas par smon pa/ de'i 'gal rkyen zhi zhing mthun phyogs rgyas
par smon pa/ zhar byung khyad par ba 'ga' zhig smon pa/ bden brjod kyi mtha' rten pa'i/ /dang po la yang spyi dang bye brag gnyis kyi dang po ni/ srid gsum bcud kyis nya
phyis yangs pa'i khog /thub bstan mu tig phyur bur nyer spungs pa/ /phan dang bde ba'i gdugs dkar grib bsil du/ /'jig rten khams kun yongs su ngal gsor shog /ces pa ste
tshig 'di dag snyan dngags kyi gzhung dang sbyar na gzugs can gyi rnam grangs yin kyang / brjod don gyi snying po go bde bar bshad na/ de yang srid pa gsum ni/ 'dod khams/
gzugs khams/ gzugs med khams te khams gsul la zer zhing / de na gnas pa'i bcud kyi sems can rnams kyi mos pa'i blo gros kyang nya phyis kyi khog pa ltar gtsang zhing
yangs pa'i nang du/ thub pa'i bstan pa rin po che mu tig phyur bur nye bar spungs pa bzhin mdzes shing rgyas par 'gyur pa dang / de'i mthu las phan pa dang

bde ba'i tshogs rnams gdugs dkar po'i gzugs su bkod pa de nyid srid mthar khyab pa'i grib bsil du/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa kun ngal gso ba ste sdug bsngal gyi gdung ba
zhi nas ci bde bar skyid par shog cig pa'o/ /gnyis pa bye brag bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa dang tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i bstan pa la smon tshul ni/ rin chen grub
pa'i ring lugs sa srungs dbang / /smin grol man ngag gser sbyangs rgyan spras nas/ /thos bsam sgom pa'i gom stabs lhod po ru/ /sA lo'i sman ljongs gzhi la rgyu bar shog /sde
'di bud lus thugs rje brgya byin gtsug /reg pas ba ston bzhed srol lha gzugs su/ /sgyur mdzad tshar chen yab sras bstan pa'i nyi/ /'od brgyas gling bzhi'i snang ba rgyas
par shog /ces 'byung ba'i tshigs su bcad pa dang po'i don ni/ kun mkhyen bu ston rin chen grub pa'i ring lugs sa srungs dbang po ste/ glang po che'i mchog gi gzugs su
smos pa de smin grol man ngag gis mtshon pa'i chos tshul ma tshang ba med pa rnams kyis gser sbyangs kyi rgyan bzhin du spras nas mdzes pa'i dpal du 'gyur ba dang / de thos
bsam sgom gsum gyi cha nas nyams su len pa'i gdul bya gom stabs lhod po ru zhes pa dal zhing chod che'i skas shin tu rgya che bar gyur nas/ sA la'i sman ljongs sam gangs
ri'i khrid kyis phyogs thams cad du khyab par shog cig pa'o/ /de yang sA la ni spos 'byung ba'i shing

gi ming yin la/ sngon bod kyis phyogs phal mo cher lha shing shugs pa'i nags tshal stug pos khengs zer ba dang rjes su mthun par bod kyi ming la sA la'i sman ljongs zhes zer
ba yin no/ /tshigs bcad phyi ma'i don ni/ sde bzhi'i 'byung gnas bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i bstan pa 'di nyid bar skabs su nyams chags che bar bzhugs kyang / ji ltar
lha min gyis bcoms pa'i lha'i lus nyams dmas par gyur pa dang / /brgya byin gyi gtsug gi nor bus reg pa'i mod la lha'i gzugs snga ma kho bzhin du bsos nas 'gro ba bzhin/
bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i bstan pa gud pa'i lus su gyur pa de nyid kyang / gang gi thugs rje'i dpung bskyed pa'i brgya byin gyi gtsug tor rtse mos reg nas gso ba mdzad
pa po tshar chen yab sras yin pas na/ de'i bzhed srol snyan brgyud tshad ma bzhi ldan gyi bstan pa'i nyi 'od rgyas nas/ gling bzhi'i khams su spyod pa'i gdul bya rnams
la phan bde'i snang ba rtag tu rgyas par shog cig pa'o/ gnyis pa de dag gi 'gal phyogs zhi zhing mthun phyogs rgyas par smon tshul ni/ phyag rgya ba sogs sna tshogs chos
kyi rig /ma 'dres rgya gar mkhas grub ring lugs gser/ /'di phyi'i bde skyid rin du brims pa'i zongs/ /gtan bde'i gling bgrod ded dpon cher 'gyur shog /rnam thos bu sogs
rdo rje'i chos skyong ba/ /'phrin las spu sdug bkra ba'i mdongs mtha' la/ /zhon nas yid srubs che ba drung phyungs te/ /

rang bstan mtho ris mdun sar gar byed shog /ces byung bas tshigs bcad dang po'i don ni/ de yang phyag rgya chen po ba zhes dwags po bka' brgyud pa'i rjes 'brang mang po ha
shang gi sgom tsam la zhen nas lta sgom rnam dag tu 'khrul'phrul ba sogs kyis mtshon/ /gangs ljongs 'di nyid du rang rang 'dod pa'i grub mtha' sna tshogs kyi chos lugs mang
ba zhig mchis mod/ de dag phal cher yang dag dang ltar snang ma phyed pa'i skyon gyis rag gan dang 'dra ba'i chos kho na yin la/ tshul de lta bu ma 'dres pa rgya gar gyi
mkhas grub shing rta chen po dag gi bzhed srol ji lta bar kun mkhyen bu ston chen pos bkral ba'i ring lugs 'di ni bsregs bcad brdar ba'i gser bzhin du ngo mtshar bla na
med pa'i chos yin cing / bdag nyid legs su 'dod pa rnams kyis ni chos dang chos ma yin pa gnyis kyi rnam par dbye ba phyed par byas te/ tshe 'di dang phyi ma'i mthar tug
gi bar bde skyid legs tshogs ma lus pa 'byung ba'i rin du brims pa'o zong mchog kun mkhyeen bu'i lugs bzang 'di kho nar zhugs na/ gtan bde'i gling du bgrod pa'i ded dpon
skal ba bzang po'i mchog tu 'gyur bar the tshom med pas de kho nar 'gyur bar shog cig pa'o/ /tshigs su bcad pa phyi ma'i don ni/ sngon gzhon nu gdong drug gis rang gi jo
jo tshogs bdag glang sna'i mche ba bcag pa'i gtam brgyud sogs dang sbyar ba ste rgyal po chen po rnam thos kyi bu la sogs pa rdo rje'i chos skyong ba rnams kyang /

'phrin las rnam pa bzhi'i spu sdug bkra ba'i mdongs mtha' ste rma bya la zhon nas/ yid bsrubs zhes pa nag phyogs bdud kyi mthu stobs dang mche ba ma lus pa drung nas phyungs
te/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i rang bstan mtho ris lha'i mdun sar bstan pa dang / bstan 'dzin skyong ba'i gar yongs su byed par shog cig pa'o/ /gsum pa zhar byung khyad
par ba 'ga' zhig smon tshul ni/ gnas skabs su yang rdzogs ldan skye dgu'i tshe/ /bsod nams dbang thang bgo bsha' byar yod pas/ /rtsed pa'i gdung ba mngon sum lta ci zhig
/rmi lam du yang myong bar mi 'gyur shog /lo chen bu la snying nas gsol 'debs rnams/ /yang srid kun tu dga' ldan zhing mchog der/ /mi pham mgon pos dbugs dbyung rjes
bzungs te/ /rlabs chen rgyal sras spyod pas dus 'dar shog /ces 'byung pas/ tshigs su bcad pa dang po'i don ni/ gnas skabs su yang sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams
kyis smon lam dang bden pa'i stobs brjod pa'i mthu las/ rdzogs ldan gyi skye dgu'i tshe dang bsod nams dbang thang la sogs pa rnams kyang / da lta snyigs ma'i dus 'dir
bgo bsha' bya ba bzhin du longs spyod yod pa yin pas na/ de'i 'gal zlar gyur pa tshe thung / nad mug /'khrug rtsod sogs rtsod pa'i dus kyi sdug bsngal gyi gdung ba 'di
dag sems can rnams kyi mngan sum du myong dgos pa lta ci smos/ rmi lam tsam du yang myong bar mi 'gyur bar

shog cig pa'o/ /tshigs bcad phyi ma'i don ni/ skad gnyis smra ba'i lo tsA ba chen po bu ston rin chen grub la snying nas gus pas gsol ba 'debs pa'i rigs kyi bu rnams kyang
yang yang srid par nying 'tshams sbyor dgos pa'i skye ba kun tu dga' ldan gyi zhing mchog der skyes nas/ rgyal ba ma pham mgon pos chos bstan pa'i sgo nas dbugs dbyung zhing
rjes su bzungs te/ de'i mthu las bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs rlabs po che skad cig re la rdzogs par byed pa'i rgyal sras kyi spyod pas dus rtag tu 'da' bar byed
par shog cig pa'o/ / bzhi pa bden brjod kyi mtha' rten pa ni/ mchog gsum grub pa lha dang rig 'dzin tshogs/ /snyan pa'i glu len rol mo 'khrol bzhin du/ /bkra shis me tog
mandar yi char/ /'dzim ma'i khyon kun ma lus khyab par shog /ces so/ /don ni sangs rgyas dang chos dang dge 'dun te dkon mchog gsum dang / rim pa gnyis kyi ting nge 'dzin
dang ye shes la brtan pa thob pa'i grub pa'i dbang phyug rnams dang / bden tshig grub pa'i lha dang drang srong gi rig pa 'dzin pa'i tshogs rnams kyis kyang / gong gi smon
lam de dag myur tu 'grub pa'i phyir du/ bden pa'i stobs brjod pa'i sgo nas snyan pa'i glu dbyangs len zhing rol mo 'khrol bzhin du/ thog mtha' bar gsum du dge ba'i bkra
shis pa'i me tog mandar ba'i char chen po phabs nas/ 'dzin ma'i khyon kun te sa 'og /sa steng / sa bla ma lus par dge legs

chen pos khyab par shog cig pa'o/ /gsum pa mdzad byang bshad pa ni/ ces dpal ldan zhwa lu pa'i bstan pa la bka' drin che ba'i dam pa rnams la gsol 'debs kyi tshugs su bcad
pa padma rA ga'i 'phreng ba 'di ni dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i khyab bdag mkhan rin po che tshe dbang lhun grub rab brtan bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i gsung gis bskul
ba dang du blangs te/ za hor gyi bandes sbyar ba'i yi ge pa ni gnas brtan 'jam dbyangs grags pa'o/ /zhes so/ /de yang chos dang 'khor dang / ston pa dang / bka' bsdu
ba rnams phun tshogs bzhi ldan du mdzad pa ste/ chos phun sum tshogs pa ni/ dpal ldan zhwa lu pa'i bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes pa'o/ /'di ni mkhan chen bsod
nams mchog grub la sku tshe'i 'gal rkyen zhi ba sogs kyi ched du/ rgyal ba lnga pa rang nyid nas mtshan bsgyur gnang ba yin no/ /ston pa phun sum tshogs pa ni za hor gyi
bandes zhes pa'o/ /de'i mtshan dngos ni/ kun mkhyen rgyal ba'i dbang po ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho ste de nyid la za hor gyi bandhe zhes brjod pa'i rgyu mtshan gang
zhe na/ ji skad du/ smon 'gro paN chen gyis/ za hor rgyal rigs yongs 'du'i 'khri shing rtser/ /

'jig rten dbang phyug dgyes pa'i me tog dkar/ /yongs 'dzin lha dang bcas pa'i gtsug rgyan du/ /bsngags 'os 'di ni a ma ngo mtshar phul/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ 'di nyid za hor
rgyal po'i rgyal rgyud las 'khrungs pa yin cing / sngon gyi mkhan slob chos gsum gyi nang mtshan mkhan po bodhis twa 'am/ zhi ba 'tsho/ de'i sring mo slob dpon chen po'i
gsang yum lha lcam mandha ra ba dang / jo bo dpal ldan a ti sha rnams dang gdung gcig pa yin no/ /bka'i sdud byed phun sum tshogs pa ni gnas brtan 'jam dbyangs grags pa'o/
/ / /da ni bdag gis rtsom pa mthar phyin pa'i bya ba 'ga' zhig brjod par bya ste/ rnam dag gangs ri'i bskor ba'i ljongs nyang zhabs 'dzin ma'i lte ba mchog /dran pa'i
gshed bu 'byung ba'i yul/ /dbus 'gyur 'chang dang rjes mtshungs par/ /thub dbang gnyis pa rin chen grub/ /yab sras ma dros chu gter las/ /slob brgyud mkhas dbang dal 'gro'i
klung / /khor yug gser ldan gzhi la 'bab/ thub bstan rnyog pa'i dri ma bkrus/ /thar 'dod skom gyi gdung ba bsal/ /log par smra ba'i rdul tshogs bcom/ /legs bshad a dum
wa ra rgyas/ /skal bzang 'dul bya'i bhra ma ra/ /rnam grol bdud rtsis cher myos pa'i/ /dregs pa'i glu dbyangs snyan pa'i dpyid/ /phyogs kyi bu mo'i rna bar ster/ /de slad
dkon mchog bstan pa la/ /rab dkar mos dge'i 'o mtsho rgyas/ /dad pa'i wu

'phreng gyen phyur ba'i/ /gsung nan 'dzum rlabs g.yo ba'i ngor/ /dri med blo gsal zla shel ngos/ /lhag bsam ri dwags mtshan ma can/ /bstan pa'i ku mud skyong pa pos/ /lo rgyus
'od dkar 'phreng ba sbyar/ /gang tshe sgro sku stug po'i sprin/ /rnam dpyod rlung gi pha mthar bskrad/ /rang gzhan rnying gi mun 'joms pa'i/ /ngo mtshar snang ba rgya
cher spros/ /dad sogs nor bu'i gdengs ka can/ /gzur gnas ltos 'gro'i tshogs rnams kyang / /yid dbang rgya mtsho'i dba' klong du/ /dga' bas rol mo byos shig gu/ /ljon shing
me tog rgyas pa'i padmo'i tshal/ /bya dang ri dwags rtse ba'i nags klung du/ /gcig par chos don sems pa'i dgon pa bas/ /rang blo'i skyo ba sangs phyir 'di rtsams so/ /deng
dus long gtam g.yengg.yang bas yid khrid nas/ /dag pa'i gtam bzang sgrob pa nyin skar bas/ /'ga' zhig srid kyang nyas bshad srad bu la/ /khungs med rang bzo'i rdzun
g.yu spel ba nyid/ /thos pa tsam gyis nyes 'joms kun dga'i yid/ /gang gi rjes 'gro ji bzhin 'gugs nus pa/ /phun tshogs rnam thar nor bu'i lcags kyu 'dis/ /tshogs gnyis glang
po'i kha lo gyen du drangs/ /lo rgyus tshul la gdung pa'i shes ldan gyi/ /rna bar bdud rtsi'i gzegs ma 'di spros pas/ /phyogs lhung gdon gyis brlams pa'i 'byung bo'i
bya/ /log lta'i skad ngan 'tsher yang ga zha'i gnas/ /'on te 'khrul na bdag blo rmongs pa'i skyon/ /skyon med legs bshad matsis na bla ma'i drin/ /drin lan 'khor phyir dben
pa'i ri sul du/ /

du ma'i rnam thar skyong bar kho bo 'dun/ /'dun ldan yid kye re ba skong ba'i mchog /mchog tu mkhas shing grub par nges pa'i dpal/ /dpal ldan rnam 'dren bzang po de dag la/
/la 'ur dang bas thal mo sbyor bar rigs/ /rig gnas sde snod gsum dang rgyud sde'i don/ /don gnyis lhun grub bsam 'phel dbang gi rgyal/ /rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen gzigs
bu ston rje/ /rje btsun khyod las gzhan pa'i skyabs gnas gang / /e ma de phyir tshe rabs thams cad du/ /kun mkhyen mchog gi dge ba'i bshes mdzad nas/ /rgyal ba dgyes pa'i
kun spyod 'ba' zhig gis/ /thub pa'i dgongs pa skyong bar byin gyis rlobs/ /'dir 'bad dge tshogs dung dang mu tig kun mud zla zer ke la sa/ /gcig tu byas 'dra'i kha dog
dkar gang zhig bdag gis bsags pa de/ /srid zhi'i 'dren pa sgyu 'phrul sras po'i lung dang rtogs pa'i bstan srog gi /snying po mchog tu bu ston kha che'i chos tshul dri med
dar bar shog /yi ge'i gzugs kyi dundhu bhi/ /gzugs 'dzin dbyug gus bskul ba dang / /sgra dbyangs rna bar len pa rnams/ /dge ba'i longs spyod 'phel gyur cig /ces dpal ldan
zhwa lu pa'i bstan pa la bka' drin che ba'i skyes bu dam pa rnams kyi rnam thar gyi cha shas nas btus pa'i lo rgyus kyi yi ge ngo mtshar dad pa'i 'jug ngogs zhes bya
ba 'di ni/ yul mdo khams smad kyi chos grwa chen po

dga' ldan bkra shis 'khyil gyi gzhung lugs rab 'byams pa brag dgon zhabs drung dkon mchog bstan pa rab rgyas zhes bya bas lha rdzas me tog dang bcas te gsung nan chen po'i
bskul bar brten/ 'dren mchog sbas pa'i sangs rgyas byang gling pa ye shes dpal 'byor dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas dang / rje btsun gnas lnga rig pa'i paNDi ta chen po dharma
bha dra la sogs pa 'gran gyi do zla ma mchis pa'i yongs 'dzin dam pa rnams kyi bka' drin kho nas 'tsho ba'i shAkya'i dge slong spong ba pa blo gsal bstan skyong gis/
rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i myos byed ces pa shing mo lug gi lo/ rgyal gyi zla ba'i dmar po'i phyogs kyi dga' pa gnyis pa'i nyid gdan sa chen po zhwa lu ri phug gi sgrub khang
rnam grol yang rtser sbyar ba 'dis kyang / /rgyal ba'i bstan pa rin po che phyogs thams cad du dar zhing rgyas la yun ring du gnas rang gi so gnyis kyi dus sopar gyur
