cig / / /swasti/ rgyal ba'i zhing khams 'dzam gling byang gi phyogs/ /rab dkar bsil ri'i 'phreng bas bskor ba'i ljongs/ /mdangs ldan 'khod snyoms gtsang stod g.yon ru'i cha/
/legs bshad rin chen 'byung gnas zhwa lu ba'i/ /bstan 'dzin nor bu'i 'phreng ba rim byon gyi/ /rtogs brjod tshangs pa'i bu mo brgyud mang ltar/ /byed po gang gis slar
yang glegs bam rgyun/ /mi zad chos sbyin char du phabs pa 'di/ /kye ma log lam 'phyan pa'i skye bo'i mig /sngon byon dam pa'i tshul la yar blta zhing / /yang

dag chos kyi lam la 'go gyur na/ /ci ma rung snyam lhag bsam dkar pos byas/ /gang tshe mi dbang dpal 'byor lhun po pa/ /yab sras mkhyen brtse'i 'dzum dkar g.yo ba yi/ brkos
dang yi ge'i mthun rkyen la sogs pa/ /bka' yi 'khor los sbyor ba'i dge mtshan byin/ /'dis mtshon dus gsum 'bad pa'i legs byas kyi/ /'babs ldan brgya phrag tshogs pa'i gangga'i
klung / /thub bstan rgya mtshor bzhugs nas 'gro rnams la/ /zhi bsil bdud rtsi rtag tu sbyin gyur cig /'bral yod dad ldan sbyin bdag 'khor slob bcas/ /gnas skabs tshe
ring nad med dpal 'byor rgyas/ /tshe rabs kun tu mi pham mgon po dang / /rab gsal rgyal ba'i dbang pos rjes 'dzin shog /bdag kyang deng nas byang chub ma thob bar/ /yang
dag dge ba'i bshes dang mi 'bral bar/ /zab dang rgya che'i dam chos 'dzin pa la/ /'jam dbyangs gsang bdag lta bur 'gyur bar shog /rtsa brgyud bla ma'i byin rlabs bden
pa dang / /rgyu 'bras rten 'brel bslu ba med pa dang / /lhag bsam dag pa'i stobs kyis smon pa'i don/ /ma lus ji bzhin 'grub pa'i bkra shis shog / sarba mangga laM/

shog stong /

/ /rang gi rnam thar byas pa shel dkar me long zhes bya ba bzhugs so/ /

rgyal khams gyi bya bral ba dpal rin chen mang thos blo gsal bstan skyong gis/ /rang gi rnam thar du byas pa bde sdug gi tshor ba sna tshogs bdag gir spyad pa'i tshul shel
dkar me long zhes bya ba/ bla ma dang lhag pa'i lha gnyis su med pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ rnam mkhyen myu gu'i gsos gyur sman char gyi/ /byed po ba ston sras slob bcas pa yi/
/rtogs brjod chu 'dzin glal ba'i sgra dbyangs la/ /dad pa'i gtsug ldan mgu ba'i 'jo sgeg 'dzin/ /zhabs sen zla tshes gsar pa'i 'dzum ris can/ /zur phud bung ba'i mdog
can la rol

nas / snying gi ze'u 'brur kun dga'i dpyi 'jo ba/ /drin can bla ma'i rnam thar bsam bzhin dad/ /rang bzhin lhun gyis grub pa'i gshis ngo na/ /bkug pas mi khugs rgyugs pas mi
zin par/ /bzang ngan sna tshogs ston pa'i sgyu 'phrul gar/ /sgyur byed rig pa'i khye'u chung 'di ko mtshar/ /'di don 'khrul sangs dbyings su ma 'khyol bar/ /kun rtogs rlung
gis btegs nas srid pa'i mtshor/ /rgyu 'bras sdug bsngal dal 'gro'i ri mo la/ /longs su spyad pa'i pha mtha' zad nus cing / /kho bo mang thos

blo gsal bstan skyong la/ /mkhas btsun bzang po'i rnam thar yod min kyang / /sngar spyad bde sdug tshor myong rang dga'i gtam/ /sgrog la de don gnyer rnams rna ba klog /zhes
tshigs su bcad pa sngon du btang nas/ /de yang kho bo cag lta bu shes rgyud tha mal du gnas kyang / sprul sprul dang sku skye'i ming gi grags skam tsam la brten nas gzhan
gyi 'dren par rlom zhing / deng sang gi skye bo klad chung rnams ni skad stod la bsnyegs pa'i khyi rgan ltar 'a 'ur sgrog pa 'byung la/ chos nas bshad pa ltar bla slob
kyi matsan nyid tshol ba'i shes ldan ni nyin mo'i rgyu skar las kyang grangs nyung bar gyur cing / de las gzhan du zhen pas 'jug tsul tsam zhig gis tsam bu dang zol sbyor
'ba' zhig byed pa'i

grwa pa bu slob tu gtogs pa phal cher yang / dran tshad bong bu'i dbyangs ring bzhin du 'dzer bar byed la/ /'ga' zhig ni yid phrag dog gi chang gis kun tu myos shing / chags
sdang drag po'i gdon gyis khog pa dkrugs nas bdag cag gis mi gnod mi 'tshe na yang gdug 'dre nyid du blta bar byed cing tshad mar grags pa'i skyes bu dam pa chen po dag
la yang rnam pa sna tshogs pas bskur ba btab ste ngan 'gro'i 'bab stegs la gzhol bar byed pa dag kyang snang ngo / /rgyu mtshan de dag gis phyi nas bla ma'i ming tsam la
bsnyad nas bdag cag gi spyod tshul gzhan gyis smra ba po byung na ni/ ba'i nyal lugs kyis be'u ldan skyog skye ba'i dpes mtshon te bdag cag la brten nas ngag gi

nyes pa sgro bskur gyi brjod bya lhag por byas pa'i brdzun gyi phung po cir 'gyur ba dag mi shes so/ /gang bdag cag rang gi kun tu spyod pa ma bcos pa nyid bskul ba po gzhan
gyi ngor yi ger bkod tshe zog gis ma khyab pa'i phyir/ /ngag gi nyes pa brdzun du byas pa dag khegs par nges te/ de skad du'ang / g.yung ston rdo rje dpal gyi gsung las/
slob mas brtsams pa'i rnam thar phal cher ni/ che brjod grags pas bla ma zog por gtong / /des na rang gi rnam thar rang gis ni/ /sgro bskur spangs nas mdor bsdus yi ger
bkod/ /ces gsungs pa ltar ro/ /bdag cag gi spyod tshul la yang dkar nag 'dra 'dres su gyur pa'i nang nas 'dir dkar po'i cha dbye zhing bsdus nas brjod par bya'o/ /e ma ho/
de la dus thog ma med pa nas ma rig pa nas rga shi'i bar gyi rten 'brel bcu gnyis lugs 'byung ldog gi tshul du 'khor lo bskor zhing 'gro ba rigs drug gi sprul pa'i sku
ya mtshan can sku dang mdzad pa ma nges pa/ dga' ba dang sdug pa la a pha'i re mos dang rkyal pa'i re mos/ shi sha nang rdzog kho na

byas pa'i skyes rabs kyi 'phreng ba bsam las 'das pa byung ba ni bshes spring las/ re re rgya mtsho bzhi bas lhag pa yi/ /'o ma 'thung ste da dung so so yi/ /skye bo'i rjes
su 'brang bas 'khor ba pas/ /de bas ches mang snyed cig gtung 'tshal lo/ /re re'i bdag nyid rus pa'i phung po ni/ /lhun po mnyam pa snyed cig 'das gyur cig /ma yi thugs
mtha' rgya shug tshig gu tsam/ /ril lus bgrangs kyang sa yis lang mi 'gyur/ /zhes sogs gsung ste/ de lta bu'i tshul rgyas pa ni thams cad mkhyen pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan
'das kyi drung du phyin nas zhu dgos pas/ de'i sar sgrib gnyis kyi ri chen pos lam bcad nas kho bo cag mi thar ro/ /thog med dus nas 'khor ba'i grong khyer 'dir/ /'khrul
pa lu gu brgyud du bcings pa las/ /'gro ba rigs drug bar ma ngor bcas pa'i/ /skye ba'i cho 'phrul sna tshogs bstan tshod gda'/ /bdag skyes ba'i yul ni nyang stod rig pa'i
'byung gnas kyi sa'i cha/ /kun mkhyen 'phags 'od rin po che sku 'khrungs sa

la kha dang se zhes zer ba la phyis su ming 'gyur nas za kha dang seb zer ba'i grong gi nyi 'dang lu ma bya ba gna' dus bla ma dpyal pa dang / rdo rje gdan gyi mkhas grub lha'i
dbang po sogs kyi gnas gzhi 'ga' btab nas stong pa'i shul de dag las/ grong lu ma skyid sbug ces bya ba mi rabs mang por phyug po chen po dang khral tsho'i rgan dpon
sogs byas pa'i mi kha drag can mang du byung ba'i brgyud du bdag gi pha ni tshangs pa dkar po zhes bya/ ma ni dge skyed bu 'khrid ces bya ba/ pha de lo nyi shu rtsa gcig
pa dang / ma de lo sum cu so brgyad lon pa rab byung bcu gsum pa'i mig dmar zhes pa shing pho byi ba'i lo/ hor zla dang po'i nyi su gcig res gza' da lta bas spen pa dang
bu ston sogs kyis bzhed pa 'das pa'i lugs ltar na nyi ma'i zhag gi tho rengs stag gi sgang tsam la kho bo skyes so zhes grag go/ ma de yang zhag gnyis nas tshe'i dus byas
pa zhig byung ste/ kha chems su lu ma lcang ra ba'i bu mo zla ba chog 'dzam la ma ma 'chol zer ba ltar byas skad do/ /de ltar yang ma gcig gi nu ma la bu gnyis kyis 'thung
pas mi

ngoms pa 'dra snyam nas rmo rmo rab byung ma rnam rgyal bzang mos thur mas ja 'dur drangs nas gsos so/ /phyis lus po skam shing rid pa'i rgyu mtshan des byas pa 'dra zer ro/
/rmo rmo dang a ner gyur pa'i btsun ma rab byung ma yod pa de dag ni sngar zhwa lu phu'i bsam gtan sgang pa kun spangs ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi slob mar gyur pa chang 'thung
dang bkal 'thag mi mdzad cing / 'dul khrims gtsang ba lam rim bde lam gyi 'khrid thun skyong ba zhig ste/ de dag gis shin tu byams shing gces par byas nas legs par
bskyangs so/ /gog pa tsam du yod dus 'du 'byung mkha' 'gro ma zer ba zhig khyim du bos nas lha 'bebs kyin yod pas/ de la 'dre zhig bzhugs nas bu chung 'di la gdan dang lcog
rtse rgyob zer nas rgyag bcug pa la kho bo bzhag /khye'u 'di bla ma grub thob gcig gi sprul pa yin pas gtsang sbra gyis shig ces smras 'dug go /rig pa'i 'byung gnas nyang
stod 'dzin ma'i char/ /mtha' gnyis spangs pa'i rigs kyi thig

le las/ /sngon tshe'i smon lam bdud rtsis nyer drangs nas/ /dal 'byor rten gyi utpal 'di ko bzhad/ /lo ngo bzhi lon dus rmo rmo sogs kyis 'khyer nas zhwa lu'i dga' lung ri
khrod du slebs nas ri phug gi gser phib byang mar rje sman khang pa mjal bar 'khrid pas/ der shin tu ngu zhing mi sdod pa la/ gtsug lag khang gi steng du tshogs dung btang
pas ngu 'phro rbad kyi chad/ dung btang song nga 'gro zer ba zhig byung 'dug chung ngu'i dus nas nga'i mgo la sus kyang lag pa ma reg cig /skra gcod mkhan paN chen rin
po che la zhus pas paN chen rin po che'i phyag la btsog pa shor yong zer srung ba zhig yong zer/ rtsed mo byed pa'i tshe sku chung chung kho na dgos pas mgron po phyogs nas
byung ba la sku 'dra'i skyos ma khyer shog cig byas pas/ 'ga' zhig gis ched du btsal nas sku chung ster ba dang / gzhan kha cig gis rdo dang rde'u sgrugs te 'di la rang
byon ga ge dang che ge yod do byas nas byin pas dga' 'gro ba zhig byung 'dug zla mnyam gyi byis pas kho bo'i ming la yang sku 'dra tshe ring zhes btags so/ /rmo rmos lhan
pa tshos thig khra bo can gyi dum bu la thang ka'i gzugs

brnyan bcos te thig ser po rnams 'jam dbyangs/ dkar po spyan ras gzigs/ dmar po tshe dpag med/ sngon po phyag rdor rnams yin no byas pas/ de dag rang gi nyal ba'i sngas mgor
bkrams/ sku 'dra chung chung dang rang byon yin zer ba'i rdo rnams stegs la bsgrigs/ dkar yol chag dum du yon chab 'bul ba dang / gzhan dag la nga'i rten mjal la shog zer
nas rten bshad gtong / ting khrus kyis zer dkar yol chag dum gyis chu de ster rgyu byung pa la dga' ba zhig kho bo rang gis dran no/ /nged rang ma skyes pa'i gong du zhwa
lu spyi so bas grub dbang blo gsal bstan rgyan gyi yang srid skor la sa skya'i bdag po dbang 'dus snying po la lung bstan zhus pa la bka' lan stsal ba ni 'di ltar ro/
/smin drug zla ba'i nyer brgyad kyi tho rangs rmi lam du bud med gzhon nu zhig gis/ /e ma ho/ blo gsal bstan rgyan de/ shar gyi phyogs na gnas pa ste/ /rtsa yi ming can
yul gru ru/ /khyim na zangs kyi ming yod pa/ /phan yos 'brug lo pa dang / /ma ni mi phyugs sprang mo 'dra/ /khyi dang 'brel ba'i ngo yang

che / bu ni phag byi gang rigs te/ /ming ni blo gsal bstan skyong ngo / /zhes pa'o/ /de yang kho bo'i ma de nyang stod rtse chen zangs ras pa'i khyim nas bag mar btang ba dang
lo bdag khyi lo ma yin pa/ pha tshangs pa dkar po 'brug lo pa dang / nu zho blud pa'i ma de ni dbul zhing phongs pa sprang mo 'dra ba ste/ lung bstan gyi tshig zin ltar
byung nas slar yang / kho bo rang smos pas bab cing re zhig gsang ba gal che gsungs so/ /de skabs zhwa lu ri phug gi gdan sar sa skya'i yab rje khong rang gi bla ma yin
pa chos rje rin chen sbyin pa chos 'phel bzhugs pas/ khong gis byang gling bla brang gi dbang khang chen mor bos te ngos 'dzin gyi ster bya phran bu dang pha ming rnams
la mi 'khrol dgos pa'i gsung shog bskur ba yin 'dug kyang / kho bo lo lngar slebs pa dang bla ma de gshegs so/ /de phyin chad skyes sprul gzhan gyi lugs ltar sngon gyi shul
mchod mkhan nas dngos po khab skud par longs pa tsam zhig dang / kha lta 'jug mkhan byi'u thang ma gcig kyang med/ de'i phyir 'dod yon gyi 'du longs dang / sngar gyi
dpya dngos la do dam dang / grwa bu slob kyi skyong dar dang / nya ma yon bdag gi ngo srung dang / sde dgon gyi phyogs ris

dang / gyon pa lus chas dang / rta chas kyi gshom ra sogs dgos pa med pa'i phyir/ sprang po yan pa blo bde bya ba de bdag lags so/ /skyid pa yang byung ngo / /dbang 'byor skyes
bu'i yon tan dkar po'i 'od/ /gzhan phan mkha' la 'gyed par mi nus mod/ /skye bar grags pa'i ming gi stong gzugs 'di/ /cal sgrogs khron pa'i chab mtshor skyes so lo/
/de nas yul du phyin pas res 'ga' shu ba lta bu'i rma 'bras dang / res lkog ma skrangs yong ba/ chu nad kyis thebs pa sogs na tsha dang / rang nyid spyod pa 'tshub pa dang
bu rdzi g.yeng ba che bas g.yang la lhung ba dang / chu la shor ba sogs kyis 'chi tshad tshad mang po byung / 'di tsam na rang gi a ne rab byung ma gzhon pa zhig gis kyang
bslab khrims ma thub pas des lan nam/ nub re bzhin gnyid cung zad re byung ba dang har bsad rgyab nas dngos su lus po phal cher mi yin pa la gdong pa glang po che 'dra
ba/ sma ra dang / smin ma sogs las me 'bar ba zhig 'ongs nas sdigs mo sna tshogs byed byed do/ /de la rang gi mig btsums pa dang / gzhan gyi lag pas mig bkabs kyang mi
sgrib par

mthong gin yod/ thabs ci byas kyang phan par ma gyur te btsun pa bya dgos par yin nam zer/ rang lo bdun pa rab myos zhes pa lcags pho rta'i lo/ /cho 'phrul smon lam gyi dus
bkra shis lhun por phyin nas paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i spyan sngar gtsug phud phul/ 'di nas sngar gyi 'khrul snang de yang sangs song / yi ge'i phyi mo ka kha sogs
chung dus rtsed mo dang bsres nas bslab pas tshul gsal po da lta mi dran 'dug 'di dus klog bde ba tsam yong / rje sman khang pa las blo sbyong don bdun gyi 'khrid thob/ sems
bskyed cig mdzad pa'i nub mo chos zhu mkhan gzhan gyi lad mo byas nas gnyid ma log par phyag kyang btsal lo/ /lo dgu tsam lon dus ri phug tu rje sman khang pa'i drung
du bsdad nas bla mas tshig bkra bzang ba yin gsungs/ rje rin po ches mdzad pa'i lam rim gsol 'debs yon tan gzhir gyur ma bya ba de thog ma kho nar 'dzin du bcug /mtshan
mo mar me'i 'od la yang bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsol 'debs dpal gang drin ma shlau ka re bslabs so/ /bla ma 'di ni sku 'khrungs sa kho bo rang gi grong dang khad nyer
'khrungs te chung dus lha sdings dgon pa'i btsun khral rgyab pas cha

rkyen gyis phongs nas yul don dgos pa byung zhing / rjes su 'brong rtse chos sde'i btsun pa mdzad/ dgon pa de'i las tshan yod dgu mdzad dgung lo nyi shu rtsa lnga la dbu mdzad
kyi go sar phebs/ paN chen dpal ldan ye shes las rab tu byung zhing bsnyen rdzogs kyang mdzad/ yongs 'dzin paNDi ta ye shes rgyal mtshan sogs bla ma mang po bsten/ phyis
tshe blos btang gi bya bral la phebs te lho gro bo lung / kong po rtsa ri/ byang rwa sgreng sogs gnas mang po bskor zhing gnyan khrod rnams su gcod mdzad/ dgung lo bzhi
bcu la zhwa lu ri phug tu phebs nas drung cu re dgu'i bar gnas 'di nyid du sku tshe 'da' bar mdzad cing lung rtogs kyi yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnga' yang 'phral
sbas pa'i tshul tsam du bzhugs pa yin no/ de'i skabs su glu 'di'ang sems la shar 'dug a ho/ bla ma'i gdan sa ri phug byang chub kyi shing khrod/ /bu nga'i rkang chung g.yas
pa'i rgyag sa ru bzang byung / /sbas pa'i bshes gnyen blo bzang chos 'phel gyi rgyal mtshan/ /bu nga'i chos kyi slob dpon dam pa ru shar byung / /tshig bkra bzang po dam
chos yon

tan gyi gzhir gyur/ /bu nga'i chos sgo 'byed pa'i lde mig tu gtad byung / /bu ston chos rje'i bstod pa'i rab byed de rnam gsum/ /bu nga'i dang pa'i gsol 'debs snying po ru
thos byung / /a ho/ sngon sbyangs las 'phro sad pa'i yang rtse 'dra los yin/ /gsol lo mchod do bla ma mkha' 'gro yi chos skyong / /drongs shig drongs shig thar pa'i lam sna
der drongs shig /mdzod cig mdzod cig skyabs dang dpung gnyen zhig mdzod cig /gzigs shig gzigs shig 'gro ba'i sdug bsngal la gzigs shig /stsol mdzod stsol mdzod dngos grub
char 'bebs rang stsol mdzod/ /snyan no snyan no bkra shis dge mtshan gyi glu sgra/ /ldir shog ldir shog 'dzam gling mdzes rgyas du ldir shog /ces byas so/ /rang lo bcur
slebs pa dpal gdong zhes pa chu mo bya'i lo/ /hor zla gsum pa'i tshes brgyad la ri phug gi tshogs su mang ja rnam gzhag dang bcas pa rang gi a nes btangs nas sgrigs la
phyin no/ mang ja grol ba dang chos rje rin chen lhun grub kyi byang gling bla brang du 'khrid nas gsol ja/ 'bras sil/ sder ka sogs btang / chos rje rin chen sbyin pa chos
'phel gyis bzhes pa'i rtse zhwa gcig g.yogs/

grub dbang blo gsal bstan rgyan gyis mdzad pa'i spyan ras gzigs kyi bsgom bzlas ma Ni'i phan yon dang bcas pa zhig gi lung dang dpe gnang ngo / /de nyin grangs chen grwa tshang
la yang grwa ja btangs nas tshogs su phyin pas nag nya'i rgyan 'grems che rabs rten 'brel legs zhes grwa tshang nas dkar spro kha btags bcas pa byung ngo / /lo de'i
hor zla bzhi pa'i nyi shu gcig la bkra shis kyi gtsug lag khang zhwa lu ri phug gi byang gling bla brang du mkhan po rin po che don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos te byams pa
rin chen lhun grub dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas dang / las kyi slob dpon mtshungs med rin chen legs bshad chos 'phel gyis mdzad nas dge bsnyen nas bzung / tshigs snga
ma dge tshul gyi bar legs par bsgrubs so/ /de nyin zhwa lu chos sde chen po'i spyi so nas kha btags mtshan grangs dang bcas pa dang / nor bu bde ldan nas sde pa dge slong
rgyal mtshan lags dang / spyi pa rin chen tshogs 'phel lhan rgyas nas sngar rje drung 'jam dbyangs bshes gnyen de nyid kyi zhal chems su gsungs pa ltar/ kho bo la gyon pa
gsar bzos kyis bskon dang / grub dbang rin po ches

rje drung de nyid la gnang ba'i spyan ras gzigs dang / bu ston yab sras rnams kyi bris thang gcig /phyag 'phreng gzungs gzhugs la yod pa'i thub pa'i dbang po'i sku gcig /rje
yang dgon pa'i ri chos yon tan kun 'byung gi glegs bam gcig /dar yug che legs dang bcas pa thugs la btags so/ / | kwa ye 'di na mchog tu dkar pa'i phan bde'i snang ba 'di
dag ni/ /rab gsal dbyig gi khu ba las 'phos gzegs ma dar ba'i tshul min te/ /mngon mtho nges legs dmigs bu mchog gyur chos 'dul gser gyi kong bu'i nang / /'chal tshul
sgrib pa'i mun pa za byed glal ba'i lce las gyur pa yin/ /de phyir rnam gsum brje ba'i las la brel ba yang / /tshul chos 'dab stong rang dgar grol ba'i zlos gar min/ /bslab
gsum lha yi skye mched gsar du ngoms pa'i slad/ /mkhan slob sna tshogs las ba bkug pa'i phyag bris yin/ /brang 'gro gdug pa'i tshang bzhin du/ /mdzes pa'i dpal la zhe
skrag nas/ /tshangs spyod nor bu'i thems skas la/ /'dzegs pa 'di 'dra gzengs su mtho/ /de yang chang ni snga gong nas mi 'thung zhing 'di

tsam nas phyi dro'i kha zas dang / mtshan mo gcer nyal byed pa la bag yod par byas so/ /rje sman khang pa de rgyun gyi zhal 'don la 'jam dbyangs kyi bstod pa gang blo ma/ 'jam
dpal mtshan brjod/ shes bya mkha' dbyings ma/ rdo rje rnam 'joms kyi gzungs ring / gsang ba 'dus pa'i rtsa brgyud le'u dang po 'jigs byed rtog bdun gyi brgyud le'u dang
po/ dus 'khor bsdus brgyud kyi 'jig rten khams la/ sgrol ma/ sher snying / smon lam rnam gsum/ bla mchod bde stong dbyer med ma bcas chags med lta bu mdzad nas gsung pas/
kho bos 'jigs byed dang dus 'khor ma yin pa'i gzhan ma rnams zhor 'degs yong pa byas so/ /dbyar gnas kyi dus bla ma dang lhan du bkra shis lhun por paN chen thams cad
mkhyen gzigs chen po'i bka' chos zhu bar phyin te/ tshogs chen gyi mang ja tsha rting ma'i skabs seng g.yab tu nyan pas/ mngon rtogs rgyan gyi gzhung dang / 'dul ba'i rgya
gzhung 'dra mo zhig nas lung gnang ba nyi ma 'ga' byung / de nas dbu ya bzhes pa yin zer gsung chos chad song / rje sman khang pas

bkras lhun tshogs chen la mang ja zhus pa'i spos bskor zhig la yang phyin/ sngags khang du seng chen blo bzang bstan 'dzin dpal 'byor dang / grogs po nub kyi spyi khang du
sngags chen po thub pa blo bzang tshul khrims mjal/ bla ma de la steng grib kyi bsnyun gzhi byung nas gsung 'phros mi go ba 'dug kyang zhabs 'bring pa zhig gis gsung bsgyur
nas btsun chung 'di shes rab che ba zhig yod pa 'dra/ bkra shis lhun po'i btsun pa byed chug zer/ bla mas 'di zhwa lu ba'i bla ma'i sku skye yin tshul zhus song bas/ bla
ma'i sku skye yin na ka mtshan nyid kyi grwa sar bcug pas dge bshes che ba gcig yong / gzhan shab be shob be nor ma nyan la 'gro ba 'dug zer ro/ /yar lam zhwa lu bla brang
gi klu sdings su sde pa rin chen zla bas zhabs tog zab pa byung ste 'di nas bzung sde pa de spyir rje sman khang pa la dad pa che ba sgos su nged rang gi sbyin bdag
gi mthil byas nas drin shin tu che'o/ /rang lo bcu gcig tu slebs pa dngos po zhes pa shing pho khyi'i lo/ byang phyogs khal kha'i mong gol gyi bla ma mkhan chen no mo han
ri phug tu phebs nas/ khyab bdag bla ma dam pa ye shes

dpal 'byor dang / byang gling rin po che'i drung du bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa nas brgyud pa'i rgyud sde mang po'i dbang bka' gsan rgyu mdzad cing / bum chu zhal 'byed dang
ri phug tshogs chen la mang ja dngul zho re'i 'gyed bcas gnang gin 'dug rje sman khang pas kho bo la/ dbang gang gnang de tsho khyed kyis thob dgos pa 'dug ste phyag rten
re tsam 'bul rgyu med pa dang dad pa go ba med pa'i thob thob de 'dras grul ci btub/ 'on kyang zhu ba la 'gro'am mi 'gro a ne chen mo la gros dris mdzod gsung / dga' lung
du a ne sgrub pa mo la zhus pas/ bla ma'i sku skye yin pas chos zhu los dgos/ cis kyang dbang thob pa gyis shig ces kha btags bzang po 'ga' dang dngul Tam ka dkar po
bco lnga tsam bskur byung ngo / /de nas bla ma rnam pa gnyis la bdag kyang dbang la 'jug par zhu zhus te/ thog mar byang gling bla brang gi dbang khang chen mor rje btsun
dam pa byams pa rin chen lhun grub pas dpal phyag na rdo rje 'gro bzang snying po'i lugs kyi dbang bka' dang / de'i sang nyin khyab bdag ye shes dpal 'byor gyi rdo rje
rtse mo rigs bsdus kyi dbang gi sta gon mdzad/ 'di

skabs pha bla ma ye shes dpal 'byor gyis dbang gnang ba la/ rtse mo rigs bsdus/ shAkya seng ge gtsug tor dgu ba/ ma hA ma ya lha lnga/ gdan bzhi yab dka'/ bde mchog padma dra
ba/ mnyam sbyor rigs bsdus/ gshed dmar bir lugs lha lnga/ gshin rje gdong drug rwa lugs lha nyer gcig ma/ rnam 'joms dkar po lha bcu dgu grub chen sa wa ri pa'i lugs ste
dbang bka' dgu thob cing / gdan bzhi ma gtogs rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor kho na la brten par mdzad do/ /byang gling rin po ce las phyag rdor 'gro bzang / dpal mchog rigs
bsdus/ yo ga khams gsum rnam rgyal/ don zhags lha mang / gdugs dkar nyer bdun ma/ 'od zer dri med lha drug gtsug gtor dri med lha lnga dang bcas pa dbang bka' bdun po
rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor la brten nas thob bo/ /de'i mthar tshe sgrub bu ston gong khug ma yang gnang ngo / /nged rang la a nes gnang ba'i dngul dang kha btags rnams yon
du phul lo/ / | a hor 'dren mchog kai la sha ri la/ /gzhan 'ga'i bskul tshig nyi gzer lhung ba'i tshe/ /dbang gi chu rgyun ri dang tsa yi klung / /gang blo'i 'dzin mar
'jo ba'i skal bzang thob/ /

rje sman khang pa'i drung du rdo rje 'jigs byed lha bcu gsum ma'i dbang bka' tshar gnyis dang / de'i sgrub thabs/ rje btsun tsong kha pa chen pos mdad pa'i za ma tog gi lung
/ 'brong rtse lha sras rjes mdzad pa'i bskyed rdzogs kyi 'khrid yig lung / dpal mo lugs kyi bcu gcig zhal lha lnga'i dbang / de'i smyung gnas sgrub skor paN chen blo bzang
chos rgyan gyis mdzad pa'i lung / gcod dbang nam mkha' sgo 'byed dang gcong gzhung thar 'dod ded dpon ma'i lung 'khrid/ rje tsong kha pa sogs nas brgyud pa'i dbyangs
can dkar mo'i rjes gnang / sgrol dkar rjes gnang / klu dbang rgyal po'i rjes gnang / rgya gar zangs gling pa nas brgyud pa'i khyung nag me'i spu gri'i rjes gnang / nA ro
mkha' spyod kyi sindhu ra'i dkyil 'khor du byin rlabs tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gi yi ge bzhin thob bo/ /gzhan yang rje rin po ches mdzad pa'i lam rim chen mo sogs lung
mang po gzhan gyi zhor la zhus so/ /rang gi rmo rmo rab byung ma la li'i maNDal yod pa de 'khyer nas bla ma'i lad mo byas te maNDal phul/ kham pa dge slong zhig la rje'i
lhung bzad 'dug pa nga la gnang dgos byas pas byin byung

ste / gung tshigs kyi dus su phud mchod gtor ma chang bu dang bcas pa re yang bsham mo/ /rang lo bcu gnyis pa na tshod ldan zhes pa shing mo phag gi lo sar pa dang rje sman
khang pas ri phug gi ma Ni ring mo la zhig gso mdzad pa'i phyag g.yogs zhus/ sngar byang gling rin po ce dgongs pa zab cing rje sman khang pa la chos gsan pa dang / kho
bo rang gi rtsa ba'i bla ma yin pa sogs bskur ba zhu rgyu med rung / zhwa lu pa'i grwa pa mi bsrun pa 'ga' dang khong rang gi phyag g.yog 'byung po mi ma yin las gdug rtsub
dang cho 'phrul che ba rnams kyis thugs skyogs nas bla ma sman khang pa'i nye gnas dge slong gcig yod pa la brdung 'tshog byed zer ba dang / skabs gzan dang gzhan la brnyad
nas bka' skyon khyi 'khrug pa ltar mdzad do/ /bla ma sman khang pa yang / sngar ni ri phug tu dge sbyor gang 'phel bgyis nas zhwa lu ba'i zhabs tog las/ zhabs 'dren
byas pa med/ da cha 'di ltar yin na ri khrid gcig btsal nas 'gro gsungs te phebs par thag bcad dus/ smon 'grub khyung rtse nas gzhis rtse rdzong gi phyag mdzod byed pa'i
gnyer pa zla don can dang / khyung rtse ram pa ba'i sde pa mgrin gcig tu bla ma gnyis la nged rang tsho'i

sa cha 'gol ba zhig tu gzims khang rgyab phyogs pa zhu zer yang grong ltag gi dgon pa mi dgos gsungs nas ma bzhed/ 'ga' zhig nas tshong 'dus kyi chu byang na bram tshal brag
grub zer ba'i brag phug ngo mtshar can zhig yod zer ba gsan nas bla ma nyid gzigs par phebs song / yar phebs dus brag phug ngo mtshar che rgyu cang mi gda'/ rtog ldan dang
btsun ma khyo shug byas nas bsdebs shul tu 'dug /'o skol de 'drar sdod mi nyan gsungs/ de nas 'brong rtse chos sde na bla ma'i sku mched dge slong zhig yod pa'i sa nas
yi ge slebs te/ ston kha bla ma gnyis car 'di phyogs spyan 'dren zhu ba lags pas cis kyang phebs pa zhu zer nas de phyogs su phebs/ yar lam nor bu khyung rtse na nged rang
gi a lce tshe ring dbang mo can yod pa'i sar zhag 'ga' bzhugs/ nor bu khyung rtse'i lha khang mjal/ de na nged rang char lugs pa rnams kyi shing rta chen po bdag chen
rdo rje'i 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan gyis rang gnas phog pa'i lam 'bras slob bshad kyi bla brgyud 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog bzang po yan chad kyi sku dang / gnas

bcu sogs rten ngo mtshar can 'dug /ngas rjes su yang phyin nas mjal lo/ /gnas gsar rgyal khang du yum chen mo sogs kyang mjal/ nged rang de dus bong ge chung bas rta mgrin
gyi sgyid ma'i 'og la phar 'dzul tshur 'dzul mang po byas so/ /ra sog tu bye mkhar ba zer ba'i grong pa phyug po gcig gis gdan drangs nas zhag mong po bzhugs/ grong pa de'i
pha rgan po zhig 'dug pas des/ las dbang zhig gis nged rang la dga' tshor chen pas nga'i bu yin zer nas byams po ci yang byas so/ /rgan po de rjes su 'das pa'i dus kyi
tshe klad pa'i dkyil nas dbang po'i ril bu gzi 'dra ba che chung byi'u'i sgong nga tsam pa rdos bcag kyang mi chag pa zhig 'thon 'dug pa nged kyis kyang mthong ngo / 'brong
rtse chos sder phebs nas btsun pa rnams la mang ja bzang ba lnga dang 'gyed bcas btang / spyir 'od dpag med kyis gos thang tshems grub ma zhig 'bul sbyor mdzad/ de skabs
sger 'brong rtse ba'i zhal ngo 'phyong rgyas sgem bu pa bsod nams stobs rgyas kyi gdung brgyud ngo ma zhug gu'i tog yin zer ba'i zhabs drung tshe dbang rnam rgyal de
bsnyun nas grong la khad 'dug /rje sman khang pa'i 'khrus dbang 'dra mo zhig gnang song

nged cag 'brong rtse gzhol du khyim tshang zhig gi mchod ston gsol zhing yod dus zhabs drung sku gshegs pas sngas bsrungs la 'byon dgos zer ba'i gdan 'dren gyi pho nya byung
/ bla mas 'brong rtse chos sde'i chog grwa'i mgo la phebs nas kun rig gi cho ga mdzad/ ngas ni chog mi shes rung btsun chung ham pa can zhig bdog pas yon la dngul srang
brgyad tsam gyi nom pa byung ba de ni blangs so/ de nas dga' bzhi'i phu gad gser bya ba'i dgon pa skyid po shing se ba'i nags tshal yod pa zhig na/ nged rang gi sru mo sgrub
chen ma bka' brgyud gsal sgron de nyid bug sgo 'dag sbyar mdzad nas mtshams la bzhugs yos pas de mjal bar phyin nas bug sgo'i dgag tu zhag gcig nyal lo/ /nyang stod
yul gyi sman ljongs bskor du phyin/ /ra sog gzhung du pha rgan gsar pa mjal/ 'brong rtse'i khab tu dpon shi'i mchod gnas thob/ /gad pa gser gyi bya skyibs can du slebs/ /sru
mo bsgom la bzhugs pa'i bug sgo ru/ /skyid nyal zhag gcig rgyab ste log nas yong / /de rjes rje sman khang pa'i phyag g.yog byas nas sger 'brong rtse ba'i tshe cho ga
lha khang du zla ba

gcig tsam du tshe sgrub mdzad/ 'brong rtse sde pa'i phyag mdzod rgan gzhon gnyis dang nang gzan mang po la tshe dbang gnang song / de grol ba dang nged rang gi khyim nas gdan
'dren byung ste 'dus 'byung gi thad ka brgyud de gu ru 'bum pa'i slob dpon chen po'i rdo sku la phyag mchod mdzad/ yul du zhag shas bzhugs nas nyin gcig bsam gtan chos
sdings kyi sa phug gzigs par phebs/ nged kyi bzhad gad la/ 'dus 'byung rlung bo'i ra ba bskor/ /skyes skam yu la thang ka bskor/ /bsam gtan chos sdings kyi sa phug bskor/
/de gnas gsum bskor ba ma lags sam/ /zer ba byas/ la rgan rgyab nas rang gnas su phebs te zhwa lur mang ja bzang ba gcig btang / slar bkra shis lhun por phebs nas tshogs
chen la mang ja/ sngags khang du rgyud ja/ rten la mchod 'bul/ skyabs mgon chen por maNDal sku gsung thugs rten dang bcas pa'i 'bul tshan rnam grangs 'ga' phul te sngar
byung ba'i dngos po rnams 'phral dag mdzad song / rang lo bcu gsum pa 'dzin byed ces bya ba me pho byi ba'i lo de la zhwa lur ni chos rje ri phug bla ma'i phyag g.yog rnams
kyi byed 'phrin la

brten / grwa dmangs dang bla ma rgya 'dre shor ba'i 'khrug long dang / dkar po grwa tshang pa'i bla ma la khong rang tsho'i grwa dmangs kyis bsnyon dor ba'i za ri zi ri 'ga'
byas song / gzhis ka rtser gorSha'i rten chas 'gyangs pa'i rkyen las rgya nag nas cang jun zer ba'i nang blon che gnyan zhig dmag sde dang bcas phebs pa yin zer/ khul 'dir
yang shing gcod sogs 'ur shogs chen po 'dug /lo de'i mjug la nged dpon slob sger 'brong rtse bas spyan 'dren zhus te/ de nyid dbus bcud bum sgrub sogs sku rim mang po
tshugs yod dus/ de na 'dug pa'i e ma mchod ye shes chos 'phel zer ba la chu nad sogs na tsha mang po langs 'dug /khong rang gi yid la yod pa'i sman pa de mi khugs par sems
la gcong snang chen po dang bcas 'das song / des rkyen byas nas nga rang la sman pa shes 'dod chen po byung ste bla ma la zhus pas/ mdo sde gser 'od dam pa nas byung ba'i
tshong dpon gyi bu khyi'u chu 'bebs kyi lo rgyus dang / rje g.yu thog pa'i rnam thar gsungs nas gso spyad 'di yang rigs gnas gzhan dang mi 'dra ba zhig yin shas 'dug
gsung ba las

mi mnyes pa byung ma song / ri phug tu phebs pa dang dpon tshang bong dkar ba la dpe cha g.yar nas sman gyi rtsa bshad phyi gsum po bzung / man ngag rgyud kyang 'dzin thub
pa 'dug rung skyor mi nus pa 'dra snyam nas ma bzung / bar skabs su bla ma na re/ bu'i sman dpe bzung pa 'dis nged la zhwa lu bas kha zer du 'ong ba 'dug /da gshol dgos gsungs/
nyin gcig bla ma phyi rol tu phebs pa'i lam du dpe cha shog khyar hrul po zhig rlung gis bteg nas phyag tu lhung byung ba la gzigs pas/ sman li zha sbyangs zhi la
bsil drod gnyis/ /dpyad la 'jam rtsub zas la phan gnod gnyis/ /spyod lam drag dal zas sman spyi 'gro'o/ /de ltar gnyen po bcu yis nad kun 'joms/ /zhes phyi ma rgyud kyi sdom
tshig gi skabs nas tshigs bcad de ltar yod pa zhig byung pas de las thugs rtog zhig 'phros nas bkag cha ma mdzad do/ de ltar sman dpe bzung rung lag len slob mkhan med
na mi phan pas/ slob dpon du 'os pa'i sman pa mkhas pa su yod ces dris pa na bkra shis lhun po ni gtsang phyogs kyi yul dbus rgyal po'i khab dang 'dra bas de na yod par
nges so zhes bya ba'i gtam thos pas/

der rgyug che ba'i lha rje 'ga' zhig brtag pa la bcug pas dpon tshang chen po zer ba'i bgres po zhig thon byung ste/ kho nga can la zhus pas ngas mi yong gsungs nas ma gnang
/ de nas sman thang grang khang par zhus pas sman slob par zhal gyis bzhes so/ /rang lo bcu bzhir slebs pa dbang phyug ces pa me mo glang gi lo shar ba dang / bkra shis
lhun por phyin nas 'tsho byed sman ram pa dka' chen blo bzang don yod de nyid kyis phyi ma rgyud kyi rtsa mdo chu mdo'i le'u sogs la 'grel bshad mdzad nas bslabs/ bla sman
blo bzang tshul khrims kyis sman sbyor sogs cha lag gzhan rnams la 'khrid mdzad do/ /'on kyang rig gnas kyi nang nas gso dpyad 'di'i khag len tshad dang ldan par byed
na gzhan thams cad bzhag nas 'di kho na la 'dril dgos pas nged cag 'dra bas skrug rnam bar snyan kyang tshems kyis phed pa mi 'dug go/ de ltar yang rang gi ji ltar nus pa'i
sgo nas nad pa dag la phan par bya ba ste/ zur mkhar la thog pa paN chen mnyam nyid rdo rje'i gsung mgur las/ bdag nyams myong rgan tshang mi ldan

yang / /nad 'du ba'i gegs 'phrang sel nus snyam/ /bdag blo zhib gzegs cha mi ldan yang / /nad bcos nor thal song byed ma myong / /bdag byams dang snying rje mi ldan yang ma
nad pa brtse bas 'dor ma myong / /bdag rdzas la ser sna ma bral yang / /sman yon dang gtang rag rtsod ma myong / /pha mnyam med gu Na'i bka' drin yin/ /drin 'khor thabs
med do chos kyi rje/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar ro/ /yul gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir gso ba rig pa'i gzhung bshad man ngag gi bskor la yang snga phyi gnyis su byung ba'i snga ma
ni mkhas mchog dpa' bo las byung ba'i yan lag brgyad pa'i bskor yin te deng sang bshad pa'i 'phrin las yod par mi snang / de dang 'brel ba'i man ngag gi bstan bcos dpal sa
skya'i sman dpyad rgyal bo'i dkor mdzod kyi lung nyan no/ /gzhung phyi ma ni shing rta chen po g.yu thog yon tan mgon pos srol phye ba'i dpal ldan rgyud bzhir grags pa
ni rgyud bshad rang rkang tshugs pa cher mi snang yang lung dang lag len dang bcas pa bzhugs pas kho bos kyang thos par byas so/ /rgyud bzhi'i phyogs su gtogs pa'i man ngag
la zur

mkhar ba'i bye ba ring bsrel ma bu'i skor gyi yig sna phal che ba'i lung / gong sa lnga pa chen po'i bla sman pa dpon tshang dar mo ba blo bzang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i
gdams ngag bka' rgya ma'i lung / mi'i dbang po 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i rgyud bzhi'i 'bru 'grel baiDUr sngon po sogs mang yang lung rgyun dang bcas
lag len dar ba man ngag lhan thabs su grags pa ste/ de rnams thos par byas pa yin no/ /srog gi dbang po 'tsho ba'i lus kyi sgor/ /gnag dka' zug rngu'i dug mda' 'phen pa'i
dgra/ /glo bur rkyen gyis 'jug pa 'di las gzhan/ /sgra tshang dmag dpung ldan yang rgol du med/ /de phyir gso ba rig pa'i gzhung lugs 'di/ /rang gzhan kun la gces pa'i
rin chen yin/ /phyi nang gzhal bya gtan la ma phebs na/ /tshad ma'i rigs lam ston ka'i 'brug sgra tsam/ /rang lo bco lnga pa 'bru mang zhes pa sa pho stag gi lo/ /nged cag
dpon slob nyang stod phyogs la phebs nas sger 'brong rtse ba'i khab tu dbyar bzhugs mdzad cing / 'brong rtse'i phu lha do chen zer ba'i mi la sman mang

po yod zer pa thos nas sde pa 'brong rtse bas 'phrin shog brdzangs te nyang stod skyid sbug nas sman pa zhig rgyus yod la btang / 'u lag dang bcas nged rnams kyi lha do chen
la phyin pas ri de'i ngos la sngon 'ba' ra ba'i skyes mchog rin po che sogs kyi slob mar gyur pa lha do rtog ldan mkhas grub bde legs rin chen gyi sgrub gnas byung shul
lha do dgon pa zer ba ra ri tsam 'dug /ri dpyad de la dpags na sngo sman mang po skyes tshod 'dug ste rgyus yod la byung ba'i sman pa de ni rgyus mi 'tshal ba zhig gis sa
ngo 'phrod pa dang blo bskyed thon pa ma byung mod kyi/ khong gi lag na 'brug pa dpag bsam dbang pos mdzad pa'i phyi ma rgyud kyi dka' 'brel mdor bsdus shig snang ba sman
ngos 'dzin tshul zur lugs su 'dug pas cung phan pa byung / phyis kyi ldan ma dge bshes bstan 'dzin phun tshogs kyi mdzad pa'i nus pa rkyang sel la rtsa ba bcol ba'i shel
gong 'phreng rtsa 'gril 'di dag ni/ rgyas rgyas lta bur snang rung sman ngos 'dzin tshul dpyad dka' ba'i the tshom gyi gzhi mang du snang ngo / /ri phug tu 'byor nas don
yod zhags pa'i cho ga'i rgyugs 'pher ba byas te/ khyab bdag bla ma ye shes

dpal 'byor gyi drung du don zhags kyi dbang dang dkyil chog sogs kyi lung rnams kyang zhus so/ /rang lo bcu drug pa myos ldan zhes pa sa mo yos kyi lo shar ba dang sngar nas
'brum nad kyi bags rgya khyab lta bur yod pas ra sog tu khron kha spel ba zer ba'i grong pa zhig tu mi god che ba byung nas bla ma sman khang pa skye gnas spor 'dren gyi
sbyin sreg mdzad par spyan drangs so/ kho bo rang ni zhwa lu mthil du don zhags sgrub mchod la yod pas/ bla mas bag sangs snang ba'i sa nas bang chen byung ste/ sku stod
la snyel gzhi yod pa langs pas gsol sman dgos zer ba gnang / kho bos gsol sman 'ga' bskur bas cung zhig bde ru song nas ri phug tu phebs rung de nas bzung sku stod kyi
bsnyun gzhi sku smad la babs nas rgyun du bsnyun pa zhi ba byung / de la bcos thabs 'dam byas bya ba med kyang sku na smin pa'i bgres nad kyi thog tu gyur nas zhi med du
ma song / lo de'i mjug ma he mchod pa yin pa dang bcas zhwa lu mthil du gdan drangs/ der bdud rtsi lnga lum gyi 'phrod brten gnang pas dwangs bskyed che ba byung / rang lo
bcu bdun pa gnam gnod zhes

pa lcags pho 'brug gi lo/ /hor zla gsum pa'i nang du nor bu grang khang nas mgyogs byams g.yar po btang byung ba la bla ma phebs te 'brong rtse'i skyid tshal klu sdings su
bzhugs/ 'brong rtse chos sder gos sku thog so bzhi la khebs pa/ lha mgron du gtso bo thung pa'i dbang po/ ldem gnyis su byams pa dang spyan ras gzigs/ steng du jo bo rje
dang / rje btsun tsong kha pa chen po ste sku lnga yod pa zhig gsar bzhengs mdzad/ hor zla lnga pa'i tshes bco lnga la gos sku bkrams chog pa byung pas rje sman khang pas
rab gnas mdzad/ dge ba'i rtsa ba mthar phyin byed smon lam tshigs su bcad pa bco lnga skor zhig rtsom pa mdzad nas kho bos yi ger bris/ tshems bu ba mi bdun dang lha bris
pa gcig sogs las byed rnams yon dang zhabs tog gis mgu bar byas so/ /de skabs 'brong rtse zhol/ bran bu/ ra sog gu la sogs kyi grong phyug pa phal cher dang / mo dgon than
thun yod pa rnams kyis che bas nyin gang tsam dang / gzhan ma rnams kyi ja chang mar krog gis mtha' brten pa'i dad 'bul byed mi shin tu mang / 'brong rtse chos sde'i
btsun pa rnams la dga' tshor yod yod mi 'dra zhing / lar

deng sang btsun pa dang mi nag pa go ldog gis mi nag pa dad pa che tshod tsam phyogs gang na yang gda'/ de yang snying rje padma dkar po las/ byang phyogs na pho brang rgyas
ldan du/ bram ze dang / khyim pa bstan pa la dad pa byung ste shi nas dga' ldan du skye la/ rab tu byung pa phal cher chos bzhin mi spyod pas log par ltung ngo / /zhes
'byung ste/ 'di 'dra rnams la dgongs sam snyam mo/ /de nas slar nyang chabs la ko ba btang ste rim gyis ri phug tu phebs/ nged kyis rtse mo'i cho ga bzung pas dbang gzhi
dkyil zin pa tsam nas 'phro la lus song ste/ nam zla ston ka song nas grang ngar ches pa dang chu ngan pas bla ma sku khams je lod du gyur/ bcos ka sna tshogs phul yang phan
par ma gyur te/ lo de'i smin drug zla ba'i tshes bcu'i nyi ma tsha rting khar gzhogs g.yas 'og tu 'jug pa sogs mdzad nas sku gshegs so/ /bshes gnyen gamigs bus stor ba'i
thang yangs su/ /mya ngan me lce 'bar bas snying bsregs mod/ /rnam dpyod gom pa shin tu 'khyor bzhin du/ /rjes kyi bya ba'i 'khur po 'bad pas bteg /rang

lo bco brgyad du slebs pa khyu mchog ces pa lcags mo sbrul lo shar pa'i hor zla dang po la rjes sman khang pa'i gdung la satstsha 'debs pa dang / mchod rten khang bu brtsegs
pa sogs bzhengs grub par byas/ de nas ni rang gi sems yang 'gyur te/ skyes rabs las/ mdza' ba yun ring 'khod 'khod nas/ /'chi bas so sor 'bral gyur te/ /sdug bsngal chen
po ldang gyur pa/ /de ni 'jig rten 'di na nges/ /zhes dang / spyod 'jug las kyang / mi mdza' rnams kyang med 'gyur zhing / /mdza' ba rnams kyang med par 'gyur/ /bdag kyang
med par 'gyur ba ste/ /de bzhin thams cad med par 'gyur/ /rmi lam nyams su myong ba bzhin/ /dngos po gang dang gang spyad pa/ /de de dran pa'i yul du 'gyur/ /'das pa
thams cad mthong mi 'gyur/ /zhes sogs gsungs pa'i don la nges shes drag po skyes/ /rang gi 'phral spyod dang gzhan dag gi bya spyod la ni gting nas khrel/ rgyu mtshan de'i
slad du ni yid la brnags pa'i tshul 'di ltar yin te/ kye ho/ zin pa'i mi zin sems kyi 'char sgo gya ma gyu/ /gyu gyu tsam las gtad so 'di yin ci yang med/ /med

dgag dbyings nas dug lnga'i rnam rtog ci ma dgu/ /dgu dgu bcu bcus grangs kha mi rdzogs ches cher 'phel/ /'phel kha chad pa'i slad du bsgrub bya dam pa'i chos/ /chos ltar bcos
pa'i gzugs brnyan 'di ni rang la sdig /sdig grogs ngan pa'i snang tshul nags la ma mched bzhin/ /bzhin bzang tshogs pa'i 'gam 'thung 'di la gad mo bro/ /bro pa ji bzhin
lang ling 'phyas 'chos kho nas g.yeng / /g.yeng ba spangs tshe nyi ma ring la sems yang skyo/ /skyo skyo'i snying la mi dran dgu dran ci yang skye/ /skye ba dman la 'dod
chags chu ltar 'khol long long / /long ba gong po g.yang la lhung 'dra'i gti thug go /go ba lug las chung zhing blun po'i 'du shes can/ /can can rnams ni phongs la sar
shing btsugs nas su/ /su dag phung gzhi sde 'khrug spyod pa sa 'dir mang / /mang po'i 'phrod du 'khyams pa'i yon tan de labs tshe/ /tshe srog rlung nang mar me bzhin du
g.yo bas na/ /na so gzhon pa'i sdug yus 'chu dus su la tshong / /tshong 'dus tshogs pa'i mgron po

so sor gyes pa ltar/ /ltar snang mdza' dang mi mdza'i tshul yang de bzhin te/ /te lo pa sogs sngon byon grub pa'i rnam thar la/ /la gor bsams nas dben zhing nyams dga'i khang
bu ru/ /ru ru bzhin du gcig pur 'dug la sems la ltos/ /phyi mtshams phyi ru rgyal chen mtho byas rang gzhan rgyu 'grul spang bar bya/ /nang mtshams nang du dran shes mtho
byas rnam rtog g.yer ba spang bar bya/ /gsang mtshams gsang bar bsnyen sgrub mtho byas tha mal 'dzin pa spang bar bya/ /phyi nang gsang ba'i mtshams gyi bya ba bar chad
med par 'grub gyur cig /ces bya ba ltar lo de'i hor zla dang po'i nyi shu lnga nas brtsams te sgrub gnas sman khang du lo gsum gyi bar la mtshams dam po la bzhugs so/
/de nas rang lo nyi shu rtsa gcig pa nyi sgrol zhes pa shing pho spre'u'i lo/ /hor zla bzhi pa'i tshes gsum la mtshams grol/ tshes brgyad kyi nyin gnas bkra shis kyi gtsug
lag khang kun skyob gling du mkhan po rin po che snang mtha'i mgon po rje btsun thams cad mkhyen pa blo bzang dpal ldan bstan pa'i nyi ma phyogs las rnam rgyal dpal bzang
po'i zhal

snga nas dang / las kyi slob dpon seng chen blo bzang bstan 'dzin dpal 'byor/ kha skong dkyil chen dpon slob brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan sogs dad pa'i dge 'dun grangs tshang
'i dbus su bsnyen par rdzogs pa dge slong gi dngos po bsgrubs so/ /zab gsang rgyud sde'i gter sgo 'byed pa yis/ /rdo rje slob dpon mchog gi rten du'ang / /dge slong rab mchog
yin par gsungs pa'i phyir/ /a ho 'dir 'bad mchog tu skal ba bzang / /thon pa spyi khang du rje blo bzang yon tan mjal zhing / rgyal ba dge 'dun grub kyi gsung kha shas
kyi lung thob/ sngar mtshams la yod dus nub gcig gi rmi lam du/ nged rang sdod pa'i sman khang gi spyil bu de'i thog na sngar mig gis mthong ma myong ba'i rgyal ba lnga
pa rin po che'i 'khrungs rabs thang kha'i gras yin zer/ gos chen tshems grub kyi thang kha snying nge ba la tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i sku zhing khams la 'og na gtong
skud ser po'i yi ge'i bcad 'then nas tshar chen chos rje la na mo/ /zer ba zhig yod pa bkrams 'dug /thang kha de la dga' tshor dang mos mos byas pas/ sku de ni rdo rje
'chang

dang mi 'khrugs pa gang yin ngo mi shes par sngo cham gyis 'gyur song ba dang gnyis sad/ yang nub gcig zhwa lu'i mo bran gyi lho sgo'i thang tsam na tshar chen rin po che yin
dbang byed pa'i bla ma sku gzugs chen pozhal rgyan nag zhul le ba/ sku gzan mtshal kha sku ther smug po thul che la kha gsar pa bzhes pa'i gzi brjid shin tu che ba zhig
skor ba la phebs kyin 'dug /phyi bzhin du bsnyegs nas nged rang gis kyang phyin pa rmis/ mi ltas de dag la brten nas tshar lugs kyi chos rgyun rnams thob 'dod byung ste/
sa skya mdar grangs chen sogs na chos zhu sa'i bla ma 'dra e yong snyam stod phyogs la 'gro ba'i blo skyes te bkra shis lhun po nas yar lam ka brgyad sbug tu gnas 'grel
byas/ snar thang dang gangs can chos 'phel mjal nas khro phur phyin/ de skabs gangs can chos 'phel ba rnams kyang khro phu smon lam la tshogs 'dug /gangs can bla brang 'dzin
ma rta gtong zla bas sne len dang bcas rgyal ba mi pham mgon po mjal/ shabs sgo lnga'i mi rnams kyis byams chen gyi spyan sngar bro gzhas phul ba la sde pa de dang ldan
du bltad mo byas/ de nas shabs

dge sdings brgyud nas sa skyar slebs/ rigs 'dzin pho brang du rje btsun 'chi med bstan pa'i nyi ma mjal bar phyin pas khri chen kun dga' bkra shis la der phebs pa dang mjal/
'jam mgon rdo rje rin chen la 'di de dus dgung lo drug tu phebs pa'ang mjal tsam byung / de phyin chos zhus yang ma byung zhing chu de yang ma 'phrod pas gnas mjal rags
rim byas nas 'dar du 'gro rgyur rigs 'dzin pho brang gi gsung brtag la ma bab pas bshol/ tshur lam gzhong pa la brgyud nas sde pa tsha rong gi klu sdings spro khang dang
bcas pa legs po zhig 'dug pa de g.yar nas zhag gnyis bsdad/ de nas srad chu mi zan brgal nas lhun po rtse mjal/ chag chag la rgyab ste ngor du 'ongs pas spe grong du mi
nyag steng 'i dpon gnyer rgan po des bsnyen bkur zhabs tog zab/ dpon gnyer khong rang sne sbyor la 'ongs te ngor dgon pa'i lha khang rnams mjal/ mchod khang gcig tu bde mchogbong
zhal gyi blos bslangs zhig mthong ba rjes su 'gro dus rtsad gcod byas pas de 'dra med zer ro/ gzhong pa la 'thon nas

yar lam rtse mtho'i klu sdings su sde pa rin chen zla ba'i sar zhag sdod byas nas rang gnas su slebs so/ /ras dkar lcog bu'i gur khang dang 'grogs nas/ /ka brgyad sbug tu padma'i
gter lung mjal/ dpal gyi snar thang mjal nas lcags skor btab/ /lus sros g.yang la bskyur ba'i nyen mthong nas/ /a lce wa mo'i 'gro lugs de ru byas/ /gangs can chos
'phel bskor nas khro phur phyin/ /byams chen zhal bzang mthong pas smon lam btab/ /sa skya e waM bskor ba e ma ho/ /'di skabs bla ma zhabs dkar tshogs drug rang grol stod
phyogs nas mar phebs te khong gi grub rtags la dad mos can 'ur langs pa phal cher 'di tsam na sgyid pa skyur zhing thang chad pa 'dra zhig gis bskur 'debs dang zhabs 'dren
tho re ba yang byed kyin gda'/ lar snyigs dus kyi skye bo rnams la yid brtan 'cha' ba ni mi rung la gad mo bro ba tsam ni 'dug go/ nged kyi khyab bdag bla ma dam pa ye
shes dpal 'byor la/ nyid kyis gsan pa'i dbang chos tshang ma bum pa gang byo'i tshul du gnang bar gsol ba btab pas zhal gyis bzhes nas thog mar grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe

dbang dang / bla ma zhi khro 'chi med dpal ster gyi tshe dbang stsal/ de nas tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i rnam thar dang / rgyal sras bka' 'bum thor bu'i lung sogs mdzad/
rje nyid dang ri phug gdan sa ba ye shes bsam grub gnyis nas nged la phebs sgor/ da lta'i bzhugs sa 'di gling gi mtha' mar song bas mi 'os 'dug /sku gong ma'i gzim khang
du spo dgos gsung / de ltar bgyi'o zhus nas ngor du phyin/ khang ser du bla chen kun dga' ye shes las/ ngor lugs kyi gur lha brgyad/ zhal lha lnga bcas kyi rjes gnang dang
nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs brang ti paN chen gyi yi ge bzhin dang / dge slong rin po che ngag dbang bzang po las dmar mo skor gsum gyi chos skor glegs bam gyi lung
rdzogs par nyan/ sngar mtshams la yod dus nub gcig ngo mi shes pa'i ri ngos kyi dgon pa gcig na khang pa ser po steng shod can gagayab skor dang bcas par slebs te/ khang
pa steng ma de nas mi ro bzan ser po la bsgril nas khyer yong ba zhig dang 'phrad pa rmis/ phyis dgon pa de ngor du 'dug khang pa

de khang ser ni ma yin 'dug pas ci yin rung / rjes su thar rtse bla brang du phyin dus de kho nar 'dug go /mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin gyi bka'
drin la brten nas/ sprul pa'i sku 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse sogs la chos kyi phan thogs pa byung pas de la lta ba 'dra/ de skabs nged rang nas mi nyag steng pa'i dpon gnyer
chen po zung 'brel gyi bka' brgya char gcig byas so/ /dpon gnyer nas zhabs tog dang 'bul ba bzang po byas/ tshur lam bon do'i lha mo de yang mjal/ ri phug tu slebs te
byang gling sgrub khang du spo bar brtsams pa na/ sngar rang chung ngu'i dus btab pa'i byang chub ljon shing yod pa de la me tog ser che li ba 'dug /sems 'phreng ba tsam
byung pas dge slong bkra shis dpal 'byor na re/ 'di bkogs nas khyer gtong zer/ don grub dang gnyis kyis de bkogs nas sgrub khang gi ldum rar btsugs song yang yun mi ring
bar bskams so/ /lo de'i chu stod kyi zla ba'i bden bzhi'i chos 'khor bskor ba'i dus chen nas khyab bdag ye shes dpal 'byor gyis/ gtso bor bu ston bka' 'bum dang gzhan yang
dbang rjes gnang du ma'i chos 'khor bar ma chad

par bskor te hor zla brgyad pa'i mjug tsam la grol bar byas so/ /de dus chos zhu ba'i mthun rkyen gang dgos nor bu bde ldan pa'i chen po'i drung gis gnang bar zhal bzhes bzang
po mdzad/ rjes su dgos dus su ni rtse mthor mkhan po dngos grub rdo rje phebs pa'i thugs spro 'bul ba byed pa la 'khyogs nas 'dir ci yang ma byung ste/ 'brug nub tu bsgrags/
char pa shar du phab pa'i dber song / bka' chos re zhig mtshams gsol nas rje bla ma la brtan bzhugs maNDal sku gsung thugs rten phul bas/ dge slong bkra shis dpal
'byor gyis tshe lha'i sku de'i mgul phog pas rnam rtog kyang za ba zhig byung / 'on kyang bla mas ma gzigs par tshang sgrigs thub pa byas so/ thub bstan snyigs mar spyod
pa'i dus mtha' 'dir/ /bdag 'dra'i zhing sar chos kyi sman char gang / /phab phyir dus gsum rgyal ba thams cad las/ /kye lags bka' drin che'o rje bla ma/ /de yang sngar sa
skya'i yab rje ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros kyi gnas gsar pa ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas las tshar lugs kyi gsang chen slob bshad

phal che ba gsan nas spel gang thub mdzad pa'i dus kyi slob ma rtse gdong zhabs drung dge 'dun bkra shis dpal 'byor kho na ma gtogs gzhan mi snang pas/ tshar lugs kyi chos
bka' zhu rgyu don du gnyer bya'i snying por byas nas rgyan gong sogs mgon khang rnams su 'phrin bcol byas/ rang gi g.yog don grub lus she thang pas bong bu'i gzhogs khal
tsam gyi khres po 'khyer/ dge slong bkras dpal nas kyang rdog khres rgyab/ kho bos chos gos snam sbyar dang lag tu sba dbyug bzung ste lam du bzhugs/ shas ra gru kha brgyud
de rong chung 'phrang bskor nyi ma dbus kyi rgyal khams su phyin no/ lha sar slebs pa dang jo bo shAka rnam gnyis drung du smon lam yid ches par btab/ po Ta lar dga'
ldan khri rin po che yongs 'dzin ngag dbang chos 'phel de skabs zhwa lu'i mkhan po yin pa dang / 'di khar phyag mdzod sogs kyi ngo tshab sde pa rin chen zla bas yi ge 'bul
rgyu bskur byung pas thog mar mjal/ rgyal dbang sprul pa'i sku tshul khrims rgya mtsho'i mjal phyag zhus/ de nas dge slong bkras dpal 'phan yul du 'phrin yig

'bul bar brdzangs pas/ tshur slebs nas bla ma des bka' chos gnang ris mi 'dug zer/ bla ma'i yig len na'ang 'di lo lam 'bras slob bshad 'chad mi thub pas 'dir ma phebs mdzod
zer ba 'dug rung / bla ma rang dang mjal nas chos thob pa srid dam snyam/ nyang bran phu'i ka ma la bya ba'i la chen po 'dzegs nas gro pa'i nang brgyud 'brug sgur phun tshogs
bde gling du zhabs drung rin po che mjal bar phyin/ bka' chos rgya che ba gnang mi thub pas mkha' spyod skor gsum dang gshed dmar spros med tsam 'bul lo/ /ltag la kin
mkhar gdong gzhis ka bya ba yod/ sa cha de sngon bka' gdams pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyer 'ga' byon pa'i gnas yin pa dang mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub yang der
'khrungs pas byin rlabs nan tar che/ der chos 'chad dgos pas sprul pa'i sku rang sngon la byon cig gsungs/ nged rnams kyi mkhar gzhis su phyin pas zhag 'ga' nas bla ma phebs
byung / der bsu ba byas te bka' chos kyi rting bskul zhus pas tshes bcu dang bsgrags nas rje btsun rdo rje rnal

'byor ma nA ro mkha' spyod kyi sindhu ra'i dkyil 'khor du byin rlabs mdzad/ de nas bskyed rim rnal 'byor bcu gcig dang / rdzogs rim rtsa dbu ma che chung / chos nyid dngos
ston gyi byin rlabs/ gser chos chig brgyud bsam mi khyab sogs dang / indra mkha' spyod mai tri mkha' spyod gnyis kyi byin rlabs yi ge so so'i lung dang bcas rgyas par stsal/
gshed dmar spros med de dpe ma rnyed pas gnang ma thub/ rjes su chos mang po gnang rgyu'i zhal bzhes dang / nged sdod ring gi mthun rkyen sogs thugs la btags so/ /bla
ma 'di nged rang zhwa lu sku zhang pa'i lce'i gdung las 'khrungs shing dpal sa skya'i rtse gdong bdag po rin po che ngag dbang nor bu rgyal mtshan gyi sku'i skye ba gsum
pa/ grub mtha' ris med mkhyen pa'i mkhas grub tu gyur kyang 'phral khyim pa'i spyod pa ltar mdzad nas sbas pa'i tshul du bzhugs pa zhig go/ 'od gsal lha las chad pa'i gdung
sprul mchog /lce btsun dge 'dun bkra shis dpal 'byor gyi/ /zhabs kyi padmo mchod nas mchogi lam/ /mkha' spyod grub pa'i snyan brgyud ma lus thob/ /de

nas nyan po'i nang brgyud nas dge ba'i bshes gnyen shar pa yon tan grags kyi thugs dam 'bum pa rnams mjal zhing bskor ba 'ga' byas 'on kyang shar 'bum pa la bskor ba btabs
na rkang lag gi nad dang / spyang lung 'bum pa la bskor ba btabs nas mig sogs dbang po'i nad la phan pa yin zer skor ba byed pa mang po yong gin yod tshod 'dug nged ni sngar
rwa sgreng du btsun chung gcig gis/ mi rtag pa ma go ba'i skor pa rkang pa na zer ba'i lo rgyus ltar/ de dus rkang pa cung mi bde zhing de la phan du re bas bskor ba
de chos su song snyam pa rang ni ma byung / spyir 'phan po'i yul gyi ljongs de dag ni sngon bka' gdams pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen byang chub sems dpa' chen pos yongs su bzung
zhing byin gyis brlabs pas/ rgya gar gyi gnas chen rnams mjal ba dang khyad par ma mchis pa zhig yin 'dug ste/ nged rang de dus chos don gnyer las gnas skor la spro ba
med pas gar phyin yang bang chen la phyin pa 'dra kho na mang ngo / /lar nas za nyal 'gro 'chag sogs bya spyod thams cad gzhan

dang mi mthun pa'i khum chud pa zhig kyang yod do/ /a ho/ bltad mo'i slad du lha khang mang po ma mjal zhing / /sgo yon sdud phyir mgur dbyangs gre 'gyur yang ma 'then la/
/srang khar DA ru dkrol ba'i gcod mkhan yang mi shes te/ /gar phyin lam gzhung srong ba rnal 'byor nga'i 'gro lugs ni/ /byad bzhin can la tshogs gsog spong dag kyang ma zhus
shing / /phyug po'i bu la gsol gsol mchod mchod kyang ma byas la/ /kha drag can la mgo 'bul lus 'bul kyang mi shes te/ /gang byung rang khar 'debs pa rnal 'byor nga'i
za lugs yin/ /re dogs rgod po'i nyan rna sangs po yang ma bgyis shing / /jus med jus rtog rnon po'i 'pher rgya yang ma byas la/ /gyod kha lding ba'i phong ra'i slob dpon
kyang mi shes te/ /snyems chung rang so 'dzin pa rnal 'byor nga'i sdod lugs yin/ /de nas rgya lcags ri gong kha'i phu de la phyin 'phan yul 'jog po'i nang gi la chen zhig
'dzegs pas yer pa lha ri snying po'i mgul du slebs so/ /khres po bzhag ste zla ba phug mjal bar phyin pas nang de na sgom chen pa tshe mtshams la bzhugs pa zhig yin

zer / dge slong rgan po ral pa can zhig gis 'khrid nas lha lung dpal rdor bros pa'i brag phug sogs steng shod tshad mar mchod mjal btang / de nas grwa ba zhig la gnas tshang
g.yar nas chos rgyal srong btsan sgam pa'i sgrub phug dang / dge slong rma bya'i chub dang / grub thob ku mA ra sogs kyis bzhengs pa'i lha rten rnams mjal lo/ /yer bde
ngo mtshar che bas 'dir lo 'ga' sgrub pa byas nas sdod rgyu byung na dga' ba la bsam pa'ang byung ngo / /a a/ rab dkar ke la sha yi thod bcings pa'i/ /nags tshal me tog bkra
ba'i sa 'dzin mgul/ /dal 'bab lhung lhung snyan pa'i rdza rnga sgrog /yid 'ong padma spungs 'dra'i brag ri'i rtser/ /ngo mtshar rten gyi 'khor lo gzi 'od 'bar/ /steng
na chu 'dzin dkar po lang long 'khrigs/ /bar na ha ri tsaDdra dri bzhon rgyas/ /mdun na baiD'urya 'dra'i spangs ljongs mdzes/ /bag phebs rgyu ba'i ri dwags skyid nyal can/
/sna tshogs mtshon gyi mdangs ldan spu sdug gis/ /'dab gshog gos su gyon pa'i bya tshogs rnams/ /so so'i mgrin rnga ched du ngom ngom 'dra/ /'di ru shog dang zer

'dra'i dur khrod de/ /mi rtag 'chi ba dbyangs su len len bzhin/ /'di 'dra'i gnas su chos nyid don gzigs pa'i/ /sngon sbyangs las 'phro can tsho'i dga' ba la/ /de nas lha sar
phyin te sde pa gzhung gi bla brang phyag mdzod lcog spe tshe brtan bkra shis kyi shag tu bskang gso gtong mkhan zhwa lu pa dge slong zhig yod pa des bsnyen bkur zab/ sde
pa des kyang nged la kha btags phul zhing mjal 'phral phebs byung / rnam rgyal grwa tshang nas phyag mdzod blo bzang dar rgyas dang 'jam dpal gnyis nas bos te gung tshigs
drangs/ chu bzang ri khrod na khong gnyis po'i gzim khang spro mo zhig 'dug pa der phyin nas re zhig bsdad/ dga' ldan khri zur rin po che byang chub chos 'phel las seng
ldeng nags sgrol dang / ba ri lugs kyi rdo rje rnam 'joms ljang gu'i rjes gnang chos 'brel du zhus/ dge bshes grags pa klu sgrub dang / khri pa tshang gi gsol dpon chos
mdzad rgya mtsho chos 'phel la bu ston gyi gsung kha shas kyi lung bklags/ khri chen byang chub chos 'phel gyis nged la gung tshigs lhan rgyas mdzad nas dri ba mang po
gnang zhing mnyes po mdzad/

chu bzang du re zhig bsdad na dgongs pa dang gsang 'dus ye shes zhabs lugs kyi dbang zhig kyang gnang bzhed 'dug rung dge slong bkras dpal bas spu sud kho na byas nas slar
po tA la'i gzhon du yong dgos pa byung ngo / /rtser yongs 'dzin rin po che ngag dbang chos 'phel la chos 'brel gyi snyan gsan phab pas/ nged sku zhabs rin po che'i thugs
gnyer gsan sbyong la sku mdun du 'gro dgos pa 'dis/ chos rgya che ba ni mi yong bas khyed rang bzhed pa'i chos kyi snying po zhig smos shig gsungs/ 'o na snying po don gsum
zhu dgos zhus pas/ de yong gsung ste nyin gsum gyi bar nyams khrid shin tu smin par mdzad nas bka' drin stsal lo/ tshim par byas so dad ldan kho bo'i yid/ /ngag dbang
chos 'phel zhal gyi bdud rtsis te/ /'di phyi bar dor zin bya'i 'dun ma yang / /khyod gsung tshul bzhin bsgrubs gsal byed kyi rgyanpa'i mthu yis so/ /de skabs rgyal tshab
no min han rin po che yang po tA lar bzhugs nas nyin gcig lha sar mgyogs byams shel sgo can zhig la

phebs song bas zhal mjal zhu bar phyin/ nged kyi sku sha 'chor po 'dug byas pas/ dge slong bkras dpal na re/ /rgyag pa los yod/ mi ser mang pos gsos pa yin 'dug zer ro/ /de
nas yar 'thon khar khri rin po ches zhal lta mang po dang bcas ja bar khag gcig dang kha btags mang ba gnang byung bas/ bla ma'i phyag rdzas zhu gin med pas phar phul rung
/ ja mi khyer yang kha btags rten la phul chog pas 'khyer gcig gsung ngo / /khri rin po che dang phyag mdzod blo bzang dar rgyas lags gnyis nas bsam yas tshun gyi gnas
tshang la yi ge bskur/ lam du bzhugs nas 'ong skabs lcog spo'i a ma mchod dge slong sogs kyis skyid chu thug bskyal nas sems 'phreng zhing log go /yul gyi mja' bas bcings
pa'i sngar 'dris mi/ /gnas skabs bral ba'i gdung pa 'di yin na/ tshe 'di'i mdza' bshes kun dang gtan gyes su/ /bar do'i 'phrang la 'gro tshe ci drag gam/ /de nas dga' ldan
rnam par rgyal ba'i gling gi khri thog khang du phyin nas/ yongs 'dzin gyi gsung shog sprad pas sne len bzang po byung / dga' ldan pa'i dge bshes

shig mchod mjal gyi sne shan la btang / gser gdung rin po che sogs gtsug lag khang lte ba'i skor dang / zur du yod pa'i rgyal tshab mkhas grub kyi gzim chung sogs mjal/ khri
thog khang gi phyag mdzod khong rang gis lde mig 'khyer te gser khri'i zur sgo dbye nas gser khri la ma 'ongs pa na sdod rgyu yong ba'i smon lam rgyob zer/ nged kyi sems
la thar pa dang thams cad mkhyen pa'i go 'phang ma thob phyin chad gser khri de la sdod rgyu byung yang mi phan pa 'dra snyam nas smon lam ni ma rgyab po/ /khri thog khang
gi 'od gsal phug dang / de'i nang rten rje rin po che'i phyag dpe dang thugs dam thang ka tshun la phyag mdzod de rang gis gnas bshad btang pas yid ches ba byung ngo
/ /nged cag dga' ldan du yod dus kha ba chen po bab pas bsam yas phyogs la gzhung bskor nam gtogs dga' ldan ngos kyi la nas thar mi yong zer mkhan kho na byung rung / sngar
khri rin po ches sho mo mdzad nas lam de la phyin chog pa bab pa yin pas bla ma'i gsung tshad mar bya na mi yong snyam ste/ thag chod kyi lam

dris pas/ phyag mdzod na re/ lam kha bas chod nas thar mi yong ste/ mi nyan tsa na bya thabs med/ nga'i dge phrug cig shag na yod pa kho sngar de phyogs don phyin nas lam kha
de na mtsho yod tshul sogs cha le cho le zhig bshad rgyu 'dug /gtam gtong ba la shog byas kyi zer/ sa ma sros la btsun chung dbang po dwangs pa zhig 'ongs nas lam rgyus
bshad/ phyag mdzod kyi da dung lam rgyus la sang nyin mi zhig kyang btang gi zer/ sang snga bar phyin pas lam rgyus pa de ni nyi ma phyed tsam nas da 'di phan chad du ni
nga 'gro ma myong ba zhig yin zer log song / nged cag gi gar slebs kyi la 'dzegs nas/ nub mo brag skyib lta bu'i gangs med sa btsal nas nyal sa byas/ de nas snga bar langs
phyin pas rdza brag gcig nas sre mong zhig 'ongs te rtsed mo mang po byed cing nged cag la rtse bar du bskyal/ la rgyab nas kha ba yang mi 'dug rung lam kha ral gcig
zug nas 'gro sa ci yin ma shes par the tshom byung ba'i dus bya rgod thang dkar zhig gshom pa'i 'ur sgra dang bcas te lam shar phyogs ma de'i thad ka'i nam mkha' la 'phur
song / da 'gro sa 'di

yin pa 'dug go byas nas phyin pas pha tshad de ka nas mtsho yod zer ba de mthong ste lam ma nor ba thag chod cing bla ma'i bka' drin du shes pa byung ngo / rim gyis shing nags
mang po yod pa'i rong zhig brgyud bsam yas kyi phu g.ya' ma lung gi mda' der lcog pu byas nas zhag gcig bsdad/ nang par snga gro g.ya' ma lung mjal phyin pas sgrub phug
de na btsun ma kha shas tshogs nas tshes bcu'i cho ga gtong gin 'dug /tshig mtshams nyan pas spyan 'dren gdan 'bul gyi skabs na 'dug /ayon chen po dang dngos su mjal ba'i
mos pa byas nas sku 'dra la byin rlabs zhus smon lam btab/ lam du brag dmar mgrin bzang mjal nas bsam yas su slebs/ mchod rten dkar po ba bya ba'i gnas tshang zhig tu
bsdad/ gnas tshang gi mi gcig la bza' btung byin nas rgyus sna bcol/ dpal dbu rtse rigs gsum gyi gandho la'am/ sngon rgya nag gi sked du zan yangs te mi 'gyur lhun gyis
grub pa'i gtsug lag khang lte ba dang / mtha' skor gyi gling phan tshul du yod pa'i lha khang rnams legs par mjal/ nyin gcig

mchim bu'i dben gnas su phyin nas gu ru padma'i sgrub phug ngo mtshar ba rnams mjal zhing mda' de na bka' blon bshad sgra gnas kyis bzhengs pa'i gnas bcu dang rje 'bangs nyer
lnga'i sku byon gtsa po yod pa'i lha khang gsar pa 'dug pa'ang mjal lo/ /rin chen shel gyi bye ma gdal steng du/ /ngo mtshar stong gsum spyi pud ri gling gi/ /bkod pa
lhun stug bsam yas lha gnas che/ /mig gi steng 'thung phye nas legs par mjal/ /gang tshe sngon gyi rje 'bangs de dag gi /phyag rjes rmad du byung ba 'di mthong tshe/ /bdag
nyid chain po'i yon tan gzhan yang 'dis/ /mtshon nas dad pa'i padmo lan brgyar bzhad/ /de nas zur mkhar rdo'i mchod rten bskor zhing smon lam btabs nas lam la bzhugs nas
'ong dus/ dge slong bkras dpal bas/ khong rang gi lus po'i grib ma la bltas nas nga'i grib ma 'di ni bcom ldan 'das kyi 'khrungs rabs su 'byung ba'i shi ba'i rgyal po'i
spyan slong mkhan gyi bram ze kho'i 'dra ba la zer/ yud tsam phyin pas lam nor te gtsang 'gram gyi bye ma'i klung chen po la 'thoms nas bye ri mang po bskor zhing

bsgral dgos pa byung ngo / /sngon mkhas grub ayon pa rin chen dpal bzang de rgya gar rdo rje gdan la phebs dus su rang gi 'khor la/ da ste gtam ngan pa ma zer cig /la nyeng
na ba yong ngo zhes gsung bcad nas phebs/ zer ba'ang bden po yin pa 'dra snyam pa byung ngo / /de nas rdo rje brag gi ko gru don nas gong dkar chos sder yang zhag gcig nyal/
rim gyi gam pa la rgyab nas snang dkar rtse sogs brgyud ra lung mthil du gnas mjal byas nas gnas rnying du phyin/ dbu rtse zer ba'i gtsug lag khang rnying ma der gnas
tshang g.yar nas mchod mjal byas dus rta mgrin yang gsang bzhugs pa'i gtsang khang de'i sgo steng na gnas rnying gi thog ma'i gnas gzhi 'debs pa po slob dpon padma'i dngos
slob rgya'i sngags 'chang chen po 'jam dpal blo gros kyi sku 'dra 'dug pa de ni sngags pa rgan po sngags gos ther ma dkar po sogs snam chas dngos gnas gyon pa 'dra ba
ya mtshan pa zhig tu mthong / chos sde de'i dang po yang thang la bsam na ngo mtshar che la gad mo bro ba/ deng sang gi

nyams su lugs la bsams na ngu bro bar gda'/ 'on kyang lung pa ltar bud med kyis dkon gnyer byed pa ni mi 'dug /rgyab de na rgyang ro ser sdings pa'i 'du khang gsar pa zhig
'dug /de na grwa rgan zhig bsdad 'dug pa na re/ nga tso rgyud pa'i 'du khang mjal du shog zer/ der phyin pas/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i gser sku gcig bstan nas/ 'o 'di rgyud pa'i
rten yod na med na rang yin/ dngul rdo tshad gcig gzi ba yod zer/ nga'i sems la/ glen pa yi dam la rin thang gi tshad bshad nas/ khyod lta tsong snying 'dod pa yin 'dug
ste/ nga la dngul med snyam pa yang byung ngo / e ma ho/ gnas ra lung mthil gyi spang gshong steng / /sngon grub pa'i phyag bris rgya che ba/ /rgyu rin chen sna tshogs las
grub pa'i/ /dpal bde mchog 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor sogs/ /rten ngo mtshar can mig gis bdud rtsir gyur/ /yum dman mo'i rten bshad rna ba'i dpyid/ /'di bskal ba'i mtha' zad
ma yin tshe/ /ma DA ki'i tshogs dang mjal bar nges/ /khyed pho skyes dpa' bo los kyang yin/ /nga lugs zung gi gnas la blta mkhas kyang / /

khyed skya ser ci yin ma 'tshal ba/ /las sgrib pa stug pos lan nam snyam/ /yul gnas rnying 'phags pa'i zhing khams der/ /ban glen pa 'chal ba'i glen gtam la/ /snying dad pa'i
ku mud ma bzhad kyang / /gnas byin rlabs che bas yid dga' 'phrog /a la la tshogs drug gi 'char sgo ru/ /yul snang gi ltad mo ngo mtshar che/ /de nas rgyal rtse dpal 'khor
bde chen/ /rtse chen chos sde/ /'brong rtse chos sde rnams su gnas rten mjal ba dang bsnyen bkur zhu mi 'ga' byung ste/ de dag gi ngor zhag re gnyis lcag ngal byas/ 'brong
rtse chos sde dgon pa spyi so de nas kyang ja zhu dang 'bul ba mtshon tsam byung bas mang ja gcig btang / gnas gsar rgyal khang gi yum chen mo mjal nas smon lam btab/
rgya phub shar mor sngon 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis tshogs 'khor mdzad dus rang byon du phebs pa'i mgon po de la zhib lta bya dgos snyam tsa na/ dge slong
bkras dpal ba khong gi char khebs sle khra zhig 'dug pa skya la grad nas ngal bas snying don

'gro ba lta bu'i sems gcong langs nas ngan smras byed pa 'dug go /e ma gnas gsar rtsis kyi lha khang du/ /rang byung mgon po'i zhal dkyil blta snyam kyang / /bgres rgan ser
sna langs pas rkang gling btang / /de yis mgon po skyengs nas phag tu yib/ /rim gyi ri phug tu 'byor nas khyab bdag bla ma dam pa ye shes dpal 'byor mjal bas dgyes pa'i
rtse mor son pa byung ngo / /rang lo nyi shu rtsa gnyis pas skyong zhes pa shing mo bya'i lo gsar du tshes pa dang sngar nas gsol ba btab pa bzhin rje bla mas dpal dus kyi
'khor lo'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor chen po bzhengs su gsol te/ byis pa ltar 'jug pa'i dbang bdun/ drang nges kyis phye bas dbang gong ma bzhi/ rdo rje slob dpon bdag
po chen po'i dbang dang bcas pa smin rgyas su stsal lo/ /a hoHrnam 'dren mchog des sa skyong lor/ /dus kyi 'khor lo'i smin byed zab mo stsal/ /'di tsam kho nas khyod nyid
dus 'khor te/ /phyi nang gzhan gsum tshul la mkhas pas kyang/ /gzhan yang yo ga rdo rje dbyings/ /'jam dpal gsang ldan sogs bka' chos rgya che ba gnang

ba'i mur hor zla gnyis pa'i tshes mgor bla ma dam pa de yon bdag 'ga' zhig gi sar rkyen sel gyi tshe bka' gnang ba sogs la spyan 'dren rim pas byung ste phebs pas/ gsol ma
'phros pa 'dra ba zhig gis rkyen byas nas ri phug tu phebs pa'i sang nyin de rang nas 'phyal shin tu bltems nas zla ba de'i tshes bcu gnyis kyi nyin gzugs sku'i bkod pa bsdus
nas bdag cag mgon skyabs dang bral ba'i mya ngan gyi khri mun du tshul pa'i skal ba dman pa dang sbyar ro/ /de nas sku zhang rin po che dang nor bde chen po'i drung
gis ni/ sngar byang gling pa byams pa smon lam bsam gtan dang / rin chen byams pa chos 'phel gnyis la yang gdung me mchod la phul ba med/ da res yang sku chas khrol 'khyil
che ba rang med pas me mchod 'bul mi thub pa 'dra gsung / nged kyi me mchod rang la 'bul dgos byas nas mar zhu sogs kyi mthun rkyen yang rang gis phul/ dgung zhag bdun
gyi bar la rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sindhu ra'i dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod dang bla ma mchod chog rgyas par byas so/ /dgongs rdzogs kyi rim pa

grol nas bkra shis lhun por rje bla ma shar rtse rdo rje 'chang blo bzang yon tan dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas la gsol ba btab ste/ theg pa chen po blo sbyong don bdun ma'i
nyams 'khrid shin tu smin pa yongs 'dzin ye shes rgyal mtshan pa'i 'khrid yig gi steng nas zhus shing / bya rgyud thub pa dam tshig gsum bkod lha lnga'i dbang dang / sbyong
rgyud kyi gtso bo kun rig rnam par snang mdzad kyi dbang zhus te/ de'ang dam tshig gsum bkod na gtsang sbra med pa dang sdom pa ma blangs pa'i khyim pa sogs kyis kyang
nyams su blang chog par gsungs la/ deng sang gi skye bo ma sdam pa sdig pa can rnams kyi gnyen po'i lhur gzigs nas rje btsun tA ra nA thas kyang 'di'i zab sku bzhengs
ba tshunachad kyi spel gang thub mdzad cing / 'on kyang dus dbang gis dar rgyas cher 'gro ba ni ma byung 'dug /de'i dbang yang da lta sa zhal gnyis ka la med cing dge lugs

yid ches nas

zhus pa yin/ kun rigs dbang rgyun zhwa lu pa rang la yod pa'i bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i phyag bzhes gtsang sing nge ba gzhan dang ma 'dres pa de ni bdag po byed mkhan ma
byung ba bros la shor nas mi gda'/ sa dkar snying gsum gyi phyogs na kun rigs dar ba 'dug ste sengge'i ya 'gal dang phag pa'i ma 'gal sbyar ba'i ya ma cha ru 'dug /sa lugs
kyang ngas thob zin pa yin/ dge lugs la yod pa'i kun rig gi dbang 'di bu ston las brgyud cing / yig cha yang 'dul 'dzin grags rgyal bas mdzad pa'i dkyil chog 'di bu ston
thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsung dang 'brel mi che ba med pa bcas bu lugs kyi dbang gi go bcad chog pa 'dug pas zhus pa yin/ gzhan yang rje rin po che'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor
srad brgyud lugs dga' ldan lha brgya ma'i 'khrid dang / bla mchod bde stong dbyer med pa'i 'khrid sogs zhus te/ ci 'byor ba'i dngos po phul nas kyang mnyes par byas/ /sngags
khang du bka' drin mtshungs zla ma mchis pa'i sang chen rdo rje 'chang blo bzang bstan 'dzin dpal 'byor las dpal gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod rdo rje lha so gnyis kyi

dbang bka' dang / gsang 'dus sngags btu'i rjes gnang dang bcas pa yang mnyam med tsong kha pa chen po'i bzhed srol las byung ba thob ste/ gangs ri'i khrod 'dir rgyud gsang
ba 'dus pa'i phyogs su rje rin po che yab sras las gzhan phan gyi rgyun dar ba mi snang ba'i dbang de la yid rangs pa'i mthar thug pa gcig ni byung ngo / ri phug tu slebs
nas chos rje ma Ni ba rin chen don grub las rgyal po bka' 'bum gyi lung dang rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rwa 'khrid mkha' 'gro snyan brgyud zhus/ khong la gsang 'dus mi bskyod

pa'i nor/ /bsags pa don ldan rab kyi yang rtse yin/ /smad pa'i dpelo de'i hor zla lnga pa'i nang du 'od gsal lha las chad pa'i gdung brgyud dri ma med par 'khrungs pa'i

mchog

cu skor dang / 'bru khal nyis brgya skor byung 'dug /de nas sku 'bum chen mo'i gser gdugs tshang ma gsar bzo dang / gdugs 'dzin yang gser zangs dang / bum ldir ngos kyi sgo
