nas rnam smin bskyed pa'i rgyal po 'byung / /zhes dang / gter kha gzhan nas phyag rdor gyi sprul par lung bstan pa'i sne'u gdong gong ma chen po dbang grags pa rgyal
mtshan gyis bzhengs pa

byang chub mchod rten gyi gser zangs gsar sgron byas/ da dung mchod rten gcig tsam la gdugs khebs pa'i zangs gser 'khrol 'khyil thon pa yod kyang / 'di skabs mgo byed du bskos
pa dag ni spyang ki la sha gnyer bcol ba der gda'o/ /'on kyang 'di tsam ma yong ba'ang sde pa rin chen zla ba khong rang gi byas nas byung ba yin/ gzhan sus kyang pho
skyes nas byung ba med do/ /lo de'i hor zla lnga pa'i tshes bco lnga la sku zhang rin po che yang spyan drangs/ nged rang dang chen slob sogs bla ma khri gdan sa ba drug
/dbu chos dang bcas pa'i grwa sa rags bsdus tshogs nas yo ga rdo rje dbyings kyi rab gnas 'bring po kha skong gi rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg dang bcas pa bsgrubs so/ /de nas lo
'ga'i bar du lo phyugs legs pa dang / lhag par las khri 'dzugs mkhan zhwa lu rang gi shing bzo ba dag gis byas pa'i myong ba med par mchod rten la shing brtsegs mang po
g.yogs pa'i shing cha gram 'grig gis ri phug gi skye shing phal cher gcod dus ma yin pa la gcod dgos byung rung / lo de la ma skyes pa gcig kyang med par je 'phel du song
nas skyes so/ /lar zhwa lu ba rnams kyi bde skyid kyi rtsa ba sku 'bum 'di la thug 'dug go /

dad pa'i 'dzin mar lhag bsam mtha' dag gzugs cansdong bu 'khrungs/ /phun tshogs 'byor pa'i yal 'phreng rgyas pa'i rtser/ /gtong ba'i dri bsung 'thul ba'i me tog gis/ /rgyal
ba'i mchod rten che la srid zhu spel/ /gang tshe rab btagsdad ldan yangs pa'i sbyin po'i tshogs/ /legs byas mdun sar gom stabs brel ba yi/ /gser ldan ma yang bzod min dad
tshul gyis/ /dbyar gyi 'jo sgeg ci yang 'dzin pa snyam/ bsod shis brjod rgyannams dkar po'i snang bas 'gro ba kun/ /skye rga na 'chi'i 'dzin 'khris gang mtsho las/ /pha
mthar phyin pa bde chen chos kyi sku/ /dag pa gnyis dang ldan pas srung gyur cig /dbyar zhugs mtshams la bsdad nas 'dod lha 'ga'i bsnyen pa byas/ hor zla brgyad pa'i tshes
gsum la mtshams grol nas bkra shis lhun por rje btsun dam pa blo bzang yon tan las dpal 'khor lo bde mchog lU i pa'i dbang bka'/ bde mchog bong zhal can gyi dbang bka'/
dril bu lha lha'i dbang bka'/ rnam snang mngon byang gi dbang bka'/ stag phu sprul sku'i yig cha'i steng nas dpal sa skya'i gser chos bcu gsum gyi rjes gnang sogs zhus
so/ /yongs kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen

ngag dbang brtson 'grus dang / dka' chen blo bzang legs bshad kyi zhabs drung du lung kha shas zhus/ sngar rang gi sman bslab pa'i slob dpon sman thang brang khang pa bgres
gzhon gnyis la rgyud bzhi'i lung sogs nged rang gis phul/ dza ya paNDi ta'i phyag mdzod de la yang dar mo bka' rgya ma'i lung byas/ slar hor zla dgu pa'i nyer lnga la ri
phug tu mtshams bcad nas dpal 'khor lo sdom pa lU i pa'i lugs kyi bsnyen chen kha skong sbyin sreg dang bcas pa bsgrubs/ de grol ba dang ri phug nas bteg /g.yang chos padma
lhun sdings kyi dga' tshal du rje bla ma gar dbang ye shes mchog grub mnyes par byas nas grub chen ma hA gu Na'i dgongs gter byin rlabs bla sgrub kyi dbang lung tshang
ma zhu ba la zhag 'ga' bsdad/ sngar bla ma sman khang pa las dngul chu'i bla ma chos bzang rin po che'i snyan pa thos nas de gong gsung chos zhu rgyu'i yi ge phul ba la
ni zhal shes tig po ma byung rung / 'di skabs de kho na mjal bar 'dod nas don grub la khres po bskur te rkang 'gros kyis g.yang chos nas phyin pas rlung po ches nas sa khud
du lus/ sang nyin nam shar la phyin nas rta nag gi phu cu de dang 'phrad/ 'khyag ling chen po sgo

tsam gyis bar gdong bcog pa 'dra ba byung yang gzhon nu nor bzang sogs kyi dka' spyad dran nas dga' ba bsgoms shing brgal nas phyin/ rgyug ma bya ba der zhag gcig bsdad nas
tho rangs snga bar phyin pas mkhar ru lam byang du shar skya ba tsam la slebs so/ /de nas dngul chu'i ri khrod du gung tshigs kyi gong du 'byor te rje btsun dha rma'i mtshan
can gyi zhal mjal bas sngar nas 'dris pa ltar mnyes mnyes mdzad pa zhig byung / bka' chos kyi snyan gsan phab pas sngon la sgra dbyangs can ma'i mtshams sbyor sogs kyi
ri mo 'bul lo gsungs/ de nas ri bo gru 'dzin gyis bla ma rin po che blo bzang tshe ring dang mnyam du sgra'i mtshams sbyor sogs 'khrid cing / snyan dngags me mong gi le'u
bar pa nas rtsom rgyugs kyang phul/ 'di skabs zla bo yang slog nas dngul chur spyil bu zhig g.yar te rang nyid gcig pur bsdad/ bar skabs su bla ma sku khams ma bde ba
dang rang gi nye gnas bskor g.yeng la yongs pa 'dzom byung pas 'jad kyi gnas rnams kyang mjal bar phyin no/ /bzhad ljongs dngul chu'i ri la bla ma rje'i/ /zhabs sen gtsug
gi nor bus gus bsten nas/ /brda sprod snyan dngags la sogs rigs gnas

dang / /zab rgyas chos kyi gnad la sgro 'dogs bcad/ /dpal sdings dgon par gsang ba'i bdag po mjal/ /bgegs dang bar chad zhi ba'i smon lam btab/ /steng ka'i gnas su sbar mo
yul tsam byas/ /grwa tshang chen mor chang gi dus ston mjal/ /yangs pa can du rten bshad cal col nyan/ /chos sgo'i yi dam mthong bas dga' ba skyes/ /dge 'phel gshin chog
'brug ltar ldir ba la/ /ma dad sgro bskur spangs nas ltad mo byas/ /de nas rang lo nyer bzhi pa'i thog thams cad 'dul du grags pa me mo phag gi lo'i hor zla bzhi pa'i sgang
tsam du slebs pa dang / rang gi zla bo yang 'bod par slebs byung ste 'dod chos kyang rags rim thob tshar bas tshogs 'khor dang bsgrags pa'i maNDal rten gsum tshang ba'i
chos yon phul/ yar lam phun tshogs gling dang jo nang du gnas 'brel byas nas zhag shas bsdad/ mar 'ong dus bya gshong mjal bar 'dod kyang lam nor nas bo dong er slebs/
kun mkhyen phyogs las rnam rgyal gyi sku 'dra du sku ma mjal/ phyag mchod mi 'dug pas yi dam dga' tsam zhig byung / sger gzhis dpal sdings su zhag gcig bsdad nas sang nyin
rta zhing btang byung ba de ni yun ring mo nas smyung bar gnas pa'i

bslab bya blangs pa/ lus dka' thub kyi brdungs pas rta khyu'i nang du pho rog dkar por byas nas 'dug pa su la yang ma mkho ba zhig ste/ nged kyi lus po 'degs thub pa lta ci
smos te/ kho rang 'gro ma thub par gangs can chos 'phel gyi thad ka der 'gyel nas 'chi la khad pa byung / rtswa sngon po btog nas gsol mchod cig byas pas ma shi tsam byung
nas phyir phebs rdzong zhus/ nga rang rkang 'gros kyis dal bus rang gnas su 'ongs nas dus mchod chen mo srang ja gnyis sbyor 'bul byas/ lo de'i hor zla lnga pa'i tshes
'go nas brtsams te drung ram pa blo bzang sogs phyogs nas yong ba dang rang re'i grwa rgyun bcas pa kha shas la bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i bka' 'bum gyi lung btang /
chos nyan pa rnams la sde pa rin chen zla bas ston mo nyin ga nga gcig dang / dngul Ti ka re dang kha btags dri med re gnang / zha lu spyi so chen pos kyang ja mar sogs kyi
zur chas dang / rang res kyang ston mo byas te zla ba lhag tsam gyis bar du chos nyan pa rnams tshogs sgrub mchod las kyang bsnyen bkur lhag pa byung ngo / /de grol pa
dang ri khrod byams pa gling du rab byung ma rnams dang / theg chen gling gi dge slong

dril ba la bcu gcig zhal dpal mo lugs lha lnga'i dbang dang / zha chong khyung rtse sogs kyi pho mo mang ba dang bcas pa thun mong du grub rgyal lugs kyi tshe bka' byas/ de
skabs nor rgyas nang ba'i yum sras kyang chos gsan par phebs te sras zhabs sdod pa dpal ldan dbang po 'di lo drug tu slebs pa'i bu chung zhig yod/ sgrub sde gong 'og gnyis
la rang res mang 'gyed mtshon tsam yang btang / dbyar mthong la man khang spel du phyin nas 'di lo g.ya' zangs sman gyi rtse mor yang phyin/ hor zla brgyad pa la mtshams
la zhugs te he ru ka'i yi ge brgyad pa'i bsnyen pa byas/ rang lo nyi shu rtsa lngar slebs pa kun 'dzin zhes pas pho byi ba'i lo shar ba dang / nged rang gis mkhan slob
sbrags ma byas te rin chen bstan 'dzin/ rin chen lhun grub rin chen rnam rgyal te bsgrub bya gsum tshan gcig bsnyen rdzogs su bsgrubs/ de yang 'dul ba las ni bsnyen rdzogs
kyi mkhan po byed pa la mkhan po rang nyid bsnyen rdzogs byas nas lo bcu lon bshad pas nged kyi 'di skabs lo lnga las ma lon/ rgya gar gyi lo tshigs de nyid ma ldog theng
re la lo rer bzhag pas bod kyi phyed lo byas pa mang bas 'di dus phyed lor bzhag pa'i lo

bcu la ngos bzung ba yin rung / rjes su bsam mno bskyar ma btang bas bsgrub bya'i lo nyi shu mang la bshol dang bcas pa sogs kyi zer bas tshig gi shugs las phyed lo ma yin
'dug /thal cha che snyam nas 'dul 'dzin chen po dharmA'i mtshan can la dri ba'i yi ge phul bas/ lan du 'dul ba nas bshad pa de spyir btang la dgongs pa yin/ dmigs bsal gnas
bla ma la brten nas lo lnga nas mkhan po byas chog par gsungs pas khyed kyi 'dul ba'i mkhanya po mdzad pa bka' drin che zhes legs so'i kha btags dang bcas pa yang gnang
byung ngo / /zla ba gnyis pa'i nang du 'di lo nged rang skag thog tu song bas/ ri phug gdan sa ba skal bzang don grub dang / mthil chen po chos rje rin chen tshogs 'phel
gnyis mtshams 'og tu phebs nas zhwa lu spyi so chen po'i ring 'tshe'i rten 'byung maNDal rten gsum dang 'brel ba'i slob dpon rnam gnyis kyis maNDal gyi mtshams sbyor bshad
pa dang gsol 'debs par mdzad song / nged rang ni sngar gyi mtshams kyi 'phro byas nas thugs rje chen po 'khor ba dang sprug dang / padma dbang chen yang gsang khros pa'i
bsnyen pa byas/ nub gcig rmi lam

du / ri phug gi 'du khang byang gi mde'i ma Ni'i khris kyi nyi ma de la thugs sras lo tsA ba sku phyam dmar po bzhes snyel 'bol dang bcas pa'i gdan la bzhugs 'dug nged rang
sku gnyer gyi gsol thabs byang ma de nas gsol ja zhu gin yod pa'i sems la thugs sras rje 'di bu ston rin po che'i chos kyi bdag po khyad par sgra la mkhas pa'u bu chen yin/
'di'i zhabs phyi zhu rgyu yod dus slob gnyer ma byas na da bzod 'gyod 'ong snyam ste/ bdag sgra'i slob gnyer zhig byed dgos pa 'dra lags zhus pas/ de ka byas pas yong
/ sgra ka lA pa'i mdo'i rtsa ba de khyer shog gsungs/ sgrub khang nas dpe cha len par 'ongs pas 'ja' 'od 'bum pa'i thad tsam du gnyid sad nas sems the bde ba zhig byung
/ yang nub gcig nam mkha' la 'phur ba rmi lam yin pas shes nas da rmi lam bzungs nas lho phyogs dpal ldan 'bras spungs kyi mchod rten blta dgos snyam sngar bzhin 'phur bas
lung pa chen po chu mang po g.yas g.yon rnams su yod pa zhig gi dkil na brag rtse mo bsnyung ba gnam la sneg pa 'dra ba zhig 'dug pa brag de la mgo thug la khad pa byung
bas rma bzos kyi dogs pas gnyid sad do/ /nam zla ston ser du

slebs pa dang ri phug nas bteg /khro phur rgyal ba byams pa mgon po la mchod 'bul smon lam yid ches btab/ rong mtsho bskor ba'i sa bstod lho pa'i rje btsun mas rong mtsho dgon
par bos nas zhag gcig bsdad/ de nas dngul chur rje bla ma dharmA'i mtshan can mjal zhing der rgyang tsam bsdad nas sdebs sbyor rin chen 'byung gnas kyi ngo mtshar rtogs
byed kyi ri mo dang / byed grub lnga bsdus sgra gcan dang bcas pa'i ri mo bslab/ sman gyi rtsa rgyud sdong 'grel la yang mdzub 'khris zhus/ rje nyid kyis brtsams chos
par la 'khod zin pa phal cher gyi lung dang rgyal ba bskal bzang rgya mtsho'i gsang ba 'dus pa'i bskyed rim la lung gnang ba 'khrid du dmigs nas gsan pas khyab gsung / dngul
chu dang / gru 'dzin ri khrod kyi dge slong rnams la mang 'gyed mtshon tsam dang padma chos sdings par mang ja gcig zhus/ mar lam gzhung ko byas nas 'ong rtsis la stabs
ma 'grig par rkang 'gros kyis yongs dgos pa byung / rang gnas su slebs nas don gnyer can kha gcig la bcu gcig zhal gyi dbang zhig byas/ rang lo nyer drug pa 'gal ba zhes
pa sa mo glang gi lo sngar nas mig gi dbang po mi dwangs pas de la phan phyir byang gter

spyan ras gzigs mig 'byed kyi bsnyen pa bskyal/ rtse mo sgrub mchod nyin gang gcig gi gtong thebs su dngul srang sum cu tham pa dang srang ja gcig sbyor 'jags byas pa da lta
yod/ ri phug bla ma chos rje ye shes bsam grub dang / dge slong blo gsal ye shes sogs la bde mchog dril bu rdul mtshon lha lnga'i dbang sogs chos than thun bshad do/ /a
ho/ rgyal khams 'grims nas bla ma 'tshol ba bdag /rmig rgyu'i chu la snyeg pa'i ri dwags min/ gdod nas sems la bzhugs pa'i gcong nad gang / /gting nas 'don pa'i sman pa
'tshol mkhan lags/ /phal cher ri la gcig pur 'khyams pa bdag /nyi shar tshang du bros pa'i 'ug pa min/ /spangs kyang ldang pas rnam g.yeng rlung 'tshub kyis/ /dad pa'i sgron
me gnal dogs yib mkhan lags/ /'ga' la chos bshad than thun byed pa bdag /nam zlas skyo bas co ka'i gre 'gyur min/ /thub pa chen po'i lung rtogs chos tshul de/ /deng dus
ches cher nyams pas smre ngag lags/ /kye ho rje btsun chos rje'i bka' drin gyis/ /chos brgyad tshe 'di'i snang shas cung zad nub/ /bdag la gzhan dga'i yon tan ci yang
med/ /spyod tshul ngan kyang ku re zhus pa lags/ /de nas da lta ri phug gi khri zer rin chen blo

bzang mkhyen rab 'di/ /nged kyi bla ma sman khang pa'i skye ba yin pa'i gleng brjod la brten/ skyabs mgon paN chen rin po che'i gsung brtag gnang ba la yang babs te byis pa
lo drug tu slebs pa dang nged rang gi zla la bsdad/ 'di lo bco lnga tshes gnyis kyi sgrub mchod la tshogs kyi sgrigs la bcug /mang ja/ rnam gzhag srang ja gcig gi sbyor
'jags dang chos spyod rags bsdus kyi rgyugs sprod rgyu yod pa byas so/ /bar skabs su lnga bsngus kyi ri mo byas te 'di nas lo 'ga' re'i lag 'dzin gyi le'u tho tshang ma
'don thub pa byung rung / bar skabs nas lag len bya rgyu ma byung ngo / /rang lo nyer bdun pa rnam 'gyur zhes pa lcags pho stag gi lo gsar pa dang sdeb rin chen zla bas nged
rang gi brtan bzhugs tshigs bcad 'ga' dgos gsung pa'i 'phrin shog byung ste/ phun tshogs bde ldan ma 'di 'phral du brtsams nas phul/ hor zla dang po'i tshes bco lnga
la don zhags sgrub mchod nyin gang dang bcas pa'i zhabs tog yon zab pa dang bcas te zhwa lu 'dus sde'i tshigs 'don du 'dzugs pa gnang / sde pa rang sku gzugs gcong nge las
med kyang de nyin tshogs su spos bskor mdzad par na bza' mchor bzhes nas

phebs 'dug /lo 'di la phyag rdor gos sngon dang 'byung 'dul sogs kyi bsnyen pa byas/ nag pa zla ba la grangs chen pogrwa tshang du dus 'khor gyi tshogs 'khor gtong rgyu'i
thebs su dngul srang drug sbyar/ dar gos chen sham brtsegs kyi gdugs legs pa zhig gsar bzo byas nas dkyil 'khor la phul/ rta nag rin chen rtse'i sde pa zhabs drung blo bzang
skal bzang la spu nag dang / gzhi ka rtse dar rgyas sbag rwa ba la ras zam gyi dge bskul byas te/ skyabs mgon paN chen rin po che'i dgung lo zhe dgu'i skag tu phebs
pa'i zhabs brtan du dmigs dus mchod chen mo la ri phug 'du khang lho byang gi thugs dang rgyal mtshan tshang ma gsar spos thub par byas/ 'di skabs gna' sad lung gi btsun
chung rin chen chos legs kyis dus 'khor bsdus brgyud le'u lnga pa blo 'dzin byas nas nged la rgyugs phud dang bcas tshogs su bla chen bzhengs/ smon tshig gsar rtsom dgos
zhes bskul nas ming blo gsal mi pham zhes pa'ang btags pa da lta dge sleng bla chen zer ba 'di yin no/ /dar rgyas sbag rwa ba'i tshong dpon g.yul rgyal nor bu khong rang
'ongs te bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i sku 'dra rin po cher sku ber dang dbu zhwa gsar pa phul/ tshogs su mang ja bskol/ nged la tshe dbang zhus song

rang re'i sku skye sogs btsun chung kha shas dang byams pa gling gi btsun ma gsang pa 'ga' rab byung du bsgrubs/ dbyar zhugs ri khrod byams pa gling du phyin nas bde mchog
lU yi pa'i sgo nas las thams cad pa'i sbyin sreg rgyas par byas shing grwa btsun rnams la chos phran bu bshad/ slar ri phug tu grangs che bla ma phun tshogs chos 'phel dang
/ bla chen blo gsal mi pham la bsnyen rdzogs byas/ rang lo nyer brgyad pa bong bu zhes pa lcags mo yos kyi lo rdo rje rnam 'joms dang gshed dmar lha lnga'i bsnyen pa btang
/ rje bla ma dge slong a wa dha tAM pa chen po ri phug tu phebs te phyag na rdo rje 'khor lo chen po lha bco brgyad kyi dbang dang gsang sngags lam rim sogs gsung chos
kha shas zhus shing thob/ phar nA ro mkha' spyod kyi dbang 'khrid tshang ma phul/ de sngon sde pa rin chen zla ba la yang 'di lo drug cu re gcig gi skag yin pa dang /
sde pa rang bkra shis lhun por bzhugs thub na rab/ de min rtse thor bzhugs nas sger gzhis dpal sdings phyogs su ma phebs zer ba byas rung ma gsan par phebs tshar 'dug /zla
ba gsum pa'i mjug la dpal sdings su sku gshegs

pa'i bsngo zhus slebs byung / sde pa 'di nged rang la drin che ba yin pas sgrib sbyong gang shes dang tshogs su mang ja btang zhing smon lam 'don du bcug pa yin/ dam rdzas
bdud rtsi ril bu'i bsgrub pa zhig kyang byas nas grol ba dang mnyam du sngar nas gsung chos zhu rgyu'i snyan gsan phab tshar bas rtag brtan dam chos gling gi chos grwar rje
btsun rdo rje 'chang spo ra ba chen po'i spyan sngar 'gro ba'i lam zhor du gnyan yod bya rgod gshong mjal/ bya gshong gi thugs rje chen po 'di bcu gcig zhal nam mkha'
rgyal po dang 'jigs pa brgyad skyob gang yin ni cha mi 'tshal/ chos rgyal srong btsan sgam pos bzhengs pa'i gsung 'byon ngo mtshar shin tu che ba yin par 'dug /rnam sras
mdung dmar 'di yang sngon ser chen du ngos 'dzin pa la chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston chen pos mdung dmar zhal gzigs nas zhal gser gyi steng du slar mtshal zhus pa
yin zhes grags zil chen po zhig ni 'dug /rtag brtan du slebs nas rje bla ma mjal bas de ring tshes nyi shu brgyad tsam du 'dug /tshes gcig la dbang gi sta gon byas nas chos
tshugs par byed do gsungs/ de bar las med du sdod par phangs nas sang nyin snga bar lcags zam

don / rkang 'gros kyi chos lung byang rtse mjal du phyin/ rje grol mchog gi dngul gdung rin po che soegs rten gsum rnams la byin rlabs zhus/ phag mo dur khrod du gcod dmigs
bsdus pa zhig byas/ dge sleng rnams la mang ja gcig bskol rgyu sprad/ slar 'ongs te tshes dkar ba dang dpal ldan shangs pa bka' brgyud pa'i phyag bzhes ltar bde mchog ne
gu lha lnga'i dbang mdzad/ rim gyi rtsa ba ne gu chos drug /sdong po phyag rgya chen po/ /yal ga lam khyer rnam gsum/ me tog mkha' spyod dkar dmar/ 'bras bu 'chi med 'phyug
med de/ shangs pa'i gser chos lngar grags pa'i nang nas rje bla ma de la ji ltar mnga' ba phal cher zhus shing thob/ jo nang sogs rten mjal yang tshang bar byas so/ e
ma ho/ nub si lam la yi sgo nas 'thon/ /yul gnyan yod bya gshong lha khang mjal/ /dpal nags rgyal ri bo'i ljongs su phyin/ gnas jo nang dben pa'i chab skor slebs/ /khong
sbas pa'i skyes mchog 'gro ba'i mgon/ /rje a wa dhutI'i zhabs la gtugs/ /lam rgyud sde lnga yi snying po mchog /dpal shangs pa'i gser chos gdams ngag zhus/ /sprang 'khos
med kyi btsun pa

blo gsal bdag /pho thos rgya can zhig ma lags te/ /don dbang 'khrid gnad la sgro dogs bcad/ /da ya mtshan che ba ma lags sam/ /de nas rang gnas su slebs te ma he mchod pa byed
ran pas don gnyer can kha shas la gshed dmar lha lnga'i dbang dang chos skyong rnams kyi rjes gnang btang / chos khrims pa rin chen skal bzang chos 'phel sogs la bsnyen
rdzogs kyi bslab sdom phog /rang lo nyer dgu pa dga' ba zhes pa chu pho 'brug gi lo'i nang du yi ge brgya pa 'bum ther gcig dang ri khrod lo ma khyon ma'i bsnyan pa dang
bu mchog 'ga' re grangs gsog byas/ rang sdod sa'i khang pa hrul bas bcos phran bu bya dgos byung lhun grub pho brang du spos nas bsdad/ bsam grub chos sdings nas lo snga
ma ma ha skad gtong byed pa'i rtogs ldan de glo bur du 'das ze bsngo zhus skyel mkhan zhig kyang byung / khong dang nged na mnyam du 'dug pas skyo shas che ba dang rang
rtag tu sdod pa'i grab gshom khang pa sogs la bcos byed pa 'di'ang 'khrul 'dug snyam pa skyes/ de rjes dga' lung ri khrod nas rab byung ma rnams kyi zhus te bcu gcig zhal
lha lnga'i dbang sogs chos than thun bshad/ de nas dgun mtshams sogs byas so/ /rang lo sum cu pa rnam

gsal / tshad ma rig gter/ sdebs sbyor me tog gi chun po/ kun blos mdzad pa'i 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma'i sgrub dkyil nag 'gros/ ri khrod ma'i bum chog /rje btsun gyi rab gnas
don gsal/ a mes zhabs kun bsod kyis mdzad pa'i rab gnas don thams cad grub pa sogs kyi lung dang / 'jam dbyangs smra ba'i seng ge/ 'jam dbyangs dmar ser sa lugs/ 'jam dkar
ma ti lugs rnams kyi rjes gnang lung bcas pa/ sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo 'od zer drug sbrags kyi rjes gnang tshe 'khrid zla ba'i chu rgyun dang bcas pa/ dur bdag gi
rjes gnang chos skor tshang ma'i lung dang bcas pa zhus shing thob bo/ /sa skya tshogs su chos dung dkar po rgyang grags bus pa'i mang ja bzang ba gcig btang / thar rtse
rdo rraje 'chang mai tri andan shA sa na dha ra shri bha dra'i zhal snga nas kyang zhabs brtan lha khang gi gong ma yab sras la bka' chos 'bul bar phebs te zhal spro lha
khang du bzhugs pa dang mjal/ gdugs dkar nyer bdun ma'i dbang gi mtshams sbyor zhig dgos gsung ba zhabs 'gyur zhus/ zla ba bdun pa'i tshes brgyad la sngon 'gro snang ba gsum
po rdzogs nas dbu rtse'i 'du khang gi 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar ba'i spyan sngar sems

bskyed chen mo mdzad/ de nyid ban tshang pa dang dung pa/ rgya gling pa/ nged cag chos zhu ba dang bcas pa rnams la sku gdung rin po che sku sger gyi phyag 'gyed zab pa gnang
zhing lam 'bras bla ma brgyud pa'i gos thang zhe gcig 'du khang gi nang du 'gram pa dang / chos dung dkar rgyang 'bud pa/ bla ma yab sras snam sbyar rdo rje gsang lam
bzhes shing sku'i nyer spyad du 'os pa gser chas bsgrigs pa sogs zab zab mdzad pa'i phyag len snang / de nas rgyud gsum tshugs pa'i bar la chos seng 'dug pas nged rang zhwa
lur 'ongs te sngar phun khang chos mdzad sku zhabs kyi nor bum sgrub rgyu yod pa 'di skabs 'jug pa sogs la bkras lhun du 'khor tsam phyin/ slar bde chen sprul sku dang
/ dka' chen blo bzang dge legs/ stod phyogs nas bu lung bla ma rin po che yang phebs te sgrub thabs rin chen 'byung gnas kyi rjes gnang cha tshang dang / dpal 'khor lo bde
mchog lU yi pa'i dbang bka' rnams so so'i dgongs bzhed ltar phul/ de tshar ba dang sa skya nas sbar shabs brgyud nas bka' rgya gtong rgyu yin gsung pa la ni ma byung /
bka' chos re zhig ma tshugs na dgun mtshams la yang sdod ran pas

khyad par byung ste nyer len gyi pho nya btang bas/ phyir phebs su 'jam mgon bla ma gzhi bsnyen kha so'i bcad rgya gnang grub/ de rtsis kyi 'phral rang du shog gsung pa'i dus
gtugs shig byung / bkras rdzong nas phun khang gi rta drel sogs zhus te myur shed kyi phyin pas sa skyar slebs pa'i nub de rang la sku mtshams grol te sang nyin tho rangs
bla brang shar pa tsho lags zer/ 'bod mkhan zhig 'dug /nged rang gi zla bo dang rta slog po sogs ni gnyid du song nas lan med/ nged kyi bltas pas bka' dbang zhu ba la
phebs zer/ de nas bzhi thog pho brang gi chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che'i bzhugs khri padma can gyi sar dpal kye rdo rje'i rgyu dus dbang gi sta gon mdzad/ slob
bshad lugs kyi rgyud sde'i rab dbye sogs nas drangs pa'i dbang bshad rgyas drags nas sta gon de la yun ring po 'gor rung gsung chos grol nas skya rengs 'char ba'i grabs mi
'dug /de dus 'jam mgon bla ma rang gi dbu bla'i gras kyang yin pas gyang ra dpon slob tu grags pa dang / phyag mdzod zer khang nas bgres po yang dbang zhu bar phebs/ sang
de yang snga mo nas khong gnyis kyis nged bos byung ste phyin pas/ dge slong chos don grub na re/ kha sang dkyil 'khor bris thig ma

zin dogs snga mo mdzad pa yin/ de ring da lta med do zer nas phyir log dgos pa byung / de ltar rgyu dbang grub nas bkra shis brtsegs par phebs te rgyud gsum gyi bka' chos tshugs
so/ /lha rigs 'khon gyi sa 'dzin skya bo'i rtser/ /rgyal rnams mkhyen pa'i mkha' dbyings las 'das dhIH 'phos pa'i ngo mtshar dpal gyi dum bu'i dri/ /lha bcas 'gro la
shin tu bsil ba'i sman/ /byams pa'i rang bzhin ngag dbang kun dga'i gnyen/ /phyogs rnams kun las rnam par rgyal ba'i mtshan/ /bzang po'i mgon khyod mtha' klas dkyil 'khor
lha'i/ /spro dang bsdu ba yongs kyi byed par nges/ /rigs kyi thig le'i dge mtshan dpyid ka yis/ /bzung bas rdo rje theg pa'i dga' tshal nang / /rin chen chos kyi snyan
sgrog ko ki la/ /phan bde'i dus ston 'dren phyir sa 'di'i rgyan/ /thog mar smin byed dbang gi chos sgo dbye/ /bar du rgyud don mthar thug gtan la phab/ /mtha' mar zab mo'i
gdams pas tshim mdzad pa/ /bka' drin gsum gyi phung po khyod kho na/ /'di skabs 'jam mgon rdo rje rin chen gyi drung du/ /sbyong rgyud dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis kyi dbang
lung tshang ba dang /

gsang ba 'dus pa ye shes zhabs lugs kyi dbang / nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs/ /kun bsod kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub dkyil lung / /tshe dbang 'chi med dpal ster sogs thob bo/
/gung pa blo rgyam pa la dri med rnam gnyis kyi dbang 'bul dgos gsung pa phul/ bkra shis brtsegs nas 'jam mgon bla mas nged la sgrub thabs rin 'byung dgos phebs byung yang
gzhung bshad kyi phyag dpe gzigs dgos dang thug pas sngon la ni 'bul mi thub/ rjes su ni long med pas ma 'grig go /de nas sa skya mdos chen dang dgung gsar sogs grub mtshams
su zhwa lu nas yi ge slebs te/ ri bo dga' ldan du rdor dbyings gi dbang rgyun spel mkhan zhwa lu na 'os pa su yod rtsad gcod la gzhung nas bka' rgya byung pas/ nged
'os tho la phul tshar bas bka' chos 'phral du grub thabs dgos tshul dang / yang de rting nged rang la rgyal tshab rin po ches bka' rgya mdzad nas zla ba dang po'i tshes
bco lnga tshun la lha sar 'byor pa yong dgos gsung ba phebs par ma zad gzhung sa'i bka' bkod yul gnyan la brten zhwa lur bzhugs pa'i bla ma slob dpon rnams thugs tshab tshab
mdzad pas yi ge skyel ba la de dus khams 'grul yod pas

stabs mi res yong mi nus pa gnyis tsam re yong gin 'dug pa sogs mi ser grong pa ngan hrul rnams la bsun rkyen byed pa 'dra snyam nas bkra shis brtsegs su rgyu rkyen zhus pas/
da 'o na gsang dbang gi lam song mtshams su bzhag chog gsungs te dkyus kyi bka' chos tshar ba dang / nged rang gcig pu la gsang dbang rdzogs pa'i bar gnang / gser dngul
dar gos/ snam bu sogs ci 'byor gyi dngos po phul/ nged rang la yang snga phyir gsol ras mang po gnang ba byung / sa skya nas btegs 'ongs te mar lam gyi rta bsu btang nas
phran du 'bod pa 'dug pas phyin/ phran sa nang pa'i sde pa sku ngos rnams la tshe dbang byabs khrus sogs byas/ ri phug tu rang lo so bdun pa kun ldan zhes pa lcags pho
byi ba'i lo shar pa dang / skyabs mgon chen po dang 'jam mgon bla ma yab sras rnams kyi zhabs brtan du dmigs te zhwa lu 'dus tshogs nas cho 'phrul zla ba'i dus chen la sgrol
dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i cho ga gtong thabs su dngul srang lnga bcu tham pa deb sbyor byas pa da lta gong 'phel du yod/ 'di skabs rkang pa cung ma bde bas gzhung sar
dgongs zhu byas pas lo 'di'i zla ba gnyis

pa'i nang du dga' ldan byang rtse dge bshes dge legs bzang po rdor dbyings kyi dbang zhu bar rdzong brda gnang / rgyal tshab rin po ches kho bo la da lam khyed rang 'byung
khams ma bde phyir khrol cha byas pa yin gsung pa sogs bka' shog bskur pa'i rten la gos ser gyon ldang gcig /phyag mdud/ kha btags nyin mo bde legs ma bcas dang / gzhung
gi dbang yon du ja sgam gcig /dngul srang bcu/ gos chen yug /mchod dod srang do/ kha btags a she bcas 'byor byung / dge bshes khong yang lam bar du rkang 'bam gyis bsnyun
nas 'di khar rdor dbyings kyi sta gon dang dbang dngos gzhi la ma gtogs nged kyi sar phebs ma thub/ khong gis sar nged kyi phyin nas yo ga Tika dang / rdo rje 'byung ba'i
lag len rin chen bsam 'phel sogs rdor dbyings kyi chos skor tshang ma phul/ zhabs kyi bsnyel gzhi de la yang nged rang gis bcos kas phan pa byung / de mtshams su rgyud
smad pa'i dge bshes ngag dbang dar rgyas kyang chos gsan par phebs/ khong dpon slob stabs gcig tu dpal 'khor lo bde mchog bong zhal can gyi dbang bka' dang / nA ro mkha'
spyod kyi dbang 'khrid cha tshang btang / sku skye byams pa rnal rgyal la 'jam

dbyangs smra seng gi rjes gnang sogs shes rab 'phel ba'i rten 'brel sgrib thub pa byas/ yo ga'i dbang sogs kyi phyag len dka' gshis nged rang gis dbang gi sa bcad bsgrigs pa
zhig phul bas dge bshes de mtshan nyid par song bar brten sa bcad de la mnyes po byung song / bsnyen pa byed tshul sogs zin bris than thun dgos gsung pa rnams kyang de
'phral bris nas phul lo/ /rgyal tshab rin po chos kyang rjes su zhwa lu pa'i chos gzhis sogs la rgyab snon bka' shog gnang ba sogs gzigs zos che ba mdzad rung / rang re zhwa
lu ba'i mis ni bka' shog gi rgyab rtsi mi 'pher zhing nang du ltogs gshe tshal phyi ru 'bul ba lung gi gleng gzhi las byung ba'i legs 'od nyes 'ong du song ba'i gtam
brgyud kyi 'gran zlar 'phyan pa kho na byas so/ /e ma hoH gnas shrI bhU mi'i dgon pa ru/ /rje sa skya'i bla chen zhabs la gtugs/ /ma bdag med DA ki'i thugs kyi bcud/ /khong
paN grub dbang po birawa pa/ /dbyings phyag rgya chen por gshegs pa'i lam/ /chos snyan brgyud tshad ma bzhi ldan gyi/ /tshul ma nyams gsung ngag slob bshad la/ /sems yid
ches drag pos rna gtad byas/ /yulaH

bsil ldan rgyal po'i bka' lung gis/ /yongs sde snod 'dzin pa'i bshes gnyen la/ /dpal rdo rje dbyings kyi smin grol bshad/ /nad zug rngu'i mtshan mar sbar 'don btang / /sprang
'khos med kyi blo gsal glen sgom bdag /pho mkhas po btsun po gcig ma lags te/ /khong dad ldan 'ga'i bla ma go chod byung / /de ya mtshan che ma lags sam/ /de nas dge bskos
rin chen mkhas grub la zhwa lu mthil gyi chen po'i 'os bsdu byas pas khong gi bsam mno ya mtshan pa zhig la kha bo la rdor dbyings kyi dbang gcig kyang zhus song / gzhan
ni zhwa lu ba'i deng sang gi bla ma slob dpon byed pa gzhan tsho ni rngan pa sbyin rgyu yin pas dbang zhu ru shog byas kyang bros 'gro dgos pa tsam yin 'dug /sngar phun
khang chos mdzad sku zhabs dang nor brang lde chung ba sku bgres pa gnyis la zhu sna bcol nas bla brang chen por sgrol dkar gyi zab thang zhwa lu'i 'du khang gi thog
tshad ma gcig bzhengs rgyu'i snyan gsan dngos rgyu dngul srang lnga bcu la bskor ba dang bcas pa phul ba don smin bka' drin bskyangsbrkyangs pas/ 'di skabs nor bu gra' khang
nas gnyer don grub tshe ring ming bkra bzang pas skyol shog ces khong pa zab thab skyel du byung / nged rang

skag thog tu 'byor pa la grangs che grwa tshang gi bla ma dbu chos rnams byon nas sgrol dkar gyi tsha mchog dang 'brel ba'i brtan bzhugs phul/ de nyin zab thang bkrams nas
rab gnas dang khong rnams la'ang sgrol dkar gyi rjes gnang bas/ de nas ri khrod byams pa gling gi rab byung ma 'dus spyi nas gnas bcu'i phyag mchod sogs dang mkha' 'gro brtan
bzhugs rnams kyi sgo nas ring 'tsho'i rten 'byung phul te so so'i dngos po phyir sprod dang mang ja sogs btang / ston ser du slebs pa dang / skyin khang lcog spel bas
'bod mkhan byung ste der rkyen sel gyi rim gro mang du byas/ de gong ka bzhi ba'i bud med kyis mi bsad lab gleng la brten nas ka lcog gnyis po 'khrug pa shor te lcog spel
bam thub rung ka bzhi bas rgyal chen shugs ldan par bcol gtam gyis lcog spel bar 'bu tshe zad grog mo'i sgo drung du slebs tshar ba yin zhes brjod kyin yong 'dug ste/
ang yig pa sangs ma rgyas/ nye gnas sangs rgyas pa'i dpe bzhin ka bzhi ba rang gi mi ngo drag pa tsho shi/ lcog spel ba la da lta phan chad du mi shi byung ma song / gzhan
ni mi la shi chad los yong / de nas nged kyi tsha chu'i 'phrod bstenbrtan byas pas

rje bla ma seng chen rdo rje 'chang yang de na phebs 'dug pa mjal/ chab kyi 'phrod ngo chung bas 'phral la theg rgyu yin gsung / nged kyi snyugs su bsrings na ma gtogs ha go
mi yong zhus pas re zhig bzhugs te mjug la 'phrod ngo yang byung tshod gda'/ dbang ldan chos 'khor ba rnams kyis nged 'bod pa 'dug pas lam zhor du bal bu lha khang mjal
bar phyin nas zhag gcig sdad/ de na lha gcig khri btsun chos rgyal srong btsan sgam po'i btsun mor byon dus kyi mchod gnas bal po'i paNDita manydzu shrI las bzhengs pa'i
rdo rje dbyings kyi rtsa ba'i lha so bdun po thams cad chos rgya 'cha' ba'i tshul can shin tu ngo mtshar ba 'dug /gshed dmar lha lnga'i lha khang zhig kyang 'dug ste rnal
'byor dbang phyug gi lugs dang mi mthun no/ /de nas rim gyi grwa tshang gi bla ma dbu chos rnams kyang bsu ba la phebs/ thab bsu'i gur zhig 'dug par ja zhal dngas pa gsol
nas chos 'khor du phyin no/ /slob dpon chos 'dzin lags kyi shag tu zhag gcig bsdad nas sang nyin yar lam slob dpon tshul khrims lags kyi shag tu bos nas gung tshigs drangs/
'du khang rtser phyin nas lha mo mjal zhing rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje'i bzhugs khri de la bsdad cing /

grwa tshang gi gro so phye mar sogs bteg byung / grwa byings la theg ma'i chos 'brel du sman bla mdo cho ga yid bzhin dbang rgyal gyi lung btang / de nas dpal phyag na rdo
rje 'gro bzang snying po'i lugs dang / gshed dmar lha lnga'i dbang bka' byas/ nged rang gis mang 'gyed dang / 'jog rtse mo'i cho ga nag 'gros su bkod pa'i glegs bam gsar
bris spus gtsang gcig /rtse mo sgrub mchod nyin gang gcig gi gtong thebs su srang bcu gsum sbyar/ dbang ldan sger gsum po'i gzhis so sor spyan 'dren byung pas phyin te bar
che dang cha lur rdor dbyings kyi zhi ba'i sbyin sreg re dang / gzhan tshang mar tshe bka' byabs khrus sogs byas/ slar chos 'khor du 'ongs te slob dpon blo gsal lags nas
grang chung du bsnyen bkur zhag shas zhus shing / de nas grwa tshang gi 'du khang du maNDal rten gsum sogs 'bul tshan rnams len par phyin pas slob dpon tshul khrims lags
kyis/ nged kyi che brjod dang grwa tshang gi bstod ra gnyis po 'dra se 'dres se byas pa'i maNDal gyi mtshams sbyor bshad pa ni myog la mang ba zhig mdzad song / sger 'bul
phran phran ma gtogs grwa tshang gi 'bul ba tshang

ma phyir slog byas/ de nas btegs pa'i lam zhor du 'dus byung smon skyid kyi sde pa tshe brtan phun tshogs la sger du phyag drug pa bar chad kun sel gyi rjes gnang dang spyir
tshe bka' byabs khrus sogs byas shing yar lam rang gi gzhis su nang mi rnams 'phrad tsam dang bskyal chad dka' spel ba'i rgan dpon de la steng grib byung zer ma nyan par
bos rung 'tsho thub re mi 'dug pas de 'phral tsam la 'ongs te ron skams su phyin pas der yod pa'i sgang la rgan dpon yang 'das 'dug /de nas rang gnas su slebs pa dang dgun
mtshams tshugs thub par bgyis so/ /ne'u gsing sngon po'i do ra 'khrigs pa'i tshal/ /dge bcu kun tshang skyin mkhar yul gyi phur/ /dad ldan sbyin pos bsnyen bkur btab
pa las/ /rang byung khrus kyi rdzing bur chu 'dugs bsten/ /'jam mgon tshangs pa lha yi me tog nyid/ /bsam bzhin byon pa'i mkhyen rab chos kyi rje/ /gang gi bsti gnas dbang
ldan chos 'khor du/ /brgyud pa'i mtshan don skyong ba'i lhag bsam bstar/ /de nas nam zla dgun gyi rgyal mo'i bkas/ /dal 'gro'i rgyun rnams dar thag brkyangs nas byung /
/rnal 'byor ngas kyang ri sul spong khang du/ /bem chung gos su

gyon nas mnyam par bzhag /rang lo so brgyad pa 'phar ba zhes pa lcags mo glang gi lo shar pa dang / sgrol dkar sgrub mchod la zab sku sbyar zhing mang 'gyed btang / sngar gyi
rgyun las dge sbyor skyong khul yod dus drung chen chos mdzad lags nas lde chung pa rgyal chen rtse ba la dge bskul mdzad/ 'di kha'i mchod rten rnams kyi rdza hrul ba
kun gsar spos kyi nyams gso byung ste mchod yon gyi cho ga 'bul ba dang / grub nas rab gnas sogs byas/ nged rang gis zhwa lu phu nas rdo drangs te mkhan brgyud/ sangs rgyas
so lnga/ sman bla bde gshegs brgyad sogs rdo lha mang po bzhengs pa ha lam bskos tshar pas sngar mkhan chen rin chen 'jam dpal gyi phyi rten tsha khang ring mo la nyams
gso dang bsgrags rdo lha rnams sgrig thub pa byas/ sog po ne man tho yon mkhas dbang don grub rgyal mtshan la sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor dang / bde mchog padma dra ba/ gshin
rje gdong drug rnams kyi dbang bka' sogs chos phran bu bshad/ 'di lo la sing dpung 'jug la brten zhwa lu mkhan po'i chos gzhis la rta dmag gal/ ngo tsha ba rnams kyis
chos sde spyi sor

kha phangs byas te mgon khang gi spyan gzigs me mda' gri sogs sprod dgos pa dang / kho bos dngul srang lnga bcu khro la 'don sogs rna mchog bregs kyang rkub kyi lhan pa mi
zin pa zhig gda'/ sa skyar 'jam mgon bla ma yang sku khams ngan pa'i gnas tshul thos nas gsol 'debs kyi rten dang bcas pa'i zhu yig 'bul mkhan btang / phyir phebs su bsnyel
gzhi byung tshul zhib bsed dang / byang kha'i dogs gnas 'dug pas byad bzlog dang tshe sgrub gang drag byed dgos pos khams dngas po byung na nged rang dpon slob dam tshig
gtsang bas sngar gyi chos 'phro yod pa'ang tshang bar bed do gsungs pa'i bka' bzang po dang thugs dam bris sku kha shas bskur nas ri phug tu phul gsung ba 'byor ro/ de
'phral zhwa lu tshogs su mang ja dang / mgon khang rnams su bskang 'phrin gtong 'jug kho bo rang nas kyang zhabs brtan la 'bad rung / rmi lam du'ang rje nyid na bza' med
pa'i sku gcer bu mdzad nas bzhugs pa zhig byung ste slar zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes dkar 'phral gzugs sku chos dbyings su thim pa byung tshod 'dug /da ni gang la bsam yang
snying po med pa dang / kho bo rang gi chos sgrub blo 'di'ang ra ma rgan mo na ring gi rdzab la btang pa dang

khyad par mi 'dug /ra ma rgan mo des kyang rtsa ne ring gcig 'then bsam phe/ gnyis 'then bsam phe/ mthar thams cad la kha tsogs tsam re byas nas rtsa za rgyu med par nyal 'dug
pa 'ong / de bzhin du rang res kyang chos gcig la tshwa bltas/ gnyis la tshwa bltas/ mthar thams cad la tshwa blta ba tsam re byas/ nyams myong sna kha gcig kyang mi
yong ba 'dug /yang kha gcig na re/ khyod kyi chos bya lugs ma shes pa yin/ chos mang po zhu ba dang rnam grangs mang po'i nyams len g.yeng ba'i rgyu yin/ chos gcig la bsgril
dgos/ sngon gyi bka' gdams pas kyang / phan bya mang po sgrib shing yin/ /rang mgo 'don na gcig la bsgril/ /zhes gsungs pa mi gda' 'am zer/ de ka yin pa 'dug ste mi yong
ba 'dug /byung na lta byad 'dod pa gcig yin/ de ni bka' sde snod gsum po thams cad bslabs po gsum du dril nas rang sems 'dul rgyu'i skad cha yin gyi/ chos spyod bcu la
sogs pa'i rnam grangs mang po ma byed zhog zer ba'i tshig tu 'gro ba dka'o/ /rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i go 'phang sgrub pa la tshogs dpag tu med pa gsog dgos pas las
sla

ba zhig gis mi yong ngo / /byang chub sgrub rgyu sogs kyi bsam mno med par nyi ma phul byed yin na ci dga' bar zad do/ /ngas ni bka' sde snod gsum dang rgyud sde bzhi bo mi
dgos/ mu stegs rgyang 'phen gyi grub mtha' yan chad la blo'i dpyad pa dor ba bya ba'i tshul yod pa ma shes so/ /da lta'i bod kyi btsun pa khyu gcig la kha ton skyor rgyu
rnam grangs mang po ni 'ong gin 'dug /de gcig la bsgril nas rang mgo thon pa byung na yi ge klog po slob kyang mi dgos so/ /ngas ni rang mgo 'don na gcig la bsgril/ zer
ba dang / spyod 'jug las/ sems bsrung brtul zhugs ma gtogs pa/ /brtul zhugs mang pos ci zhig bya/ /zhes dang / shes spring las/ bsnyengs dang bral la mang du gsol ci 'tshal/
/phan pa'i gdams ngag don po 'di lags te/ /khyod ni thugs thul mdzod cig bcom ldan gyis/ /sems ni chos kyi rtsa ba lags por gsungs/ /zhes pa rnams gnad gcig tu go mod
kyi/ de ni kha na mi 'dug cing 'dzin pa'i thabs su rnam grangs mang po dgos pa yang yod/ mi dgos pa yang yod pas/ ham pa'i sbar tshod de 'dra rang thams cad la mi rung ngo
/ /he he/ de nas se ra'i dge bshes dge 'dun blo gros sogs la rje btsun tsong kha ba'i 'khrid yig yid ches

gsum lnad gyi bzhed srol ltar nA ro chos drug gi 'khrid btang / nA ro chos drug la bu ston sogs kyi brgyud po 'ded rgyu byas pa'ang deng sang dge lugs pa'i 'khrid tshul 'di
ma gtogs gzhan ma rnyed do/ /de rjes dge slong ye shes rnam rgyal sogs la nA ro mkha' spyod kyi 'khrid lung tshang ba byas so/ /rang lo so dgu pa dge byed ces pa chu pho
stag gi lo skyabs mgon chen po'i zhabs brtan tshe sgrub lo 'khor gyi dgos cha gnang bas lo hril gyis/ mtshams byas nas bde mchog dkar po sogs kyi tshe bsnyen btang zhing
zhabs brtan sgrub tshul byas/ hor zla lnga po tsam la chos seng gi tshul du mtshams grol nas ngor du phyin/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen gzigs byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin
gyi drung du dpal kyai rdo rje bka' bab bzhi'i dbang dang / lam dus kha gso'i dbang dang rjes gnang kha shas zhus/ rje bla ma ngag dbang legs grub pa'i spyan sngar bde
mchog mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho dang / gur rigs bsdus kyi dbang bka' zhus/ kho bo rang gis mkhan chen sku bgres gzhon sogs la 'od zer dri med kyi dbang dang / rnam sras bka'
chen bco lnga'i rjes gnang phul/ ngor dgon pa'i mgon khang

bka' rgya ma sogs tshang mar mchod mjal zhus/ de skabs a mdo brag dgon rin po che yang nged rtsad gcod cing ngor du phebs/ khong la 'dod chos rnams rtsol ba gang che dgos pa'i
rgyab skyor du rgyal tshab tshe smon gling gis bka' shog gcig kyang bskur 'dug /sde dge sprul pa'i sku dang yang de dus mjal zhing slar ri phug tu dbang gsan par phebs
rgyu'i skor la mkhan rin po ches nged la gnyer gtam mdzad/ tshur 'khor nas bkras lhun du rje btsun bla ma ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma blo bzang chos dbyings bde chen mtsho
mo phebs pas mjal bar phyin nas seng gdong rigs lnga'i rjes gnang sogs zhus/ ri phug tu slebs pa dang rgyud smad pa'i dge bshes ngag dbang dar rgyas kyang chos gsan par
phebs/ de yang brag dgon rin po ches gsan rgyu'i skor ni khong rang gi phyag bris su mdzad pa 'di ltar ro/ /drin can rtsa ba'i bla ma rdo rje 'chang chen po'i zhabs kyi
padmo'idrung du/ sprang 'khyams bdag gi bka'achos snyan gsan zhu rgyu'i tho ni/ gsang 'dus 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ gsang 'dus 'jig rten dbang phyug /ma hA ma ya/ kyai rdor/ bde
mchog la wa bcu gsum ma/ bde mchog padma dra ba/ bde mchog sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor/ rtse mo rigs

bsdus / khams gsum rnam rgyal/ dpal mchog rdor sems/ 'jam dpal gsang ldan/ gtsug dgu/ mi 'khrugs pa lha bcu gsum/ 'od zer dri med/ gzungs grwa lnga/ don zhags lha mang / phyag
rdor 'gro bzang / rnam 'joms dkar po/ rdo rje gdan bzhi/ 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma rwa tshar lugs/ gdong drug /'chi bdag 'joms pa/ rta mgrin yang gsang / g.yu thog snying
thig /tshe dbang 'chi med dpal ster/ 'jam dpal smra seng gi rjes gnang dang las tshogs/ mgon po beng gi rjes gnang / jem dmar grwa mngon lugs kyi rjes gnang / ging lnga
gza' gdong gi rjes gnang / lcam sring gtso 'khor gsum gyi rjes gnang / 'jigs byed rwa 'khrid/ grub rgyal tshe 'khrid/ rgyud bzhi dang / zhwa lu'i gdan rabs gsar rtsom mdzad
pa'i lung bcas lags pas thub bstan spyi dang / sgos su kun mkhyen bu stobs zhabs kyi ring lugs spel ba'i thugs smon gyi mthu grub pa'i don bzhi gus ldan gyi re ba yongs
su rdzogs pa'i thugs bskyed dang brtse gzigs cis kyang bka' drin skyong dgos/ bdag gis kyang thob thob mang po'i rnam grangs gsog 'dod dang / gzhan gyis ma thob pa zhig
rang

gis thob zer ba'i grags pa sgrub 'dod dang / tshul 'di la brten nas zang zing gi bde ba bsgrub 'dod gtan nas ma lags kyis/ spyir bka' drin can gong ma de dag gi thugs dgongs
rdzogs pa dang sgos su bdag gi bla ma rje dhA dzI'i matsan can de nyid dgung lo brgyad cu'i ngo mthong kyang / kun mkhyen bu ston zhabs kyis dka' ba brgya phrag gis btsal
ba'i dbang rgyun lha'i bdud rtsi lta bu de dag khyed rang gis gcig thob na/ ngas kyang thob pa dang khyad par mi 'dug pas brtson pa bskyed e thub ces spyan chab sgo ra
yang yang gsung pa gyen bzlog ma nus par 'di bzhin zhus pa lags pas rjes brtse'i klod nas 'dor pa med pa zhu/ pha tshe rabs kyi bla ma khyed dang mjal/ /bdag sprang 'khyams
kyi bsam don 'grub bo snyam/ /da legs bshad gsung gi bdud rtsi yis/ /yid re ba rdzogs par mdzad du gsol/ /zhes pa'o/ /de ltar spyir kho bo la rgyud nas bshad pa'i rdo
rje slob dpon gyi mtshan nyid ni 'ga' yang yod pa ma yin mod/ bstan pa'i snying po gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa la thug kyang / rje btsun sa paN gyis/ 'on kyang so so thar
pa ni/ /nub kyang gzugs brnyan tsam zhig snang / /rdo rje theg pa'i bstan pa ni/ /gzugs brnyan tsam yang mi snang ngo / /zhes gsungs

pa'i dgongs pa yang / lam gyi rtsa ba dbang bskur ba'i gzugs brnyan tsam la yang ma brten par/ rang dgar dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga byed pa dang / byin rlabs kyi cho ga phra mo
tsam la brten nas rtsa rlung thig le'i lam sogs bsgom pa'i phyag len bod 'dir da lta yan chod du shin tu mang ba byung pa 'di la dgongs shing / rdo rje 'chang nas rtsa ba'i
bla ma'i bar du brgyud nas bskur pa'i dbang gi rgyun 'di dag nub na ni gsang sngags kyi bstan pa rnal ma mi dgos gzugs brnyan tsam du yang 'jog pa'i gzhi ma grub ste/
dper na bslab bsdom ma blangs pa'i khyim pa chos shes pa gzhi gcig tu mang du tshogs kyang dge 'dun gyi sder mi 'gro ba bzhin no/ /tshul de lta bu'i dgag bya 'gag pa'i thabs
tsam du dbang gi rgyun tho yig tu gsal ba'i nang nas kyai rdor dpal mchog rigs bsdus/ khams gsum rnal rgyal gsum po ma gtogs pa'i gzhan tshang ma bskur thub par byas
so/ /brag dgon sprul pa'i sku 'di nyid dang / mkhas pa la grub pas khyad par du byas pa zhig yod pas kho bo rang gis chos zhus pa la dpal dus kyi 'khor lo sdom pa chen po'i
dbang / bde mchog sdom 'byung / mai tri bcu gsum ma/ gshed dmar bcu gsum ma/

'jigs byed dpa' bo gcig pa bu lugs/ rnam snang mngon byang / 'chi med rnga sgra/ mi 'khrugs pa lha dgu/ gdugs dkar nyer bdun mo rnams kyi dbang bka' dang / gzhan yang rjes
gnang zur bka' dang lung mang ba zhig bcas thob bo/ /e ma ho/ ston chu 'dzin gsar gzhon 'khrig pa las/ /sgra dbyar gyi rnga gsang mtho na yang / /char nor 'dzin gsher ba'i
rgyun med na/ /sman rtsi bcud lo tog 'phel ba min/ /shing dri zhim padma'i ge sar la/ /yid dga' byed skye bo mang yod kyang / /khong rkang pa drug pa ma gtogs pa'i/ /bcud
sbrang rtsi len pa nus ma yin/ /brlan nyal 'gros bslad pa'i 'o ma'i rgyun/ /mi mkhas rmongs phal gyis bdud rtsier len/ /pho nyam chung rus pa'i gos can 'dis/ /rdzas de
nyid so sor phye la ltos/ /'di na mkhas blun bye brag mi 'byed cing / /chos dbang chos min dbye ba'ang mnyam pa nyid/ /nor dang grags pa su ches thub bstan skyong / /de
phyir 'gal 'di kun bzod par gsol/ /de nas rtsibs ri chu bzang nas gnas brtan spong pa la bskal bzang dar rgyas yang phebs te/ khong gi bsdebs su lhun po rtse'i slob dpon
zla ba dang / dbu mdzad sogs la sgrub thabs rin 'byung gi rjes gnang lung dang bcas pa tshar pa byas/ rang lo bzhi bcu mdzes byed

ces pa chu mo yos kyi lo zla ba gnyis pa tsam la sde dge sprul pa'i sku mtshams khongs su phebs pa la rdor dbyings dang don zhags kyi dbang bka' sogs dgongs bzhed kyi chos
bka' rnams phul/ slar hor zla lnga pa'i mjug tu dge slong sbyin pa sogs rang re'i grwa pa mang ba zhig la chos skyong yongs rdzogs kyi rjes gnang btang / dam rdzas bdud rtsi
ril bu'i sgrub pa zhig kyang byas/ ma he mchod pa ran gong du ri phug gi thugs rnams gsos/ legs bshad chos gling nas dge slong sri rdor bos te mgon po bed dang lha mo'i
'chams sku dang / rnam sras kyi chibs sengge sogs la nyams gso phul/ bug 'don gyi mtshan mo sngar bzhin skad gtong pa he ru ka'i chas sprad nas byung pa la bka' bsgo sogs
byas/ dngos gzhi'i skabs zhwa lu mthil du phyin nas lha mgon gnyis la 'chams gos gsar pa re dang snyan rgyan gsar bzos byas pa 'bul sbyor dang sbrags pa'i mang ja btang
/ 'chams gos bla brang chen por zhus pa'i rgyu cha phul ba sogs sdom dngul srang drug cu skor song / 'di skabs khal kha khu ral gyi rje btsun dam pa'i dgongs rdzogs sgrub
mkhan byung pa lo tsA ba tshul khrims kyis byas nas zhwa lur mang ja 'gyed bcas stsal/

tA bla ma blo bzang zla ba dang / gung tshe ring bkra shis sogs nged 'phrad par yang slebs byung / grangs che grwa tshang gi 'du khang der dbang ldan chos 'khaur ba'i dbu chos
la bsnyen rdzogs byas/ lcog spe'i sku dngos sogs mi mang ba zhig la tshe dbang dang / rin sdings grwa tshang pa rnams la chos 'brel gyi tshul du bu ston snying thur bsgrags/
nA lendra gzim 'og sprul pa'i sku sa skyar phebs pa'i lam zhor du 'di khar phebs nas mjal 'phrad tsam byung / rang lo zhe gcig pa khro mo zhes pa shing pho 'brug
gi lo/ 'chi med rnga sgra/ mi g.yo ba sngon po bus btsugs/ sgrol ljang rnams kyi bsnyen pa bskyal/ sog po rnam rgyal dang shes rab bcas su nA ro mkha' spyod kyi dbang 'khrid
btang / rin sdings bla ma bstan 'dzin chos bzang la rjes gnang kha shas byas/ skyabs mgon thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen pos rgyun ldan nged rang la bong ba>gser dgongs
kyi gzigs gsos dang / bka' drin tshad med pas bskyangs pa ltar/ gong gi zhabs brtan gtsor 'don dang / dge sbyor gang yong byas/ zhwa lu ri mthil gyi 'du khang chen po'i seng
g.yab la thig tshad blangs nas shambha ma'i sprul pa'i rgyal po bdun/ rigs ldan nyer lnga/ rgyan drug

mchog gnyis/ rgyal sras zhi ba lha/ jo 'brom yab sras gsum/ bu sto nayab sras gsum/ rje yab sras gsum/ gzhan yang dus 'khor/ bde mchog /gshed dmar sogs 'dod lha du ma dang
bcas pa'i thang bskor bzhengs rgyu phun khang chos mdzad sku zhabs su gnyer gtam zhus pa lo 'di'i hor zla bdun pa'i nyi shu brgyad la las grwa tshugs pa mdzad nas bla brang
nas gos chen zhus pa'i rin sogs rgyu 'gro chang ma phab pas dngul srang nyis brgya dang bzhi bcu zhe dgu zho drug skar lnga bcas song / grang gsar dang dkar ras sgong
shun ma phran tshags 'di kha nas 'don rgyu yod pa dang / phun khang nas chwa shi'i sogs dgos cha snang chung rigs tshang ma rtsis 'gro ma gnang bar 'phar song 'dug ston ser
du song ba dang skyin mkhar tsha chur phyin nas sngar lam ltar sde pa lcog spel bas bsnyen bkur dang / dbang ldan chos 'khor bas 'bod mkhan slebs te grwa tshang du gdugs
kar nyer bdun ma'i dbang dang rab byung bsnyen rdzogs zhu mkhanya dril bas grwa tshang rang nas nyi shu rtsa bzhi byung / 'di skabs sngar mkhas mchog bstan pa'i sgron
mes bzhengs pa'i gtsug lag khang 'og ma der sdad nas chos 'chad pa byas/ sman bla sgrub mchod la ja thug 'ga'

dang bcas pa'i 'gyed zho re btang / 'du khang rtser phyin nas lha mo la gtor ma phul zhing 'phrin 'chol zhus/ slar rang gnas su 'ongs te mtshams bcad nas da lta phan chad du
mi tshe de za ri zi ri gcig la bskyal ba la ni snying po yod yod mi 'dra/ mig btsums nas 'gro dus gdeng thob pa zhig bya snyam pa lan re tsam 'ong gin 'dug ste tshwa bro
rgyu zhig cang mi gda'o/ e ma ho/ sngar 'gyur rdzogs pa chen po'i sngags 'char ltar/ /kun bzang dgongs pa mngon 'gyur bdag la med/ /lhan skyes phyag rgya chen po'i sgom
chen ltar/ /rnam rtog chos sku'i yo lang bdag la med/ /don dam gzhan stong dbu ma'i slob dpon ltar/ /bde snying brtag brtan ther gzugs bdag la med/ /dbu ma thal 'gyur mkhyen
pa'i dge bshes ltar/ /zhen lta'i rtsod rengs brdung rgyu bdag la med/ /shes bya'i gshil 'khor 'das dbyer med go /shes byed log pas 'khor 'das so sor gyes/ /'khor ba
shul du spangs kyi mi lang pas/ /de ru 'khrul ba spangs phyir thos bsam byas/ /rgyal bas chos rnams nyon mongs 'dul phyir gsungs/ /dben pa bsten nas sems la lta dwog bcug
/de yi rgyab skyor bla ma yi dam la/ /sgo gsum 'jug pa'i dril nas gsol ba btab/ /lam gyi 'bras su thob na re dwogs zad/ /dge rtsa rang la bsngo ba 'brel

med phyir/ /'gro la bsngos nas smon lam 'debs pa 'di/ /chos med blo gsal kho bo'i nyams len lags/ /rang lo zhe gnyis pa sna tshogs zhes pa shing mo sbrul gyi lo bde mchog dril
bu lus dkyil gyi bsnyen pa byas/ hor zla bzhi pa'i tshes bco lnga la sngar gyi thang bskor rnams ri phug gi 'du khang lhor bkrams shing dge 'dun rnams la mang ja 'byed
zhwo re dang bcas pa btang / de nyin dus 'khor byang chen pa'i dbu mdzad gsang sngags chos grags sogs la bsnyen rdzogs kyang byas/ dbyar zla 'bring po'i nang du ngor tar
pa rtser mkhan chen rin po che las lam dbang dang rjes gnang lung dang bcas pa 'ga' zhus/ mkhan chen nyid dang zhabs drung dbon sogs la rdo rje mi 'khrug pa lha bcu gsum
gyi dbang phul/ ldan ma khams tshan du dpon slob rin po ngag dbang legs grub pa'i drung du/ 'jam dbyangs ar pa ce lha lnga'i dbang / rigs byed ma lha lnga'i dbang / klu
sgrub lugs kyi bcu gcig zhal gyi dbang sogs zhus/ lam zhor du dkyil byang dang phu man khang spel du phyin nas tshe bka' byabs khrus sogs byas/ rang gnas su slebs nas mtshams
byas pa'i skabs shig rmi lam du zhwa lu'i 'du khang nang der ngo mi shes pa'i grwa

pa mang po tshogs 'dug /nged rang lus shin tu gcong pa zhig byas nas de na yar phyin pas khyams smad tsam na bud med hrul le ba mang po 'dug pa rnams kyis byan rlabs zhus/
mkhan po'i khri'i rtsa de na khri gsar pa zhig 'dug pa la bsdad nas/ sems can thams cad bde dang ldan gyur cig /ces nged kyis tshigs bcad de bskul bas 'ur ding song / mtshams
der dge skos yin rgyu ba des yi ge zhig sprad nas dpyad khra ba 'di la lung zhig zhu dgos zer ba dpyad khra la lung zhus nas ci byed snyam pa'i blo kyog ge ba zhig la
gnyidgnyis sad do/ /dgon pa 'di la kho bo rang gi ci 'byor pas zhabs tog phran bu byas pa rnams brgyud nas sems can la phan pa'i thabs su smon lam btab na bzang ba dang
/ chos kyi phan thogs ci yang mi yong ba la blta ba 'dra/ pha pha/ da ni sems yang skyo mo zhig 'dug go /dus ni lo re bzhin du ngan du 'gro/ ltad mo sna tshogs mthong gin
'dug /bod kyi bla ma dang chos dpon tshe smon gling lta bu blo gzu bos brtags na 'gran zla bral ba zhig yin 'dug kyang / de 'dra zhig

byung song / bka' blon bshad sgra dbang phyug rgyal po 'di smon lam gyi 'khrul las gzhung sa dga' ldan pho brang ba'i don la lus srog 'dor ma nus pa'i skyes bu ngo mtshar can
zhig yin 'dug kyang lam du mi 'gro ba dang / rjes su sku srog la nyen che ba tsam gyi skyon byung song / de bzhin du bkra shis lhun por nor bu grwa khang gi lde chung
brgya bo zer ba bla brang rgyal mtshan mthon po la med thabs med pa zhig yin 'dug kyang / kho rang gi las sam gang yin kyang de 'dra zhig byung song / /pha pha/ lo 'di'i
mjug la de gong lha sar rgya mi chi krong thang zer bas tshe smon gling la 'o rgyal bzos pa'i sku chas bod khongs chos sde rnams kyi nyams gso'i thebs sugong ma chen pos
gnang bas 'di kha zhwa lu'i gtsug lag khang sogs la yang zhabs pad spel gzhi nas mtshams sbyor mgo 'dren brkyangs te dngul rgya dngul srang chig stong bdun brgya thob pa
byung 'dug /de skor la 'di kha nas khang snying bla ma ye shes bzang po dang spyi gnyer rin chen mkhas grub gnyis lha sar byon pas don go yang chod po byung ste/ dngul rnams
sngon cig gzhung gnas rang du phul nas bka' 'dzin zhus/ slar 'di kha nas nged kyis bka' blon spel bzhi rang nas ar po'i do dam gnang

grogs zhus pas/ sku mched rje drung lags dang sku zhang khri chen sku tshab la gtong gnang mdzad/ nyams gso'i thebs ma yin pa'i grwa pa la 'gyed sogs dngos gnas stsal ba don
mi gnyis po 'byor 'phral rang la mang 'gyed byung song / rang lo zhe gsum pa zil gnon zhes pa me pho rta'i lo gtsug lag khang gi nyams gso'i rim gror phyag rdor 'byung
tshul gyi sbyin sreg sogs byas kyai rdor gyi bsnyen tshan e 'grub snyam yang aTTa khri bdun tsam song ba dang rkyen 'ga' zhig gi bar chad du song / dus 'khor gyi gtso bo
yab yum gyi bsnyen pa byas/ hor zla bzhi pa'i tshes bco lnga la rang re'i sku skye blo bzang mkhyen rab dang / blo chen bsod nams chos 'phel sogs bsnyen rdzogs bsgrubs/ zhwa
lu matil du nyams gso'i mchod yon gyi cho ga 'bul bar yang 'khor tsam phyin/ lo 'di dang phyi lo bcas su zhwa lu spyi so nas dgun grang sgang la las gra gshol zhing de
min ar po kho na byas pas rgyan gong la spen bad bcas gsar bzhengs lta bu dang / zhwa lu mthil gyi gzhal yas khang lho ma'i g.yu thog gi shing cha tshang ma dang rdza hrul
ba rnams gsar spos/ 'di khang steng gi g.yab ring / seng g.yab kyi ka ring / 'di khang gi

sgo / gnas khang gi rgyal sgo shar ma bcas pa gsar spos dang / ri phug gi 'du khang lha byang ka spungs khri chen pho brang rnams la nyams gso gnang smin byung / mdor na gzhung
nas thon pa'i dgos po sha khu sha thim khar nyang stod khal kha dus 'khor grwa tshang 'dus spyi nas g.yam leb gang dgos dang / sgo bang ma nyung tsam bskyel 'dren tshang
ma byas pa la rin sogs ji song zhal 'debs su phul ba dang / rin sdings grwa tshang nas dngul srang sum cu tham pa dang gos yug gcig phul ba sogs dang 'bul phran tshags
dang bcas pa yid chos kyi gnas su song pa las bar mdor chud bzos med pa dang chod cheb byung ste rgyal tshab tshe smon gling de yang thugs bskyed bzang po yin pa'i rtags
su go /ar po 'di tsam byas pa la do dam byed po'ang las mi sogs 'brum nad ma thar ba kho na yin zhing 'di skabs nad bag je 'phag du 'gro yang las thag ma gshol bar la
bag nad sogs kyi skyon ci yang ma byung ba yin no/ /'jigs 'ji rdam rdam rgya nag phyogs nas yongs/ /tshir tshir dam dam se ra'i dgon par byung / /bred bred zhumazhum bod
kyi rje 'bangs dang / /zab zab dril dril bstan 'gro'i bde skyid do/ /mtho mtho dma'

dma' deng gi 'byor rgud 'di/ /smyo smyo gog gog 'bras bur yid ches kyang / /hral hral hrul hrul zhwa lu'i gnas dgon la/ /zab zab sig sig ar po 'grub nas song / /reng reng rong
rong can tshor kha skyengs dang / /sgangasgung sging sging kha cig ma mgu rung / /legs legs 'grig 'grig tsam 'di spel gzhi ba'i/ /dad dad mos mos 'phrul gyis byung ngo
lo/ /kho bo rang nas kyang sngon mo nyin gang gcig dang bzo rigs pa sogs la rngan pa lta bu'i gsol ras kha btags dngul sngags mdud dam rdzas sogs kyi ster bya gang dgos
rang don zhe bzhag byas nas byin te rtsis 'gro sogs gang yang med do/ /rang lo zhe bzhi pa spre'u zhes pa me mo lug gi lo shar pa dang / 'chim med dpal ster gyi tshe bsnyen
sogs btang / hor zla bzhi pa'i dus mchod kyi skabs spyi pa sogs las tshan bsko bzhag byas dus lo snga ma chos khrims pa dge slong rin chen blo gros kyis/ /zhwa lu mthil
du dbyar gnas la gtang gzhi 'phar ma btang bar 'ga' res phrag dog dang ko lang byas te/ kho par mdzo ba yar 'gel gyis spyi pa'i 'os bsdu dang / nged kyis kho bar dkon
gnyer bskos par ma dga' ba'i yi ge sbyor ba sogs za zir 'ga' yang byed kyin gda'o/ /lar tshe bcu pa la hab rgyugs byed pa

'di kun ya nga ba kho nar zad do/ /lo 'di'i mjug la ri phug dpon slob rin chen dpal ldan yang rkang 'bam gyi bsnyung ba la 'di nas bcos thabs gang drag byas nas na tsha drag
tu song rung / chen po dang gnyis po za gyod phran bu zhig la ma 'cham par gcig gis gcig la ngan smras kyi yi ge gtong res byas pas rlung 'tshang nas glo bur du gshegs/
de'i lo rting ma'i dus tshod de la chen po kho rang yang 'das te chen slob 'di gnyis ka mjug tu mtha' zhan pa zhig byung song / nam yang 'chi ba yong snyam pa med pa'i grabs
gshom dang / tshig gi mtho dma' re tsam dang za rgyu phran bu re'i don la nyal gnyid zas bcud mi myong ba'i dran rgyu rgod po 'di tsho'i snying la 'dre ci 'dra zhig
rang 'changang gin yod dam snyam rang nyid skyo shas che la blo sna thung du song / rang lo zhe lnga ba phur bu zhes pa sa pho spre'u'i lo shar ba dang gsang ba 'dus pa ye
shes zhabs lugs lha bcu dgu'i grangs bsnyen btang / chos mdzad byang chub smon lam dbus nas ched gtad 'ong pa la shangs chos ne gu'i chos skor ha lam pa zhig bshad/ zhwa
lu dang rgyan gong du phyin nas rdo rje dbyings kyi rab gnas kyi cho ga nyin gang re byas/ ston mjug tshwa chu'i 'phrod brten la skyin mkhar du phyin nas

lcog spel ba'i gzhis su tshe bka' sogs byed pa la zhag shas bsdad/ sngar dbang ldan chos 'khor gyi 'du khang rtser spen bad gsar sgron gyi thebs su nged rang gi dngul sRang
bco lnga sprad pa dang gzhan dad 'bul phran tshags byung ba sogs la brten grwa pa rnams kyi spen bad sgron tshar ba dang / rtse mo sgrub mchod la 'bod pa 'dug pas/ der phyin
nas grwa dbyings la rtse mo'i dbang bcu po tshang ba byas/ tshogs su mang ja 'gyed Tam ka re dang bcas pa btang / spen bad kyi ngos su mi'i maNDal gnyis sbyar nas rab
gnas shig byas/ phyis su nyams pa ma gtogs sngar spen bad kyang byung 'dug pa dang gtsug lag khang 'di la mkhyen rab chos rjes bzhengs nas 'khrul zhig rin po ches rab gnas
mdzad/ yo ga'i grwa ba phal mo che nas grwa pa bsdus te 'dir rdo rje rtse mo'i sgrub mchod shin tu rgyas pa mdzad de bod gangs can gyi ljongs su yo ga'i sgrub mchod de
las rgyas pa sngar lo chen rin chen bzang po'i dus su'ang ma byung na gzhan lta ci smos zhes grags so/ /deng sang zhwa lu na rgyun yod pa'i yog dbyangs phal che ba yang
de dus dar 'dug /de yang yog dbyangs 'di rnams kyang tho gling sogs zhang zhung nang pa nas brgyud de sri'u chu ba lce blo ldan seng ge'i slob brgyud la ma nyams pa yod
pa thugs sras lo tsA bas slob par mdzad nas mkhyen rab

rin po che yan chod la dge 'phel chos rdzong gi rdo rje dbyings kyi sgrub mchod la mdzad srol byung zhing / de rjes dbang ldan chos 'khor du byung / de nas yang shin tu nyag
phra bar song pas sde pa gtsang pa karmma phun tshogs rnam rgyal gyis zhwa lu nas btsun pa bos pa la phogs rgyab nas gzhis ka rtse'i rdzong du sbyor thar byed du bcug 'dug
/sngon gyi rgyal po de tsho khyim pa yin rung chos nyams che la bstan pa la lhag bsam dkar ba 'di lta bu deng sang gi chos pa'i nang tshan dge bshes yin rgyu ba tsho'i
rmi lam du lo la sgugs kyang mi 'char ba nges so/ /gzhis ka rtser yog dbyangs kyi slob dpon bla ma kun dga' dpal 'phel zhes bya ba dang / slob sbyong mkhan gyi gtso bo
mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub yin gda'/ dbyangs rkang grangs nyis brgya lhag tsam bslab ces gsungs so/ /kho bos dbang ldan chos 'khor du rtse mo sgrub mchod la
phyin nas dbang bskur skabs 'dir/ dbang gzhi dkyil gyi dus slob dpon dam chos lags kyis bkras dbyangs bram ze'i tshangs dbyangs ring mo tshar gcig 'then par mdzad/ gzhan
dbyangs 'then mkhan gcig kyang ma byung ngo / /grwa'i dbang tshugs nas kho bo rang yang skad 'dzer zhing gu dog tsam byung rung / /dbang tshang ma

bskur thub pa bgyis so/ /'phags yul mkhas dbang kun dga' snying po dang / /gangs can bstan pa'i mnga' bdag bu ston rje'i/ /phyag bzhes dri bral rnal 'byor rgyud skor la/ /mos
pas bag chags 'jog tshul tsam zhig byas/ /'di na la la tshig 'phreng lbu bas khengs/ /gzhan dag mgrin bzang rgan po'i rang sgra ngoms/ /phal cher za chog tsam zhig lhur
len med/ /dbang gis chu rgyun sgrengs la yi rangs byos/ /de nas dus gtor gyi ltad mo tshar 'phral bteg nas skyal chad spel sogs 'bod mkhan mang ba 'dug kyang ma phyin par
ron skam du tshe bka' sbyin sreg sogs byas te ri phug tu yong / sde dge sprul pa'i sku khams nas phebs pa dang ngos 'phrad du byon/ dgongs bzhed kyi bde mchog sdom po
'byung ba lha bcu gsum sogs dbang chos kha shas phul/ thar rtse mkhan rin po che 'jam dpal bzang po sde dge nas yar phebs pa'i nged rang la rta sogs bdog pa'i skyes bzang
po stsal 'dug pas nye gnas mjal dar 'bul ba la ngor du btang / sde pa gzhung gi bde rim du dgra sri phung sri sogs gnon dgos pa'i bka' rgyang pa chas dngos 'byor pas padma
dbang chen yang gsang khros pa'i sgo nas sri rnams sa gnas dmigs can du phyin te mnan chog byas/ skyabs mgon chen po'i bka'

'brel 'ga' zhig gi don du phyag mdzod nyi ma don grub la yang tshar kha shas phebs byung ba mtshams 'og tu mjal/ nged rang la gyon pa sogs mthun rkyen mang po gnang zhing rgyun
du thugs zos che ba mdzad pa zhig yod/ rang lo zhe drug pa zhi ba zhes pa sa mo bya'i lo shar pa dang sngar gyi rgyun las mtshams la yod dus de gong bla brang gi dgung
gsar nyin kha ba bab pa sogs brtags dpyad 'tshub tsam dang /hor zla dang po'i mjug tsam la skyabs mgon chen po'ang sku khams cung zad ma dwangs pa byung pas zhabs brtan
gyi rnam pa dngos po phran bu dang bcas pa'i maNDal rten gsum dang sku tshe tshe rdzas 'bul bar phyin/ rje btsun sgrol ma'i snang brnyan li ma khyad mtshar gcig dang /
gyon chas sogs gsol ras gya nom pa stsal/ phun khang chos mdzad sku zhabs su rkyen sel tshe dbang sogs phul te ri phug tu slebs 'phral rin lding grwa tshang gi dbu mdzad
bsnyen rdzogs bsgrubs/ sde dge sprul pa'i sku dbus phyogs su bka' 'gyur gyi lung gsan par phebs zhor 'di khar mjal 'phrad mdzad/ par bde mchog dril bu lus dkyil gyi dbang
bka'/ dril bu rim lnga'i 'khrid rkyen sel gyi tshe bka' sogs phul/ tshur yang man

ngag brgya rtsa'i lung sogs gsung chos kha shas zhus/ sprul pa'i sku 'di'i mkhyen rab dang thugs brtson gang la brtags kyang 'gran zla bral ba zhig 'dug pas nged rang gi chos
ma thob pa rnams kyang 'dis gsan na chog pa'i re 'dun yod pa bzhin snyan bskul gyis zhu ba phul/ de nas rang re'i grwa rgyun bstan 'dzin spo legs lha ldan du bka' blon
lha rnga ba'i em mchod la 'gro rgyu dang / dkar po grwa tshang gi dbu mdzad sogs bsgrub bya gsum la bsnyen rdzogs byas/ hor zla bzhi pa'i nang du ri phug gi dus 'khor lha
khang gi lcags dra gsar 'dzugs byas te lcags dra rang la dngul srang drug cu re dgu dang zho bdun song zhing / 'di skabs kyi bzo ba'i gla lto 'phar du song / de nas kho
bo rang gis sngar rgya dngul spang drug cu re gsum sku rgyur byas nas bzhengs pa'i bu ston tshe 'dzin mtha' yas dang / yang rgya dngul srang bdun cu sku rgyur byas pa'i
sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i dngul sku lcags dra'i nang du bzhugs su gsol/ de nyin dge 'dun rnams la yang mang ja 'gyed Tam ka re dang bcas pa phul dge rtse 'brel thogs
kyis mtshon pa'i sems can thams cad la bsngos nas smon lam btab/ gzhan gyis byin pa'i dad rdzas chud zos su ma song ba 'di a bo bo bo'i 'dun ma drag shos yin/

tshong dang bun kha mi dgos sbyin bdag btsal nas 'bul sdud byed pa dang / grong chog rgyu pa sogs sngar ma byas shing da byed par mi 'gyur pa ni gzigs pas gsal ba lags/ zhwa
lu sogs dgon pa'i dkor ni phran tshogs byung rung phar dkor lan ma bcal ba med pas 'dir kho bos dge phyogs su btang ba 'di dag shin tu snang chung rung / gzhan gyi chu
thigs re tsam dad pas phul ba'i sgyu ma'i longs spyod la snying po grub pa'i phyir byas kyi/ brnyad dge ba la btags nas kha bsag dang / zhogs slong dang / thob mjal sna tshogs
kyis sdig pa'i nor blangs pa las byung pa ni ma yin no/ /'dus byas kyi dge ba stong las 'dus ma byas kyi dge ba gcig dga' ba'i go ba ra ri tsam dang de kho na nyid
kyi yul la mos pa brtan po yod pas kho bo zang zing gi longs spyod bsgrubs nas dge rtsar ba kho na yang ma lags so/ /yi ger bris pa 'di rlom sems kyi ma yin gyi/ zhen pas
'jug pa'i skye bo 'ga' zhig yid dga' ba dang / rjes su slob par 'dod pa rnams kyis tshul go pa'i ched du yin no/ /zla ba bzhi pa'i nang du chab mdo byams pa gling gi phyag
mdzod chen mo skal bzang chos ldan dang / rtse gnyer blo gros chos 'phel sogs 'phags pa

lha blo bzang 'jigs med dpal ldan bstan pa'i nyi ma sku gshegs pa'i dgongs rdzogs sgrub par bkra shis lhun por phebs pa'i mar lam 'di khar ngos 'phrad la yang 'khor tsam phebs
byung / dbyar mtshams grol nas phu shar du ri Shi'i chu bdugs zhag shas bsten cing / de rjes bu lung bla ma rin po che phebs par dgongs bzhed kyi bde mchog dril bu lha
lnga'i dbang / 'chi med bdud rtsi bum pa'i snod rung gi dbang / spyan ras gzigs 'khor ba dong phrug gi rigs gtad sogs phul/ nged rang gis kyang khong la jo nang lugs kyi
dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i mchog dbang gong ma zhus nas sbyor ba yan lag drug gi 'khrid dang / de'i rgyab chos su rje btsun sgrol mgon chen pos mdad pa'i dus 'khor gyi yig
sna tshang ma'i lung zhus shing thob/ de nas rin chen smon lam bsam gtan dang / rig 'dzin rgyal po gnyis la bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa 'bog pa'i las grwa zhig byas/ slar
mtshams byas nas kha 'don ci shes rnams gang yod bgyis so/ / | da len dam pa'i chos la ma 'bungs na/ /dal 'byor 'di ni rgya ma lan cig yin/ /da len 'chi ba snying nas ma
dran na/ /rtag 'dzin 'di ni bdud kyi zhags pa yin/ /da

len yid ches dad pa ma skyes na/ /las 'bras 'di ni mi bslu nges pa yin/ /da len dge sdig blangs dor ma mkhas na/ /ngan 'gro'i gtam yang 'jigs su rung ba yin/ /da len 'khor
ba'i mtsho las ma grol na/ /de nas thar pa'i dus ni nam zhig yin/ /da len nges 'byung gting nas ma skyes na/ /ci byas tshe 'di'i grabs gshom 'ba' zhig yin/ /da len bslab
gsum rgyud la ma 'byor na/ /btsun pa'i gzugs brnyan 'di ni ku ra yin/ /da len sems kyi rgyal sa ma zin na/ /bsam gshis 'di ni 'dre ngan bsregs shor yin/ /da len nyon mongs
dgra bo ma thul na/ /rang gi rang nyid gtan rlag gtong ba yin/ /da len tshe 'di blo yis ma thong na/ /'khor ba 'di ru gtan 'khyamasabyed pa yin/ /da len byams dang snying
rje ma 'byongs na/ /byang chub sems kyi re ba zad pa yin/ /da len bdag 'dzin 'khri ba ma chod na/ /zab mo nges don go ba med pa yin/ /kwa ye da dung sems la gros tob la/
/blo sna tsab tsob ma mang bya bral ba/ /g.yeng ba spangs na gar bsdad dben dgon yin/ /gnas spos ri rdzong mang pos dgos pa med/ /sems kyi long na byas tshad dge ba yin/
/kha g.yeng mig g.yeng chos spyod dgos pa med/ /'chi

pa bsan na nor rdzas gang du khyer/ /ser sna'i sdug gsog rem la dgos pa med/ /mos gus yod na byin rlabs 'bad med 'jug /phyag mdud byin rten hral hrul dgos pa med/ /rang rgyud
dag na 'dre yang chos skyong yin/ /lha gsol klu gsol bskang gso dgos pa med/ /bskyed rdzogs bsgoms na mthu nus shuT las 'byung / /rnga brdung rol mo'i dkrol bya dgos pa
med/ /sems la phan na gang yang man ngag yin/ /yig nag dpe cha'i dkon dregs dgos pa med/ /rgyal bas chos rnams nyon mongs gnyer por bstan/ /kha bshad grub mtha'i phyogs
'dzin dgos pa med/ /rang la rang gis bskul phyir bris pa 'di/ /gzhan la phog pa srid na bzod par gsol/ /de nas zla ba bcu tsam nas skyabs mgon chen po sku khams nyog tshul
byung pas/ rtse shod gnyis car nas nged rang dang / zhwa lu 'dus spyi yang sgrol dkar dang 'chi med rnga sgra'i sgrub mchod 'phar ma gtong rgyu'i dgos cha sogs byung ste/
spyir lo snga gting 'di dag la zhwa lu tshogs chen la bla brang nas mang ja rkang tshugs pa dang / rtse phyag mdzod nas tshe dpag med la na bza' khyed 'phags gcig kyang
'bul ba gnang / zla ba bcu gcig pa'i chos nyi shu lnga la kun skyob gling du phyin nas/ gong gi zhabs brtan gsol 'debs

kyi rten du/ ngos rang nas maNDal sku gsung thugs rten/ dngul gyi tshe bum/ gser zho bzhi/ dngul srang lnga bcu/ mdzod btags bcas dang / zhwa lu chos sde spyi so nas maNDal
sku gsung thugs rten/ tshe dpag med kyi snang brnyan li ma/ dngul srang nyi shu mdzod btags bcas phul/ phun khang du rje seng chen sprul pa'i sku dang thog mar mjal zhing
nged rang nas gsol ja bzhes 'bras dang maNDal rten gsum tshang pa/ dngul srang bco lnga/ gser zho gang / kha btags bcas phul zhing / phun khang chos mdzad sku zhabs lhan
rgyas mdzad nas tshe bka' byabs khrus shig kyang song / rnam sras mchod pa char pa dang gzhung sa chen po nas khong rang la bka' rgya mdzad de khyi lo 'di nas bzung bstan
srid bde rim du mdas dang gtor ma sogs chags med bsgrub dgos zhes dngul srang bcu dang 'bru ru'i khal bdun cu rtsa lnga'i bka' 'dzin bcas gtong ba gnang byung ba yang
gal chung du ma song ba bsgrubs khul zhus/ 'di skabs 'bras ma gshong du dmag gi sgra che tsam yod pa'ang 'jam chags su gyur pas yid bde ba byung / skyabs mgon rin po che'i
spyan bsal gzhon gras zhig bkra shis lhun po'i btsun pa byas nas

'dir ri khrod la 'ongs pa nyi ma la dbang 'khrid kha shas btang zhing chos mgo thon thabs byas yod/ 'di yang de sngon dge sbyor ji ltar byed kyi yod kyang sdod tshugs bar lta
rgyu yod rung / da ni 'di yang bya byed mang ba tsam gyi mi tshe khyol rgyu zhig ka yin pa 'dra/ lar deng sang gi chos pa thams cad dang por chos mthun dkon/ bar du blo
sna phran bu chos la phyogs pa dang / cung zad go go thos thos 'dra byung tshe/ rjes su nga mkhas nga grub kyi 'jig rten chos brgyad kho nar 'gro ba gda' 'o/ /rang lo zhe
bdun pa thun mong zhes pa lcags pho khyi'i lo sngar gyi rgyun las dge sbyor 'phel zhing skyid mgo zin pa byung ste/ tshe 'di phun tshogs thams cad la cang mi bro ba'i
phar su la bltas kyang 'gram chu mi ldang ba dang tshe thung 'di la lam sna zin tsam zhig ma byung na mi'i skye ba blang ma blang la khyad par ci yang mi 'dug sngar stong
'chal chen po de tsam zhig la song / da byed ri shi snyam pa las gzhan gyis byin pa'i dngos po la 'di mkho ba 'dug dga' ba la bsam pa lta bu dang / grogs mdza' dang mi mdza'
ba la khyad par yod yod 'dra ba'i rnam rtog gi lbu ba mang po yal 'gro ba gda'/ lo 'di'i zla ba dang po'i tshes bcu bzhi'i nyin rgya nag rgyal po rda'o kwong sku gshegs
pa'i bod du zla ba gsum pa'i nang du wang shu

'byor te rgya nag lugs kyi mya ngan byed dgos kyin 'dug zer/ nga'i sems la 'chi ba zer ba 'di las dbang che ba sa phyogs gang na'ang med par thag gcod 'dug ste/ 'di ni sus
kyang mi go ba grabs gshom mang po dang / don med pa'i las la 'jug pa 'di tsho rang ya nga ba yin nam snyam pa las ni gzhan ma byung / sog pa'i rgyal po se chen khang dang
/ mkhan chen na min han gyi bla brang bde ldan gling gis sog 'grul bkra shis lhun por 'byor ba 'dra la yi ge re tsam nged rang la bskur 'dug pas chos dang mthun pa'i yig
len brdzangs/ zla ba bzhi pa la ri phug gi 'du khang lho'i seng g.yab la ling dmar ljang gi tsha khebs dang / 'du khang byang du kha btags ser po la par du btab pa'i sku
mang po brgyan bkod kyi tshul du sbyar/ gzhi gsum gyi lag len sogs bstan pa'i rtsa ba tshul khrims kyi bslab pa rin po che yongs sbyong gi ched du dmigs nas seng ldeng
gi gaNDi tshad dang ldan pa zhig kyang gtsug lag khang gi rtsis sprod du phul ba yin/ shing tshal dkar po ba'i a mi sra thar yang 'di skabs nas sa skya'i tshogs su chos dung
dkar po rgyang grags gdong rgyu'i mang ja dang / 'di khar yang sman zla nyin thub kyi mang ja 'gyed

dang bcas pa byung ste sa skyar 'di nas khri zur rin po cher zhu yig phul ba yin rung / ma bzhugs pa dang thug ste phun tshogs pho brang nas bdag rkyen rogs lam yang dag mdzad
de nged la yang 'byor len gyi gsung shog gnang ba byung ngo / /bud med 'di 'chi ba ngo shes shing / blo thag chod po byas 'dug pa 'di tsam deng sang gi btsun ma rnams
la mi yong zhing / dngos po la chags pa yin nam zer shi nas che ge mo 'dre ru skyes 'dug bya ba dang / ga ge mo la shi btsan gcig gnod kyin yod 'dug /de che ge mo yin nam
gang du 'ong ba 'di tsho'i byed lugs dang mi 'dra ba'i rang re yid mgu ba byung / nga ni 'dus byas kyi dge rtsa byed nam shi bar byed pa yin/ shi nas lhag lus sus za yang
nged la ni khyad par med do/ /kha gsag zhogs slong rnyed pas rnyed pa 'tshol/ /thob mjal tshul chos g.yo sgyu ma byas shing / /dad pas byin pa'i dngos po gang dang gang
/ /lhag ma med par mchod sbyin zhing du bsngos/ /nye 'brel sbyin bdag phyogs dkar sems 'dzin du/ /til tsam mi brul bcol chung khrel med kyi/ /bla gzugs rkub btsums sbar

gi rje btsun bla ma ye shes kyi DA ki ma sku khams cung zad mi dwangs par brtan bzhugs dang 'brel ba'i gsol 'debs kyi zhu 'phro na rten bcas phul/ rtsibs ri chu bzang
nas dge slong skal bzang dar rgyas dbus gnas la phebs pa yang 'di skabs 'khor byung ste mjal 'phrad byas/ de gong char dkon tsam byung bas rgyab ri mkha' spyod kyi ri rtse
nas khrus gsol zhig byas par do nub de rang la char babs/ dam rdzas bdud rtsi ril bu'i bsgrubs pa byas te ril bu zos pa'i sems can rgyud grol phyir smon lam sogs kyang
yid ches par btab/ zla ba bdun pa'i mjug la sprul pa'i sku 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse yang dbus gnas 'khor te 'di khar yar lam phebs/ gang ci'i gsung gleng zhib rgyas mdzad

lhun grub kyi rnam thar gyi lung phul/

de rjes dben dgon pa dge slong blo bzang ye shes sogs la gtsug tor dri med kyi rigs btad dang chog 'khrigs kyi lung btang / dbyar gnas grol nas skyin khar tshwa chu la phyin
pas la rgan gyi ri gsham na rang re'i tsha bo smin drug dge rgan dang bcas pas ja thab dang lal la bzhon g.yag rna ba gnyis kyi ca bkod byung / ron skam du zhag gcig bsdad
nas sang nyin snga bar phyin pas rab brtan gros spe'i ltag der lcog spe'i sras po sku 'bring dpon g.yogs gnyis byas nas bsu bar phebs pa mjal/ yar lam lhun grub tu ja

gyi lhung bzed sogs nang rten rnams kyang mjal/ grwa tshang la mang ja gcig btang / tshur mang ja 'dren sogs byung / grwa pa mang rabs la tshe bka' sogs byas/ ri phug
tu slebs nas sprul pa'i sku 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse phebs te/ de nyin zla ba dgu pa'i mar ngo'i tshes bcu dang thug pas rdo rje rnal 'byor nA

ro mkha' spyod kyi sinnghu ra'i dkyil 'khor du byin rlabs phul/ zla ba dkar ba dang thar rtse zhabs drung rin po che kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dang / khra le chos rje
dge legs rgya mtsho sogs kyang phebs pas byang gling bla brang gi dbang khang du dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i sku gsung thugs yongs su rdzogs pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor

ma'i bka' sogs kyang mchad par byas so/ /nged rang nas kyang sprul pa'i sku'i drung du rngog pa'i rdo rje gdan bzhi/ yab bka' yum bka' ye shes dbang phyug ma'i dbang
lung / sgrol ma bla med kyi dbang rgyun man ngag dang bcas pa/ 'jam dpal chos dbyings gsung dbang gi dbang bka' gong dkar nas brgyud pa sogs chos mang ba zhus so/ /'di skabs
