zhing mtha' rten sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i rjes gnang byas te chos grol nas dgun mtshams dam par byas pa yin no/ /e ma hoH shar la rgan la mo brganal nas phyin/ /yul
skyin mkhar 'phrang la lam gtad byas/ /sman tshwa chu'i 'phrod brten zhag 'ga' bsten/ /khong nyam ma pho mo'i zhal bzang mjal/ /dpal thar pa gling gi dgon pa ru/ /rje
dpyal ston chos kyi bzang po sogs/ /sngon sgra bsgyur lo tsA mdzad rnams kyi/ /rten ngo mtshar can kun la byin rlabs zhus/ /gnas de yi lo rgyus dris tsa na/ /khong sku gnyer
de smra bcad dam po 'dug /ban de kun g.ya' spangs mtshams de na/ /tshe gang 'phyid kyi lcam pa ha lo 'dra/ /sems skyo ba skyes nas rang gnas slebs/ rje 'jam dbyangs mkhyen
brtse'i bkas bskul nas/ /dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i smin grol sogs/ /chos zab mo phar brdal tshur brdal byas/ /

sprang 'khos med kyi btsun pa blo gsal bdag /pho rgod po dang drung po mi 'dug ste/ /mgon bu ston rje'i brgyud pa pher tsam byung / /de ya chen che ba ma lags sam/ /rang lo
zhe brgyad du slebs pa dga' byed ces pa lcags mo phag gi lo shar nas zla ba gnyis pa'i mgo la bkra shis lhun por phyin/ skyabs mgon rin po cher lo 'khor gyi tshe rdzas
dang zhabs brtan rten 'byung dod dngul srang lnga bcu tham pa phul/ tshur yang gos chen gyi ring 'gag dang thang zhwa gser thebs sogs gsol ras gya nom pa stsal/ rtse phyag
nyi don lags nas kyang dngos po'i gnang sbyin bzang po mdzad/ phun khang du seng chen sprul pa'i sku dang / drung yig chos mdzad chen por tshe bka' sogs phul/ sngar gyi
rgyun thud nas mtshams la yod dus nyang stod khar kha dus 'khor ba'i dbu mdzad de phyogs su yong dgos zer ba'od du byung yang 'gro ba ma shar/ lo 'di'i zla ba bzhi pa'i
tshes brgyad la rje bla ma dngul chu ba dha rma'i mtshan can de nyid kyang zhi bar gshegs/ dbus nas khri byang chub chos 'phel gyi 'dra brnyan mtshar ba zhig phyag mdzod
nas bskur ba yin nam 'dir phebs te nged rang la bla ma rnams mnyes shing rjes su 'dzin pa'i rten 'brel ni bzang ba

tsam byung / zla ba lnga pa'i tshes bcu la rin lding grwa tshang ba byams pa 'gyur med la bsnyen rdzogs dgos pa'i las grwa zhig byas/ drug pa'i tshes bzhi la dpal ldan chos
'phel dang / dpal ldan phun tshogs gnyis bsnyen rdzogs byas te/ nga rang gis sdom pa phog tshad la mkhan slob sbrags ma byas pa kho na las gzhan med/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen
pa'i bka' las/ 'dul ba yi ger 'bri mi rung / /dpe klog gi chog lta ci smos/ /zhes 'byung bas chog gang byas dpe la ltos mi dgos bar byas so/ /deng sang bod 'di na 'dul
ba'i lag len sham zhig ni yod yod mi 'dra/ gzugs brnyan zhig ni 'dug /de rgyu mtshan du byas nas ngas bstan pa la bya ba byas so zhes brjod kyang 'ud gog rang du mi 'gro
ba tsam yod do/ /mkhan slob grong dpon tshogs pa'i bzhugs gral der/ /las chog yi ge 'khrugs pa'i bab bcol gtam/ /bsnyan da nas bsgrub bya bong bu ser po la/ /dge slong
ming du 'chos pa'i ya mtshan mang / /brtan mkhas yon tan rang la mi ldan zhing / /bslab gsum don gnyer bsgrub bya'ang dkon mod kyi/ /dus mthar so thar sdom pa'i gsar spel
rgyun/ /lag len tshad mas byas pa'i rnam thar yin/ /spong bdun tshul khrims dag pa'i lcags kyu yis/ /

sems kyi glang chen smyon pa ma btul na/ /gur kum chos kyis bkra ba'i chos gos kyis/ /rang lus lan brgyar dkris kyang ci la phan/ /de phyir mkhan slob ded dpon la brten nas/
/bsrung thabs yan lag lnga yi grur bzhugs na/ /blo gros dman yang chos 'dul rgya mtsho las/ /tshul khrims nor bu thob par the tshom med/ /zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bcu gsum
nyin rje btsun dam pa 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang po khams phyogs su 'gro don la phebs pa'i tshur lam 'di khar chibs bskyod gnang ste/ de gong sgrub mchod tshar pa byas
nas phebs 'phral kho nar dpal mchog rdo rje sems dpa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dngos sta sbrel ba'i dbang dang / de'i sang nyin nas phar rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa lha
bcu gsum/ 'jigs byed dpa' bo gcig pa bu lugs/ /shangs chos ne gu'i sgyu lus dbang mo che/ /bde mchog lha lnga'i dbang bzhi lus bsgrigs dang / /rgyud sde lnga gtso bsdus
kyi byin rlabs/ /su kha chos drug gi dbang khrid mdor bsdus/ nged rang nas brtsams pa'i yog sna kha shas kyi lung phul/ tshur rgyud sde lnga rigs bsdus kyi dbang bka' chen
mo/ phyag chen bka' lnga sogs shangs chos

lhag ma'i dbang khrid cha tshang / ma hA ma ya lha lnga'i dbang bcas zhus/ phan tshun 'bul nod dang brtan bzhugs rten 'brel 'grig thabs legs par mdzad/ tshes bco brgyad kyi
skya rengs shar pa tsam la khong dpon g.yog rnams la bka' bsgo bkra shis rgyas pa phul nas phebs rdzong zhus/ de nas ljongs skyur dang sbrags phu shar man spel lcang rar
chu bzhugs la zhag 'ga' bsdad/ de 'khor nas rje bla ma lcags zam pa phebs te jo nang lugs kyi dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang bka' rdzogs par zhus/ byis 'jug gi dbang tshugs
pa dang kha ba babs te dbang gi dus 'go'i mtshams su slebs pa dang ri klung med par dar dkar gyi bsgril ba bzhin du song / rigs ldan sprul pa'i sku rnams dges pa'i mtshan
ltas su go/ nged rang nas rje bla ma nyid la sgrol ma bla med dang / rgyud sde lnga rigs bsdus kyi dbang bka' chen mo rnams phul/ phan tshun 'bul nod dang lhag par kho
bo rang la dus 'khor lhan skyes la sbyor drug gi bla ma brgyud pas bskor ba'i bris thang zhig stsal nas chos 'di'i bdag poi khyed rang la zhu ba lags so gsung / dgun bzhugs
byas nas dus 'khor thugs dkyil gyi grangs bsnyen btang / rang lo zhe dgu pa yongs 'dzin

zhes pa chu pho byi ba'i lo shar pa dang / zhwa lu sbyas chan po/ sku zhang / shing tshal dkar po ba/ nor bu bde ldan pa sogs so so nas ring 'tsho'i maNDal rten gsum sogs byung
/ yar 'brog bsam sdings nas rje btsun bla ma ye shes phyi DA ki mas kyang gsung shog gis drangs pa'i ring 'tsho'i rten gsum dngos po'i gnang sbyin gya nom bstsal/ zla
ba gsum pa'i nang du bkris lhun por phyin/ rang re nas rgya dngul srang brgya dang sum cu skor sku rgyur byas pa'i rgyal ba byams pa mgon po'i dngul sku bzhengs tshar bas
gzungs 'bul dang bal bu lha bzo ba gnyis la yon dngul srang bdun cu skor/ gyon pa lus chas kyi bskor sogs lha bzo pa rnams mnyes par byas/ rten la rab gnas mdor bsdus
shig bsgrubs/ skyabs mgon paN chen rin po cher 'char can gyi sku tshe'i tshe rdzas dang / dngul srang lnga bcu/ gser zho gang sogs phul/ tshur yang stod 'phags gos grub khyad
'phags zhig gnang / phun khang chos mdzad chen po dpon 'khor rnams dang chabs gcig seng chen sprul pa'i sku la tshe dbang sogs phul/ rang gnas su 'byor te hor zla bzhi
pa'i tshes 'gor dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rab gnas bkra shis

rgyas byed 'bring po'i steng nas dngul sku la spyan dbye'i cho ga phul zhing / tshes bco lnga la dge 'dun rab tu mang pos ser sbreng dang bcas dngul sku dus 'khor lha khang
gi lcags dra'i nang du gdan 'dren zhus/ tshogs yongs su mang ja 'gyed Tam kha re dang las tshan che gra bcu gsum la kha btags re bcas btang / bar skabs su dpon slob ri phug
gnas la bu ston bka' 'bum gyi lung sogs kyang gang 'tshams re bklags/ hor zla drug pa'i tshes bzhi la grangs che dpon slob la bsnyen rdzogs dang / dga' lung gi btsun
gsar ma kha gcig la rab byung gi sdom pa phogs/ bdun pa'i tshes gsum la byams gling rab byung ma nyi ma chos bzang dang / rnam rgyal chos sgron/ khrims ldan gling ma rnams
dang bcas pa yong nas tshogs 'khor dang bcas pa'i ring 'tsho'i maNDal bshad pa dben dgon bya bral sprul skus mdzad nas 'bul ba byung / tshes bco lnga la dga' lung 'dus
spyi dang / tshes bco brgyad la dbang ldan chos 'khor ba'i bla ma dbu chos/ nyi shu lnga la grangs che grwa tshang gis ring 'tsho'i gsol 'debs maNDal rten gsum dang bcas
pa gong 'khod so so nas bstar/ ljongs bskyur la phu shar man spel lcang gshongs su r-i Shi'i chu bdugs brten pa sogs kyang

byas / dga' lung du a ne sgrub pa mo dang 'phrad kha'i rting ma de byung / dgun bzhugs kyi sgrub pa la yod dus lo de'i zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes bdun la a ni dgung lo brgyad
cu gya brgyad du phebs pa yang sku gshegs/ gdung ma mchod 'bul bas mtshon rjes sgrub rnams kyang ne gnas don grub kyis dngos gtsang bsgrubs/ sgrub khang sger gyi zhwa
lu 'dus tshogs dang / dga' lung dgon du sman bla nyin gang dang / yon dngul Tam ka re 'phar du btang / rang lo lnga bcu pa bdag med ces pa chu mo glang gi lo shar pa'i hor
zla dang po'i tshes bdun la skyabs mgon paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa dag zhing la phebs tshes bcu gsum la nye gnas bkra shis lhun par mngags nas dngul gdung rin po che'i
zhal 'debs su rgya dngul rta rmig ma gcig dang / bod dngul srang lnga bcu gser brgyad rdo sogs phul/ hor zla bzhi pa'i tshes bco lnga la skyabs mgon de nyid kyi dgongs
rdzogs su dmigs nas ri mthil tshogs chen la mang ja 'gyed dngul Tam ka re tshogs gdan grum gang ba bcu 'dul sbyar byas/ zla ba lnga pa'i mjug tu bkra shis lhun po'i rgyud
grwa'i dge bshes bzhi bla brang chen po nas gtong gnang mdzad par dri

med rnam gnyis kyi dbang lung dang / dngul gdung rin po che'i srog shing 'dzugs pa'i phyag len zhib rgyas su phul/ rang lo nga gcig pa kun dga' zhes pa shing pho stag gi lo
sku zhang khri chen yang dbus phyogs su bsnyung nas 'di khar phebs byung ba sman spyad rim gros zlog med kyi lo de'i zla ba lnga pa'i tshes mgor sku khams ma 'tsho/ yar
'brog bsam sdings gi zhabs drung rdo rje phag mo yang zhing gshegs pa'i mchod bsngo slebs/ gdung 'bul dngul srang tsum cu skor phul/ hor zla gsum pa'i nag nya la nye gsan
kyi dkor lan du khang snying grwa tshang par gsang 'dus sgrub mchod nyin 'khyongs gcig gi bsnyen bkur 'gyed bcas dang / tshogs gdan grum tse yug gnyis sbyor du bcug /ston
kha skyin mkhar tshwa chur bskyod nas tshur lam mthar pa grwa tshang gi 'bod nan ches pas thar pa'i 'du khang du ser skya mang po la tshe bka' rgyas par byas/ grwa pa rnams
la mang 'gyed gcig btang / tha skar zla ba'i lha babs dus chen la bkra shis lhun por phyin nas tshogs chen la mang ja zab pa gcig dang lha khang rnams la stong mchod
rgyas pa gcig phul/ chos 'brel zhu mkhan mang du byung pa ba phan btags/ de nas gor dmag gi gzir cha yang langs pas bla gzhung

gi dmag bzlog zhabs rim bsgrub dgos mang ba byung pa dngos po rnams bkye nas zhwa lu ba'i grwa pa rnams sgrub tu bcug rang res kyang smon 'dun gang shes byas/ zla ba bcu gnyis
pa'i nang sa gung bshad sgra chen po gor dmag gi skor la phebs zhor rgyan gong lha mo mjal skabs nye gnas btang nas mtshams zhu sogs phul/ rang lo nga gnyis pa srin bu
zhes pa shing mo yos kyi lo'i zla ba dang po'i nang rang gi nye gnas la dog cha che ba'i rmi ltas byung pa der dmigs rim 'gro gang shes byas kyang zla ba lnga pa'i nang
khams ma 'tsho/ dge phrug ri phug gnas kyi rjes sgrub khang drag stong 'jug gis dge rtse gong 'phel 'byung ba'i smon 'dun gang drags bgyis/ 'di nas bzung dpon slob rin po
che nas 'khur blangs te shi gson gyi dngos phran byung rigs sha khu sha thims su gtong 'jug gis zhwa lur sman bla sgrub mchod kyi rten dngul srang lnga bcu tham pa dang
/ kun mkhyen bu ston chen po'i dus mchod gsar sbyor byas par srang brgya dang sum cu so gnyis kyi ma rtsa sbyar ba da lta gong 'phel du yod/ zla ba drug pa'i tshes bzhi
la dus 'khor lha khang du bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa sogs bla ma rnam bzhi'i thugs dman brten/ 'di kha'i

dngul sku rin po che rnam gsum sogs rten gsum khag gi spyan sngar zangs dmar la dngul gyi kha brgyan yod pa rgya mtsho mar kha la bco brgyad 'gro gsar bskrun gyis 'gro song
Tam srang sum cu so brgyad song / lo 'khor mar me 'bul thebs she dpon rnam rgyal lags nas dngul srang sum cu dang 'di nas Tam srang nyi shu bcas bsdoms Tam srang lnga bcu
tham pa bla brang chen por gsol 'debs kyis lo ltar dngul bskyed zhu rgyu'i phyag tham kyang don smin stsal/ zhwa mthil dngul gdung lha khang / mkhan chen rnam gnyis/ gnas
bcu lha khang du thub dbang bcas la snam sbyar re dang lhung bzed/ ri phug tu bka' bzhi pa'i thugs dam nang rten la snam sbyar/ dus 'khor lha khang du dngul sku rnam gnyis
la tsha rong rtsis dpon de nyid nas skyabs rten du phul bas sku rgyan byu ru sran tsam rdog brgya dang brgyad yod pa gcig /yang dpal lhun rtsis dpon sku zhabs kyi 'di

song / zhwa mthil du mkhan chen sku dus su bzhengs pa'i rnga bo che cha gcig la rnga khri bkrol brkos kyi sbag mtshal gser gyis ri mos phyug cing rnga gzungs dang bcas par
shing cha dang bzo rigs pa rnams kyi yon rdzong sogs 'gro song bsdoms Tam srang sum cu so bzhi dang zho brgyad song / zla ba bdun pa'i nang bkras lhun phyag mchod skyabs
dbyings na mkhan chen por mi rje phun khang brgyud snga phyi nas gsol ba btab kyang phyag tog du ma 'khel 'di lo 'phral mar bka' bzhes dang lhag par sku bcar chos 'phel lags
nas gang spyi'i zhu thabs bsaskyangs te/ rgyal po chen po rnam thos sras gtso bor bzhugs pas lha mgron rYagal ba rin chen grub/ rje bla ma/ paN chen blo bzang chos rgyan/
bstan pa'i nyi ma phyogs las rnam rgyal/ phyag na rdo rje/ las gshin/ lha mo rdo rje rab brtan ma bcas kyi gos sku gsar bzhengs kyi rgyu rtsar gos tshos sna kha nyis
brgya dang dngul Tam srang nyis brgya dang / rgya dngul thur 'debs kyi srang lnga bcu tham pa Tam srang lnga bcu nga lnga ri nges gos sne bcas gos dngul tshang ma bsgril
ba'i Tam srang lnga brgya zin ngas 'bum laM zhus/ zla ba bcu pa'i nang bzhengs grub pa dang skyabs dbyings

chen por legs 'bul zhu mi mngags te gos sku gdan zhu byas/ zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes dgu la rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga rgyas pa 'phrin bcol dang bcas pa bgyis/ tshes bco lnga'i
nyin rta bdag brgyad sogs bsu ba gser sbreng dang bcas zhwa mthil du spyan drangs/ de nyin rdo bcal du tshogs yongs kyi bskangs 'phrin rgyas bar zhus 'di nas zhal gro'i
zab ja 'gyed Tam re/ mchod pa sna lnga brgya tshar/ lhag por bla brang chen po nas zab ja 'gyed re las sne khag la rnam gzhag bcas bka' drin bskyangs de mtshungs 'di kha
nas zor las par 'chams phod rgyab dar tshos sna/ las mkhan mun pa nag por 'chams phod rgyal mtshan dar ru chung bcas cha 'grig la Tam srang nyi shu brgyad ri pa'i le tshan
sbyar/ spyi so dang grwa tshang bzhi/ nor bu bde ldan/ shing tshal ba/ dpal lhun dge slong bstan 'dzin/ lha rnga dben chos/ dge slong blo gros/ dge chos 'phel tshe ring
/ grong pa gser byang / nor bu dkyil khang pa/ so so nas gro so phye mar/ mang ja re dang / mchod pa rgyas bsdus sna tshogs bcas zhal gro'i tshul du bsgrubs pa'i legs
tshogs che ba byung / de sngon gor dmag gi skor la gzir cha che zhing rgya mi am ban nas ser dmag tshun chad bskul ba sogs

te mchod rdzas gshom grogs zhu ba phul ba ltar bsnon ma rgya rta gcig mdzad de rgya rta gnyis kyi rtsis gzhi bskor te bzang gos spyad ldan gzhi mtshungs phye phur cha gcig
/rgyal mtshan sham bu dgu brtsegs yod pa ka 'phan lag ring cha gnyis dang zab ja gcig bcas 'di skabs su gnang / ma he mchod par zhwa lu ba'i bla ma las sne khag gis gdan

yod pa 'byor pa yang 'dir phul/ zhwa lu skor dpon sprod khongs su dngul gyi ma Ni lag skor kyang sbyar/ sngon du sman bla'i pho brang gsar bskrun bgyis pa rgyal rtse rin

pa'i/ /ser gzugs tshogs pa'i yang rtse yin nam snyam/ /tshe thung nam 'chi cha med tshe zhabs la/ /yun ring sdod

pas grabs gshoms ma byas shing / /sgo gsum dge ba'i phyogs su gang 'gro byas/ /snyigs dus 'dun ma'i yang rtse yin nam snyam/ /rang sems 'khrul pa'i snang bas bcings pa la/

snyam la/ /chags sdang nye ring nam yang ma byas zhing / /byams dang snying rje gang drag bsgom tshul byas/ /phan sems che ba'i yang rtse yin nam snyam/ /'khos med btsun

gser phib/

sku 'bum thang bcas par bsdoms zangs dmar gyi rgya mtsho khebs bcus gsum khor yug gcig /jo khang gi rgya mtsho khabs bcas de dag gi rgyu 'gro yongs bsgril Tam srang brgyad
cu gya dgu zho gang bcas song ba 'di khar nyar tshags byas pa'i dkar me'i shul bogs thog nas tshang ma yong ba byas/ phyin chad chu dwangs nya gsal gyi dpe bzhin khungs sogs
ra 'phrod pa'i dkar me'i bogs char zha chag med pa yong ba'i deb sbyor gtan tshigs yig rigs sogs byas/ ri phug gzim sbug pa rgya mtsho gsar bskrun 'di nas bgyis/ zla

po'i rjes gnang dang chos mtshan khag klu pa'i gser chos 'phags pa spyan ras

gzigs seng ge sgra'i rjes gnang dang chos mtshan tshe 'khrid zla ba'i chu rgyun gyi 'khrid/ mi 'khrugs pa sa lugs bkra shis lha mo brgyad bskor gyi dbang / tA ra nA tha'i sgrol
dkar tshe 'khrid/ bde can pho 'khrid dpa' bo g.yul 'jug /bde mchog lU i pa'i dbang bzhi/ mthun drug rnal 'byor/ rta mgrin gsang sgrub skyer sgang lugs kyi byin rlabs/
zla rgyal lugs rta mgrin lcags ral can gyi rjes gnang dang chos mtshan/ bde mchog lU i pa'i bskyed rdzogs kyi 'khrid/ brang ti pa mtshan gyi yig cha'i steng nas 'jam dbyangs
dmar ser gyi rjes gnang / dus 'khor bsrung 'bi lha gsum gyi rjes gnang / 'jam dbyangs smra seng gi rjes gnang / sa lugs rme brtsegs kyi rjes gnang / rme brtsegs lo
lo'i sgrub skor/ 'jam dpal nag po'i chos skor/ mi g.yo dkar po'i rjes gnang / de dag gi yig cha'i lung / sa lugs lo gyon ser po'i rjes gnang sgrub skor/ she'u lo tsA ba'i
yig steng nas jo lugs dang 'dzam dkar 'bru gzhon gyi rjes gnang lung / mgon po phyag drug pa'i gtor dbang bar chad kun sel/ dmag zor rgyal mo'i rjes gnang / mkhan chen sangs

rgyas phun tshags kyi yig steng nas sa skya'i gser cos khyung nag 'byung po 'ur 'ded kyi rjes gnang de'i sgrub skor gyi lung / khyung khra man ngag lugs kyi rjes gnang / bcu
gcig zhal lha lnga'i rjes gnang / rgyal sras dngul chu ba'i smyung gnas cho ga'i lung / dge lugs 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma'i sgrub thabs za ma tog gi lung / gser chos seng
gdong sngon mo'i rjes gnang paN chen nags rin lugs seng gdong dmar mo'i rjes gnang / dbyangs can sa la'i pho nya'i rjes gnang / khro bo gtsug tor 'bar ba'i rjes gnang /
de'i sgrub skor thu'u bkwan blo bzang chos kyi nyi mas mdzad pa/ rdo sems bla med lugs kyi rjes gnang / de dag gi yig cha skyid shod bstan 'dzin 'phrin las kyi thugs sraslo
tsA ba'i snyan brgyud dbyangs can dkar mo'i rjes gnang / de dag gi yig cha'i lung / gser chos 'dzam lha srog sgrub dmar po'i rjes gnang / 'dzam dmar gra sngon lugs gi
rjes gnang / tshe dbang bu ston gong khug ma'i dbang dang de'i lung / sman bla'i mdo chog gzhan phan bde 'jug gi lung bcas bgyis/ sa zla'i nang lha ldan jo shAg rnam gnyis
sogs la stong mchod 'bul thebs Tam srang brgya dang bco brgyad

sa dbang dpal lhun chen por bcol gdam zhus pa'i mchod 'bul sogs la zhal 'debs dang bcas gang legs thugs rje che 'dug /tshes bdun la ri phug gdan 'dzin pa sogs la bsnyen rdzogs
kyi las grwa byas/ tshes bco lnga'i nyin brgya mchod sna lnga tshar gnyis dang / mang 'gyed/ gtsang jo bo gangs ra ba'i grwa pa kha shas la bsnyen rdzogs kyang bgyis/
sog po sangs rgyas rdo rje sogs bkras lhun grwa pa 'ga' la sems bskyed mchod pa yang byas/ de nas gor dmag gi gzir thag chod nas/ sa gung bshad sgra chen po sger gzhis spel
gzhir chibs bskyod bskyangs pa'i zhor du 'dir phebs pa'i nyin rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs dang / de'i sang nyin byabs khrus tshe dbang sgra mi snyan
gyi tshe gzungs 'khrid bcas phul/ de nas ngor mkhan chen rin po che sogs grwa pa 'ga' la/ sbyong dkyil bcu gnyis kyi dbang / de'i dbang chog gzhan phan rgya mtsho'i lung
/ 'phags pa don yod zhags pa'i dbang / rdo rje dbyings tsa lugs kyi dbang / phyag rgya chen po lhan cig skyes sbyor gyi 'khrid lung / de'i chos skor yongs

rdzogs kyi lung / ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang bzhi byin rlabs/ rgyab chos skyes mchog 'bar ra ba'i mgur 'bum lung / blo sbyong tshig gdams lung / 'od zer dri med chog bsgrigs/
dri med rnam gnyis kyi mchod rten srog shing 'dzugs thabs/ gtsug gtor gdugs dkar 'don thabs sangs rgyas rnal 'byor du byed pa sogs kyi lung phul/ tshur yang / dpe chos rin
spungs sogs chos 'ga' zhig zhus/ de nas dge slong a rig pa sogs grwa pa 'ga' la/ sgrol ma rnal 'byor ma'i lung / de'i skabs dkyil chos 'byung bcas kyi lung dang bskyed
rdzogs kyi 'khrid/ mdo za ma tog nas 'byung ba'i yig drug phan yon rnams bshad/ zla ba dang po'i nang du dpal lhun rtse phyag la snying po don gsum gyi 'khrid/ byabs khrus
tshe dbang sogs bgyis te ri phug tu zla ba gcig ring bsnyen mtshams sogs mdzad pa'i rgyab gnyer kyang zhus/ rang lo bzhi pa dmar ser zhes pa me mo sbrul gyi lo dben dgon
chos sder dpal lhun sku zhabs nas sman bla sgrub mchod kyi thebs rtsa 'bul sbyor gnang ba/ bka' 'gyur bla ma sogs phebs nas sman bla'i rjes gnang dang / gzhan

phan bde 'jug gi lung bcas zhus/ rtse phyag nyi don lags 'dir phebs par yang byabs khrus tshe bka' sogs phul/ zla ba gnyis pa'i nang bsam yas rten gsum khag la stong mchod
'bul thebs Tam srang brgya tham pa dang / snyan shal le tshan bcas/ sa gung bshad sgra chen por 'bul rdzong zhus pa'i mchod 'bul rnams sbyor dngos rjes gtsang bka' drin che
ba byung / mi rje phun khang dang she dpon rnam rgyal lags su byad 'grol byabs khrus tshe dbang brgya tshar/ nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs bcas phul/ she dpon lags
nas dad 'dun chen pos zhwa lu matil du rta mgrin lha khang dang dngul gdung lha khang du zangs dmar gyi rgya mtsho dngadakar me'i 'bul thebs Tam srang brgya tham pa bcas
'bul sbyor mdzad/ de nas theg gling sgrub sde'i dge slong rnams la bcu gcig zhal dpal mo lugs kyi dbang dang / de'i dbang chog lung paN chen blo bzang chos brgyan gyi mdzad
pa'i smyung gnas cho ga'i lung / sgrol mchod paNDal bzhi pa'i lung bcas bgyis/ mkhas btsun gzhon nu grub kyi gdung rten nyams chags su gyur pa 'di nas chos 'khor yan
gsar bzhengs/ gzungs bsaskyar

'bul / bum ldir ngos dngul ga yod pa'i nang mkhas btsun rin po che'i bris sku bcas gzim sbug tu bzhugs su gsol ba dang / nyi shu gcig mchod skabs dmigs rten bu ston gyi gos
sku bzhengs rgyu dpal lhun rtse phyag tu gnyer gdams zhus pa gsar bzhengs grub pa'i 'gro song Tam srang brgya dang drug cu tham pa song ba rnams/ 'dir skyabs rten du phul
ba'i 'di nas dmigs bsal 'bul dgos gang yang ma byung shing / phyags mtshungs mang thebs Tam srang bco lnga sbyor 'jags mdzad/ rab gnas tshar ba dang / sa zla'i tshes bco
lnga'i nyin rten 'brel khyad 'bul sbyor dang / mang 'gyed/ brgya mchod tshar gnyis bsgrubs/ dge slong a rig pa dang sangs rgyas rdo rje sogs grwa pa 'ga' la nA ro mkha'
spyod ma'i byin rlabs dang / de'i 'khrid yongs rdzogs/ rgyab chos be'u 'bum gyi lung / dngul chu bka' 'bum gras rnal 'byor ma'i dbang chog /sbyin sreg rgyun 'khyer shog
gcig ma'i lung sogs byas/ drug pa'i tshes bzhi la dus 'khor lha khang du thub dbang shar li gcig phul/ lo ltar khrus gsol mchod 'bul/ rab gnas sogs bgyis/ bde chen sprul
sku rin po che/ phyag rdor 'gro bzang gi dbang dang byabs khrus

tshe bka' sogs gsan par phebs pa'i thugs bzhed bskangs/ chab mdo tshong dpon dbang phyug sogs la bsnyen rdzogs kyang byas/ ston po skyin mkhar tshwa chur bskyod/ tshur slebs
nas bla ma skal bzang sogs grwa pa 'ga' la 'dzam lha dkar po'i rjes gnang / blo sbyong don bdun ma'i 'khrid/ zhen pa bzhi bral/ skyid sdug lam 'khyer/ phar phyin drug bshad
pa jo bo'i rnam thar blo sbyong brgya rtsa'i lung / kha rag sgom chung gi ang yig bdun cu ba dngul chu rgyal sras pa'i mdzad pa'i blo sbyong bcas kyi lung / bu ston
gyi blo sbyong chos chen bco lnga'i 'khrid bshad lung stag phu'i yig steng nas rdor sems bla med rjes gnang lung / jo lugs phyag 'tshal nyer gcig gi rjes gnang / nA ro mkha'
spyod kyi byin rlabs dang de'i 'khrid yongs rdzogs bcas grub/ de rjes nyang stod theg mchog gling gi mkhan po sogs grwa pa 'ga' la bsnyen rdzogs kyi las grwa yang bgyis/
shing tshal tshong dpon nas ser skya mgo dmangs la tshe bka' sogs bya dgos dbu nan bgyis kyang byed blo ma shar/ slar yang bskyar nan gyis bskul ba ltar zla ba bcu gnyis
pa'i chos 'gor

ri phug tu tshogs chen la 'chi med rnga sgra'i dbang sman bla sgrol dkar gyi rjes gnang lung chos spyod rab gsal gyi lung / mjug tu ser skya khag mang la tshe dbang bu ston
gong khug ma'i dbang thams cad mkhyen pa rgyal ba rin chen grub kyi mkhan slob dge 'dun spyi dang / mi sde bcas pa la zhal gdams mdzad pa'i lung yang bsgrags/ thams cad
la tshe 'di phyir phan pa'i bslab bya gang drag kyang byas/ rang lo nga lnga pa dus kyi pho nya zhes pa sa rta gnam lo shar nang sngar rgyud sde rnams/ sa chen kun dga' blo
gros kyi par brkos mdzad pa'i par shing stong phrag lnga dang lnga brgya lnga bcas zhwa mthil du bzhugs yod pa bar lam par thams cad 'dzings rkyen la brten rim pas nyams
chags che bar par shing tshang ma ri phug tu gdan zhus kyi ka btags brkos te/ par khri gsar bsgrigs bgyis nas ri phug rang du par khang dmigs bsal 'gad gtsang thar yod/
de dag gi 'gro song yong bsgril gyi Tam srang sum cu tham pa song / grwangs che grwa tshang du nag nya'i dus 'khor sgrub mchod skabs dkyil 'khor gyi gdugs dngul srang nyi
shu tham pa'i rin thang yod pa phul/ 'phar du 'gyed Tam re btang / ri

phug gi 'du khang byang gi seng g.yab la thang bskor bsnyen rdzogs sdom brgyud/ bstan pi btad rabs bdun gnas bcu sogs kyi bris thang gsar bskrun gyis gong sham/ 'ja'/ ton chob
bzo rigs pa'i gla yon sogs dang ling dmar ljang gi gdung khebs bcas yongs bsgril Tam srang brgya dang nyi shu rtsa gnyis gnas pa dang / rab gnas grub ste sa zla'i dus
chen la 'bul sbyor gyi rab ston mang 'gyed dang brgya mchod sna lnga tshar gnyis bsgrubs/ de nyin rgyal rtse rin lding pa sogs grwa pa 'ga' la bsnyen rdzogs byas/ zhwa lu
bla brang gi ar zug gang legs yong re'i bkod pa bshad/ 'di nas ar ston zab rgyas/ zhwa lu ri mthil gyi rdo ting de bzhin khang par gnod tshab che ba'i ting tshab 'khar
rnga zhig kyang sbyar/ nyer gcig mchod pa'i skabs bstan 'gyur bris ma pod nyis brgya dang bzhi la smon tshig yod pa'i na bza' kha gru re dang gdong dar gos tshos sna gsum
brtsegs pa grwa mtshungs phul ba'i srang bzhi bcu zhe dgu'i rgyu 'gro dang / de nyin mang 'gyed skar lnga re dang / brgya mchod bcas phul/ zla ba brgyad pa'i nang tshes
bcu bzhi nas bzung bar

mkhan chen rin po che sogs dbang cha kha shas la rnam snang mngon byung gi dbang / de'i dbang chog lung / spyan ras gzigs padma dra ba'i dbang / ma hA ma yA lha lnga'i dbang
/ sdom 'byung lha bcu gsum pa'i dbang / dril bu lha lnga'i dbang / dril bu lus dkyil dbang bzhi/ gshed dmar bcu gsum gyi dbang / phyag rdor 'gro bzang gi dbang / phyag
rdor 'khor chen gyi dbang / rnam sras bka' chen bcu drug gi rjes gnang / dus 'khor gyi bsrung ba'i lha gsum gyi rjes gnang lung / padma'i sgrub dkyil mchon 'phring sbyin
sreg sgyu ma chen po'i mngon dkyil rnam snang mngon byang dkyil chog sdom 'byung mngon dkyil dril bu lag dkyil rdul tshon lha lnga'i mngon dkyil gshed dmar lha bcu gsum pa'i
sgrub dkyil bcas kyi lung / bde mchog gi lU i pa'i dbang chog gdan gzhi'i lhan thabs gdugs dkar nyer bdun ma'i dbang chog thugs rje chen po'i sgrub thabs/ gtar ma'i cho
ga 'khrul med rab gsal gyi rnam bshad rdo dbyings dbang chog dus 'khor bsnyen thabs gnas brtan mchod chog don zhags dbang chog bcas kyi lung / rje dge 'dun rgya mtshos
mdzad pa'i me tog

bcud len gyi 'khrid/ bde mchog rim lnga'i bskyed rdzogs kyi 'khrid bcas phul/ tshur yang 'jigs byed ro langs brgyad bskor gyis dbag gshe dmar lha lnga'i dbang / sems bskyed
mchod pa dang / tshe dbang zla 'phel sogs chos tshan mang ba zhus/ de rjes dpal lhun sras sku 'bring gtsug phud 'bul ba dang rab byung chabs cig bsgrubs/ mi ring ba gzhan
sgrub cha 'ga' dang bcas bsnyen rdzogs kyang bsgrubs/ zla ba bcu gcig pa'i nang kham mnga' ris sprul sku sogs la bde mchog gha do pa'i zhal can lha so bdun gyi dbang bzhi
gu ge paNDi ta'i yig cha'i steng nasabagyis/ bong bu'i khra thig bskyed rdzogs mdor bsdus kyi lung / nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs de'i 'khrid yongs rdzogs zhal bzhes
yig chung gsum gyi lung / zhwa lu'i mkhan brgyud rnam thar lung bcas bgyis/ rang lo nga drug pa don grub ces pa sa mo lug gi lo sngon du bla ma skal bzang 'dir 'byor
skabs sku zhabs zhi bzang rin po cher zhu yig dang bcas bka' 'gyur chab par ma blu yon du zhu rgyu rnams mngags cha bgyis par 'di lo zla

gnyis pa'i nag gdan zhu thub pa sogs byung / grang che grwa tshang gi ar zug las grwa tshugs rgyu sogs la mngags cha bgyis/ de sngon khar kha dus 'khor grwa tshang gi dus 'khor
gyi dbang chos sogs zhus byung yang stabs ma 'grig 'di lo dbu nan gyis gdan zhu slebs par zla ba gsum pa'i tshes gsum nyin ngo g.yog rnams kha khar bskyod nas tshes
bzhi la dben dgon du 'byor tshes lnga'i nyin slob ma rjes 'dzin dang / tshes drug la sta gon byas chos grol skabs ri klung thams cad kha bas g.yogs pa dang 'brug sgra dal
gyis sgrog pa sogs byung pa ni byang phyogs shambha la'i rig ldan rgyal po dgyes pa'i mtshan ltas kyi rten 'brel yin nam snyam/ tshes brgyad nas bzung te byis pa ltar 'jug
pa'i dbang / dbang gong ma che chung bdag po chen po'i dbang sogs zhib rgyas byas/ gzhan yang mi 'khrugs pa'i dbang / gdugs dkar nyer bdun ma'i dbang / rdo rje shugs kyi
rdzas gnang / sman bla'i rjes gnang / rnam 'joms kyi rjes gnang / dus 'khor sgrub dkyil bstod chen chos phreng bcas kyi lung / mjug tu ser skya mang por tshe dbang byabs
khrus sogs bgyis/ spyir

deng sang phal cher dang khyad par dpal 'khor chos sde'i grwa khyun 'di rnams chos zhu me shes pa lta bu 'dug na'ang / g.yung ston gyis gsung las/ phan bde'i 'byung gnas rgyal
ba'i bstan pa la/ /phan gnod byed pa'i gang zag mu bzhi yod/ /chos dang chos min byed pa'ang mu bzhi yod/ /gang zag tshad 'dzin spangs pa'i rnam thar yin/ /zhes pa ltar/
sus bstan pa la phan thogs mi thogs mi shes pas dbang chos rnams phra zhib dang / bshad pa sogs go gang bde byas pa yin/ de mtshungs nged rang gi snga phyir dbang rjes
gnang dang 'khrid sogs la chos nyan pa bos nges gang thub shod khul byas/ grwa tshang rang dang gser khang 'ong nas rab byung zhu mi dang bsnyen rdzogs kyi las grwa sogs
mang ba byas/ rgyal rtse rin lding grwa tshang nas gdan zhu dbu nan che yang 'gro ba ma shar/ tshes bcu dgu'i nyin dus gtor snga myur gyis rnam sras mchod pa gzabs gshoms
bgyis par bsdad/ tshes nyer gcig la chas te tshur lam spel gzhi ru zhag gcig bsdad nas khrus gsol rab gnas dang / pho mo mang bor tshe bka' byabs khrus kyang byas/ yar
lam zhwa mthil du phyin

nas gtsug lag khang du mchod 'bul khrus gsol/ rung khang bla brang sogs la rab gnas kyang bgyis/ 'di skabs ri mthil nas bsu ba gser sbrengs sogs bkod gshom rgyas pa byung /
tshes nyer lnga la ri phug tu 'byor/ grangs che grwa tshang par ar don zab pa zhig btang / de nas khams pa'i bla ma chos dbang grags pa dang / bla ma skal bzang sogs la
kye rdor man ngag lugs lha dgu'i dbang rgyal thang lugs kyi gcod dbang dang 'khrid/ gcod kyi nying khu'i 'khrid yig tA ra na thas mdzad pa dang / ngag 'don rgyun 'khyer mjug
tu ngo gcod bya 'bebs sogs yod pa bcas ya tshan gyis lung bsgrags kha khar bskyod skabs shi gson gyi dngos po byung rigs rnams sa zla'i dus chen nyin mang ja grwa re
la Tam re zin nges spungs 'gyed grwa tshang bzhi so sor dngos po Tam srang bzhi re zin pa'i dngos po de mtshungs theg gling ri khrod byams pa gling / bsam gtan sgang / dga'
lung / chos phug sogs so sor dngos po rnams cha dgos byas pa'i gtsang dag 'gro ba byas nyin der 'di kha'i grwa khyun 'ga' la bsnyen rdzogs kyang byas/ de rjes bde chen
sprul sku rin po cher phyag rdor 'khor chen lha bco brgyad kyi dbang byabs khrus tshe bka' sogs phul/ tshur yang

bka' gdams thig le bcu drug gi dbang zhus/ zla ba drug pa'i tshes brgyad la grangs che grwa tshang 'dul khang gi rab gnas cho ga rgyas par grub zhal gro rab ston mang 'gyed/
nag nya'i tshes bco lnga'i nyin 'di nas sbyar ba'i sngar yod tshogs mchod thebs rtsa'i kha skong bcas bsdoms Tam srang brgyad nyin khyod gcig gi thebs rtsa Tam srang sum
cu tham pa rtsis pa'i zhing ngor bzang gcig sbyar nyi shu gcig mchod skabs bde chen ral gcig la ngal gsol bla ma brgyud pas bskor ba/ gsang ba 'dus pa la rim lnga'i brgyud
pas bskor ba/ gshin rje'i gshed la spros med brgyud pas bskor ba/ dus kyi 'khor lo la sbyor drug brgyud pas bskor ba ste 'khrid chen bzhi'i bris thang thog tshad ma bzhi
la rgyu 'gro yongs bsgril Tam srang drug cu re brgyad dang zho drug thob/ rab ston mang 'gyed dang bcas gong tshes nyin sbyar/ chab mdo zhi bzang rin po che'i mdzod pa
nor rgyas dang bla ma skal bzang sogs la dbang sdus lha mo rig byed ma'i mthun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang dang / bIr bsrung dus 'khor gyi bsrung pa'i lha gsum gyi rjes
gnang byabs khrus tshe bka' sogs byas/ lha babs dus chen la dkar dbu mdzad sogs la bsnyen rdzogs

kyang bgyis de nas dad rang gi chos nyid du 'char ba'i sgya ma'i chos thams cad phal cher zin te skyas chen nam 'degs cha ma 'khel ba'i mjug sdud pa lta bu dang lhag par 'brel
yod shi gson rnams kyi ched du dmigs bcom ldan 'das rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa'i sgrub mchod gsar 'dzugs thebs rtsar Tamasrang drug cu tham pa yang sbyar/ phyogs mtshungs
cho ga'i nag 'gros dang bcas pa bsgrigs nas par la brkos/ phogs rten du sngar chu dkar ba'i sa zhing bar skabs su gzhan tshong byas pa sogs byung par brten da cha zhing rin
gtso bo'i 'dam bla rnying sde nyi ma lags kyi sku zla rtse phyag nyi don chen po'i sku'i gcunggcong mo 'das pa ched du Tam srang brgya dang lnga bcu tham pa phul ba dang
/ mdzod pa mkhas grub gyi grwa sa'i dkor lan lta bur srang bdun cu don lnga phul ba dang / tshe smon gling gi ar po'i rten gzhung par bcol mo zhus gras nas rgyal rtse
grong chu'i 'bru gang 'tsham gnang ba dngul bsgyur gyi srang bzhi bcu zhe gsum zha bla'i bogs dngul srang bcu gnyis bcas byung pa la gzhi byas pas lo ltar sgrub mchod pa
brgya dang bcu la phogs 'bru gtsang lcag dong bcu re yong pa zhus shing gser zangs kyi rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa lha tshogs bcu

gsum dang shing brkos kyi blos bslangs dkyil 'khor yang bzhengs so/ a ho/ skye bo tshims par byas pa'i ngogs/ /kun phan rab dkar lhag bsam bsten pa yis/ /nus pa'i yon tan shin
tu nyag phra yang / /padmo'i dri bsang cung zad 'thul par byas/ /nyang stod stag tshal sman ljongs ne'u gsing gi/ /me tog sna tshogs bkra ba'i ri bo'i sul/ /su dag snying
gi udpal bzhad byed pa/ /kA la tsakra'i gnas su nye bar bsgrubs/ /gang tshe cha bsags nor bu'i grong bsti ba'i/ /chos kyi rgyal po dgyesdges pa'i mtshan ma dang / /lhan
cig dkar po'i legs bris bu rnams kyi/ /sa 'dzi na zla ba zhu ba'i mdangs kyis bkris/ /mthong dang dran pa'i yid kyis ri mo can/ /'brel bcas mngon par mtho ba'i them skas
la/ /blo gros rkang pa gnyis pa'i 'jo sgeg gis/ /gtan bde'i gling du phyin byed smon pa btab/ /tshe 'dir zhen pa'i kun rtog rmig rgyu'i chu/ /skom pa'i gya gyur spyod
'dod ri dwags sogs/ /snying rje'i gnas su go ba'i skyo shas kyi/ /rtag tu snying la bdud rtsi'i bcud len sbyin/ /de nas rang lo nga bdun pa drag po zhes pa lcags spre lo
shar pa'i nang bkras lhun du mchod 'bul dang rtse shod tshe rdzas 'bul rgyu

sogs sngar rgyun bzhin bgyis/ mthun bar la chos 'brel zhu mi byung bar yang so sor 'dod chos ltar phan btags/ grangs che grwa tshang par nag zla'i sgrub mchod skabs shing tshal
dkar pos phul ba'i gdung khebs ling dmar ljang gi gong pa 'ja' sogs 'di nas phul/ dngul dkar gyi phung skyogs bcas sbyar/ sa zla'i dus chen nyinbka' gtan gsung sgrogs
kyi thebs rtsar Tam srang brgya dang nyer gcig /mchod pa'i kha srong dngul srang nyi shu rtsa brgyad bcas sbyar mang 'gyed Tam re btang / de yang zhwa lu 'di bzhin spyan
ras gzigs kyi zhing khams rang byung thugs rje chen po'i snang brnyan khyad par can bzhugs pa sogs yin par ma zad sku gsung thugs yon tan 'phrin las lnga tshang na gzhan
las khyad par 'phags shing / phyogs 'di'i skye bo rnams la phan pa dang lhag par kho bo rang yang rje btsun spyan ras gzigs 'di'i lam gyi rim pa la brten nas dga' ldan
du skye ba 'dzin pa'i ched du dmigs rgya dngul srang brgyad cu gya lnga dang zho bzhi gser zho bcu gnyis phra rgyan gru g.yu gsum bcas yod pa de yang dpal lhun rtsis dpon
'di nyid kyi grogs ldan mdzad tshe khong rang yang spyan ras gzigs kyi rjes su 'dzin pa'i

dbang bka' bskur ba sogs sbyin bdag bskul ba'i thabs rnam ma byas shing rgyu la dpags pa'i lha bshos ltar rang 'khos kyis nor lag tu gang 'byor la byas pa kho na yin no/ /nor
'dzin phun tshogs zhwa lu gser khang gi /rab byung 'phags pa'i snang brnyan gtsor gyur pa'i/ /sku gsung ghus dang yon tan 'phrin las lnga/ /tshang phyir dngul dkar las
grub khyad 'phags bskrun/ /'di yi dge bas mthong thos dran reg gi /sems can rnams kyang sgrib sbyang tshogs rdzogs nas/ /tshe rabs kun tu bde skyid ldan pa dang / rnam mkhyen
byang chub go 'phang thob par smon/ /tshe rabs mang bor bsags pa'i bden 'bras kyi/ /mi 'dod sdug bsngal sna tshogs 'byung ba dang / /dal 'byor rten la snying po ma
lon pas/ /'gro ba kun la khyad par bdag cag rnams/ /grub mchog mi tra'i zhal las bab pa yis/ /zab don mngar ba'i sbrang rtsi legs 'thung ste/ /dga' phab rgyas myos sems kyi
bhra ma ra/ /dga' ldan padmo'i tshal du 'jug par spro/ /sa gsum mun pa sel ba'i sgron me mchog /rgyal ba'i gsung rab bka' 'gyur dri ma med/ /glegs bam brgya phrag bzhengs
pas legs byas kyis/ /bstan pa rin chen phyogs brgyar 'bar

gyur cig /deng dus skye bo phal cher bsod nams dman/ /gsung rab klog dang mchod 'bul sri zhu sogs/ /bsgrub par dka' ba'i rang gi dad brtson gyis/ /dngul srang brgya phrag brgal
ba thebs rtsar sbyar/ /deng dus skye bo phal cher bsod nams dman/ /rlabs chen dge ba'i rtsa bas 'brel thogs kyi/ /shi gson rnams kyi gtsos pa'i 'gro ba kun/ /sdug bsngal
gsum gyi btson ra las thar te/ /rnam mkhyen rgyal ba'i go 'phang thob par smon/ /e ma hoH sprang 'khos med blo gsal bstan skyong la/ /nor gsog srun blo na ma mchis kyang
/ /khong dad ldan shi gson dngos nor rnams/ /don snying po lon phyir dge phyogs bsgyur/ /yul mchod dang sbyin gtong bya ba'i gnas/ /mi bdag la khyad par ma mchis kyang
/ /don phyogs ris cung zad mi bdog pas/ /phyogs gang du byas kyang mnyam nyid do/ /dus deng sang dpal ldan zhwa lu 'dir/ /rje bu ston bstan pa nyag re phra/ /chos thos
bsam sgom gsum lta gzhog gi /rten lha khang rnams kyang 'o re rgyal/ /tshul de 'dra bsam tshe mchi ma bku/ /khong gong ma'i mdzad pa yang yang dran/ /sprang bdag la nus
pa ma mchis kyang / /don de phyir skrad skrad shig shig byas/ /khong phyogs na bzhugs pa'i

skye bo kun/ /mi kho bo phyogs rigs cha snyam nas/ /khong zhwa lu par 'dod zhen che'o zer/ /bdag chags sdang che mang mthol bshags 'bul/ /dus nam zla dpyid kyi rgyal mo la/
/bya khu byug gsung snyan 'khrol byed kyang / /khong lcog chung byi'u rang sa nas/ /skad gre 'gyur ngoms par mi byed dam/ /dus deng sang snyigs mar song ba yi/ /gnas gang
du skyes kyang bde ba med/ /yul 'dzam gling phyogs su skyes pa'i rten/ /drod ma thob bar du mi 'byung shog /khong 'brom ston rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas la/ /gnas dga' ldan
zhing du 'khrungs pa'i brdar/ /snyun 'dze yi zhabs g.yas chad pa ltar/ /sprang bdag la de bzhin 'byung bar shog /da sgyu ma'i skyes chen bteg ma thag /steng ya ki'i dga'
ldan lha yi gnas/ /rje byams pa mgon po'i zhabs drung du/ /dus myur du skye ba'i bkra shis shog /de nas dbyar gnas grol ba dang bkras lhun nor yon chen po phebs te dgos bzhed
kyi tshe bka' byabs khrus dang lung kha shas phul grang chu'i 'phrod brten zhag 'ga' byas/ chab mdo 'phags pa lhun grub dang bkras lhun dge bshes dbyig gnyen phebs par
dbang chos kha

shas dgos gsung ba khas len zhus rung / rmi lam du kun mkhyen bu ston rin po che sngon la dngos gnas yin pa 'dra ba zhig la/ rjes su 'jim pa'i skur gyur nas dum bu mang bar
zhag song zla ba de'i tshes brgyad la dgong mo gsang ba'i bdag po'i bzlas pa byed khul la glo bur du chab seng gro nas grib gdong thug tu rgyab nas de kha rang la lam seng
skyas chen bteg na dga' ba 'dug kyang gang ltar shim na rom na kho na la da phan sdod pa sogs byung / dge phrug gi zur gnas dang dge slong rin chen smon lam bsam gtan
gnyis kyi nyal gnyis zas bcud spangs pa'i nad g.yog dang lhag par ri zur gnas kyi rim gro sogs gang drag ci drag byas/ /de phan chad ri zur gnas la lung ma thob pa phran
bu ma gtogs chos 'chad nyan sogs re ba bral song khyad par chab mdo 'phags pa lha sku phreng dang po'i thugs sras rgya rwa sprul sku nged kyis rta lo'i nang tsam la phebs
zhus kyang ma phebs par 'di skabs phebs pas mjal phrad tsam yang ma thub/ 'on kyang nged rang nas chos gsan rgyu rnams nged rang ni nad pa'i lci ba sogs bshad nyan gyi re
bral brten/ dge phrug ri zur nas kyis ngor thar rtse'i mkhan rin po che la yi ge phul te khong rang gi

'dod chos rnams thob thabs byas 'dug /de nas bzung te dkon mchog gi bka' drin la brten rang lcogs kyi dge sbyor la dga' ba bsgom bzhin pa'i ngang nas gzhan gyi ngo phrad mi
dgos pa sogs rgyas bcad kyi sdod zos bde mo 'di byung ba'i shin tu yang yid spro/ da ma shi bar la lam 'di rang la 'gro ba'i ngang nas dge rtsa rnams mkha' mnyam gyi sems
can thams cad la bsngo ba dang / smon lam 'debs mu ru mchis/ gnas skabs shi gson khag gi ngo 'dzin phran bu 'ong ba rnams ni dpon slob rin po che nas mi 'phyug pa 'dug
/lhag par nyin mtshan khor mo yug chu nad g.yog byed 'os sogs gang spyir bu blo gros can 'di dang / dge slong rin chen smon lam bsam ga tan 'di gnyis kyi rang gi blo dang
mthun pa'i brtson 'grus ni deng dus kyi ca la nyin skar dang mtshungs pa'i shin tu dga' ba thob/ da sgyu ma'i skyes chen nye 'byang gang la bteg kyang yid bde/ nged kyi
yid la bya 'dod kyi mngags gtam phran bu yod rigs ni brjod zin/ gzhan ma chags zhen ni til gyi 'bru tsam yang mi 'dug pa'i/ rjes kyi bya ba rnams dpon slob rin po che rang
nas bsam blo ga le

thongs las bslos dpyad pa'i mi 'thus pa mi 'dug go /a ho/ chos 'brel dngos thob kyi bla ma sum cu so gsum la 'dud do/ /snyigs dus bu slob kyi bsod nams 'og sgo'i nang du rang
zad do/ /rnal 'byor nga 'chi bdag pho nya'i bya gtong grogs po dang phrad song / /a ho phebs bzhud gnang byung gza' bdud kyi rgyal po rA hu la/ /a ho dad ldan gyi yon
bdag shi gson 'brel thogs kyi nor rdzas/ log tsho sna tshogs las byung pa'i mchod sbyin gtong phod che ba tsho'i/ 'phral gang byung du snyed pa dag bsod nams gsog thabs su
bsgyur yod/ /a ho phebs bzhud gnang byung 'chi bdag gi rgyal po rA hu la/ /a ho rnal 'byor bdag 'jig rten phyi ma'i lam chen la thegs 'gro/ /tshe 'di'i bya ba phal cher
gad mo shor shor rang du grub song / /zhen chags 'khri ba med pas blo bde'i yang rtse gcig rang myur shog /a ho phebs bzhud gnang byung brtan gyis mdun ma yi yang rtse/
/ces so/ /de nas chab mdo 'phags pa lhun grub kyang na tsha sna tshogs zhig gis mnar nas sman dpyad rim gro gang drag bgyis kyang phan ma thogs par khams ma 'tsho ba kho
pa rang gi shul dngos phran bu rjes su dge sgrub la

btang zhing khyad par bdun tshigs ngo re bzhin dge slong bzhi grwa res byams smon 'dod du 'jug pa sogs byas te khang pa nged la ched du gtad nas yong pa yin 'dug pa'i dga'
ldan du skye ba dang nged rang yang de'i mjug tu dga' ldan du skyes nas phan thogs byed rgyu e yong snyam pa yin/ dga' ldan phun tshogs gling du rje spor pa chen po de nyid
dang bu lung sku zhabs bcas kyi dgongs bzhed bzhin bla brang chen por gser snyan gsol nas bde mchog bstod chen gyi 'grel pa'i mjug gi par shing ma tshang ba rnams tshang
ma brkos/ ngam ring nas rje kun dga' grol mchog gi gsung gang yod dang khyad par jo nang 'khrid brgya phun gling bar khang du spyan 'dren zhu thub pa byas/ rje btsun tA
ra nA tha'i gsung 'bum dkar chag kyang legs par yong thabs byas/ zla ba drug pa'i tshes bzhi la skyabs mgon paN chen rin po che bkra shis lhun po'i tshogs phebs mdzad
nas gsung bsngo gnang rgyu yin 'dug pa'i 'di nas kyang zhabs brtan tshigs bcad maNDal sku gsung thugs rten sogs dang bkras lhun tshogs chen la mang ja bcas zhus de yan

chad kyi da lta phan la rang gi tshe 'di'i byas byung cung zad yod pa rnams bskul ba po gzhan gyi ngor bris nas thag chod par byas so/ /sgyu ma mi rtag ston pa'i grong khyer
du/ /sgyu ma'i lus 'di sngon las dbang gis thob/ /sgyu ma 'khrul pa'i bya spyod sna tshogs kyang / /sgyu ma'i dpe brgyad lta bur gsal bar byas/ /deng sang dus nas skya
bo phal cher ni/ /ri bong rwa yi gzugs brnyan sna tshogs pa/ /nam mkha'i me tog sil mas mchod pa yi/ /ngang tshul 'ud khog bsgrags nas smra ba mthong / /a ho dman rmongs
bdag la bsngags 'os kyi/ /mkhas dang grub pa'i yon tan cang med kyang / /rang mnyam 'gro la ba 'gre cu 'gre rnams/ /mos ldan 'ga' yi bskul nas yi ger bkod/ /yon tan med pa'i
blun po bdag 'dra la/ /gzhan gyi sgro btags sna tshogs byung gis dogs/ /kho bos 'di rang 'di 'dra bgyis so zhes/ /rang gi gnas tshul drang por brjod pa'o/ /dge 'dis bdag
gi mthong thos dran reg gi /bzang ngan 'brel po thegs pa'i sems can rnams/ /tshe rabs kun tu dal 'byor rten brgyud nas/ /bla med rdzogs pa'i byang chub thob gyur cig
/bkra shis kun 'byung rtsa ba'i bla ma dang / /bkra shis dngos grub mchog stsol yi dam lha/ /bkra shis bsrung ma'i tshogs kyi dus kun

tu / /bkra shis rgya mtshos lhag par skyong gyur cig /ces rang gi rnam thar du byas pa bde sdug gi tshor ba sna tshogs bdag gir spyad pa'i tshul shel dkar me long zhes bya
ba 'di ni dang por yun ring po zhig nas chos rje byang gling rin chen dpal tshul nas ja 'dren dang bcas bskul ba dang rang gi bu ri phug khri zur rin chen blo bzang mkhyen
rab pa'i yid 'dod bsgrub phyir dang / bar du chab mdo sku zhabs zhi bzang rin po che nas chab shog dang bcas bskul ma mdzad rung kho bo la yon tan gyi cha shas ril tsam
med pa de 'dra bris kyang don med snyam nas zhag rung tham/ ngor e waM chos ldan nas mkhan rin po che kun dga' sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi bka' nan lci ba phebs
pa dang / phyis su bsam na bla ma dang sku skye'i mtshan 'di bzhin la brtags tshe skyur dad che ba tsam byung na grub thob bIr wa pa dang gtum cha che ba tsam byung na
lho brang mar pa sogs yin zhes skyon yon tan du blangs te ltos bcas rnams kyi dril sgrog par byed la de ltar na/ mdo sde rgyan las/ bshes gnyen dul ba zhi zhing nyer zhi
ba/ /yon tan lhag por brtson bcas lung gis phyug /de nyid rab tu rtogs pa smra mkhas

ldan / /brtse ba'i bdag nyid skyo ba spangs la brten/ /zhes gsungs pa sogs kyang don med pa dang rang nyid kyang zog poji 'dra zhig tu btang yong mi shes snyam rang gis byas
tshul gang yin la sgro ma btag bskrun pa ma btab rang bzhin brjod pa kho na byas te blo gsal ri khrod pa rang nyid kyi mig dmar zhes pa shing pho byi ba'i lo hor zla bcu
gnyis pa'i yar ngo rgyal ba gsum pa'i nyin gdan sa chen po zhwa lu ri phug tu spyod pa'i yi ge ba ni bu dam tshig can bla zur blo bzang mkhyen rab dang nye par gnas pa
dge slong rin chen smon lam bsam gtan gnyis kyi bgyis pa'o/ /'dis snyung 'khor pa sdug bsngal gyi rgya mtsho chen po myur du skebs par gyur cig / /swa sti/ rmad byung mdzad
bzang rin chen 'byung pa'i gnas/ /dad ldan yid kyi re 'dod bskong ba dang / /bka' drin cha shas bsab dang bsgrib byang ched/ /dam pa'i zhabs 'khod dge slong smon bsam
gyis/ /lhag bsam dag pas par du bskrun pa'i dge/ /dpal ldan bla ma'i thugs dgongs rdzogs pa dang / /spyi sgos bstan dang de 'dzin sku tshe brtan/ /bdag sogs 'gro kun 'bral
med rjes 'dzin shog / manggalaM

gtsug na zla ba gser mngal mig stong ldan/ /lha yi bla ma yid srubs gos ser can/ /mig nyid yid skyes gdengs can la sogs pas/ /zhabs pad gus bsten zas gtsang sras la 'dud/ /don
dam gzhan stong mi 'gyur bde ba che/ /rnam kun mchog ldan dmigs bcas stong pa nyid/ /zung 'jug 'od gsal phyag rgya chen mo la/ /gus pas 'dud do mtshan rtog dag las skyobs/
/dge legs rin chen bye ba'i gter gnas shing / /dam chos phud sgra 'di dbyangs snyan g.yob yi/ /rgyal ba'i bstan skyong nor bdun gdengs ka can/ /dpal ldan skal ba bzang
po rgyal gyur cig /khyod kyi yon tan mi zad rgya mtsho las/ /thu thigs tsam zhig bdag gi dad pa'i blos/ /gus bar blangs nas nyung ngu rnam gsal gyi/ /ngo mtshar gtam
brjod phreng ba 'di dbye'o/ /zhwa lu gser bkang zhes pa'i grong khyer du/ /lung rtogs yon tan mdzod

'dzin 'gos kyi rigs/ /sku zhang blon po rin chen seng ge dar/ /gdung brgyud 'dzin pa bsam grub dpal bzang yab/ /rin chen chos 'dzom zhes bya'i yum mchog la/ /lcags pho bya
yi lo la ngo mtshar sku/ /dul zhing rgyud 'jam yum gyi nor 'dzin gzhir/ /smon lam dag pa'i chu gtsang la bsten nas/ /snying rje'i 'dab stong dad pa'i ze'u 'bru can/ /rnyed
dka'i a dum wa ra chos skyong 'bum/ /bstan pa'i sgron me dam pa 'di 'khrungs so/ /de tshe bstan la dga' ba'i 'chi med dbang / /dga' mgu rangs pa'i yid kyi dpalaldan zhing
/ /rin chen lha rdzas me tog sna tshogs kyis/ /rmad byung gzhon nu mchod par byas zhes thos/ /de tshe snying rje cher g.yo zhing / /chos 'chad gsan dang dgon pa 'debs
tshul dang / /mnyam gzhag ting 'dzin zab mo 'di pa la mnga' pas/ // /rgyun mi 'chad pa 'ang byung pa yin no gsung / /khyod thugs spros med mkha' dbyings dwangs pa la/ /mi
'gyur bde ba'i dkyil 'khor rab rgyas pas/ /mchog ldan legs pa'i mar gyur padmo'i gnyen/ /lham me lhang nge lhan ner gyur pa'i tshe/ /mtshan rnyog mun pa'i smag rum drung
phyungs nas/ /ting 'dzin 'od kyi dra bas khyab pa dang / /don dam bde gshegs snying po'i pad dkar phreng / /kun du gsal ba'i 'dzum dkar ma g.yos sam/ /dge ba'i bshes gnyen
bkra shis rin chen pa/ /legs par bsten te bod kyi klog yig sbyangs/ /bod kyi

skad la bag chags chung pa yis/ /klog dang yi ge slob pa dka' zhes gsung / /de nas brtsams te dgung lo nyer gnyis bar/ /khyim na gnas pa'i tshul bzung de yi tshe'ang / /shes
rab gsum la blo gros sbyangs pa mdzad/ /nyer gnyis pa la lung rtogs yon tan mdzod/ /'jam dbyangs dkon mchog bzang pos mkhan po dang / /kun dga' dpal bzang pa yis slob dpon
mdzad/ /dge tshul sdom bzhes nyer drug phebs pa'i tshe/ /mkhan po don grub grags pa dpal bzang dang / /las kyi slob dpon bsod nams grags pa'i zhabs/ /gsang sde ston pa
bsod nams blo gros pas/ /legs par mdzad de dge slong sdom pa bzhes/ /nyid sku btso ma'i gser mdog dpal yon can/ /ngur smrig gos kyi dra bas legs 'khyud de/ /bcas ldan yongs
rdzogs shAkya'i dge slong mchog /bstan pa'i sgron me dam par gyur pa'i tshe/ /thub dbang zas gtsang sras po 'gro ba'i gnyen/ /nyi khri chig stong drub brgya'i rjes 'brang
can/ /mi zad dga' ba'i gter chen rab g.yos nas/ /ston pa'i rgyal tshab dam par dbang bskur ro/ /sku zhang dge slong mkhan chen chos grub dang / /brag dmar rab 'byams
bla ma don rin pa/ /dka' bzhi thugs rje dpa' ba bshes gnyen bzang / /dge 'dun grub dang snye mo sku zhang ba/ /ting 'dzin 'od zer bsod nams grags pa'i zhabs/ /gsal ba grags
dang gong ma kun dga' legs/ /rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' dbang phyug dang / /gong ma chos

rje bdag chen blo gros pa/ /chos rin dpal ba chos grags rgyan cho dang / /sku zhang mkhyen rab rab 'byams bde bzang pa/ /kun bzang rtse pa zhwa dmar bzhi pa dang / /dka' thub
pa dang stag lung bla ma gsum/ /kun mkhyen don dpal dpon slob ngag dbang grags/ /gnas brtan legs rgyal dpal sdings sgra ba dang / /grags pa rgya mtsho rgya ston lcags
ri ba/ /thar pa bzang po stag tshang lo tsa ba/ /dkon mchog tshul khrims chag lo bzhi pa dang / /bcags thang ras chen dwags po paN chen sogs/ /yongs su 'dzin pa bcu phrag
lnga bsten nas/ /bod du 'gyur ba'i bka' dang bstan bcos dang / /sgra dang tshad ma snyan ngag sdeb sbyor dang / /dbang dang byin rlabs snying po'i don khrid sogs/ /legs
par gsan pas thos pa'i pha rol son/ /bdag nyid chen po 'di yis dus 'khor gyi/ /'grel chen dang ni dpag bsam 'khri shing dang / /'dul ba mdo rtsa la sogs rgya gar gyi/ /bstan
bcos brgya phrag tsam gyi rgya dpe dang / /bod skad legs par sbyar te gzigs par mdzad/ /mngon brjod bstan chos sna tshogs gsal ba dang / /mtshan brjod 'grel ba dbu ma
la dga' bas/ /mdzad pa gnyis sogs gzhi 'gyur mang po dang / /byams chos rgyud gsum la sogs mang dag la/ /'gyur bcos mdzad cing hor khongs bsab pa sogs/ /thub bstan rin chen
gsal ba'i sgron me mdzad/ /bdag cag rnams kyis pod dpe lag bzung ste/ /rje btsun nyid kyis de yi rgya

dpe brtsams/ /phyag tu bzhes te bod skad du bsgyur ba/ /yig ge gcing kyang lhag chad med pa nyid/ /bod klog bzang ba kun gyis non dka' ba/ /drung du yun ring gnas pa kun la
gsal/ /gzhon nu'i dus na lha khang bskor ba'i tshe/ /mgon po beng gis 'di la gsung byung ste/ /rigs kyi bu khyod mngon par sangs rgyas par/ /kho bos skyab dang bsrung dang
sba zhes gsungs/ /grong khyer skya bo nad kyis dkrugs pa'i tshe/ /grong khyer nad las bsrung ba'i thugs dam mdzad/ /gdugs mdzes gnyis rim phub pa'i sgrol ma yis/ /snyug
tshal rim pa gsum gyis bskor ba dang / /slob dpon chen po dpal ldan be ru pas/ /khyed nyid 'od gsal mnal du song ba'i tshe/ /dges rdor dbang bskur zhu gsung byon pa dang
/ /khams pa brtson 'grus nga la nyid kyi rdzas/ /mang dag bskur pa phyi rol lam zhugs te/ /rku bar brtsams pa zin tshe thams cad gnang / /sku 'dab btsos pa rlung gis khyer
te lhung / /de nyid skye bo gzhan gyis bdag gir byas/ /kho bos blos btang zhes gsungs de la stsal/ /thub pa'i bstan dang sems can mang po la/ /phan par gyur na dmyal
ba'i g.yang sa la'ang / /'jigs mi bya zhes bsrungs zhal gyis 'ches/ /yos lo hor zla lnga pa'i nyer lnga'i nyin/ /byams pa gling gi smon lam 'dzugs tshe phebs/ /de nub bdag
gi rmi lam la rten nas/ /mngon mthar 'jam pa'i dpal gyi rjes bzung bas/ /rig gnas kun gyi srol 'byed bla na med/ /dga' ldan gnas na mi

dges ba'i bshes/ /phul byung mchod 'os dam pa khyod phyag 'tshal/ /zhes pa'i bstod pa rje btsun zhal gyis bzhes/ /bdag gis 'di phyi'i lung bstan zhus pa'i tshe/ /slar yang
snying po'i zhu ba 'di ltar lags/ /'das dang ma 'ongs yang dag lta ba la/ /gnas na dge ba'i bshes kyi bgyi 'os yin/ /de pas gzhan du 'bad kyang don 'grub dka'/ /gsal bar
gyur rnams mngon sum lam du bkod/ /spros dang bcas pa ces 'i 'jigs pas nongs/ /shes gsung phyi mtha' rig pa'i lung bstan mdzad/ /dkon mchog brtsegs pa'i mdo sde 'ba' bsgyur
ba'i/ /paN chen lha dbang byang chub ces pa der/ /gyur pa yin zhes zhal gyis 'ches par mdzad/ /ting 'dzin 'od kyi dra ba'i mtha' can la/ /byams chos gsan te zhwa lur bshad
pa mdzad/ /de tshe lha yi tshogs kyis me tog phul/ /dpal 'khor bde chen gser cong khang du/ /rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur zhus pa lo mang mdzad/ /de tshe mgon po khyod nyid
mnal ba'i dus/ /chos khrims bsod don gser chos ring dgag gi /stod cha bgyis te me chen 'bud pa rmi/ /legs par dpyad pas dkor gyi 'bras bur gzigs/ /dbus su byon stag lung
chos rje dang / /zhwa nag pa dang zhwa dmar la sogs bsten/ /bla chen gsum la sgra dang snyan ngag sogs/ /gsung gi bdud rtsi'i dga' ston yang yang stsal/ /spyan ras gzigs
dbang chos grags rgya mtsho yis/ /'jig rten dbang po'i sku sogs legs gnang ste/ /khyod kyi skye bo sgra dang snyan ngag dang / /sdeb sbyor mngon brjod la

sogs tha snyad kun/ /legs par slob pa'i bstan pa'i sgron mer bskos/ /nga gsum pa la rgya ston lhags ri pa'i/ /gdan sar phebs te chos kyi 'khor lo bskor/ /nga lnga pa la grwa
pa mngon shes kyi/ /gdan sar bzhugs te bstan pa'i sgron me sngar/ /don bzhi pa la kun mkhyen bu ston gyi/ /gdan sar phebs te zab rgyas chos 'khor bskor/ /mkhas pa chen
po sa skya lo tsa sogs/ /lo tsa legs par shes pa rnam dgu dang / /gangs can khrod na tha snyad gtsug lag la/ /legs par byang pa'i mkhas mang du ma yod/ /mkhas grub dam pa
dpal ldan dbu rgyan rjes/ /mkhas pa'i dbang po rtse thang 'bum ram pa/ /mkhan chen chos grub seng ge la sogs pa'i/ /gangs ri'i khrod kyi mkhas grub mang po yis/ /gsung gi
bdud rtsi gus pa'i sgo nas bzhes/ /nyin par rtsom 'chad sgyur pas dus 'da' zhing / /mtshan mo'i tshe la 'od gsal ngang du gzims/ /khrom dang 'bag 'cham la sogs 'ba' yi
tshe/ /rmi lam sgyu ma'i dran 'dun cung zad mdzad/ /de tshe sgyu lus  du gzims so gsung / /bdud rtsi ril bu thog mar bsgrubs pa'i tshe/ /mkhyen rab chos rje steng gi nam
mkhar byon/ /'chi med bdud rtsi sgrub lugs legs po gnang / /sku gsung thugs la ye shes legs phab ste/ /'phar g.yo seng ge'i sgra dang ting 'dzin byams/ /thod pa'i nang gi
'chi med bdud rtsi lung / /skye bo'i nad dang sdug bsngal chen po'i tshogs/ /'joms par byed pa'i sman mchog 'di nyid yin/ /gsung rab phal la zhu dag mdzad pa'i tshe/ /kun
mkhyen gnyis pa sa paN nyid dang

mtshungs / /gnyis med ting 'dzin ngang la 'jog pa tshe/ /nA ro'i zhabs dang dpal ldan bir wa pa/ /byams pa'i thugs kyis 'gro kun skyong ba'i tshe/ /zhi ba lha dang rgod tshang
rgyal sras pa/ /dri med ngur smrig 'dzin pa'i tshul zhugs tshe/ /dpal ldan a ti sha dang mgon po khyod/ /nam yang dbye ba med par bdag gis khums/ /thub dbang shAkya'i
tog dang mi pham mgon/ /'jam pa'i dbyangs dang spyan ras gzigs dbang dang / /klu sgrub thogs med la sogs shing rta che/ /rnams dang khyod nyid mtshungs zhes zhal gyis bzhes/
/de ltar dgung lo brgyad cu rtsa brgyad bar/ /rtsom 'chad bsgyur dang dbang dang gdam ngag dang / /rjes gnang rigs gtad lung dang rigs pa dang / /rnam dkar dge bcu pha
rol phyin drug dang / /chos spyod bcu yis gangs ri'i khrod 'di ru/ /thub pa'i bstan pa ches cher gsal bar mdzad/ /gyu bdun pa la rang gi dbon gyur pa/ /pad dkar lo tsa
bla ma'i gdan sar bskos/ /khong gis rin chen las grub sku 'dra dang / /gsar 'bum thog tshad ngo mtshar che ba bzhengs/ /grwa pa mngon shes gtsug lag khang chen gsos/ /grwa
thang dgon par sde snod bshad grwa dang / /rje btsun nyid kyi lo mchod sman bla btsugs/ /de tshe bstan la dga' ba'i lha tshogs kyis/ /me tog char phab thog la thogs med
par/ /ting phor yon chab me tog tshogs kyis gang / /skye bo thams cad dad pa'i gnas su bzhag /skye dang skye ba'i tshe rabs thams cad du/ /mgon po khyed sku yang yang lta
ba dang / /gsung mchog bdud rtsi'i ro la rol ba dang / /

g.yo med khyod thugs phyag rgya chen po dang / /bdag brgyud gcig tu 'dres te bstan pa dang / /rnam mnga' 'gro ba'i don chen 'grub par shog /dge ba'i gtam 'di ri bo'i mgul par
du/ /rgyal khams sprang po ratna bha dras bsdebs/ /de las byung pa'i rab dkar dge tshogs kyis/ /'gro kun myur du smin cing grol gyur cig /i ti/ /ces pa'i zhu pa po ni
chos rje smyug la ba'o/ / /shubha / /
